MAT 1:1 Yesu Kilisi buyeiw leind wei yeip eivek qapiya eno inye eivek velei wei Dawit o, de Dawit on eivek velei wei Apraham o.
MAT 1:2 Apraham on Isaka ma, de Isaka yon Yakop ma, de Yakop on Yuda ma me liyeiw is,
MAT 1:3 Yuda yon Peres aluw Sela mend, de luw tend lei Tamar, de Peres on Hesron ma, de Hesron on Ram ma,
MAT 1:4 Ram on Aminadap ma, de Aminadap on Nason ma, de Nason on Salmon ma,
MAT 1:5 Salmon on Boas ma de ta lei Rahap, de Boas on Obet ma de ta lei Rut, de Obet on Jesi ma,
MAT 1:6 de Jesi yon king Dawit ma. De Dawit on Salomo ma, e tiwei ta Yuria venei yo,
MAT 1:7 Salomo yon Rehoboam ma, de Rehoboam on Abiya ma, de Abiya yon Asa ma,
MAT 1:8 Asa yon Jehosapat ma, de Jehosapat on Jehoram ma, de Jehoram on Usia ma,
MAT 1:9 Usia yon Jotam ma, de Jotam on Ahas ma, de Ahas on Hesekia ma.
MAT 1:10 Hesekia yon Manase ma, de Manase yon Amon ma, de Amon on Yosia ma.
MAT 1:11 De Yosia yon Jekonaia ma me moxo lis liyeiw mindei gyeik xel Babilon lam wo vevek me zeimaxoun xel Israel de qou xel me la Babilon.
MAT 1:12 Ka xel la Babilon: Woyom Jekonaia yon Seatiel ma, de Seatiel on Serubabel ma.
MAT 1:13 De Serubabel on Abiut ma, de Abiut on Eliakim ma, de Eliakim on Aso ma.
MAT 1:14 De Aso yon Sadok ma, de Sadok on Akim ma, de Akim on Eliut ma,
MAT 1:15 de Eliut on Eliesa ma, de Eliesa yon Matan ma, de Matan on Yakop ma.
MAT 1:16 De Yakop on Yosep ma, de Yosep on Maria leya, Maria wei qou Yesu wei xel mi taxe bei Kilisi yo, moux on Anutu beyal bei e qou moux alis vex wei e yo noum.
MAT 1:17 Inyon nambei 14 neumambu wei Apraham me ela Dawit o, de 14 neumambu nanghei Dawit me ela tyip ingwei xel la xeitueing anghei Babilon o, deka xel la xeitueing anghei Babilon eno 14 neumambu me ela tyip wou bouk wei Yesu Kilisi yo.
MAT 1:18 Tine inye pavulek en ingwei Yesu Kilisi umbek o: Moxo ta Maria eno xel beyal bei e mendei wou Yosep, luw se ghei dei lekti ekom vexo xei qou veil en Laweeng Vambuing nikanzek.
MAT 1:19 Maria leya Yosep on tambiy wei bombek om embei se bong niyalenyeing wou vexo eivek xel moux alis vex dalus mend, om embei na veil e xupekeing.
MAT 1:20 Ekom Yosep nanghei di wounalei en tine, Tambiy Ngandoung xe angela lam wou e eivek maviing me neil, “Yosep wa velei wei Dawit o, wa seng gwaleeng qe wa qou Maria nambei veneim, en yak tiwei tumi eivek e yon inye lam wou Laweeng Vambuing.
MAT 1:21 Tyek vexo bou neu moux ti, yond wa taxe e lei bei Yesu, en tyek devind e xe xel veil xel xe sewokeing.”
MAT 1:22 Lul dalus tine la teyei lek ambei ingwei Tambiy Ngandoung neil eivek poropet mya yo:
MAT 1:23 “Wei, vexawo wei paleveeng o ti tyek xei qou veil me bou neu moux ti, de tyek xel taxe e bei Imanuel.” Qes ambei nye, “Anutu toundei is xey.”
MAT 1:24 Ka Yosep qandi lek de moxo wong ambei kawei Tambiy Ngandoung xe angela neil wou e yo, me qou Maria nambei e venei.
MAT 1:25 Ekom moxo se yeip is e qe ka Maria qou neu moux woy le. De moxo taxe neu lei Yesu.
MAT 2:1 Ka Yesu umbek eivek Betelem wei Yudia nei, eivek bouk wei king Herot eno xel lundpeyei wei mendalus wei mi yei dee lek betum eno lam anghei ninei me lam Yerusalem
MAT 2:2 me teling, “Tambiy tiwei umbek ambei king wei Yudayeiw eno toundei inya? Xa xei e xe betum anghei ninei me na lam en xa bei bong lalo wou e.”
MAT 2:3 King Herot ngo qayeeng tine eno moxo is xel Yerusalem dalus wounaleind ngenong.
MAT 2:4 Woyom moxo taxe xel lumuki leitata me xel putoung wei petieing wei xomaxoneing dalus o, moxo teling wou xel bei Kilisi tyek dumbek anghei inya?
MAT 2:5 Xel neil elox, “Eivek Betelem wei Yudia nei, en inye qayeeng vati wei poropet byex takwei yo:
MAT 2:6 “‘Ekom Betelem wang eivek tembuing danghei wei Yuda yo wa leim se nayak en beyeeng leilaing wei Yuda yo, en eivek wang eno tyek wa xe tambiy ti bong ambei wa xe leilaing me tyek mendei bei gyovaxa wei a xe xomaxoneing wei Israel o.’”
MAT 2:7 Woyom Herot taxe xel lundpeyei wei mendalus o xupekeing me ngo teyei wou xel bei lek bouk vati eno betum lam nale.
MAT 2:8 Moxo wong xel la Betelem me neil, “Xam la me wimexe e wo nimza en yak on. Ka xam ghe gweiwou e, xam ghe bong qayeeng nam wou ay, en kandek ana bong lalo wou e is.”
MAT 2:9 Ka xel ngo king xe qayeeng woy, xel la wou sakwaing no me la, me betum wei xel yei ghei ninei eno la tax en xel, dekalekom la nale ghey lek beyeeng kawei yak on toundei ghei yo.
MAT 2:10 Gyeik xel yei betum eno xel wo xeindlala ngandoung.
MAT 2:11 Xel la eivek xomek lalei me yei yak on is ta Maria, de xel ev vaxend qatu eivek dom wo lalo wou e. Woyom xel tax xel xe vaxak malew dom wong ghol, me xax myalouk, me xax myalouk nge wei mi wo xeimangou yo la wou e.
MAT 2:12 De Anutu peti xel eivek maviing bei xel se nox wou Herot, qe xel na nox sakwaing ba me nox bend.
MAT 2:13 Ka xel lundpeyei wei mendalus la veil, Tambiy Ngandoung xe angela lam wou Yosep eivek maviing. Me neil, “Qandi lek me qou yak on aluw ta me pek me la Izip. Xam a mi mendei inyon deka a neil wou wang bole, en Herot di yimexe yak on en embei nyeis e mey.”
MAT 2:14 Om moxo qandi lek, me qou yak on aluw ta me la eivek boukeing me la Izip,
MAT 2:15 de moxo mindei inyon deka Herot mey le. Me lul tine la teyei lek ambei Tambiy Ngandoung neil eivek poropet mya yo. “A taxe neung moux bei e nam veil Izip.”
MAT 2:16 Gyeik Herot woulek bei xel wei lundpeyei wei ninei eno tyoxe e, moxo lalei wo vanei mouyo, om wong qayeeng nikanzek bei xel nyeis xel yak moux dalus eivek Betelem me xel yak wei beyeeng paviyeing wei xel xe vakovek qes yuw o me e teiloum axo, teyei lek bouk wei e ngo wou xel lundpeyei wei ninei yo.
MAT 2:17 Woyom lul tine la teyei lek ambei Anutu neil eivek poropet Yelemia mya yo.
MAT 2:18 “Vya ti eno xel ngo eivek beyeeng Rama, inyon engeing me talot ngandoung, Resel di eng en neuyeiw dalus mey, me vexo embei xel se bong e lalei bo nimza, en nambei neuyeiw dalus mey de ti se toundei mapieing.”
MAT 2:19 Ka Herot mey woy eno Tambiy Ngandoung xe angela ti lam wou Yosep eivek maviing nanghei Izip
MAT 2:20 de neil, “Qandi lek, me qou yak on aluw ta me lox me la tembuing wei Israel nei, en xel wei embei nyeis yak on na mey eno mey.”
MAT 2:21 Om moxo qandi lek me qou yak on aluw ta me lal lox me la tembuing wei Israel o.
MAT 2:22 Ekom e ngo bei Arkelaus yeiteyei Yudia eivek ma Herot nimbeeng, om moxo yaleeng en embei se na inyon. Ekom Anutu neil wou Yosep eivek maviing ti, om moxo la distrik Galili,
MAT 2:23 me la dei eivek beyeeng wei xel mi taxe bei Nasaret. Om tine la teyei lek ambei ingwei neil eivek poropet myend o. “Tyek xel taxe e bei tambiy wei Nasaret o.”
MAT 3:1 Eivek bouk ti beimambei yon eno Yoan lipekeing lam, moxo neil qayeeng eivek tembuing bandaing wei Yudia nei
MAT 3:2 me neil, “Xam pekwi xow, en tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno lam paviy.”
MAT 3:3 Tambiy tine inye tiwei Anutu luk en e eivek poropet Yesaya mya yo: “Tambiy ti vya taxe lam anghei tembuing bandaing nei, ‘Menyex wou sakwaing en Tambiy Ngandoung, wong sakwaing on wo bombek en e.’”
MAT 3:4 Yoan xe teimb on xel duw angya leliy kamel nivlus, me mi vex let wei xel duw en leliy ninavi yo vivekwou xeikatu. E xeeng yaeing on zevak me beyexta nilouk wei qeis lalei yo.
MAT 3:5 Xomaxoneing nanghei Yerusalem me nanghei Yudia tambak nei me danghei dalus wei memiing Yorodan vi eno xel lam wou e.
MAT 3:6 Xel neil xel xe sewokeing teyei, de Yoan lipek xel eivek memiing Yorodan.
MAT 3:7 Ekom moxo yei xel ngenong wei Parisi me Sadyusi lam en embei qou lipekeing, moxo neil wou xel: “Xam on myeiy nilul neu! Eti neil wou xam bei tyek xam a pek me ghe na veil Anutu lalei vanei wei di lam o?
MAT 3:8 Wangwei xam pekwi xow neing nei yon kwa wei xam eno talex lek bei xam ghe pekwi xow.
MAT 3:9 De xam seng boueivek naleimim me na neil wou venaxow bei, ‘Xa mami Apraham.’ A neil wou xam bei Anutu teyei bei bong qakous beimambei ne qandi lek me ghok ambei Apraham neuyeiw.
MAT 3:10 Qov di yeip wou xax qes woy, om xax tambak wei se mi vuk neing nimza eno tyek xel buv veil me banex ena eivek nenyex.
MAT 3:11 “A lipek xam en memiing bei xam pekwi xow. Ekom Tambiy tiwei tyek nam yus en ay eno e nikanzek ghanaw a veil, a se nimza teyei bei qalei e xe vaxalambes. Moxo tyek zipek xam en Laweeng Vambuing me nenyex is.
MAT 3:12 Moxo zeim taliv eivek mema, en embei seyex wit en beyal myapapu veil wit neing, de qekuwou me na toung eivek xomek yaeing, ekom moxo tyek banyuw myapapu lek nenyex wei se mi mey yo.”
MAT 3:13 Woyom Yesu lam anghei Galili me la Yorodan bei Yoan zipek e.
MAT 3:14 Ekom Yoan embei paseisexe e me neil, “Teyei bei a qou lipekeing wou wang, nambei nya wang lam wou ay?”
MAT 3:15 Yesu neil elox, “Embong ondek wang bong ambei a neil ne, eivek kwa nimza tine uw teyei bei bong sakwaing dalus embo bombek.” Om Yoan betiwou e xe qayeeng.
MAT 3:16 Ka Yesu lipek woy, moxo lek lam veil memiing. Gyeik kayon bombek eno tyoung gheyapu tax, de moxo yei Anutu xe Laweeng Vambuing lam ambei menek beliy me dei lek e.
MAT 3:17 Vya ti lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei me neil, “Tine inye a Neung Moux, wei a laleing vind o. A laleing wo xeilala en e.”
MAT 4:1 Woyom Laweeng Vambuing qou Yesu me la tembuing bandaing nei bei tambiy mapetok bo axeing wou e.
MAT 4:2 Yesu vambu yaeing teyei lek bendiyeing mepyeiyuw me boukeing mepyeiyuw is om maxepya e.
MAT 4:3 Tambiy mapetok wei mi wo axeing eno lam wou e me neil, “Wangwei wa Anutu Neu Moux, ond neil me qakous ti beimambei ne pekwi nambei belet.”
MAT 4:4 Yesu neil elox, “Xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye: ‘Xomaxoneing se mindei mapieing en belet venaxow, qe xel mi dei mapieing en qayeeng tambak wei mi lam eivek Anutu mya yo.’ ”
MAT 4:5 Woyom tambiy mapetok qou e me la beyeeng vambuing Yerusalem me wong e nale lek xomek vambuing on pundanghou.
MAT 4:6 Moxo neil, “Wangwei wang on Anutu Neu Moux ond vyeip me la tembuing. En xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, “‘Moxo tyek bong qayeeng nikanzek wou e xe angela en xel gyeiteyei wang, me tyek xel a zeim wang zekna eivek memend, en kandek qakous ti se byex wa vaxam.’ ”
MAT 4:7 Yesu neil elox wou e, “Inyon xel byex eivek xoulek is bei: ‘Wa se toung wa xe Tambiy Ngandoung Anutu eivek axeing.’”
MAT 4:8 Kalekom tambiy mapetok qou e me la lek lukendu vaxading. De talex tete lalei wei tembuing sapa me lulul nimzamza dalus eno wou e.
MAT 4:9 E neil, “Wangwei wang dev vaxam qatu eivek me ghe bong lalo wou a nei on tyek am bong lul dalus tine wou wang.”
MAT 4:10 Ekom Yesu neil wou e, “Sandang, la dingta veil ay! En xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, ‘Wang bong lalo wou Tambiy Ngandoung wa xe Anutu me ghe bong xuk wou e venaxow.’ ”
MAT 4:11 Woyom tambiy mapetok la veil e, dom angela lam me vind e.
MAT 4:12 Ka Yesu ngo bei xel toung Yoan eivek xeitueing, moxo lox me la Galili.
MAT 4:13 De la veil Nasaret, me la dei eivek Kapenaom, wei di yeip wou lounyeing Galili vi yo, eivek tembuing wei Sebulon me Naptali.
MAT 4:14 Eivek kwa tine eno Yesu wong e la teyei lek ambei qayeeng wei Anutu neil eivek poropet Yesaya mya yo:
MAT 4:15 “Tembuing wei Sebulon me tembuing wei Naptali, eno di yeip wou lounyeing vi, me la valu wei Yorodan nei, me tembuing wei Galili wei xel amba lam dei lek o.
MAT 4:16 Om xomaxoneing wei mindei eivek mapetok ngandoung eno yei xeiyaing ngandoung ti. Me xel wei mindei eivek mapetok eno xeiyaing byex la lek xel.”
MAT 4:17 Lek bouk tiyon eno Yesu neil qayeeng atax wou xel, “Xam pekwi xow, en tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno lam paviy.”
MAT 4:18 Bouk ti eno Yesu la ghavineeng wou lounyeing Galili nenyawes, yei tambiy yayuw wei lindama yo, inyon Simon xel mi taxe bei Petele luw li Andrias. Luw di nex lewek eivek lounyeing, en nambei xel on ingwei mi qou woing o.
MAT 4:19 Woyom Yesu neil, “Muw lam me betiwou ay, en tyek a bong muw a qou xomaxoneing nambei muw ghe mi qou woing o.”
MAT 4:20 Lutika eno luw ghanaw luw xe lewek dom betiwou e.
MAT 4:21 Yesu la no, me yei tambiy yayuw inyon Jems wei Sebedi neu moux me li Yoan. Luw toundei eivek bot is ma teiv Sebedi, me di menyex wou lal xe lewek. Woyom Yesu taxe la wou luw.
MAT 4:22 Se wo lululek en luw ghanaw luw xe bot me ma teiv dom betiwou e.
MAT 4:23 Yesu la ghavineeng eivek Galili tambak, me di teyoxe xel eivek xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o, me moxo di neil Xoulek Nimza wei tete lalei, me wong xel wei vanei leimalei eno wo nimzalek eivek xel xomaxoneing on senghoing.
MAT 4:24 Yesu xe pavulek la wo sapa eivek Siria, me xomaxoneing qou xel dalus wei vanei leimalei wong xel o me lam wou e, eti yeiw wei vanei nilul is vanei ngandoung, me laweeng nilul dei eivek xel me xel wei vanei wei nietekeing mi wong xel mi pewilexe lek tembuing me xel wei kanzek mey eno Yesu wong xel wo nimzalek.
MAT 4:25 Xel qendu ngandoung wei betiy e eno lam anghei Galili me Dekapolis, me Yerusalem, me Yudia me Yorodan loxalu nei.
MAT 5:1 Yesu yei xel qendu ngandoung on lam, om moxo lek la lukendu nenyawes. Ka e la dei, e xe xel betiyeing lam wou e.
MAT 5:2 Om moxo teyoxe wou xel me neil,
MAT 5:3 “Anutu bo mata wou xel wei woulek bei xel kanyo eivek nund laweeng o, en tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno inyon xel xe.
MAT 5:4 “Anutu wong mata la wou eti yeiw wei mi wo talot o, en tyek bo xel laleind vevop.
MAT 5:5 “Anutu wong mata la wou eti yeiw wei mi beoux xow o, en tyek bong tembuing tambak wou xel.
MAT 5:6 “Anutu wong mata la wou eti yeiw wei mindei maxep me kwend mi tip en sakwaing bombek o, en tyek bong e na teyei lek wou xel.
MAT 5:7 Anutu wong mata la wou eti yeiw wei lalei pyaweing o en tyek talex lalei pyaweing wou xel.
MAT 5:8 Anutu wong mata la wou eti yeiw wei laleind wo vako yo, en tyek xel gyei Anutu.
MAT 5:9 “Anutu bo mata wou eti yeiw wei mi leis qayeeng mey me wo lalei vevopeing wou xomaxoneing o, en tyek xel taxe xel bei Anutu neuyeiw.
MAT 5:10 “Anutu bo mata wou eti yeiw wei mi qou nimaying en sakwaing bombek o, en tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno inyon xel xe.
MAT 5:11 “Anutu bo mata wou xam gyeik xel xomaxoneing embei bo nol wou xam o me na neil qayeeng nilul lek xam, me bo nimaying me tyonyeing lek xam me na neil qayeeng leimalei dalus wei nilul o lek xam en xam ghe mi betiwou ay.
MAT 5:12 Xam laleimim embo nimza me ghe bong xeimimlala, en xam xe xouveing ngandoung toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu, en eivek sakwaing ambei nyon eno xel wo nimaying wou xel poropet eti yeiw wei la tax en xam o.
MAT 5:13 “Xam on nambei mileeng wei tembuing o. Ekom wangwei nenyeing wei mileeng on na ma, on tyek xam ghe bong vati wou me mileeng enox bong nenyeing no? Inyon tyek se nox bo nimza no, om xam banex ena myayaing me xel xomaxoneing bakei lek.
MAT 5:14 “Xam on xeiyaing wei tembuing sapa yo. Beyeeng ngandoung wei toukale lek qetyei eno se teyei bei ghupek.
MAT 5:15 Xomaxoneing se mi byex eivek lam me toung ela xeinghembi eivek dipek. Qe xel mi lax lek vaxa wei mi nale lek o, me mi wong xeiyaing wou xel dalus wei mindei eivek xomek lalei yo.
MAT 5:16 Om nambei nyon eno xam ghe bong xam xe xeiyaing etel atax wou xomaxoneing mendghalus, en kandek xel gyei xam xe kwa nimza yon me sanghoxe xam Mamim lei eivek tyoung gheyapu.
MAT 5:17 “Xam seng bou kwamim bei a lam bei semaleeng qayeeng petieing veil o qayeeng poropet. A se lam bei semaleeng qe a lam bei bong embo neing lek.
MAT 5:18 A neil wou xam zonghek, ka tyoung gheyapu luw tembuing nati, tyek qayeeng nayaka ti tyek se nati, o dee nayak wei xel byex eno tyek se nati veil petieing qe ka lulul dalus na teyei lek bole.
MAT 5:19 Om wangwei xelti embei gyei qayeeng petieing ne nayak ti nambei lul bandaing me na teyoxe xel valu me xel bong ambei nyon, eno tyek e lei bo nayaka eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei, ekom eti yeiw wei mi betiwou me teyoxe xel moux alis vex en petieing o, eno tyek xel a neil e lei bo ngandoung eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 5:20 Om a neil wou xam bei wangwei xam se betiwou kwa bombek wei Anutu xe yo, me xam xe kwa bombek se ghanaw kwa bombek wei xel Parisi me xel putoung wei petieing, ond xam seng teyei being na eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu yo.
MAT 5:21 “Xam ghe ngo bei inyon qayeeng wei xel neil wou bumyeiw on takwei nei yo, ‘Xam seng nyeis xel amey, me e tiwei leis nge mey eno tyek bale lek qayeeng.’ Qou e loum 20:13
MAT 5:22 Ekom a neil wou xam eti yeiw wei laleind mi wo myavanei wou liyeiw ba eno tyek bale lek qayeeng. A neil no, eti yeiw wei neil qayeeng nol lek liyeiw ba eno tyek na gyei lei ngandoung wei kanzol o. Ekom wangwei tambiy ti e neil, ‘Wang on bandol!’ eno tyek na eivek nenyex wei beyeeng nilul o.
MAT 5:23 “Nambei nyon om wangwei wa being na toung xound lek qeind, ekom wang wou naleim bei lim neil qayeeng ti lek wang,
MAT 5:24 ond wa toung wa xe da e na mya wou qeind. De wang nox me na bole me menyex qayeeng is lim, woyom wang noum me ghe na toung wa xe da.
MAT 5:25 “Wa menyex wou qayeeng daing is tambiy wei embei qou wang me na bong qayeeng en wang o. Wang bong inye gyeik ingwei muw anghei di la wou sakwaing o, enok na qou wang me na wou tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng o, me tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng eno bong wang na wou beyeiv, me xel a toung wang na eivek xeitueing.
MAT 5:26 A neil wou wang zonghek, tyek wa seng teyei bei na myayaing, qe ka wa dexouv xomek xeitueing en wa xe malew kayo dalus bole.
MAT 5:27 “Xam ghe ngo qayeeng wei xel neil o, ‘Xam seng bo kwapesiv.’ Qou e Loum 20:14
MAT 5:28 Ekom a neil wou xam bei eti yeiw wei mi yei vex me lalei mi zeim e lek en vex eno inyon wong kwapesiv is e woy eivek lalei.
MAT 5:29 Wangwei wa mam payeiv bo wang bong sewokeing, ond wa qepei veil me banex ena. Inye nimza bei wa saing neing ti na veil de xel se banex wa neing dalus na eivek beyeeng wei nilul o.
MAT 5:30 Me wangwei wa memam payeiv e bo wang bong sewokeing, ond qateiv veil me nex ela. Inye nimza bei wa saing neing ti de xel se banex wa neing dalus na eivek beyeeng wei nilul o.
MAT 5:31 “E neil is ambei nye, ‘Xelti embei qateiv luw venei xe iingama ond e bong qapiya wei qateiveing iingama yo ti wou e.’
MAT 5:32 Ekom a neil wou xam, eti bei qateiv iingama wei luw venei, gyeik venei se wo kwa nol, ond wo venei wong ambei vex wei mi wo kwapesiv o, me eti bei dii vex wei qateiv iingama eno wo kwapesiv is e.”
MAT 5:33 Yesu neil no, “Xam ghe ngo bei inyon xel neil wou bumyeiw takwei nei, ‘Wa se pyalek qayeeng wei wang neil zonghek is inyapunei yo, qe xam ghe gweiteyei qayeeng zonghek is inyapunei wei xam ghe neil wou Tambiy Ngandoung o.’
MAT 5:34 Ekom a neil wou xam, xam se neil qayeeng zonghek is inyapunei. Xam se neil tyoung gheyapu nei bei byexaxoun qayeeng ti, en inye Anutu xe siaking,
MAT 5:35 o xam se neil lek tembuing, en inye e xe pom wei mi lax vaxa lek o, o xam se neil lek Yerusalem, en inyon beyeeng ngandoung wei King wei ghanaw veil o.
MAT 5:36 Me wa se neil qayeeng zonghek is inyapunei lek lumkanzek, en wa seng teyei bei bong lum velus ti bo teleing o bo ngak.
MAT 5:37 Qe wa mou neimbei ‘E’ o wa neimbei ‘Ma.’ Qayeeng wei xel mi tetulexe eno lam wou tambiy kawei nilul o.
MAT 5:38 “Xam ghe ngo qayeeng wei xel neil o woy, ‘Wangwei xelti embo nol wou wa mamghalus, ond wang bo nol wou e manghalus is ambei nyon, me wangwei xelti qatuw wa newoum apek ond wa qatuw e newou pek is ambei nyon.’
MAT 5:39 Ekom a neil wou xam bei xam seng bong myaveweeng nox wou xel wei nilul o. Wangwei xelti petapexe wa ling nge payeiv, ond wa pekwi ling valu nox wou e is.
MAT 5:40 Me wangwei xelti embei bo qayeeng en wang me na qou wa xe teimb, ond wang bong e qou wa xe teimb ding is.
MAT 5:41 Wangwei tambiy ti tendu wang bei wa qalei e xe qoupek me ghe na teyei lek kilomita ti, ond wang na is e teyei lek kilomita yuw.
MAT 5:42 Wangwei tambiy ti teling wang en lulti yon wang bong wou e, de tambiy ti embei qou lulti wou wang dekakom bong enoum on wa se pesek.
MAT 5:43 “Wang ngo ingwei xel neil o woy, ‘Wa laleim devind nimpapu de ghe gwei xel wei vevek amba bo nol.’
MAT 5:44 Ekom a neil wou wang, wa laleim devind xel wei vevek amba yo me na zeimemam en eti yeiw wei embei bo nol wou wang o,
MAT 5:45 om nambei nyon xam on tyek mendei nambei Mang wei toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu yo neuyeiw, eno moxo mi wong sayeiv mi siing lek xel nilul me nimza, me wong luing mi tei lek xel wei bombek o me xel wei se bombek o is.
MAT 5:46 Wangwei wa laleim devind eti yeiw wei laleind mi vind wang, on tyek wa qou xouveing vati? Beip xel wei mi qou takis eno se mi wong inyon?
MAT 5:47 Me wangwei wa neil bendiyeing wou limyeiw venaxow, on tyek wa qou lul vati ghanaw xel valu? Xel wei mendalus eno se mi wong inyon is?
MAT 5:48 Xam a mi mendei embo nimzayang, nambei xam Mamim wei tyoung gheyapu mindei nimzayang o.
MAT 6:1 “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow en xam seng bong xam xe kwa wei bombek o eivek xel xomaxoneing mend bei xel gyei. Wangwei xam ghe bong ambei nyon nei, ond tyek xam se qou xouveing ti wou xam Mamim eivek tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 6:2 “Om wa being bong lul wou xel wei kanyo yo, ond wa se neil me xel davei vuk me natax en wang nambei xel wei myend yuw mi wong eivek xomek qekueing ama me sakwaing mema nayak, bei xel xomaxoneing bo lei ngandoung wou xel o. A neil wou xam zonghek bei, xel qou nind xouveing dalus woy.
MAT 6:3 Ekom gyeik wa being bong wou xel wei kanyo yo, wa seng bong wa memam qeinz boulek vati wei wa memam payeiv embei bong o,
MAT 6:4 en kandek wa xe wongeing e mi mendei xupekeing. Woyom Mam yei vati wei wang wong xupekeing o, eno tyek bong xouveing wou wang.
MAT 6:5 “Me gyeik wa bei zeimemam, wa seng bong ambei xel wei myend yuw o, en xel laleind mi vind bei na mi bale me na zeim memend eivek xomek qekueing ama me na mi bale wou sakwaing nayak en kandek moux alis vex a mi gyei xel. A neil wou xam zonghek bei, xel qou nind xouveing dalus woy.
MAT 6:6 Ekom gyeik wa bei zeimemam, ond wang na eivek bam lalei me na toung qapomb zeyi dom na zeimemam wou Mam, wei mi dei xupekeing o. Woyom Mam wei mi yei vati wei mindei xupekeing, eno tyek bong xouveing wou wang.
MAT 6:7 Me gyeik xam a bei zeimemamim, xam se zeimemamim ding nambei xel wei mandalus mi wong o, en xel wou naleind bei tyek Anutu na ngo xel xe qayeeng ngenongakes on.
MAT 6:8 Xam seng ghok xel, gyeik ingwei wa seng ghei teling wou e yo, eno xam Mamim woulek woy en vati wei wambei teling wou e yo.
MAT 6:9 “Woyom tine inye xam a bei zeimemamim eno nambei nye: “ ‘Xa Mami eivek tyoung gheyapu, wa leim e mi mendei vambuing.
MAT 6:10 Wa xe tete lalei e nam. Xa teyei bei betiwou wa laleim lek tembuing, nambei xel mi betiwou nanghei tyoung gheyapu yon.
MAT 6:11 Gweimbeeng wang bong xami yaeing wei bouk titi eno wou xa.
MAT 6:12 Wa semaleeng sewokeing wei xa yo, xa is ambei nyon xa semaleeng sewokeing wei xel ba mi wong wou xa yo.
MAT 6:13 Me wa se qou xa na eivek axeing, qe wa qou xa veil tambiy nilul on.’
MAT 6:14 En wangwei wa semaleeng sewokeing wei xomaxoneing wong wou wang o, on tyek Mam wei toundei tyoung gheyapu nei tyek semaleeng wa xe sewokeing is.
MAT 6:15 Ekom wangwei wa se semaleeng xomaxoneing nge xe sewokeing veil, ond tyek Mam se semaleeng wa xe sewokeing is.
MAT 6:16 “Gyeik wambei vambu yaeing, ond wa seng gweimam nol nambei xel wei myend yuw mi wong o, en xel mi wo mend nol me talex wou xel moux alis vex bei xel vambu yaeing. A neil wou xam zonghek, xel qou nind xouveing dalus woy.
MAT 6:17 Ekom gyeik wambei vambu yaeing, on wa pelei wel lek lum me davu mam,
MAT 6:18 om wa seng bong kwa wei vambuing yaing gyeip yaeing wou xomaxoneing mendghalus. Ma, wang bong wou Mam manghalus wei mindei xupekeing o. Mam wei toundei xupekeing eno venaxow mi woulek, vati wei xel mi wong xupekeing o, eno tyek bong xouveing wou wang.
MAT 6:19 “Xam se qekuwou xam xe lulul nimzamza lek tembuing ne, wei xevek me niyeis mi wo nol wou yo, me xel wei panaxeing o mi dembu xomek me panax.
MAT 6:20 Ekom xam a mi qekuwou xam xe lulul nimzamza e na eivek tyoung gheyapu nei, wei xevek me niyeis se teyei bei bo nol wou, me panaxana se teyei bei dembu me na lalei me panax.
MAT 6:21 En nanghei ingwei wa xe lul nimza toundei ghei yo, eno wa laleim tyek na mendei is ambei nyon.
MAT 6:22 “Xe mendghalus ne lam wei xe neing o. Wangwei wa mam on nimza, on wa neing dalus on tyek na pup en xeiyaing.
MAT 6:23 Ekom wangwei wa mam aluw on nilul, yon wa neing dalus on tyek bo mapetok. Om wangwei xeiyaing wei toundei eivek wang on bo mapetok, yon mapetok on tyek bong ngandoung eivek wang mouyo!
MAT 6:24 “Tambiy ti se teyei bei bo xuk wou teiv yayuw. Moxo tyek lalei bo nol wou nge, de lalei devind nge, me tyek na mi ngo e xe qayeeng, de na toung demi wou nge. Wa seng teyeimbei bong xuk wou Anutu me malew is.
MAT 6:25 “Nambei nyon a neil wou xam bei, xam seng bounaleim ngenong en mapieing wei xam o me na neimbei, ‘Tyek xey a gha vati? O na num va? De xe neing eno tyek xey a byex vati?’ Mapieing ne ngandoung ghanaw yaeing, me neing ne ngandoung ghanaw teimb.
MAT 6:26 Xam ghe gwei menek menek wei senghoing bandaing nei, xel se mi xen o se mi qekuwou o toung lulul eivek xomek yaeing. Ekom xam Mamim wei toundei tyoung gheyapu nei eno mi vet xel. Beip xam seng ghanaw menek menek on veil, ei?
MAT 6:27 Eti yeiw wei mi wou naleind ngenong eno teyei bei tetulexe seivma nayaka lek e xe mapieing?
MAT 6:28 “Me xam ghe di wou naleimim ngenong en teimb en va? Xam ghe gwei qapaing mavya wei toungale yon. Xel se mi wong pok o duw teimb.
MAT 6:29 Ekom a neil wou xam bei Salomo mi vunek en lul nimzamza, ekom e xe vunekeing nimza yon se nambei qapaing mavya ti beimambei ne.
MAT 6:30 Wangwei inye Anutu mi vunekwou qeis qeis wei xuk o nambei nyon, ond inyon gweimbeeng me yanyeing eno xel mi nex ela eivek nenyex. Beip moxo se mi vunekwou xam? Xam on xe wongeingis on nayaka.
MAT 6:31 Om xam seng bounaleim ngenong, me na neimbei, ‘Tyek xey a gha vati?’ o ‘Tyek xey a num vati?’ o ‘Tyek xey a bunek en vati?’
MAT 6:32 En xel wei mendalus eno mi yimexe lul dalus ti beimambei ne, de xam Mamim wei tyoung gheyapu eno woulek woy en vati wei xam a bei qou yo.
MAT 6:33 Ekom xam ghe gwimexe e xe tete lalei me e xe sakwaing bombek bole, de lulul dalus ti beimambei ne eno tyek bong wou xam is ambei nyon.
MAT 6:34 Nambei nyon xam seng bou naleimim en yanyeing, en yanyeing tyek bounalei en venaxow. Nimaying wei bouk titi eno teyei lek bouk tiyon venaxow.
MAT 7:1 “Xam seng gwei xel nge xe kwa me baluk en, enok Anutu bong kwa nambei nyon wou xam is.
MAT 7:2 En eivek sakwaing kawei xam ghe wei xel nge me ghe luk en e, eno tyek Anutu bong kwa nambei nyon wou xam, me vati wei xam ghe mi wong wou xel nge yo, tyek Anutu bong ambei nyon wou xam is.
MAT 7:3 “Wang wei myasa wei dei eivek lim nge ma yon en va, de wa seng wei pelang wei di yeip eivek wamaxow mam on?
MAT 7:4 Inye nambei nya wang neil wou lim, ‘Wong a laluwexe myasa yon lam myayaing veil wa mamghalus,’ de pelang wei toundei eivek wamaxow mamghalus on?
MAT 7:5 Wa tambiy wei wa myam yuw o, myaxeeng eno wa laluwexe pelang veil venaxow mamghalus bole, woyom tyek wang gwei embo nimza me laluwexe myasa veil lim manghalus.
MAT 7:6 “Xam se qou lul wei vambuing wei xel wong wou Anutu yo me ghe bong wou xel naw on, me wa se banex wa xe viyaviy na wou xel bok on. Wangwei wang bong nei, tyek xel bakei lek angya vaxend, de woyom tyek xel pekwi me noum wou xam me zanga xam ghe bo tiptip.
MAT 7:7 “Xam teling on tyek bong wou xam. Xam ghe gwimexe on tyek xam ghe gweiwou. Xam ghe nyeis memamim lek qapomb on tyek natax veil xam.
MAT 7:8 En xel dalus wei mi teling eno mi qou, me eti mi yimexe eno mi yeiwou, me eti yeiw wei mi leis memend lek qapomb eno tyek natax.
MAT 7:9 “Xam eti yeiw, wangwei e neu moux teling wou en belet, tyek wang bong qakous ti wou e?
MAT 7:10 O wangwei e teling wou wang en woing, tyek wang bong myeiy ti wou e?
MAT 7:11 Xam mayeiw on nilul, ekom xam ghe mi wong lul nimza wou neumyeiw, om xam Mamim wei toundei tyoung gheyapu nei tyek bong lul nimza wou eti yeiw wei mi teling wou e yo!
MAT 7:12 Om kwa tambak wei wambei xel bamba bong wou wang eno wang bong ambei nyon wou xel, eno tine inye qayeeng qes wei petieing o me qayeeng qes wei xel poropet o.
MAT 7:13 “Xam a mi na nox tete mya nayak. En tete mya wei ngandoung me sakwaing ngandoung eno inyon la wou beyeeng wei qoueing nilul o, me xel ngenong eno mi la lox.
MAT 7:14 Ekom tete mya nayak me sakwaing nayak on la wou beyeeng wei mapieing o, me moux alis vex nuyuw ka mi yei me betiwou.
MAT 7:15 “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow en poropet wei tyonyeing. Xel mi lam wou xam eivek teimb wei sipsip nivlus o, ekom xel laleind ond xok ambei naw bemeeng.
MAT 7:16 Nangya xel xe kwa yon tyek xam ghe boulek e neing. Beip xel xomaxoneing mi qou xax wain neing lek qeis wei niying o, o xel mi qou xax basunghek lek qeis wei nileli yo?
MAT 7:17 Nambei nyon xax sapa wei nimza eno mi vuk neing nimza, dom xax nilul mi vuk neing nilul.
MAT 7:18 Xax nimza ti se teyei bei buk neing nilul, o xax nilul ti se teyei bei buk neing nimza.
MAT 7:19 Xax sapa wei se mi vuk neing nimza eno xel mi vuv veil me nex ela eivek nenyex.
MAT 7:20 Om tyek xam ghe gwei lek xel xe neing me ghe boulek xel.
MAT 7:21 “Se xel dalus wei mi taxe a bei, ‘Tambiy Ngandoung, Tambiy Ngandoung,’ eno tyek na eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu yo, qe eti yeiw wei mi wong e betiwou Mang wei tyoung gheyapu yo lalei.
MAT 7:22 Xel ngenong tyek na neil wou ay lek bouk kayon, ‘Tambiy Ngandoung, Tambiy Ngandoung, beip xa se mi neil qayeeng poropet eivek wa leim, me eivek wa leim eno xa mi tiy memo la myayaing me na wong lulvako ngenong?’
MAT 7:23 Woyom tyek a neil wou xel bombek, ‘A se woulek xam nayaka. Xam wei ghe mi wo kwa nilul, xam la veil ay!’
MAT 7:24 “Nambei nyon xel sapa wei mi ngo a xe qayeeng tine me mi betiwou eno inye nambei tambiy lupeyei wei ev beeng lek qakous o.
MAT 7:25 Luing tei, me memiing butek, me laweeng vei xomek wo pimapi, ekom xomek se qepei me teila, en nambei mundeeng on nale nikanzek eivek qakous.
MAT 7:26 Ekom eti yeiw wei se mi ngo a xe qayeeng ti beimambei ne me betiwou, eno nambei tambiy wei ev xomek lek luzeeng bandaing o.
MAT 7:27 Luing tei, me memiing butek, me laweeng vei xomek wo pimapi, om xomek qepei me teila niseikeing.”
MAT 7:28 Yesu neil qayeeng ti beimambei ne ma woy, xel qendu ngandoung on etek en e xe qayeeng wei di teyoxe yo,
MAT 7:29 en moxo teyoxe xel teyei lek tambiy wei lei ngandoung o, de se nambei xel xe putoung wei petieing o.
MAT 8:1 Moxo di loum axone veil lukendu, eno xel qendu ngandoung ti betiwou e.
MAT 8:2 De tambiy ti is vanei lepa eno lam ev vaxakatu eivek wou e me neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wangwei wa laleim devind nei, yon wang bong am bo nimzalek.”
MAT 8:3 Yesu tatei mema la me axlek e, de neil, “A laleing vind! Wang bo vako.” Lutika eno moxo xe vanei lepa yon ma veil e.
MAT 8:4 Woyom Yesu neil wou e, “Wang wei inyon dom wa se neil wou xelti. Qe la, me talex xow wou lumuki me toung xound teyei lek Mose neil o, en xel boulek pavulek ne bei wa xe myavanei yon ma.”
MAT 8:5 Ka Yesu la eivek beyeeng Kapenaom, beyeiv wei mi yeiteyei 100 vevekyeiw eno ti lam wou e me teling wou en vineing.
MAT 8:6 Moxo neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, a xe xukxe eno vanei wong om di yeip lek zek eivek xomek lalei. Moxo kanzek mey me di axe vanei ngandoung.”
MAT 8:7 Yesu neil wou e, “Tyek a nak me na bong embo nimzalek.”
MAT 8:8 Ekom beyeiv neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, a se nimza bei wang nam eivek a bang lalei. Qe wa mou neil qayeeng dom a xe xukxe e bo nimzalek.
MAT 8:9 En a maxow ne a mindei kwanghembi eivek xel wei wo leind ngandoung o, me xel vevek mindei kwanghembi eivek ay. Wangwei a neil wou tine, ‘La,’ ond moxo la. De na neil wou nge yon, ‘Lam,’ ond moxo lam. Me a neil wou a xe xukxe, ‘Wong tine,’ ond moxo mi wong.”
MAT 8:10 Yesu ngo qayeeng tine, moxo etek mouyo me neil wou eti yeiw wei di betiwou e yon, “A neil wou xam zonghek, a se mi xei tambiy ti eivek Israel eno xe wongeingis ambei nye.
MAT 8:11 A neil wou xam bei inyon xel ngenong tyek nam anghei ninei me xeinei, me nam mendei me gya mata ngandoung on is Apraham aluw Isaka lal Yakop eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 8:12 Ekom xomaxoneing wei Israel wei tete lalei eno tyek Anutu banex xel na myayaing eivek mapetok ngandoung, nanghei inyon eno tyek xel bong talot ngandoung me dexound newound bo nyiknyik.”
MAT 8:13 Woyom Yesu neil wou beyeiv, “La! En tyek na tyip ambei ingwei wang wongis bei etyip o.” De e xe xukxe wo nimzalek seivma kayon.
MAT 8:14 Woyom Yesu lam eivek Petele xe xomek, moxo yei Petele yeing avexta gying wong me e di yeip lek zek.
MAT 8:15 Moxo axlek e mema de gying on ma veil e, me vexo qandi lek me di menyex lulul wou e.
MAT 8:16 Soukeing tiyon, eno xel ngenong wei memo dei eivek xel eno liyeiw qou xel me lam wou Yesu. Me e neil de xel laweeng nilul on la myayaing me wong xel ngenong wei vanei eno wo nimzalek.
MAT 8:17 De kwa tine la teyei lek vati wei Anutu neil eivek poropet Yesaya mya yo: “E maxow qou xe xe myavanei leimalei me semaleeng xe xe vanei leimalei veil.”
MAT 8:18 Gyeik Yesu yei xel qendu ngandoung wei nale vivekwou e yon, moxo neil nikanzek wou xel betiyeing bei, “Xey a na nge loxalu wei lounyeing nei.”
MAT 8:19 Woyom putoung wei petieing o ti eno lam wou e me neil, “Putoung, wambei mi na inya yo eno tyek a betiwou wang.”
MAT 8:20 Yesu neil elox bei, “Xel naw bemeeng xe eeng me menek menek xe lewis, ekom Xomaxoneing Neu Moux xe beyeeng wei embei ni lu lek eno ma.”
MAT 8:21 Betiyeing nge neil wou e, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wong a la ev mang wole.”
MAT 8:22 Ekom Yesu neil wou e, “Wa betiwou ay, dom wong xel meyeing di ev xel venaxow xe meyeing.”
MAT 8:23 Woyom moxo la eivek bot de e xe xel betiyeing betiwou e.
MAT 8:24 Se wo lululek, qe laweeng ngandoung ti tyip wou xel lek lounyeing masenghoing, omek laweeng vei lounyeing lam embei sevunexe bot is xel. Ekom Yesu vena di yeip.
MAT 8:25 Xel betiyeing la me piyexe e, me neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, vind xa! Xey am bim a qou nilul ne!”
MAT 8:26 Moxo neil elox, “Xam xe wongeingis on nayaka, nambei nya xam ghe waleeng?” Woyom moxo qandi lek me luk nikanzek wou laweeng me mamileeng wei di vuk me lam on yeip kanzek, me wo nimza no.
MAT 8:27 Xel moux on etek me teling, “Tambiy tine e vati? Om memiing aluw laweeng ngo e vya!”
MAT 8:28 Ka Yesu la tei lounyeing nge loxalu wei Gadarayeiw xe tembuing nei, eno moux yayuw wei memo dei eivek luw eno lam myayaing veil eeng wei xel qateiv eivek qakous o me lam wou e. Tambiy yuw on bemeeng om xelti se teyei bei na nox sakwaing tiyon.
MAT 8:29 Woyom luw ghak, “Anutu Neu Moux, wa being bo vati wou uw? Beip wang lam inye bei bo nol wou uw de bouk anghei?”
MAT 8:30 Bok qendu ngandoung ti di ya ghei dingta ka nanghei inyon en xel.
MAT 8:31 Laweeng nol yon tay wou Yesu, “Wangwei wa tiy xa na myayaing nei, on wong xa la eivek bok qendu ngandoung nei.”
MAT 8:32 Moxo neil wou xel, “Xam la!” Om xel lam myayaing me la eivek xel bok on, me bok qendu tiyon dalus veimyend me la oing mazanghei me heivek lounyeing de mey eivek memiing.
MAT 8:33 Xel wei mi yeiteyei bok on yei tine, om xel veimyend me la eivek beyeeng on me neil qayeeng dalus en tine, me vati wei belup wou moux yuw wei memo mindei eivek luw o.
MAT 8:34 Woyom xel tambak wei beyeeng on la wou Yesu. Me gyeik xel yei e, xel luk nikanzek wou e bei ena veil xel xe tembuing.
MAT 9:1 Yesu lek la eivek bot ti, me la nge loxalu nei me la tyip emaxow beeng qes.
MAT 9:2 Xel valu qou tambiy bezombeing ti wei xel liw lek lelek o me lam. Yesu yei xel xe wongeingis, om neil wou tambiy wei bezomb on, “A neung, wa qou laleim vevopeing. A semaleeng wa xe sewokeing veil.”
MAT 9:3 Xel putoung valu wei petieing eno xel neil wou ma en tine bei, “Tambiy tine embei qou Anutu nimbeeng!”
MAT 9:4 Yesu woulek xel xe woueing nalei me neil, “Xam ghe di wou naleimim nilul eivek laleimim enva?
MAT 9:5 Qayeeng tina inye xeiles bei a neil: ‘A semaleeng wa xe nilul,’ o a neimbei, ‘Qandi lek me la’?
MAT 9:6 Ekom inyon xam ghe boulek bei, Xomaxoneing Neu Moux wo lei ngandoung lek tembuing en semalenyeing sewokeing.” Woyom moxo neil wou tambiy wei bezomb on bei, “Qandi lek, de qou wa xe lelek me la bam.”
MAT 9:7 De moux moxo qandi lek me la beeng.
MAT 9:8 Xel qendu ngandoung on yei tine, xel etek en ingwei xel yei Anutu xe nikanzek me sanghoxe Anutu, e tiwei wong nikanzek wou xomaxoneing ti yo.
MAT 9:9 Ka Yesu la nanghei inyon, moxo yei tambiy ti lei Matai toundei eivek xomek takis. Moxo neil wou e, “Betiwou ay,” om Matai qandi lek me betiwou e me la.
MAT 9:10 Kale Yesu di ya eivek Matai xe xomek, xel ngenong wei mi qou takis me xel sewokeing eno lam me di ya is e me e xe xel betiyeing.
MAT 9:11 Xel Parisi yei tine, om xel teling wou xel betiyeing, “Nambei nya xam xe putoung di ya is xel wei mi qou takis me xel wei mi wo sewokeing o?”
MAT 9:12 Yesu ngo tine me neil, “Xel wei vanei ma eno se mi la wou dokta, qe xel wei vanei yo.
MAT 9:13 Ekom xam ghe na me na qou kwa wou qayeeng tine qes: ‘A laleing vind lalei pyaweing de a laleing se vind seing xound.’ En a se lam bei taxe xel wei bombek o, qe xel wei sewokeing o.”
MAT 9:14 Woyom Yoan xe xel betiyeing lam me teling wou Yesu, “Nambei nya ekom xa is xel Parisi mi vambu yaeing, de wa xe xel betiyeing se mi vambu yaeing?”
MAT 9:15 Yesu neil elox bei, “Nambei nya xel wei lam en iingama eno na qou laleind maying gyeik tambiy wei embei dii vex eno nanghei toundei is xel? Ka bouk wei xel embei qou tambiy wei iingama yo me na veil xel, woyom tyek xel vambu yaeing.
MAT 9:16 “Tambiy ti se mi qou qaeing vako myasepu me duw eivek teimb takwei, en qaeing vako wei xel duw on tyek tetei me zex teimb on bo nilul.
MAT 9:17 Xel ti se mi taw wain vako eivek wain takwei ninavi. Wangwei xel bong ambei nyon nei, wain ninavi yon tyek na tip, de wain on tyek na taw veil de ninavi yon tyek bo nol. Qe xel mi taw wain vako yon eivek ninavi vako, me luw xouing tyek mendei nimza.”
MAT 9:18 Ka moxo neil qayeeng tine, gyovaxa ti lam me ev vaxakatu eivek wou e tax me neil, “A neung vex mouk mey. Ekom wang nam a ni memam lek e, en vexo e mendei mapieing no.”
MAT 9:19 Yesu qandi lek me la is e, me e xe betiyeing is ambei nyon.
MAT 9:20 De woyom vex tiwei mi qou gyand teyei lek vakovek qes xoumeeng yuw eno lam me di la yus en e me axlek e xe teimb ding on myasepu.
MAT 9:21 Vexo neil wou xow, “Wangwei a mou daxlek e xe teimb, on tyek a bo nimzalek.”
MAT 9:22 Yesu pekwi me yei vex on me neil, “A neung vex, wa laleim embo nimza, wa xe wongeingis wong wang wo nimzalek.” Om vexo wo nimzalek gyeik kayon.
MAT 9:23 Yesu la eivek gyovaxa xe xomek me yei xel wei di vei sakwep me wo talot me yei xel qendu yon di wo nindenduing,
MAT 9:24 moxo neil, “Xam la veil. Vexawo ne se mey qe di yeip.” Ekom xel napexe e.
MAT 9:25 Ka Yesu tiy xel qendu ngandoung on la myayaing, moxo la lalei me zeim vex on mema, de vexo qandi lek.
MAT 9:26 Qayeeng la wo ngandoung en tine eivek tembuing danghei danghei nei dalus.
MAT 9:27 Ka Yesu la nanghei inyon me la, tambiy matekeing yayuw betiwou e, me di taxe la wou e, “Dawit Neu Moux, pyanaleim en uw!”
MAT 9:28 Moxo la eivek xomek, eno tambiy yuw wei mend tekeing o lam wou e, me moxo teling luw, “Muw ghe wongis bei a teyei bei bong tine?” Luw lewexe, “Ee, Tambiy Ngandoung.”
MAT 9:29 Woyom moxo toung mema lek luw mendghalus me neil, “Muw ghe wongis om lul tine e na teyei lek wou muw.”
MAT 9:30 De luw mendghalus yeila. Yesu peti luw, “Kandek muw seng bong xelti boulek lul tine.”
MAT 9:31 Ekom luw la myayaing nei me teyoxe qayeeng on lala en Yesu eivek tembuing danghei danghei dalus tiyon.
MAT 9:32 Ka luw la veil, xomaxoneing qou tambiy ti myatueing wei memo dei eivek me se teyei bei baluk o me lam wou Yesu.
MAT 9:33 Me gyeik Yesu tiy memo yon la myayaing, tambiy wei myatu yon luk. Xel qendu ngandoung on etek me neil, “Lulti nambei tine eno xelti se mi yei eivek Israel ti.”
MAT 9:34 Ekom xel Parisi neil, “Moxo mi tiy xel angya nikanzek wei gyovaxa lukanzek wei xel memo yo.”
MAT 9:35 Yesu mi la eivek beyeeng nayak dalus me beyeeng me teyoxe xel eivek xomek qekueing ama wei xel Yuda yo me neil Xoulek Nimza wei tete lalei yo me wong xel wei vanei leimalei eno mi wo nimzalek.
MAT 9:36 Gyeik ingwei yei xel qendu ngandoung on, moxo pyanalei en xel, en nambei xel lundpeyei yon la bandabanda, me xel mindei e wo nol nambei sipsip wei gyovaxa ma veil o.
MAT 9:37 Woyom moxo neil wou e xe xel betiyeing, “Neing zuw ngenong ekom xel xukxe yon nuyuw ka.
MAT 9:38 Om xam teling wou xuk ma bei e bong xel xukxe na eivek e xe xuk me na qou neing eivek xuk.”
MAT 10:1 Yesu taxe e xe xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw on lam wou e me wong nikanzek wou xel bei xel a mi tiy laweeng nilaxes me bong xel wei vanei leimalei eno bo nimzalek.
MAT 10:2 Xel sinale xoumeeng yuw ne leind ambei nye. Tiwei tax eno Simon e lei nge xel mi taxe bei Petele me li Andrias, Jems wei Sebedi neu moux o me li Yoan,
MAT 10:3 Pilip me Batolomiu, Tomas me Matai tambiy wei mi qou takis o, Jems Alpias neu moux, me Tadius,
MAT 10:4 Simon wei Selot me Yudas Iskariot, tiwei tyek na neil Yesu teyei me na toung e na eivek xel ba memend o.
MAT 10:5 Yesu wong xel xoumeeng yuw ne eno la de peti xel bei, “Xam seng na eivek xel amba senghoing o ghe na eivek Samaria xe beyeeng on ti,
MAT 10:6 qe xam ghe na wou xel sipsip wei Israel wei lati yo.
MAT 10:7 Ka xam a being na eno xam ghe na neil qayeeng tine, ‘Tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno lam paviy.’
MAT 10:8 Xam ghe bong vanei e ma, me xam a piyexe xel meyeing, de ghe bong xel wei lepa yo bo nimzalek me xam a tiy memoyeiw na veil. Lul wei xam ghe qou bandaing, eno xam ghe bong wou xel bandaing.
MAT 10:9 Xam se qou lulti nambei ghol o silva malew o kopa malew gyand eivek xam xe let.
MAT 10:10 Gyeik xam ghe na wou sakwaing eno xam se qou vaxak ti, o teimb yuw, o vaxalambes o patongeeng is. En xel wei mi wo xuk eno tyek xel bong yaeing wou xel.
MAT 10:11 “Wangwei xam a being na eivek beyeeng nayak o beyeeng, ond xam ghe gwimexe tambiy wei nimza yo ti me ghe na mendei is e eivek e xe xomek deka xam ghe na veil le.
MAT 10:12 Ka xam a being na eivek xomek ti, eno xam a neil bendiyeing wou xel.
MAT 10:13 Wangwei xel wei xomek on na qou xam is xeindlala, xam ghe bong xam xe lalei vevopeing wou xel, ek wangwei na ma, ond xam a qou xam xe lalei vevopeing noum wou xow.
MAT 10:14 Wangwei xelti se qou xam o na ngo qayeeng wei xam o, ond xam pepa vegyuveeng veil vaxamim gyeik xam a being na veil xomek o beyeeng nayak o.
MAT 10:15 A neil wou xam zonghek bei, gyeik bouk wei Anutu embei bo qayeeng en xomaxoneing eno nimaying ngandoung tyek qandi wou beyeeng nayak tiyon ghanaw Sodom aluw Gomora.
MAT 10:16 Wei, ambei bong xam ghe na nambei sipsip eivek xel naw bemeeng senghoing. Nambei nyon xam a qou lupeyei nambei myeiy me mendei males nambei beliy.
MAT 10:17 “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow en xel xomaxoneing, tyek xel a qou xam me na wou xel kanzol me tyek xel bo nol wou xam me sesa xam eivek xomek qekueing ama.
MAT 10:18 Tyek xel a qou xam me na bale wou xel lei ngandoung wei seyap o me xel king mend en ay, en nambei xam ghe mi betiwou ay me ghe neil xoulek teyei wou xel me xel amba.
MAT 10:19 Ekom gyeik xel a zeimaxoun xam, xam seng bou kwamim ngenong en vati wei xam ambei neil o, bei tyek xam a neil ambei nya. Lek seivma kayon eno Anutu tyek bong vati wei xam ambei neil o,
MAT 10:20 en inye tyek xam venaxow se neil, qe inye xam Mamim xe Laweeng eno tyek baluk eivek xam myamim.
MAT 10:21 “Li venaxow tyek na neil li teyei me xel nyeis e mey, me ma ti tyek bong ambei nyon wou neu, de neuyeiw tyek bo vevek is mamata me xel ba nyeis xel amey.
MAT 10:22 Xomaxoneing dalus tyek laleind bo nol wou xam en ay, ekom eti yeiw wei nale nikanzek me ena bouk loxyus eno tyek Anutu devind xel veil meyeing.
MAT 10:23 Wangwei xel bo nilul wou xam eivek beyeeng ti, ond xam a pek me ghe na beyeeng nge. A neil wou xam zonghek bei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux noum eno tyek xam seng na eivek beyeeng tambak wei Israel o buplek.
MAT 10:24 “Yak wei wevek xomek o se ghanaw e xe putoung, o xukxe ti se ghanaw e xe teiv.
MAT 10:25 Ekom wangwei yakyak wei wevek xomek o teyei lek e xe putoung, ond inyon woy. Me wangwei xukxe teyei lek e xe teiv, ond inyon woy is ambei nyon. Wangwei xomek ma eno xel taxe bei e Belsebul, ond tyek xel bo lei wei nilul o wou e xe xel wei xomek on!
MAT 10:26 “Om xam seng gwaleeng en xel. Lul dalus wei xel vun eno tyek nam yanyateiv. Me qayeeng tambak wei yeip xupekeing eno tyek xomaxoneing boulek.
MAT 10:27 Vati wei a neil wou xam eivek boukeing, eno xam a neil eivek bendiyeing. Me qayeeng wei xam ghe di ngoung wouma eivek nenyamim, eno tyek xam bale lek xomek demi qetyei me na neilteyei.
MAT 10:28 Xam seng gwaleeng en xel wei embei nyeis xam neing a mey yo, dom xel se teyei bei nyeis xam numim pieing. Qe xam ghe gwaleeng en Anutu wei teyei bei bo nol wou xam numim pieing me xam neing eivek nenyex wei luta yo.
MAT 10:29 Beip xel se mi xouv menek nayak yuw en selewa gyand nayak ti? Ek wangwei xam Mamim lalei se devind nei on tyek menek menek nayak on ti se teyei bei deteina lek tembuing.
MAT 10:30 De nge is xam lumim velus dalus on eno Anutu pyaw memawou woy.
MAT 10:31 Om xam seng gwaleeng. Xam ghe ghanaw menek nayak ngenong on.
MAT 10:32 “Eti yeiw wei mi neil a teyei natax wou xomaxoneing eno tyek a neil e teyei natax wou Mang anghei tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 10:33 Ekom eti bei dax a vun atax wou xomaxoneing, eno tyek a dax e vun is ambei nyon atax wou Mang nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 10:34 “Xam seng bou kwamim bei a qou lalei vevopeing me na lam tembuing. A se qou lalei vevopeing me na lam qe ngeyeing vevek.
MAT 10:35 En a lam bei pekwi ‘moux ti lalei bo nol wou ma, de neu vex ti lalei bo nol wou ta, me neu vex lalei bo nol wou yeing avexta.
MAT 10:36 Moux ti eivek xel venaxow eno tyek bo nol wou emaxow xe xel wei xomek o.’
MAT 10:37 “Xelti embei lalei devind ma luw ta ghanaw ay, eno tyek se bong ambei a xe. Xelti embei lalei devind neu moux aluw neu vex ghanaw ay, ond tyek se bong ambei a xe.
MAT 10:38 Me xelti embei se qalei e xe xax pepeeng me betiwou ay, ond se teyei bei bong ambei a xe.
MAT 10:39 Tambiy ti embei bong e xe mapieing embo nimza, on tyek na saing e xe mapieing. Dom xelti embei saing e xe mapieing en ay, ond tyek gyeiwou mapieing zonghek.
MAT 10:40 “Tambiy ti embei qou xam eno qou ay, me eti qou ay eno qou tiwei wong a lam o.
MAT 10:41 Tambiy ti embei qou poropet ti me gyeiteyei en nambei e mi neil qayeeng poropet ond tyek na qou xouveing wei poropet o. Me tambiy ti embei qou xel wei bombek o ti me gyeiteyei en nambei e yon tambiy wei bombek o yon tyek na qou xouveing wei tambiy wei bombek o.
MAT 10:42 Me wangwei xelti bong mayamya memiing tyuweing ti wou xel beimambei wei leind maeing on ti en nambei inyon e a xe betiyeing, ond a neil zonghek wou xam bei, moxo tyek se saing e xe xouveing.”
MAT 11:1 Ka Yesu neil qayeeng wei embei teyoxe e xe xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw eno ma, moxo la nanghei inyon me la en embei na teyoxe me na neil qayeeng eivek beyeeng wei Galili nei.
MAT 11:2 Gyeik Yoan ngo eivek xeitueing en vati wei Kilisi di wong o, moxo wong e xe xel betiyeing la,
MAT 11:3 bei teling e, “Beip inye wang on tiwei tyek nam o, o xa mendi daxe tambiy bange?”
MAT 11:4 Yesu neil elox, “Xam lox neil wou Yoan en vati wei xam ghe ngo me ghe wei yo:
MAT 11:5 Xel matekeing eno mend yeila, me xel wei vaxend nol eno di la, me xel wei wo vanei lepa eno wo nimzalek, me xel wei nenyend wo qatu eno ngo wou, me xel meyeing eno qandi lek, de Xoulek Nimza eno xel neil wou xel kanyoyeiw.
MAT 11:6 Mata e na wou xel wei xel xe wongeingis se tei en qayeeng wei ay yo.”
MAT 11:7 Ka Yoan xe xel betiyeing la veil, Yesu luk wou xel qendu yon en Yoan: “Xam ghe la tembuing bandaing nei bei na gwei vati? Ghet wei laweeng di vei elox me loum o?
MAT 11:8 Wangwei na ma nei, yon xam ghe la being na gwei vati? Moux ti wei vunek en teimb nimza yo? Ma, xel eti yeiw wei mi vunek en teimb nimza eno mindei eivek king beeng.
MAT 11:9 Woyom xam ghe la being na gwei vati? Poropet ti? Ee, a neil wou xam bei, Poropet tiyon ghanaw xel poropet ba veil.
MAT 11:10 Tambiy tine tiwei xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, “ ‘Wei, tyek a bong a xe nenyalesana ti na mamunghexeing en wang, tiwei tyek menyex wou sakwaing atax en wang o.’
MAT 11:11 A neil wou xam zonghek: Yoan Lipekeing ghanaw xel wei tayeiw wou xel lek tembuing ne yo leind, ekom e tiwei lei maeing eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno ghanaw e.
MAT 11:12 Eivek bouk wei Yoan Lipekeing neil xoulek me elam tyip gweimbeeng ne, eno xel wo vevek nikanzek en na qou tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu yo, de xel wo vevek nikanzek om inyon wo nimaying ngenong wou e.
MAT 11:13 En xel poropet dalus me petieing neil qayeeng poropet me e lam tyip wou bouk wei Yoan o.
MAT 11:14 Me wangwei wa laleim devind bei na qou vati wei a neil ne, ond e yon Eliya wei embei nam o.
MAT 11:15 Tambiy wei nenya nale lek e yo, ond e ngo qayeeng tine.
MAT 11:16 “Tyek a neil qayeeng lek vati bei talex moux alis vex wei gweimbeeng ne? Xel on ambei yakyak wei mindei eivek beyeeng vateivek me mi taxe la wou xel bamba:
MAT 11:17 “‘Xa vei sakwep en xam, ekom xam seng aw, me xa wong lalo wei lalei pyaweing o, ekom xam seng wong talot.’
MAT 11:18 En Yoan lam eno se mi ya yaeing me num numeing, me xel neil, ‘Moxo memo ti toundei eivek e.’
MAT 11:19 Xomaxoneing Neu Moux lam ya yaeing me num numeing, me xel neil, ‘Wei, inye e wei mi zongaxei me num ngenong o. E yon gweleeng wei xel wei mi qou takis me sewokeing o.’ Ekom e xe lupeyei nimza yon talex bei e xe xuk on la bombek.”
MAT 11:20 Woyom Yesu neil beyeeng tiyon en ingwei mi wong lulvako eivek o, ekom xel on se pekwi xow.
MAT 11:21 “Xam Korasin me xam Betsaida ghe gwaleeng amim en tyek xam a tulek nimaying. Wangwei lulvako wei a wong eivek xam eno xel bong eivek Taia me Saidon, on beip xel pekwi xow takwei nei me byex teimb wei talot o de ev vewev me pelei lek xow.
MAT 11:22 Ekom a neil wou xam bei, lek bouk wei Anutu embei bong qayeeng en xomaxoneing dalus eno tyek nimaying ngandoung qandi wou xam ghanaw veil nambei ingwei qandi wou Taia me Saidon o.
MAT 11:23 De xam Kapenaom, tyek xel a zeim xam ghe zekna pu wei tyoung nei? Ma yo, tyek wa deteina beyeeng wei meyeing o. En wangwei lulvako wei a wong wou xam eno xel bong eivek Sodom, yond tyek Sodom na mi mendei me e nam atyip bouk tine is.
MAT 11:24 Ekom a neil wou xam bei lek bouk wei ngoeing qayeeng eno tyek bo nimaying ngandoung wou xam ghanaw Sodom.”
MAT 11:25 Lek seivma tiyon Yesu neil, “Mang, a sanghoxe wang, Tambiy Ngandoung wei tyoung gheyapu me tembuing o, en nambei wang vun lulti beimambei ne veil xel wei lundpeyei me kwa nimza yo, dom ghe talex eyeip yaing wou xel yakyak.
MAT 11:26 Ee Mang, en inye wang betiwou wamaxow xe woueing nalei nimza.
MAT 11:27 “Lulul dalusateiv eno Mang toung eivek a memang. Xelti se yeimawou xomaxoneing Neu Moux qe Ma venaxow, me xelti se yeimawou Ma qe Neu Moux venaxow me eti yeiw wei Neu Moux beyal bei talex e wou xel o.
MAT 11:28 “Xam dalus wei ghe mi wong pok ngandoung me ghe mi qalei nimaying eno xam lam wou ay me tyek a bong xam ghe na mendei veil xuk wei xam ghe wong o.
MAT 11:29 Xam qalei a xe pelang maying lek xow me qou kwa wou ay, en a ne a laleing xeiles me laleing vevopeing, me tyek xam numim na mendei me na qou laweeng.
MAT 11:30 En a xe pelang on levismaeing me a xe maying ne vevopeing.”
MAT 12:1 Lek bouk wei Sabat eno Yesu la eivek xuk wei wit. E xe xel betiyeing maxepya xel om xel embei qou wit lu valu me gya.
MAT 12:2 Xel Parisi yei tine, eno xel neil wou e, “Wei! Wa xe xel betiyeing di wong vati wei se la teyei lek petieing o lek bouk wei Sabat o.”
MAT 12:3 Moxo lewexe, “Beip xam seng pyaw vati wei Dawit wong gyeik ingwei e me e xe xel wei mi la is eno maxepya xel o?
MAT 12:4 Om Dawit la eivek xomek wei Anutu xe yo, de e me e xe xel wei mi la is e yo ya belet wei vambuing wei xel peti yo, en inyon xel lumuki venaxow xe.
MAT 12:5 O xam seng pyaw eivek qapiya wei petieing o, bei lek Sabat eno xel lumuki wei mi wo xuk eivek xomek vambuing eno pyalek petieing wei Sabat o, eno se wo sewokeing?
MAT 12:6 A neil wou xam bei tiwei toundei inye eno ghanaw xomek vambuing.
MAT 12:7 Wangwei xam ghe boulek qayeeng tine qes, “‘A laleing vind lalei pyaweingxow, de se seing xound,’ xam seng teyei bei toung nimaying lek xel wei se wo sewokeing o.
MAT 12:8 En Xomaxoneing Neu Moux on Tambiy Ngandoung wei Sabat o.”
MAT 12:9 Yesu la veil beyeeng tiyon, me la eivek xel xe xomek qekueing ama,
MAT 12:10 me tambiy wei mema bezomb eno ti toundei inyon. Xel di yimexe qayeeng qes wei xel embei bong qayeeng en Yesu yo, om xel teling wou e, “Beip inyei teyei lek bei xey a bong xel wei vanei eno bo nimzalek Sabat, o ma?”
MAT 12:11 Moxo neil wou xel, “Wangwei xam ti xe sipsip ti deteina eivek leiveeng lek Sabat, tyek wa seng na zeim e me na puw e nam myayaing?
MAT 12:12 Xel xomaxoneing on ghanaw sipsip veil! Omva petieing neil embei xey a bong kwa nimza lek Sabat.”
MAT 12:13 Woyom moxo neil wou tambiy on, “Tatei memam.” Om moxo tatei mema de mema wo nimza no, nambei mema nge.
MAT 12:14 Ekom xel Parisi la myayaing me luk wouma bei tyek xel nyeis Yesu nambei nya.
MAT 12:15 Om Yesu la veil beyeeng tiyon, en woulek vati wei xel Parisi embei bo wou e yo. Xel ngenong betiwou e, me moxo wong xel dalus xe vanei ma,
MAT 12:16 de peti xel bei eti se neil e teyei bei e eti.
MAT 12:17 Kwa tine la teyei lek vati wei Anutu neil eivek poropet Yesaya mya yo.
MAT 12:18 “Wei, inye a xe xukxe tiwei a beyal o, a laleing vind e me na wo xeinglala en e. Tyek a toung a xe Laweeng lek e, me moxo tyek baluk en kwa bombek wei moux alis vex wei tembuing sapa yo.
MAT 12:19 Tyek moxo se neil qayeeng is lalei vanei me taxe niseikeing, me xelti tyek se ngo e vya eivek sakwaing mema nayak on.
MAT 12:20 Wangwei ghet na pyaw nayaka eno tyek se pyaw veil, me wangwei lam bo lu bandaing tyek moxo se nyeis lam amey, qe ka e menyex wou sakwaing bombek me e bo neing lek.
MAT 12:21 Eivek e lei eno xomaxoneing eivek tembuing bamba tyek na toung mend en e.”
MAT 12:22 Woyom xel qou tambiy wei memo wong e ma tuzeyi me myatu yo me lam wou Yesu, me e wong moxo wo nimzalek, en kandek moxo teyei bei baluk me gyeina.
MAT 12:23 Xomaxoneing dalus etek me neil, “Beip inye Dawit Neu Moux?”
MAT 12:24 Ekom gyeik xel Parisi ngo tine, xel neil, “Tambiy tine mi tiy memo en nikanzek wei Belsebul o, lukanzek wei xel memo yo.”
MAT 12:25 Yesu woulek xel xe woueing nalei om neil wou xel, “Tete lalei dalus wei dembuma yo tyek bo nol wouma, me beyeeng ngandoung o xomek ti dembuma on tyek se bale nikanzek.
MAT 12:26 Wangwei Sandang na tiy Sandang na veil, on moxo dembu venaxow. Woyom nambei nya moxo xe tete lalei tyek bale nikanzek?
MAT 12:27 Me wangwei a tiy memo na veil angya Belsebul nikanzek nei, ond eti mi vind xel wei xam o me xel mi tiy memo yon la myayaing? Om xel wei xam eno tyek talex wou xam bei qayeeng wei xam on se la wo bombek.
MAT 12:28 Ekom wangwei a tiy memo yon na veil nangya Anutu xe Laweeng, woyom Anutu xe tete lalei eno lam wou xam woy.
MAT 12:29 “Nambei nya tambiy ti teyei bei na eivek tambiy wei nikanzek o beeng me na qou e xe lulul, ka e tup tambiy nikanzek on bole? Woyom e teyei bei na panax lulul eivek e xe xomek.
MAT 12:30 “Moux wei se mindei is ay, eno inye mi wo vevek wou ay, de tambiy wei se mi qekuwou moux alis vex is ay eno mi tiy xel lala.
MAT 12:31 Om a neil wou xam bei, sewokeing tambak me qayeeng lukeingyak wei xomaxoneing mi wong eno Anutu teyei bei semaleeng veil, ekom tambiy ti embei baluk yak lek Laweeng Vambuing eno e xe nilul on tyek se semaleeng veil.
MAT 12:32 Tambiy ti embei baluk qayeeng nilul lek Xomaxoneing Neu Moux on tyek semaleeng veil, ekom xelti embei baluk nilul lek Laweeng Vambuing on tyek nilul wei e yon se teyei bei semaleeng veil, eivek bouk tine me bouk loxyus wei di lam o is.
MAT 12:33 “Wangwei xax on nimza, ond tyek neing on bo nimza is, o wangwei xax on bo nilul on tyek neing on bo nol is ambei nyon, en xel mi woulek xax lek e neing.
MAT 12:34 Xam on myeiy nilul neuyeiw, nambei nya tyek xam baluk qayeeng nimza? En qayeeng mi lam veil xomaxoneing laleind me xel myend mi luk.
MAT 12:35 Xomaxoneing wei nimza eno tyek bo lulul nimza wei mindei eivek e lalei yo, dom xomaxoneing wei nilul eno tyek bo lul wei nilul wei toundei eivek e yo nam myayaing.
MAT 12:36 Ekom a neil wou xam bei gyeik Anutu embei daxe xomaxoneing, xel eti yeiw wei mi neil qayeeng bandabanda dalus eno xel a tul pavulek wei xel o teyei.
MAT 12:37 En wamaxow xe qayeeng eno tyek Anutu na neimbei wa bombek, de wamaxow xe qayeeng eno tyek na neimbei wa tambiy nilul.”
MAT 12:38 Woyom xel Parisi valu me putoung wei petieing o neil wou Yesu, “Putoung, xa bei ghei dee wei lulvako valu wou wang.”
MAT 12:39 Moxo lewexe, “Xel moux alis vex nilul wei bouk tine wei mi toung demind wou Anutu yo eno mi teling en dee wei lulvako! Ekom xel se teyei bei gyei dee ti, qe tyek xel gyei dee wei poropet Yona yo.
MAT 12:40 En Yona toundei bendiyeing yal me boukeing yal eivek woing ngandoung on bambou, om Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek mendei bendiyeing yal me boukeing yal eivek tembuing lalei.
MAT 12:41 Lek bouk wei ngoeing qayeeng eno xel wei Niniwe tyek qandi me bale me bo qayeeng en xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne me na neil xel xe nilul teyei, en xel pekwi xow gyeik ingwei Yona la neil xoulek o. Wei, gweimbeeng tambiy ti ghanaw Yona veil, eno lam toundei inye.
MAT 12:42 Kwin wei xonei eno tyek nam bale lek qayeeng is xel wei gweimbeeng ne me bo qayeeng en xel, en vexo lam anghei tembuing myasepu bei nam a ngo Salomo xe kwa nimza. De gweimbeeng ne tambiy ti ghanaw Salomo eno lam toundei inye.
MAT 12:43 “Gyeik laweeng nilaxes lam myayaing veil xomaxoneing ti, eno la eivek beyeeng bandaing me yimexe beyeeng wei embei na qou laweeng o ekom se yeiwou ti.
MAT 12:44 Woyom neil, ‘Tyek a nox mena beyeeng wei a ghanaw o.’ Gyeik e lam tyip me yei xomek wei xelti se qou yo. Eno xel pepa e wo vako me vunekwou e wo nimza.
MAT 12:45 Woyom moxo la me qou laweeng lim yuw ba wei nilul ayang ghanaw e yo, me xel la lalei me dei inyon. Om tambiy tiyon xe deing wo nilul ghanaw ingwei mindei tax o. Inyon tyek bong ambei kayon wou xel nilul wei gweimbeeng ne yo.”
MAT 12:46 Gyeik Yesu di luk is xel qendu yon, moxo ta me liyeiw moux toukale myayaing, en xel embei baluk is e.
MAT 12:47 Xel ti neil wou e, “Wa tam me limyeiw moux lam toukale myayaing, en xel embei baluk is wang.”
MAT 12:48 Yesu neil elox wou e, “A tang eti, me a lingyeiw eti?”
MAT 12:49 Om seloung mema la wou e xe betiyeingyeiw, me neil, “Inye a tang me a lingyeiw moux.
MAT 12:50 En eti yeiw wei mi betiwou Mang wei toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu yo lalei yond inyon a ling moux me a ling vex me a tang.”
MAT 13:1 Lek bouk kayon eno Yesu la myayaing veil xomek me la toundei wou lounyeing vi.
MAT 13:2 De xel qendu ngandoung ti qekuma vivekwou e om moxo lek la eivek bot ti me la dei eivek lalei, de xomaxoneing dalus on toukale nenyawes.
MAT 13:3 Woyom moxo neil lulul ngenong wou xel eivek qayeeng pakeing, me neil, “Xukana ti la vuw lul vei eivek xuk.
MAT 13:4 Ka moxo di vuw lul vei lala, eno valu teila lek sakwaing, me menek menek lam ya e ma.
MAT 13:5 De valu teila lek tembuing wei qakous o, en inyon tembuing nayaka toundei lek qakous mapu yon. Om belup daing me lam, en nambei tembuing on se la ghembi.
MAT 13:6 Ekom gyeik ingwei seiv leklam nale ghey, eno seiv leis vei yuvek lek me mupek, en luselis ma veil.
MAT 13:7 De vei valu teila senghoing eivek qeis wei yingying o om tyip me sevunexe lulul vei yon.
MAT 13:8 De vei valu teila lek tembuing nimza, me vuk neing teyei lek 100, me valu vuk 60 de valu 30 inye vati wei ev o.
MAT 13:9 Eti nenya nale lek e, ond wong e ngo.”
MAT 13:10 Xel betiyeing lam wou e me teling, “Nambei nya wang mi luk is xomaxoneing eivek qayeeng pakeing?”
MAT 13:11 Moxo neil elox bei, “Lupeyei nimza wei tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu wei mi yeip xupekeing eno Anutu wong wou xam dom se wong wou xel.
MAT 13:12 Eti yeiw wei liw nenyend wou a xe qayeeng petieing on tyek lupeyei gyeip yaing wou xel, me xel a qou lupeyei ngenong is. Ekom xel wei se mi ngo, eno lupeyei nayak wei xel qou yon eno tyek Anutu bouveil xel.
MAT 13:13 En qes tine om a mi luk wou xel eivek qayeeng pakeing. “Xel mendghalus tyek gyei, ekom tyek xel se gyei lulti. Me xel a ngo, ekom tyek xel se ngo wou me boulek qayeeng qes.
MAT 13:14 Om xel wong qayeeng wei poropet Yesaya neil eno wo neing lek. “ ‘Tyek xam a ngo qayeeng lumama ekom tyek xam seng boulek. Tyek xam a mi gwei lumama ekom tyek xam seng gwei lulti.
MAT 13:15 En xel xomaxoneing tine laleind wo nikanzek, me xel on nenyend wo qatu me xel mendghalus on tuzeyi. Enok xel gyei nangya mendghalus, me na ngo gya nenyend, me boulek eivek naleind me pekwi me noum, de tyek a bong xel bo nimzalek.’
MAT 13:16 Ekom xam Anutu e bong mata wou xam, en nambei xam mamimghalus yei ay me nambei xam nenyamim ngo wou qayeeng.
MAT 13:17 A neil wou xam zonghek bei xel poropet ngenong me xel moux wei bombek eno embei gyei vati wei xam ghe wei gweimbeeng ekom xel se yei, me xel embei ngo vati wei xam ghe ngo gweimbeeng ekom xel se ngo.
MAT 13:18 “Woyom ngo wou vati wei qayeeng pakeing neil en xukana vuw vei eno qes.
MAT 13:19 Gyeik xelti embei ngo qayeeng ne en tete lalei me se boulek nei, on tambiy ka nilul eno lam me tetei vati wei xend eivek e lalei yo veil. Vei tine inye vei wei vuw lek sakwaing o.
MAT 13:20 De vei wei teila lek tembuing wei qakous qakous, eno inye tambiy wei ngo qayeeng me lutika eno qou is lalei nimza me wo xeilala yo.
MAT 13:21 Ekom luselis wei e yo ma om nale nayaka. Gyeik nimaying wei xel mi pesek qayeeng o nimaying wei xomaxoneing wo nol wouma en Anutu xe xoulek eno lam, lutika eno moxo saing e xe wongeingis.
MAT 13:22 De vei wei teila eivek qeis wei yingying o, eno inyon tambiy wei ngo qayeeng, ekom wounalei en mapieing tine me lul dalus wei tembuing eno sevunexe om se vuk neing.
MAT 13:23 Ekom vei wei teila lek tembuing nimza yon, inyon tambiy wei ngo qayeeng me woulek. Moxo vuk neing teyei lek 100 o 60 o 30 inyon vati wei xend o.”
MAT 13:24 Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing nge wou xel no. “Tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu yon nambei tambiy ti vuw vei nimza eivek e xe xuk o.
MAT 13:25 Ekom ka xel dalusateiv yeip, e xe xel vevek amba lam me vuw vyaing eivek wit masenghoing dom la veil.
MAT 13:26 Ka wit tyip me lu belup, woyom vyaing tyip is ambei nyon.
MAT 13:27 “Xukma xe xukxe lam wou e me neil, ‘Teiv, beip wa seng vuw vei nimza eivek wa xe xuk? De woyom vyaing beimambei ne lam anghei inya?’
MAT 13:28 “Moxo neil elox bei, ‘Vevek amba ti lam wong tine.’ “Xel xukxe teling wou e, ‘Wambei xa na me na puw veil?’
MAT 13:29 “Moxo lewexe bei, ‘Ma, en nambei wa bei puw vyaing eno tyek wa puw wit luselis is.
MAT 13:30 Wong luw xouing ling deka bouk wei qoueing neing o le. Lek bouk kayon eno tyek a neil wou xel wei mi qou neing o, “Xam a puw vyaing atax me na tup buing en nyuweing, woyom xam qeku wit me na qou me nam eivek a xe xomek yaeing.” ’ ”
MAT 13:31 Moxo neil qayeeng pakeing nge wou xel no: “Tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno nambei mastet vei, wei tambiy ti qou me xen eivek e xe xuk o.
MAT 13:32 Inyon nayakameng ka veil vei dalus, ekom gyeik ingwei tyip ngandoung, inyon ling ngandoungateiv ghanaw lul dalus wei ev eivek xuk me wong ngandoung nambei xax, omek menek menek wei senghoing bandaing nei mi lam me qo lewis lek mema mema.”
MAT 13:33 Yesu lox neil qayeeng pakeing nge no, “Tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu yon nambei yis wei xel vex mi qou me maleeng eivek palawa me wong palawa vuklek me wo ngandoung.”
MAT 13:34 Yesu mi luk ti beimambei ne dalus wou xel qendu ngandoung on eivek qayeeng pakeing. Moxo se mi neil qayeeng ti yeipyaing wou xel qe mi neil eivek qayeeng pakeing.
MAT 13:35 Om nambei nyon kwa tine la teyei lek lulti Anutu neil eivek poropet mya. “Tyek a tax myang en neileing qayeeng pakeing. Tyek a neil pavulek en lul leimalei wei mindei xupekeing takwei wei tembuing lam nale yanyateiv o me elam gweimbeeng ne.”
MAT 13:36 Woyom moxo ghanaw xel qendu yon me la eivek xomek. E xe xel betiyeing lam wou e me neil, “Neil e yeip yaing wou xa en qayeeng pakeing qes wei vyaing tyip eivek xuk o.”
MAT 13:37 Moxo lewexe bei, “Tambiy tiwei vuw vei nimza yon, inyon Xomaxoneing Neu Moux.
MAT 13:38 Xuk on tembuing sapa, de vei nimza yon teyei lek neuyeiw wei tete lalei yo. De vyaing on Sandang neuyeiw,
MAT 13:39 me vevek amba wei vuw xel on inye tambiy kawei mapetok o. De bouk wei qoueing neing on inyon bouk wei embei na tip lek o, de xel wei embei qou neing eno inye xel angela.
MAT 13:40 “Ka xel a puw vyaing me banyuw lek nenyex, yon tyek xel bong ambei nyon lek bouk loxyus.
MAT 13:41 Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek bong e xe xel angela na myayaing nei, me tyek xel a puw lul dalus wei mi wong sewokeing mi tyip o me xel dalus wei mi wong nilul ayang eno veil e xe tete lalei.
MAT 13:42 Tyek xel banex xel na eivek nenyex ngandoung de nanghei inyon eno tyek xel deeng me zanga newound bo nyiknyik.
MAT 13:43 Woyom xel wei bombek o tyek na siing ambei sayeiv eivek tete lalei wei xel Mend xe yo. Tambiy ti nenya nale lek e, ond wong e ngo.
MAT 13:44 “Tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei nambei xel vun qoupek wei malew eivek xuk ti. Gyeik tambiy ti yeiwou, eno la vun no, de woyom moxo wo xeilala me la wong vateivek lek lul dalus wei e yo dom la xouv xuk tiyon.
MAT 13:45 “Nge no, tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno nambei tambiy wei mi wo vateivek lek lulul o ti eno di yimexe viyaviy nimzamza.
MAT 13:46 Gyeik moxo yeiwou ingwei nimza maseim o ti, moxo la me wong vateivek lek e xe lul dalus de la xouv.
MAT 13:47 “Nge no, tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu yon nambei lewek wei xel nex e teila eivek lounyeing me qou woing leimalei dalus o.
MAT 13:48 Lewek on pup, xel wei mi qou woing eno puw e leklam yasewis. Woyom xel dei tembuing me beyal woing wei nimza me toung eivek pasik ngenong, dom xel nex nilul o la.
MAT 13:49 Tine inye vati wei tyek qandi lek bouk loxyus o. Angelayeiw tyek nam me beyal xel wei nilul o veil xel wei bombek o
MAT 13:50 me banex xel na eivek nenyex ngandoung wei tyek xel na mi deeng me zanga newound bo nyiknyik o.”
MAT 13:51 Yesu teling, “Xam ghe woulek lul dalus ti beimambei ne?” Xel lewexe, “Ee.”
MAT 13:52 Moxo neil wou xel bei, “Nambei nyon xel putoung tambak wei petieing wei woulek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno nambei xomek ti ma wei qou e xe lul wei xomek vateivek o me lul wei takwei me vako eno is me qou de lam myayaing.”
MAT 13:53 Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing ti beimambei ne ma, moxo la veil inyon.
MAT 13:54 Moxo la beeng qes, me teyoxe xomaxoneing eivek xel xe xomek qekueing ama, om xel etek. Xel neil, “Xomaxoneing ne qou kwa ti beimambei ne nanghei inya me di wong lulvako ne?
MAT 13:55 Beip inye se kamunda neu? De ta se lei Maria, me Jems, me Yosep me Simon me Yudas eno se e liyeiw?
MAT 13:56 Beip inye e liyeiw vex se toundei is xey? Woyom moux tine qou lulti beimambei ne dalus nanghei inya?”
MAT 13:57 De xel laleind wo maying en e. Ekom Yesu neil wou xel, “Eivek e maxow beeng qes me eivek e maxow xe xomek inyon poropet wei lei maeing o.”
MAT 13:58 Om moxo se wong lulvako ngenong ti nanghei inyon, en nambei xel xe wongeingis eno ma.
MAT 14:1 Lek bouk kayon eno Herot seyap tiwei tax o ngo qayeeng en Yesu,
MAT 14:2 om neil wou e xe xel xukxe bei, “Tambiy tine inye Yoan lipekeing. Moxo qandi veil meyeing! Qes tiyon om qou nikanzek me di wong lulvako tine.”
MAT 14:3 Takwei eno Herot zeimaxoun Yoan me tup e dom toung e eivek xeitueing en Herodias, li Pilip venei,
MAT 14:4 en nambei Yoan neil wou moxo, “Inye se nimza bei wa qou lim Pilip venei.”
MAT 14:5 Herot embei nyeis Yoan, ekom moxo yaleeng en xel xomaxoneing on, en inye xel wou kwend bei tambiy on poropet ti.
MAT 14:6 Lek Herot xe bouk wei umbek lek eno lam om Herodias neu vexawo yon lam aw om Herot wo xeilala me lalei vind vexo,
MAT 14:7 om wong qayeeng neing is nikanzek wou vexo bei tyek bong vati wei embei teling eno wou e.
MAT 14:8 Lek ta xe woueing nalei, vexo neil, “Wang bong Yoan lipekeing lukanzek wou ay lek dipekta ne.”
MAT 14:9 King moxo lalei wo nimaying, ekom e xe qayeeng wei neil zonghek is vexo me e xe xel wei lam en yaeing o, om moxo neil wou e xe xel bei vexo xe telinyeing embo neing lek
MAT 14:10 om wong xel la qateiv Yoan kwa tip eivek xomek xeitueing.
MAT 14:11 Moxo lukanzek eno xel toung lek dipekta me qou me la wong wou vexawo yon, de vexo qou me la wong wou ta.
MAT 14:12 Yoan xe xel betiyeing lam me qou e neing me la ev. Woyom xel la neil wou Yesu.
MAT 14:13 Yesu ngo vati wei belup on, moxo la veil beyeeng me la lek bot me la ingwei xel ma veil o. Xel qendu ngandoung on ngo tine me betiy e me la vaxend nanghei beyeeng nayak ngenong on.
MAT 14:14 Yesu teila me yei xel qendu ngandoung on, moxo lalei pyaxow en xel om wong xel xe vanei wo nimzalek.
MAT 14:15 Ka ingwei di souk o, xel betiyeing lam me neil wou e, “Beyeeng bandaing tine xel ma veil, de moxo di bouk tiyo inye mouyo. Wong xel qendu ngandoung on la, en kandek xel na beyeeng nei me na bou xend yaeing valu yo.”
MAT 14:16 Yesu neil elox, “Xel na enva? Xam ghe bong lul yaeing valu wou xel en xel gya.”
MAT 14:17 Xel neil wou e, “Yaing ngenong ma veil xa yo, inye belet lim de woing yuw xemou.”
MAT 14:18 Moxo neil, “Xam qou dalus me lam inye wou ay.”
MAT 14:19 De moxo neil wou xomaxoneing on bei xel mendei tembuing lek lesilek on. Moxo qou belet lim on me qou woing yuw on is dom yeila tyoung gheyapu nei, me wo dange wou dom dembu. Woyom wong wou e xe xel betiyeing, me xel betiyeing wong wou xel xomaxoneing on.
MAT 14:20 Xel dalus on ya me enden xel, de xel betiyeing qekuwou myapapu wei xel se ya yo eivek pasik xoumeeng yuw.
MAT 14:21 Xel moux wei ya yaeing on teyei lek 5,000. Xel se pyaw memend wou xel vex alis neundyeiw.
MAT 14:22 Lutika eno Yesu wong xel betiyeing la eivek bot me la tax en e me la nge loxalu, dekakom wong xel qendu ngandoung on la.
MAT 14:23 Ka ingwei wong xel on la woy, moxo venaxow lek la lukendu bei na zeimema. Gyeik ingwei boukeing di lam eno e maxow toundei inyon,
MAT 14:24 ekom bot vena la dingta takwei nei veil tembuing, me laweeng vei mamileeng vuk me lam leislek bot is xel.
MAT 14:25 Ka embim boyaing eno Yesu di la wou xel, me la lek lounyeing mapu.
MAT 14:26 Xel betiyeing yei moxo di la lek lounyeing mapu, om xel yaleeng me neil, “Inye memo ti nu.” Om xel yaleeng me nyayek.
MAT 14:27 Ekom Yesu wo daing me neil wou xel, “Xam nale nimkanzek! Inye ay yo. Om xam seng gwaleeng.”
MAT 14:28 Petele neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wangwei inye wang nei, ond neil me a lak wou wang lek memiing on.”
MAT 14:29 Moxo neil, “Lam.” Woyom Petele teila veil bot, dom la lek memiing mapu me la wou Yesu.
MAT 14:30 Ekom moxo yei laweeng, moxo yaleeng mouyo, me di teila eivek manghembi, om taxe niseikeing, “Tambiy Ngandoung, vind ay!”
MAT 14:31 Lutika eno Yesu tatei mema la me vyex e. Moxo neil, “Wa xe wongeingis on nayaka. Wa laleim on wo yuw enva?”
MAT 14:32 Woyom luw lek la eivek bot, de laweeng on mey.
MAT 14:33 Woyom xel wei toundei eivek bot on wong lalo wou e, me neil, “Neing ayang wang on Anutu Neu Moux.”
MAT 14:34 Ka xel la nge loxalu, xel teila Genesaret.
MAT 14:35 Xel xomaxoneing wei beyeeng on woulek Yesu, xel wong qayeeng la wou xel xomaxoneing wei mindei paviy beyeeng dalus on. Xomaxoneing dalus on qou xel xe xel wei vanei yo me lam wou e
MAT 14:36 me tay wou e bei xel mou daxlek e xe teimb myasepu, me eti yeiw wei axlek e eno wo nimzalek.
MAT 15:1 Woyom xel Parisi valu me xel putoung wei petieing eno lam anghei Yerusalem me lam wou Yesu me teling,
MAT 15:2 “Nambei nya wa xe xel betiyeing mi pyalek petieing wei buyeiw xe kwa wei takwei yo? Xel se mi sekweyexe memend atax ekom mi ya xend yaeing!”
MAT 15:3 Yesu neil elox bei, “De nambei nya xam ghe pyalek qayeeng petieing wei Anutu xe yo en xam bumim venaxow xe kwa yon?
MAT 15:4 En Anutu neil, ‘Wa mi gwevek mam aluw tam xe qayeeng’ me ‘Xel tiwei embei neil vyalek ma luw ta eno xel nyeis e mey.’
MAT 15:5 Ekom xam ghe mi neimbei wangwei tambiy ti e neil wou ma luw ta, ‘Vati wei ambei devind muw eno a beyal wou Anutu takwei nei,’
MAT 15:6 tambiy moxo tyek se gwevek ma no. Lek kwa tiyon xam ghe mi toung demimim wou Anutu dom ghe mi sanghoxe lul wei xam bumimyeiw o.
MAT 15:7 Xam wei myamim yuw o! Poropet Yesaya neil zonghek gyeik moxo neil en xam xe kwa yo.
MAT 15:8 “‘Xomaxoneing ti beimambei ne mi pamilexe ay en myend, ekom xel laleind on toundei dingta en ay.
MAT 15:9 Xel mi wong lalo wou ay bandaing, en xel xe teyoxeing ekom xel xe petieing yon lam wou xomaxoneing.’”
MAT 15:10 Yesu taxe xel qendu yon lam wou e me neil, “Xam a ngo me ghe boulek.
MAT 15:11 Vati wei mi la eivek eti yeiw myend eno se mi wong e wo nilaxes, qe vati wei lam myayaing veil e mya, eno mi wong e wo nilaxes.”
MAT 15:12 Woyom xel betiyeing lam wou e me teling, “Beip wa seng woulek bei xel Parisiyeiw laleind wo myavanei gyeik xel ngo qayeeng tine yo?”
MAT 15:13 Moxo neil elox bei, “Lul dalus wei Mang wei toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu nei se ev eno tyek xel a puw is luselis.
MAT 15:14 Wong xel toukale. Xel on mend tuzeyi. Wangwei tambiy wei matekeing o natax en moux wei matekeing, luw xouing tyek deteina eivek leiveeng.”
MAT 15:15 Petele neil, “Neil qayeeng pakeing tine qes wou xa.”
MAT 15:16 Yesu teling wou xel, “Beip xam se ghei woulek no?
MAT 15:17 Xam seng wei bei vati wei mi la eivek xomaxoneing myend me la eivek e xeita de woyom lam myayaing veil e me la eivek leiveeng?
MAT 15:18 Ekom vati wei lam myayaing veil wa myam inyon lam anghei wa laleim nei, me ti beimambei ne mi wong xomaxoneing mi wo nilaxes.
MAT 15:19 Inyon woueing nalei nilul, leiseing xel, kwa nilul wei iingama, kwa nilul wei kwapesiv o, panaxeing, qayeeng tyonyeing me lukyak lek xel nge eno lam myayaing veil xe laleind.
MAT 15:20 Lulti beimambei ne ingwei mi wong xomaxoneing mi wo nilaxes, ekom yaeing is memend laxes eno se mi wong e wo nilaxes.”
MAT 15:21 Yesu la veil beyeeng tiyon me la tembuing danghei wei Taia me Saidon nei.
MAT 15:22 Kenan vex ti lam wou e, me di eng niseikeing, “Tambiy Ngandoung, Dawit Neu Moux, pyanaleim en ay! A neung vex toundei eivek nimaying ngandoung en memo wo nilul wou e.”
MAT 15:23 Yesu se neil qayeeng ti lox. Om e xe xel betiyeing lam wou e me neil, “Wong vex on la, en vexo di eng xounaxoun me lam yus en xey.”
MAT 15:24 Moxo lewexe, “Anutu wong a lam en xel sipsip wei Israel o venaxow wei lati yo.”
MAT 15:25 Vex on lam me ev vaxakatu eivek atax wou e de neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, vind ay!”
MAT 15:26 Yesu neil elox bei, “Inye se nimza bei qoueing yakyak xe belet me banex e na wou xel naw.”
MAT 15:27 Vexo neil, “Ee, Tambiy Ngandoung, ekom xel naw mi ya myapapu wei mi teila eivek xel xe teiv xe lelek xeinghembi yo.”
MAT 15:28 Woyom Yesu lewexe, “Vex, wa xe wongeingis on ngandoung! Wa xe telinyeing on embo neing lek nambei wa laleim vind o.” Om neu vex on wo nimzalek seivma kayon bombek.
MAT 15:29 Yesu la veil beyeeng tiyon dom la lounyeing Galili. Woyom moxo lek la lukendu nenya me dei tembuing.
MAT 15:30 Xel qendu ngandoung on lam wou e, xel qou xel bezombeing, me matekeing, vaxa nol, me myatueing me xel valu beti is me toung xel wou Yesu vaxa, de e wong xel wo nimzalek.
MAT 15:31 Xel xomaxoneing on etek en ingwei xel yei tambiy wei myatu eno luk no, me xel bezombeing wo nimzalek, me vaxa nol la me ingwei matekeing eno yeila. Me xel sanghoxe Anutu wei Israel o.
MAT 15:32 Yesu taxe e xe xel betiyeing la wou e me neil, “A laleing pyaxow en xel xomaxoneing ti beimambei ne, en xel lam toundei inye is ay teyei lek bouk yayal de xel se ya lulti. Ambei se bong xel na maxep, enok xel mend bivek me pewilexe wou sakwaing.”
MAT 15:33 E xe xel betiyeing lewexe, “Tyek xa qou belet anghei inya me na bong wou xel ngenong ne eivek beyeeng bandaing ne?”
MAT 15:34 Yesu teling, “Xam ghe di qou belet vamva?” Xel neil elox bei, “Lim yuw, de woing nayak matika is.”
MAT 15:35 Moxo neil wou xel qendu yon bei xel mendei lek tembuing.
MAT 15:36 Woyom qou belet lim yuw on is woing, de wong dange wou woy, om dembu me wong wou xel betiyeing, me xel la wong wou xel xomaxoneing on.
MAT 15:37 Xel on dalus ya me enden xel. Dekalekom xel betiyeing qekuwou myapapu wei wo pupuv o me sei ela eivek pasik lim yuw me e pup.
MAT 15:38 Xel wei ya yaeing on teyei lek 4,000. De xel se pyaw memend wou vex alis neuyeiw.
MAT 15:39 Ka Yesu wong xel on la, moxo la eivek bot me la beyeeng wei Magadan nei.
MAT 16:1 Xel Parisi me xel Sadyusi lam wou Yesu me wo axeing wou e me teling wou bei e talex dee wei tyoung gheyapu nei ti wou xel.
MAT 16:2 Moxo neil elox bei, “Gyeik soukeing lam, eno laxap wo gyand om xam ghe neimbei ‘Inye tyek bo nimza,’
MAT 16:3 de satiboukeing lul eno xam ghe neimbei, ‘De wangwei sayeiv nam a tyip, me na siing lek tyoung me wo gyand ekom laxap wo xeingak me sevun tyoung, woyom xel woulek bei laweeng tyek na tyip me luing detei.’ Xam ghe mi wei dee wei tyoung me ghe woulek ewo nimza, ekom nambei nya xam seng woulek dee wei bouk ti gweimbeeng ne yo.
MAT 16:4 Xel moux alis vex nilul wei bouk tine wei mi toung demind wou Anutu yo eno xel embei gyei dee wei lulvako yo, ekom xel se teyei bei gyei dee ti qe dee wei poropet Yona yo.” Woyom Yesu la veil xel me la.
MAT 16:5 Gyeik xel betiyeing la is Yesu me la lounyeing nge loxalu, xel naleind ma me se qou belet ti.
MAT 16:6 Yesu neil wou xel, “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow en yis wei xel Parisi me Sadyusiyeiw o.”
MAT 16:7 Xel neil tine eivek ama senghoing me neil, “En inye nambei xey se qou belet ti.”
MAT 16:8 Yesu woulek xel xe qayeeng wei xel di luklek on om neil wou xel, “Xam xe wongeingis on nayaka. Nambei nya xam ghe di pyalek ama en ingwei belet ma yo?
MAT 16:9 Beip xam seng ghei woulek? Beip xam seng wou naleimim en belet lim wei xel xomaxoneing 5,000 ya yo, me pasik vamva wei xam ghe qekuwou yo?
MAT 16:10 O belet lim yuw wou xel 4,000, me pasik vamva wei xam ghe qekuwou yo?
MAT 16:11 Nambei nya xam seng woulek bei a se di luk wou xam en belet om a neil qayeeng tine wou xam? Ekom xam ghe gweiteyei xow en yis wei xel Parisi me Sadyusiyeiw o.”
MAT 16:12 Woyom xel woulek bei moxo se di teling xel bei xel gyei xow teyei en yis wei xel mi toung eivek belet o, qe en teyoxeing wei xel Parisi me Sadyusiyeiw o.
MAT 16:13 Yesu la eivek tembuing danghei wei Sisalia Pilipai eno moxo teling wou e xe xel betiyeing, “Xel xomaxoneing mi neil embei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux on eti?”
MAT 16:14 Xel neil elox bei, “Xel valu mi neil embei wa Yoan lipekeing. De valu mi neil embei wa Eliya, me valu mi neil embei wa Yelemia o tambiy wei poropet o ti.”
MAT 16:15 Om moxo teling xel, “ekom xam ghe neimbei ay eti?”
MAT 16:16 Simon Petele lewexe, “Wang on Kilisi, Anutu mapieing neu moux.”
MAT 16:17 Yesu neil elox, “Simon Yona neu, mata e nak wou wang, en xomaxoneing ti se neil inye teyei wou wang, qe inye lam wou Mang wei toundei tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 16:18 De a neil wou wang bei wang on Petele qes bei qakous, me lek qakous tine tyek a bong a xe xel wongeingis bo ngenong, me bale nikanzek lek e de nikanzek wei meyeing eno tyek se nam lelolexe inyon.
MAT 16:19 Tyek am bong ki wei tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei eno wou wang, om vati wei wambei tup lek tembuing eno tyek Anutu na tup anghei tyoung gheyapu nei, de vati wei wa tul lek tembuing ne eno tyek Anutu na tul veil anghei tyoung gheyapu nei.”
MAT 16:20 Woyom moxo peti e xe xel betiyeing bei xel se neilteyei bei e Kilisi.
MAT 16:21 Qandi eivek bouk kayon eno Yesu neilteyei wou e xe xel betiyeing bei tyek na Yerusalem me na qou myavanei ngenong lek xel teivateiv me xel lumuki leitata me xel putoung wei petieing o memend, me xel nyeis e mey de lek bouk yal eno moxo tyek qandi lek veil meyeing.
MAT 16:22 Om Petele qou moxo me la nenyawes me luk niseikeing atax wou e, “Tambiy Ngandoung, se teyei ti! Lul tine tyek se belup wou wang!”
MAT 16:23 Yesu pekwi ma me neil wou Petele, “Sandang, la a deming! Wambei bale zeyi ay. Wa lum on se betiwou lulul wei Anutu yo, qe lulul wei xomaxoneing o.”
MAT 16:24 Woyom Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing, “Wangwei tambiy ti embei betiwou ay, ond e dax xow vun dom qalei e xe xax pepeeng me betiwou ay.
MAT 16:25 En wangwei xelti embei zeimaxoun e xe mapieing yond tyek na saing veil, ekom xelti embei saing e xe mapieing en ay eno tyek na qou e xe mapieing.
MAT 16:26 Wangwei tambiy ti e qou lul dalus wei tembuing sapa ne yo, dom na saing ning mapieing, on tyek na qou lul nimza vati? Moux on tyek bo xouveing vati zeyi ning nu pieing?
MAT 16:27 En Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek nam is Ma xe xeiyaing ngandoung is e xe xel angela, de woyom moxo tyek bong xouveing wou xel titi teyei lek vati wei xel mi wong o.
MAT 16:28 A neil wou xam zonghek, xel valu wei toukale inye eno tyek se daxe meyeing atax, qe ka xel gyei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux nam eivek e xe tete lalei le.”
