MAT 17:1 Ka bouk limti la veil eno Yesu qou Petele me Jems me Yoan inyon Jems li, me qou xel venaxow me la lek lukendu vaxading ti.
MAT 17:2 Nanghei inyon eno moxo neing pekwi me wo bange wou xel mend. Me ma siing nambei sayeiv me e xe teimb wo pus ambei xeiyaing.
MAT 17:3 Dekakom Mose luw Eliya lam tyip wou xel mendghalus me di luk is Yesu.
MAT 17:4 Om Petele neil wou Yesu, “Tambiy Ngandoung, inye nimza bei xey a toumendei inye. Wangwei wa laleim devind nei, on tyek a sakev xomek nayak yayal, ti wou wang, de ti wou Mose de ti wou Eliya.”
MAT 17:5 Ka moxo di luk, laxap teltyip me lam wo tenu zeyi xel, me vya ti lam anghei laxap nei me neil, “Tine inye a neung, e tiwei a laleing vind o, a wo xeinglala en e. Om xam a mi ngo e!”
MAT 17:6 Xel betiyeing ngo tine me xel ev vaxend qatu eivek de mend la lek tembuing, is yalenyeing mouyo.
MAT 17:7 Ekom Yesu lam axlek lal. Moxo neil, “Qandi lek. Mal seng gwaleeng.”
MAT 17:8 Om lal veil mendlek, eno lal se yei xelti, qe Yesu venaxow.
MAT 17:9 Ka xel di lam axo veil lukendu, Yesu luk nikanzek wou xel bei, “Xam se neil wou xelti en vati wei xam ghe wei ne, qe ka Xomaxoneing Neu Moux qandi lek veil meyeing le.”
MAT 17:10 Xel betiyeing teling wou e, “Inye xel putoung wei petieing eno neil embei Eliya tyek nam a tax enva?”
MAT 17:11 Yesu neil elox bei, “Xam ghe boulek neing bei Eliya e nam me menyex wou lulul dalus.
MAT 17:12 Ekom a neil wou xam bei, Eliya lam takwei nei, ekom xel se woulek e, qe xel wong kwa leimalei wou e teyei lek woueing nalei wei xel o. Eivek sakwaing kayon eno Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek na qou nimaying ngandoung lek xel memend.”
MAT 17:13 Woyom xel betiyeing woulek bei moxo di luk en Yoan Lipekeing.
MAT 17:14 Yesu is betiyeing yal on la wou xel qendu yon. Moux ti lam wou Yesu me ev vaxa qatu eivek wou e manghalus.
MAT 17:15 Moxo neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wa pyanaleim en a neung moux en mi puw vaxa mema me mindei eivek nimaying. Moxo mi pewilexe eivek nenyex, o mi teila eivek memiing.
MAT 17:16 A qou e me na lam wou wa xe xel betiyeing, ekom xel se teyei bei bong embo nimzalek.”
MAT 17:17 Yesu neil elox bei, “O xam moux alis vex wei se mi wongis eno xam xe woueing nalei me kwa eno se la teyei lek. Tyek a mendei is xam bouk vamva? Me teyei lek bouk vamva eno tyek a mi qalei nimaying wei xam o? Qou ghavis on me lam wou ay.”
MAT 17:18 Yesu neil laweeng nol on, dom e lam myayaing veil ghavis on, om ghavis on wo nimza lek seivma kayon bombek.
MAT 17:19 Woyom xel betiyeing venaxow lam wou Yesu me teling, “Nambei nya ekom xa se teyei bei tiy inyon na myayaing?”
MAT 17:20 Moxo neil elox bei, “Xam xe wongeingis on nayaka. A neil wou xam zonghek, wangwei xam xe wongeingis nayaka nambei mastet neughalus, wa teyei bei neil wou lukendu tine, ‘La veil inye me la inyei,’ on tyek na ngo me na. Lulti tyek se bo pok wou wang. [
MAT 17:21 Ekom lul ambei nye tyek se nam myayaing, qe nangya zeimeing me vambueing yaeing.”]
MAT 17:22 Yesu is e xe xel betiyeing la me qekuma nanghei Galili, woyom moxo neil wou xel, “Tyek xel a toung Xomaxoneing Neu Moux na eivek xomaxoneing memend.
MAT 17:23 Me tyek xel nyeis e mey, de lek bouk yal eno moxo tyek qandi lek mapieing.” Xel betiyeing ngo qayeeng tine om moxoyeiw laleind wo maying.
MAT 17:24 Ka Yesu lis e xe xel betiyeing la tyip Kapenaom, xel wei mi qou takis wei xomek vambuing eno lam me teling wou Petele, “Beip xam xe putoung se mi toung takis wei xomek vambuing o?”
MAT 17:25 Moxo neil elox wou xel bei, “E, mi toung o.” Ka Petele lam eivek xomek eno Yesu luk ti myaxeeng me teling, “Simon, wang wou naleimim ambei nya? Xel king wei tembuing ne yo mi qou takis leimalei wou eti, wou xel venaxow neundyeiw, o wou xel amba?”
MAT 17:26 Petele neil, “Wou xel amba.” Yesu neil wou e, “Om xel venaxow neundyeiw se teyei bei toung takis.
MAT 17:27 Ekom xey se bong anghei xel laleind bo nol wou xe nei, om la lounyeing nei me nex wa xe ying la eivek. Woing tiwei wang qou tax o, wa tax e mya de tyek wangwei malew selewa ngandoung ti. Wa qou me ghe na bong wou xel en aning takis de wa nim is ambei nyon.”
MAT 18:1 Lek bouk kayon eno xel betiyeing lam wou Yesu me teling, “Eti wo lei ngandoung eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei?”
MAT 18:2 Moxo taxe yak tika me wong e nale eivek xel senghoing.
MAT 18:3 De neil, “A neil wou xam zonghek, wangwei xam se pekwi me ghe ghok ambei yak kane, on tyek xam seng teyei bei na eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu yo.
MAT 18:4 Nambei nyon, eti yeiw wei mi beoux xow nambei yak kane eno wo lei ngandoung eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 18:5 “Me eti yeiw wei qou yak ambei nye eivek a leing, eno qou ay.
MAT 18:6 Enok tambiy ti bong yak ti beimambei wei wongis a ne detei en sewokeing, ond inye teyei bei xel banoux qakous ngandoung lek e kwa dom banex e deteina heivek mamileeng me e mey.
MAT 18:7 “Inye lalei pyaweing en xomaxoneing wei tembuing ne eno mi wong xel amba mi tei en sewokeing. Zonghek, lul nilul ambei nyon eno tyek nam, ekom tambiy wei wong inyon tyip eno e gyaleeng!
MAT 18:8 Om wangwei wa memam o wa vaxam na toung wang eivek sewokeing, ond qateiv veil me nex e la. Inye nimza bei wang na eivek mapieing luta luta is memam tixemou o vaxam tixemou, enok wa memam yuw o vaxam yuw ekom xel banex wang na eivek nenyex wei luta luta yo.
MAT 18:9 Me wangwei wa mamghalus na toung wang eivek sewokeing, ond qepei e lam myayaing me nex e la. Inye nimza bei wang na mendei mapieing is mamghalus tixemou enok wa mamghalus yuw ekom xel banex wang na eivek nenyex wei luta luta yo.
MAT 18:10 “Xam ghe gweiteyei en kandek xam se neimbei yakyak ambei inye lul bandaing. En a neil wou xam bei xel xe angela eivek tyoung gheyapu nei eno mi yei Mang wei tyoung gheyapu nei manghalus.
MAT 18:11 [En Xomaxoneing Neu Moux lam bei qou eti yeiw wei lati yo noum.]
MAT 18:12 “Wang wou naleim ambei nya? Wangwei tambiy ti xe sipsip teyei lek 100, ekom ti nati, yond tyek moxo se teyei bei ghanaw 99 on lek qetyei dom na gyimexe tiwei lati yo?
MAT 18:13 De wangwei e gyeiwou nei, a neil wou xam zonghek, moxo tyek bo xeilala en tiwei lati yo de se 99 wei se lati yo.
MAT 18:14 Eivek sakwaing ambei nyon eno Mam wei toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu embei yakyak on ti se nati.
MAT 18:15 “Wangwei lim bo sewokeing wou wang, ond eivek muw venaxow senghoing eno la me neil e xe nilul teyei wou e. Wangwei e ngowou wa xe qayeeng, yon nambei wang qou lim loum.
MAT 18:16 Ekom wangwei e se ngowou nei, yon wa qou tambiy ti o yuw is xow, en kandek ‘pavulek tambak wei moux yuw o yal eno na byexaxoun qayeeng.’
MAT 18:17 Wangwei e bei se ngowou xel xe qayeeng, yon wa neil wou kongrikesin dalus. Ek wangwei e pyalek kongrikesin xe qayeeng, ond xam ghe gwei e bei inyon tambiy wei mandalus o tambiy wei mi qou takis o ti.
MAT 18:18 “A neil wou xam zonghek, vatiyeiw wei xam ghe tup lek tembuing eno tyek Anutu na tup eivek tyoung gheyapu, de vatiyeiw wei xam ghe tul lek tembuing eno tyek Anutu na tul veil eivek tyoung gheyapu.
MAT 18:19 “A neil wou xam no bei, wangwei xam on yuw na toung laleimim lekti en vati wei muw ambei teling en eno tyek Mang wei tyoung gheyapu nei bong wou muw.
MAT 18:20 En wangwei muw yuw o mal yal a being nam qeku lekti eivek a leing, inyon a toundei is mal.”
MAT 18:21 Woyom Petele lam wou Yesu me teling, “Tambiy Ngandoung, teyei lek lu vamva eno a teyei bei semaleeng ling xe nilul gyeik ingwei embo sewokeing wou ay yo? Ena teyei lek lim yuw?”
MAT 18:22 Yesu neil elox, “A neil wou wang, se lu lim yuw, qe teyei lek lu lim yuw me e mi na lumama teyei lek 70.
MAT 18:23 “Nambei nyon, tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno inye nambei king ti embei menyex wou malew vateivek is e xe xel xukxe wei xel qou wou e yo.
MAT 18:24 Ka moxo qandi en menyex wou malew vateivek, moxo taxe tambiy wei qou malew 10,000 eno lam wou e.
MAT 18:25 Ekom moxo se teyei bei bong malew zeyi, om teiv wo qayeeng nikanzek bei xel bong vateivek lek lis venei neu me lulul dalus wei e beeng o de bong ena zeyi malew vateivek wei qou yo.
MAT 18:26 “Xukxe ev vaxa qatu eivek atax wou e me tay, ‘Wam di daxe ay, en tyek a bong lulul dalus nouk wou wang.’
MAT 18:27 Teiv wei xukxe yon pyanalei en e, om semaleeng malew vateivek wei qou yo dom wong e la.
MAT 18:28 “Ekom xukxe tiyon la myayaing, moxo yeiwou e xe laxous tiwei luw mi wo xuk lekti yo wei qou malew 100 wou e yo. Moxo sex e kwa de luk nikanzek wou e, ‘Wang bong vati wei wang qou wou ay eno noum!’
MAT 18:29 “Moxo xe laxous wei luw mi wong xuk lekti eno ev vaxa qatu eivek me tay wou e, ‘Wam di daxe ay, en tyek a bong malew vateivek wei a qou eno nouk zeyi wou wang.’
MAT 18:30 “Ekom moxo se lewexe lek. Qe la veil de toung laxous la eivek xeitueing deka embong malew vateivek wei qou yo noum zeyi le.
MAT 18:31 Woyom laxousyeiw valu yei vati wei belup on eno xel laleind wo myavanei ngandoung. Om xel la neil wou xel xe teiv en lul sapa wei belup on.
MAT 18:32 “Woyom teiv taxe xukxe la lalei me neil, ‘Wa xukxe nilul ayang. A semaleeng wa xe malew vateivek dalus wei wang o, en nambei wang tay wou ay.
MAT 18:33 Se teyei bei wa pyanaleim en laxous nge wei muw ghe mi wo xuk o nambei ingwei a wong wou wang o?’
MAT 18:34 Teiv moxo lalei wo vanei wou e om toung e la wou xel belimbo wei xeitueing o bei xel bong vanei wou e, deka e bong lulul dalus wei e qou yo noum bole.
MAT 18:35 “Tine inye Mang wei tyoung gheyapu nei tyek bong wou xam titi yo, wangwei wa se semaleeng nilul wei limyeiw nge wong wou wang eivek laleim o.”
MAT 19:1 Gyeik Yesu neil qayeeng ti beimambei ne ma, woyom moxo la veil Galili me la eivek tembuing wei Yudia me la loxalu wei memiing Yorodan nei.
MAT 19:2 Xel qendu ngandoung betiwou e, om moxo wong xel wo nimzalek nanghei inyon.
MAT 19:3 Xel Parisi valu lam wou e bei bong axeing wou e. Xel teling, “Beip inyei petieing neil embei moux ti qateiv iingama wei venei yo veil en woueing nalei wei emaxow o?”
MAT 19:4 Yesu neil elox, “Beip xam seng pyaw qayeeng wei di yeip eivek qapiya wei Anutu yo bei, eivek myaxeeng eno ‘Anutu toung xomaxoneing, moux aluw vex,’ Myaxeeng selis 1:27
MAT 19:5 de neil, ‘En qes tine moux tyek na veil ma luw ta me luw venei na toung lekti me luw bo neing tixemou?’ Myaxeeng selis 2:24
MAT 19:6 Om luw se wo yuw no, qe luw wo neing tixemou. Nambei nyon vati wei Anutu tup lekti, eno xomaxoneing ti se qateiv e tip.”
MAT 19:7 Xel teling, “Woyom nambei nya Mose wong qayeeng nikanzek bei moux e bong qapiya wou venei en qateiv iingama de bong vex on na?”
MAT 19:8 Yesu neil elox, “Mose lenghek lek bei xam qateiv iingama en nambei xam laleimim on wo nikanzekta. Ekom myaxeeng eno kwa nambei inyon eno ma.
MAT 19:9 Om a neil wou xam bei wangwei tambiy ti venei se bo kwapesiv is tambiy nge ekom leya qateiv iingama wei luw o, dom dii vex nge yond moux on venaxow wo kwapesiv.”
MAT 19:10 Xel betiyeing neil wou e, “Wangwei kwa nambei nyon gyeip senghoing eivek moux ti luw venei, ond inye nimza bei moux tiyon se dii vex.”
MAT 19:11 Yesu neil elox wou xel bei, “Xel ngenong tyek se qou qayeeng tine, qe wou xel valu wei Anutu wong nikanzek wou xel eno tyek bong ambei nyon de tyek xel se diima.
MAT 19:12 En moux valu nikanzek wei embei bo yak eno ma gyeik ingwei umbek o, me xel valu eno xomaxoneing veil e nikanzek, de xel valu eno se ii vex en xel wou kwend en xuk tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu yo. Tambiy ti embei qou kwa nambei nye ond wong e qou.”
MAT 19:13 Woyom xel qou yakyak me lam wou Yesu bei e ni mema lek xel me na zeim wou xel. Ekom xel betiyeing luk nikanzek wou eti yeiw wei qou xel me lam o.
MAT 19:14 Yesu neil, “Wong xel yakyak on lam wou ay, de xam se bale zeyi xel, en tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei eno inye wou xel ambei nyon.”
MAT 19:15 Gyeik e li mema lek xel woy, woyom moxo la veil inyon me la.
MAT 19:16 Tambiy ti lam wou Yesu me teling, “Putoung, lul nimza vati a teyei bei bong dom na qou mapieing luta?”
MAT 19:17 Yesu neil elox, “Wang teling ay en vati wei nimza yo en va? Inyon Anutu venaxow nimza. Wangwei wa bei qou mapieing luta nei, ond wa betiwou qayeeng petieing dalus.”
MAT 19:18 Moux moxo teling, “Tina?” Om Yesu neil elox, “ ‘Wa seng nyeis xel amey. Wa seng bo kwapesiv is vex wei dei leya yo. Wa se panax. Wa seng bong qayeeng tyonyeing wou xel.
MAT 19:19 Wa mi gwevek mam aluw tam. Wa laleim e mi devind nimpapu nambei wa laleim mi vind wamaxow o.’ ”
MAT 19:20 Tambiy ghavis on neil wou e, “Petieing dalus eno a mi betiwou. De vati tyek am bong no?”
MAT 19:21 Yesu lewexe, “Wangwei wambei mendei bo nimza nei, ond la wo vateivek lek lulul dalus wei wang o me wong wou xel kanyoyeiw, de tyek wa qou lul nimza ngenong nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei. Woyom wang nam betiwou ay.”
MAT 19:22 Ekom tambiy ghavis on ngo qayeeng tine, om moxo lalei wo maying ngandoung me la, en nambei e xe lulul ngenongakes.
MAT 19:23 Woyom Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing, “A neil wou xam zonghek, inye pok ngandoung en lulul ana embei na eivek tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei yo.
MAT 19:24 A neil wou xam no bei, inye pok neing en ingwei kamel embei na eivek ying manghalus wei duweing o, de pok wei malew ana ti embei na eivek tete lalei wei Anutu xe yo eno ghanaw xel amba ne.”
MAT 19:25 Yesu xe xel betiyeing ngo tine, moxoyeiw etek niseikeing me teling, “Wangwei nambei nyon nei ond tyek eti mendei mapieing luta?”
MAT 19:26 Yesu yeila xel de neil, “Wou xel xomaxoneing eno inye se teyei, ekom is Anutu eno lulul dalus on teyei.”
MAT 19:27 Petele lewexe lek e, “Xa ghanaw lul dalus bei betiwou wou wang! Woyom tyek xa qou vati?”
MAT 19:28 Yesu neil wou xel, “A neil wou xam zonghek, gyeik kawei lul dalus embei bong vako, eno Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei mendei lek e xe sia vambuing wei lei ngandoung o, xam eti yeiw wei ghe mi betiwou ay eno tyek xam mendei lek a xe sia xoumeeng yuw wei vambuing, me ghe gwei veleivlei xoumeeng yuw wei Israel o teyei.
MAT 19:29 Me xel sapa wei ghanaw xel xe xomek, o liyeiw moux, o liyeiw vex, o ma, o ta, o neuyeiw, o xuk en a leing yon tyek na qou 100 ngenong is me tyek xam a qou mapieing luta luta.
MAT 19:30 Ekom xel ngenong wei lam atax eno tyek nox yus, de xel ngenong wei lam yus eno tyek na tax.”
MAT 20:1 “En tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno nambei tembuing ma ti la satiboukeing lulayang bei na qou xel moux en xel na bong xuk eivek e xe xuk wain.
MAT 20:2 Moxo lewexe lek xel bei dexouv xel en malew selewa ti lek bouk titi dom wong xel la eivek e xe xuk wain.
MAT 20:3 “Lek seivma nambei limvey eno tambiy moxo la me yei xel valu toungale eivek beyeeng vateivek dom xel se di wong lulti.
MAT 20:4 Moxo neil wou xel, ‘Xam is ambei nyon xam ghe na bong xuk eivek a xe xuk wain, de tyek a dexouv xam en xouveing wei bombek o.’
MAT 20:5 Om moxoyeiw la. “Moxo lox me la lek ingwei seivma evlek me seivma yal soukeing eno wong kwa kawei yo no.
MAT 20:6 Lek seivma lim soukeing kayon eno moxo la no me yei xel valu nanghei toungale bandabanda. Moxo teling xel, ‘Nambei nya xam ghe mi nale inye bouk tine dalus dom xuk maeing?’
MAT 20:7 “ Xel lewexe, ‘En nambei xelti se qou xa en xuk.’ “Moxo neil wou xel, ‘Xam is ambei nyon xam ghe na bong xuk eivek a xe xuk wain.’
MAT 20:8 “Lek soukeing kayon, eno xuk wain ma neil wou e xe tambiy wei lam xeinghembi en e yo bei, ‘Taxe xel wei wo xuk o lam me xouv xel. Myaxeeng eno wa dexouv xel wei lam yusayang o me mendi na dekakom ghe na wou xel wei lam atax o.’
MAT 20:9 “Xel wei wo xuk lek seivma lim eno lam me xel titi qou malew selewa titi.
MAT 20:10 Om gyeik xel wei lam wo xuk atax eno xel embeik nge tyek xel a qou malew zekna ghanaw xel valu wei lam yus o. Ekom xel titi eno qou malew selewa titi.
MAT 20:11 Xel qou xouveing woy, eno moxoyeiw luk ngenong is tembuing ma.
MAT 20:12 Moxoyeiw neil, ‘Xel moux tiwei lam wo xuk yus eno xel wo xuk teyei lek seivma ti, ekom wang wong xel qou malew teyei lek ambei xa wei wo xuk ngandoung wou seiv myavanei lek bouk tine dalus o.’
MAT 20:13 “Ekom moxo lewexe lek xel on ti, ‘Gweleeng, a se wo nol wou wang. Beip wa seng lewexe lek bei bong xuk en malew selewa ti?
MAT 20:14 Qou wa xe xouveing me la. Ambei bong malew wou tambiy wei lam wong xuk yus o nambei ingwei a wong wou wang ne yo.
MAT 20:15 Beip inye se di yeip wou a bei a bong vati en a maxow xe malew? O inye a memang les om wang qouwou ay?’
MAT 20:16 “Om nambei nyon xel wei la yus eno tyek na tax, de xel wei lam atax eno tyek na yusayang.”
MAT 20:17 Ka Yesu di la pu Yerusalem nei, moxo qou e xe xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw me xel venaxow la nenyawes me neil wou xel,
MAT 20:18 “Wei, xey am bei na pu Yerusalem nei, en Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek xel a toung e na eivek xel lumuki leitata me xel putoung wei petieing o memend. Me tyek xel bo qayeeng en e me na neimbei e mey,
MAT 20:19 me tyek xel a toung e na eivek xel amba memend en xel a neil seloukeing lek e me sesa e me na tuw e lek xax pepeeng. De lek bouk yal eno moxo tyek qandi lek mapieing!”
MAT 20:20 Woyom Sebedi neu luw lam is tend wou Yesu, me ev vaxa qatu eivek me teling Yesu en e xe lalei vineing.
MAT 20:21 Moxo teling, “Inye wa laleim vind vati?” Vexo neil, “A laleind vind bei a neung yuw ne eno nge mendei wou wa memam payeiv de nge wou wa memam qeinz eivek wa xe tete lalei.”
MAT 20:22 Yesu neil wou luw, “Muw seng woulek vati wei muw ghe teling en o. Muw ghe teyei bei num eivek mayamya wei ambei num eivek ne?” Luw neil, “Uw a teyei.”
MAT 20:23 Yesu neil wou luw, “Tyek muw a num eivek a xe mayamya, ekom deing wou a memang payeiv o qeinz eno inye se wou ay bei a zenghek lek. Beyeeng tine inye wou eti yeiw wei Mang venaxow menyex woy wou xel o.”
MAT 20:24 Ka xel xoumeeng ngo qayeeng tine, eno xel wo veweeng wou Yoan aluw li.
MAT 20:25 Yesu taxe xel xouing lam me neil, “Xam ghe woulek bei king wei xel amba eno mi wo ninkanzek bei gyeiteyei xel, me xel xe lei ngandoung mi wo ninkanzek bei moux alis vex na mi betiwou qayeeng tambak wei xel o.
MAT 20:26 Om se is xam. Qe eti bei bo lei ngandoung eivek xam senghoing ond e bong ambei xam xe xukxe,
MAT 20:27 me eti embei na tax ond e bong ambei xam xe xukxe bandaing,
MAT 20:28 teyei lek ambei nyon eno Xomaxoneing Neu Moux se lam bei tyek moux alis vex devind e, qe lam bei bong e xe mapieing nambei xouveing en xomaxoneing ngenong.”
MAT 20:29 Ka Yesu lis e xe xel betiyeing la veil Jeriko, xel qendu ngandoung on betiwou e.
MAT 20:30 Moux matekeing yayuw toundei wou sakwaing vi, om gyeik luw ngo bei Yesu di lamela, luw taxe, “Tambiy Ngandoung, Dawit Neu Moux, pyanaleim en uw!”
MAT 20:31 Xel qendu yon luk nikanzek wou luw bei denduing ma, ekom luw taxe niseikeing, “Tambiy Ngandoung, Dawit Neu Moux, pyanaleim en uw!”
MAT 20:32 Yesu nale dom taxe luw. Moxo teling, “Muw ambei a bong vati wou muw?”
MAT 20:33 Luw lewexe, “Tambiy Ngandoung, uw ambei gheina yo.”
MAT 20:34 Yesu lalei pyaxow en luw om axlek luw xouing mendghalus. De se denlek en luw mend yeila de luw betiwou e.
MAT 21:1 Ka xel la tyip paviy Yerusalem me la Betpage lek lukendu Oliv nei, Yesu wong betiyeing yuw la,
MAT 21:2 me neil wou luw, “Muw ghe na beyeeng tiwei muw mamim di yeila nei, lutika eno tyek muw ghe gwei dongi ti xel tup anghei inyon, is neu lingheing toukale lip ta. Muw wa tul luw xouing me na qou me ghe nam wou ay.
MAT 21:3 Wangwei xelti neil lulti wou muw, ond muw a neil wou bei Tambiy Ngandoung embei bong xuk en, dom tyek bong luw noum daing.”
MAT 21:4 Lul tine la teyei lek lul tiwei Anutu neil eivek poropet mya yo:
MAT 21:5 “Neil wou Sayon neu vex, ‘Wei, xam xe king lam wou xam. Moxo lam ambei tambiy wei lei maeing o me dei lek dongi ti. Moxo dei lek dongi lingheing ti me lam.’”
MAT 21:6 Betiyeing aluw la me wong e la teyei lek kawei Yesu neil wou luw o.
MAT 21:7 Luw qou dongi ta me neu lingheing, me vax luw xe teimb ding lek luw, de Yesu deilek lek.
MAT 21:8 Xel qendu ngandoung on vax xel xe teimb ding lek sakwaing, de xel valu qateiv xax memama me liw lek sakwaing.
MAT 21:9 Xel qendu ngandoung wei la mamunghexeing en e me xel wei di betiwou eno di taxe bei, “Hosana ena wou Dawit Neu Moux! Mata ena wou tiwei lam eivek Tambiy Ngandoung lei yo! Hosana ena eivek tyoung gheyapu nei!”
MAT 21:10 Gyeik Yesu la eivek Yerusalem eno moux alis vex dalus wei beyeeng ngandoung on etek om xel teling, “Tambiy on eti?”
MAT 21:11 Xel qendu yon lewexe, “Tine inye Yesu, poropet wei lam anghei Nasaret eivek Galili yo.”
MAT 21:12 Yesu la eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o me tiy xel wei di xouv lulul me wo vateivek anghei inyon o. Moxo qapyex lelek wei xel di pelipek malew me eti yeiw wei di wo vateivek lek menek beliy o.
MAT 21:13 Moxo neil wou xel, “Xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, ‘A xe xomek tyek xel taxe bei xomek wei zeimeing mema yo,’ ekom xam ghe pelipek e xok ambei ‘eeng wei xel panaxana yo.’”
MAT 21:14 Xel wei mend tekeing me vaxend nol eno lam wou e eivek xomek vambuing, me moxo wong xel wo nimzalek.
MAT 21:15 Ekom xel lumuki leitata me putoung wei petieing lam yei lul nimza wei e wong o me yakyak wo vyend eivek xomek vambuing lalei, “Hosana ena wou Dawit Neu Moux,” om xel laleind wo nilul.
MAT 21:16 Xel teling e, “Beip wang ngo vati wei xel yakyak ti beimambei ne di neil ne?” Yesu neil elox. “E. Beip xam seng mi pyaw qayeeng, “‘Eivek yakyak me yakyeis myend wang menyex wou bei xel a mi sanghoxe wa leim’?”
MAT 21:17 Om moxo la veil xel me la Yerusalem me la Betani, de moxo dei inyon boukeing tiyon.
MAT 21:18 Satiboukeing lul, eno Yesu di la wou sakwaing bei nox Yerusalem, ekom maxepya e.
MAT 21:19 Moxo yei xax basunghek ti toukale wou sakwaing nenyawes, om la ingwei xax toukale ghei yo ekom se yei neing ti qe lis bandaing. Woyom moxo neil wou xax on, “Tyek wa seng nox buk neing no!” Se wo lululek en xax basunghek on mupek.
MAT 21:20 Gyeik xel betiyeing yei tine, moxoyeiw etek mouyo. Xel teling, “Xax basunghek tine mupek daing ambei nya?”
MAT 21:21 Yesu neil elox bei, “A neil wou xam zonghek, wangwei wa laleim se bo yuw en wa xe wongeingis nei, ond se nambei vati wei a wong wou xax basunghek ne venaxow, qe wa neil wou lukendu tine is ambei nyon, ‘La nex xow la eivek mamileeng,’ ond tyek bong ambei kawei wang neil o.
MAT 21:22 Wangwei wang bongis nei, tyek wa qou vatiyeiw wei wang teling en o eivek zeimeing mema.”
MAT 21:23 Yesu la eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing, ka moxo di teyoxe eno xel lumuki leitata me teivateiv wei xomaxoneing o lam wou e. Xel teling, “Wang di wong lulti beimambei ne nangya lei ngandoung wei eti yo? Me eti wong lei ngandoung tine wou wang?”
MAT 21:24 Yesu neil elox bei, “Tyek a bong telinyeing ti wou xam is ambei nyon. Wangwei xam a neil enoum wou a bombek nei, on tyek a neil wou xam en lei ngandoung wei eti ingwei a di wong lulti beimambei ne nangya ne.
MAT 21:25 Yoan xe lipekeing on lam anghei inya? Beip inyon lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei, o inyon lam wou xomaxoneing?” Xel di luk en inye wouma me neil ambei nye, “Wangwei xey a neimbei, ‘Nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei,’ ond moxo tyek teling, ‘Woyom nambei nya xam seng wongis e?’
MAT 21:26 Ek wangwei xey a neimbei, ‘Inyon lam wou xomaxoneing,’ ond xey a ghaleeng en xomaxoneing, en xel dalus woulek bei Yoan ne poropet ti.”
MAT 21:27 Om xel neil e lox wou Yesu, “Xa loungen o.” Woyom moxo neil, “Ay is ambei nyon tyek a se neil wou xam en lei ngandoung vati wei andi wong lulti beimambei ne en o.
MAT 21:28 “Xam ghe wou naleimim ambei nya? Inyon tambiy ti neu moux yayuw. Moxo la wou neu nge wei tax o me neil, ‘Neung, la me wo xuk eivek xuk wain gweimbeeng.’
MAT 21:29 “Moxo neil, ‘Tyek a se na.’ Dekalekom moxo lalei pekwi dom la.
MAT 21:30 “Woyom ma la wou nge wei moun me neil ambei kawei yo no. Moxo lewexe, ‘Mang, tyek a na yo.’ Ekom moxo se la.
MAT 21:31 “Eivek neu yuw on eno luw nge na wong ambei ingwei ma neil o?” Xel lewexe, “Nge wei tax o.” Yesu neil wou xel, “A neil wou xam zonghek, xel wei mi qou takis me vex wei kwapesiv o tyek na eivek tete lalei wei Anutu yo natax en xam.
MAT 21:32 En Yoan lam wou xam bei talex sakwaing wei bombek ayang o wou xam, ekom xam seng wongis e, qe xel wei mi qou takis me xel vex wei kwapesiv o eno wongis. Me xam ghe wei inye, ekom xam seng pekwi xow me ghe wongis e.
MAT 21:33 “Xam a ni nenyamim wou qayeeng pakeing nge no, inyon tembuing ma ti ev e xe xuk wain. Moxo qo tete zeyi e vivekwou, me ev leiveeng wei qeing wain eivek o me ev xomek vaxading wei yeingteyei yo ti. Woyom moxo wong e xe xuk wain wou xel xukana valu dom la sakwaing anding.
MAT 21:34 Bouk wei uleing wain neing o lam paviy, om moxo wong e xe xukxe la wou xel wei yeiteyei xuk wain bei na dul e xe neing valu.
MAT 21:35 “Xel wei mi yeiteyei xuk wain eno zeimaxoun e xe xukxeyeiw, xel sesa ti, de leis nge mey, dom nex tiwei yal o en qakous.
MAT 21:36 Woyom moxo wong xukxe valu lox me la wou xel no, xel la ngenong ka ghanaw nge tax veil, me xel wei mi yeiteyei xuk wain eno wong ambei kawei xel wong nge tax o wou xel.
MAT 21:37 Ti yusayang eno moxo wong e maxow neu moux la wou xel. Moxo neil, ‘Tyek xel a ni nenyend wou a neung moux xe qayeeng.’
MAT 21:38 “Ekom xel wei mi yeiteyei xuk wain eno yei e neu moux om xel neil wouma, ‘Tine inye xukma neu moux wei tyek na qou lulul dalus o. Xam lam, en xey a nyeis e mey de na qou e xe lulul dalus.’
MAT 21:39 Om xel zeimaxoun e me nex e la myayaing veil xuk wain de leis e mey.
MAT 21:40 “Nambei nyon om gyeik xuk wain ma nam, ond tyek moxo bong vati wou xel wei mi yeiteyei xuk wain on?”
MAT 21:41 Xel neil elox bei, “Moxo tyek bo nol wou xel on bo nilul ayang me nyeis xel amey, de tyek moxo bong xuk wain on nox wou xel ba, eti yeiw wei teyei bei tyek bong xuk neing valu wou e gyeik bouk wei uleing neing o.”
MAT 21:42 Yesu neil wou xel, “Xam seng mi pyaw vati wei yeip eivek qapiya vambuing yo: “‘Qakous wei xel kamunda pesek, eno wong ambei qakous ti myaxeeng me mi byexaxoun xomek o. Inye Tambiy Ngandoung venaxow wong tine belup, me wo nimza eivek xa mami’?
MAT 21:43 “Nambei nyon a neil wou xam bei Anutu tyek na qou e xe tete lalei veil xam me bong wou xomaxoneing qendu ti wei tyek bong neing atyip o.
MAT 21:44 De eti detei lek qakous nei tyek dembu me bo myapapu, ekom qakous embei detei lek tambiy ti eno tyek bo myasa bandaing.”
MAT 21:45 Gyeik xel lumuki leitata me Parisi ngo Yesu xe qayeeng pakeing tine, xel woulek bei Yesu di neil inye lek xel.
MAT 21:46 Om xel yimexe sakwaing wei xel embei zeimaxoun e yo, ekom xel di yaleeng en xel qendu ngandoung on en nambei xomaxoneing ngenong yei bei e yon poropet.
MAT 22:1 Yesu luk is xel lu nge no eivek qayeeng pakeing, me neil embei,
MAT 22:2 “Tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno nambei king ti wei menyex wou mata ngandoung wei iingama yo en neu moux.
MAT 22:3 Moxo wong e xe xel xukxe la wou eti yeiw wei wong qayeeng la me neil wou xel bei xel nam en mata ngandoung wei iingama yo, ekom xel pesek bei se nam.
MAT 22:4 “Woyom moxo wong xel xukxe valu no la me neil, ‘Neil wou xel wei a wong qayeeng la wou xel bei a menyex wou a xe yaeing woy, “Wei, a xe manghaxo me leliy wei ling tata yo eno xel leis me ghuw, me lul sapa a menyex wou woy. Xam lam en mata ngandoung wei iingama ne.” ’
MAT 22:5 “Ekom xel se di li nenyend wou qayeeng qe xel la. Ti la e xe xuk, de nge la emaxow xe xuk malew.
MAT 22:6 De xel ba zeimaxoun e xe xel xukxe me wo nol wou xel de leis xel mey.
MAT 22:7 King moxo lalei wo vanei mouyo. Om wong e xe xel vevekyeiw la me semaleeng xel tiwei leis xel xukxe mey yo me nyuw beyeeng ngandoung wei xel on is.
MAT 22:8 “Woyom neil wou e xe xel xukxe bei, ‘A menyex wou mata ngandoung wei iingama eno woy, ekom xel wei a wong qayeeng la bei xel nam eno xel on se nimza teyei bei nam.
MAT 22:9 Om xam ghe na sakwaingta dalus me eti yeiw wei xam ghe gweiwou eno xam a qou me ghe nam eivek mata ngandoung wei iingama ne.’
MAT 22:10 Om xel xukxe la eivek sakwaingta dalus nei me qekuwou xomaxoneing dalus wei xel yeiwou yo, xel nimza me nilul is, om xomek lalei wei mata ngandoung wei iingama yon puplek en xel.
MAT 22:11 “Ekom gyeik king lam lalei me yei xel on, moxo woulek bei tambiy ti toundei inyon eno se byex teimb wei iingama yo.
MAT 22:12 Moxo teling, ‘Gweleeng, wang lam eivek xomek ne lalei nambei nya, ekom wang seng byex teimb wei iingama yo?’ Ekom tambiy on se wo lukluk.
MAT 22:13 “Woyom king neil wou e xe xel xukxe, ‘Xam tup e mema vaxa, dom nex e la myayaing nei eivek mapetok ngandoung nanghei inyon eno xel mi eng me mi nga newound mi wo nyiknyik.’
MAT 22:14 “En nambei Anutu taxe xel ngenong, ekom beyal xel nuyuw ka.”
MAT 22:15 Woyom xel Parisi la myayaing me yimexe sakwaing wei xel embei pakei qayeeng lek e en e maxow xe lukeing o.
MAT 22:16 Xel wong xel xe betiyeing la wou e is xel wei Herot o. Xel neil, “Putoung, xa woulek bei wang on moux wei wang mi neil zonghek o me inyon wang mi teyoxe sakwaing wei Anutu xe lalei nimza is zonghek o. Wa seng mi waleeng en xelti, en nambei wa seng mi li nenyam wou xelti xe qayeeng.
MAT 22:17 Woyom neil wou xa, wang wou naleim ambei nya? Beip inye teyeimbei xey a toung takis wou Sisa o xe se toung?”
MAT 22:18 Ekom Yesu woulek xel xe woueing nalei nilul on, om neil, “Xam wei myamim yuw o, nambei nya xam ghe di wong en xam ambei bong axeing wou ay?
MAT 22:19 Xam talex malew selewa wei xel mi toung takis eno ti me a xei.” Xel qou malew selewa ti me talex wou e,
MAT 22:20 om Yesu teling xel, “Eti xe tenu tine? Me eti lei tine?”
MAT 22:21 Xel neil elox bei, “Sisa.” Woyom moxo neil wou xel bei, “Xam ghe bong vati wei Sisa xe yo ena wou Sisa, de vati wei Anutu xe yo ena wou Anutu.”
MAT 22:22 Xel ngo tine eno xel etek mouyo. Om xel la veil e me la.
MAT 22:23 Lek bouk kayon Sadyusiyeiw wei mi neil embei xel meyeing tyek se qandi lek, eno lam wou e is telinyeing ti.
MAT 22:24 Xel neil, “Putoung, Mose neil wou xa bei wangwei moux ti e mey de neu ema, ond e li moux e dii vexeiv on me bo li neuyeiw en e lei e se ma.
MAT 22:25 Woyom inyon xel lim yuw lindama toundei eivek xa senghoing. Xel lind ti tax o ii vex on me mey, de moxo se wong yak ti, om li nge wei nexlek eno ii li venei vexeiv on.
MAT 22:26 Sakwaing kayon eno li nge wei yuw me nge yal, me ela tei lek tiwei lim yuw eno teyeima.
MAT 22:27 De loxyus eno vex on mey.
MAT 22:28 Woyom lek bouk wei qandieing lek eno eivek xel lim yuw on eti venei? En inyon nambei xel xouing ii vex tiyon.”
MAT 22:29 Yesu neil elox, “Xam ghe neil esewok en inyon xam seng mi pyaw qayeeng wei di yeip eivek qapiya vambuing o me xam seng woulek Anutu xe nikanzek.
MAT 22:30 Gyeik bouk wei qandieing lek veil meyeing eno xomaxoneing tyek se diima o diima nox me noum. Tyek xel ghok ambei angelayeiw wei tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 22:31 Ekom qayeeng tiwei qandieing lek veil meyeing, eno beind xam seng pyaw vati wei Anutu neil wou xam bei,
MAT 22:32 ‘A ne Anutu wei Apraham xe yo, Anutu wei Isaka xe yo me Anutu wei Yakop xe yo.’ Moxo se Anutu wei meyeing o, qe Anutu wei mapieing o.”
MAT 22:33 Xel xomaxoneing qendu tiyon ngo tine, xel etek en e xe teyoxeing.
MAT 22:34 Xel Parisi ngo bei Yesu qateiv xel Sadyusi xe lukeing, om xel Parisiyeiw toung lekti.
MAT 22:35 Eivek xel senghoing eno tambiy ti, wei wo lupeyei en petieing, eno wo axeing wou Yesu en telinyeing tine,
MAT 22:36 “Putoung, qayeeng petieing tina inye ngandoung ghanaw veil eivek petieing?”
MAT 22:37 Yesu neil elox, “‘Xam laleimim devind Tambiy Ngandoung xam xe Anutu is xam laleimim dalus me is xam numim dalus me is xam lumimpeyei dalus.’ Petieing 6:5
MAT 22:38 Tine inye qayeeng petieing tiwei tax o me ngandoung ghanaw veil.
MAT 22:39 De nge yuw wei teyei lek eno nambei nye, ‘Wa laleim devind nimpapu nge nambei wa laleim mi vind xow o.’ Lumuki 19:18
MAT 22:40 Petieing dalus me qayeeng poropet dalus eno milek qayeeng petieing yuw ne.”
MAT 22:41 Ka xel Parisi di qekuma eno Yesu teling xel,
MAT 22:42 “Xam ghe wou naleimim ambei nya en Kilisi? Eti neu e?” Xel neil elox bei, “Dawit neu moux o.”
MAT 22:43 Moxo neil wou xel, “Woyom nambei nya Laweeng Vambuing wong kwa wou Dawit me moxo taxe e ‘Tambiy Ngandoung’? En moxo neil ambei nye,
MAT 22:44 “‘Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou a xe Tambiy Ngandoung, “Dei wou a memang payeiv deka a toung wa xe xel vevek eivek wa vaxam xeinghembi le.”’
MAT 22:45 Woyom wangwei Dawit a mi taxe e bei ‘Tambiy ngandoung,’ on nambei nya ekom e yon Dawit neu moux?”
MAT 22:46 Xelti se teyei bei neil qayeeng nge nox wou e, de lek bouk kayon me ela eno xelti se mi teling e no en lulti.
MAT 23:1 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel qendu ngandoung on is e xe xel betiyeing,
MAT 23:2 “Xel putoung wei petieing me xel Parisi eno mindei lek Mose xe sia.
MAT 23:3 Om xam a mi betiwou xel me ghe bong lul dalus wei xel neil wou xam o. Ekom xam seng bong vati wei xel wong o, en nambei xel se mi wong e teyei lek vati wei xel mi teyoxe yo.
MAT 23:4 Xel tup nimaying ngandoung me toung lek xel xomaxoneing on ghandiwek, ekom xel venaxow se teyei bei zeim lek angya memend deyis bei bong ena veil.
MAT 23:5 “Lul sapa wei xel mi wong en embei xel xomaxoneing gyei, me lek xel dambend me memend eno xel mi tup deneing wei xoulek o lek me e wo myasapa, me mi tup yis ding lek xel xe teimb ding myasepu.
MAT 23:6 Xel laleind mi vind bei na mi mendei mya eivek bouk wei mata ngandoung o me eivek xomek qekueing ama lalei.
MAT 23:7 Xel laleind mi vind bei moux alis vex a mi neil bendiyeing wou xel eivek beyeeng vateivek me na mi taxe e bei ‘Putoung.’
MAT 23:8 “Ekom xam eno xel se taxe xam ‘Putoung,’ en xam xe putoung tixemou tateis me xam dalus on limim ama.
MAT 23:9 De xam se taxe xelti lek tembuing bei ‘mang,’ en xam Mamim tixemou, me e toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 23:10 O xel ti se taxe xam ‘putoung,’ en xam xe putoung tixemou, inyon Kilisi.
MAT 23:11 Xam xe teiv eivek xam senghoing eno e mi mendei nambei xam xe xukxe.
MAT 23:12 En wangwei eti yeiw embei sanghoxe xow on tyek e lei detei eivek, de eti embei beoux xow on tyek e lei zekna.
MAT 23:13 “Xam putoung wei petieing me xam Parisiyeiw, xam ghe gwaleeng amim, xam wei myamim yuw o! Xam on ghe mi toung xomek mya wei tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu nei yo zeyi moux alis vex mend. Xam venaxow seng la eivek, me xam ghe mi nale zeyi xel wei di wong me yei en embei na eivek o.
MAT 23:14 [Xam putoung wei petieing me xam Parisiyeiw, xam ghe gwaleeng amim, xam wei myamim yuw o, en xam ghe mi wo nol wou xel vexeiv bend, me xam ghe mi tyoing lek me ghe mi zeimemam ding, nambei nyon tyek xam a qou myaveweeng ngandoung.]
MAT 23:15 “Xam putoung wei petieing me xam Parisiyeiw, xam ghe gwaleeng amim, xam wei myamim yuw o! Xam ghe mi ghavineeng lek tembuing me mamileeng being bong tambiy tixemou bo betiyeing wei xam o, me gyeik e wong ambei betiyeing ti, eno xam ghe mi wong moux on la eivek nilul ngandoung eno ghanaw veil eivek nenyex wei luta yo nambei xam venaxow.
MAT 23:16 “Xam wei matekeing ambei talex sakwaing wou xomaxoneing bamba eno xam ghe gwaleeng amim. Xam ghe mi neimbei, ‘Wangwei tambiy ti na neil zonghek is inyapunei lek xomek vambuing, ond inyon se byexaxoun qayeeng. Ekom wangwei e neil zonghek is inyapunei lek ghol wei xomek vambuing o, ond inyon byexaxoun qayeeng.’
MAT 23:17 Xam on bandol me mamim tekeing! Tina inye ngandoung, ghol o xomek vambuing wei wong ghol wo vambuing o?
MAT 23:18 Xam ghe mi neil is ambei nyon bei, ‘Wangwei xelti e neil zonghek lek qeind is inyapunei ond inyon se byexaxoun qayeeng, ekom wangwei xelti neil zonghek is inyapunei lei lek xound wei toundei lek qeind, ond inyon byexaxoun qayeeng.’
MAT 23:19 Xam moux wei mamim tekeing o. Tina inye ngandoung, xound o qeind wei wong xound on wo vambuing o?
MAT 23:20 Nambei inyon, tambiy tiwei neil zonghek is inyapunei lei lek qeind on neil zonghek is inyapunei lei lek lulul dalus wei toundei lek o.
MAT 23:21 Me tiwei mi neil zonghek is inyapunei lei lek xomek vambuing eno neil lek tiwei mindei eivek o.
MAT 23:22 Me eti neil zonghek is inyapunei lei lek tyoung gheyapu eno neil lek Anutu xe siaking me tiwei mindei lek o.
MAT 23:23 “Xam putoung wei petieing me Parisiyeiw, xam ghe gwaleeng amim, xam wei myamim yuw o! Xam ghe wong ti eivek xoumeeng wei lul senyeing wei xuk lalei. Ekom xam ghe saing qayeeng ngandoung dalus wei petieing o veil, nambei qayeeng bombek, lalei pyaweing me wongeingis. Xam betiwou qayeeng ngandoung wei petieing ne yo dom xam naleimim se ma petieing bamba.
MAT 23:24 Xam wei mamim tekeing wei ghe mi talex sakwaing! Xam ghe mi tiy mamayek veil xam xe louk, ekom xam ghe lep kamel.
MAT 23:25 “Xam putoung wei petieing me Parisiyeiw, xam ghe gwaleeng amim, xam wei myamim yuw o! Xam ghe mi sekweyexe mayamya me dipek demi, ekom eivek lalei eno pup en kwa eivekeing me ghe mi wou kwamim ngenong en lulul leimalei.
MAT 23:26 Xam Parisiyeiw wei mamim tekeing o! Myaxeeng eno xam sekweyexe mayamya me dipek lalei bole, dekakom demi embo vako is.
MAT 23:27 “Xam putoung wei petieing me Parisiyeiw, xam ghe gwaleeng amim, xam wei myamim yuw o! Xam on nambei leiveeng meyeing wei xel pelei pen teleing lek o, wei wo nimza maseim lek demi yo, ekom lalei yon pup en xel meyeing kanzek me lul dalus wei nilaxes o.
MAT 23:28 Xam is ambei nyon eivek sakwaing kayon, eno xel mi yei xam lek demi om xel embeik nge xam on bombek, ekom xam laleimim on pup en kwa wei tyonyeing me kwa wei pyaweing lek qayeeng o.
MAT 23:29 “Xam putoung wei petieing me Parisiyeiw, xam ghe gwaleeng amim, xam wei myamim yuw o! Xam ghe ev leiveeng meyeing en xel poropetyeiw me ghe vunekwou leiveeng wei xel bombek o.
MAT 23:30 Me xam ghe neil, ‘Wangwei xa mendei eivek bouk wei xa bumiyeiw, tyek xa se teyei bei devind xel me na nyeis xel poropet a mey.’
MAT 23:31 Om xam venaxow ghe talex lek xow bei xam on neumambu wei xel wei leis poropetyeiw mey o.
MAT 23:32 Woyom xam la wong sewokeing teyei lek ingwei bumyeiw mi wong o.
MAT 23:33 “Xam on myeiy me myeiy nilul neuyeiw xam! Tyek xam a pek veil myaveweeng wei nenyex luta yon nambei nya?
MAT 23:34 Nambei nyon tyek a bong xel poropetyeiw me xel wei lundpeyei nimza me xel putoung wei petieing o nak wou xam. Xel valu tyek xam ghe nyeis xel a mey dom na tuw valu lek xax pepeeng, de xel valu tyek xam ghe bo nol wou xel eivek xomek qekueing ama me na tiy xel na beyeeng nge me na nge.
MAT 23:35 Om nambei nyon, xel dalus bombek gyand wei xel leis xel mey lek tembuing eno tyek mendei lek xam, qandi eivek Abel wei bombek o tax me e na Belekia neu moux Sakalias, tiwei xam ghe leis e mey eivek xomek vambuing me qeind senghoing o.
MAT 23:36 A neil wou xam zonghek, lul nimaying dalus tine tyek nam lek xam qendu ti gweimbeeng ne dalus.
MAT 23:37 “O Yerusalem, Yerusalem, xam eti yeiw wei ghe mi leis xel poropetyeiw me ghe nex xel wei lak wou xam en qakous. Taxombouk eno ambei mi qeku xam neumimyeiw lekti, nambei qouklex mi qekuwou neuyeiw eivek banis xeinghembi yo, ekom xam laleimim se vind.
MAT 23:38 Wei, xam xe xomek tyek lelolexe me mendei bandaing.
MAT 23:39 En a neil wou xam bei, tyek xam seng nox gwei a no qe ka xam a neimbei, ‘Mata ena wou e tiwei lam eivek Tambiy Ngandoung lei yo.’ ”
MAT 24:1 Yesu la veil xomek vambuing on me la eno e xe xel betiyeing la wou e. En xel embei talex xomek nimzamza wei toungale is xomek vambuing o wou e.
MAT 24:2 Moxo neil, “Xam ghe wei lulti beimambei ne? A neil wou xam zonghek bei, tyek xel se teyei bei bong qakous nge mendei lek nge, qe tyek xel banex dalus deteina.”
MAT 24:3 Ka Yesu toundei lek lukendu Oliv, xel betiyeing venaxow lam wou e me teling. “Neil wou xa, gyeik inya tyek tine belup, me dee vati tyek nam a tax en ingwei wa being nam o me ingwei bouk na tip lek o?”
MAT 24:4 Yesu lewexe, “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow en kandek xelti se nam a tyoxe xam.
MAT 24:5 En tyek xel ngenong nam lek a leing, me na neimbei, ‘A Kilisi yo,’ me na tyoxe xomaxoneing ngenong.
MAT 24:6 Tyek xam a ngo vevek me qayeeng laweeng wei vevek o, ekom xam seng gwaleeng. Lulti beimambei ne tyek neing atyip, ekom bouk loxyus eno se ghei lam.
MAT 24:7 Tembuing nge tyek qandi me bo vevek is tembuing nge, me tete lalei nge tyek bo vevek is tete lalei nge. Inyon tyek maxep ngandoung me tyek tembuing api nanghei beyeeng danghei danghei nei.
MAT 24:8 Lul dalus ne inye myavanei nambei myaxeeng wei yak mi umbek o.
MAT 24:9 “Woyom tyek xel a zeimaxoun xam me bo nol wou xam de nyeis xam amey, me tembuing sapa tyek laleind bo nol wou xam en ay.
MAT 24:10 Lek bouk kayon xel ngenong tyek na toung demind wou xel xe wongeingis de tyek xel a dax ama vun me laleind bo nol wou ma,
MAT 24:11 me poropet tyonyeing ngenong tyek nam a tyip me na tyoxe xomaxoneing ngenong.
MAT 24:12 En kwa nilul on tyek bo ngandoung, de xel ngenong tyek na saing kwa wei lalei vineing o,
MAT 24:13 ekom eti yeiw wei nale nikanzek me ena bouk loxyus eno tyek Anutu devind xel veil meyeing.
MAT 24:14 De Xoulek Nimza tine en tete lalei eno tyek xel a neil e na eivek tembuing dalus en tembuing sapa na ngo, de woyom bouk loxyus eno tyek nam.
MAT 24:15 “Deka xam ghe gwei lul nilul ayang, wei mi wo nol wou lulul eno bale eivek beyeeng vambuing on nambei poropet Daniel neil en o.” Daniel 9:27 (Yon xam wei ghe mi pyaw qayeeng ne eno xam woulek e wo nimza.)
MAT 24:16 “Woyom eti yeiw wei mindei eivek Yudia eno xel a pek me na lek lukendu.
MAT 24:17 De wangwei tambiy ti toumendei lek xomek demi qetyei eno tyek se detei nox a qou lul valu eivek beeng lalei.
MAT 24:18 De tambiy ti toumendei eivek xuk eno se teyei bei nox me na qou e xe teimb ding nge.
MAT 24:19 Inyon tyek bo nilul ayang lek bouk tiyon en xel vex wei xeipouyek o me tayeiw wei di wo luul wou neu yo!
MAT 24:20 Xam a zeimemamim enok bouk wei pekeing eno qandi lek bouk wei nityuweing o lek bouk wei Sabat o.
MAT 24:21 En lek bouk tiyon nimaying ngandoung tyek nam. Myaxeeng wei tembuing qandi vako yo me elam tyip gweimbeeng ne, eno nimaying ambei nyon se lam tulek xomaxoneing, de loxyus eno nimaying ambei nye tyek se nox atyip no.
MAT 24:22 Wangwei Anutu se qateiv bouk tiyon bo sepi, yond tyek qetya xomaxoneing on veil, ekom wounalei en moux alis vex wei beyal om qateiv bouk wo sepi.
MAT 24:23 Lek bouk kayon eno wangwei xelti na neil wou wang bei, ‘Wei, Kilisi inye!’ o, ‘Moxo inyei!’ ond wang seng bongis qayeeng on.
MAT 24:24 En xomaxoneing tyonyeing valu tyek na neimbei a Kilisi o a poropet ti. Me tyek xel nam a tyip me bong dee me lulvako, wangwei xel teyei nei on tyek xel a tyoxe xomaxoneing wei Anutu beyal o.
MAT 24:25 Wei, a neil wou xam a tax en lul dalus tine wei tyek nam atyip o.
MAT 24:26 “Om wangwei xelti e neil wou xam, ‘Wei, moxo toundei eivek tembuing bandaing nei,’ yon xam seng na inyei, o ‘Moxo inye, toundei eivek xomek lalei nei,’ ond xam seng bongis.
MAT 24:27 En nambei kawei zivip mi nex mema lam anghei ninei is xeiyaing me byex la lek tembuing tambak nei me la xeinei, om tyek bong ambei nyon lek bouk wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei noum o.
MAT 24:28 Lek beyeeng wei meyeing mi yeip lek o, inyon xel tuw mi qeku lak inyon.
MAT 24:29 “Ka nimaying sapa tine na ma veil le, woyom lutika eno “‘sayeiv tyek bo mapetok, de dentouk tyek se teyeimbei tel, me betum tyek detei nanghei tyoung nei, de tyoung dalus tyek bo pimapi.’
MAT 24:30 “Lek bouk kayon dee wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek nam mendei yaingateiv eivek tyoung, me xel veleivlei dalus wei tembuing eno tyek deeng. De tyek xel gyei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux mendi nam lek laxap, is nikanzek me xeiyaing ngandoung.
MAT 24:31 Me moxo tyek bong e xe angelayeiw na is vukxax wei wo vya xoulekeing, me tyek xel qekuwou e xe xomaxoneing wei beyal o eivek tembuing sapa me ena tembuing myasepu dalus.
MAT 24:32 “Woyom xam a qou kwa wou xax basunghek. Gyeik xam ghe gwei bei xax mema wo nilouk me lis vako byex lek, xam ghe boulek bei bouk wei seiv embei siing eno lam paviy.
MAT 24:33 Nambei nyon om gyeik xam ghe gwei lul dalus ti beimambei ne, xam ghe boulek bei Xomaxoneing Neu lam paviy me toungale wou qapomb.
MAT 24:34 A neil wou xam zonghek bei, xel moux alis vex ti gweimbeeng ne tyek se mey qe ka lulti beimambei ne neing atyip le.
MAT 24:35 Tyoung gheyapu me tembuing tyek nati, ekom a xe qayeeng tyek se teyei bei nati.
MAT 24:36 “Xelti se woulek bouk o seivma wei Kilisi embei noum o, xel angela eivek tyoung gheyapu, o Neu moux se woulek, qe Ma venaxow.
MAT 24:37 Nambei ingwei eivek bouk wei Noaka yo, om tyek xel bong ambei kayon eivek bouk wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei noum o.
MAT 24:38 Myaxeeng lek bouk wei memiing se ghei butek o, xomaxoneing mi ya me num, me iima, me iima lox me loum, me la tyip wou bouk wei Noaka la eivek sip o.
MAT 24:39 Xel se woulek vati wei embei belup wou xel o dekakom memiing butek me qou xel dalus me la. Kwa kayon eno tyek bong ambei nyon lek bouk wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux noum o.
MAT 24:40 Moux yayuw toundei eivek xuk yaeing eno tyek Anutu na qou nge na veil de nge na toumendei.
MAT 24:41 Vex yayuw tyek mendi zouk wit, de tyek Anutu na qou nge de nge na toumendei.
MAT 24:42 “Nambei nyon xam ghe gweiteyei xow, en nambei xam seng woulek bouk vati wei xam xe Tambiy Ngandoung tyek nam o.
MAT 24:43 Ekom xam ghe bou naleimim bei, wangwei xomek ma boulek seivma vati wei xel panaxeing embei nam o, moxo tyek mendei bin e xe xomek en kandek xelti se dembu me na eivek.
MAT 24:44 Om xam is ambei nyon xam ghe gweiwou xow, en Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek nam lek seivma wei xam seng woulek bei tyek nam o.
MAT 24:45 “Woyom xukxe eti ingwei lupeyei nimza wei mi yeiteyei e xe xuk wo nimza nei? Wei e xe teiv toung e yeiteyei xel xukxe eivek e beeng bei e mi bong yaeing wou xel lek bouk wei teiv beyal o bombek?
MAT 24:46 Inyon nimza wou xukxe tiyon wei e xe teiv yei bei moxo mi wong xuk on gyeik e loum o.
MAT 24:47 A neil wou xam zonghek bei, teiv tyek na toung embo lei ngandoung en lul dalus eivek e beeng.
MAT 24:48 Ekom wangwei xukxe tiyon tambiy nilul ti om mi neil wou xow, ‘A xe teiv la toundei dingta takwei nei,’
MAT 24:49 woyom moxo la me leis e xe xel wei xel xouing mi wo xuk lekti yo, de mi ya me num is xel wei mi num me wo nol o.
MAT 24:50 Teiv wei xukxe tiyon tyek noum lek bouk wei xukxe se woulek me seivma wei se woulek o.
MAT 24:51 Teiv tyek bo myaveweeng ngandoung wou e me na toung e na is xel wei myend yuw o, nanghei inyon eno tyek xel deeng me xel newound bo nyiknyik.
MAT 25:1 “Lek bouk kayon eno tete lalei wei tyoung gheyapu eno tyek ghok ambei vexawo xoumeeng wei paleveeng eno qou xel xe lam me la bei na daxe moux wei embei dii vex o.
MAT 25:2 Xel lim eno loungeing de xel lim eno lundpeyei nimza.
MAT 25:3 Xel lim wei loungeing eno qou xel xe lam ekom xel se qou wel ti is.
MAT 25:4 De xel wei lundpeyei nimza eno xel qou wel eivek qakous botol is xel xe lam.
MAT 25:5 Tambiy wei embei dii vex eno se lam daing, om xel xouing mend yeip om xel yeip.
MAT 25:6 “Lek boukeing masenghoing eno xel ngo taxeing ti lam, ‘Wei, inye tambiy wei embei dii vex eno lam! Xam lam myayaing me la pelong e!’
MAT 25:7 “Woyom xel vexawo paleveeng tiyon dalus qandi lek me yeiwou xel xe lam.
MAT 25:8 Xel wei loungeing eno neil wou xel wei lundpeyei nimza yo, ‘Xam wong xam xe wel valu wou xa, en xa xe lam embei mey.’
MAT 25:9 “Xel neil elox bei, ‘Ma, wel ne se teyei xam me xa is. Embong ondek xam ghe na wou eti yeiw wei mi wo vateivek lek wel o, me ghe na bou valu wou venaxow.’
MAT 25:10 “Om ka vex lim on tupwou sakwaing bei na bou wel, tambiy wei embei dii vex eno lam tyip. Vexawo paleveeng wei yeiwou xow eno la lalei is e me la mata ngandoung wei iingama yo. Dom qepei qapomb lox zeyi.
MAT 25:11 “Kalekom vexawo lim wei loungeing on lam is ambei nyon me neil, ‘Teiv! Teiv! Tax qapomb veil xa!’
MAT 25:12 “Ekom moxo neil elox bei, ‘A neil zonghek wou xam bei a loung en xam.’
MAT 25:13 “Nambei nyon om xam ghe gweiteyei xow, en xam seng woulek bouk o seivma vati wei embei noum o.”
MAT 25:14 Yesu neil no, “Anutu xe tete lalei inye nambei tambiy ti embei na sakwaing anding, om moxo taxe e xe xel xukxe me toung lul dalus eivek xel memend bei xel a mi gyeiteyei.
MAT 25:15 Moxo wong malew 5,000 wou ti, de malew 2,000 wou nge de malew 1,000 wou nge teyei lek nikanzek wei xel titi yo. De woyom moxo la sakwaing anding.
MAT 25:16 Tambiy tiwei qou 5,000 eno la me wong xuk daing me qou malew valu is no teyei lek malew 5,000.
MAT 25:17 Om nambei nyon is, nge wei qou malew 2,000 eno wo xuk me qou 2,000 lek mapu.
MAT 25:18 Ekom tambiy tiwei qou malew 1,000 eno qou inyon dom la, de ev leiveeng eivek tembuing me vun e xe teiv xe malew eivek.
MAT 25:19 “Ka xel xe teiv la dei enden woy, om moxo loum wou xel xukxe om embei menyex wou malew wei toung is xel o.
MAT 25:20 Moux tiwei qou malew 5,000 eno qou 5,000 nge is me lam. Moxo neil, ‘Teiv, wang wong 5,000 wou ay. Wei, a qou malew 5,000 lek mapu is.’
MAT 25:21 “E xe teiv neil elox bei, ‘Nimzayang, wa xukxe nimza me wang mi wo xuk wo nimza! Wang mi weiteyei xuk wo nimza is lul nayaka. Om tyek a toung wang gweiteyei lul ngenong. Lam me wo xeimlala is wa xe teiv!’
MAT 25:22 “Moux wei qou malew 2,000 eno lam is ambei nyon. Moxo neil, ‘Teiv, wang wong malew 2,000 wou ay. Wei, a wo xuk me na qou 2,000 is no.’
MAT 25:23 “E xe teiv neil elox, ‘Nimzayang, wa xukxe nimza me wang wo xuk wo nimza! Wang mi weiteyei xuk wo nimza is lul nayaka. Om tyek a toung wang gweiteyei lul ngenong. Lam me wo xeimlala is wa xe teiv!’
MAT 25:24 “Woyom tambiy wei qou malew 1,000 eno lam. Moxo neil, ‘Teiv, a woulek woy bei wang on tambiy wei nimseikeing o, wang mi qou neing eivek xuk wei se wa memam xuk o, me ghe mi qekuwou vei wei wa seng vuw o.
MAT 25:25 Om a xaleeng me na la vun wa xe malew eivek tembuing. Wei, Inye vati wei wa xe yo.’
MAT 25:26 “E xe teiv neil elox bei, ‘Wa xukxe nilul wei qabonghapus o! Om wang woulek inyon bei a mi qou neing wei se a memang xuk o me na qekuwou vei wei a se vuw o?
MAT 25:27 Inyon nimza, wang teyei bei toung a xe malew eivek xomek wei malew o, en kandek gyeik ingwei ambei noum ond a na qou is ingwei xel toung valu lek mapu is o.
MAT 25:28 “‘Xam qou malew on veil e me wong e la wou tambiy wei qou malew 10,000 o.
MAT 25:29 En xel dalus wei qou lul valu woy eno tyek na qou valu lek mapu, en e qou lulul ngenong. Ek wangwei xelti xe lul nayaka ond tyek na zeim lul nayak kayon veil e.
MAT 25:30 Dom banex xukxe nilul on na myayaing eivek mapetok ngandoung. Nanghei inyon eno tyek na deeng de zanga newou bo nyiknyik.’
MAT 25:31 “Gyeik ingwei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei noum eivek e xe xeiyaing ngandoung, me xel angela dalus is e, eno tyek moxo mendei lek e xe siaking eivek xeiyaing ngandoung wei tyoung gheyapu nei.
MAT 25:32 Xel xomaxoneing dalus lek tembuing sapa tyek qeku nam wou e manghalus, de moxo tyek na pum xomaxoneing na yuw nambei gyovaxa mi pum sipsip veil xel meme yo.
MAT 25:33 Moxo tyek na toung sipsip na wou mema payeiv de xel meme na wou mema qeinz.
MAT 25:34 “Woyom king tyek na neil wou xel wei dei wou e mema payeiv o, ‘Xam tiwei Mang wong mata wou xam eno xam lam, xam a qou xam xe lul dalus eivek tete lalei wei menyex wou woy wou xam gyeik ingwei toung tembuing o.
MAT 25:35 En maxepya ay eno xam ghe wong yaeing valu me a xa. A kwang tip en memiing eno xam ghe wong me a num. A ne nambei xel amba ekom xam ghe qou ay me la eivek xomek lalei.
MAT 25:36 Teimb ma veil ay ekom xam ghe byex teimb lek ay. Vanei wong ay ekom xam ghe weiteyei ay. A la eivek xeitueing ekom xam ghe lam wei ay.’
MAT 25:37 “Woyom xel wei bombek eno tyek na neil e nox wou e, ‘Tambiy Ngandoung, gyeik inya xa xei maxepya wang me na vet wang, o wa kwam tip me xa wong numeing wou wang me wang num?
MAT 25:38 Gyeik inya xa xei wang on nambei xel amba om xa qou wang lam, o teimb ma veil wang om xa vunekwou wang?
MAT 25:39 Gyeik inya xa xei wang wo vanei o wang la eivek xeitueing me xa lak a xei wang?’
MAT 25:40 “King tyek na neil enoum, ‘A neil wou xam zonghek, vati wei xam ghe wong wou a lingyeiw ti beimambei ne ti wei lei maeing o, ond inyon xam ghe wong wou ay.’
MAT 25:41 “Woyom moxo tyek na neil wou xel wei dei wou e mema qeinz o, ‘Xam la veil ay, xam eti yeiw wei ghe dei eivek myaveweeng o, xam la eivek nenyex wei se mi mey yo wei xel menyexwou tambiy mapetok me e xe angelayeiw o.
MAT 25:42 En maxepya ay ekom xam seng wo lulti wou ay bei angha. A kwang tip, ekom xam seng wong lulti me a num.
MAT 25:43 A lam ambei xel amba, ekom xam seng qou a la eivek xomek. A teimb ma ekom xam seng byex teimb ti lek ay. Vanei wong ay me a la eivek xomek xeitueing ekom xam seng weiteyei ay.’
MAT 25:44 “Tyek xel a neil enox bei, ‘Tambiy Ngandoung, gyeik inya xa xei maxepya wang o wa kwam tip o wang lam ambei xel amba o teimb ma o vanei wong wang o wang toundei eivek xeitueing ekom xa se vind wang?’
MAT 25:45 “Moxo tyek na neil enox bei, ‘A neil wou xam zonghek, vati wei xam seng wong wou tiwei lei maeing en lulti beimambei ne, ond xam seng wong wou ay.’
MAT 25:46 “Woyom tyek xel na qou myaveweeng wei luta yo, dom xel wei bombek eno tyek na qou mapieing luta luta.”
MAT 26:1 Ka Yesu neil qayeeng ti beimambei yon ma woy, moxo neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei,
MAT 26:2 “Xam ghe woulek woy bei, bouk yayuw xemou nanghei di yeip zeyi Pasova, ingwei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek xel bong ena wou xel en xel a tuw e lek xax pepeeng o.”
MAT 26:3 Woyom xel lumuki leitata me xel teivateiv wei xel xomaxoneing qekuma eivek xomek wei lumuki lukanzek, wei lei Kaiapas o,
MAT 26:4 me xel di luk me yimexe sakwaing wei xel embei tyoxe me na zeimaxoun Yesu me nyeis e mey o.
MAT 26:5 Xel neil ambei nye, “Ekom se lek bouk wei mata ngandoung o, enok xel xomaxoneing on baluk ngenong de nyeis ama.”
MAT 26:6 Ka Yesu la Betani me la toundei eivek xomek wei tambiy ti lei Simon, wei takwei eno qou vanei lepa,
MAT 26:7 de vex ti lam wou e is botol qakous wei wel xeimangou wei malew ngandoung o, de vex on taw wel lek e lu gyeik moxo di yeip pepenyeing lek zek o.
MAT 26:8 Ekom xel betiyeing yei tine, eno xel laleind wou nilul, me neil, “Nambei nya vex ne wo nol wou wel ne?
MAT 26:9 Wel tine teyei bei xey a bo vateivek lek me na qou malew ngandoung me na bong wou xel kanyoyeiw o.”
MAT 26:10 Yesu woulek inye woy, om neil wou xel, “Nambei nya xam ghe wong nimaying wou vex ne? Vexo wong lul nimza tine wou ay.
MAT 26:11 Xel kanyoyeiw eno tyek na mi mendei is xam taxombouk, dom ay tyek a se mendei is xam taxombouk.
MAT 26:12 Vex ne taw wel lek aneing, om vexo wong inye bei menyex wou a neing en eveing eivek leiveeng meyeing.
MAT 26:13 A neil wou xam zonghek, eivek tembuing sapa wei xel embei na neil Xoulek Nimza nei eno tyek xel a mi neil vati wei vex ne wong ne, me tyek xel a mi bou naleind en e.”
MAT 26:14 Woyom xel xoumeeng yuw on ti lei Yudas Iskariot la wou xel lumuki leitata
MAT 26:15 me teling, “Xam ambei tyek ghe bong vati wou ay wangwei am bong e nak wou xam nei?” Om xel pyaw memend wou malew teyei lek silva xoumeeng yal (30) wou e.
MAT 26:16 Woyom nanghei inyon me ela eno Yudas di yimexe sakwaing wei embei bong Yesu na eivek xel memend o.
MAT 26:17 Lek bouk atax wei Bouk Wei Yaeing Belet Wei Yis Ma Veil o, xel betiyeing lam wou Yesu me teling, “Wambei xa na menyex wou yaeing anghei inya en kandek wang gwa Pasova?”
MAT 26:18 Moxo neil elox, “La eivek beyeeng ngandoung on me ghe na wou tambiy tinei me na neil wou e, ‘Putoung neil embei: A xe bouk wei xel beyal eno paviy. Ay is a xe xel betiyeing bei nak angha Pasova eivek wa bam.’ ”
MAT 26:19 Om xel betiyeing wong ambei kawei Yesu neil wou xel o me menyex wou Pasova.
MAT 26:20 Gyeik ingwei di souk, eno Yesu la dei lek lelek is xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw.
MAT 26:21 Ka xel di ya, moxo neil, “A neil wou xam zonghek bei, xam on ti tyek na neil a teyei me na toung ay eivek xel vevek amba memend.”
MAT 26:22 Xel laleind wo nimaying me xel titi di neil wou e bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, Beip se ay?”
MAT 26:23 Yesu neil elox bei, “Tiwei embei toung mema eivek dipek is ay eno tyek na neil a teyei me na toung a na eivek xel vevek amba memend.
MAT 26:24 Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek na nambei kawei xel byex eivek xoulek en e yo. Ekom nimaying ena wou moux tiwei embei neil Xomaxoneing Neu Moux teyei, dom na toung e na eivek xel ba memend! Inye nimza, bei tambiy tiyon ta se bou e.”
MAT 26:25 Woyom Yudas tambiy tiwei embei neil e teyei me na toung e na eivek xel ba memend o neil, “Putoung, neing ayang beip se ay?” Yesu lewexe, “Nambei wang neil on.”
MAT 26:26 Ka xel di ya, Yesu qou belet, de wong dange wou me dembu, de wong wou e xe xel betiyeing, de neil, “Xam qou me wa. Tine inye a neing.”
MAT 26:27 Woyom moxo qou mayamya, me wong dange wou dom wong wou xel de neil, “Xam dalus a num eivek.
MAT 26:28 Tine inye a gyand wei qokatu yo, en a qapyex lek xel ngenong bei e mi semaleeng sewokeing sapa.
MAT 26:29 A neil wou xam, tyek a se nox me na num wain tine no me e mi na deka bouk tiyon tyek a num wain vako is xam eivek Mang xe tete lalei.”
MAT 26:30 Woyom xel wong lalo ti, de xel la myayaing me la lukendu Oliv.
MAT 26:31 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel, “Boukeing kane tyek xam xe wongeingis detei, en xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, “‘Tyek a nyeis tambiy wei mi yeiteyei sipsip o, dom xel sipsip na pek me davuna.’
MAT 26:32 Ekom tyek a qandi lek me na tax en xam me nana eivek Galili.”
MAT 26:33 Petele neil elox bei, “Wangwei xel betiyeing dalus a saing xel xe wongeingis en wang, ond tyek a se teyei bei saing wang.”
MAT 26:34 Yesu neil elox wou e bei, “A neil wou wang zonghek, boukeing kane, wei qouklex seng ghe sesa vya, tyek wang dax a vun luyal.”
MAT 26:35 Ekom Petele neil embei, “Wangwei a mey is wang, ond a se teyei bei dax wang vund.” Me xel betiyeing dalus neil qayeeng kayon teyeima.
MAT 26:36 Woyom Yesu la is e xe xel betiyeing me xel la beyeeng ti lei Getsemani, me moxo neil wou xel, “Xam a toumendei inye nayaka le, dom a na inyei me na zeimemang bole.”
MAT 26:37 Moxo qou Petele me Sebedi neu moux luw xouing is e. Moxo lalei wo nimaying me axe nilul ayang.
MAT 26:38 Moxo neil wou lal, “A nung axe nimaying ngandoung om am bim a mey. Xam a toumendei inye me ghe gweiteyei is ay.”
MAT 26:39 Moxo dula nayaka, de yeip ma eivek tembuing me zeimema, “Mang, wangwei nambei nyon nei, ond teyei bei wa zeim mayamya tine veil ay. Ekom wa se betiwou a xe woueing nalei, qe wa betiwou wamaxow xe woueing nalei.”
MAT 26:40 Woyom moxo loumelam wou betiyeing yal on me yei lal di yeip o. Moxo teling Petele, “Se teyei bei mal mendi gweiteyei is ay teyei lek seivma ti?
MAT 26:41 Xam a mi gweiteyei me na zeimemamim en kandek xam se detei eivek axeing. Laweeng lalei vind bei bong xuk, ekom neing mi wong nimbayaing.”
MAT 26:42 Moxo lox me la luyuw no me zeimema, “Mang, wangwei mayamya tine se teyei bei ghanaw ay me a num, ond wa betiwou wamaxow laleim.”
MAT 26:43 Ka moxo loumelam, moxo yei lal di yeip no, en nambei lal mend yeip.
MAT 26:44 Om moxo ghanaw xel me lox tiwei yal o no me zeimema, me neil ambei kawei yo no.
MAT 26:45 Woyom moxo loum wou e xe betiyeing me neil wou lal, “Xam anghei dei weip me ghe qou laweeng? Wei, seivma lam paviy, me gweimbeeng xel neil Xomaxoneing Neu Moux teyei me toung e la eivek xel wei sewokeing o memend.
MAT 26:46 Qandi lek, en xey a na! En inye tambiy wei embei neil a teyei me na toung a na eivek xel memend eno lam!”
MAT 26:47 Ka moxo nanghei di luk, Yudas, tambiy tiyon eivek xel xoumeeng yuw eno lam tyip. Xel qendu ngandoung lam is e eno xel qou ngeyeing vevek me pebumeeng. Xel lumuki leitata me xel teivateiv wei xomaxoneing eno wong xel lam.
MAT 26:48 Tambiy wei embei neil Yesu teyei me na toung e na eivek xel ba memend eno wong dee ti bei xel boulek: “Tiwei tyek a toung myang lek e ling ond moux tiyo inyon, om xam a zeimaxoun e.”
MAT 26:49 Lutika eno Yudas lam wou Yesu me neil, “Boukeing Putoung!” dom toung mya lek e ling.
MAT 26:50 Yesu neil elox bei, “Gweleeng, wang bong vati wei wang lam en o.” Woyom xel moux on dulam paviy me zeimaxoun e.
MAT 26:51 Ekom Yesu xe xelti mema la en e xe ngeyeing vevek, de tetei elam dom qateiv xukxe wei lumuki lukanzek on nenyalis tip veil.
MAT 26:52 Yesu neil wou e, “Toung wa xe ngeyeing vevek on lox eivek beeng, en xel eti yeiw wei puw ngeyeing vevek tyek na mey angya ngeyeing vevek.
MAT 26:53 Xam ghe wou naleimim bei tyek a se teyei bei taxe Mang, me lutika eno moxo tyek bong xel angela ngenong ghanaw xel qendu xoumeeng yuw wei vevek o me nam devind ay?
MAT 26:54 Ekom wangwei a bong ambei nyon on qayeeng wei di yeip eivek Anutu xe qapiya vambuing ne tyek se bo neing lek. En Anutu xe qapiya neil embei, lul dalus tine eno e nam belup wou ay.”
MAT 26:55 Lek seivma kayon eno Yesu neil wou xel qendu yon, “Beip a ne tambiy panaxeing me leiseing xel o, om xam ghe lam is ngeyeing aluw pebumeeng bei bo nol wou ay me na zeimaxoun ay? Bouk tambak ne a mindei eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing me na mi teyoxe xel, ekom xam seng zeimaxoun ay.
MAT 26:56 Ekom tine dalus lam tyip nambei ingwei xel poropet byex eivek qapiya yo embo neing lek.” Woyom xel betiyeing dalus pek veil e me la.
MAT 26:57 Woyom xel moux wei zeimaxoun Yesu eno qou moxo me la wou lumuki lukanzek Kaiapas. Inyon xel putoung wei petieing me xel teivateiv wei di qekuma yo.
MAT 26:58 Ekom Petele di betiwou e me la kwanding ka veil e. Moxo la eivek tete lalei wei lumuki lukanzek beeng o. Ka la dei inyon is xel belimbo, bei gyei vati wei embei belup wou Yesu yo.
MAT 26:59 Xel lumuki leitata me xel kanzol dalus di yimexe qayeeng tyonyeing wei xel embei neil lek Yesu en kandek xel na nyeis e mey en o.
MAT 26:60 Ekom xel se yeiwou qayeeng ti, de xel ngenong lam neil qayeeng ekom ma. Dekalekom moux yayuw lam
MAT 26:61 me neil embei, “Tambiy tine neil ambei nye, ‘A teyei bei lelolexe Anutu xe xomek vambuing de na nox me na dev eivek bouk yal.’ ”
MAT 26:62 Woyom lumuki lukanzek nale ghey me neil wou Yesu, “Se teyei bei wa neil qayeeng ti noum? Inye qayeeng vati ingwei xel di neil lek wang ne?”
MAT 26:63 Ekom Yesu nanghei toungale kanzek. Om lumuki lukanzek neil wou e, “A teling wou wang eivek Anutu mapieing lei, Neil wou xa wangwei wa Kilisi, Anutu Neu Moux nei.”
MAT 26:64 Yesu neil elox bei, “Ee, nambei kawei wang neil on. Ekom a neil wou xam dalus, kalekom tyek xam ghe gwei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux mendei wou mema payeiv wei Anutu tiwei Nikanzekta me di lam lek laxap wei tyoung gheyapu yo.”
MAT 26:65 Woyom lumuki lukanzek lex e xe teimb de neil, “Moxo lukyak lek Anutu yo! Nambei nya xey a ngo qayeeng valu is no? Wei, xam venaxow ghe ngo qayeeng lukeingyak wei e neil o.
MAT 26:66 Xam ghe wou naleimim ambei nya?” Xel neil elox bei, “Moxo teyei bei mey o.”
MAT 26:67 Woyom xel pesuv myend louk lek e manghalus me lund memend de venoux e, de xel valu petapexe e
MAT 26:68 me neil, “Kilisi, wa neil qayeeng poropet wou xa. Eti leis wang?”
MAT 26:69 Petele moxo toundei myayaing eivek tete lalei wei xomek o. Xukxe vexawo ti lam wou e me neil, “Wang is en wang mindei is Yesu wei Galili yo.”
MAT 26:70 Ekom moxo axvun eivek xel dalus mend. E neil elox bei, “A loung en vati wei xam ghe di luk en o.”
MAT 26:71 Woyom moxo la myayaing wei tete mya nei. Inyon vexawo nge yei e me neil wou xel xomaxoneing nanghei inyon, “Tambiy tine mi la is Yesu wei Nasaret o.”
MAT 26:72 Petele lox me la axvun no me neil zonghek is inyapunei bei, “A loung en moux tiyon!”
MAT 26:73 Kalekom xel wei toungale inyon eno la wou Petele me neil, “Neing ayang wang on xel xe ti, en xa woulek wa vyam wei wang di luk on.”
MAT 26:74 Woyom moxo neil vya lek xow me luk ninkanzek, “A neil neing wou xam bei, a loung en tambiy tiyon!” Se denlek en qouklex sesa vya.
MAT 26:75 Woyom Petele wou kwa en qayeeng wei Yesu neil o, “Qouklex se ghei sesa vya, eno tyek wang dax a vun luyal.” De moxo la myayaing me la eng ngandoungateiv mouyo.
MAT 27:1 Satiboukeing lulayang, eno xel lumuki leitata dalus me xel teivateiv wei xel xomaxoneing eno lam me di luklek qayeeng bei nyeis Yesu e mey.
MAT 27:2 Xel tup e, de qou e me la wou eivek Pailat mema, lei ngandoung wei seyap o.
MAT 27:3 Yudas tiwei neil Yesu teyei me toung e la eivek xel vevek memend o, yei bei xel byex qayeeng lek Yesu woy bei nyeis e mey, om moxo kwa pakou no me qou malew selewa xoumeeng yal (30) wei xel lumuki leitata me xel teivateiv wong wou e yo me lox wong elox wou xel.
MAT 27:4 Moxo neil, “A wo sewokeing, en a neil tambiy wei nilul ma veil e yo teyei me na toung e lak eivek xam memamim.” Xel neil elox bei, “Inyon se dei yeip wou xa ti. Qe inyon di yeip wou wamaxow o.”
MAT 27:5 Om Yudas nex malew lox eivek xomek vambuing lalei dom la. Woyom Yudas venaxow la qo kwa me mey.
MAT 27:6 Xel lumuki leitata zeim malew lek me neil, “Inye se la teyei lek qayeeng petieing bei xey a toung malew tine na eivek deng xeikatu wei xomek vambuing yo, en inye malew wei qapyex gyand o.”
MAT 27:7 Om xel luk wouma me tup qayeeng bei dexouv tembuing wei xel wei mi betiy dengmuing o en malew tiyon en leiveeng meyeing wei xel amba yo.
MAT 27:8 Om qes ambei nyon xel mi taxe Tembuing on Gyand me elam tyip gweimbeeng ne is.
MAT 27:9 Woyom lul tine la teyei lek lulti Anutu neil eivek poropet Yelemia mya yo. “Xel qou malew selewa xoumeeng yal (30) on teyei lek ambei xouveing wei xel xomaxoneing wei Israel beyal bei dexouv tambiy tiyon o,
MAT 27:10 me xel xouv tembuing wei xel wei mi betiy dengmuing en o ti, nambei Tambiy Ngandoung peti wou ay yo.”
MAT 27:11 Dekale Yesu nale wou lei ngandoung wei seyap o ma, me moxo teling e, “Beip wang on king wei Yudayeiw o?” Yesu neil elox bei, “Nambei wang neil on.”
MAT 27:12 De woyom xel lumuki leitata me teivateiv byex qayeeng lek Yesu, moxo se neil qayeeng ti lox wou xel.
MAT 27:13 Woyom Pailat teling e, “Beip inye wa seng ngo pavulek wei xel di luk en wang ne?”
MAT 27:14 Ekom Yesu se neil lulti lox, de se neil lulti lek qayeeng wei xel byex lek e yon, om tine wong lei ngandoung wei seyap o wounalei ngenong.
MAT 27:15 Lei ngandoung wei seyap o xe kwa wei mi betiwou lek bouk wei Pasova eno mi tul xeitueing ti la teyei lek xel moux alis vex mi beyal o laleind.
MAT 27:16 Lek bouk kayon eno tambiy nilul ayang ti lei Barabas eno toundei eivek xeitueing.
MAT 27:17 Om xel qendu yon qekuma, Pailat teling xel, “Luw nge na xam ambei a bong e nak wou xam, Barabas o Yesu wei xel mi taxe bei Kilisi yo?”
MAT 27:18 En moxo woulek bei xel venaxow xe laleind nilul, om xel qou Yesu me wong wou e.
MAT 27:19 Ka Pailat toundei lek sia wei ngoeing qayeeng o, moxo venei wong qayeeng tine lam wou e: “Kandek wa seng bong lulti lek moux wei bombek o, en inye a axe nimaying ngandoung ti gweimbeeng eivek maviing en e.”
MAT 27:20 Ekom xel lumuki leitata me xel teivateiv zeim xel qendu ngandoung on laleind lek bei e bong Barabas na wou xel dom nyeis Yesu e mey.
MAT 27:21 Lei ngandoung wei seyap o teling, “Xam ambei a bong luw nge na, nak wou xam?” Xel lewexe bei, “Barabas.”
MAT 27:22 Pailat teling, “De tyek a bong vati wou Yesu tiwei xel taxe bei Kilisi ne?” Xel dalus lewexe bei, “Tuw e lek xax pepeeng!”
MAT 27:23 Pailat teling, “En va? E wong sewokeing vati?” Ekom xel taxe lox wou e niseikeing bei, “Tuw e lek xax pepeeng!”
MAT 27:24 Pailat woulek bei tyek xel se ngo e vya, de inyon vevek ngandoung embei qandi lek, om moxo qou memiing me sekweyexe mema eivek xel qendu ngandoung on dalus mend. Moxo neil, “Inye se sewokeing wei ay yo en moux tine gyand. Qe inye di yeip wou xam venaxow!”
MAT 27:25 Xomaxoneing dalus lewexe, “Wong e xe gyand on lam lek xa me lek xa neumiyeiw!”
MAT 27:26 Woyom moxo wong Barabas la wou xel. Dom neil wou xel vevekyeiw on bei xel sesa Yesu nangya yisviyeing, dekakom wong e la me xel tuw lek xax pepeeng.
MAT 27:27 Woyom xel vevek wei lei ngandoung wei seyap o qou Yesu me la lalei eivek xomek seyap me qeku xel dalusateiv wei vevekyeiw o nale vivekwou e.
MAT 27:28 Xel kwax e xe teimb veil dom byex teimb ding gyand nge lek e no,
MAT 27:29 de xel bembinexe yis wei ying o lekti nambei qelumking de toung lek e lu. Xel toung xax nayak ti eivek e mema payeiv de dundek wou e ma me luk seloukeing lek e. Me neil, “Bendiyeing, king wei xel Yudayeiw o!”
MAT 27:30 De xel pesuv myend louk lek e, de xel qou e xe patongeeng me sesa e lu gya lumama.
MAT 27:31 Ka xel luk seloukeing lek e woy, xel kwax teimb wei xel byex lek e eno veil dom byex e maxow xe teimb lek no. Woyom xel qou e me la bei na tuw e lek xax pepeeng.
MAT 27:32 Xel di tupwou sakwaing me la, eno xel la tyip wou tambiy wei Sairini yo ti, lei Simon, om xel tendu bei moxo e qalei xax pepeeng.
MAT 27:33 Xel lam tyip wou beyeeng tiwei xel mi taxe bei Golgata (E qes ambei nye bei Beyeeng wei Lukanzek o).
MAT 27:34 Nanghei inyon eno xel wong wain wei xel maleeng is lul senyeing o wou Yesu bei e num. Moxo num me axe le, ekom se num.
MAT 27:35 Ka xel tuw e lek xax pepeeng woy, woyom xel nex qakous dee bei dembu e xe teimb wouma.
MAT 27:36 Xel dei tembuing, me di yei e teyei nanghei inyon.
MAT 27:37 Louk apu en e lu eno xel tuw qayeeng vati wei xel wong qayeeng en e yo bei: TINE INYE YESU, KING WEI YUDAYEIW O.
MAT 27:38 Tambiy panaxeing yayuw eno xel tuw luw is e, nge wou e mema payeiv, de nge wou e mema qeinz.
MAT 27:39 Eti yeiw wei di lam me la eno lukyak lek e, me bimexe lund
MAT 27:40 me neil, “Wa kawei wang neimbei tyek lelolexe xomek vambuing dom ghe dev vako eivek bouk yal o inyon, om vind xow! Wangwei wa Anutu Neu Moux nei, tei lam veil xax pepeeng!”
MAT 27:41 Eivek kwa kayon teyeima eno xel lumuki leitata me xel putoung wei petieing me xel teivateiv lukyak lek e.
MAT 27:42 Xel neil, “Moxo vind xel bamba, ekom se teyei bei devind venaxow! Wangwei e king wei xel Israel o, yon e detei nam veil xax pepeeng en kandek xey a bongis e.
MAT 27:43 Moxo mi wongis Anutu. Om wangwei Anutu lalei devind e nei yon e devind moxo, en mi neil embei, ‘A ne Anutu Neu Moux.’ ”
MAT 27:44 Eivek sakwaing ambei nyon eno panaxeing yuw wei xel tuw is e eno lukyak lek e is.
MAT 27:45 Lek ingwei seivma evlek me e la seivma yal wei soukeing eno mapetok ngandoung sevunexe tembuing tambak on.
MAT 27:46 Me embim seivma yal eno Yesu taxe niseikeing bei, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?” Qes ambei nye bei, “A xe Anutu, a xe Anutu, nambei nya wang saing ay?”
MAT 27:47 Woyom xel valu wei toungale inyon ngo tine, om xel neil embei, “Moxo taxe Eliya yo.”
MAT 27:48 Lutika eno xel xe ti veimya me la qou balam. Moxo toung eivek wain senyeing me e pup, de tup lek xax mema nayak ti, dom zeim e la wou Yesu mya bei e num.
MAT 27:49 Xel valu neil embei, “Wong xey a axe le bei, Eliya nam devind e.”
MAT 27:50 Ekom Yesu nyayek niseikeing no, de wong e xe nulaweeng la dom mey.
MAT 27:51 Lek kayon bombek eno qaeing ngandoung wei mii eivek xomek vambuing lalei eno lexla yayuw anghei pu me ela nge xo. De tembuing pi me wong qakous on dembu.
MAT 27:52 Leiveeng meyeing ngenong mya tax de xel vambuing ngenong wei mey eno neing qandi lek mapieing.
MAT 27:53 Xel lam myayaing veil leiveeng meyeing, deka Yesu qandi lek woy eno xel la eivek beyeeng vambuing Yerusalem me tyip wou xel xomaxoneing ngenong.
MAT 27:54 Lei ngandoung wei vevek o is xel vevekyeiw toukale inyon is e me yei Yesu teyei eno yei tembuing pi me lul dalus tiwei qandi yon, om xel yaleeng, me neil, “Neing ayang tambiy tine inye Anutu Neu Moux!”
MAT 27:55 Xel vex ngenong toukale kwanding, me di yei. Xel on ingwei mi betiwou Yesu nanghei Galili bei na devind e.
MAT 27:56 Eivek vex vex on senghoing, inyon Maria wei Makdala me Maria wei Jems aluw Joses tend, me Sebedi neu luw tend.
MAT 27:57 Ka moxo di souk, tambiy wei lulul ana eno lam anghei Arimatia, e lei Yosep. Moxo yon betiyeing wei Yesu yo ti.
MAT 27:58 La wou Pailat, me teling wou en Yesu neing, om Pailat lewexe lek bei vevekyeiw bong Yesu neing na wou Yosep me e qou me na.
MAT 27:59 Yosep qou neing on me beliv eivek qaeing teleing vako ti,
MAT 27:60 me liw eivek e maxow xe leiveeng meyeing vako wei xel qateiv eivek qakous o. Dom moxo wilexe qakous ngandoung ti la zeyi leiveeng meyeing mya de la.
MAT 27:61 Maria wei Makdala luw Maria nge eno toundei inyon paviy leiveeng meyeing.
MAT 27:62 Bouk wei Yudayeiw mi menyex wou lulul wei yaing eno lak veil, de bouk Sabat eno xel lumuki leitata me Parisiyeiw la wou Pailat.
MAT 27:63 Xel neil wou e bei, “Teiv, xa wou naleimi en tambiy tiwei tyonyeing on wei nanghei toundei mapieing eno neil, ‘Ka bouk yal nak veil on tyek a qandi lek no.’
MAT 27:64 Om wang bo qayeeng nikanzek en xel a toung leiveeng on mya zeyi embo nikanzek me ena tyip wou bouk yal. Enok e xe xel betiyeing nam me panax e neing dom na neil wou xel xomaxoneing bei moxo qandi lek veil meyeing. Tyonyeing tiwei yus ne tyek ghanaw tyonyeing wei wong a tax o.”
MAT 27:65 Pailat neil embei, “Xam a qou xel belimbo wei mi yeiteyei leiveeng meyeing mya yo ti. La wong leiveeng mya yon wo nikanzek nambei xam ghe wou naleimim en o.”
MAT 27:66 Om xel la lax leiveeng mya zeyi me toung newiy lek qakous dom wong xel belimbo la nale zeyi.
MAT 28:1 Ka bouk wei Sabat eno la veil, me di wong en embei boyaing lek bouk ti myaxeeng wei sounda qes tiyon o, Maria wei Makdala is Maria nge la en embei na gyei leiveeng meyeing.
MAT 28:2 Woyom lutika eno tembuing pi ngandoung, en nambei Anutu xe angela lep me lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei, me la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei, me wilexe qakous la nale nenya dom dei lek.
MAT 28:3 E ma yon siing ambei zivip, me e xe teimb on teltyip ambei laxap.
MAT 28:4 Xel belimbo yon yaleeng en e, me etek niseikeing de pewilexe la yeip lek tembuing ambei xel meyeing.
MAT 28:5 Ekom angela neil wou vex yuw on, “Muw seng gwaleeng, en a woulek bei muw ghe di wimexe Yesu, wei xel tuw lek xax pepeeng o.
MAT 28:6 Moxo se toundei inye, en moxo qandi lek, nambei kawei neil o. Muw lam wei nimbeeng kawei yeip lek o.
MAT 28:7 Muw ghe na daing me ghe na neil wou e xe xel betiyeing, ‘Tambiy moxo qandi lek veil meyeing me la tax en xam me la Galili. Tyek xam ghe na gwei e nanghei inyei.’ Wei, a lam en ambei nam a neil wou xam.”
MAT 28:8 Om xel vex on tup me la nanghei ingwei leiveeng nei. Luw yaleeng ekom luw wo xeindlala mouyo, me veimyend bei na neil wou e xe xel betiyeing.
MAT 28:9 Se denlek en Yesu la tyip wou luw. Moxo neil, “Satiboukeing.” Luw lam wou me axlek e vaxa dom wo lalo wou e.
MAT 28:10 Woyom Yesu neil wou luw, “Muw seng gwaleeng. Muw la neil wou a lingyeiw bei xel na Galili, de tyek xel gyei ay anghei inyei.”
MAT 28:11 Ka vex yuw on di la wou sakwaing, xel belimbo yon valu la eivek beyeeng ngandoung me la neil qayeeng on wou xel lumuki leitata en lul dalus wei belup on.
MAT 28:12 Xel lumuki leitata is xel teivateiv qekuma me neil qayeeng ti. Xel wong malew ngandoung wou xel vevekyeiw,
MAT 28:13 me neil wou xel, “Xam a neil ambei nye bei, ‘Gyeik ingwei xa xeip eno moxo xe xel betiyeing lam eivek boukeing me panax e neing de qou me la.’
MAT 28:14 Wangwei qayeeng tine na wou lei ngandoung wei seyap o, tyek xa menyex wou qayeeng is e, en kandek xam seng na eivek nimaying.”
MAT 28:15 Om xel vevekyeiw qou malew on me wong ambei kawei neil wou xel o. De pavulek tine eno xel Yudayeiw mi neil e lala eivek ama senghoing me e lam tyip bouk ti gweimbeeng ne.
MAT 28:16 Woyom xel betiyeing xoumeeng ti la Galili, me la lukendu tiwei Yesu neil wou xel bei xel na yo.
MAT 28:17 Gyeik xel yei e, eno xel wong lalo wou e, ekom xel valu laleind wo yuw.
MAT 28:18 Woyom Yesu lam wou xel me neil, “Lei wei ngandoung dalus eivek tyoung gheyapu me lek tembuing eno Anutu wong wou ay.
MAT 28:19 Nambei nyon xam ghe na bong xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa ne bong ambei a xe betiyeing, me ghe zipek xel eivek Mang lei me Neu lei me Laweeng Vambuing lei,
MAT 28:20 me teyoxe xel bei xel bongis lul tambak tiwei a mi peti wou xam o. Wei, inye neing ayang, a mindei is xam teyei lek bouk sapa ne, me tyek a mi mendei is xam me ena tyip wou bouk wei la tip lek o.”
MAR 1:1 Inye Xoulek Nimza wei myaxeeng en Yesu Kilisi, Anutu Neu Moux o eno nambei,
MAR 1:2 Poropet Yesaya byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, “Wei! Tyek a bong a xe nenyalesana ti natax en wang, me tyek e menyex wou wa xe sakwaing.”
MAR 1:3 “Vya taxeing ti lam anghei myayaing wei tembuing bandaing nei, ‘Menyex wou sakwaing en Tambiy Ngandoung, me wong sakwaing e wo bombek en e.’ ”
MAR 1:4 Om Yoan Lipekeing lam lipek xel eivek tembuing bandaing me neil xoulek bei xel pekwi xow en Anutu e semaleeng xel xe sewokeing veil en talex lek bei xel pekwi xow.
MAR 1:5 Me danghei wei Yudia nei eno xel dalus is xel dalus wei Yerusalem eno la wou e me neil xel xe sewokeing teyei. De Yoan lipek xel eivek memiing Yorodan.
MAR 1:6 Yoan mi byex teimb wei xel menyex wou en kamel nivlus o me vex let wei leliy ninavi yo vivekwou xeikatu. Me mi ya zevak me beyexta nilouk wei qeis lalei yo.
MAR 1:7 De inye e xe xoulek, “Tambiy ti tyek nam yus en ay eno e xe nikanzek ghanaw ay. A se teyeimbei dundek me na tul yis wei e xe vaxalambes.
MAR 1:8 A lipek xam en memiing, ekom moxo tyek zipek xam en Laweeng Vambuing.”
MAR 1:9 Lek bouk tiyon Yoan di lipek xel eno Yesu lam anghei Nasaret wei Galili nei me Yoan lipek e eivek memiing Yorodan.
MAR 1:10 Ka Yesu leklam veil memiing woyom moxo yei tyoung dembu me tax, me Laweeng Vambuing lep me lam lek e nambei menek beliy ti.
MAR 1:11 De vya ti lam anghei tyoung gheyapu me neil, “Wang on a Neung, wei a laleing vind o. A laleing wo nimza wou wang.”
MAR 1:12 Se denlek en Laweeng Vambuing wong Yesu la eivek tembuing bandaing,
MAR 1:13 me Yesu la mindei eivek tembuing bandaing on teyei lek bouk xoumeeng vey (40), me Sandang wo axeing wou e. Moxo mindei is leliy leliy bemeeng de angelayeiw mi vind e.
MAR 1:14 Ka xel toung Yoan eivek xeitueing, woyom Yesu la eivek Galili, me neil Xoulek Nimza wei Anutu xe yo.
MAR 1:15 E neil, “Bouk wei Anutu neil atax eno wo neing lek. Me Anutu xe tete lalei lam paviy. Om xam pekwi xow me ghe bongis Xoulek Nimza!”
MAR 1:16 Ka Yesu di tupwou lounyeing Galili vi, moxo yei Simon me li Andrias. Luw di nex lewek eivek lounyeing, en luw mi wong xuk wei qoueing woing o.
MAR 1:17 Yesu neil, “Muw betiwou ay, me tyek a bong muw ghe bo xuk wei qoueing xomaxoneing o.”
MAR 1:18 Lutika eno luw ghanaw luw xe lewek dom betiwou e.
MAR 1:19 Gyeik Yesu dula nayaka eno yei Sebedi neu moux Jems me li Yoan toundei eivek bot me di senzi luw xe lewek.
MAR 1:20 Moxo taxe luw lutika me luw ghanaw ma Sebedi eivek bot is e xe xukxe wei xouveing o dom betiwou e.
MAR 1:21 Xel la tyip Kapenaom, me gyeik bouk wei Sabat o lam eno Yesu la eivek xomek qekueing ama me di teyoxe xoulek wou xel.
MAR 1:22 Xel xomaxoneing on etek en qayeeng wei e di teyoxe wou xel on, en se teyoxe xel ambei xel putoung wei petieing o, qe nambei tambiy wei luk is nikanzek o.
MAR 1:23 Se denlek en tambiy ti wei laweeng nilaxes toundei eivek e, me toundei eivek xomek qekueing ama is xel eno nyayek ngandoung bei,
MAR 1:24 “Yesu wei Nasaret, wa being bo vati wou xa? Wang lam bei semaleeng xa veil? A woulek bei wang on eti. Wang on vambuing tiwei Anutu yo!”
MAR 1:25 Yesu neil e, “Tip lukeing. De lam myayaing veil tambiy yon!”
MAR 1:26 Laweeng nilaxes on bimexe moux on nikanzek, de nyayek me lam myayaing veil tambiy on.
MAR 1:27 Xomaxoneing tambak on dalus etek en inyon me xel teling ama, “Tine inye vati? Inye teyoxeing vako ti is nikanzek me neil laweeng nilaxes dom xel betiwou e vya.”
MAR 1:28 Pavulek wei e yo la wo tambak daing eivek tembuing danghei dalus wei Galili yon.
MAR 1:29 Xel la veil xomek qekueing ama eno lutika xel la is Jems me Yoan bei na xomek wei Simon me Andrias o.
MAR 1:30 Simon yeing avexta wo gying om di yeip lek zek, me se wo lululek eno xel neil wou Yesu en vexo.
MAR 1:31 Om moxo la wou e, me zeim e mema de vind vexo dei ghey. Gying on la veil e dom vexo qandi me di yeiwou yaeing wou xel.
MAR 1:32 Ka sayeiv teila me di wo mangamong eno xomaxoneing qou xel dalus wei vanei yo me memo nilul wei dei eivek o me la wou Yesu.
MAR 1:33 Xel beyeeng dalus on qekuma wou xomek mya,
MAR 1:34 me Yesu yeiwou xel ngenong wei xe vanei leimalei eno ma. Moxo tiy memo ngenong is ambei nyon, ekom se wong memo yon luk, en xel woulek bei e eti.
MAR 1:35 Satiboukeing lulayang wei di wo matektekeing, eno Yesu qandi lek me lam veil xomek me la ingwei xel ma veil o, me la di zeimema.
MAR 1:36 Simon me e xe laxousyeiw la bei na gyimexe e,
MAR 1:37 me gyeik xel yeiwou e, xel neil wou e, “Xomaxoneing dalus di yimexe wang!”
MAR 1:38 Yesu neil elox, “Xey ambei na beyeeng bamba wei paviyeing nei, en kandek a neil xoulek anghei inyon is. Qes tiyon om a lam.”
MAR 1:39 Om moxo ghavineeng la eivek Galili, me la neil xoulek eivek xel xe xomek qekueing ama me tiy xel memo.
MAR 1:40 Tambiy tiwei vanei lepa yon lam wou Yesu me ev vaxa qatu eivek dom tay wou e, “Wangwei wa laleim e devind nei, yond wang bong am bo vako.”
MAR 1:41 Yesu lalei pyaxow en moxo, yom tatei mema la me axlek moxo. Me neil, “A laleing vind. Wang bo vako!”
MAR 1:42 Lutika eno lepa la veil e dom moxo wo vako.
MAR 1:43 Yesu wong moxo la lutika dom peti e nikanzek,
MAR 1:44 “Wang gweiteyei en wa se neil inye wou xelti. Ekom la talex xow wou lumuki me wong da la nambei ingwei Mose wo qayeeng petieing o bei neing ayang wang wo vako no, inye nambei pavulek ti wang bong ambei nyon en tyek xel boulek bei wang nimzalek.”
