MAR 1:45 Ekom ma, tambiy on la myayaing me neilteyei wou xel tambakateiv on, om qayeeng la wo sapa en vati wei e wong o. Om nambei nyon Yesu se teyeimbei na eivek beyeeng yanyateiv, om moxo mindei myayaing eivek beyeeng wei xel ma veil o. Ekom xomaxoneing nanghei di lam wou e nanghei beyeeng danghei danghei nei.
MAR 2:1 Bouk valu lak veil, eno Yesu lox me la Kapenaom me xomaxoneing ngo bei e toundei eivek beeng.
MAR 2:2 Om xomaxoneing ngenong qekuma om xomek lalei yon puplek, me elam myayaing wei xomek mya eno is, de moxo di neil Anutu xe xoulek wou xel.
MAR 2:3 Xomaxoneing valu lam, xel qou tambiy wei vaxa bezomb o ti me lam wou e, moxo kanzek mey, de xel vey qalei e lek lelek.
MAR 2:4 Tyek xel se teyeimbei qou e me na wou Yesu en inye xel ngenong pup xomek lek, om xel gwang xomek demi qetyei nanghei kawei Yesu toundei eivek o, de xel wong tambiy wei vaxa bezomb on teila kaka is lelek wei di yeip lek o.
MAR 2:5 Gyeik Yesu yei xel xe wongeingis, moxo neil wou vaxa bezombeing on bei, “A neung moux, wa xe sewokeing on a semaleeng veil.”
MAR 2:6 De woyom xel putoung valu wei petieing eno toundei inyon, xel venaxow di wou naleind naleind bei,
MAR 2:7 “Nambei nya xomaxoneing tine neil qayeeng ambei nyon? Moxo lukyak lek Anutu! Eti teyeimbei semaleeng sewokeing veil, qe Anutu venaxow?”
MAR 2:8 Lutika eno Yesu axe lek xow en vati wei xel venaxow di wou naleind en o, om moxo neil wou xel, “Nambei nya xam ghe di wou naleimim en tine?
MAR 2:9 Qayeeng vati wo pok bei a neil wou vaxa bezombeing on, ‘Wa xe sewokeing a semaleeng veil,’ o a neimbei, ‘Qandi, de qou wa xe lelek me la?’
MAR 2:10 En kandek wang boulek bei inyon Xomaxoneing Neu Moux wei wo lei ngandoung lek tembuing bei semaleeng sewokeing.” Moxo neil wou tambiy vaxa bezomb on,
MAR 2:11 “A neil wou wang, qandi, de qou wa xe lelek me la bam.”
MAR 2:12 Moxo qandi lek me qou e xe lelek me la myayaing eivek xomaxoneing on dalus mend. Tine wo etekeing wou xel tambakateiv on om xel sanghoxe Anutu lei, me neil, “Xa se mi xei lulti nambei tine!”
MAR 2:13 Yesu la myayaing wei lounyeing Galili nei no. Xel qendu ngandoung ti di lam wou e, me moxo di teyoxe xel.
MAR 2:14 Ka moxo di la eno yei Alpias neu moux Livai toundei eivek xomek takis. Om Yesu neil wou e, “Betiwou ay.” Om Livai qandi lek me betiwou e.
MAR 2:15 Ka Yesu di ya eivek Livai beeng, xel wei mi qou takis me xel wei mi wo sewokeing on ngenong eno di ya is e me e xe xel betiyeing, en inyon xel ngenong wei mi betiwou e yo.
MAR 2:16 Gyeik xel putoung wei petieing wei Parisi yo yei e di ya is xel sewokeing me xel wei mi qou takis eno xel teling wou e xe xel betiyeing: “Nambei nya moxo di ya is xel wei mi qou takis me xel wei sewokeing o?”
MAR 2:17 Yesu ngo qayeeng tine me neil wou xel, “Xel wei vanei ma veil eno se mi yei dokta, qe xel wei vanei eno mi yei dokta. A se lam bei taxe xel wei bombek o, qe xel wei sewokeing o.”
MAR 2:18 De Yoan xe xel betiyeing me xel Parisi eno, mi vambu yaeing. Xomaxoneing valu lam me teling wou Yesu, “Inye nambei nya ekom Yoan xe xel betiyeing me xel betiyeing wei Parisi eno di vambu yaeing, dom wa xe eno ma?”
MAR 2:19 Yesu lewexe, “Inye nambei nya ekom xel wei qayeeng la wou xel eno vambu yaeing gyeik e lam toundei is xel ne? Xel se teyei en nambei e nanghei toundei is xel.
MAR 2:20 Ekom bouk tyek nam gyeik ingwei xel a qou moux wei ii venei yo me na veil xel, dom lek bouk kayon eno tyek xel vambu yaeing.”
MAR 2:21 “Xelti se teyeimbei duw qaeing vako myasepu eivek qaeing lexeing wei takwei yo, wangwei e bong ambei nyon, qaeing myasepu wei vako eno sul me tetei ingwei takwei yo tip me wo myasapa.
MAR 2:22 Me tambiy ti se teyeimbei taw wain vako eivek wain takwei ninavi. Wangwei e bong ambei nyon, wain vako tyek buklek me natax wain takwei yon ninavi, wain vako is leliy ninavi takwei yon luw xouing tyek bo nol. Ma, e taw wain vako yon eivek ninavi vako.”
MAR 2:23 Sabat ti eno Yesu di la eivek xuk wei wit o lalei me e xe xel betiyeing di la ghavineeng is, gyeik xel pax me la eno xel pyaw wit neing valu.
MAR 2:24 Parisiyeiw neil wou e, “Wei, nambei nya xel wong lul wei qayeeng petieing peti yo lek bouk wei Sabat o?”
MAR 2:25 E lewexe, “Beip xam seng mi pyaw vati wei Dawit wong o, gyeik e me e xe xel wei mi la is e eno maxepya xel en lul wei yaeing eno ma?
MAR 2:26 Eivek bouk wei Abiata lumuki lukanzek eno moxo la eivek Anutu xe xomek me ya belet wei xel mi toung wou Anutu manghalus wei petieing lewexe lek o, inye xel wei lumukiyeiw eno venaxow mi ya. De moxo wong valu wou e xe xel wei mi la is e yo.”
MAR 2:27 Woyom moxo neil wou xel, “Sabat on Anutu toung en xomaxoneing, de Anutu se toung xomaxoneing bei devind Sabat.
MAR 2:28 Omva Xomaxoneing Neu Moux ne Tambiy Ngandoung me lei ngandoung wei Sabat o.”
MAR 3:1 De Yesu la eivek xomek qekueing ama no, me moux wei mema bezomb eno ti toundei inyon.
MAR 3:2 Xel on valu di yimexe qayeeng qes wei xel embei byex qayeeng lek Yesu yo, om xel di yei e teyei teyei bei tyek e bong tambiy on bo nimzalek Sabat.
MAR 3:3 Yesu neil wou moux wei mema bezomb on bei, “Nale ghey nanghei mya nei wou xel dalus ne mend.”
MAR 3:4 Woyom Yesu teling xel, “Beip inye petieing neil en Sabat bei: wongeing nimza o wongeing nilul, vineing xomaxoneing na toumendei mapieing o leiseing e mey?” Ekom xel dei kanzek.
MAR 3:5 Moxo yei e vivekwou xel is lalei vanei, me lalei wo maying is en xel laleind on wo nikanzekta, om moxo neil wou moux on, “Tatei memam wo bombek.” Moxo tatei mema, dom mema wo nimzalek.
MAR 3:6 Lutika eno xel Parisi la myayaing me yimexe sakwaing is Herot xe xel valu bei tyek xel nyeis Yesu na mey ambei nya.
MAR 3:7 Yesu is e xe xel betiyeing vup xow veil xel me la ingwei lounyeing nei, me xomaxoneing ngenong lam anghei Galili eno betiy xel.
MAR 3:8 Xel ngo lul dalus wei e di wong on, om xomaxoneing ngenong lam wou e nanghei Yudia, Yerusalem, Idumia me tembuing danghei wei sekla Yorodan me vivek la pu wei Taia me Saidon nei.
MAR 3:9 En nambei xel qendu ngandoung on lam om Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei xel gyeiwou bot nayak ti wou e boy, en kandek xel xomaxoneing on ti se tendu ma nam paviy e.
MAR 3:10 En e wong xomaxoneing ngenong wo nimzalek, om eti yeiw wei lam is vanei nilul eno tendu ma lam bei daxlek e.
MAR 3:11 Xel laweeng nilaxes yei e, xel mi ev vaxend qatu eivek wou e me taxe bei, “Wang on Anutu Neu Moux.”
MAR 3:12 Ekom Yesu peti xel nikanzek bei xel se neil e teyeimbei e eti.
MAR 3:13 Yesu la pu wei lukendu nei me taxe la wou xel eti yeiw wei e wounalei en o, me xel lam wou e.
MAR 3:14 E beyal xel xoumeeng yuw me wong lei sinale wou xel, en kandek xel a mi mendei is e me e mi bong xel na myayaing nei me na neil xoulek,
MAR 3:15 me wong nikanzek wou xel bei xel a mi tiy xel memo.
MAR 3:16 Inye xel xoumeeng yuw wei e beyal o, Simon, tiwei e taxe e lei nge bei Petele.
MAR 3:17 Sebedi neu moux Jems me e li Yoan (wei e taxe xel leind bei Boaneges, qes ambei nye bei dewek neuyeiw moux),
MAR 3:18 Andrias, Pilip, Batolomiu, Matai, Tomas, Alpias neu moux Jems, Tadius, Simon wei Selot wei mi wo vevek en xel xe seyap o
MAR 3:19 me Yudas Iskariot, tiwei tyek na neil Yesu teyei me na toung e na eivek xel memend o.
MAR 3:20 Woyom Yesu la eivek xomek ti, me xel ngenong qekuma no, omek e is e xe xel betiyeing se teyeimbei gya xend yaeing.
MAR 3:21 Gyeik e tamali ngo qayeeng en tine eno xel la bei na qou e, en xel neil embei, “Moxo mav o.”
MAR 3:22 Me xel putoung wei petieing o me eti yeiw wei lep me lam anghei Yerusalem eno neil, “Yesu moxo eno Belsebul gyovaxa wei memo eno dei eivek e, om mi tiy memo la myayaing nangya e xe nikanzek.”
MAR 3:23 Om Yesu taxe xel me luk wou xel eivek qayeeng pakeing: “Nambei nya Sandang teyeimbei tiy Sandang na myayaing?
MAR 3:24 Wangwei tete lalei ti venaxow dembu xow na yuw, tete lalei tiyon se teyeimbei bale nikanzek.
MAR 3:25 Wangwei xomek ti venaxow dembu xow na yuw, xomek tiyon se teyeimbei bale nikanzek.
MAR 3:26 Me wangwei Sandang bo vevek me dembu venaxow na yuw, e maxow se teyeimbei bale nikanzek, en tyek ma na ma.
MAR 3:27 Ekom xelti se teyeimbei na eivek tambiy wei nikanzek eno beeng me na qou e xe lulul dalus veil e beeng. Qe ka e tup tambiy on natax bole, woyom na qou lulul eivek e xe xomek lalei.
MAR 3:28 A neil wou xam zonghek, sewokeing dalus me lukeingyak wei xomaxoneing eno tyek Anutu semaleeng veil xel.
MAR 3:29 Ekom wangwei eti yeiw baluk yak lek Laweeng Vambuing, tyek e xe nilul on Anutu se teyeimbei semaleeng veil, ma, nimaying wei e xe sewokeing on tyek na mi gyeip luta luta.”
MAR 3:30 Moxo neil tine en nambei xel di neil embei, “E yon laweeng nilaxes toundei eivek.”
MAR 3:31 Woyom Yesu ta me liyeiw moux lam tyip me nale myayaing de wong xelti la lalei me taxe e.
MAR 3:32 De xel qendu ngandoung ti toundei vivekwou e. Om xel neil wou e, “Tam alis limyeiw moux toungale myayaing en embei gyei wang.”
MAR 3:33 Ekom neil elox, “Inyon a tang me a lingyeiw moux on eti?”
MAR 3:34 Woyom yei xel wei toundei vivekwou e yon me neil, “Wei! Xel ne a tang me a lingyeiw moux!
MAR 3:35 Eti yeiw wei mi wong ambei Anutu lalei vind o, yond inye a ling moux me a ling vex me a tang.”
MAR 4:1 Yesu lox teyoxe xel qendu ngandoung wei qekuma is e yon no nanghei lounyeing nenyawes. Inyon xel qendu ngandoung wei nale wou e ma yon ngenong, om moxo la eivek bot lek lounyeing me la dei dom xel xomaxoneing dalus on toungale wou lounyeing nenyawes.
MAR 4:2 Om moxo di teyoxe xel en lul ngenong eivek qayeeng pakeing, me eivek e xe teyoxeing eno inye,
MAR 4:3 “Ngo! Xuk ma ti la en embei na davuw e xe lulul vei eivek xuk.
MAR 4:4 Ka moxo di vuw lulul vei lala, valu teila wou sakwaing, me menek lam ya ema.
MAR 4:5 De valu teila lek qakous qakous, wei tembuing nimza maeing, om lulul vei yon vindek lam daing, nambei tembuing on se la ghembi.
MAR 4:6 Ekom gyeik sayeiv leklam, lulul vei wei tyip on eno sayeiv leis om xel mey en nambei xel luselis ma.
MAR 4:7 De vei valu teila eivek qeis wei yingying, wei ling me leklam apu me nale zeyi lul tyipeing, om xel se vuk neing.
MAR 4:8 De vei valu teila lek tembuing nimza om tyip me lam apu, ling ngandoung me vuk neing ngenong nambei xoumeeng yal (30), 60 me 100.”
MAR 4:9 Woyom Yesu neil, “Eti nenya toundei lek e bei e ngo, yond wong e ngo wou qayeeng.”
MAR 4:10 Gyeik xel qendu ngandoung la veil, de e venaxow toundei eno xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw me xel ba wei vivekwou e eno teling en qayeeng pakeing beimambei ne.
MAR 4:11 Moxo neil wou xel, “Anutu xe qayeeng xupekeing wei tete lalei, eno wong wou xam. Ekom wou xel wei toundei myayaing, eno lul dalusateiv a neil eivek qayeeng pakeing.
MAR 4:12 Om “‘xel a mi gyei le ekom tyek xel se gyeiwou, me na mi ngo, ekom xel se teyeimbei boulek, wangwei se nambei nyon nei tyek xel pekwi xow me Anutu semaleeng xel xe nilul veil.’”
MAR 4:13 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel, “Beip xam seng woulek qayeeng pakeing tine? Woyom nambei nya tyek xam ghe boulek qayeeng pakeing dalus?
MAR 4:14 Tambiy wei mema xuk eno vuw Anutu xe xoulek.
MAR 4:15 Xomaxoneing valu eno nambei vei wei teila lek sakwaing, wei xel vuw xoulek, gyeik kawei xel ngo yo, Sandang lam me zeim xoulek wei xel xen eivek xel eno veil.
MAR 4:16 De xel valu eno nambei vei wei xel vuw xoulek lek qakous qakous o, xel ngo xoulek me lutika eno xel qou is xeindlala.
MAR 4:17 Ekom xel xe luselis eno ma, xel nale teyei lek seivma nayaka. Gyeik ingwei nimaying o xomaxoneing wo nol wou xel, en ingwei xel betiwou Anutu xe xoulek, om xel nind wongeingis eno tei daing.
MAR 4:18 Xel valu nambei vei wei xel vuw eivek yis wei niying o. Xel ngo xoulek,
MAR 4:19 ekom xel wo laleind maying en mapieing tine, kwa wei embei bo lulul ana eno mi tyoxe xel, me woueing nalei en lul valu lam eivek me nale zeyi xoulek, om se wo neing.
MAR 4:20 Ekom xel valu, eno nambei vei wei xel vuw lek tembuing aneing wei nimza yo, om xel ngo xoulek me laleind vind om xel vuk neing teyei lek xoumeeng yal (30), 60 me 100 inyon vati wei xel ev o.”
MAR 4:21 Moxo neil wou xel, “Beip wang qou lam me ghe lam bei toung eivek dengmuing lalei o lelek xeinghembi? Ma, wa toung lek vaxa wei mi nale lek o?
MAR 4:22 En vatiyeiw wei dei xupekeing, eno tyek nam yanyateiv, de vatiyeiw wei yeip xupekeing eno tyek xel a qou me nam myayaing.
MAR 4:23 Wangwei xelti nenya toundei lek e bei e ngo, ond wong e ngo wou qayeeng.”
MAR 4:24 Om moxo neil wou xel, “Xam a ni nenyam wou vati wei xam a bei ngo yo eno xam ghe bou naleimim en embo nimza. Vamva wei xam ghe ngo yo eno tyek Anutu bong lupeyei vamva yon noum wou xam me tyek bong lupeyei valu lek mapu wou xam is.
MAR 4:25 De wangwei eti na qou lupeyei, ond tyek na qou lupeyei valu lek mapu is. Dom wangwei eti se qou lupeyei ond tyek lupeyei kawei qou yo eno tyek na zeim veil e.”
MAR 4:26 De Yesu neil no, “Tete lalei wei Anutu yo, teyei lek ambei moux ti vuw vei lala lek tembuing.
MAR 4:27 Boukeing me bendiyeing eno moxo mi yeip o qandi lek, de vei wei xen eno tyip me ling ambei nya eno se woulek.
MAR 4:28 Tembuing venaxow wong lul on tyip, yateiv belup atax dekakom wo lis lek, de woyom vuk neing lek lu.
MAR 4:29 Dekalekom gyeik neing wo ngandoung me zuw, eno moxo zeim ngeyeing wou en nambei inye bouk wei qoueing neing o.”
MAR 4:30 De Yesu neil no, “Tyek xey a boulek Anutu xe tete lalei eno nambei nya? O tyek xey a neil qayeeng pakeing vati en e neilteyei?
MAR 4:31 Inye nambei mastet vei, vei ne nayakamaing ka veil vei wei wang mi xen eivek tembuing o.
MAR 4:32 Ka gyeik eveing o, ling me wo teta me wo ngandoungateiv ghanaw lulul dalus wei eveing eivek xuk on, is mema ngandoung, inyon menek menek tyek nam bako lewis eivek e xe senyoleeng.”
MAR 4:33 Yesu luk qayeeng pakeing ngenong is xoulek wou xel, teyeimbei xel a ngo wou.
MAR 4:34 Moxo se neil luti wou xel, qe di neil qayeeng sapa yon eivek qayeeng pakeing. Ekom gyeik e venaxow mindei is e xe xel betiyeing eno moxo mi neil lul dalus yeip yaing wou xel.
MAR 4:35 Lek bouk kayon gyeik soukeing di lam, eno moxo neil wou e xe xel betiyeing, “Xey ambei na nge loxalu nei.”
MAR 4:36 Xel ghanaw xomaxoneing qendu ngandoung on dom xel qou e me la lek bot tiwei Yesu toundei lek o. Inyon bot valu la is xel.
MAR 4:37 De inyon laweeng valeivek ti tyip, me mamileeng di vuklek me lam leislek bot me embim a puplek.
MAR 4:38 Yesu toundei eivek bot leyus, me di yeip lek pilo. Xel betiyeing piyexe e me neil wou e, “Putoung, inyon wa seng pyanaleim en ingwei xey a bim a mey ne?”
MAR 4:39 Moxo qandi lek me luk nikanzek wou laweeng de neil wou mamileeng wei di vuk me lam on, “Denduing ma! Dom weip kanzek!” Woyom laweeng mey de mamileeng yeip kanzek.
MAR 4:40 E neil wou xel betiyeing, “Nambei nya ekom xam ghe waleeng? Beip xam seng ghei wongis?”
MAR 4:41 Xel yaleeng ngandoung me teling wouma, “Tambiy tine eti? Omek laweeng me mamileeng ngo e vya ne!”
MAR 5:1 Xel la nge loxalu wei lounyeing Galili me la tembuing danghei wei xel Gerasa nei.
MAR 5:2 Gyeik Yesu lam myayaing veil bot, lutika eno moux tiwei laweeng nilaxes dei eivek e eno lam veil beyeeng wei meyeing o, me lam wou e.
MAR 5:3 Moux tine mindei eivek beyeeng wei meyeing o, xelti se teyeimbei tup e no, o se teyeimbei xel bako e nangya sen.
MAR 5:4 En e yon xel mi toung sen eivek e mema me vaxa, ekom moxo mi tax sen la yuw me pyaw aen mi pek lek vaxa. Xelti se ninkanzek teyei bei bong embo males.
MAR 5:5 Boukeing me bendiyeing eivek eeng wei meyeing me lukendu nayak senghoing, eno moxo mi eng ngandoung me ghuw xow angya qakous.
MAR 5:6 Gyeik e yei Yesu nanghei dingta, moxo veimya me la ev vaxa qatu eivek wou e manghalus.
MAR 5:7 Moxo ghak niseikeing bei, “Yesu, Anutu Neu wei gheyapu ghanaw veil o, wambei bong vati wou ay? Neil neing lek Anutu lei, bei tyek wa seng bong myaveweeng wou ay!”
MAR 5:8 En Yesu neil wou e woy bei, “Wa laweeng nilaxes on, lam myayaing veil moux tine!”
MAR 5:9 Woyom Yesu teling e, “Wa leim va?” Moxo neil elox, “A leing qendu ngandoung wei vevek, en inye xa ngenong.”
MAR 5:10 Om moxo tay wou Yesu lumama bei, e se bong xel na myayaing veil tembuing senghoing kayon.
MAR 5:11 Bok qendu ngandoung ti eno di ya paviy lukendu nayak on nenyawes.
MAR 5:12 Xel memo on tay wou Yesu bei, “Wong xa la eivek xel bok on.”
MAR 5:13 Moxo lenghek lek xel, om laweeng nilaxes on lam myayaing me la eivek bok. Bok qendu ngandoung on teyei lek ambei 2,000 eno veimyend niseikeing me la oing mazanghei me lepla eivek lounyeing me num memiing de mey.
MAR 5:14 Xel wei mi vet bok eno pek me la neil qayeeng tine eivek beyeeng nayak me beyeeng beimambei nei om xomaxoneing la myayaing bei na gyei vati wong tiyon.
MAR 5:15 Gyeik xel lam wou Yesu, xel yei moux tiwei memo ngenong mindei eivek e yo, eno byex teimb me e lupeyei yon yeip yaing, om xel yaleeng.
MAR 5:16 Eti yeiw wei xel yei eno neil wou xomaxoneing en vati wei belup wou moux wei memo mindei eivek o, me neil e lala en bok is ambei nyon.
MAR 5:17 Woyom xomaxoneing tay wou Yesu bei e na veil xel xe tembuing danghei tiyon.
MAR 5:18 Ka Yesu embei na eivek bot, moux wei memo dei eivek e yon lam tay wou Yesu bei na is e.
MAR 5:19 Yesu se lewexe lek e, qe neil, “La bam wou limyeiyeiw me neil wou xel, en vati wei Tambiy Ngandoung wong wou wang o, en ingwei lalei pyaxow en wang o.”
MAR 5:20 Om tambiy on la veil e me di neilteyei eivek tembuing danghei dalus wei Dekapolis nei en vati wei Yesu wong wou e yo. Om xomaxoneing dalus on etek en qayeeng on.
MAR 5:21 Gyeik Yesu lox me la nge loxalu lek bot eivek lounyeing eno xomaxoneing qendu ngandoung qekuma me lam wou e gyeik e toungale paviy lounyeing o.
MAR 5:22 Woyom gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama eno ti lei Yairus, lam inyon. Yei Yesu, om moxo ev vaxa qatu eivek wou e vaxa,
MAR 5:23 me tay wou e, “A neung vex yak eno e bim a mey, om lam liw memam lek vexo en kandek e xe vanei e ma dom mendei mapieing.”
MAR 5:24 Om Yesu la is e. Xel qendu ngandoung ti betiwou e me vingama vivekwou e.
MAR 5:25 Me vex ti mindei inyon, eno e xe gyand mi lam teyei lek vakovek qes xoumeeng yuw.
MAR 5:26 Vexo mi qou vanei ngenong wou dokta ngenong me saing malew dalus wei e yo, ekom vanei yon se ma qe mi wo nol wou e.
MAR 5:27 Gyeik vexo ngo qayeeng en Yesu, vexo lam apu paviy e demi eivek xel qendu yon me axlek e xe teimb ding,
MAR 5:28 en vexo wounalei, “Wangwei a mou daxlek e xe teimb, tyek a bong nimzalek.”
MAR 5:29 Lutika eno vexo gyand touk me vexo axe lek xow bei wo nimzalek veil myavanei wei mi qou yo.
MAR 5:30 Lutika eno Yesu woulek bei nikanzek valu la veil e. Moxo pekwi ma vivekwou eivek xel qendu ngandoung on me teling, “Eti axlek a xe teimb?”
MAR 5:31 E xe xel betiyeing neil elox, “Wang wei xomaxoneing qendu ngandoung on nale lip is wang on, om nambei nya wang teling, ‘Eti axlek ay?’ ”
MAR 5:32 Ekom Yesu vena di yei e vivekwou bei gyei bei eti ka wong inye.
MAR 5:33 Woyom vex on vena woulek vati wei tyip wou e yo, om lam me ev vaxa qatu me yeip ma eivek tembuing me etek is yalenyeing, dom neil wou e zonghek en lul dalus.
MAR 5:34 Moxo neil wou vex on, “A neung vex, wa xe wongeingis wong wang wo nimzalek. La is laleim vevopeing. Vanei wei wang qou yo eno ma dom wang wo nimzalek.”
MAR 5:35 Ka Yesu nanghei di luk, moux valu lam anghei Yairus xe xomek, inyon gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama yo. Xel neil, “Wa neum vex eno mey, wa seng bo nimaying ti wou Putoung no.”
MAR 5:36 Yesu se li nenya wou vati wei xel neil o, qe neil wou gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama yo, “Wa seng gwaleeng. Qe wang bongis.”
MAR 5:37 Moxo se wong xelti betiwou e qe Petele, Jems me Yoan wei Jems li moux o.
MAR 5:38 Gyeik xel lam xomek wei gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama yo, Yesu yei xomaxoneing di wo nindenduing is engeing me di wo talot.
MAR 5:39 Moxo eivek la lalei me neil wou xel, “Nambei nya xam ghe di eng me ghe wong nindenduing ngandoung on enva? Vex yak ne mou se mey ti qe di yeip o.”
MAR 5:40 Ekom xel napexe e. Ka e tiy xel dalus la myayaing, eno qou vex yak on ma me ta me e xe betiyeing wei la is e yo me xel la eivek ingwei vex yak on di yeip anghei yo.
MAR 5:41 E zeim vexo mema dom neil wou vexo, “Talita kum,” qes ambei nye, “Vex yak, a neil wou wang, qandi lek!”
MAR 5:42 De lutika eno vex on nale ghey me vivek eivek xomek. En inye vex on xe vakovek qes xoumeeng yuw. Om xel on etek niseikeing.
MAR 5:43 Moxo wong petieing tine bei xel se bong xelti boulek inye, me neil wou xel bei xel bong lul yaeing valu wou vexo bei e gya.
MAR 6:1 Yesu la veil inyon me la e maxow beeng qes Nasaret, me e xe xel betiyeing eno la is e.
MAR 6:2 Lek bouk Sabat eno moxo la teyoxe xel eivek xomek qekueing ama me xel ngenong wei ngo e eno etek. Xel neil, “Tambiy tine qou qayeeng me kwa nimza ne nanghei inya, me mi wong lulvako ne nangya mema?
MAR 6:3 Beip inye se kamunda? Beip inye se Maria neu moux, Jems, Yosep, Yudas me Simon lind? Beip e liyeiw vex se toundei is xey?” Om xel yei e wo nol.
MAR 6:4 Yesu neil wou xel, “Eivek beyeeng valuvalu eno xel mi sanghoxe poropet lei. Ekom eivek e venaxow beeng qes, me eivek e liyeiyeiw senghoing me eivek emaxow beeng, eno inyon poropet wei lei ma yo.”
MAR 6:5 E se teyei bei bong lulvako nanghei inyon, qe liw mema lek xomaxoneing nuyuw wei vanei yo me wong xel wo nimzalek.
MAR 6:6 De etek en xel on se mi wongis. Woyom Yesu la ghavineeng me teyoxe xel eivek beyeeng nge me la nge.
MAR 6:7 Dekakom moxo taxe xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw on lam wou e, me wong xel mi la yuyuw de wong nikanzek wei tiyeing laweeng nilaxes o is wou xel.
MAR 6:8 De moxo peti xel bei, “Xam se qou lulti en sakwaing qe xam a qou patongeeng dom xam se qou belet, vaxak de malew eivek xam xe bak.
MAR 6:9 Xam a byex vaxalambes, dom xam se byex teimb nge lek mapu.
MAR 6:10 Gyeik ingwei xam ghe na eivek xomek ti eno xam a mi mendei inyon deka xam ghe na veil beyeeng nayak tiyon le.
MAR 6:11 De wangwei beyeeng on ti se qou xam, o na ngo xam, ond xam pepa vegyuveeng veil vaxamim gyeik xam a being na veil o, en xel boulek bei xel wo kwa yon nol wou xow.”
MAR 6:12 Xel la myayaing me neil xoulek bei xomaxoneing pekwi xow.
MAR 6:13 Xel di tiy memo ngenong la myayaing me di taw wel lek xomaxoneing ngenong wei vanei wong xel eno is, om xel wong xel wo nimzalek.
MAR 6:14 King Herot ngo, en Yesu lei wei xel woulek eivek tembuing sapa. Xel valu di neil, “Yoan Lipekeing eno qandi lek veil meyeing, omek mi wong lulvako en nikanzek wei toundei eivek e yo.”
MAR 6:15 Xel valu neil embei, “E yon Eliya.” De valu neil embei, “E yon poropet, nambei poropet wei takwei qenang eno ti.”
MAR 6:16 Ekom gyeik Herot ngo tine, moxo neil, “Yoan, tambiy tiwei a qateiv e kwa tip me e mey, eno qandi lek veil meyeing!”
MAR 6:17 En myaxeeng eno Herot venaxow wong qayeeng nikanzek bei xel a zeimaxoun Yoan, me na tup e me na toung eivek xeitueing. E wong tine en nambei Herodias, wei li Pilip venei wei e ii yo.
MAR 6:18 En Yoan vena neil wou Herot, “Inye se la teyei lek qayeeng petieing bei wang dii lim venei.”
MAR 6:19 Om Herodias lalei wo vanei wou Yoan om embei nyeis e. Ekom vexo se teyei,
MAR 6:20 en nambei Herot yaleeng en Yoan me mi yei e teyei, en woulek bei tambiy on bombek me moux wei vambuing o. Gyeik Herot ngo Yoan, moxo etek niseikeing me wounalei ngenong. Ekom e lalei vind en embei ngo e.
MAR 6:21 De woyom Herodias yimexe sakwaing wei embei nyeis Yoan e mey yo. Om lek bouk wei Herot umbek lek eno moxo wong mata ngandoung wou e xe xel wei leitata me lei ngandoung wei xel vevek me xel wei mi la tax en xel moux wei Galili yo.
MAR 6:22 Gyeik Herodias neu vex lam lalei me aw, vex on wo Herot me xel wei di ya is e eno laleind wo nimza. King neil wou vexawo yon, “Wa teling ay en vatiyeiw wei wa laleim vind o, ond tyek am bong wou wang.”
MAR 6:23 De neil zonghek is vex on is qayeeng neing, “Vati wei wambei teling ay eno tyek a bong wou wang. De wangwei wa teling bei a dembu a xe tete lalei na yuw me na bong wou wang on tyek a dembu de na bong veweeng wou wang.”
MAR 6:24 Vexo la myayaing me teling wou ta, “Tyek a teling wou en vati?” Ta neil elox bei, “Yoan Lipekeing lukanzek.”
MAR 6:25 Lutika eno vexo lox daing me la lalei wou King me neil wou e: “Am bei wang bong Yoan Lipekeing lukanzek wou ay gweimbeeng kane lek dipekta.”
MAR 6:26 King moxo lalei wo maying ngandoung, en nambei ingwei neil zonghek is xel wei lam di ya is e yo, om embei se pesek lek vexawo yon.
MAR 6:27 Om wo daing me wong e xe vevek tiwei mi qateiv xel kwend eno is qayeeng nikanzek bei e na qou Yoan lukanzek. Moux moxo la qateiv Yoan kwa eivek xeitueing,
MAR 6:28 de qou e lukanzek lek dipekta me loum. Moxo wong ela wou vexawo yon, me vex on wong ela wou ta.
MAR 6:29 Gyeik ingwei Yoan xe xel betiyeing ngo tine eno xel lam qou e neing me liw e la eivek leiveeng meyeing ti.
MAR 6:30 Woyom sinaleyeiw qekuma vivekwou Yesu me wo qayeeng wou e en lul dalus wei xel wong me teyoxe yo.
MAR 6:31 Woyom nambei xomaxoneing ngenong di lox me loum, om xel nind seivma wei xel embei gya eno ma, om moxo neil wou xel, “Xam lam is ay, xam venaxow ghe gwei beyeeng wei xel ma veil o me ghe na qou laweeng.”
MAR 6:32 Om xel venaxow la ba nei eivek bot, me la ingwei xel ma veil o.
MAR 6:33 Ekom xel ngenong yeimend wou xel di la yo om xel veimyend lek vaxend nanghei beyeeng tambak nei me la inyon natax en xel.
MAR 6:34 Gyeik Yesu la yasewis eno yei xel qendu ngandoung on, om lalei pyaxow en xel, en xel on xok ambei sipsip wei gyovaxa ma veil o. Om moxo teyoxe xel en lulul ngenong.
MAR 6:35 Gyeik ingwei sayeiv di teila eno e xe xel betiyeing lam wou e me neil, “Beyeeng tine xel ma veil, de inye sayeiv di teila.
MAR 6:36 Wong xomaxoneing on la en kandek xel na ingwei xuk lalei nei me ne na beyeeng wei toundei paviyeing on me na bou xend lul yaeing valu.”
MAR 6:37 Ekom moxo lewexe, “Xam venaxow ghe bong lul valu wou xel en xel gya.” Xel neil wou e, “Malew ngandoung ma en ingwei xey a bei bou belet lek wou xel qendu ngandoung tine en yaeing. Tyek inyon teyei lek ambei dentouk qes lim yal en tambiy ti xe malew wei xouveing en xuk o!”
MAR 6:38 Moxo teling, “Xam ghe di qou belet vamva? Xam la wei.” Gyeik xel la yeiwou eno xel neil, “Belet lim de woing yuw is.”
MAR 6:39 Woyom Yesu wong xel la neil wou xel bei, xel mendei qendu qendu lek lesilek wei neluy yon.
MAR 6:40 Om xel dei qendu qendu teyei lek 100 me 50.
MAR 6:41 Moxo qou belet lim on me woing yuw on dom yeila tyoung gheyapu, de wong dange wou Anutu me dembu belet lim on. Me wong wou e xe xel betiyeing bei xel bong wou xomaxoneing me moxo vena dembu woing yuw on is ambei nyon wou xel dalus.
MAR 6:42 De xel on dalus ya me enden xel,
MAR 6:43 de xel betiyeing qekuwou belet me woing myapapu wei yo eivek pasik xoumeeng yuw.
MAR 6:44 Xomaxoneing wei ya yaeing on, eno moux teyei lek 5,000.
MAR 6:45 Lutika eno Yesu tendu e xe xel betiyeing on la eivek bot me wong xel la tax en e me la lounyeing loxalu wei beyeeng Betsaida nei, dekalekom wong xel bembeeng on la.
MAR 6:46 Ka e wong xel xomaxoneing on la woy, moxo lek me la lukendu nenyawes on bei na zeimema.
MAR 6:47 Gyeik ingwei di bouk eivek eno bot la tyip lounyeing masenghoing, dom e venaxow tateis toundei lek tembuing.
MAR 6:48 Moxo yeila xel betiyeing di wo pok lek sepaeing bot, en nambei laweeng ngandoung vei xel. Embim boyaing eno Yesu di la mapu lek lounyeing wou xel mend bei xel teyei bei gyei e,
MAR 6:49 ekom gyeik xel yei e di la lek lounyeing eno xel embeik nge inyon meyeing ti nu. Om xel nyayek niseikeing,
MAR 6:50 en nambei xel dalus yei e om xel nind yaleeng niseikeing. Lutika eno luk wou xel me neil, “Xam nale nimkanzek! Xam seng gwaleeng en inye ay yo.”
MAR 6:51 Om moxo lek la eivek bot is xel, de laweeng ma. Om moxoyeiw etek,
MAR 6:52 en xel se woulek qes wei Yesu wong gyeik dembu belet o. Ma. En inye xel laleind on wo nikanzekta.
MAR 6:53 Gyeik xel la nge loxalu, xel la yasewis lek tembuing Genesaret me tup bot nale inyon.
MAR 6:54 Ka xel lam myayaing veil bot, eno se denlek en xomaxoneing woulek Yesu.
MAR 6:55 Xel veimyend me la eivek beyeeng tambak on me qalei xel wei vanei yo lek ghus me qou xel me la ingwei xel ngo bei toundei nanghei yo.
MAR 6:56 Me beyeeng dalus wei moxo la eivek o, beyeeng me beyeeng nayak me beyeeng danghei danghei nei, xel mi toung xel wei vanei eno eivek beyeeng wei vateivek o. Xel mi tay wou bei e bong xel vanei daxlek e xe teimb ding myasepu. Om eti yeiw dalus wei mi axlek e yo eno mi wo nimzalek.
MAR 7:1 Xel Parisi me xel putoung wei petieing eno valu wei lam anghei Yerusalem eno qekuma is Yesu,
MAR 7:2 me yei e xe betiyeing on valu se betiwou kwa wei Yudayeiw wei xel mi sekweyexe memend o qe xel di ya yaeing is memend laxes.
MAR 7:3 (Parisi me xel dalus wei Yudayeiw eno se mi ya qe ka xel mi sekweyexe memend wole, nambei xel xe kwa wei buyeiw takwei yo.
MAR 7:4 Gyeik xel nam anghei ingwei beyeeng vateivek ond xel se mi ya qe ka xel lipek wole. Me xel mi betiwou lul ngenong valu wei buyeiw takwei yo, nambei ingwei sekweyexeing mayamya, deng, me dengmuing.)
MAR 7:5 Om Parisiyeiw me xel putoung wei petieing o teling Yesu, “Nambei nya wa xe xel betiyeing se mi wong e teyei lek kwa takwei wei xel bundyeiw o qe xel mi ya xend yaeing is memend laxes?”
MAR 7:6 E neil elox, “Yesaya neil zonghek gyeik e neil qayeeng poropet en xam wei myamim yuw o. En nambei xel byex eivek qapiya eno nambei nye, “‘Xomaxoneing ti beimambei yon mi sanghoxe ay angya myend bandaing, ekom xel laleind on mindei dingta veil ay.
MAR 7:7 Xel mi wong lalo wou ay bandaing. Ekom xel mi teyoxe xomaxoneing bei xel a mi betiwou petieing ne nambei Anutu xe.’
MAR 7:8 Xam ghe saing Anutu xe petieing dom ghe di zeimaxoun xomaxoneing xe kwa wei takwei yo.”
MAR 7:9 Me e neil wou xel, “Xam ghe woulek ewo nimza en kwa wei toungeing Anutu xe petieing la dei nenyawes bei kandek betiwou bumyeiw xe kwa wei takwei yo!
MAR 7:10 En Mose neil, ‘Wa mi gwevek mam aluw tam xe qayeeng,’ de ‘Eti yeiw wei neil vyalek ma luw ta eno xel nyeis e mey.’
MAR 7:11 Ekom xam ghe neimbei wangwei moux ti e neil wou mamata, ‘Vineing vati wei a bei bong wou muw eno inye kolban qes ambei nye lulul da wei a beyal bei na bong wou Anutu yo,’
MAR 7:12 woyom wa seng wong e lox me la wo vineing ti wou ma o ta.
MAR 7:13 Nambei xam ghe wong nikanzek wei Anutu xe xoulek eno ma dom ghe mi betiwou xam xe kwa takwei wei xam ghe mi qou wou bumyeiw o. Me ghe wong lulul ngenong ambei nyon.”
MAR 7:14 Yesu taxe xel xomaxoneing ngenong la wou e no me neil, “Xam dalus a ngo wou ay, me na mi bou kwamim en tine bo nimza.
MAR 7:15 Lul tiwei mindei myayaing me la eivek xomaxoneing eno se teyeimbei bong embo nilaxes. Qe vati wei lam myayaing veil xomaxoneing laleind eno tiyon mi wong e wo nilaxes.”
MAR 7:17 Gyeik e ghanaw xel qendu tiyon me la eivek xomek, e xe xel betiyeing teling e en qayeeng pakeing tine.
MAR 7:18 Moxo neil bei, “En xam is ambei nyon xam seng woulek qayeeng ne qes? Beip xam seng woulek bei lulti mi la eivek xomaxoneing nanghei myayaing eno se teyeimbei bong embo nilaxes?
MAR 7:19 Lulul ne eno se teyei bei na eivek e lalei qe tyek na eivek e xeita, de e laluwexe ela myayaing eivek leiveeng.” (Eivek neileing tine, Yesu neilteyei bei lul yaeing dalus on vako.)
MAR 7:20 Moxo neil no bei, “Vati wei lam myayaing veil xomaxoneing eno inye wong e wo nilaxes.
MAR 7:21 En lam eivek xomaxoneing laleind eno inyon woueing nalei nilul, kwa nilul wei kwapesiv o, panaxeing, leiseing xel a mey.
MAR 7:22 Wongeing kwapesiv is vex wei dei leya yo, kwa eivekeing, yei tambiy nge wo nol, tyonyeing, kwa wei betiyeing wou lalei vineing wei neing o, yeimalek, lukyak lek tambiy nge, byexeing vaxa, me kwa wei bandol o.
MAR 7:23 Kwa nilul beimambei ne dalus eno lam eivek xomaxoneing laleind me wong xomaxoneing wo nilaxes.”
MAR 7:24 Yesu la veil beyeeng tiyon me la danghei tiwei Taia nei. E la eivek xomek on ti de embei xelti se boulek e. Ekom se teyeimbei bun xow.
MAR 7:25 Qe lutika eno vex tiwei laweeng nilaxes dei eivek neu vex eno ngo qayeeng en e, lam ev vaxa qatu me yeip ma eivek wou e vaxa.
MAR 7:26 Vex tiyon inyon nanghei Grik, me umbek eivek Siria Ponisia. Vexo tay wou Yesu bei e tiy memo yon na myayaing veil e neu vex.
MAR 7:27 Moxo neil wou vex on, “Xey a bong yakyak gya vati wei xel laleind vind o dalus me na pup atax bole, en inye se nimza bei qoueing yakyak xe belet me banex ena wou naw.”
MAR 7:28 Vexo neil elox, “Ee, Tambiy Ngandoung, ekom xel naw mi ya yaeing myapapu wei yakyak mi wong e mi teila eivek lelek xeinghembi yo.”
MAR 7:29 Woyom moxo neil wou vex on, “Wang neil e loum ambei nyon om wang na, en memo la veil neum vexo.”
MAR 7:30 Vexo lox beeng me yeimbei neu vexo di yeip lek zek dom memo yon la veil e.
MAR 7:31 Woyom Yesu la veil beyeeng danghei wei Taia me la lox danghei wei Saidon, me la lox danghei wei Dekapolis me la tyip ninei wei lounyeing Galili ne.
MAR 7:32 Nanghei inyon eno xomaxoneing valu qou moux wei nenya wo qatu me mya wo nimaying om se teyeimbei baluk embo nimza yo me lam wou Yesu me xel tay wou e, bei e ni mema lek moux on.
MAR 7:33 Ka Yesu qou moux on me la nenyawes, dingta ka veil xel qendu ngandoung on, de moxo toung mema deyis la eivek moux on nenya luw. Woyom pesuv myalouk me toung mema deyis lek moux on ghas.
MAR 7:34 Moxo yeila tyoung gheyapu dom poux laweeng nikanzek me neil wou e, “Epata.” Qes ambei nye, “Wa tax!”
MAR 7:35 De lutika eno moux moxo nenya deng, me ghas tul de moxo luk eyeip yaing.
MAR 7:36 Yesu peti xel lumama bei eti se neil wou xelti en lul tiwei xel yei yo, ekom xel wo nikanzek en neileing qayeeng tine teyei.
MAR 7:37 Xomaxoneing on etek niseikeing. De xel neil, “Moxo wong lul sapa wo nimza. Moxo wong nenya qatu ngo wou me myatueing eno luk.”
MAR 8:1 Lek bouk tine eno xomaxoneing qendu ngandoung nge qekuma no. Gyeik xel xend lul yaeing ma, eno Yesu taxe e xe xel betiyeing lam wou e me neil,
MAR 8:2 “A laleing pyaxow en xomaxoneing beimambei ne, xel dei is ay woy teyei lek bouk yal ekom lul wei yaeing eno ma.
MAR 8:3 Wangwei a bong xel na bend is maxep, tyek xel mend bivek me pewilexe wou sakwaing, en nambei xel on valu lam anghei dingta.”
MAR 8:4 E xe xel betiyeing lewexe, “Ekom eivek beyeeng wei xel ma veil ne, tyek xey a qou belet e teyeimbei xey a bet xel?”
MAR 8:5 Yesu teling, “Xam ghe di qou belet vamva?” Xel neil, “Lim yuw o.”
MAR 8:6 Moxo neil wou xel qendu ngandoung on bei xel mendei lek tembuing. Woyom qou belet lim yuw on me wong dange wou Anutu, dom dembu me wong wou e xe xel betiyeing bei xel na bong enana wou xomaxoneing on, me xel pum wou xel qendu ngandoung on.
MAR 8:7 De xel di qou woing nayak matika is ambei nyon om moxo wong dange en woing is, me neil wou xel betiyeing bei xel dembu wou xel.
MAR 8:8 Xomaxoneing on ya me e den xel woy. Dekakom xel betiyeing qekuwou myapapu wei nanghei toundei eno eivek pasik lim yuw.
MAR 8:9 Xel teyei lek ambei 4,000 moux eno lam toundei. Me Yesu wong xel la,
MAR 8:10 de moxo lek la eivek bot is e xe xel betiyeing me la danghei wei Dalmanuta nei.
MAR 8:11 De Parisiyeiw lam me wo vevek wou qayeeng is Yesu. En xel embei daxe e, om xel neil wou e bei embong lulvako yo ti me talex dee wei tyoung gheyapu yo ti me talex bei Anutu wong e lam.
MAR 8:12 Moxo axe nimaying me poux laweeng me neil, “Nambei nya xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne mi teling ay en dee wei lulvako yo? A neil wou xam zonghek, tyek xel se gyei dee wei lulvako yo ti.”
MAR 8:13 Woyom moxo ghanaw xel, de lox me la eivek bot me la nge loxalu nei lek lounyeing.
MAR 8:14 Dom xel betiyeing naleind ma en qoueing belet, ekom inye tixemou wei xel qou is xow eivek bot o.
MAR 8:15 Yesu peti xel, “Xam ghe gwei xow teyei. Xam ghe gweiteyei xow en yis wei Parisiyeiw me ingwei Herot o is.”
MAR 8:16 Woyom xel betiyeing di luklek tine wouma me neil, “Beind moxo neil qayeeng tine en inye nambei belet ma veil xey.”
MAR 8:17 Yesu woulek qayeeng wei xel di neil wouma yon om teling xel, “Nambei nya xam ghe di luk wouma bei belet ma? Beip xam seng ghei wei o ghe woulek? Beip xam laleimim on nanghei di wo nikanzek?
MAR 8:18 Beip xam mamim toundei lek xam, ekom xam seng wei, me xam nenyamim nale lek xam, ekom xam seng ngo me xam seng wou naleimim?
MAR 8:19 Gyeik a dembu belet lim on wou xel 5,000, xam ghe qekuwou belet myapapu pup eivek pasik vamva?” Xel neil, “Xoumeeng yuw.”
MAR 8:20 “Me gyeik a dembu belet lim yuw on wou 4,000, xam ghe qekuwou myapapu pup eivek pasik vamva?” Xel lewexe, “Lim yuw.”
MAR 8:21 E neil wou xel, “Inyei xam seng ghei woulek?”
MAR 8:22 Xel lam tei Betsaida, me xomaxoneing valu qou moux matekeing ti me lam tay wou Yesu bei e ni mema lek e.
MAR 8:23 Moxo zeim moux matekeing on mema me qou e me la myayaing veil beyeeng. Gyeik ingwei pesuv myalouk lek moux on manghalus, de toung mema lek e, de Yesu teling, “Wang wei lulti?”
MAR 8:24 Moxo yeila me neil, “A xei xomaxoneing on eno di ghavineeng me lox me loum ekom xel xok ambei xax.”
MAR 8:25 Yesu lox toung mema lek moux on manghalus no. Woyom moxo ma yeila me wo nimza me e yei lul dalus on yanyateiv.
MAR 8:26 Yesu wong moxo la beeng, dom neil, “Wa seng na eivek beyeeng.”
MAR 8:27 Yesu me e xe xel betiyeing la ghavineeng eivek beyeeng nayak nayak wei toundei paviy Sisalia Pilipai. Xel di la wou sakwaing eno moxo teling xel, “Xomaxoneing mi neil embei ay eti?”
MAR 8:28 Xel neil elox, “Xel valu mi neil embei wa Yoan Lipekeing, de valu neil embei wa Eliya, de xel valu mi neil embei wang on poropet wei takwei eno ti.”
MAR 8:29 Moxo teling, “Dom nambei nya wou xam? Xam ghe mi neil embei ay eti?” Petele lewexe, “Wang on Kilisi yo.”
MAR 8:30 Yesu peti xel bei xel se neil e teyei wou xelti.
MAR 8:31 Woyom moxo teyoxe wou xel bei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux eno na qou myavanei ngenong me xel teivateiv wei Yuda yo me xel lumuki leitata, me xel putoung wei petieing o tyek pesek e de xomaxoneing tyek nyeis e mey deka bouk yal na veil eno moxo tyek qandi lek no.
MAR 8:32 Moxo neil eyeip yaing wou xel en tine, om Petele qou e me la nenyawes me neil e.
MAR 8:33 De Yesu pekwi me yei e xe xel betiyeing, moxo neil Petele. Yesu neil, “Sandang, la a deming! Wa seng wou naleim en lul wei Anutu yo, qe lul wei xomaxoneing o.”
MAR 8:34 Woyom moxo taxe xel qendu yon lam wou e is e xe xel betiyeing me neil: “Wangwei xelti embei betiwou ay, ond e daxow vun me qalei e xe xax pepeeng me betiwou ay.
MAR 8:35 En eti yeiw embei zeimaxoun e xe mapieing, on tyek na saing, dom eti yeiw embei saing xel xe mapieing en ay me Xoulek Nimza wei ay eno tyek mendei bo nimza.
MAR 8:36 Wangwei tambiy ti e qou lul dalus wei tembuing sapa ne yo, ekom na saing e xe mapieing nei, on tyek lulul wei e qou yon devind e nambei nya?
MAR 8:37 O moux on tyek bong vati na zeyi e xe nu pieing?
MAR 8:38 Om wangwei xelti nigyaleeng en ay me a xe xoulek eivek bouk wei xel xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne eno toung demind wou Anutu me wo sewokeing nilul wou xel ne mendghalus, yon tyek Xomaxoneing Neu Moux nigyaleeng en e gyeik ingwei embei noum eivek ma xe xeiyaing ngandoung is xel angela vambuing o.”
MAR 9:1 Me moxo neil wou xel, “A neil wou xam zonghek, xel valu wei toungale inye eno tyek se balwou meyeing qe ka xel gyei tete lalei wei Anutu xe yo nam is nikanzek bole.”
MAR 9:2 Ka bouk limti la veil le woyom Yesu qou Petele, Jems me Yoan is xow de qou lal me lek lukendu vaxading ti, wei xel venaxow la toundei yo. De nanghei inyei eno moxo neing pekwi wou lal mend.
MAR 9:3 E xe teimb on teltyip me wou teleing ghanaw eti yeiw lek tembuing sapa wei embei sekweyexe xel xe teimb bo pus o.
MAR 9:4 Woyom Eliya me Mose lam nale nanghei inyon wou lal mend me di luk is Yesu.
MAR 9:5 Petele neil wou Yesu, “Putoung, inye nimza bei xey a toumendei inye. Om xa bei sakev xomek sel yayal, ti wou wang, ti wou Mose de ti wou Eliya.”
MAR 9:6 (Moxo neil ambei nyon en se woulek bei na neil vati, en nambei lal yaleeng mouyo.)
MAR 9:7 Woyom laxap ti lam me li tenu zeyi xel, de vya ti lam eivek laxap me neil: “Tine inye a Neung Moux, e tiwei a laleing vind o. Xam a mi ngo e vya!”
MAR 9:8 Se wo lululek, en gyeik ingwei lal yei e vivekwou eno lal se lox yei xelti no is xel, qe Yesu venaxow.
MAR 9:9 Ka xel di loum axone veil lukendu, Yesu wong qayeeng nikanzek wou lal bei kandek lal se neil wou xelti en vati wei lal yei yo, qe ka Xomaxoneing Neu Moux qandi lek veil meyeing bole.
MAR 9:10 Lal zeimaxoun qayeeng on wou lal venaxow me di luklek, “Qandieing veil meyeing ne inye qes ambei nya?”
MAR 9:11 Woyom xel teling e, “Nambei nya putoung wei petieing o neil embei Eliya e nam atax?”
MAR 9:12 Yesu neil elox, “Neing o, Eliya lam atax, me menyex wou lul dalus lox eivek no. Ekom qayeeng nge eno xel byex eivek xoulek bei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux na qou myavanei ngandoung me xel pesek e?
MAR 9:13 Ekom a neil wou xam, Eliya vena lam o, me xel wong vati wei xel wou naleind en o dalus wou e. Nambei ingwei xel byex eivek xoulek en e yo.”
MAR 9:14 Gyeik xel loum wou xel betiyeing valu, xel yei xel qendu ngandoung ti vivekwou xel me xel putoung wei petieing o di pyalek ama is xel.
MAR 9:15 Se denlek en xomaxoneing dalus yei Yesu, xel etek me veimyend me la neil bendiyeing wou e.
MAR 9:16 Moxo teling, “Xam ghe di pyalek ama is xel en vati?”
MAR 9:17 Moux ti eivek qendu yon lewexe, “Putoung, a qou neung moux me na lam wou wang, en laweeng wei myatueing o ti nale eivek e om se mi luk.
MAR 9:18 Gyeik ingwei embei zeimaxoun e nikanzek, eno mi nex e lek tembuing. Moxo myapeleis mi taw lam lox e mya, de newou mi wo nyiknyik me mema vaxa mi wo nikanzek. A teling wou wa xe xel betiyeing bei xel a tiy laweeng nilul on na veil e ekom xel se teyei.”
MAR 9:19 Yesu neil elox, “O xam wei gweimbeeng ne xam xe wongeingis eno ma. Tyek a mi mendei is xam bouk vamva? Tyek a qalei nimaying wei xam o bouk vamva? Qou yak on me lam inye wou ay.”
MAR 9:20 Om xel qou moxo me lam wou e. Gyeik laweeng on yei Yesu, eno se wo lululek en bimexe yak on la wo peleipelei lek tembuing me myapeleis di taw lam lox e mya.
MAR 9:21 Yesu teling wou yak on ma, “Moxo mi wong ambei nye teyei lek bouk vamva?” E lewexe, “Gyeik ingwei e nanghei yak o.
MAR 9:22 Inye mi nex ela eivek nenyex o memiing lumama bei nyeis e mey. Ekom wangwei wa teyei being bo lulti wou, yon wa pyanaleim en xa me devind xa.”
MAR 9:23 Yesu neil, “Nambei nya wang neimbei ‘Wangwei wa teyei nei?’ Ond lul dalus ena teyei lek wou eti yeiw wei mi wongis o.”
MAR 9:24 Se wo lululek en ghavis on ma taxe lox, “A wongis o ekom a laleing wo yuw om wa devind ay!”
MAR 9:25 Gyeik Yesu yei xel qendu tiyon di veimyend me lam wou xel ne, moxo luk niseikeing wou laweeng nilaxes on. De moxo neil, “Wa laweeng wei nenya qatu me myatueing, a peti wang bei wang nam myayaing veil e dom wa seng nox me na eivek e no.”
MAR 9:26 Laweeng on nyayek me bimexe e niseikeing dom la myayaing veil e. Yak on xok ambei xel meyeing, om xel ngenong on neil embei, “Moxo mey o.”
MAR 9:27 Ekom Yesu zeim e mema me e nale lek vaxa, me nale ghey.
MAR 9:28 Ka Yesu lox xomek lalei, e xe xel betiyeing teling wou e xupekeing, “Nambei nya xa se teyeimbei tiy e na myayaing?”
MAR 9:29 E neil elox, “Lul ambei nye eno teyeimbei nam myayaing en zeimeing mema tixemou ne.”
MAR 9:30 Xel ghanaw beyeeng tiyon me la lox Galili. Yesu embei xelti se boulek ingwei xel toundei ghei yo,
MAR 9:31 en nambei e di teyoxe e xe xel betiyeing. Moxo neil wou xel, “Tyek xel a toung Xomaxoneing Neu Moux na eivek xomaxoneing memend. Tyek xel nyeis e mey, deka bouk yal ena veil, woyom moxo tyek qandi lek.”
MAR 9:32 Ekom xel se woulek vati wei e neil o qes de xel yaleeng om xel se teling e en inyon.
MAR 9:33 Xel lam tyip Kapenaom. Gyeik e la eivek xomek woy, moxo teling xel, “Xam ghe di lam wou sakwaing eno xam ghe pyalek ama en vati?”
MAR 9:34 Ekom xel toundei kanzek en nambei xel di lam wou sakwaing eno xel pyalek ama bei eti eivek xel eno wo lei ngandoung.
MAR 9:35 Yesu dei tembuing me taxe xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw on lam me neil, “Wangwei xelti embei na mya, ond e nam ti yusayang, me bong ambei xukxe wei xel dalus o.”
MAR 9:36 Moxo qou yak tika me wong e nale eivek xel senghoing. Dom qava e eivek mema me neil wou xel,
MAR 9:37 “Eti lalei vind yak ambei nye wei wongis me qou e eno qou a manghalus en a leing yond lalei vind me qou ay, me eti lalei vind ay me qou ay eno lalei se vind a maxow me qou ay, qe qou tambiy tiwei wong a lam o.”
MAR 9:38 Yoan neil, “Putoung, xa xei moux ti di tiy xel memo nangya wa leim om xa neil wou bei e tip, en nambei tambiy ne se mi betiy xey.”
MAR 9:39 Yesu neil, “Xam se neimbei e tip, en eti yeiw wei di wong lulvako eivek a leing eno tyek se neil nilul ti lek ay.
MAR 9:40 En eti yeiw wei se pesek xey, eno inyon xe xe.
MAR 9:41 A neil wou xam zonghek, eti bong mayamya memiing ti wou xam en a leing, en inye nambei xam on Kilisi xe, yond tyek se teyei bei saing e xe xouveing.
MAR 9:42 “Me wangwei tambiy ti embei bong yakyak on ti wei wongis ay eno detei en sewokeing, on Anutu tyek bong myaveweeng ngandoung ghanaw veil, nambei ingwei xel tup qakous ngandoung e vivekwou e kwa me banex ena eivek mamileeng o.
MAR 9:43 Wangwei wa memam bo wa detei en sewokeing, on wa qateiv veil. Inye nimza bei wang na eivek mapieing is memam tixemou de is mema yuw eno tyek wang na eivek nenyex wei se mi mey yo.
MAR 9:44 [Nanghei inyon eno xel xe meii se mi mey me nenyex se mi mey.]
MAR 9:45 Me wangwei wa vaxam bo wa detei en sewokeing nei, on wa qateiv veil. Inye nimza bei wang na eivek mapieing is vaxam tixemou, de wa vaxam yuw eno tyek xel banex wang na eivek beyeeng wei nenyex luta yo.
MAR 9:46 [Nanghei inyon eno xel xe meii se mi mey me nenyex se mi mey.]
MAR 9:47 Me wangwei wa mamghalus bo wa detei en sewokeing nei, yond qepei elam myayaing. Inye nimza bei wang na eivek tete lalei wei Anutu is mam tixemou dom se yuw, on tyek banex wang na eivek beyeeng wei nenyex luta yo,
MAR 9:48 nanghei inyon eno “‘xel meii mi byex xomaxoneing neing eno se mi tip, me nenyex se mi mey o.’
MAR 9:49 Nenyex tyek detei lek xomaxoneing sapa me bong xel bo vako nambei xel mi selew lulul en mileeng o.
MAR 9:50 “Mileeng on nimza, ekom wangwei e xe nenyeing on nama eno tyek wang teyei bei bong enox bo nenyeing ambei nya no? Xam ghe teyei lek mileeng om tyek xam mendei lalei vevopeing is ama.”
MAR 10:1 Woyom Yesu ghanaw beyeeng tiyon me la eivek tembuing danghei tiwei Yudia nei me la Yorodan veweeng aning. Xomaxoneing qendu ngandoung mi lam wou Yesu no om di teyoxe xel nambei e xe kwa wei e mi teyoxe xel o.
MAR 10:2 Parisi valu lam me wo axeing wou e om xel teling, “Beip inyei petieing lenghek bei moux qateiv iingama wei luw venei yo veil o ma?”
MAR 10:3 E neil elox, “Mose wong qayeeng petieing vati wou xam?”
MAR 10:4 Xel neil, “Mose lenghek lek bei moux a byex qapiya wei qateiveing iingama veil dom bong vex on na.”
MAR 10:5 Yesu neil elox, “Inyon Mose byex petieing tine wou xam en inye nambei xam laleimim on wo nikanzek.
MAR 10:6 Ekom eivek myaxeeng selis wei toung tembuing is tyoung eno ‘Anutu toung xomaxoneing valu moux de valu vex.’
MAR 10:7 ‘En qes tine moux tyek na veil ma luw ta de luw venei na toung lekti,
MAR 10:8 me tyek luw xouing bo neing tixemou.’ Om luw se wo yuw no qe neing tixemou.
MAR 10:9 Nambei nyon vati wei Anutu tendulekti, eno moux ti se qateiv.”
MAR 10:10 Gyeik xel toundei eivek xomek no, eno xel betiyeing teling Yesu en tine.
MAR 10:11 E lewexe, “Tambiy ti qateiv iingama wei luw venei yo veil, dom dii vex nge no, ond wong kwapesiv wei inye la sewok wou venei.
MAR 10:12 De wangwei vex on qateiv iingama wei luw leya yo veil, dom mendei wou moux nge ond vex on wo kwapesiv.”
MAR 10:13 Xel xomaxoneing on di qou yakyak me lam wou Yesu bei e niw mema lek xel, ekom xel betiyeing neil xel.
MAR 10:14 Gyeik Yesu yei tine, moxo lalei wo vanei om neil wou xel, “Wong yakyak on lam wou ay. Xam se zeimaxoun xel, en tete lalei wei Anutu xe yo inye xel yakyak ambei nye xe.
MAR 10:15 A neil wou xam zonghek, tambiy ti se teyei bei na eivek tete lalei wei Anutu xe yo wangwei e se ghok xel yakyak wei leind maeing ne.”
MAR 10:16 Om moxo qava yakyak on eivek mema me liw mema lek xel dom wo mata wou xel.
MAR 10:17 Ka Yesu di la wou sakwaing, moux ti veimya me la wou e me ev vaxa qatu eivek wou e. Moxo teling, “Putoung nimza, a bong vati en na qou mapieing luta luta wei Mang Anutu neil zonghek bei bong wou neuyeiw loxyus o?”
MAR 10:18 Yesu neil elox, “Nambei nya wang taxe ay nimza? Xelti se nimza qe Anutu venaxow.
MAR 10:19 Wang woulek qayeeng petieing ne woy: ‘Wa seng nyeis xelti na mey, wa seng bo kwapesiv, wa se panax, wa seng bo qayeeng tyonyeing me ghe bo qayeeng en xel nge, wa seng bong tyonyeing me tetei xel nge xe lulul, wa mi sanghoxe mam aluw tam.’ ”
MAR 10:20 E neil e lox wou e, “Putoung, qayeeng ti beimambei ne dalus eno a mi betiwou gyeik ingwei a yak o.”
MAR 10:21 Yesu yei e me lalei vind e. Moxo neil, “Wang ma en lul tika. La me wo vateivek lek lul dalus wei wang o de wong malew wou xel kanyo, on tyek wa qou lulul nimzamza eivek tyoung gheyapu. Dom lam betiwou ay.”
MAR 10:22 Moxo ngo qayeeng tine om yei manol. De la is lalei maying en nambei e xe lulul ngenongakes.
MAR 10:23 Yesu pekwi ma wou e xe xel betiyeing me neil wou xel, “Inye wo pok en xomaxoneing wei lulul ana embei na eivek tete lalei wei Anutu yo!”
MAR 10:24 Xel betiyeing etek en e xe qayeeng. Ekom Yesu neil no, “Xam neungyeiw, inye wo pok en ingwei laeing eivek tete lalei wei Anutu yo!
MAR 10:25 Inye wo pok en ingwei kamel embei na nox ying manghalus wei duweing lul en o, nambei nyon eno moux wei lulul ana eno inye wo pok ngandoung en ingwei embei na eivek tete lalei wei Anutu xe yo.”
MAR 10:26 Xel betiyeing etek ngandoung, me neil wouma, “Wangwei nambei nyon nei, on tyek eti na eivek Anutu xe tete lalei?”
MAR 10:27 Yesu yei xel bombek me neil, “Is xomaxoneing eno xel se teyei, ekom se nambei nyon is Anutu. Anutu teyeimbei bong lulul dalus.”
MAR 10:28 Petele neil wou e, “Wei, xa ghanaw xa xe lulul sapa dom na betiwou wang o!”
MAR 10:29 Yesu neil elox, “A neil zonghek wou xam, xel eti yeiw wei ghanaw bend o liyeiw moux o liyeiw vex o tayeiw o neuyeiw o xuk yaeing en ay me Xoulek Nimza ne,
MAR 10:30 de tyek xel a qou 100 lek mapu eivek bouk tine, me tyek xel a qou xomek ngenong, liyeiw moux, liyeiw vex, tayeiw, neuyeiw, me xuk yaeing ngenong, me tyek xel bo nol wou xel is de tyek loxyus eno xel a qou mapieing luta luta.
MAR 10:31 Ekom xel ngenong wei tax eno tyek nox yus dom xel wei loxyus eno natax.”
MAR 10:32 Xel di la wou sakwaing me la pu Yerusalem nei, me Yesu la mamunghexeing, de xel betiyeing eno di wou naleind ngenong me xel wei mi betiwou eno yaleeng. De qou xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw no me la nenyawes me neil wou xel en vati wei tyek nam belup wou e yo.
MAR 10:33 Moxo neil, “Wei, xey a bei na pu wei Yerusalem nei me tyek xel a neil Xomaxoneing Neu Moux teyei me na toung eivek xel lumuki leitata me putoung wei petieing o memend. Tyek xel bo qayeeng en e me natup qayeeng en embei nyeis e mey de bong e na wou xel amba,
MAR 10:34 wei tyek xel baluk yak lek e me pesuv myenlouk lek e, me sesa embo nol me nyeis e mey. Ka bouk yal nak veil moxo tyek qandi lek.”
MAR 10:35 Woyom Sebedi neu moux a luw lam wou e. Luw neil, “Putoung, uw ambei wang bong vati wei uw ambei teling wang en eno wou uw.”
MAR 10:36 Moxo teling, “Inye muw ambei am bong vati wou muw?”
MAR 10:37 Luw neil elox, “Gyeik wa mendei lek wa xe siaking is wa leim ngandoung, yon wong uw nge dei wou wa memam payeiv de nge mendei wou wa memam qeinz.”
MAR 10:38 Yesu neil, “Muw seng woulek vati wei muw ghe di teling en o. Muw ghe teyeimbei tyek na num eivek mayamya wei a num eivek o de muw ghe teyei bei zipek is lipekeing wei a lipek en ne?”
MAR 10:39 Luw lewexe, “Uw teyei.” Yesu neil wou luw, “Tyek muw teyei bei num eivek mayamya wei a num eivek ne, me ghe zipek is lipekeing wei a lipek is o,
MAR 10:40 ekom ingwei deing wou a memang payeiv o qeinz inyon se wou ay bei a zenghek lek. Beyeeng beimambei ne inye wou xel wei Anutu menyex woy wou xel o.”
MAR 10:41 Gyeik ingwei xel xoumeeng on ngo qayeeng en tine, xel laleind wo vanei wou Jems me Yoan.
MAR 10:42 Yesu taxe xel xouing lam wou e me neil, “Xam ghe woulek bei inyon eti yeiw wei xel yei bei inyei gyovaxa wei xel amba wei mi wo nikanzek lek yeing xel teyei, me xel wei wo lunkanzek en xel amba eno mi yeiteyei xel wo nikanzek.
MAR 10:43 Ekom se nambei nyon is wou xam. Qe eti yeiw wei embei bong lei ngandoung eivek xam senghoing, ond e mi bong ambei xam xe xukxe,
MAR 10:44 me eti yeiw embei na mamunghexeing eivek xam senghoing ond embong ambei xukxe bandaing wei xel dalus o.
MAR 10:45 En Xomaxoneing Neu Moux se lam bei xomaxoneing bo xuk wou e me devind e qe lam bei bong xuk me devind xomaxoneing ngenong me bong mapieing wei e yo nambei malew me na bey xel ngenong.”
MAR 10:46 Woyom xel lam Jeriko. Ka Yesu is e xe xel betiyeing, is xel qendu ngandoung on xel xouing lam veil beyeeng on me la eno matekeing ti lei Batimius inyon Timius neu moux toundei wou sakwaing nenyawes me tay lulul wou xel.
MAR 10:47 Gyeik e ngo bei inyon Yesu wei Nasaret o, moxo taxe bei, “Yesu Dawit Neu Moux, wa laleim e pyaxow en ay!”
MAR 10:48 Xel ngenongakes luk nikanzek wou e me neil wou embei denduing ma, ekom moxo taxe no niseikeing bei, “Dawit Neu Moux, wa laleim e pyaxow en ay!”
MAR 10:49 Yesu nale me neil, “Taxe e lam.” Om xel taxe la wou moux matekeing on, “Wang bo xeimlala dom bale lek vaxam! En moxo taxe wang o.”
MAR 10:50 Moxo nex e xe teimb ding nge mapu teila nenyawes, dom vyeip me la wou Yesu.
MAR 10:51 Yesu teling e, “Wambei a bong vati wou wang?” Moux matekeing neil, “Putoung, ambei gheina yo.”
MAR 10:52 Yesu neil, “La, wa xe wongeingis wong wang wo nimzalek.” Lutika eno moxo ma yeila dom betiwou Yesu me tupwou sakwaing.
MAR 11:1 Ka xel la paviy Yerusalem me la tyip Betpage me Betani lek lukendu Oliv nei, Yesu wong e xe xel betiyeing yayuw la,
MAR 11:2 de neil wou luw, “La wou beyeeng wei di yeip atax wou muw mamim on, de lutika gyeik muw ambeing na eivek, on tyek muw ghe gwei dongi lingheing ti xel tup anghei inyon, dongi lingheing tiyon xelti se ghei dei lek. Muw wa tul yis veil dom na qou me nam inye.
MAR 11:3 Wangwei xelti teling muw, ‘Muw ghe di wong ambei nyon enva?’ Yond muw a neil wou e, ‘Tambiy Ngandoung embei bong xuk en dom tyek bong enoum daing.’ ”
MAR 11:4 Luw la me yei dongi lingheing ti toungale myayaing eivek sakwaing mema nayak, me xel tup lek xomek mya om luw tul.
MAR 11:5 De xomaxoneing valu toungale inyon eno teling, “Inyon muw ghe di wong vati, me ghe di tul dongi lingheing on?”
MAR 11:6 Luw neil elox ambei kawei Yesu neil wou luw o, me xel xomaxoneing on wong luw qou me la.
MAR 11:7 Woyom luw qou dongi me la wou Yesu me nex xel xe teimb lek demi, de moxo dei lek.
MAR 11:8 Xomaxoneing ngenong vax xel xe teimb wei samyekeing o lek sakwaing de xel valu vax xax mema is lis wei xel qateiv eivek xuk yaeing o.
MAR 11:9 Xel wei la mamunghexeing me xel wei di betiy eno taxe bei, “Hosana! Xeilala wei xa yo ena wou tiwei lam eivek Tambiy Ngandoung lei yo!
MAR 11:10 Xeilala wei xa yo ena lek tete lalei wei xa bumi Dawit wei di lam o! Hosana ena gheyapu nei!”
MAR 11:11 Yesu la eivek Yerusalem me la eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o. Moxo yei e vivekwou lulul sapa, ekom inye embei bouk eivek om la myayaing me lox me la Betani is xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw.
MAR 11:12 Nge yanyeing wei xel di la veil Betani, eno maxepya Yesu.
MAR 11:13 Om yeila nanghei dingta me yei xax basunghek ti lis, om la en embei gyei bei ewo neing lek. Gyeik la tyip wou eno se yei lulti qe lis venaxow, en inye se bouk wei xax basunghek mi vuk o.
MAR 11:14 Woyom e neil wou xax, “Xelti tyek se nox me na gya neing lek wang no.” Me e xe xel betiyeing ngo ingwei e neil o.
MAR 11:15 Ka xel la tyip Yerusalem, Yesu la eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing me tiy eti yeiw wei di xouv me wo vateivek nanghei inyon o. Moxo qapyex lelek wei xel wei di pelipek malew wei xel bamba yo me qou malew wei xomek vambuing o me sia wei eti yeiw di wo vateivek lek beliy o,
MAR 11:16 me peti xel bei xelti se qalei lulul wei vateivek o me qateiv me na nox tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o.
MAR 11:17 Me ka e di teyoxe wou xel, moxo neil, “Inye xel byex eivek Anutu xe xoulek eno neil ambei nye: Yelemia 7:11 “‘A xe xomek tyek xel taxe bei inye xomek wei xel tembuing sapa nam a mi zeimemend eivek o.’ Ekom xam ghe wong e wo ‘xomek xupekeing wei xel panaxana yo.’”
MAR 11:18 Xel lumuki leitata me putoung wei petieing o ngo tine me yimexe sakwaing wei xel embei nyeis e mey yo, xel yaleeng en e, en nambei xel dalus wei qekuma yon etek en e xe teyoxeing.
MAR 11:19 Gyeik ingwei bouk eivek eno xel lam veil beyeeng ngandoung on me la.
MAR 11:20 Eivek satiboukeing, ka xel di la wou sakwaing, eno xel yei xax basunghek mupek lek luselis me la pundanghou.
MAR 11:21 Petele wounalei en me neil wou Yesu, “Putoung, wei! Xax basunghek wei wang neil vyam lek eno mupek on!”
MAR 11:22 Yesu lewexe, “Xam ghe bongis Anutu.
MAR 11:23 A neil wou xam zonghek, wangwei xelti e neil wou lukendu tine, ‘Qandi me nex xow la eivek mamileeng,’ me e lalei se bo yuw qe e bongis vati wei neil, on tyek bo neing lek ambei kawei e neil o.
MAR 11:24 Nambei nyon a neil wou xam, vati wei xam ghe zeimemamim en, eno xam ghe bongis bei xam ghe qou woy, me inyon tyek bong ambei xam ghe teling en o.
MAR 11:25 Me gyeik wa bale en zeimeing mema me wangwei wa laleim embo nilul wou xel nge, ond semaleeng e xe sewokeing veil e, en kandek Mam wei toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu nei eno semaleeng wa xe sewokeing veil.”
MAR 11:27 Xel la tyip Yerusalem no, me ka Yesu di ghavineeng eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o, xel lumuki leitata me putoung wei petieing o me xel teivateiv lam wou e.
MAR 11:28 Xel teling, “Lulul wei gweimbeeng ne eno wang di wong nangya eti lei me eti wong lei ne wou wang bei wang bong tine?”
MAR 11:29 Yesu neil elox, “Tyek am bong telinyeing ti wou xam. Xam ghe zewexe lek ay, on tyek a neil wou xam en lei wei andi wong lulti beimambei ne nangya ne.
MAR 11:30 Xam neil wou ay. Yoan xe lipekeing, inyon lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei, o lam wou xomaxoneing?”
MAR 11:31 Xel di luklek inyon wouma eivek xel venaxow senghoing me neil, “Wangwei xey a neimbei, ‘Nanghei tyoung gheyapu,’ on tyek moxo teling, ‘Ekom nambei nya xam seng wongis e?’
MAR 11:32 Ek wangwei xey a neimbei, ‘Yoan xe lipekeing on lam wou xomaxoneing on inyon se teyei,’” en xel yaleeng en vati wei xomaxoneing tyek bong o, en xel dalus wongis bei Yoan on poropet ti neing ayang.
MAR 11:33 Om xel lewexe lek Yesu, “Xa loungen.” Yesu neil, “Tyek a se neil teyeimbei eti wong lei ne wou ay me andi wong lulti beimambei ne.”
MAR 12:1 Woyom Yesu luk wou xel teivateiv eivek qayeeng pakeing. “Tambiy ti ev xuk wain. E qo tete vivekwou, me ev leiveeng wei qeing wain o, me ev xomek vaxading wei yeingteyei xuk wain o. Woyom moxo toung xuk wain eivek xel valu memend bei xel bo xuk vateivek lek me dembu wain neing wou ma, veweeng wou xuk ma de veweeng wou xel venaxow dom la beyeeng dingta.
MAR 12:2 Lek bouk wei uleing wain neing eno moxo wong xukxe ti la wou xel wei mi yeiteyei xuk bei na qou wain neing valu eivek xuk wain.
MAR 12:3 Ekom xel zeimaxoun e, me leis e wo nol dom wong moxo lox me la mema nivax.
MAR 12:4 Woyom moxo wong xukxe nge la wou xel, me xel sesa moux tine lek e lu de xel se ngo e vya qe xel wo niyalenyeing ngandoung wou e.
MAR 12:5 E wong xukxe nge lox no, om tiyon mou xel leis e mey. E wong xel ngenongakes la, ekom xel sesa valu, de xel leis xel valu mey.
MAR 12:6 “E xe tixemou tateis toundei en ingwei embei bong ena yo, neu moux tiwei e lalei vind o. E wong ela ti yusayang, me neil, ‘Tyek xel gwevek a neung xe qayeeng.’
MAR 12:7 “Ekom xel xukxe wei wain o neil wouma, ‘Tambiy tine tyek na qou ma xe lulul dalus. Xam lam en xey a nyeis e mey o, dom lulul dalus on tyek inyon xe xe.’
MAR 12:8 Om xel zeimaxoun e me leis e mey, dom nex e la myayaing veil xuk wain.
MAR 12:9 “Woyom Yesu teling xel “tyek xuk wain ma bo vati? Tyek moxo nam dom nyeis xel xukxe dom bong xuk wain na wou xel bange.
MAR 12:10 Beip xam seng mi pyaw xoulek tine? “‘Qakous mundeeng ti wei xel kamunda pesek, eno wong ambei qakous ti myaxeeng wei nale me mi byexaxoun xomek o.
MAR 12:11 Tambiy Ngandoung wong tine, me xa xei lek mami me inye wo etekeing wou xa.’”
MAR 12:12 Woyom xel leitata yimexe sakwaing ti en xel embei zeimaxoun e en nambei xel woulek bei e neil qayeeng pakeing lek xel. Ekom xel yaleeng en xel qendu ngandoung on, om xel ghanaw e me la.
MAR 12:13 Kalekom xel wong Parisi valu me xel wei Herot o valu la wou Yesu bei tandei e en emaxow xe qayeeng wei embei neil ena sewok o.
MAR 12:14 Xel lam wou e me neil, “Putoung, xa woulek bei wang on tambiy neing. Wa seng mi waleeng en xelti, me wa seng mi wei bei inyon xel eti yeiw, qe wang mi teyoxe sakwaing wei Anutu yo me ghe betiwou qayeeng zonghek. Om petieing neil embei xey a toung takis wou Sisa o xe se toung?
MAR 12:15 Xey a toung o xe se toung?” Ekom Yesu woulek bei xel on myend yuw om neil wou xel bei, “Nambei nya xam ghe di tandei ay? Qou selewa ti lam wou ay, me a xei.”
MAR 12:16 Xel qou selewa ti me lam, om moxo teling xel, “Eti xe tenu ing tine? Me eti lei inye?” Xel neil elox, “Sisa.”
MAR 12:17 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel, “Xam ghe bong vati wei Sisa xe yo wou Sisa, dom ghe bong vati wei Anutu xe yo wou Anutu.” Om xel on etek en e.
MAR 12:18 Woyom xel Sadyusi, wei mi neil embei xel meyeing tyek se qandi lek eno lam wou e is telinyeing ti.
MAR 12:19 Xel neil, “Putoung, Mose byex qayeeng wou xey bei wangwei moux ti li na mey de venei nanghei toundei ekom neu ma, yond moux tiyon dii vexeiv on me bo li neuyeiw.
MAR 12:20 Woyom xel lim yuw lindama eno toundei. Tiwei tax eno ii vex on me mey ekom se wo neu ti.
MAR 12:21 Li nge wei yuw eno ii vexeiv on dom mey is, ekom se wo neu ti. Kwa kayon eno li tiwei yal o betiwou.
MAR 12:22 Om nambei nyon eno xel lim yuw on ti se wong neuyeiw ti, dekakom vex on mey loxyus en xel dalus.
MAR 12:23 Lek bouk wei qandieing lek, eno tyek vex on eti venei? En inyon xel lim yuw ii vex tiyon.”
MAR 12:24 Yesu neil elox, “Xam ghe neil qayeeng on la sewok en xam seng woulek xoulek wei dei yeip eivek qapiya me nikanzek wei Anutu yo.
MAR 12:25 Gyeik bouk wei xel meyeing qandi lek, eno xel se teyeimbei diima me diima nox me noum, tyek xel ghok ambei xel angela wei tyoung gheyapu yo.
MAR 12:26 De qayeeng wei meyeing e qandi lek, beip inye xam seng pyaw eivek qapiya wei Mose me eivek pavulek wei nenyex tum lek xax nayaka yo, de eivek pavulek wei Anutu neil wou e yo, ‘A ne Anutu wei Apraham, Anutu wei Isaka me Anutu wei Yakop o?’
MAR 12:27 Moxo se Anutu wei xel meyeing, qe e Anutu wei xel wei mapieing. Om qayeeng wei xam ghe neil on eno la sewok.”
MAR 12:28 Putoung wei petieing o ti lam me ngo xel di pyaw lekama lox me loum is Yesu. Me ngo bei Yesu lewexe lek qayeeng on wo nimza, om teling e, “Qayeeng petieing tina, inye ngandoung ghanaw veil en qayeeng petieing dalus?”
MAR 12:29 Yesu lewexe, “Tiwei ngandoung ghanaw veil eno inye: ‘Xam Israel ngo, Tambiy Ngandoung xe xe Anutu, emaxow tixemou yon Tambiy Ngandoung.
MAR 12:30 Xam laleimim devind Tambiy Ngandoung xam xe Anutu is laleimim dalus me is numim pieing dalus me is xam lumimpeyei dalus me is xam nimim kanzek dalus.’
MAR 12:31 Nge wei yuw eno inye: ‘Wa laleim e mi devind nimpapu nambei wa laleim mi vind xow o.’ Qayeeng petieing ti se ngandoung ghanaw yuw ne.”
MAR 12:32 Moux on neil elox, “Putoung, wang neil neing bei Anutu yon tixemou me xel ba ma dom emaxow.
MAR 12:33 Laleim vind e is laleim dalus me is wa lumpeyei dalus me is wa nimkanzek dalus me wa laleim devind nimpapu nambei wa laleim mi vind venaxow o. Inyon ngandoungateiv ghanaw xound wei seing dalus o me da leimalei.”
MAR 12:34 Gyeik Yesu yei bei e neil qayeeng nambei xel wei lupeyei nimza, om neil wou e, “Wa seng dei dingta veil tete lalei wei Anutu yo.” De woyom xel yaleeng om xelti se lox teling e no.
MAR 12:35 Ka Yesu di teyoxe xel eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o, e teling, “Nambei nya ekom xel putoung wei petieing o neil embei Kilisi yon Dawit neu?
MAR 12:36 Dawit venaxow neil angya Laweeng Vambuing, me neilteyei bei: “‘Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou a xe Tambiy Ngandoung: “Wa mendei wou a memang payeiv deka a toung wa xe xel vevek amba na xeinghembi eivek wa vaxam bole.”’
MAR 12:37 Dawit venaxow taxe Kilisi ne Tambiy Ngandoung. Nambei nya Kilisi yon Dawit neu is ambei nyon?” Xel qendu ngandoung on liw nenyend wou e is xeindlala.
MAR 12:38 Ka Yesu teyoxe xel, eno neil, “Xam ghe gwei xow teyei en xel putoung wei petieing o. Xel embei mi ghavineeng is teimb ding me xel embei xel a mi neil bendiyeing teiv wou xel eivek beyeeng wei vateivek o,
MAR 12:39 me xel embei mi mendei lek sia nimza wei xel wei leitata mi deilek o eivek xomek qekueing ama me mindei lek sia nimza wei tax wei xel lei laeing o eivek mata ngandoung.
MAR 12:40 Xel mi tyoxe xel vexeiv me qou xel xe xomek me talex xow en zeimeing mema ding. Xel moux ambei nyon eno tyek na qou myaveweeng ngandoung ghanaw xel bamba.”
MAR 12:41 Yesu dei paviy ingwei xel mi toung da nanghei yo, me di yei bembeeng vex alis moux di toung xel xe da la eivek qoupek malew wei xomek vambuing o. Xomaxoneing ngenong wei lulul ana eno toung malew ngandoung.
MAR 12:42 Ekom vexeiv kanyo ti eno lam me toung selewa nayak yayuw, nikanzek wei selewa ne eno teyei lek selewa gyand ti.
MAR 12:43 Yesu taxe e xe xel betiyeing lam wou e, me neil, “A neil wou xam zonghek, vexeiv kawei kanyo ne eno toung malew ngandoung eivek qoupek malew wei xomek vambuing o ghanaw xel bamba dalus.
MAR 12:44 En xel dalus wong xel xe lulul dalus eivek lulul ngenong wei xel o. Ekom vex on lulul ma dom wong e xe kayo dalus, de wong ingwei embei toumendei mapieing en eno dalus.”
MAR 13:1 Ka Yesu la veil tete wei xomek vambuing, eno e xe betiyeing ti neil wou e, “Putoung! Wei, qakous qakous ngandoung nimza yon, me xomek nimzamza yon.”
MAR 13:2 Yesu lewexe, “Wang wei xomek ngandoung dalus ne? Qakous ne ti tyek se mendei lek nge mapu, qe tyek xel lelolexe dalusateiv dom banex e deteina.”
MAR 13:3 Ka Yesu dei lek lukendu Oliv nei wou xomek vambuing vi valu nei, Petele me Jems, Yoan me Andrias xel teling wou e xupekeing,
MAR 13:4 “Neil wou xa, gyeik inya ekom lulti beimambei ne nam atyip? Me dee vati tyek xa boulek bei lul dalus ne embim bo neing lek?”
MAR 13:5 Yesu neil wou xel, “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow, en kandek xelti se nam a tyoxe xam.
MAR 13:6 Xel ngenong tyek nam lek a leing, me na neimbei, ‘A Mesia,’ me tyek xel a tyoxe xel ngenong.
MAR 13:7 Gyeik xam a ngo xel vevek ngandoung me qayeeng laweeng en xel vevek ngandoung o, on xam seng detek, lul ambei nyon tyek nam atyip, ekom bouk loxyus eno nanghei.
MAR 13:8 En xomaxoneing wei tembuing nge tyek qandi lek me bo vevek is xomaxoneing wei tembuing nge yo, tete lalei nge tyek bo vevek is tete lalei nge, me tyek inyon tembuing api eivek beyeeng valu beti, me maxep ngandoung tyek nam. Lulti beimambei ne tyek nam myaxeeng nambei vex wei mi axe vanei natax en ingwei yak mi umbek o.
MAR 13:9 “Xam a mi gwei xow teyei. En tyek xel a zeim xam me na qou me na wou xel kanzol me xel sesa xam eivek xomek qekueing ama. Tyek xam bale wou lei ngandoung wei seyap o mendghalus me king en ay. De tyek xam a tul pavulek wou xel en vati wei xam ghe wei lek mamim o eno wou xel.
MAR 13:10 Me xam a neil Xoulek Nimza wou xomaxoneing tembuing sapa yo bole.
MAR 13:11 Gyeik ingwei xel embei zeimaxoun xam me bo qayeeng en xam on xam seng bounaleim ngenong en vati wei xam ambei neil o. Xam a neil vati wei Anutu wong wou xam lek bouk kayon bombek. En inye xam venaxow tyek se baluk qe Laweeng Vambuing tyek na neil inyon teyei.
MAR 13:12 “Li moux tyek na neil li moux teyei me na toung e na eivek xel memend me xel nyeis e mey, de mayeiw tyek bong ambei inyon wou neuyeiw. Neuyeiw tyek bo nol wou mamata me na toung xel na eivek meyeing.
MAR 13:13 Me xomaxoneing dalus tyek laleind bo vanei wou xam en ay, ekom eti embei bale nikanzek me ena bouk loxyus wei lulul ne embei na tip lek on tyek Anutu devind xel en xel se mey.
MAR 13:14 “Deka xam ghe gwei lul nilul ayang, wei mi wo nol wou lulul eno na bale nanghei beyeeng vambuing wei tyek se teyeimbei bale yo.” (Yon xam wei ghe mi pyaw qayeeng ne eno xam woulek.) “De wong xel wei toundei eivek Yudia nei pek me la lukendu qendu nei.
MAR 13:15 Wangwei xelti na toumendei lek xomek demi qetyei eno tyek douk me noum, de se na eivek e xe xomek lalei me na qou vati wei e yo me na myayaing.
MAR 13:16 Wangwei xelti la toundei eivek xuk yaeing eno tyek se nox xomek me na qou e xe teimb ding nge.
MAR 13:17 Tyek inye bo nilul eivek bouk kayon en xel vex wei xeipouyek o me xel tayeiw wei di wo luul wou neuyeiw o!
MAR 13:18 Xam a zeimemamim wou Anutu en kandek lul tine e se nam eivek bouk wei laweeng nityuweing wei nigheghoing o,
MAR 13:19 en bouk ti beimambei yon tyek bo bouk wei nimaying ngandoung me tyek se teyei lek nambei myaxeeng selis wei Anutu toung tembuing me elam tyip gweimbeeng ne yo me lul nimaying ti tyek se nox teyei lek no.
MAR 13:20 Wangwei Tambiy Ngandoung se qateiv bouk wei nimaying eno bo sepi, on tyek xelti se mendei mapieing, ekom wounalei en e xe xel wei beyal wou emaxow o, om qateiv bouk wo sepi.
MAR 13:21 Lek seivma kayon, wangwei xelti e neil wou xam, ‘Wei, Kilisi inye!’ o ‘Wei, e inyei!’ yond xam seng bongis e xe qayeeng.
MAR 13:22 En xomaxoneing tyonyeing valu tyek na neimbei a Kilisi o a poropet eno tyek nam a tyip me bong dee me lulvako valu wangwei xel teyei nei on tyek xel dandiy xomaxoneing wei Anutu beyal o.
MAR 13:23 Om xam ghe gweiteyei xow. A neil wou xam atax en lul dalus wei bouk tine embei nam o.
MAR 13:24 “Ka bouk ti beimambei wei nimaying ngandoung ne na ma veil, “ ‘Eno sayeiv tyek bo mapetok, me dentouk tyek se tel,
MAR 13:25 de betum tyek detei nanghei tyoung, de lul nikanzek wei tyoung dalusateiv ne eno tyek bo pimapi.’
MAR 13:26 “Woyom lek bouk kayon eno xomaxoneing tyek gyei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek nam eivek laxap ngandoung is nikanzek ngandoung me xeiyaing ngandoung.
MAR 13:27 Me tyek bong e xe xel angela na qekuwou e xe xel wei beyal o eivek beyeeng dalusateiv me e na tembuing sapa nei, nanghei ingwei tembuing la tip lek o, me ena ingwei tyoung dalus la tip lek o.
MAR 13:28 “De xam ghe boulek xax basunghek, gyeik ingwei xax mema byex lis vako lek woy, yon xam ghe boulek bei, buk wei seiv embei siing eno lam paviy.
MAR 13:29 Om nambei nyon, gyeik ingwei xam ghe gwei lul beimambei wei a neil wou xam en o belup, on xam ghe boulek bei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux lam paviy, me toungale wou qapomb.
MAR 13:30 A neil wou xam zonghek, xel qendu ti gweimbeeng ne tyek se mey qe ka lul dalus ti beimambei ne nam atyip bole.
MAR 13:31 Tyoung me tembuing tyek nati, ekom a xe qayeeng tyek se nati.
MAR 13:32 “Xelti se woulek bouk o seivma, me angelayeiw eivek tyoung gheyapu eno se woulek, o Neu moux se woulek is, qe Ma venaxow.
MAR 13:33 Xam ghe gwei xow teyei me mendi daxe! En xam seng woulek bouk kayon bombek.
MAR 13:34 Inye nambei tambiy ti la dingta. Gyeik ingwei moxo la veil beeng dom toung e xe xukxe bei xel a mi gyeiteyei e xe lulul, de pum xuk wou xel titi bei xel bong dom neil wou tiwei mi nale zeyi xomek mya bei e mi gyeiteyei.
MAR 13:35 “Nambei nyon xam a mi gweiteyei me ghe daxe en xam seng woulek bouk gyeik ingwei xomek ma embei noum o, beip eivek soukeing, o boukeing masenghoing, o gyeik ingwei qouklex sesa vya, o di nexla yo.
MAR 13:36 Wangwei e noum lutika nei, on wei xam seng bong e gyei ingwei xam ghe di weip o.
MAR 13:37 Vati wei a neil wou xam, eno a neil wou xel dalus, ‘Xam a mi gweiteyei me ghe daxe!’ ”
MAR 14:1 Bouk yuw nanghei di yeip zeyi mata ngandoung wei Pasova me mata wei Yaeing Belet Wei Yis Ma Veil o. Om xel lumuki leitata me xel putoung wei petieing eno xel di yimexe sakwaing en xel embei zeimaxoun Yesu xupekeing dom nyeis e mey.
MAR 14:2 En xel neil, “Xey ambei se bong ambei nye lek bouk ngandoung wei lalo yo, enok xel xomaxoneing ne na neilama de vevek qandi lek.”
MAR 14:3 Ka Yesu la eivek beyeeng Betani, me la toundei eivek Simon beeng, tambiy yon takwei eno qou vanei lepa me di ya lek zek, de vex ti lam is botol qakous wei wel xeimangou wei malew ngandoung o, me lam dembu botol qakous on dom taw wel lek Yesu lu.
MAR 14:4 Xel valu wei toundei inyon eno yei tiyon om xel laleind wo nol me luk ngenong wouma, “Nambei nya ekom vex ne wo nol wou wel ne?
MAR 14:5 Wel tine teyeimbei xey a bong vateivek lek me na qou malew selewa teyei lek xouveing wei vakovek qes ti yo de na bong wou xel kanyo.” De xel neil vex on.
MAR 14:6 Yesu neil, “Nambei nya xam ghe wong nimaying wou vex ne? Xam wong e toundei, vex ne wong lul nimza ne wou ay.
MAR 14:7 Xel wei kanyo eno tyek na mi mendei is xam takwei takwei, om xam a mi devind xel taxombouk teyei lek ingwei xam ambei bong o. Dom ay ne tyek a se mendei is xam taxombouk.
MAR 14:8 Lul vati wei vex on teyeimbei bong eno e wong woy de taw wel lek a neing atax en menyex wou aning meyeing en eveing.
MAR 14:9 A neil wou xam zonghek, xel embei mi neil Xoulek Nimza nanghei inyayeiw eivek tembuing sapa eno tyek xel a mi tul pavulek en vati wei vex ne wong wou a ne, eno tyek xel a mi bou naleind en e.”
MAR 14:10 Woyom Yudas Iskariot, Yesu xe betiyeing xoumeeng yuw eno ti, la wou xel lumuki leitata me neil e teyei wou xel bei tyek na toung Yesu na eivek xel memend.
MAR 14:11 Xel ngo qayeeng tiwei Yudas neil ne om xel wo xeindlala. Me neil zonghek wou e bei tyek xel bong malew valu wou e. Om di yimexe sakwaing wei embei toung Yesu na eivek xel memend o.
MAR 14:12 Lek bouk tiwei tax wei Bouk Wei Yaeing Belet Wei Yis Ma Veil eno lam. Om xel betiwou kwa wei xel mi leis sipsip lingheing en yaeing lek bouk wei Pasova yo, eno xel betiyeing neil wou Yesu bei, “Wambei xa na menyex wou mata wei bouk Pasova nanghei tina en kandek wang na gwa eivek?”
MAR 14:13 Woyom Yesu wong xel betiyeing yuw la, me neil wou luw ambei nye, “Muw ghe na eivek Yerusalem nei. Moux ti tyek qalei deng mouing is memiing me nam pelong muw, ond muw betiwou e.
MAR 14:14 De muw a neil wou xomek ma tiwei embei deivek na yo bei, ‘Putoung teling, “A xe xomek lalei toundei inya, wei ambei gha yaeing wei bouk Pasova yo is a xe xel betiyeing ne yo?”’
MAR 14:15 Moxo tyek talex xomek lalei ngandoung nge wei di yeip gheyapu eno wou muw, me lulul wei yaeing lek o me deing lek eno xel menyex wou woy. Muw menyex wou lulul yaeing wou xey anghei inyon.”
MAR 14:16 Betiyeing aluw la, me la eivek beyeeng on me yei lul dalus e la teyei lek ambei kawei Yesu neil wou luw o. Om luw menyex wou mata wei bouk Pasova yo nanghei inyon.
MAR 14:17 Gyeik ingwei bouk eivek eno Yesu lam tyip is e xe xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw.
MAR 14:18 Ka xel toundei lek lelek me di ya, moxo neil, “A neil wou xam zonghek bei, tyek xam ti venaxow na neil a teyei me na toung ay eivek xel ba memend, tambiy tiwei di ya yaeing is a ne.”
MAR 14:19 Moxoyeiw laleind wo nimaying, om xel titi di teling wou e, “Beip inye se ay, ei?”
MAR 14:20 Moxo neil elox, “Xam xoumeeng yuw on ti, tiwei di ya belet lek dipek is ay ne.
MAR 14:21 Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek betiwou sakwaing kawei xel byex eivek xoulek wei Anutu en e yo. Ekom inye wo lalei pyaweing en tambiy tiwei embei neil Xomaxoneing Neu Moux teyei me na toung e na eivek xel ba memend o, eno tyek na qou myaveweeng ghanaw veil. Om inye nimza bei moux tiyon ta se bou e.”
MAR 14:22 Ka xel di ya, Yesu qou belet, me wong dange wou dom dembu, me wong wou e xe xel betiyeing, me neil, “Xam qou, tine inye a neing.”
MAR 14:23 Woyom moxo qou mayamya wain, me wong dange wou dom wong wou xel, me xel dalus num eivek.
MAR 14:24 Yesu neil wou xel, “Tine inye a xe gyand wei na byexaxoun qokatu yo, wei a qapyex bei devind xomaxoneing ngenong o.
MAR 14:25 A neil wou xam zonghek, tyek a se nox me na num wain neing no qe ka gyeik bouk wei a num wain vako eivek tete lalei wei Anutu yo.”
MAR 14:26 Gyeik xel wong lalo ti woy, xel la myayaing me la lukendu Oliv.
MAR 14:27 Yesu neil wou xel, “Xam dalus xe wongeingis tyek detei veil en xel byex eivek xoulek wei Anutu yo eno nambei nye: “ ‘Tyek a nyeis gyovaxa wei sipsip o, dom tyek sipsip na pek me davuna.’
MAR 14:28 Ekom ka a qandi lek veil meyeing le, tyek a na tax en xam me nana Galili.”
MAR 14:29 Petele neilteyei, “Wangwei xel dalus xe wongeingis detei veil me xel na veil wang, on tyek a se teyeimbei na veil wang.”
MAR 14:30 Yesu lewexe, “A neil zonghek wou wang, gweimbeeng boukeing wei qouklex seng ghei sesa vya luyuw eno tyek wamaxow ghe dax a vun luyal.”
MAR 14:31 Ekom Petele nale nikanzek en qayeeng me neil wou Yesu, “Ma mouyo wangwei a mey is wang nei on tyek a se teyeimbei dax wang vun!” Me xel betiyeing dalus neil ambei nyon teyeima.
MAR 14:32 Xel la beyeeng ti lei bei Getsemani, me Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing, “Xam a toumendei inye dom a na zeimemang.”
MAR 14:33 Om Yesu qou Petele luw Jems me Yoan me lal la is e, ekom moxo axe nimaying ngandoung me lalei wo nimaying.
MAR 14:34 Yesu neil wou xel, “A axe nimaying ngandoung lek xow teyeimbei a mey. Mal a toumendei inye me ghe gweiteyei teyei embo nimza.”
MAR 14:35 Yesu dula nayaka, de teila yeip ma eivek tembuing dom zeimema bei wangwei inye teyei nei ond nimaying ne deteina veil e.
MAR 14:36 Moxo neil, “Aba, Mang, lulul sapa yon teyeimbei wang bong. Zeim mayamya tine veil ay. Ekom wa se betiwou a laleing, qe wa betiwou wamaxow laleim.”
MAR 14:37 Woyom Yesu loumelam wou e xe betiyeing a lal me yei lal di yeip. E neil wou Petele, “Simon, wa ghei di weip? Inye se teyeimbei wam di gweina nayaka, ei?
MAR 14:38 Om mal mendi gweiteyei teyei me na zeimemamim en kandek mal se detei en axeing. Xam laleimim embei bong xuk, ekom neing wo nimaing.”
MAR 14:39 Lox me la lunge no me zeimema nambei nge tax o.
MAR 14:40 Gyeik e loumelam, e yei lal lox me la yeip no, en nambei lal mendghalus wo nimaying. Om lal se wou naleind en vati wei lal embei neil wou e yo.
MAR 14:41 Yesu loumelam tiwei luyal o, dom neil wou lal, “Mal anghei di weip me ghe qou laweeng. Woy, seivma lam o. Wei, Xomaxoneing Neu Moux xel embei neil e teyei me na toung e na eivek xel wei sewokeing o memend.
MAR 14:42 Mal qandi lek! Me xey a la! Wei, tiwei embei neil a teyei me na toung a na eivek xel memend eno lam tyip on!”
MAR 14:43 Ka Yesu nanghei di neil qayeeng, Yudas wei betiyeing xoumeeng yuw eno ti lam tyip is xel qendu ngandoung on, xel zeim ngeyeing vevek me pebumeeng, xel lumuki leitata, me putoung wei petieing o me xel teivateiv eno wong xel lam.
MAR 14:44 Tambiy tiwei embei neil Yesu teyei me na toung e na eivek xel vevek memend eno talex dee ti wou xel bei, “Tambiy tiwei ambei sesuvexe eno, tiyo inyon, om xam a zeimaxoun e me ghe gweiteyei de na qou e me na.”
MAR 14:45 Yudas lam me la daing wou Yesu me neil wou bei, “Putoung!” Dom sesuvexe e.
MAR 14:46 Om xel xomaxoneing on zeimaxoun Yesu.
MAR 14:47 Woyom xel wei toungale paviy yon ti tetei e xe ngeyeing vevek me qateiv xukxe wei lumuki lukanzek on nenyalis nge tip me teila.
MAR 14:48 Yesu neil wou xel, “Xam ambei a panaxana ti, om xam ghe lam is ngeyeing vevek me pebumeeng bei nam a zeimaxoun a ne?
MAR 14:49 Teyei lek bouk tambak eno a mindei is xam, me na wo teyoxeing eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o, ekom xam seng zeimaxoun ay. En qayeeng wei yeip eivek Anutu xe xoulek eno embo neing lek.”
MAR 14:50 Woyom xel betiyeing dalus ghanaw e de pek me la.
MAR 14:51 Xomaxoneing ghavis ti, se byex lulti qe teimb teleing ti wei sevun xow eno ti, me di betiwou Yesu gyeik ingwei xel zeimaxoun e yo,
MAR 14:52 ekom moxo pek veil xel xeitouk me la dom ghanaw e xe teimb teleing on toundei yus.
MAR 14:53 Xel qou Yesu me la wou lumuki lukanzek, de xel lumuki leitata dalus me teivateiv, me putoung wei petieing o xel xouing lam qekuma.
MAR 14:54 Petele di betiwou e me la kwanding, me la eivek tete lalei wei xomek wei lumuki lukanzek o, nanghei inyon eno la dei is xel belimbo wei mi yeiteyei xomek vambuing o me di pavang xow wou nenyex.
MAR 14:55 Xel lumuki leitata is xel kanzol dalus eno di yimexe pavulek wei e wong esewok o en ingwei xel embei nyeis e mey yo, ekom xel se yeiwou ti.
MAR 14:56 Xel ngenong byex qayeeng tyonyeing lek e, ekom xel xe qayeeng se la teyeima.
MAR 14:57 Woyom xel valu nale ghey me wong pavulek tyonyeing tine lek e:
MAR 14:58 “Xa ngo e neil, ‘Tyek a lelolexe xomek vambuing tine wei xomaxoneing ev ne dom eivek bouk yal eno tyek a dev nge no, wei xomaxoneing se ev angya memend o.’”
MAR 14:59 Ekom pavulek wei xel neil on la bandabanda de se teyeima.
MAR 14:60 Woyom lumuki lukanzek eno nale wou xel mend me teling Yesu, “Qayeeng vati ingwei xel moux tine di byex lek wang ne? Se teyeimbei wa neil qayeeng ti nox wou xel?”
MAR 14:61 Ekom Yesu toungale kanzek de se neil qayeeng ti lox. Lumuki lukanzek lox me la teling wou e no, “Inye wa Kilisi. Anutu wei xa mi sanghoxe yo neu, ei?”
