MAR 14:62 Yesu neil, “Inye ay yo. Me tyek xam ghe gwei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux na toumendei wou Anutu Nikanzekta mema payeiv me nam is laxap wei tyoung gheyapu yo.”
MAR 14:63 Lumuki lukanzek lex emaxow xe teimb de teling, “Xey a ngo qayeeng wei xel valu byex lek e is en va?
MAR 14:64 Emaxow neil teyei me xam ghe ngo qayeeng lukeingyak wei neil lek Anutu yo. Om xam ghe wou naleimim ambei nya?” Xel dalus yei me luk en e bei, “Wo esewok teyei lek ingwei e mey yo.”
MAR 14:65 Woyom xel valu pesuv myend louk lek e, me xel tup e ma tuzeyi, de lund memend me venoux e me neil, “Neil qayeeng poropet wou xa bei eti leis wang!” Om xel belimbo wei mi yeiteyei xomek vambuing eno qou e me leis e.
MAR 14:66 Ka Petele toundei nge xo eivek tete lalei eno, lumuki lukanzek xe xukxe vexawo ti lam.
MAR 14:67 Gyeik vexo yei Petele di pavang xow wou nenyex, vexo yei e bombek me neil, “Wang is ambei nyon wang mi la is Yesu wei Nasaret o.”
MAR 14:68 Ekom Petele axvun. E neil, “A loungen e yo, a se woulek qayeeng tiwei wang di luklek on.” Dom la myayaing paviy tete mya me la nale. [De qouklex ti sesa vya.]
MAR 14:69 Gyeik vex xukxe yei e ghei inyon, vexo neil no wou xel wei toungale yon, “Tambiy tine inye tambiy wei xel o ti.”
MAR 14:70 Ekom moxo lox me la axvun no. Denlek ka, xel wei toungale paviyeing eno neil wou Petele, “Neing ayang wang on tambiy wei xel o ti, en inye wang lam anghei Galili.”
MAR 14:71 Petele neil, “A neil zonghek lek inyapunei lei bei a loung en tambiy tiwei xam ghe di luk en e yon. Wangwei a tyoing nei yon tyek a qou myaveweeng.”
MAR 14:72 Se denlek en qouklex sesa vya luyuw. Woyom Petele wounalei no en qayeeng wei Yesu neil woy wou e yo, “Ka qouklex se sesa vya bo luyuw atax eno tyek wang dax a vun luyal.” Om moxo eng niseikeing.
MAR 15:1 Eivek satiboukeing lul eno, xel lumuki leitata, is xel teivateiv, me putoung wei petieing o me xel kanzol dalus tup qayeeng ti wouma. Xel tup Yesu dom qou e me la me toung e la eivek Pailat mema.
MAR 15:2 Pailat teling, “Inye wa king wei xel Yudayeiw o?” Yesu neil elox bei, “nambei wamaxow ghe neil on.”
MAR 15:3 Xel lumuki leitata byex qayeeng lek e en lulul ngenong.
MAR 15:4 Om Pailat teling e no, “Inye wambei se neil enox ei? Wei lul vamva eno xel di byex qayeeng lek wang en.”
MAR 15:5 Ekom Yesu se neil qayeeng ti lox, om Pailat moxo wounalei ngenong.
MAR 15:6 De inye bouk wei Pasova wei Pailat mema mi tena xel xeitueing ti mi la teyei lek ingwei xomaxoneing venaxow laleind vind o.
MAR 15:7 Xomaxoneing ti lei Barabas eno la xeitueing is xel valu wei wo vevek wou Rom me leis seyap valu mey o.
MAR 15:8 Xel qendu ngandoung lam wou Pailat me teling bei, embong wou xel ambei ingwei mi wong o.
MAR 15:9 Pailat teling, “Xam ambei a memang tena king wei Yudayeiw eno nak wou xam?”
MAR 15:10 Moxo neil inye en woulek woy bei xel lumuki leitata eno laleind wo nol wou e me zeimaxoun Yesu me qou me lam wou e.
MAR 15:11 Ekom xel lumuki leitata eno zeim xel qendu ngandoung on laleind lek bei Pailat mema tena Barabas nam wou xel de se Yesu.
MAR 15:12 Pailat teling xel no, “De woyom, tyek a bong ambei nya en tambiy tiwei xam ghe taxe bei king wei Yudayeiw ne?”
MAR 15:13 Xel taxe niseikeing no, “Tuw e lek xax pepeeng.”
MAR 15:14 Pailat teling, “En va? E wong sewokeing vati?” Ekom xel taxe niseikeing la ghey bei, “Tuw e lek xax pepeeng!”
MAR 15:15 Pailat embei bong xel qendu ngandoung on laleind bo nimza, om mema tena Barabas lam wou xel. De neil wou e xe xel bei xel sesa Yesu dom wong ela eivek xel vevek memend bei xel atuw e lek xax pepeeng.
MAR 15:16 Xel vevek qou Yesu me la eivek tete lalei wei seyap bend o me taxe xel vevek on dalus lam.
MAR 15:17 Xel byex teimb ding mateyek lek e, woyom xel bembinexe qapangek ying lekti nambei qelumking de toung lek e lu.
MAR 15:18 Me xel taxe la wou e bei, “Bendiyeing, king wei Yudayeiw o!”
MAR 15:19 Xel sesa e lu lumama nangya lengwes de pesuv myend louk lek e. Xel ev vaxend qatu eivek de sanghoxe e.
MAR 15:20 Me gyeik ingwei xel luk seloukeing lek e woy, eno xel kwax teimb ding wei mateyek o veil dom byex emaxow xe teimb lek e. Woyom xel qou e me la myayaing bei na tuw e lek xax pepeeng.
MAR 15:21 Tambiy ti nanghei Sairini, e lei Simon, Aleksanda luw Rupus mend, moxo di la vaxa wou sakwaing nanghei danghei wei tembuing ba me embei na eivek beyeeng ngandoung on, omva xel tendu bei e qalei xax pepeeng.
MAR 15:22 Xel qou Yesu me la beyeeng wei xel mi taxe bei Golgata (qes ambei nye bei beyeeng wei lukanzek).
MAR 15:23 Woyom xel wong wain wei xel maleeng is xax mer myalouk eno wou e, ekom moxo se num.
MAR 15:24 De xel tuw e lek xax pepeeng. De nex qakous dee bei gyei vati wei xel titi embei qou yo dom xel pum e xe teimb wouma.
MAR 15:25 Inye seivma tiwei limvey gyeik xel tuw e lek xax pepeeng o.
MAR 15:26 Qayeeng wei xel byex bei bong qayeeng en e yo eno pyaweing ambei nye: KING WEI YUDAYEIW O.
MAR 15:27 Xel tuw panaxeing yayuw lek xax pepeeng is e, nge wou mema payeiv de nge wou mema qeinz.
MAR 15:28 [Me xoulek wei Anutu wei di yeip eivek qapiya eno wo neing lek en ingwei neil embei, “Me xel yei e nambei tambiy wei mi pyalek petieing o.”]
MAR 15:29 Xel eti yeiw wei di lam me la paviy e eno lukyak lek e, de xel bimexe lund, “Ei! Wa tambiy tiwei tyek lelolexe xomek vambuing ne dom ghe dev eivek bouk yal.
MAR 15:30 Woyom wa devind xow me tei lam veil xax pepeeng de wa se mey!”
MAR 15:31 Eivek sakwaing ambei nyon eno xel lumuki leitata me putoung wei petieing o eno lukyak lek e eivek xel venaxow senghoing. Xel neil, “E vind xel valu me xel se mey ekom moxo se teyeimbei devind venaxow is ambei nyon!
MAR 15:32 Wangwei e Kilisi, me King wei Israel o, ond wong e tei lam gweimbeeng veil xax pepeeng, en kandek xa ghei me na bongis o.” Luyuw wei xel tuw is e eno lukyak lek e is.
MAR 15:33 Lek seivma evlek eno mapetok sevunexe tembuing sapa me ela seivma yal.
MAR 15:34 De lek seivma yal eno Yesu nyayek niseikeing me neil, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?” Qes ambei nye, “A xe Anutu, a xe Anutu, nambei nya wang saing ay?”
MAR 15:35 Gyeik xel valu wei toukale paviyeing eno ngo tine, om xel neil, “Ngo, moxo taxe Eliya yo.”
MAR 15:36 Tambiy ti veimya me la qou wain senyeing pup eivek balam, me toung lek lengwes de wong ela wou Yesu bei e num. Moxo neil, “Gweimbeeng wong e venaxow toundei. Me xey a xei bei Eliya nam zewax e detei nam.”
MAR 15:37 De woyom Yesu nyayek ngandoung dom mey.
MAR 15:38 Qaeing wei xomek vambuing eno lex eivek masenghoing me la yayuw nanghei pu me elam axo myasepu yang.
MAR 15:39 Me gyeik beyeiv wei xel vevek eno toungale wou Yesu manghalus me yei Yesu mey ambei nya yo eno neil, “Neing ayang moux tine inye Anutu Neu Moux!”
MAR 15:40 Vex valu di yei nanghei dingta. Eivek xel senghoing eno inyon Maria wei Makdala, Maria wei Jems ghavis on ta me Joses, me Salome.
MAR 15:41 Eivek Galili eno vex ti beimambei ne mi betiwou e me yeiteyei e en vineing. Vex ngenong valu wei lam apune is e me la Yerusalem eno toundei nanghei inyon is.
MAR 15:42 De inye souk me bouk wei xel embei menyexwou lulul wei Sabat o me bouk ne la tax en Sabat.
MAR 15:43 Nambei nyon Yosep wei Arimatia, tambiy yon lei nimza wei kanzol o, wei emaxow mi axe tete lalei wei Anutu yo eno se yaleeng, qe la nale wou Pailat ma me teling en Yesu neing.
MAR 15:44 Pailat etek en ngo bei Yesu mey woy, om taxe beyeiv wei xel vevek o me teling e, “Wangwei bei Yesu mey woy?”
MAR 15:45 Gyeik Pailat ngo wou beyeiv wei xel vevek bei Yesu mey eno moxo lenghek lek Yesu neing wou Yosep.
MAR 15:46 Om Yosep xouv qaeing teleing valu, dom zewax Yesu neing tei lam, me vevilexe eivek qaeing pus dom liw e la eivek leiveeng wei xel qateiv eivek qakous o. Woyom wilexe qakous la zeyi leiveeng mya.
MAR 15:47 Maria wei Makdala me Maria wei Joses ta eno yei ingwei e yeip anghei yo.
MAR 16:1 Gyeik Sabat la veil, Maria wei Makdala, Maria wei Jems ta, me Salome lal xouv lulul wei xeimangou yo valu is wel en kandek lal na taw lek Yesu neing.
MAR 16:2 Satiboukeing lul lek bouk tiwei tax o eivek Sounda tiyon, ka sayeiv lam tyip le, eno lal la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei.
MAR 16:3 Me lal teling wouma, “Eti tyek gwilexe qakous veil leiveeng meyeing mya en ghal?”
MAR 16:4 Ekom gyeik lal yeila punei, lal yei bei qakous wei wilexe me la toungale yon inyei ngandoungateiv.
MAR 16:5 Ka lal la eivek leiveeng meyeing lalei, lal yei tambiy ghavis ti, vunek en teimb ding wei teleing o ti me toundei wou mema payeiv om lal etek.
MAR 16:6 Om moxo neil, “Mal seng detek en inye mal ghe di wimexe Yesu wei Nasaret o, tiwei xel leis lek xax pepeeng o. Moxo qandi lek! Moxo se toundei inye. Mal lam wei beeng wei xel liw e lek o.
MAR 16:7 Dom mal la neil wou e xe xel betiyeing me Petele bei, ‘Moxo la tax en xam me la Galili. Tyek xam ghe gwei e nanghei inyei, nambei kawei neil wou xam o.’ ”
MAR 16:8 Xel vex la myayaing de pek me la veil leiveeng meyeing, is etekeing me woueing nalei ngenong, om xel se neil qayeeng en lulti wou xelti, en nambei xel yaleeng.
MAR 16:9 Gyeik Yesu qandi lek Sounda satiboukeing lul lek bouk ti tax o, moxo la tyip atax wou Maria wei Makdala, tiwei e tiy memo lim yuw veil e yo.
MAR 16:10 Vexo la me neil wou xel wei mi la is e yo, me eti yeiw wei di wo talot me eng o.
MAR 16:11 Gyeik xel ngo bei Yesu toundei mapieing me vex on yei e, eno xel se wongis.
MAR 16:12 Dekalekom Yesu lam tyip wou luw yayuw wei xel o, ekom wo bange om luw se woulek, gyeik ingwei luw di la wou sakwaing me la beyeeng nayak nei.
MAR 16:13 Luw lox me la me neil wou xel betiyeing valu, ekom xel se wongis luw.
MAR 16:14 Kalekom Yesu la tyip wou xel betiyeing xoumeeng ti gyeik xel toundei me di ya yo, moxo luk niseikeing wou xel en xel se wongis me xel wei laleind wo nikanzek en nambei xel embei se bongis eti yeiw wei yei e yo, gyeik ingwei e qandi lek o.
MAR 16:15 Moxo neil wou xel, “Xam la eivek tembuing sapa nei me neil Xoulek Nimza wou xomaxoneing dalus.
MAR 16:16 Xel tiwei wongis me lipek eno tyek Anutu devind xel en xel se mey, ekom eti yeiw wei se wongis eno tyek na qou myaveweeng gyeik ingwei xel bo qayeeng o.
MAR 16:17 Me dee beimambei ne tyek na is eti yeiw wei wongis o. Eivek a leing eno tyek xel a tiy memo na myayaing, de tyek xel baluk eivek vya vako.
MAR 16:18 Tyek xel a zeim myeiy angya memend me gyeik xel anum lul wei wevek eno tyek se bo nol wou xelti, tyek xel a niw memend lek xel wei vanei yo, dom tyek xel bo nimzalek.”
MAR 16:19 Ka Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu luk is xel woy, woyom Anutu qou e me la ghey eivek tyoung gheyapu me e la dei wou Anutu mema payeiv.
MAR 16:20 Woyom xel betiyeing la myayaing me neil xoulek la danghei danghei nei, me Tambiy Ngandoung wo xuk is xel, me byexaxoun e xe qayeeng nangya dee wei di betiwou xuk on.
LUK 1:1 O lei ngandoung Tiopilas, xel ngenong mi byex pavulek lek vatiyeiw wei Anutu wong ela teyei lek eivek xa senghoing o.
LUK 1:2 Xel betiwou eti yeiw wei yei lulul on lek mend atax, gyeik ingwei lulul on qandi lek o. Me xel on xukxe wei Anutu xe xoulek o. Om xel tul pavulek on wou xa.
LUK 1:3 Om ay is ambei nyon ambei byex pavulek on me na bong e nak wou wang. A mi wong xuk endenlek telinyeing lulul on qes wo nimza, om a byex ela teyei lek ingwei lulul on qandi yo.
LUK 1:4 Wa pyaw dom ghe boulek embo nimza bei qayeeng wei xel teyoxe wou wang on neing ayang.
LUK 1:5 Eivek bouk wei Herot king wei Yudia eno lumuki ti mindei e lei Sakalias, e eivek qendu tiwei Abiya yo. Moxo venei Elisabet yon eivek velei wei Aron o.
LUK 1:6 Luw xouing mindei ewo bombek wou Anutu manghalus. Me luw mi betiwou Tambiy Ngandoung xe petieing dalus me xoulek dalus, me sewokeing ma veil luw.
LUK 1:7 Ekom luw neund ma, en Elisabet mi mouyeeng me luw wo teiv aluw vexta.
LUK 1:8 Bouk ti gyeik Sakalias xe lumukiyeiw qendu tiyon la wong xuk, eno moxo la wong xuk lumuki wou Anutu manghalus is ambei nyon.
LUK 1:9 Om xel betiwou lumukiyeiw xe kwa wei xel mi nex qakous dee me beyal e, bei ena lalei eivek Tambiy Ngandoung xe xomek vambuing me na besei da wei xeiliy.
LUK 1:10 Gyeik bouk wei seing xound xeiliy eno lam tyip, xel dalusateiv di qekuma nanghei Anutu beeng me zeimemend anghei myayaing.
LUK 1:11 Woyom Tambiy Ngandoung xe angela ti lam nale wou e, moxo nale wou qeind wei seing xound xeiliy eno nenya valu wei payeiv o.
LUK 1:12 Gyeik Sakalias yei angela, eno etek me yaleeng.
LUK 1:13 Ekom angela neil wou e, “Sakalias wa seng gwaleeng, en Anutu ngo wa xe zeimeing mema. Om veneim Elisabet tyek bou neum moux ti, me tyek wa taxe e lei Yoan.
LUK 1:14 Tyek wang bo xeimlala ngandoung me laleim bo nimza. Me xel ngenong tyek bo xeindlala en e xe umbekeing,
LUK 1:15 en moxo tyek bo lei ngandoung wou Tambiy Ngandoung manghalus. Moxo e se num wain o memiing wei nikanzek o. De gyeik ingwei toukami eivek ta veis eno na pup en Laweeng Vambuing.
LUK 1:16 Moxo tyek na qou xel Israelyeiw ngenongakes me noumenam wou Tambiy Ngandoung xel xe Anutu.
LUK 1:17 Moxo tyek na qou nikanzek wei Laweeng Vambuing o nambei Eliya wei takwei yo me natax en Tambiy Ngandoung. Moxo tyek bong mayeiw laleind pekwi nox wou neuyeiw. Me moxo tyek pepyawexe xel wei mi pyalek qayeeng o me xel a qou lupeyei nimza nambei xel wei mi betiwou sakwaing bombek o. Moxo tyek menyex wou xomaxoneing en xel gyeiwou xow en Tambiy Ngandoung nam o.”
LUK 1:18 Sakalias teling angela bei, “Tyek a boulek inyon ambei nya? A wo teiv takwei me a veneing wo vexta is ambei nyon.”
LUK 1:19 Angela lewexe bei, “A Gabriel. A mi nale wou Anutu manghalus, om wong a lam a luk is wang me na neil wou wang en xoulek nimza tine.
LUK 1:20 Om ngo, gweimbeeng kane wa myam tyek na tu me tyek wa se teyei bei baluk, qe ka bouk wei lulti yon neing etyip bole en wa seng wongis a xe qayeeng. Lulti yon tyek bo neing lek e xe bouk bombek.”
LUK 1:21 Dekalekom xomaxoneing di axe Sakalias me di wou naleind bei nambei nya ekom dei enden eivek xomek vambuing.
LUK 1:22 Gyeik ingwei moxo lam myayaing, eno moxo se teyeimbei baluk wou xel. Om xel woulek bei mapekwi me yei lulti eivek xomek vambuing, en mi talex lulul angya mema wou xel en se teyeimbei baluk.
LUK 1:23 Gyeik bouk wei moxo xe xuk la wou eivek, moxo lox me la beeng.
LUK 1:24 Kalekom venei Elisabet xei qou veil me e mindei xupekeing teyei lek dentouk qes lim.
LUK 1:25 Vexo neil embei, “Tambiy Ngandoung wong tine wou ay eivek bouk ti beimambei ne, moxo talex e xe lalei nimza me zeim a xe niyalenyeing veil eivek xomaxoneing senghoing.”
LUK 1:26 Eivek dentouk tiwei limti eno Anutu wong angela Gabriel la Nasaret inyei beyeeng ti eivek Galili.
LUK 1:27 La wou vexawo wei paleveeng o ti wei xel tup qayeeng lekti bei e na wou moux ti e lei Yosep bei e dii, inyon Dawit buyeiw ti. Vexawo paleveeng on lei Maria.
LUK 1:28 De angela la wou vexo me neil embei, “Bendiyeing vex, Anutu lalei wo nimza wou wang. Tambiy Ngandoung e toumendei is wang.”
LUK 1:29 Maria lalei wo maying en e xe qayeeng me wounalei bei, “Qayeeng tine inye nambei nya?”
LUK 1:30 Ekom angela neil wou vexo bei, “Maria, wa seng gwaleeng, en Anutu lalei wo nimza wou wang.
LUK 1:31 Wei, tyek wa xeim a qou veil me wang bou neum moux ti, me wa taxe e lei Yesu.
LUK 1:32 Tyek moxo bo lei ngandoung me tyek xel a neimbei Anutu gheyapu neu moux. De Tambiy Ngandoung Anutu tyek bong siaking wei bu Dawit xe eno wou e.
LUK 1:33 Me tyek mendei king en xomek wei Yakop o luta, e xe tete lalei tyek se tip.”
LUK 1:34 Maria teling wou angela bei, “Ekom inyon tyek bong ambei nya, inye a paleveeng o?”
LUK 1:35 Angela lewexe, “Laweeng Vambuing tyek nam wou wang me Anutu gheyapu xe nikanzek tyek bo tenu zeyi wang. Om yakyeis tiwei wa being bou yon vambuing, me tyek xel a neimbei inyon Anutu Neu Moux.
LUK 1:36 Me gweimbeeng nimpapu Elisabet tyek bou neu moux ti eivek ingwei wo vexta yo. Takwei eno xel mi neil embei mi mouyeeng ekom wo neu me dentouk qes limti la veil.
LUK 1:37 En lulti tyek se bo pok wou Anutu.”
LUK 1:38 Maria lewexe, “Ee, a Tambiy Ngandoung xe xukxe vexawo, om e bong wou ay ambei ingwei wang neil on.” Woyom angela la veil e.
LUK 1:39 Lek bouk kayon eno Maria yeiwou xow me la daing eivek beyeeng ti lek lukendu wei Yudia nei.
LUK 1:40 De vexo la eivek Sakalias beeng me la neil bendiyeing wou Elisabet.
LUK 1:41 Gyeik ingwei Elisabet ngo Maria xe bendiyeing, eno neu vyeip eivek e veis. De Laweeng Vambuing pup Elisabet.
LUK 1:42 Om taxe xoulekeing me neil embei: “Anutu wo mata ghanaw veil wou wang eivek vex vex senghoing, me wo mata wou yakyeis tiwei wa being bou yon!
LUK 1:43 Ekom ay eti om lalei nimza lam wou ay? Me a xe Tambiy Ngandoung ta lam wou ay?
LUK 1:44 Wei, gyeik ingwei a nenyang ngo wa xe bendiyeing, eno yakyeis wei tumi eivek a veis eno wo xeilala me vyeip.
LUK 1:45 Nimza e na wou vex wei mi wongis bei vati wei Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou e, eno tyek bo neing lek!”
LUK 1:46 Me Maria neil ambei nye: “A nung pieing e sanghoxe Tambiy Ngandoung
LUK 1:47 me axe laweeng wo xeilala en Anutu, en e axe vineing,
LUK 1:48 en ay eno e xe xukxe vexawo wei lei maeing ekom yei ay me lalei pyaxow en ay. Om ngo, gweimbeeng me e mi na eno moux alis vex dalus tyek na mi taxe bei Anutu wong mata wou ay.
LUK 1:49 En tambiy nikanzekta ti wong lul ngandoung tine wou ay, e lei yon vambuing.
LUK 1:50 E lalei mi pyaxow en moux alis vex wei mi yaleeng en e yo, tyek bong ambei nyon wou moux alis vex wei gweimbeeng ne yo, me moux alis vex wei yusyus o.
LUK 1:51 E mema wong xuk wei nikanzek o, xel wei mi wou naleind en xow me toxleind eno tiy xel la danghei danghei nei.
LUK 1:52 Moxo toung mema lek xel king lox nge xo veil xel xe siaking de zeim xel wei leind maeing eno lek la.
LUK 1:53 Moxo wong lul nimzamza ngenong pup wou xel wei maxepya xel o, dom wong xel wei lulul ana eno la bandaing.
LUK 1:54 Moxo vind e xe xukxeyeiw wei Israel o, en mi wounalei en e xe lalei pyaweingxow,
LUK 1:55 wei wong wou Apraham me e neumambu takwei takwei, nambei ingwei e neil wou xey mendyeiw o.”
LUK 1:56 Maria la dei is Elisabet teyei lek dentouk qes yayal o xelti, dekakom lox me la beeng.
LUK 1:57 Gyeik bouk la wou eivek ingwei Elisabet embei bou neu yo, om vexo wou neu moux ti.
LUK 1:58 Xel wei Elisabet beeng qes o me nipapu wei toundei paviy e eno ngo ingwei Tambiy Ngandoung lalei pyaxow ngandoung en e yo, om xel wo xeindlala is e.
LUK 1:59 Lek bouk lim yal eno xel lam en xel embei ghuw yak on ninavi. Me xel embei taxe e lei Sakalias, nambei ma lei.
LUK 1:60 Ekom ta luk me neil embei, “Ma! Tyek xey a taxe e lei Yoan.”
LUK 1:61 Xel neil wou vexo, “Eivek xel wei wang eno senghoing xelti se lei nambei nyon.”
LUK 1:62 Woyom xel talex lek memend wou ma, me xel teling ma bei, moxo embei taxe neu lei va.
LUK 1:63 Moxo teling wou xel en tapele, me moxo byex qayeeng bei, “E lei Yoan.” Om xel di wou naleind ngenong.
LUK 1:64 Lutika eno Sakalias mya tax, me e ghas vevop me e luk me sanghoxe Anutu.
LUK 1:65 Xel wei e beeng qes on yei lulti yon om xel etek me luk ngenong en, de eivek xel beyeeng lukendu wei Yudia nei eno xel tul pavulek en lulti beimambei ne dalus.
LUK 1:66 Xel sapa wei ngo pavulek eno xel wou naleind ngenong me teling bei, “Bouk loxyus eno yak tine tyek bong nambei nya?” En Tambiy Ngandoung mema nikanzek toundei is e.
LUK 1:67 Moxo ma Sakalias pup en Laweeng Vambuing me neil qayeeng poropet bei:
LUK 1:68 “Xey a sanghoxe Tambiy Ngandoung, Israel xe Anutu, en lam tul xe xomaxoneing veil nilul.
LUK 1:69 Moxo wong tambiy nikanzeta wei vind xey veil nilul eno ti qandi eivek xomek wei e xe xukxe Dawit o,
LUK 1:70 (nambei ingwei e neil eivek e xe xel poropet vambuing myend takwei nei yo),
LUK 1:71 Neil embei tyek devind xe veil xel vevek ba memend me xel wei mi yei xey a wo nol o memend is,
LUK 1:72 de talex e xe lalei pyaweingxow wou xe bundyeiw me mi wounalei en e xe qayeeng vambuing wei qokatu yo,
LUK 1:73 de qayeeng zonghek wei neil neing wou xe bund Apraham o:
LUK 1:74 bei na zeim xe veil xe xe xel vevek ba memend, me bong xey a mi bong e xe xuk de xe se ghaleeng.
LUK 1:75 Eivek bouk sapa wei xey a mindei mapieing eno xey a mi betiwou kwa wei vambuing o, me sakwaing bombek wou e manghalus.
LUK 1:76 “De wang, a neung, tyek xel taxe bei wa poropet wei Anutu gheyapu nei yo. En tyek wang natax en Tambiy Ngandoung me menyex wou sakwaing en e,
LUK 1:77 de ghe bong lupeyei wou e xe xomaxoneing en ingwei embei devind xel veil nilul me semaleeng sewokeing wei xel o,
LUK 1:78 en nambei xe xe Anutu lalei pyaxow wo nimzayang en xey, om wong xeiyaing ti lam nambei sayeiv qandi me lam wou xey nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei.
LUK 1:79 En enam a siing lek xel wei mindei eivek mapetok ngandoung o, me mindei eivek yalenyeing en meyeing o. De gyeiteyei xe vaxend en xey a betiwou sakwaing wei lalei vevopeing o.”
LUK 1:80 Me yak moxo wo teiv me Anutu xe Laweeng wong nikanzek wou e me moxo la mindei eivek tembuing bandaing, deka bouk la wou eivek woyom la talex xow wou Israelyeiw.
LUK 2:1 Eivek bouk tiyon eno Sisa Ogastus king wei ngandoung o wong petieing ti la me neil embei xel a qou moux alis vex dalus wei tembuing sapa wei dei xeinghembi eivek Rom eno leind eivek qapiya.
LUK 2:2 (Inye myaxeeng selis wei xel qou xel leind gyeik ingwei Kwirinius wo lei ngandoung wei seyap wei Siria yo.)
LUK 2:3 Me xel dalusateiv la venaxow bend qes bei seyap a qou xel leind.
LUK 2:4 Yosep on neumambu wei king Dawit o. Om la veil beyeeng Nasaret eivek Galili, me lek me la Yudia, la Dawit beeng wei Betelem o.
LUK 2:5 Moxo la inyei is Maria wei xel tup qayeeng lekti bei e mendei wou e yo bei seyap a qou luw leind, gyeik inyon eno Maria xei qou veil.
LUK 2:6 Ka luw la toundei inyei, eno bouk la wou eivek ingwei yakyeis on embei dumbek o.
LUK 2:7 Om vexo wou neu touk, me beliv e eivek qaeing me liw eivek manghaxo xe dipek, en xomek wei vateivek o pup zeyi xel.
LUK 2:8 Me nanghei inyei eno xel gyovaxa wei sipsip eno valu toundei myayaing veil beyeeng, me di yeiteyei xel xe sipsip qendu ngandoung on eivek boukeing tiyon.
LUK 2:9 Dekakom Tambiy Ngandoung xe angela ti lam wou xel, me Tambiy Ngandoung xe xeiyaing ngandoung lam siing e vivekwou xel, om xel yaleeng ngandoung.
LUK 2:10 Ekom angela neil wou xel bei, “Xam seng gwaleeng. En a qou xoulek nimza me na lam wou xam, bei embong xomaxoneing dalus bo xeindlala ngandoung.
LUK 2:11 Gweimbeeng kane eivek beyeeng nayak wei Dawit xe eno tambiy tiwei qou xam ghe lam veil nilul eno umbek en xam. E Kilisi me Tambiy Ngandoung.
LUK 2:12 Tyek xam ghe boulek dee nambei nye: Tyek xam ghe gwei yakyeis ti xel beliv eivek vetivek mati me liw eivek manghaxo xe dipek.”
LUK 2:13 De lutika eno angela ngenongakes wei tyoung gheyapu eno lam is angela tiyon, me xel sanghoxe Anutu me neil embei,
LUK 2:14 “Xey a sanghoxe Anutu lei na gheyapu nei, de nanghei tembuing eno xomaxoneing wei Anutu lalei wo nimza wou xel eno na mi mendei is laleind vevopeing.”
LUK 2:15 Gyeik ingwei xel angela lox veil xel me la eivek tyoung gheyapu nei, eno xel gyovaxa wei sipsip o neil wouma bei, “Xey a la Betelem me na xei lul tiwei qandi nei, wei Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou xey en o.”
LUK 2:16 Om xel la daing me la yeiwou Maria luw Yosep, me yakyeis wei di yeip eivek manghaxo xe dipek o.
LUK 2:17 Gyeik ingwei xel yei e, eno xel neil qayeeng la wo sapa en vatiyeiw wei angela neil wou xel en yakyeis tiyon o.
LUK 2:18 Me xel dalus wei ngo inye, eno etek en vati wei xel gyovaxa wei sipsip o neil wou xel o.
LUK 2:19 Ekom Maria mi zeimaxoun qayeeng ti beimambei yon dalus eivek lalei me mi wounalei en.
LUK 2:20 Xel gyovaxa wei sipsip eno lox me la me di sanghoxe Anutu me wong xeindlala en lulul dalus wei xel ngo me yei yo. Nambei kawei angela neil wou xel o.
LUK 2:21 Lek bouk lim yal, gyeik bouk wei xel embei ghuw yak on ninavi me taxe e lei Yesu. Lei yon angela wong gyeik ingwei se ghei mi eivek ta veis o.
LUK 2:22 Gyeik bouk lam tyip en ingwei yeing wou xow bo vako wou Anutu manghalus teyei lek Mose xe petieing eno la wou eivek, om Yosep aluw Maria qou Yesu me la Yerusalem en embei na bong e na wou Tambiy Ngandoung.
LUK 2:23 Inyon nambei xel byex eivek Tambiy Ngandoung xe petieing, “Xel yak moux sapa wei umbek atax eno xam ghe bong ena nambei vambuing wou Tambiy Ngandoung nambei e xe.”
LUK 2:24 Me luw la sei xound nambei vati wei xel neil eivek Tambiy Ngandoung xe petieing o, “beliy yayuw o banax lingheing yayuw.”
LUK 2:25 Gweimbeeng eivek Yerusalem eno tambiy ti mindei e lei Simion, tambiy on mindei bombek me mi wong lalo. Moxo mi axe ingwei Mesia embei bong lalei vevopeing wou Israel o, me Laweeng Vambuing mindei eivek e.
LUK 2:26 Laweeng Vambuing talex wou e bei, tyek se mey qe ka gyei Tambiy Ngandoung xe Kilisi bole.
LUK 2:27 Laweeng Vambuing zeim e lalei lek, me e la eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing, de Yesu ma luw ta qou e me la en embei na bong vati wou e nambei kwa wei petieing neil o.
LUK 2:28 Me Simion qava e me sanghoxe Anutu me neil:
LUK 2:29 “Tambiy Ngandoung, wei ghanaw veil, nambei ingwei wang neil zonghek o, wang bong wa xe xukxe na mey eivek lalei vevopeing.
LUK 2:30 En a manghalus yei wa xe tambiy wei embei devind xa veil nilul o,
LUK 2:31 wei wang xupexe inye wou xomaxoneing dalus mend o.
LUK 2:32 E xeiyaing tiwei embei talex enam yanyateiv wou xel amba de bong wa xe xel Israel leind zekna.”
LUK 2:33 Yesu ma luw ta etek en qayeeng vati wei neil lek e yo.
LUK 2:34 Woyom Simion wo mata wou lal me neil wou moxo ta Maria, “Yakyeis tine nambei beyaleing wei tyek bong xel ngenong detei de xel ngenong qandi lek eivek Israel, me tyek mendei nambei dee ti, wei xel ngenong tyek bo vyend wou e yo.
LUK 2:35 En kandek xel ngenong xe laleind peyei eno tyek nam yanyateiv. De ngeyeing vevek ti tyek beum wamaxow num pieing is.”
LUK 2:36 Nanghei inyon eno poropet vex ti e lei Ana, Penuel neu vex eivek velei wei Asal o. Vexo wo vexta, vexo mindei is leya teyei lek vakovek qes lim yuw takwei gyeik ingwei luw iima yo.
LUK 2:37 De woyom wo vexeiv teyei lek 84 vakovek qes. Vexo se mindei veil xomek vambuing qe mi wong lalo boukeing aluw bendiyeing, me mi vambu yaeing de mi zeimema.
LUK 2:38 Lek bouk kayon eno la paviy xel me wong dange wou Anutu me luk en yakyeis on wou xel dalus wei mi toung mend en ingwei Anutu embei tul xel Yerusalem veil nilul o.
LUK 2:39 Gyeik ingwei Yosep me Maria wong lulul dalus la teyei lek petieing wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe yo, luw lox Galili me lox me la luw venaxow xe beyeeng nayak Nasaret.
LUK 2:40 Me yakyeis on wo teiv me wo nikanzek. Moxo pup en lupeyei nimza me Anutu xe lalei xeiles toundei eivek e.
LUK 2:41 Teyei lek vakovek qes sapa eno moxo ma luw ta mi la Yerusalem en embei na gyei mata ngandoung wei Pasova yo.
LUK 2:42 Gyeik Yesu xe vakovek qes xoumeeng yuw, eno xel betiwou xel xe kwa me lek me la yei mata ngandoung wei Pasova yon.
LUK 2:43 Ka bouk ngandoung wei mata dalus la veil, eno ma luw ta lox me la bend, de Yesu nanghei toundei Yerusalem, ekom luw se woulek inye.
LUK 2:44 Luw wou naleind bei la is moux alis vex valu, xel la e teyei lek bouk ti, woyom luw yimexe e eivek nipapu me luw xe gweleeng senghoing.
LUK 2:45 Gyeik ingwei luw se yeiwou e, luw lox me la Yerusalem en embei nox gyimexe e.
LUK 2:46 Ka bouk yayal la veil eno luw yeiwou e nanghei tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o, toundei eivek xel putoung senghoing, di ngo xel me di wo telinyeing wou xel.
LUK 2:47 Xel sapa wei ngo e xe qayeeng eno etek en e xe lupeyei me qayeeng bombek wei di neil elox o.
LUK 2:48 Gyeik ingwei ma luw ta yei e, eno luw etek. Moxo ta neil wou e bei, “Touk, nambei nya wang wong ambei nyon wou uw? Uw mam laleimi wo maying en wang om uw a mi ximexe wang.”
LUK 2:49 Moxo teling wou luw, “Nambei nya muw ghe mi wimexe ay? Muw seng woulek bei a toundei eivek mang beeng?”
LUK 2:50 Ekom luw se woulek vati wei di neil wou luw o.
LUK 2:51 Woyom lep me la xo Nasaret nei is luw me mi betiwou luw xe qayeeng. Ekom moxo ta mi toung lulti beimambei yon dalus eivek lalei me mi wounalei en.
LUK 2:52 Me Yesu wo teiv is lupeyei nimza, me Anutu lalei wo nimza wou e me moux alis vex laleind wo nimza wou e is.
LUK 3:1 Eivek vakovek qes 15 wei Sisa Taibilias wo king wei Rom gyeik Pontias Pailat wo lei ngandoung wei seyap wei distrik Yudia yo de Herot yeiteyei distrik Galili dom li Pilip yeiteyei distrik Itulia me Tlakonaitis, de Lisanias yeiteyei distrik Abilini.
LUK 3:2 Gyeik ingwei Anas aluw Kaiapas wo lumuki lukanzek eno Anutu xe qayeeng lam wou Yoan wei Sakalias neu yo eivek tembuing bandaing.
LUK 3:3 Woyom moxo la eivek tembuing danghei dalus wei toundei memiing Yorodan vivi yo, me la neil xoulek wou moux alis vex bei xel pekwi xow me zipek, en kandek Anutu semaleeng xel xe sewokeing veil.
LUK 3:4 Lulti yon qandi nambei poropet Yesaya byex eivek qapiya yo, “Vya taxeing ti lam eivek tembuing bandaing bei, ‘Xam menyex wou sakwaing en Tambiy Ngandoung, xam ghe bong sakwaing embo bombek en e.
LUK 3:5 Xam samax manya dalus e pup me qandax lukendu is qetyei dalus e deteina. Sakwaing dalus wei wo xeighekeing eno embo bombek, me sakwaing wei wo nol eno embo belin.
LUK 3:6 Me xel xomaxoneing dalus tyek gyei Anutu xe sakwaing wei vind xomaxoneing veil nilul o.’”
LUK 3:7 Yoan neil wou xel qendu ngandoung wei lam bei e zipek xel o, “Xam on myeiy nilul neu xam. Eti peti xam bei tyek xam a pek veil Anutu xe lalei vanei?
LUK 3:8 Xam ghe buk neing me talex bei xam ghe pekwi xow, me xam se neil wou ma bei xa bumi Apraham. En a neil wou xam bei, Anutu teyeimbei neil me qakous ti beimambei ne bong ambei Apraham neuyeiw.
LUK 3:9 Qov di yeip woy wou xax qes, me xax dalus wei se vuk neing nimza, eno tyek buv veil de banex ena eivek nenyex.”
LUK 3:10 Xel moux alis vex ngenong teling bei, “Om tyek xa bong ambei nya?”
LUK 3:11 Om Yoan neil elox wou xel bei, “Tambiy ti xe teimb yayuw toundei ond e bong nge wou tambiy wei ning teimb ma yo, de xelti xe yaeing toundei wou e ond e bong ambei nyon.”
LUK 3:12 Xel wei mi qou takis, eno valu lam is ambei nyon en embei nam zipek, om xel teling wou bei, “Putoung, tyek xa bong ambei nya?”
LUK 3:13 Moxo neil wou xel bei, “Xam a qou takis teyei lek ingwei seyap toung o, de xam se qou e zekna.”
LUK 3:14 Woyom xel vevek valu teling wou bei, “Dom xa ne bong ambei nya?” Moxo neil elox wou xel bei, “Xam seng bo nol wou xomaxoneing me panax xel xe malew. Me na byex qayeeng tyonyeing lek xomaxoneing en xel xe malew. Qe xam ghe bou naleimim bei malew wei xam ghe mi qou en xuk on teyei woy.”
LUK 3:15 Xel xomaxoneing wei mindei me axe lulti beimambei yon xel dalus di wou naleind ngenong bei, “Beip Yoan on Kilisi?”
LUK 3:16 Yoan lewexe wou xel dalus bei, “A lipek xam en memiing, ekom tambiy ti nikanzek ghanaw ay eno tyek nam, de a se nimza teyeimbei a tul yis veil e xe vaxalambes. Eno moxo tyek zipek xam en Laweeng Vambuing me nenyex is.
LUK 3:17 Moxo zeim taliv eivek mema, en embei beyal wit neing veil myapapu, de qekuwou me na toung eivek xomek yaeing, ekom moxo tyek besei myapapu lek nenyex wei se mi mey yo.”
LUK 3:18 Yoan neil qayeeng valu wei embei byex xomaxoneing laleind o de neil Xoulek Nimza wou xel.
LUK 3:19 Ekom gyeik Yoan neil xel xe seyap Herot en sewokeing wei luw Herodias wei li venei yo, me kwa nilul dalus wei mi wong eno is.
LUK 3:20 De Herot tetulexe tine is nilul dalus wei mi wong o, dom toung Yoan la eivek xeitueing.
LUK 3:21 Gyeik ingwei xomaxoneing dalus di lipek, eno Yesu lipek is. Me ka e di zeimema, eno tyoung gheyapu tax.
LUK 3:22 Me Laweeng Vambuing lep me lam wou e, nambei beliy me lam dei lek e. De vya ti lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei: “Wang on a Neung moux, wei a laleing vind o, a wo xeinglala en wang.”
LUK 3:23 Yesu xe vakovek qes la tyip ambei xoumeeng yal (30) gyeik ingwei e wong e xe xuk a tax o. Moxo Yosep neu. Yosep on Heli neu,
LUK 3:24 de Heli yon Matat neu, de Matat on Livai neu, de Livai yon Melki neu, de Melki yon Janai neu, de Janai yon Yosep neu,
LUK 3:25 de Yosep on Matatias neu, de Matatias on Amos neu, de Amos on Nahum neu, de Nahum on Esli neu, de Esli yon Nagai neu,
LUK 3:26 de Nagai yon Mat neu, de Mat on Matatias neu, de Matatias on Semen neu, de Semen on Josek neu, de Josek on Joda neu,
LUK 3:27 de Joda yon Joanan neu, de Joanan on Resa neu, de Resa yon Serubabel neu, de Serubabel on Seatiel neu, de Seatiel on Neri neu,
LUK 3:28 de Neri yon Melki neu, de Melki yon Adi neu, de Adi yon Kosam neu, de Kosam on Elmadam neu, de Elmadam on Er neu,
LUK 3:29 de Er on Yosua neu, de Yosua yon Eliese neu, de Eliese on Jorim neu, de Jorim on Matat neu, de Matat on Livai neu,
LUK 3:30 de Livai yon Simion neu, de Simion on Yuda neu, de Yuda yon Yosep neu, de Yosep on Jonam neu, de Jonam on Eliakim neu,
LUK 3:31 de Eliakim on Melea neu, de Melea yon Mena neu, de Mena yon Matata neu, de Matata yon Natan neu, de Natan on Dawit neu,
LUK 3:32 de Dawit on Jesi neu, de Jesi yon Obet neu, de Obet on Boas neu, de Boas on Salmon neu de Salmon on Nason neu,
LUK 3:33 de Nason on Aminadap neu, de Aminadap on Atmin neu, de Atmin on Arni neu, de Arni yon Hesron neu, de Hesron on Peres neu, de Peres on Yuda neu,
LUK 3:34 de Yuda yon Yakop neu, de Yakop on Isaka neu, de Isaka yon Apraham neu, de Apraham on Tera neu, de Tera yon Nahor neu,
LUK 3:35 de Nahor on Seruk neu, de Seruk on Reu neu, de Reu yon Pelek neu, de Pelek on Eber neu, de Eber on Sela neu,
LUK 3:36 de Sela yon Kainan neu, de Kainan on Apaksat neu, de Apaksat on Sem neu, de Sem on Noaka neu, de Noaka yon Lamek neu,
LUK 3:37 de Lamek on Metusela neu, de Metusela yon Inok neu, de Inok on Zaret neu, de Zaret on Mahalalel neu, de Mahalalel on Kenan neu,
LUK 3:38 de Kenan on Enos neu, de Enos on Set neu, de Set on Adam neu, de Adam on Anutu neu moux.
LUK 4:1 Yesu pup en Laweeng Vambuing, om loumelam anghei memiing Yorodan me Laweeng Vambuing qou e me la tembuing bandaing,
LUK 4:2 teyei lek bouk xoumeeng vey (40) eno tambiy mapetok wo axeing wou e. Moxo se ya bambou lek bouk ti beimambei yon, me lek bouk tiwei la tip lek eno maxepya e.
LUK 4:3 Om tambiy mapetok neil wou e, “Wangwei wa Anutu Neu Moux nei, ond neil wou qakous tine en e pekwi me bo belet o.”
LUK 4:4 Yesu lewexe me neil embei, “Xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye: ‘Xomaxoneing tyek se mendei mapieing en belet venaxow.’”
LUK 4:5 Tambiy mapetok qou e me lek me la lukendu vaxading ti me talex tete lalei dalus wei tembuing sapa eno daing wou e.
LUK 4:6 Me neil wou e, “Tyek am bong lei ngandoung me vunekeing nimzamza ne wou wang, en inye toundei eivek a memang, me ambei bong wou xelti, ond tyek a bong wou e.
LUK 4:7 Om wangwei wang bong lalo wou ay, ond tyek wa xe lulul ne dalus.”
LUK 4:8 Yesu lewexe bei, “Xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, ‘Wang bong lalo wou Tambiy Ngandoung wa xe Anutu me na mi bong emaxow xe xuk.’”
LUK 4:9 Woyom tambiy mapetok qou e me la beyeeng Yerusalem me la lax lek xomek vambuing pundanghou nei. De neil wou e, “Wangwei wa Anutu Neu Moux nei ond wa tetoing anghei inye me ghe na xonei.
LUK 4:10 En xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, “‘Moxo tyek baluk nikanzek wou e xe angela en xel nam gyeiteyei wang bo nimza.
LUK 4:11 Tyek xel a zeim wang zekna nangya memend en kandek wa seng nyeis vaxam lek qakous.’”
LUK 4:12 Yesu lewexe bei, “Xoulek neil ambei nye, ‘Wa se toung Tambiy Ngandoung wa xe Anutu eivek axeing.’”
LUK 4:13 Gyeik ingwei tambiy mapetok wong axeing ti beimambei yon ma eno mema tena e de di axe deka bouk nge le.
LUK 4:14 Laweeng Vambuing wong nikanzek wou Yesu me e lox me la Galili de pavulek wei e eno la teyei lek tembuing danghei tiyon dalus.
LUK 4:15 Moxo mi teyoxe xoulek wou xel eivek xel xe xomek qekueing ama me moux alis vex sapa mi sanghoxe e lei.
LUK 4:16 Moxo la beyeeng Nasaret, wei wo teiv lek o, de lek bouk wei Sabat eno la eivek xomek qekueing ama wei xel xe eno lalei nambei ingwei mi wong taxombouk o. Me moxo nale ghey en embei pyaw Anutu xe xoulek.
LUK 4:17 Xel wong poropet Yesaya xe qapiya vambuing wei xel mi vevilexe lek xax eno wou e. Tul me yeiwou senghoing tiwei qayeeng di yeip lek o:
LUK 4:18 “Tambiy Ngandoung xe Laweeng Vambuing lam dei lek ay en nambei e taw wel lek ay me beyal ay bei a neil Xoulek Nimza wou xel kanyo. Moxo wong a lam bei a nam a neilteyei wou xel wei la dei eivek xomek xeitueing o bei xel bong xel nam myayaing me na neil wou xel wei mend tekeing o bei xel mend gyeina me na bong xel wei xomaxoneing mi wo nol wou xel eno nam myayaing veil nimaying,
LUK 4:19 de na neil vakovek qes wei Tambiy Ngandoung embei bong lulul nimza wou moux alis vex eno teyei.”
LUK 4:20 Woyom vevilexe qapiya me wong elox wou xukxe de dei tembuing. Xel wei toundei eivek xomek qekueing ama eno dalusateiv di yei e kanzek.
LUK 4:21 Me mouk neil wou xel bei, “Gweimbeeng xoulek wei xam ghe ngo ne wo neing lek.”
LUK 4:22 Xel dalus luk nimza en e, en qayeeng nimzamza wei di neil on om xel etek me teling bei, “Beip inye se Yosep neu ei?”
LUK 4:23 Yesu neil wou xel bei, “Neing ayang tyek xam a neil qayeeng pakeing tine wou ay: ‘Dokta wamaxow ghe bong xow bo nimzalek! Wang bong lulul vatiyeiw eivek wamaxow bam qes ne, nambei vatiyeiw wei xa ngo wang wong eivek beyeeng Kapenaom o.’”
LUK 4:24 Moxo tetulexe qayeeng me neil, “A neil zonghek wou xam, xel xomaxoneing se mi lenghek lek poropet ti eivek emaxow beeng qes.
LUK 4:25 A neil neing wou xam no bei inye vexeiv ngenong toundei eivek Israel eivek bouk wei poropet Eliya yo, gyeik ingwei tyoung xey zeyi teyei lek vakovek qes yal me dentouk limti is me sewis wei maxep ngandoung yeip ela teyei lek tembuing tambak.
LUK 4:26 Ekom Anutu se wong Eliya la wou xel Israelyeiw on ti, qe wong e la wou vexeiv ti eivek beyeeng Sarepat eivek tembuing wei Saidon nei.
LUK 4:27 Me inye moux alis vex ngenong toundei eivek Israel eno vanei lepa wong xel eivek bouk wei poropet Elisa yo, ekom xelti se wo nimzalek, qe Naimang wei Siria nei venaxow.”
LUK 4:28 Xomaxoneing dalus wei toundei eivek xomek qekueing ama eno laleind wo vanei ngandoung gyeik ingwei xel ngo qayeeng tiyon o.
LUK 4:29 Xel qandi lek, me tiy e la myayaing veil beyeeng wei xel ev lek qetyei. Om xel qou e me la lek bembembek wei lukendu yon en embei tendu e doing.
LUK 4:30 Ekom dembu me la senghoing eivek moux alis vex ngenongakes on de la.
LUK 4:31 Woyom moxo lep me la xo Kapenaom nei, beyeeng on toundei eivek distrik Galili, de lek bouk wei Sabat eno mi teyoxe xomaxoneing.
LUK 4:32 Xel etek en e xe qayeeng wei teyoxe yo, en e xe qayeeng on lam is nikanzek ngandoung.
LUK 4:33 Eivek xomek qekueing ama eno tambiy ti memo laweeng nilaxes mindei eivek e. Moxo eng ngandoungateiv me neil,
LUK 4:34 “E! Wa being bong vati wou xa, Yesu wei Nasaret o? Wang lam en wa being nam bo nol wou xa? A woulek wang woy bei wa Tambiy Vambuing tiwei Anutu xe yo!”
LUK 4:35 Om Yesu luk niseikeing wou e me neil, “Denduing ma! De lam myayaing veil moux tiyon!” Om memo yon nex tambiy on la lek tembuing wou xel mend de lam myayaing veil e dom se wo nol wou no.
LUK 4:36 Xomaxoneing on dalus etek me di neil wouma bei, “Teyoxeing qayeeng tine vati? Om lam is lei ngandoung me nikanzek de luk nikanzek wou laweeng nilaxes me xel lam myayaing!”
LUK 4:37 Me e xe pavulek wei wong vatiyeiw eno la teyei lek tembuing tiyon dalus.
LUK 4:38 Yesu la veil xomek qekueing ama me la eivek Simon beeng. Gying ngandoung wo nol wou Simon yeing avexta, me gweimbeeng xel teling wou Yesu bei e devind vexo.
LUK 4:39 Om la paviy vexo me luk niseikeing wou gying, me ema veil e. Vexo qandi lek lutika me la menyex wou lul yaeing wou xel.
LUK 4:40 Gyeik ingwei sayeiv teila eno xomaxoneing qou xel dalus wei vanei nelu nelu wong xel o me la wou Yesu me e liw mema lek xel titi, moxo wong xel dalus wo nimzalek.
LUK 4:41 Xel memo ngenongakes lam myayaing veil xomaxoneing ngenong me di taxe bei, “Wang on Anutu Neu Moux!” Ekom moxo luk nikanzek wou xel me peti xel, en nambei xel woulek bei e Kilisi.
LUK 4:42 Satiboukeing lul eno Yesu qandi me la ingwei xel ma veil o. Om xomaxoneing mi yimexe e, gyeik ingwei xel la yeiwou e eno xel wong en xel embei neil axound e bei e se na veil xel.
LUK 4:43 Ekom neil embei, “A na neil Xoulek Nimza wei tete lalei wei Anutu yo, wou xel beyeeng bamba nei is, en qes tiyon om wong a lam.”
LUK 4:44 Me moxo la neil xoulek lala eivek xomek qekueing ama dalus wei Yudia nei.
LUK 5:1 Bouk ti eno Yesu la nale wou lounyeing Genesaret nenyawes, me xomaxoneing ngenong la vingama e vivekwou e, me di ngo Anutu xe xoulek.
LUK 5:2 Yesu yei bot yayuw di yeip wou lounyeing nenyawes, xel wei mi qou woing eno la veil, en xel la di sekweyexe xel xe lewek.
LUK 5:3 Yesu lek la eivek bot ti, tiyon Simon xe, me teling wou Simon bei e tendu bot na nayaka veil lounyeing nenyawes. Woyom la dei lek bot me teyoxe xel ngenongakes on.
LUK 5:4 Gyeik ingwei e neil xoulek woy, eno neil wou Simon bei, “Tendu bot e la eivek memiing manghembi me nex lewek teila eivek en kandek na puw woing o.”
LUK 5:5 Simon lewexe bei, “Teiv, boukeing tine xa wong xuk ngandoung ek xa se qou lulti. Ekom wang neil, om tyek a nox banex lewek na eivek memiing no.”
LUK 5:6 Gyeik xel wong ambei nyon eno woing ngenong eivek me lewek embei tax.
LUK 5:7 Om xel nex memend en xel wei xel xouing mi wong xuk lekti wei toundei lek bot nge yo me xel lam vind xel me toung woing eivek bot luw xouing me e puplek om wong bot luw xouing di teila eivek memiing lalei.
LUK 5:8 Gyeik ingwei Simon Petele yei inyon, eno la ev vaxa qatu eivek wou Yesu me neil embei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, la veil ay, en a moux wei sewokeing o.”
LUK 5:9 En e is liyeiw dalus wei toundei is e eno etek en ingwei xel qou woing ngenong o.
LUK 5:10 Me Sebedi neu Jems aluw Yoan wei luw mi wong xuk woing is Simon, eno luw yei me etek is. Woyom Yesu neil wou Simon bei, “Wa seng gwaleeng. En gweimbeeng me e mi na eno tyek wang bong xuk me na qou xomaxoneing.”
LUK 5:11 Om xel puw xel xe bot luw xouing la nale yasewis, woyom xel ghanaw lulul dalus toundei de la betiwou Yesu.
LUK 5:12 Ka Yesu toundei eivek beyeeng ti, eno tambiy ti lam, ninavi pup en vanei lepa. Gyeik ingwei yei Yesu, moxo yeip ma eivek tembuing wou e me tay wou e, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wangwei wa laleim devind ond wang bong am bo nimzalek.”
LUK 5:13 Yesu tatei mema la me axlek moux tiyon. Moxo neil embei, “A laleing vind, wang bo nimzalek!” De lutika eno lepa ma veil e.
LUK 5:14 Woyom Yesu luk nikanzek wou embei, “Wa se neil wou xelti, qe la, me talex xow wou lumuki, me ghe bong xound na nambei Mose neil o en e talex bei wang wo nimzalek, en xel boulek bei wa xe vanei ma.”
LUK 5:15 De pavulek wei Yesu eno la wo ngandoung, om xomaxoneing ngenong lam me ngo e de moxo wong xel xe vanei wo nimzalek.
LUK 5:16 Ekom Yesu venaxow mi la veil xel me la tembuing bandaing me la zeimema.
LUK 5:17 Bouk ti gyeik Yesu di teyoxe moux alis vex me dei, eno xel Parisi me xel putoung wei petieing eno xel lam anghei beyeeng dalus wei Galili me Yudia me beyeeng Yerusalem, me la toundei inyei. Me Tambiy Ngandoung xe nikanzek lam eivek Yesu me e wong moux alis vex xe vanei wo nimzalek.
LUK 5:18 Xel moux valu qalei tambiy wei bezomb o ti lek lelek me lam, xel di wong me yei en xel embei qou e me na xomek lalei me na niw wou Yesu ma.
LUK 5:19 Gyeik ingwei xel lam eno xel ngenongakes toundei zeyi om xel se teyeimbei gyeiwou sakwaing ti me na eivek xomek lalei. Om xel lek xomek demi qetyei me gwang danghei ti me byex yis lek lelek me wong tambiy on di teila kaka eivek moux alis vex senghoing wou Yesu ma.
LUK 5:20 Gyeik ingwei Yesu yei xel xe wongeingis, moxo neil embei, “Gweleeng, a semaleeng wa xe sewokeing.”
LUK 5:21 Xel Parisi me xel putoung wei petieing o di wou eivek naleind, “Eti ingwei embei qou Anutu nimbeeng nei? Xelti se teyeimbei semaleeng sewokeing, qe Anutu venaxow.”
LUK 5:22 Yesu woulek vati wei xel di wou naleind en o me teling, “Nambei nya xam ghe di wou naleimim en lulti beimambei ne eivek laleimim?
LUK 5:23 Qayeeng vati teyei bei neileing, ‘A semaleeng wa xe sewokeing’ o neileing bei, ‘Wa qandi lek me ghe na?’
LUK 5:24 Ekom inyon xam ghe boulek bei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux qou lei ngandoung lek tembuing en embei semaleeng sewokeing.” Moxo neil wou moux ti bezombeing on, “A neil wou wang, qandi lek, qou wa xe lelek me la bam.”
LUK 5:25 Lutika eno moxo qandi lek wou moux alis vex mend me qou e xe vati wei yeip lek o me la beeng de di sanghoxe Anutu.
LUK 5:26 Xomaxoneing dalus etek en ingwei xel yei Anutu xe nikanzek me poux zeng, de sanghoxe Anutu me neil embei, “Xey a xei lulvako ngandoung gweimbeeng.”
LUK 5:27 Ka tine la veil eno Yesu la myayaing me yei tambiy wei mi qou takis o ti lei Livai eno toundei eivek xomek takis. Yesu neil wou bei, “Wa betiy ay.”
LUK 5:28 Livai qandi lek me ghanaw lulul dalus de betiwou e.
LUK 5:29 Woyom Livai wong mata ngandoung ti wou Yesu eivek xomek wei e nei me xel qendu ngandoung wei mi qou takis o me xel valu lam ya is xel.
LUK 5:30 Ekom xel Parisi me xel putoung wei petieing o eivek qendu wei Parisi yo di neil Yesu xe xel betiyeing, “Nambei nya xam ghe di wa me ghe num is xel wei mi qou takis me xel wei sewokeing o?”
LUK 5:31 Yesu lewexe me neil embei, “Xel wei vanei ma eno se mi la wou dokta, qe xel wei vanei yo.
LUK 5:32 A se lam bei taxe xel wei bombek o, qe xel wei sewokeing o en xel pekwi xow.”
LUK 5:33 De xel neil wou embei, “Xel betiyeing wei Yoan o di vambu yaeing me zeimemend me xel betiyeing wei Parisi yo is, ekom ingwei wang eno di wo eisanou lek yaeing me numeing.”
LUK 5:34 Yesu lewexe bei, “Wang teyei bei bong xel wei lam toundei is tambiy wei embei dii vex eno vambu yaeing gyeik e toundei is xel o?
LUK 5:35 Ekom bouk tyek nam gyeik ingwei xel a qou tambiy tiwei embei dii vex eno me na veil xel, on tyek eivek bouk kayon eno xel vambu yaeing.”
LUK 5:36 Me Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tine wou xel bei, “Xelti se mi qateiv teimb ding myasepu wei vako yo me duw eivek ingwei takwei yo. Wangwei e bong ambei nyon, on tyek zex teimb ding wei vako yo, de ing vako eno tyek se ghok ingwei takwei yo.
LUK 5:37 Me xelti se mi taw wain nilouk vako eivek wain takwei ninavi. Wangwei e bong ambei nyon on tyek wain vako zex wain ninavi, de wain tyek na taw veil de wain ninavi zex me bo nol.
LUK 5:38 Ma, xel a taw wain vako eivek wain ninavi vako.
LUK 5:39 Me xel tiwei num wain takwei eno tyek laleind se devind bei na num vako, en tyek na neimbei, ‘Takwei nimza.’”
LUK 6:1 De Sabat ti eno Yesu la di ghavineeng eivek xuk lalei wei wit o. Me e xe xel betiyeing ul wit neing valu me liyexe eivek memend me wong navi veil de ya neing.
LUK 6:2 Dekakom Parisi valu teling bei, “Xam ghe wong vati wei se la teyei lek o lek Sabat enva?”
LUK 6:3 Yesu lewexe me neil, “Xam seng pyaw vati wei Dawit wong gyeik ingwei e is e xe xel maxepya xel o?
LUK 6:4 Moxo la eivek Anutu xe xomek, me la qou belet vambuing wei xel mi toung wou Anutu ma yo, moxo ya vati wei petieing lewexe lek bei, xel lumuki venaxow a mi gya yo. De moxo wong valu wou e xe xel me xel ya is.”
LUK 6:5 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel bei, “Xomaxoneing Neu Moux ne Tambiy Ngandoung wei Sabat o.”
LUK 6:6 Lek Sabat nge eno moxo la eivek xomek qekueing ama me di teyoxe xel. Tambiy ti toundei inyon eno mema payeiv bezomb.
LUK 6:7 Xel Parisi me xel putoung wei petieing o di yimexe qes wei xel embei byex qayeeng lek Yesu yo, om xel di yei e teyei teyei bei tyek se bong vanei ti bo nimzalek Sabat.
LUK 6:8 Ekom Yesu yei woueing nalei wei xel o, om neil wou tambiy wei mema bezomb bei, “Qandi lek me la nale mya wou xel sapa mend.” Om moxo qandi lek me la nale inyei.
LUK 6:9 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel, “Ambei teling xam. Nyei vati la teyei lek en bouk wei Sabat o, xey a bong kwa nimza lek, o xey a bong kwa nilul lek? Xey a devind mapieing o xey a bo nol wou?”
LUK 6:10 Moxo yei e vivekwou xel dalus, dekalekom neil wou tambiy tiyon bei, “Tatei memam.” Moxo wong ambei nyon de mema wo nimzalek.
LUK 6:11 Ekom xel Parisi me xel putoung wei petieing o laleind wo vanei me di neil wouma bei, “Tyek xey a bong vati wou Yesu?”
LUK 6:12 Lek bouk on ti eno Yesu lek lukendu ti me la en embei na zeimema. Moxo mi zeimema wou Anutu eivek boukeing tiyon dalus.
LUK 6:13 Gyeik ingwei woyaing eno Yesu taxe e xe xel betiyeing dalus lam wou e me beyal xel xoumeeng yuw wei taxe sinale lek xel o.
LUK 6:14 Ti lei Simon (wei Yesu taxe e lei Petele yo), li Andrias, Jems, Yoan, Pilip, Batolomiu,
LUK 6:15 Matai, Tomas, Jems wei Alpias neu yo, me Simon wei xel taxe bei Selot o,
LUK 6:16 Yudas wei Jems neu me Yudas Iskariot tiwei toung Yesu eivek xel vevek memend o.
LUK 6:17 Woyom Yesu lep lek lukendu me la xonei is e xe xel betiyeing me la nale lek beyeeng wei sambus o. E xe xel betiyeing ngenong toundei inyon me xomaxoneing ngenong lam anghei Yudia sapa, me nanghei beyeeng Yerusalem, me nanghei mamileeng vi wei paviy beyeeng Taia me Saidon eno lam toundei inyon.
LUK 6:18 Xel lam en embei ngo e xe qayeeng de e bong xel xe vanei bo nimzalek. Me moux alis vex wei xel laweeng nilaxes wo nol wou xel eno Yesu wong xel wo nimzalek.
LUK 6:19 Me xomaxoneing dalus di wong me yei en xel embei daxlek e, en nambei nikanzek di lam eivek e me wong xel dalus wo nimzalek.
LUK 6:20 Yesu yei e xe xel betiyeing, de neil embei, “Xam wei kanyo yo ghe bo xeimimlala, en Anutu xe tete lalei yon xam xe.
LUK 6:21 Xam wei maxep mi ya xam gweimbeeng eno ghe bo xeimimlala en loxyus eno tyek xam ghe gwa me enden xam. Xam wei ghe mi eng gweimbeeng eno ghe bo xeimimlala en tyek loxyus eno xam a mi nap.
LUK 6:22 Xam ghe bo xeimimlala gyeik ingwei xel moux laleind bo nol wou xam, gyeik ingwei xel a tiy xam me na neil qayeeng nol lek xam, me pesek xam leimim nambei nilul, qes en Xomaxoneing Neu Moux.
LUK 6:23 “Ond lek bouk kayon xam ghe bo xeimimlala me davyeip davyeip is xeilala, en xam xe xouveing ngandoung toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu nei. En nambei nyon eno xel bundyeiw mi wong kwa kayon wou xel poropet.
LUK 6:24 “Ekom xam wei lulul ana yo ghe gwaleeng amim, en xam ghe qou lulul wei wong xam laleimim wo nimza yo woy.
LUK 6:25 Xam wei ghe mi wa ngenong gweimbeeng me enden xam eno xam ghe gwaleeng amim. En tyek loxyus eno maxep gya xam. Xam wei ghe mi nap gweimbeeng ne, xam ghe gwaleeng amim. En tyek loxyus eno xam ghe bo talot me ghe deeng.
LUK 6:26 Xam ghe gwaleeng amim gyeik ingwei moux alis vex dalus baluk qayeeng nimza en xam o. En takwei eno xel bundyeiw mi wong ambei nyon wou xel poropet wei tyonyeing o.”
LUK 6:27 Yesu neil no bei, “A neil wou xam eti yeiw wei ghe mi ngo axe qayeeng o: Xam laleimim devind xel vevek amba wei xam o, de ghe bong nimza wou eti yeiw wei laleind mi wo nilul wou xam o,
LUK 6:28 Xam ghe bo mata wou eti yeiw wei mi neil vya lek xam o, dom na zeimemamim en xel wei mi wo nol wou xam o.
LUK 6:29 Wangwei xelti petapexe wa ling valu ond wa pekwi valu wou en e petapexe is. De wangwei xelti qou wa xe teimb ding, on wa se neil axound wa xe teimb wei embei qou yo.
LUK 6:30 Xam ghe bong lulul wou xel sapa wei teling xam o, me eti yeiw qou xam xe lulul, on xam se baluk nikanzek bei xel bong enoum.
LUK 6:31 Xam ghe bong wou xel bange nambei ingwei xam ambei xel bong wou xam o.
LUK 6:32 “Wangwei xam laleimim devind xel wei laleind mi vind xam o venaxow, on tyek xam a qou lul nimza vati en inyon? Xel sewokeing is ambei nyon, xel laleind mi vind xel wei laleind mi vind xel o.
LUK 6:33 Me wangwei xam ghe bong kwa nimza wou xel wei mi wo nimza wou xam o venaxow, on tyek xam a qou lul nimza vati en inyon? Xel sewokeing mi wong ambei nyon is o.
LUK 6:34 Me wangwei xam ghe bong vineing en malew wou moux alis vex valu de ghe wou naleimim bei tyek xel bong xouveing noum wou xam venaxow, ond tyek xam a qou lul nimza vati en inyon? Xel sewokeing is ambei nyon xel mi wong vineing en malew wou xel sewokeing valu en xel woulek bei tyek xel bong xouveing dalus noum zeyi.
LUK 6:35 Ekom xam laleim devind xel vevek amba, me ghe bong nimza wou xel, de ghe bong lul e na bandaing wou xel de xam seng bou kwamim bei na qou lulul ti noumenam. Woyom tyek xam xe xouveing bo ngandoung, me tyek xam ghe bong ambei Anutu gheyapu neu. En mi wong nimza wou xel wei se mi neil dange wou e yo me xel wei nilul o.
LUK 6:36 Xam laleimim e mi pyaxow nambei xam Mamim lalei mi pyaxow en xel o.
LUK 6:37 “Xam seng gwei xel nge me baluk en e, enok Anutu gyei xam me baluk en xam. Xam se byex qayeeng lek xel nge me na neimbei xel wong nilul. Enok Anutu na byex qayeeng lek xam me na neimbei xam ghe wo nilul. Xam semaleeng nilul wei xel nge yo on tyek Anutu semaleeng nilul wei xam o.
LUK 6:38 Xam ghe bong wou xel nge, on tyek Anutu bong enoum wou xam. Tyek bong lul ngenong me na toung mema lek e deteina me na qounghexe e pup me qapyex veil me bong wou xam. En lulul vamva wei xam ghe wong wou xel nge, eno tyek Anutu bong lulul vamva yon noum wou xam nambei nyon.”
LUK 6:39 De Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tine wou xel bei, “Teyeimbei moux matekeing ti natax en moux matekeing nge? Yon tyek luw xouing se deivek leiveeng?
LUK 6:40 Yak qapiya ti se ghanaw e xe putoung, qe ka e gwevek boy on tyek xel titi teyei lek e xe putoung.
LUK 6:41 “Nambei nya wang wei papu nayaka wei toundei eivek lim ma yon de wa seng wei pelang wei toukale eivek wa venaxow mam on?
LUK 6:42 Nambei nya wang neil wou lim bei, ‘Ling, wong a wo papu kawei toundei eivek wa mam on veil’ de wa seng wei pelang wei toukale eivek wa mam on? Wa tambiy wei myam yuw, myaxeeng eno wa pu pelang wei toukale eivek wa mam on, dekakom ghe gwei embo nimza me ghe bong papu nayak kawei toundei eivek lim ma yon veil.”
LUK 6:43 Yesu neil no bei, “Xax nimza se mi vuk neing nol, o xax wei nol eno se mi vuk neing nimza.
LUK 6:44 Xel xomaxoneing mi yei xaxaneing wole dekakom xel woulek bei inyon xax nimza o inyon xax nol. Xel xomaxoneing se mi la wou yis wei ying o me ul xax basunghek neing lek. Me xel se mi ul wain neing lek xax wei yingying o.
LUK 6:45 Tambiy wei nimza eno mi wong kwa nimzamza wei toundei eivek e lalei yo, de tambiy wei nilul eno kwa nilul ngenong toundei eivek e lalei. Om mi wong kwa nilul. Kwa vati wei pup e lalei lek eno mya mi neil.”
LUK 6:46 Yesu neil no bei, “Nambei nya xam ghe mi taxe ay bei, ‘Tambiy Ngandoung, Tambiy Ngandoung,’ de xam seng mi betiwou qayeeng wei a mi neil o?
LUK 6:47 Wangwei xelti nam wou ay me na ngo axe qayeeng me betiwou, on tyek a talex wou xam bei e yon nambei nya.
LUK 6:48 Inyon teyei lek moux ti embei dev xomek o. Moxo ev leiveeng la ghembi me lax mundeeng lek qakous tata eivek tembuing lalei. Dekakom ev xomek lek gheyapu. Gyeik ingwei memiing butek me lam bimexe xomek tiyon, eno xomek se qepei, en tambiy tiyon ev xomek wo nikanzekta.
LUK 6:49 Ekom tambiy tiwei ngo axe qayeeng me se betiwou, eno nambei moux tiwei ev xomek lek tembuing de se ev mundeeng la eivek qakous. Dekakom memiing butekeing lam bimexe lek xomek tiyon eno qepei me lelolexe dalus.”
LUK 7:1 Gyeik ingwei Yesu neil qayeeng tiyon dalus ma wou xomaxoneing me xel ngo woy, de moxo la eivek beyeeng Kapenaom.
LUK 7:2 Nanghei inyei eno beyeiv wei xel vevek wei Rom o ti mindei. E xe xukxe tiwei lalei mi vind e ghanaw veil eno vanei wong me embim amey.
LUK 7:3 Gyeik ingwei beyeiv ngo Yesu lam eno wong xel teivateiv wei Yudayeiw eno valu la wou e, me teling wou bei e na bong e xe xukxe bo nimzalek.
LUK 7:4 Gyeik ingwei xel lam wou Yesu, eno xel tay wou e bei, “Tambiy tine nimza, teyeimbei wa devind e,
LUK 7:5 en nambei moxo lalei mi vind xey wei Yuda yo, me ev xa xe xomek qekueing ama.”
LUK 7:6 Om Yesu la is xel. Moxo la paviy xomek, gyeik inyon eno beyeiv wong gweleeng valu la neil wou embei: “Tambiy Ngandoung, wa seng bo pok wou xow en a se teyei lek bei wang nam eivek a bang.
LUK 7:7 Inye qes ambei nye, om a wou naleing bei a se teyei lek bei a maxow a nak wou wang. Qe wa neil qayeeng dom a xe xukxe embo nimzalek.
LUK 7:8 En a maxow is a tambiy wei a mi wevek tambiy wei wo lei ngandoung en ay yo, is axe xel vevek wei mi wevek a xeinghembi yo. A neil wou tine bei, ‘La,’ on moxo la, me nge nei, ‘Lam,’ on moxo lam. A neil wou a xe xukxe bei, ‘Wang bong xuk tine,’ on moxo wong.”
LUK 7:9 Gyeik Yesu ngo qayeeng tine eno moxo etek en e, me pekwi ma wou moux alis vex ngenong wei di betiy e yon, me neil wou xel bei, “A neil wou xam, a se xei xelti xe wongeingis wei ngandoung o nambei nye eivek Israel sapa.”
LUK 7:10 Woyom xel moux wei beyeiv wong xel la eno loumelam xomek me yeimbei xukxe wo nimzalek.
LUK 7:11 Ka enden nayaka le eno Yesu la beyeeng ti xel mi neil Nain, me e xe xel betiyeing me moux alis vex ngenong la is e.
LUK 7:12 Ka la paviy tete mya wei beyeeng, eno xel qalei meyeing ti me lam myayaing, vexeiv ti neu moux tixemou yon, de moux alis vex ngenong wei beyeeng eno lam is e.
LUK 7:13 Me gyeik ingwei Tambiy Ngandoung yei vex on eno lalei pyaxow en e me neil wou e, “Wa seng deeng.”
LUK 7:14 Woyom la paviy me axlek qoupek meyeing, me xel wei di qalei eno nale kanzek. De moxo neil, “Moux ghavis, a neil wou wang, qandi lek!”
LUK 7:15 De moux meyeing on qandi lek me dei ghey me luk atax, dekakom Yesu wong e lox me la wou ta.
LUK 7:16 Xomaxoneing dalus etek en ingwei xel yei Anutu xe nikanzek me sanghoxe Anutu me neil, “Poropet ngandoung ti qandi eivek xey senghoing, Anutu lam en embei devind e xe xomaxoneing.”
LUK 7:17 Pavulek wei Yesu ne eno xel tul ela wo tambak eivek Yudia me tembuing danghei danghei nei.
LUK 7:18 Yoan xe xel betiyeing neil wou e en lul dalus ti beimambei wei Yesu wong on. Om moxo taxe e xe xel betiyeing yayuw,
LUK 7:19 me wong luw la wou Tambiy Ngandoung bei na teling e, “Inye wa tambiy tiwei embei nam o, o xa mi daxe tambiy nge?”
LUK 7:20 Gyeik ingwei moux yuw on la wou Yesu, eno luw neil wou e bei, “Yoan Lipekeing wong uw alam wou wang, bei nam a teling, ‘Inye wa tambiy tiwei embei nam o, o xa mi daxe tambiy nge?’”
LUK 7:21 Lek bouk tiyon eno Yesu wong moux alis vex ngenong xe vanei leimalei wo nimzalek, me tiy xel laweeng nol wei toundei eivek moux alis vex eno veil, me wong xel ngenong wei mend tekeing eno yeila.
LUK 7:22 Om Yesu neil elox wou nenyalesana luw bei, “Muw ghe nox a neil wou Yoan en vati wei muw venaxow ghe wei me ghe ngo yo: Xel wei mend tekeing eno yeila, xel wei vaxend nol eno qeilek me la, xel wei lepa eno wo nimzalek, nenya qatu eno ngowou, de meyeing qandi lek, me xel kanyo eno ngo Xoulek Nimza.
LUK 7:23 Xel wei yei ay me xel xe wongeingis se tei eivek en ay eno xel bo xeindlala.”
LUK 7:24 Ka Yoan xe nenyales aluw lox veil le, eno Yesu neil wou moux alis vex en Yoan bei, “Xam ghe la eivek tembuing bandaing en xam a being na gwei vati? Ghet tiwei laweeng di vei elox me loum o?
LUK 7:25 Wangwei nama nei, yond xam ghe la bei na gwei vati? Beip xam ghe la di wei tambiy wei byex teimb nimzamza yo? Ma, xel wei mi byex teimb wei malew tata yo me xel xe lul nimzamza wei neing eno mindei eivek xel king bend.
LUK 7:26 Ekom xam ghe la en xam a being na gwei vati? Poropet ti? Ee, a neil wou xam, poropet tiyon ghanaw xel poropet ba.
LUK 7:27 Tambiy tiyon xel byex eivek xoulek ambei nye, “‘Wei, tyek a bong axe nenyalesana wei mi neil qayeeng o ti natax en wang, me tyek gyeiwou sakwaing en wang.’
LUK 7:28 A neil wou xam, eivek xel wei tayeiw wou xel o eno Yoan ghanaw xel. Ekom tambiy wei lei maeing eivek Anutu xe tete lalei eno ghanaw Yoan.”
LUK 7:29 (Xomaxoneing dalus, is xel wei mi qou takis o, gyeik xel ngo Yesu xe qayeeng, eno xel neil embei Anutu xe sakwaing on wo bombek, en nambei Yoan lipek xel.
LUK 7:30 Ekom xel Parisi is xel wei lupeyei ngandoung en petieing wei Mose eno xel pesek Anutu xe woueing nalei en sakwaing nimza wei xel o, en nambei Yoan se lipek xel.)
LUK 7:31 Yesu neil, “Tyek anghei xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne me talex xel lek vati? Xel on nambei nya?
LUK 7:32 Xel on teyei lek yakyak wei mindei eivek beyeeng wei vateivek o me taxe la wou xel valu bei, “ ‘Xa vei sakwep en xam ekom xam seng aw, xa wo talot ekom xam seng eng.’
LUK 7:33 En Yoan Lipekeing lam eno se ya belet me se num wain, eno xam ghe neimbei, ‘Moxo memo toundei eivek e.’
LUK 7:34 De Xomaxoneing Neu Moux lam ya me num, eno xam ghe neimbei, ‘Tambiy yon mi ya ngenong me mi num wain ngenong de e gweleeng wei xel wei mi qou takis o me sewokeing o.’
LUK 7:35 Ekom lupeyei nimza eno yeip yaing bei inye bombek en mapieing wei xel dalus wei mi betiwou yo.”
LUK 7:36 De Parisi ti taxe Yesu bei e na gya is e, om moxo la xomek wei Parisi yo me la dei lek zek me ya.
LUK 7:37 Gyeik vex wei sewokeing o ti mindei eivek beyeeng tiyon eno ngo Yesu la di ya eivek Parisi beeng, vexo qou botol qakous nimza is wel xeimangou toukale eivek o me la.
LUK 7:38 Vexo la nale wou Yesu demi paviy e vaxa de eng, me malouk taw lek Yesu vaxa. Woyom tul luvelus me vu Yesu vaxa luw angya, me sesuvexe Yesu vaxa lumama de taw wel lek e vaxa luw.
LUK 7:39 Gyeik ingwei Parisi tiwei taxe Yesu la eno yei vex tiyon wong ambei nyon, eno luk wou xow bei, “Wangwei tambiy tine poropet ti on tyek boulek bei eti axlek e me vex tiyon nambei nya, vex on sewokeing.”
LUK 7:40 Yesu lewexe lek e bei, “Simon, axe qayeeng ti om ambei neil wou wang.” Moxo neil embei, “Putoung wa neil wou ay.”
LUK 7:41 Woyom Yesu neil wou e, “Moux yayuw qou malew vateivek wou tambiy ti, nge qou selewa vaxak xoumeeng de nge qou selewa vaxak ti.
LUK 7:42 Luw malew ma en ingwei luw embei bong enox zeyi yo, om tambiy on semaleeng malew vateivek wei luw xouing o. Om luw nge na laleind vind e ghanaw veil?”
LUK 7:43 Simon neil elox, “A wou naleing bei, tambiy tiwei e xe malew vateivek ngandoung wei e semaleeng veil o.” Yesu neil embei, “Wang wei me ghe neil bombek.”
LUK 7:44 Woyom moxo pekwi ma wou vex me neil wou Simon bei, “Wang wei vex tine? A lam eivek wa bam. Eno wa seng wong memiing valu bei a sekweyexe vaxang, qe vex tine sekweyexe a vaxang en malouk me vu gya luvelus.
LUK 7:45 Wa seng sesuvexe ay. Qe gyeik a eivek a lam wa bam eno vex tine se tip sesuvexeing a vaxang.
LUK 7:46 Wa seng taw wel lek a lung, qe vexo taw wel xeimangou yo lek a vaxang.
LUK 7:47 Om nambei nyon a neil wou wang, vexo xe sewokeing ngenong eno semaleeng veil, om vexo lalei vind a ghanaw veil. Ekom tambiy wei Anutu semaleeng e xe sewokeing nayaka eno e xe lalei vineing nayaka.”
LUK 7:48 Woyom Yesu neil wou vexo, “A semaleeng wa xe sewokeing veil.”
LUK 7:49 Xel bamba wei toundei lek zek me ya eno di neil eivek ama senghoing bei, “Eti inye om teyeimbei semaleeng sewokeing veil?”
LUK 7:50 Yesu neil wou vex on, “Wa xe wongeingis eno vind wang. Lak is laleim vevopeing.”
LUK 8:1 Ka tine lak veil Yesu la ghavineeng eivek beyeeng nge me la nge me la valu is me neil Xoulek Nimza wei Anutu xe tete lalei eno teyei. Xel xoumeeng yuw la is e.
LUK 8:2 Me vex valu wei Yesu tiy laweeng nol veil xel me wong xel xe vanei wo nimzalek o: Maria (xel mi taxe e bei Makdala) wei memo lim yuw lam myayaing veil e yo,
LUK 8:3 Joana ne Kuza venei, inyon tambiy wei wo lei ngandoung en Herot beeng o, Susana, me vex ngenong is. Vex ti beimambei yon mi wong xel venaxow xe lulul bei na mi devind Yesu lis e xe betiyeing.
LUK 8:4 Dekalekom xomaxoneing wei beyeeng sapa eno lam wou Yesu me xel qendu ngandoung qekuma me lam dei. De moxo neil qayeeng pakeing tine:
LUK 8:5 “Tambiy tiwei mema xuk eno di vuw wit vei eivek xuk. Ka di vuw vei eivek xuk, eno valu teila lek sakwaing, me xel qeilek de menek lam ya.
LUK 8:6 Valu teila lek qakous, om gyeik ingwei xel tyip eno xel mey en tembuing nilouk ma.
LUK 8:7 De vei valu teila eivek yis senghoing wei yingying o, me xel dalus tyip me ding dekakom yis sevunexe wit.
LUK 8:8 De vei valu teila eivek tembuing wei nimza yo, om tyip me vuk neing ngenong teyei lek vaxak ngenong ghanaw ingwei vuw o.” Gyeik ingwei moxo neil qayeeng pakeing tiyon ma, eno taxe bei, “Eti yeiw nenya nale lek e en ngoeing qayeeng, ond wong e ngo.”
LUK 8:9 Moxo xe xel betiyeing teling e, “Qayeeng pakeing tine qes ambei nya?”
LUK 8:10 De Yesu neil wou xel, “Lupeyei ngandoung wei qayeeng xupekeing qes wei Anutu xe tete lalei yo, Anutu wong wou xam. Ekom wou xel valu eno a mi luk eivek qayeeng pakeing en kandek, “ ‘xel gyei lumama, ekom xel se gyeiwou, de xel a ngo, ekom xel se boulek e qes.’
LUK 8:11 “Tine inye qayeeng pakeing qes: Vei yon Anutu xe xoulek.
LUK 8:12 Vei wei teila lek sakwaing eno nambei xel wei ngo Anutu xe xoulek dekakom tambiy mapetok lam zeim veil xel laleind, en kandek xel se bongis me e devind xel.
LUK 8:13 De vei wei tei lek qakous eno nambei xel wei qou xoulek is xeindlala gyeik ingwei xel ngo yo, ekom xel xe luselis se evla eivek tembuing. Xel wongis nayaka, deka bouk wei axeing lam eno xel tei veil.
LUK 8:14 De vei wei teila eivek yis wei yingying o senghoing eno xel teyei lek xel wei ngo Anutu xe qayeeng me betiwou, ekom gyeik xel la eno xel wou naleind en lulul wei deing mapieing wei xel o, me malew ngenongakes me xeilala wei tembuing ne wou xel zeyi om xel xe neing se doung.
LUK 8:15 Ekom vei wei teila lek tembuing nimza yo, eno teyei lek moux alis vex wei ngo xoulek me zeimaxoun o. Xel laleind nimza me bombek, me xel mi nale nikanzek me vuk neing lek.
LUK 8:16 “Xelti se mi byex eivek lam me vun eivek deng o mi toung eivek lelek yeipeing lek o xeinghembi. Qe moxo mi toung lek lam vaxa, en kandek xel wei eivek la lalei eno na mi gyei xeiyaing.
LUK 8:17 En lul dalus wei xupek eno tyek xel boulek, me lul dalus wei xel beliv eno tyek nam mendei yanyateiv.
LUK 8:18 “Nambei nyon xam ghe bou naleimim bo nimza en vati wei xam ambei ngo yo. Xelti xe lupeyei toundei on tyek Anutu bong valu is, ek xelti lupeyei e ma yon vati wei wounalei bei di qou eno tyek Anutu na zeim veil e.”
LUK 8:19 Yesu ta is liyeiw embei nam gyei e, ekom xel se teyeimbei na paviy e, en nambei moux alis vex ngenong qekuma me toundei.
LUK 8:20 Xelti neil wou e, “Tam alis limyeiw lam toukale myayaing, me axe en xel embei gyei wang.”
LUK 8:21 Moxo neil elox bei, “Moux alis vex wei mi ngo Anutu xe xoulek me betiwou eno inye a tang me a lingyeiw.”
LUK 8:22 Bouk ti eno Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei, “Xey ambei na lounyeing loxalu nei.” Om xel la eivek bot ti me la.
LUK 8:23 Ka bot di la eno Yesu yeip. Laweeng ngandoung ti lam lek lounyeing me vei memiing la eivek bot om xel la eivek nimaying ngandoung.
LUK 8:24 Xel betiyeing la piyexe Yesu, me neil embei, “Teiv, teiv, xey ambei zepna ne!” Moxo qandi lek me neil laweeng me memiing wei di vuklek o, me laweeng valeivek ma de memiing yeip kanzek.
LUK 8:25 Yesu teling e xe xel betiyeing bei, “Xam amim wongeingis inya?” Xel yaleeng me etek om xel di teling wouma bei, “Tambiy tine e eti? Om luk nikanzek wou laweeng me memiing me xel ngo me betiwou?”
LUK 8:26 Xel la loxalu nanghei danghei tiwei Gerasa nei, beyeeng wei toundei lounyeing loxalu wei Galili yo.
LUK 8:27 Gyeik Yesu teila me la yasewis eno moux wei memo nale eivek o ti nanghei beyeeng nayak on lam wou e. Takwei yeileing nei eno tambiy tine se mi byex teimb o se mindei eivek xomek ti, qe mindei eivek leiveeng meyeing.
LUK 8:28 Gyeik tambiy on yei Yesu, eno nyayek me teila yeip wou Yesu vaxa, de taxe xoulekeing bei, “Yesu, Anutu gheyapu Neu Moux, wa being bong vati wou ay? A tay wou wang bei wa seng bo nol wou ay!”
LUK 8:29 En Yesu luk niseikeing wou laweeng nilaxes bei enam myayaing veil moux on. Lumama eno laweeng nilaxes mi zeimaxoun e, de xomaxoneing mi qo e mema vaxa nangya sen me xel mi yei e teyei, ekom moxo mi tax sen veil xow de memo mi qou e me la ingwei xel ma veil o.
LUK 8:30 Yesu teling e, “Wa leim vati?” Moxo neil elox bei, “Qendu ngandoung.” En nambei memo ngenong la eivek e.
LUK 8:31 Me xel tay wou Yesu lumama bei e se tiy xel na eivek leiveeng tiwei qes maeing o.
LUK 8:32 Bok qendu ti di ya me nale wou qetyei nenyawes nanghei inyon. Xel memo tay wou Yesu bei e bong xel na eivek xel bok on, om lenghek lek xel.
LUK 8:33 Gyeik ingwei xel memo lam myayaing veil moux on, xel la eivek xel bok on, me bok qendu dalus on veimyend me la oing bembembek me heivek lounyeing me mey.
LUK 8:34 Gyeik ingwei xel wei mi yeiteyei xel bok on yei vati wei qandi, eno xel veimyend me la neil lulti yon teyei wou xel wei beyeeng nayak, me beyeeng beimambei nei is,
LUK 8:35 me xomaxoneing la yei vati wei qandi yo. Gyeik ingwei xel lam wou Yesu eno xel yei moux tiwei xel memo la veil e yo. De moxo byex teimb me lupeyei wo nimza, me toundei wou Yesu vaxa. De xel yaleeng.
LUK 8:36 Xel wei yei lul on qandi, eno xel tul pavulek en wou xomaxoneing en ingwei memo la veil e nambei nya yo me e wo nimzalek o.
LUK 8:37 Woyom xomaxoneing dalus wei danghei ti Gerasa yon dalus teling Yesu bei e na veil xel, en nambei xel yaleeng ngandoung. Om lox eivek bot me la.
LUK 8:38 Moux tiwei memo la veil on tay wou bei na is e, ekom Yesu wong e la de neil wou bei,
LUK 8:39 “Wang nox bam me ghe nox a neil vati wei Anutu wong wou wang o teyei.” Om tambiy on la me neil vati wei Yesu wong wou e yo dalus teyei wou moux alis vex wei beyeeng nayak on.
LUK 8:40 Gyeik ingwei Yesu lox me la lounyeing loxalu eno moux alis vex qou e is xeindlala, en xel di axe e.
LUK 8:41 Woyom moux ti lei Yairus, inyon gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama yo, eno lam me ev vaxa qatu eivek wou Yesu vaxa, me wo nikanzek wou e bei Yesu na e beeng,
LUK 8:42 en nambei e neu vex tixemou yon e xe vakovek qes nambei xoumeeng yuw eno e bim a mey. Ka Yesu di la eno moux alis vex nale vingama zeyi e.
LUK 8:43 Me vex ti toukale inyon eno gyand mi lam eivek e teyei lek vakovek qes xoumeeng yuw, me vex tiyon mi saing e xe malew la wou dokta ekom xelti se wong e wo nimzalek.
LUK 8:44 Vexo la nale wou Yesu demi me axlek e xe teimb ding myasepu, lutika eno gyand touk veil e.
LUK 8:45 Yesu teling bei, “Eti axlek ay?” Gyeik xomaxoneing axvun, eno Petele neil, “Teiv, xomaxoneing ngenong nale vingama zeyi wang o.”
LUK 8:46 Ekom Yesu neil embei, “Xelti axlek ay. A woulek ingwei nikanzek lam myayaing veil ay yo.”
LUK 8:47 Woyom vexo yei bei tyek se ghupek, om la is nietekeing me ev vaxa qatu eivek wou Yesu vaxa eivek xomaxoneing dalus mend, vexo neil ingwei nambei nya axlek Yesu me nambei nya wo nimzalek luti.
LUK 8:48 Woyom Yesu neil wou vexo, “Neung vex, wa xe wongeingis wong wang wo nimzalek. La is laleim vevopeing.”
LUK 8:49 Ka Yesu nanghei di luk, eno xelti lam anghei Yairus beeng nei, inyon gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama yo. Moxo neil embei, “Neum vex mey om wa seng bo pok wou putoung no.”
LUK 8:50 Gyeik Yesu ngo tine eno neil wou Yairus bei, “Wa seng gwaleeng, qe wang bongis, en vexo tyek bo nimzalek.”
LUK 8:51 Gyeik ingwei Yesu la tyip Yairus beeng, eno se wong xel valu la lalei is e qe Petele, Yoan me Jems, me vex yak on ma luw ta.
LUK 8:52 Dekalekom xomaxoneing dalus di eng me wo talot en e. Yesu neil, “Xam tip engeing. En vexo se mey qe di yeip.”
LUK 8:53 Xel napexe e, en xel woulek bei vexo mey.
LUK 8:54 Ekom moxo zeim vexo mema me neil embei, “A neung yak, qandi lek!”
LUK 8:55 Vexo nu loumelam eivek, me lutika eno vexo qandi lek. Woyom Yesu neil wou xel bei xel bong lul yaeing me e gya.
LUK 8:56 Vexo ma luw ta etek, ekom Yesu peti luw nikanzek bei, “Muw se neil wou xelti en lul tiwei qandi yon.”
LUK 9:1 Gyeik ingwei Yesu taxe sinaleyeiw xoumeeng yuw qekuma, eno wong nikanzek me lei ngandoung wou xel bei xel a tiy memo dalus na myayaing veil moux alis vex me bong xel wei vanei wong eno bo nimzalek.
LUK 9:2 Me moxo wong xel la bei na neil xoulek wei Anutu xe tete lalei yo me bong xel wei vanei eno bo nimzalek.
LUK 9:3 Moxo neil wou xel, “Xam a being na eno xam se qou lulti, patongeeng me vaxak me belet me malew, me xam se qou teimb nge is.
LUK 9:4 Xomek tiwei xam ghe la eivek eno xam a mi mendei eivek deka xam ghe na veil beyeeng tiyon le.
LUK 9:5 Wangwei xomaxoneing wei beyeeng ti eno se qou xam, ond xam pepa vegyuveeng veil vaxamim gyeik ingwei xam ghe na veil xel xe beyeeng o, en xel boulek bei xel wo kwa yon nol wou xow.”
LUK 9:6 Om xel betiyeing la myayaing veil inyon me la beyeeng danghei danghei nei me neil Xoulek Nimza me wong xomaxoneing wei vanei yo wo nimzalek nanghei danghei danghei nei.
LUK 9:7 Seyap Herot ngo lul vatiyeiw dalus wei qandi yon. Me di wounalei ngenong, en nambei xel valu neil embei Yoan qandi lek veil meyeing,
LUK 9:8 de xel valu neil embei Eliya lam tyip, de valu neil embei poropet wei takwei yo ti loumelam qou mapieing no.
LUK 9:9 Ekom Herot neil embei, “A qateiv Yoan kwa tip. De eti ingwei di wong lulti beimambei yon me a ngo ne?” Me di wong me yei en embei gyei Yesu.
LUK 9:10 Gyeik sinaleyeiw loumelam, eno xel neil wou Yesu en vatiyeiw wei xel wong o. Woyom qou xel me xel venaxow la veil moux alis vex me la beyeeng tiwei xel mi neil Betsaida nei,
LUK 9:11 ekom moux alis vex ngenong on woulek en ingwei Yesu la om xel betiy e. Moxo wo xeilala en xel lam o me luk wou xel en Anutu xe tete lalei, me wong moux alis vex wei vanei yo wo nimzalek.
LUK 9:12 Soukeinglul eno xel xoumeeng yuw lam wou e me neil, “Wang bong moux alis vex na beyeeng danghei danghei nei en xel na gyei xend lul yaeing me beyeeng wei yeipeing o, en nambei beyeeng wei xey a toundei eivek ne eno xel ma veil.”
LUK 9:13 Moxo neil elox bei, “Xam ghe bong lul valu wou xel en xel gya.” Xel lewexe bei, “Xa di qou belet lim ka de woing yayuw, wambei xa na bou lulul yaeing wou xel ngenong ne?”
LUK 9:14 (Nambei 5,000 moux toundei inyon.) Ekom moxo neil wou e xe xel betiyeing, “Xam ghe bong xel mendei tembuing, e teyei lek 50 eivek qendu titi.”
LUK 9:15 Xel betiyeing wong ambei nyon, me xel dalus dei tembuing.
LUK 9:16 Woyom Yesu qou belet lim on is woing yuw on me yeima lekla tyoung gheyapu nei, me wong dange wou Anutu. De dembu belet is woing me wong wou xel betiyeing bei xel bong wou xomaxoneing.
LUK 9:17 Xel dalus ya me enden xel, de xel betiyeing qekuwou myapapu wei toundei yo me sei e pup eivek pasik xoumeeng yuw.
LUK 9:18 Bouk ti Yesu venaxow di zeimema me e xe xel betiyeing toundei is e, moxo teling wou xel bei, “Moux alis vex ngenong mi neil embei ay eti?”
LUK 9:19 Xel neil elox bei, “Xel valu neil embei wa Yoan Lipekeing, de valu neil embei Eliya, de valu neil embei poropet wei takwei eno ti loumelam dei mapieing.”
LUK 9:20 Moxo teling wou xel, “De xam ambei inya? Xam ghe neimbei ay eti?” Petele lewexe, “Wa Kilisi wei Anutu yo.”
LUK 9:21 Yesu peti xel nikanzek bei xel se neil inyon wou xelti.
LUK 9:22 Me moxo neil embei, “Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek na qou myavanei ngenong, me xel teivateiv me xel lumuki leitata yo me xel putoung wei petieing o tyek pesek e me nyeis e mey deka bouk yayal na veil om qandi lek.”
LUK 9:23 Woyom moxo neil wou xel dalus bei, “Wangwei xelti embei betiy ay, ond e dax xow vun me qalei e xe xax pepeeng taxombouk me betiwou ay.
LUK 9:24 En xelti embei zeimaxoun mapieing wei e yo ond tyek na saing e xe mapieing, ekom wangwei xelti saing mapieing wei e yo en ay on tyek mendei mapieing luta.
LUK 9:25 Wangwei xomaxoneing a qou lulul wei tembuing sapa ne ekom na saing mapieing wei e yo? Yon tyek bo nimza wou e nambei nya?
LUK 9:26 Wangwei xelti embei nigyaleeng en ay me axe qayeeng, on tyek Xomaxoneing Neu Moux nigyaleeng en e gyeik ingwei embei nam is e xe xeiyaing ngandoung me eivek xeiyaing wei Ma xe yo me xel angela vambuing o.
LUK 9:27 A neil wou xam zonghek, xel wei toukale inye yo valu tyek se daxe meyeing, qe tyek xel gyei Anutu xe tete lalei.”
LUK 9:28 Nambei bouk lim yal la veil en ingwei Yesu neil inyon o, moxo qou Petele, Yoan me Jems is xow me xel lek lukendu ti me la en embei na zeimema.
LUK 9:29 Ka e di zeimema, eno mapekwi me e xe teimb teltyip nambei zivip mi nex mema yo.
LUK 9:30 Moux yayuw, Mose luw Eliya,
LUK 9:31 luw lam is xeiyaing ngandoung me di luk is Yesu. Luw di luklek ingwei tyek na veil tembuing ne yo, me embim bong e xe xuk bo neing lek nanghei Yerusalem o.
LUK 9:32 Petele me luyuw wei la is e eno lal mend yeip om lal yeip, ekom gyeik ingwei lal qandi lek, lal yei e xe xeiyaing ngandoung me moux yuw wei toukale is e yon.
LUK 9:33 Ka moux yuw on di la veil Yesu, Petele neil wou e, “Teiv, inye nimza bei xey a toumendei inye. Wong xa ev xomek sel yayal, ti wou wang, ti wou Mose de ti wou Eliya.” (Moxo se woulek vati wei neil on.)
LUK 9:34 Ka moxo di luk eno laxap ti lam me sevunexe xel, me xel yaleeng en ingwei xel la eivek laxap o.
LUK 9:35 Vya ti lam eivek laxap, me neil embei, “Tine a Neung, wei a beyal o, xam a mi ngo e.”
LUK 9:36 Gyeik vya tiyon luk woy eno xel yei bei inye Yesu venaxow. De xel betiyeing venaxow di wou naleind en inyon, de lek bouk tiyon eno xel se neil wou xelti en vati wei xel yei yo.
LUK 9:37 De bouk nge, gyeik ingwei Yesu lis e xe xel betiyeing lep me loum veil lukendu, eno moux alis vex ngenongakes lam wou e.
LUK 9:38 Moux ti eivek xel ngenong on senghoing eno taxe, “Putoung a tay wou wang bei, wang gwei a neung moux, en inyon a neung tixemou ne.
LUK 9:39 Laweeng ti mi la eivek e me lutika eno mi nyayek me nex e la di puw mema vaxa lek tembuing de wong myapeleis mi qandi eivek e mya. De laweeng tiyon se mi la veil e qe mi wo nol wou e.
LUK 9:40 A tay wou wa xe xel betiyeing bei xel a tiy laweeng nol e na veil. Ekom xel se teyei.”
LUK 9:41 Yesu neil elox, “Xam xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne xam amim wongeingis ma, me xam xe woueing nalei me kwa ne se nimza, tyek a mi mendei is xam teyei lek bouk vamva me qalei xam xe maying? Qou neum me lam inye.”
LUK 9:42 Ka yak on di lam, memo yon nex e la lek tembuing me di puw mema vaxa eivek. Ekom Yesu neil laweeng nilaxes on, me wong yak on wo nimzalek de wong e lox wou ma.
LUK 9:43 Me xomaxoneing dalus on etek en Anutu xe nikanzek ngandoung on. Ka xel dalus di wou naleind en vati wei Yesu wong o, moxo neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei,
LUK 9:44 “Xam a ngo embo nimza en vati wei am bim a neil wou xam o. Tyek xel a neil Xomaxoneing Neu Moux teyei me na toung e na eivek xomaxoneing memend.”
LUK 9:45 Ekom xel se woulek qayeeng on qes. En inyon yeip xupekeing en xel, om xel se woulek, me xel yaleeng en ingwei xel embei teling e yo.
LUK 9:46 Woyom xel betiyeing pyalek ama bei eti tyek bo lei ngandoung en xel.
LUK 9:47 Yesu yei xel laleind, om qou yak ti me wong e nale wou e wes.
LUK 9:48 Woyom moxo neil wou xel betiyeing bei, “Xelti embei zenghek lek yak kane en a leing on lenghek lek ay, me tiwei lenghek lek ay eno lenghek lek tambiy tiwei wong a lam o. En tambiy tiwei lei maeing eivek xam dalus senghoing eno tiyon lei ngandoung.”
LUK 9:49 Yoan neil embei, “Teiv, xa xei tambiy ti di tiy memo en wa leim, om xa peti e en inyon se tambiy wei xey o ti.”
LUK 9:50 Ekom Yesu neil wou embei, “Xam se peti e, en xelti embei se bo nol wou xam ond inyon xam xe.”
LUK 9:51 Ka bouk lam paviy ingwei Anutu embei qou Yesu me zek me nox me na tyoung gheyapu nei, om Yesu wounalei wo nikanzek en embei na Yerusalem.
LUK 9:52 Me moxo wong nenyalesana valu qou qayeeng me la tax, xel la eivek beyeeng wei Samaria yo ti en xel embei gyeiwou lulul dalus wou e,
LUK 9:53 ekom xomaxoneing wei inyon o se lenghek lek e, en embei na Yerusalem.
LUK 9:54 Gyeik ingwei betiyeing yuw, Jems aluw Yoan, yei kwa tine, eno luw teling, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wambei uw a taxe nenyex nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei nam gya xel ne?”
LUK 9:55 Ekom Yesu pekwi ma me neil luw,
LUK 9:56 de xel la beyeeng bange.
LUK 9:57 Ka xel di la wou sakwaing, eno tambiy ti neil wou e, “Beyeeng dalus wei wambei mi na, eno tyek a mi betiwou wang.”
LUK 9:58 Yesu neil elox bei, “Naw bemeeng eeng toundei me menek lewis toundei, ekom Xomaxoneing Neu Moux beeng wei embei ni lu lek eno ma.”
LUK 9:59 Moxo neil wou moux nge, “Wa betiy ay.” Ekom moux on neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wong a lox a ev mang wole.”
LUK 9:60 Yesu neil wou e bei, “Wong eyeip, de xel wei meyeing eno venaxow di ev xel xe meyeing, dom wang na neil Anutu xe qayeeng wei tete lalei yo teyei.”
LUK 9:61 Xel nge neil embei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, tyek a mi betiy wang, ekom teyeimbei a nox a neil woyo wou mangha tang me lingyeiw bole?”
LUK 9:62 Yesu neil elox wou e bei, “Tambiy wei mi zeim taliv ekom mi yei lox demi, eno se teyeimbei bong xuk eivek Anutu xe tete lalei.”
LUK 10:1 Kalekom Tambiy Ngandoung beyal xel 72 is me wong xel mi la yuyuw, me xel la tax en e eivek beyeeng nayak me beyeeng sapa wei embim na eivek o.
LUK 10:2 Moxo neil wou xel, “Lulul wo neing ngenong woy en qoueing, ekom xel xukxe eno nuyuw. Om xam teling wou Tambiy Ngandoung wei e xe lulul yaeing on, dekakom embong xukxe na eivek e mema xuk on me na qou neing.
LUK 10:3 Xam la! A wong xam ghe la nambei sipsip lingheing eivek naw bemeeng senghoing.
LUK 10:4 Xam se qou vaxak malew, o vaxak, o vaxalambes, me xam se neil bendiyeing wou xel wei di la wou sakwaing o.
LUK 10:5 “Gyeik xam ghe na eivek xomek ti, myaxeeng eno xam a neil, ‘Lalei vevopeing e nak wou xomek tiyon.’
LUK 10:6 Wangwei tambiy wei lalei vevopeing eno ti na toumendei eivek xomek tiyon, ond tyek wa xe lalei vevopeing na mendei is e, ek wangwei na ma on tyek lalei vevopeing on noumenam wou wang.
LUK 10:7 Xam a mi mendei eivek xomek tiyon, me xam ghe gwa me na num vatiyeiw wei xel wong wou xam o, en tambiy wei mi wong xuk eno tyek na qou e xe xouveing. Dom xam seng na ghavineeng eivek xomek nge me ghe na nge.
