LUK 10:8 “Wangwei xam ghe na eivek beyeeng ti me xel a qou xam, ond xam ghe gwa vatiyeiw wei xel yeiwou me toung elam wou xam o.
LUK 10:9 Me xam ghe bong xel wei toundei eivek beyeeng on xe vanei bo nimzalek. De na neil wou xel bei, ‘Anutu xe tete lalei lam paviy xam.’
LUK 10:10 Ekom wangwei xam ghe na eivek beyeeng ti ek xel se qou xam, ond xam ghe na bale eivek xel xe sakwaing memama me na neimbei,
LUK 10:11 ‘Vegyuveeng wei xam xe beyeeng on, wei mil xa vaxami eno xa pepa veil bei e nouk lek xam me talex xam xe nilul. De xam ghe boulek neing bei, Anutu xe tete lalei lam paviy.’
LUK 10:12 A neil wou xam, lek bouk wei wongeing qayeeng eno nimaying wei embei qandi wou beyeeng tiyon eno tyek ghanaw nimaying wei Sodom o.
LUK 10:13 “Inye wo nimaying en xam Korasin! Inye wo nimaying en xam Betsaida! En wangwei lulvako wei a wong eivek xam bamim eno xelti bong eivek Taia luw Saidon, on tyek xel pekwi xow takwei nei, me na byex teimb wei talot me dev vewev lek xow.
LUK 10:14 Ekom lek bouk wei wongeing qayeeng, eno nimaying wei xam eno tyek ghanaw nimaying wei Taia luw Saidon o.
LUK 10:15 Me Kapenaom wang, tyek xel sanghoxe wang zekna tyoung? Ma, tyek wang na xonei eivek beyeeng wei meyeing o.”
LUK 10:16 Yesu neil wou xel betiyeing bei, “Xelti embei ngo xam ond ngo ay, o xelti embei pesek xam ond pesek ay, ekom xel tiwei pesek ay eno pesek tambiy tiwei wong a lam o.”
LUK 10:17 Xel 72 loumelam is xeilala me neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, xel memo betiwou xa vyami en wa leim.”
LUK 10:18 Moxo neil elox wou xel, “A xei Sandang tei me lam nambei zivip nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei.
LUK 10:19 Xam ngo, a wong nikanzek wou xam bei xam bakei lek myeiy, me boklevek, me nikanzek wei xam o tyek ghanaw nikanzek dalus wei tambiy mapetok wei mi wo vevek o, de lulti tyek se bo nol wou xam.
LUK 10:20 De xam seng bo xeimlala bei laweeng nol betiwou xam xe qayeeng, qe xam ghe bo xeimlala bei Anutu byex xam leimim nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei.”
LUK 10:21 Lek bouk tiyon eno Laweeng Vambuing wong Yesu pup en xeilala, me neil, “Mang a sanghoxe wang, wa Tambiy Ngandoung wei tyoung gheyapu luw tembuing o, en nambei wang vun lulul ti beimambei ne en xel wei lupeyei me kwa nimza yo, de wang talex wou xel wei nambei yakyak o. Ee, Mang, en inyon wang betiwou wamaxow xe woueing nalei me ghe wong ambei nyon.
LUK 10:22 “Mang wong lulul dalusateiv wou ay, xelti se woulek Neu Moux qe Ma venaxow, me xelti se woulek Ma qe Neu Moux venaxow is xel wei beyal bei tyek talex e wou xel o.”
LUK 10:23 Woyom moxo pekwi ma wou e xe xel betiyeing me neil wou xel venaxow xupekeing, “Nimzayang ena wou xel wei yei vati wei xam ghe wei yo.
LUK 10:24 En a neil wou xam bei, poropet ngenong me xel king embei gyei vati wei xam ghe wei yon, ekom xel se yei. Me xel embei ngo qayeeng tiwei xam ghe ngo yon, ekom xel se ngo.”
LUK 10:25 Woyom xel wei lupeyei ngandoung en petieing wei Mose yo ti nale ghey bei daxe Yesu. Om teling, “Putoung, tyek a bong vati me na qou deing mapieing luta luta?”
LUK 10:26 Yesu neil elox, “Xel byex vati eivek petieing? Wang pyaw ambei nya?”
LUK 10:27 Moxo lewexe bei: “‘Wa laleim devind Tambiy Ngandoung wa xe Anutu is laleim dalus me is num pieing dalus me is wa nimkanzek dalus me is wa lumpeyei dalus,’ me ‘Wa laleim devind nimpapu nambei wa laleim vind xow o.’ ”
LUK 10:28 Yesu neil elox wou e, “Wang neil e wo bombek, wang bong ambei nyon ond tyek wa mendei mapieing.”
LUK 10:29 Ekom tambiy on embei talex xow wou Yesu bei e xe deing on bombek, om teling Yesu, “A ningpapu eti?”
LUK 10:30 Woyom Yesu neil, “Moux ti la veil Yerusalem me lep me la Jeriko, gyeik la eno la eivek xel panaxeing memend. Xel kwax e xe teimb veil e me qou de leis e wo nol me e mey pesiv de xel la.
LUK 10:31 De lek bouk kayon eno lumuki ti betiwou sakwaing kayon me la xonei, de gyeik moxo yei moux tiyon di yeip wou sakwaing om ghanaw e, de tanewou sakwaing nenyawes valu me la.
LUK 10:32 Om Livai ti is ambei nyon gyeik e lam tei wou beyeeng wei moxo di yeip lek o me yei e, eno ghanaw e me tanewou sakwaing nenyawes valu me la.
LUK 10:33 Ekom Samaria ti di lam anghei ingwei moux on di yeip o, gyeik ingwei yei e eno lalei pyaxow en e.
LUK 10:34 Moxo la wou e me taw wel me wain eivek xel qatyex on me tup en banis. Woyom zeim moux on me toung lek emaxow xe dongi, me qou me la eivek xomek wei vateivek o ti me mi yeiteyei e wo nimza.
LUK 10:35 De yanyeing eno wong selewa yayuw wou xomek vateivek ma, de neil wou e bei, ‘Wa mi gweiteyei embo nimza, deka a noum on tyek a bong malew noum zeyi wa xe malew wei wang wong lek mapu yo.’
LUK 10:36 “Wang wou naleim ambei nya, lal yal on eti nipapu ingwei la eivek xel panaxeing memend on?”
LUK 10:37 Tambiy lupeyei ngandoung wei petieing o neil elox bei, “Tambiy tiwei lalei pyaxow me vind e yo.” Yesu neil wou e, “Wang na me ghe na bong ambei nyon.”
LUK 10:38 Ka Yesu is e xe xel betiyeing di la wou sakwaing, eno la eivek beyeeng ti, wei vex ti lei Marata eno tax beeng wou e.
LUK 10:39 Vexo li vex ti, lei Maria eno la dei paviy Tambiy Ngandoung vaxa me di ngo qayeeng wei e di neil o.
LUK 10:40 Ekom Marata di wounalei ngenong en xuk dalus wei di yeiwou lul yaeing o. Vexo lam wou Yesu me teling, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wa seng wou kwam en ingwei a ling vex toundei bandaing de a maxow andi wong xuk ne? Neil wou e en e nam devind ay yo.”
LUK 10:41 Ekom Tambiy Ngandoung lewexe lek bei, “Marata, Marata, wang di wou kwam ngenong me nimseik en lulul ngenong.
LUK 10:42 Ekom lulti kawei wa bei qou eno Maria beyal vati wei nimza yo, om tyek xelti se teyeimbei bouveil e.”
LUK 11:1 Bouk ti eno Yesu la di zeimema nanghei danghei ti. Gyeik ingwei zeimema woy, eno e xe xel betiyeing ti neil wou e bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, teyoxe xa en zeimeing mema, nambei Yoan mi teyoxe e xe xel betiyeing o.”
LUK 11:2 Moxo neil wou xel, “Gyeik ingwei xam ambei zeimemamim eno xam a neil ambei nye: “‘Mang, wa leim e mi mendei vambuing, wa xe tete lalei enam.
LUK 11:3 Wa mi bong xa mi lul yaeing wou xa e teyei lek bouk titi.
LUK 11:4 Me wa semaleeng sewokeing wei xa yo, en xa is ambei nyon xa mi semaleeng sewokeing wei xel sapa wong wou xa yo. Me wa seng bong xa na eivek axeing.’”
LUK 11:5 Woyom moxo neil wou xel, “Wangwei xam on ti xe gweleeng ti, me e la wou moxo eivek boukeing masenghoing me neil wou, ‘Gweleeng, wang bong belet yayal wou ay,
LUK 11:6 en nambei a xe gweleeng ti mi tupwou sakwaing me lam wou ay, ekom lul yaeing wei ambei bong wou e eno ma.’
LUK 11:7 “Woyom tambiy tiwei toundei lalei eno lewexe bei, ‘Wa seng bo pok wou ay. En xomek mya a xey woy, me yakyak di yeip is a lek zek. A se teyeimbei qandi lek me na bong lulul ti wou wang.’
LUK 11:8 A neil wou xam, moxo tyek se qandi lek me bong belet wou e en nambei inyei e xe gweleeng o, qe en ingwei toungale nikanzek wou e yo, moxo tyek qandi me bong lulul wou e teyei lek ingwei e lalei vind o.
LUK 11:9 “Om a neil wou xam: Xam teling on tyek bong wou xam, xam ghe gwimexe on tyek xam ghe gweiwou, xam ghe nyeis memamim lek qapomb on tyek natax en xam.
LUK 11:10 En xel sapa wei mi teling en vatiyeiw eno xel mi qou, xel eti yeiw wei mi yimexe eno mi yeiwou, me eti yeiw wei mi leis memend lek qapomb eno mi tax.
LUK 11:11 “Xam mayeiyeiw on, eti wangwei neum embei teling wang en woing ti, tyek wang bong myeiy wou e?
LUK 11:12 O wangwei e teling en neughalus ti, tyek wang bong boklevek wou e?
LUK 11:13 Nambei nyon xam wei sewokeing on, ekom xam ghe mi woulek lul nimza wei xam a being bong wou neumyeiw o. Yond xam ghe boulek bei xam Mamim wei toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu nei tyek bong Laweeng Vambuing wou xel wei mi teling e yo.”
LUK 11:14 Yesu tiy memo wei myatu yo veil tambiy ti. Gyeik ingwei memo la veil eno tambiy wei myatu eno luk, om moux alis vex ngenong yei me etek.
LUK 11:15 Ekom xel on valu neil embei, “En nikanzek wei Belsebul, gyovaxa wei memo, eno e mi tiy memo nangya.”
LUK 11:16 Xel valu axe moxo me neil, “Wang bong dee wei lulvako yo ti en xa boulek bei Anutu wong wang lam.”
LUK 11:17 Yesu yei woueing nalei wei xel o me neil wou xel, “Tete lalei wei eti yeiw dembuma me wong vevek wou emaxow eno tyek bo nol, me wangwei xomek ti dembuma me bong vevek wouma eno tyek detei eivek.
LUK 11:18 Wangwei Sandang xe xel dembuma me bong vevek wouma, on tyek e xe tete lalei bale nikanzek ambei nya? A neil tine en nambei xam ghe neimbei a tiy memo nangya Belsebul.
LUK 11:19 Ekom wangwei a tiy memo na veil angya Belsebul nikanzek nei, ond eti mi vind xel wei xam o me xel mi tiy memo yon la myayaing? Om xel wei xam eno tyek talex wou xam bei qayeeng wei xam on se la wo bombek.
LUK 11:20 Ekom wangwei a tiy memo nangya Anutu mema deyis, on Anutu xe tete lalei lam wou xam.
LUK 11:21 “Wangwei moux wei nikanzek o ti bale zeyi beeng is lulul wei vevek o, on tyek e xe lulul a toumendei embo nimza.
LUK 11:22 Ekom wangwei xelti nikanzek ghanaw e veil, on tyek na bo vevek wou e me bou lul vevek wei di qou nikanzek eivek o veil e, de dembu e ning lulul wou xel ba.
LUK 11:23 “Xel eti yeiw wei se mindei is ay eno mi wo vevek wou ay, me eti yeiw wei se mi qeku moux alis vex wou is ay, eno mi tiy xel lala.”
LUK 11:24 “Gyeik ingwei laweeng nilaxes ti lam myayaing veil moux ti, on tyek na ghavineeng eivek tembuing wei memiing ma veil o. Me gyei beyeeng wei embei na qou laweeng o, ek se gyeiwou ti. Woyom tyek na neil, ‘Tyek a nox me na eivek xomek wei a lam veil o.’
LUK 11:25 Gyeik ingwei loum tei eno yei xomek xel pepa e wo vako me menyex wou.
LUK 11:26 Woyom la qou laweeng amba lim yuw wei xel ghanaw e veil en kwa nol o, me xel la dei eivek xomek lalei tiyon. Om deing wei tambiy tiyon eno wo nol ghanaw ingwei tax o.”
LUK 11:27 Ka Yesu di neil ti beimambei ne, eno vex wei toundei eivek qekueing ama yon ti taxe la wou e, “Vex tiwei wou wang me wo luul wou wang eno e mi bo xeilala.”
LUK 11:28 Moxo byex e mya leit bei, “Embong ondek xey a neimbei xel wei mi ngo Anutu xe xoulek me betiwou eno na mi bo xeindlala.”
LUK 11:29 Ka moux alis vex ngenong di lam me nyouk, om Yesu neil, “Xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne nilul ayang. Xel teling en embei gyei dee wei lulvako yo, ekom tyek xel se gyei ti, qe tyek xel gyei lulvako wei Yona yo.
LUK 11:30 En Yona wong ambei dee wou Niniweyeiw, om nambei nyon is, Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek bong ambei dee wou xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne.
LUK 11:31 “De kwin wei xonei eno tyek qandi lek bouk wei wongeing qayeeng me bo qayeeng en xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne me na neil xel xe nilul teyei, en lam anghei tembuing myasepu en embei ngo Salomo xe lupeyei, me gweimbeeng ne tambiy ti ghanaw Salomo eno toundei inye.
LUK 11:32 Lek bouk wei ngoeing qayeeng eno xel wei Niniwe tyek qandi me bale me bo qayeeng en xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne me na neil xel xe nilul teyei, en xel pekwi xow gyeik ingwei Yona la neil xoulek o. Wei, gweimbeeng ne tambiy ti ghanaw Yona veil eno lam toundei inye.
LUK 11:33 “Xelti se mi byex eivek lam me toung eivek beyeeng wei embei bund xeiyaing o, o toung eivek deng lalei. Qe xel mi toung leklam vaxa gheyapu, om xel wei la lalei eno mi yei xeiyaing.
LUK 11:34 Wa mamghalus on lam wei wa neing o. Wangwei wa mamghalus luw xouing a toumendei embo nimza, on tyek wa neing dalus na pup en xeiyaing. Ekom wangwei luw xouing bo nol on tyek wa neing na pup en mapetok ngandoung.
LUK 11:35 Om wang gweiteyei, en xeiyaing wei toundei eivek wang on se bo mapetok.
LUK 11:36 Nambei nyon wangwei wa neing dalus on na pup en xeiyaing, me boukeing e ma veil wa neing danghei ti, on wa neing dalus wo xeiyaing, nambei ingwei xeiyaing wei lam mi byex lek wang o.”
LUK 11:37 Gyeik ingwei Yesu neil xoulek ma yo, Parisi ti teling bei e na gya is e, om moxo eivek la lalei me la yeip pepeeng lek zek me ya.
LUK 11:38 Ekom Parisi yei ingwei Yesu se lipek atax ekom ya, om di wounalei ngenong.
LUK 11:39 Woyom Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou e, “Xam Parisi ghe mi sekweyexe mayamya luw dipek demi, ekom xam laleimim on pup en kwa eivekeing me nilul.
LUK 11:40 Xam xomaxoneing on bandol! Beip tambiy tiwei betiy lulul on demi eno se betiy lalei is?
LUK 11:41 Ekom xam ghe bong vati wei toundei eivek dipek lalei eno wou xel wei kanyo yo, on tyek xam ghe bo vako yang wou Anutu manghalus.
LUK 11:42 “Xam Parisi ghe gwaleeng amim en nimaying, en xam ghe mi wong ti eivek xoumeeng xoing senyeing me lulul eivek xuk wei xam o, ekom xam ghe saing kwa wei bombek me kwa wei lalei vineing Anutu yo, om xam betiwou kwa ti beimambei yon de xam ghe bong luw xouing bo nimza.
LUK 11:43 “Xam Parisi ghe gwaleeng amim en nimaying, en nambei xam laleimim mi vind sia nimza wei xomek qekueing ama yo, me xam ambei xel a mi neil bendiyeing teiv wou xam eivek beyeeng wei xel mi wo vateivek lek lulul o.
LUK 11:44 “Xam ghe gwaleeng amim en nimaying, en xam ghe xok leiveeng meyeing xupekeing wei xomaxoneing qeilek en xel se woulek.”
LUK 11:45 Xel wei lupeyei ngandoung en petieing wei Mose yo ti neil wou Yesu, “Putoung, gyeik wang neil qayeeng ambei nyon, eno wang neil xa is.”
LUK 11:46 Yesu byex e vya leit bei, “Xam wei lumimpeyei ngandoung en petieing wei Mose eno xam ghe gwaleeng amim en nimaying, en nambei xam ghe mi qou lul nimaying me ghe toung lek xomaxoneing me xel mi wo pok lek qaleing, dom xam memamim ti se mi vind xel.”
LUK 11:47 “Xam ghe gwaleeng amim en nimaying, en nambei xam ghe mi ev leiveeng meyeing wei xel poropet, wei bumyeiw leis xel mey o.
LUK 11:48 Om xam ghe talex lek bei xam ghe lenghek lek vati wei bumyeiw wong o, xel leis xel poropet mey, de xam ghe kwelexe xel xe eeng wei meyeing o.
LUK 11:49 “En nambei tiyon, om eivek Anutu xe lupeyei nimza eno neil, ‘Tyek a bong xel poropet me sinaleyeiw wou xel, tyek xel nyeis xel valu mey de bo nol wou xel valu.’
LUK 11:50 Nambei nyon xam xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne tyek na qou myaveweeng lek gyand wei xel poropet, wei xel leis gyeik bouk wei Anutu toung tembuing o,
LUK 11:51 nanghei Abel gyand me e mi la Sakalias gyand, tiwei xel leis e mey eivek qeind aluw xomek vambuing senghoing o. Ee, a neil wou xam, xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne tyek na qou myaveweeng tiyon dalus.
LUK 11:52 “Xam wei lumimpeyei ngandoung en petieing wei Mose yo ghe gwaleeng amim en nimaying. En xam ghe zeim ki wei qoueing lupeyei nimza yo veil. Xam venaxow seng la eivek, de xam ghe nale zeyi xel wei embei na eivek o.”
LUK 11:53 Gyeik ingwei Yesu la veil inyon, eno xel Parisi me xel putoung wei petieing o laleind wo nol wou e, om xel nale zeyi e nangya teling wei nikanzek o.
LUK 11:54 Xel di axe e en embei bo qayeeng en e, en ingwei e neil qayeeng ti na sewok o.
LUK 12:1 Dekalekom xomaxoneing tausen ngenongakes qekuma, omva xel di qeilekama, om Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing atax bei, “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow en yis wei Parisi mi wong o, en xel on myend yuw.
LUK 12:2 Lul dalus wei xel vun eno tyek gyeip yaing wou xel, me lul dalus wei mi yeip xupekeing eno tyek nam myayaing.
LUK 12:3 Qayeeng dalus wei xam ghe neil eivek mapetok eno tyek moux alis vex a ngo wou xeiyaing. Me qayeeng dalus wei xam ghe ngoung wouma eivek xomek lalei, eno tyek xel bale lek xomek demi me taxe na wou xel sapa.”
LUK 12:4 “Xam wei axe gweleeng o, a neil wou xam bei, xam seng gwaleeng en xomaxoneing wei mi leis neing mey yo, dom tyek xel se nox me na bong lulti no.
LUK 12:5 Ekom tyek a talex wou xam en tambiy tiwei xam a mi gwaleeng en e yo. Xam waleeng en e tiwei tyek nyeis neing a mey, dekakom e xe nikanzek teyeimbei banex xam ghe na eivek nenyex wei luta yo. Ee, a neil wou xam, xam ghe gwaleeng en e.
LUK 12:6 Beip xel mi wong vateivek lek menek tetoung lim en selewa gyand nayak yuw? Ekom Anutu nalei se mi ma xel on titi.
LUK 12:7 Neing, xam lumim velus on Anutu pyaw memawou dalus. Xam seng gwaleeng, en xam ghe ghanaw tetoung ngenongakes veil.
LUK 12:8 “A neil wou xam, xelti embei neilteyei wou moux alis vex en ay, ond Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek na neil e teyei wou Anutu xe angela.
LUK 12:9 Ekom xelti embei dax a vun wou moux alis vex, ond tyek a dax e vun wou Anutu xe angela mendghalus.
LUK 12:10 Me xel sapa wei embei neil qayeeng nilul lek Xomaxoneing Neu Moux ond tyek Anutu semaleeng sewokeing wei xel o. Ekom xelti embei baluk yak lek Laweeng Vambuing on tyek Anutu se semaleeng sewokeing wei e yo veil.
LUK 12:11 “Gyeik ingwei xel a qou xam me na eivek xomek qekueing ama wou xel gyovaxa me xel wei lei ngandoung o, ond xam seng bo lalei maying bei, ‘Tyek xa bale zeyi xow ambei nya, o tyek xa neil vati?’
LUK 12:12 Lek bouk kayon eno Laweeng Vambuing tyek talex wou xam en vati wei xam ambei neil o.”
LUK 12:13 Xel wei toundei eivek qendu ngandoung on ti neil wou e, “Putoung, wa neil wou a ling en e pum lulul wei mang ghanaw eno is ay.”
LUK 12:14 Yesu neil elox, “Moux, eti beyal ay en ngoeing qayeeng bei a pum lulul eivek senghoing wou muw?”
LUK 12:15 Woyom moxo neil wou xel, “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow, en xam seng gweimam lek lulul leimalei. En mapieing wei xomaxoneing eno se toundei eivek e xe lulul ngenong on.”
LUK 12:16 Me moxo neil wou xel en qayeeng pakeing tine: “Tambiy wei lulul ana eno xe tembuing wong lulul ngenong wo neing nimza.
LUK 12:17 Moxo venaxow wounalei bei, ‘Om tyek a bo vati? A xomek ma en ingwei ambei qeku a xe lulul yaeing eivek o.’
LUK 12:18 “Woyom moxo neil embei, ‘Inye vati wei ambei bong o. Tyek a lelolexe xomek yaeing, dom na dev ingwei ngandoung ngandoung o, me nanghei inyon eno tyek a qeku a xe lulul neing dalus me a xe lulul nimzamza dalus eivek.
LUK 12:19 Me tyek a neil wou xow bei, “A teyei woy, a xe lulul nimzamza ngenong a toung e toundei teyei lek vakovek qeskes. Tyek a mendei embo nimza, me mendi bong mangha me na num lek me na bong xeinglala.” ’
LUK 12:20 “Ekom Anutu neil wou e, ‘Wa bandol! Boukeing tine tyek wa mey. De woyom tyek eti na qou lulul wei wang mi qekuwou xow on?’
LUK 12:21 “Tiyon tyek na teyei lek xel eti yeiw wei mi qeku lulul wou venaxow o de se wo lulul ana en lulul wei Anutu yo.”
LUK 12:22 Woyom Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei, “A neil wou xam, xam seng bou naleimim en mapieing wei xam o me na neimbei, ‘Tyek xey a gha vati?’ O xam seng bou naleimim en neing wei xam o me na neimbei, ‘Tyek xey a byex vati?’
LUK 12:23 Mapieing on ghanaw lulul yaeing me neing on ghanaw teimb.
LUK 12:24 Xam ghe gwei aoho xel se mi wong xuk o qeku lulul yaeing. Xel se mi ev xomek yaeing, o xomek wei qekueing lulul yaeing eivek o, qe Anutu mi vet xel. De xam xomaxoneing on ghe ghanaw menek veil.
LUK 12:25 Wangwei xam ti me di bou naleimim ngenong nei, on tyek wa tetulexe seivma nayaka wou wa xe mapieing?
LUK 12:26 Wangwei xam seng bong lulul nayak ambei nyon, ond xam ghe di wou naleimim ngenong en lulul valu betiy en va?
LUK 12:27 “Xam ghe gwei qapaing, bei xel mi tyip ambei nya. Xel se mi wong pok, o xel se mi duw teimb. Ekom a neil wou xam Salomo byex e xe teimb nimzamza, ekom se wo nimza nambei qapaing beimambei ne ti.
LUK 12:28 Wangwei Anutu mi vunekwou qapaing wei mi nale lek beyeeng nambei nyon, wei toungale gweimbeeng de yanyeing eno tyek xel banex ena eivek nenyex, om lu vamva eno Anutu se mi vunekwou xam? Xam xe wongeingis on nayaka.
LUK 12:29 Me xam seng bou naleimim ngenong bei tyek xam ghe gwa vati, me tyek xam a num vati. Om xam seng bou naleimim ngenong.
LUK 12:30 Xel amba wei tembuing tambak o mi wong me yei en xel embei qou lulul tiyon dalus, de xam mamim woulek lulul wei xam naleimim vind o.
LUK 12:31 Ekom xam a mi gwimexe Anutu xe tete lalei bole, dekakom e bong lulul on lek mapu wou xam is ambei inyon.
LUK 12:32 “Xam sipsip neuyeiw nayak on seng gwaleeng, en xam mamim lalei wo nimza en embei bong tete lalei wou xam.
LUK 12:33 Xam ghe bong vateivek lek lulul wei xam o de ghe bong malew on wou xel wei kanyo yo. Xam a qou xam xe vaxak malew wei se mi wo nol o. Xam qeku lulul nimzamza wei tyoung gheyapu wei mindei luta yo, nanghei inyei xel panaxeing se mi la paviy, de xevek se mi qateiv.
LUK 12:34 Nanghei ingwei wa xe lulul nimzamza toundei ghei nei, eno wa laleim tyek na mendei is nanghei inyon.
LUK 12:35 “Xam davex qaeing lek me ghe gweiwou xow en xuk de mendi gweiteyei xam xe lam en emdi tum,
LUK 12:36 nambei xel moux wei mi a xe xel xe teiv wei embei noum nanghei mata ngandoung wei iingama yo. En kandek gyeik ingwei embei noum nyeis mema lek qapomb, ond xel a tax qapomb daing en e.
LUK 12:37 Inyon tyek bo nimza en xel xukxe wei toundei me yeiwou xow me axe xel xe teiv gyeik ingwei e noum me gyei xel o. A neil wou xam zonghek, teiv on tyek bunekwou xow en teimb wei xuk o de na neil wou xel me xel mendei qendu ti lek lelek de bet xel.
LUK 12:38 Xel xukxe wei toundei me axe xel xe teiv wei loum yei xel yeiwou xow, o gyeik ingwei la boukeing masenghoing, o ingwei xeiyaing nexla yo ond xel bo xeindlala.
LUK 12:39 Ekom xam ghe boulek tine bei wangwei xomek ma boulek seivma wei xel panaxeing embei nam o, on tyek se bong xel dembu e beeng me na lalei.
LUK 12:40 Xam is ambei nyon xam ghe gweiwou xow boy, en Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek nam lek seivma gyeik ingwei xam seng wou naleimim bei tyek nam o.”
LUK 12:41 Petele teling, “Tambiy Ngandoung, inye wang di neil qayeeng pakeing on wou xa maxow o wou xel sapa?”
LUK 12:42 Tambiy Ngandoung lewexe me neil embei, “Xukxe eti ingwei lupeyei nimza me mi wong xuk wo nimza yo? Wei e xe teiv beyal e la tax bei e gyeiteyei e xe xukxe me na mi dembu lulul yaeing wou xel lek bouk bombek.
LUK 12:43 Wangwei xukxe tiyon di wong xuk me teiv loumelam yei e di wong o yond embo xeilala.
LUK 12:44 A neil wou xam zonghek, moxo tyek beyal xukxe tiyon bo lei ngandoung me gyeiteyei e xe lulul dalus.
LUK 12:45 Ekom xukxe tiyon se neil wou xow bei, ‘Axe teiv la dei enden de se loum,’ om di leis xel xukxe moux me xukxe vex de di ya me num me num memiing nikanzek me wo nol.
LUK 12:46 Xukxe tiyon xe teiv tyek noum lek bouk ti gyeik ingwei se di toung ma en e yo me seivma wei se woulek o. Teiv tyek qateiv xukxe tiyon bo tiptip me na toung e na is xel wei se mi wongis o.
LUK 12:47 “Xukxe wei woulek e xe teiv lalei, ekom se yeiwou xow me se wong vati wei e xe teiv neil on tyek xel nyeis e lumama.
LUK 12:48 Ekom xukxe wei se woulek e xe teiv lalei ekom wong lulti sewok eno tyek na qou myaveweeng de xel nyeis e nayaka. Xel wei qou lulul ngenong eno tyek xel bong lulul ngenong nox zeyi. Wangwei xel bong lulul ngenong wou tambiy ti on tyek xel teling bei embong lulul ngenong nox zeyi.
LUK 12:49 “A lam me na qou nenyex me na lam me na nex e la lek tembuing, de a laleing vind bei e tum.
LUK 12:50 Ambei qou lipekeing nelu ti ekom a laleing wo nimaying en a seng ghei qou.
LUK 12:51 Xam ghe wou naleimim bei a qou lalei vevopeing me na lam lek tembuing? Ma, a neil wou xam bei a lam en ambei dembu xomaxoneing.
LUK 12:52 Dom gweimbeeng ne me e mi na, eno moux alis vex lim e toumendei eivek xomek ti, ond tyek xel dembuma na yuw, yal tyek bo nol wou yuw de yuw tyek bo nol wou yal.
LUK 12:53 Tyek xel dembuma, ma tyek bo nol wou neu moux de neu moux tyek bo nol wou ma, ta tyek bo nol wou neu vex de neu vex tyek bo nol wou ta, yeing avexta tyek bo nol wou yeing vexawo de yeing vexawo tyek bo nol wou yeing avexta.”
LUK 12:54 Woyom Yesu neil wou moux alis vex ngenong on bei, “Gyeik ingwei xam ghe wei laxap ti lam tyip inya xeinei, lutika eno xam ghe neimbei ‘Luing tyek nam,’ eno luing lam.
LUK 12:55 Me gyeik ingwei laweeng vei nanghei inya xonei eno xam ghe neimbei, ‘Inye bouk wei seiv tyek bo myavanei yo,’ eno wo neing lek.
LUK 12:56 Xam wei myamim yuw o! Xam ghe mi wei mamim wou lulul wei tembuing ne me tyoung o. Nambei nya ekom xam seng wei mamim wou lulul wei di qandi lek gweimbeeng ne yo?
LUK 12:57 “Nambei nya wa seng mi wou kwam en xow me ghe woulek bei vati la wo bombek bei wang bong?
LUK 12:58 Wangwei wam di na wou sakwaing is tambiy wei embei bong qayeeng en wang wou tambiy wei mi zeim qayeeng yon wang bo nimkanzek me menyex wou qayeeng is e. Enok na qou wang me na wou tambiy wei mi zeim qayeeng de zeim qayeeng me bo wang na wou beyeiv de beyeiv na toung wang na eivek xeitueing.
LUK 12:59 A neil wou wang, wa seng teyei being na myayaing qe ka wang bo malew dalus wei xel lax wou wang o zeyi bole.”
LUK 13:1 Lek bouk kayon eno xel valu wei toundei inyon eno neil wou Yesu en ingwei Pailat leis moux wei Galili nei valu mey gyeik xel di sei xound o. Me xel gyand semaleeng is leliy gyand.
LUK 13:2 Yesu neil wou xel bei, “Xam ghe wou naleimim bei xel Galili yon wong sewokeing ngenong ghanaw Galili valu dalus omek lulti yon qandi wou xel?
LUK 13:3 Ma, a neil wou xam, xam pekwi xow, ek na ma on xam dalus tyek na mey is ambei nyon.
LUK 13:4 De nambei nya en 18 moux alis vex wei xomek vaxading pek me leis xel mey anghei Siloam o? Xam ghe wou naleimim bei xel wong sewokeing ghanaw xel valu dalus wei toundei eivek Yerusalem nei?
LUK 13:5 A neil wou xam bei, ma! Ekom wangwei xam se pekwi xow, on tyek xam dalus na mey is ambei nyon.”
LUK 13:6 Woyom Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tine, “Tambiy ti ev xax basunghek eivek e xe xuk wain, me moxo la en embei gyei xax on neing wei toukami lek o, ekom se yei neing ti,
LUK 13:7 om neil wou tambiy wei mi yeiteyei xuk wain o, ‘Eivek vakovek qes yal eno a mi lam a xei xax basunghek on neing, ekom a se xei neing ti, om vuv veil! Nambei nya e puw tembuing denzi bandaing?’
LUK 13:8 “Ekom xukxe neil e lox wou bei, ‘Teiv, wong e toukale vakovek qes tine is me a ev tembuing vivekwou me na toung lul denzi yo eivek e qes.
LUK 13:9 Wangwei e buk neing lek vakovek qes nge yus on nimza, ek na ma ond wang buv veil.’”
LUK 13:10 Lek Sabat ti eno Yesu di teyoxe xel eivek xomek qekueing ama ti,
LUK 13:11 me vex ti toundei inyon, eno laweeng ti wong e demi wo qendu teyei lek vakovek qes 18. Me vexo se teyeimbei bale bombek no.
LUK 13:12 Gyeik ingwei Yesu yei vexo eno taxe e lam de neil wou e, “Vex, wa xe vanei ma veil wang.”
LUK 13:13 Woyom moxo li mema lek e, de lutika eno vexo nale bombek me di sanghoxe Anutu.
LUK 13:14 Ekom gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama eno lalei wo vanei, en ingwei Yesu wong vanei wo nimzalek Sabat o, om neil wou xomaxoneing bei, “Inye bouk wei wongeing xuk eno limti toundei, om xam ghe nam en e gyeiwou xam lek bouk on ti, ek se lek bouk wei Sabat o.”
LUK 13:15 Tambiy Ngandoung lewexe wou e, “Xam wei myamim yuw o, xam titi seng la mi tul yis veil xam xe manghaxo o dongi lek Sabat eivek xomek leliy, me dandiy me la bei na bong memiing wou xel?
LUK 13:16 De vex tine nye Apraham neu, Sandang qo e xoun teyei lek vakovek qes 18, om se teyeimbei a tul lul tiwei qo e xoun on lek bouk wei Sabat o de ena nivax?”
LUK 13:17 Gyeik ingwei moxo neil tine, eno xel dalus wei pesek e yon ninyaleeng, de xomaxoneing wo xeindlala en lul nimza maseim dalus wei Yesu wong o.
LUK 13:18 Woyom Yesu teling bei, “Anutu xe tete lalei teyei lek vati? Tyek a neil lek vati?
LUK 13:19 Inyon nambei mastet vei, wei tambiy ti qou me ev eivek e xe xuk yaeing. Mastet on ling me wo ngandoung nambei xax teta me menek lam mi qo lewis lek memama.”
LUK 13:20 Moxo lox teling no, “Tyek a neil Anutu xe tete lalei lek vati?
LUK 13:21 Inyon nambei yis wei vex ti qou me semaleeng is palawa ngandoung wei dipekta yo, me e wong palawa dalus on vuk lek.”
LUK 13:22 Woyom Yesu di tupwou sakwaing me la Yerusalem. Om la eivek beyeeng dalus me beyeeng nayak me teyoxe xomaxoneing.
LUK 13:23 Xelti teling wou embei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, inye xomaxoneing nuyuw tyek Anutu devind xel?” Moxo neil wou xel,
LUK 13:24 “Xam ghe bong nimkanzek me ghe na eivek xomek mya wei nayak o. A neil wou xam bei, xel ngenongakes wong me yei en embei na eivek, ekom xel se teyei.
LUK 13:25 Gyeik xomek ma qandi lek me xey qapomb zeyi, tyek xam bale myayaing me ghe nyeis memamim lek qapomb me taxe bei, ‘Teiv, tax qapomb veil xa.’ “Ekom tyek na neil wou xam bei, ‘A loung en xam, xam ghe lam anghei inya?’
LUK 13:26 “Woyom tyek xam a neil wou bei, ‘Xa xa me na num is wang, me wang nale eivek xa xe sakwaing mema nayak me ghe teyoxe wou xa.’
LUK 13:27 “Ekom moxo tyek na neil enoum bei, ‘A loung en xam, xam ghe lam anghei inya. Xam la veil ay en xam on ghe wong kwa nilul!’
LUK 13:28 “Tyek xam ghe deeng me zanga newoumim bo nyiknyik nanghei inyon, gyeik ingwei xam ghe gwei Apraham, me Isaka me Yakop me xel poropet dalus eivek Anutu xe tete lalei yo, dom xam venaxow eno tyek Anutu banex xam ghe na myayaing.
LUK 13:29 Xomaxoneing tyek nam anghei ninei me xeinei me punei me xonei, me tyek nam mendei me gya mata eivek Anutu xe tete lalei.
LUK 13:30 De ngo le, xel wei dei yus eno tyek na mendei mya de xel wei dei mya eno tyek nox mendei yus.”
LUK 13:31 Lek bouk kayon eno Parisi valu lam neil wou Yesu bei, “Wang na bange veil beyeeng ne en Herot embei nyeis wa mey.”
LUK 13:32 Yesu neil elox wou xel, “Xam ghe na neil wou naw bemeeng on bei, ‘Gweimbeeng me yanyeing eno tyek a tiy memo na me na bong xomaxoneing wei vanei yo bo nimzalek. De bouk yal eno tyek a bong axe xuk dalus na ma.’
LUK 13:33 Ee gweimbeeng me yanyeing, me yanyeing nge eno tyek a na, me neing ayang inye se nimza bei poropet ti e mey anghei myayaing veil Yerusalem!
LUK 13:34 “Yerusalem, Yerusalem, wang mi leis xel poropet mey, me ghe nex xel wei Anutu wong e lam wou wang o en qakous, taxombouk eno a mi wong en ambei qeku neumyeiw dalus lekti nambei qouklex ta mi qeku neuyeiw eivek banis o. Ekom xam laleimim se mi vind.
LUK 13:35 Wei, kale tyek wa bam lelolexe me gyeip bandaing. A neil wou xam bei, tyek xam seng gwei a no, qe ka xam a neimbei, ‘Anutu bong mata wou tambiy tiwei lam lek Tambiy Ngandoung lei yo.’”
LUK 14:1 Sabat ti, eno Yesu la ya eivek xomek wei lei ngandoung wei Parisi eno ti, de xel di yei e teyei teyei.
LUK 14:2 Tambiy nivukeing ti eno toundei mya en e nanghei inyon.
LUK 14:3 Yesu teling wou xel Parisi is xel lupeyei ngandoung wei petieing o bei, “Beip inyei teyei lek bei xey a bong xel wei vanei eno bo nimzalek Sabat, o ma?”
LUK 14:4 Ekom xel toundei kanzek. Om zeim tambiy on me wong e wo nimzalek de wong e la.
LUK 14:5 Woyom moxo teling xel. “Wangwei xam on ti neum moux ti o manghaxo ti deivek leiveeng memiing lek bouk wei Sabat o, on tyek wa seng na puw enoum myayaing daing?”
LUK 14:6 De xel se neil lulti.
LUK 14:7 Gyeik Yesu yei xel wei di lam en mata eno di beyal beyeeng nimza wei mya yo, om moxo neil qayeeng pakeing tine wou xel:
LUK 14:8 “Gyeik xelti embei taxe wang en mata wei iingama yo, on wa seng na mendei lek leitata bend. Enok ambei nyon tambiy wei e xe mata yon taxe tambiy nge wei lei ghanaw wang o.
LUK 14:9 Wangwei tambiy wei taxe muw on, tyek nam a neil wou wang, ‘Wong beyeeng wei wang on wou tambiy tine,’ woyom tyek wa nim gyaleeng de ghe na mendei demiyang.
LUK 14:10 Ekom wangwei xelti taxe wang en mata ond wang na mendei demi, deka tambiy tiwei taxe wang o nam, ond tyek na neil wou wang, ‘Gweleeng wang na mendei lek beyeeng nimza wei mya nei.’ Woyom tyek wa qou leim ngandoung eivek laxousyeiw dalus mend.
LUK 14:11 En xel sapa wei mi qoxexow eno tyek Anutu beoux xel, de eti yeiw wei mi beoux xow eno Anutu tyek sanghoxe xel.”
LUK 14:12 Woyom Yesu neil wou tambiy tiwei taxe e yo bei, “Wangwei wang bong mata ti nei, on wa se taxe wa xe gweleeng, o limyeiw o nimpapu, o xel wei lulul ana wei wa bam qes o. Wangwei wang bong ambei nyon nei on tyek xel taxe wang nox me na gwa is xel no, ond inyon xel wong xouveing loum zeyi wou wang.
LUK 14:13 Ekom gyeik ingwei wa being bo mata, yon wa taxe xel kanyo, xel wei bezomb o, xel wei vaxa nol o me matekeing o.
LUK 14:14 On tyek wa mendei eivek mata lalei. Xel on tyek se bong xouveing noum wou wang no. Qe Anutu tyek bo xouveing noum wou wang gyeik ingwei xel wei bombek o embei qandi lek veil meyeing o.”
LUK 14:15 Gyeik xel wei di ya is e lek lelek on ti ngo inyon om neil wou Yesu, “Mata e gyeip wou tambiy wei tyek na gya eivek Anutu xe tete lalei yo.”
LUK 14:16 Yesu neil elox wou e bei, “Tambiy ti embei bong mata ngandoung ti me wong qayeeng la wou xel ngenongakes.
LUK 14:17 Lek bouk kawei mata eno moxo wong e xe xukxe la neil wou xel wei wong qayeeng la wou xel o. Om xukxe neil, ‘Wei, xam lam. En gweimbeeng xa menyex wou lulul dalus woy.’
LUK 14:18 “Ekom xel dalus pakei me neil embei se na. Ti myaxeeng neil embei, ‘A mouk a xouv xuk yaeing ti, om tyek a na ghei, om tyek a se nak.’
LUK 14:19 “Nge neil embei, ‘A mouk a xouv manghaxo xoumeeng om ambei na teyoxe xel me na ghei bei xel wo xuk wo nimza, om tyek a se nak.’
LUK 14:20 “Ti neil embei, ‘A mouk a ii vex om tyek a se nak.’
LUK 14:21 “Xukxe loumelam neil inyon wou e xe teiv. Woyom xomek ma yon lalei wo vanei me luk niseikeing wou e xe xukxe, ‘Wang na daing me betiwou sakwaing ngandoung me nayak eivek beyeeng tine me na qou xel kanyo, me xel wei bezomb o, me xel wei mend tekeing o, me xel wei vaxend nol o.’
LUK 14:22 “Xukxe neil embei, ‘Teiv, a wong ambei ingwei wang neil o, ekom xomek lalei valu nanghei di yeip bandaing.’
LUK 14:23 “Woyom teiv on neil wou e xe xukxe, ‘Wang na betiwou sakwaing mema mema me betiwou tete wei xuk o, me baluk nikanzek wou moux alis vex me na qou xel me ghe nam en kandek axe xomek e pup.
LUK 14:24 A neil wou xam bei, xel wei a wong qayeeng la wou xel eno ti tyek se daxe a xe mata nayak ti.’”
LUK 14:25 Xel qendu ngandoung di betiy Yesu, om pekwi ma me neil wou xel:
LUK 14:26 “Wangwei xelti embei nam wou ay, ekom se toung demi wou ma luw ta me venei is neuyeiw, me li moux me li vex, ee, de emaxow xe mapieing, on tyek se bong ambei a xe betiyeing.
LUK 14:27 Me xelti embei se qalei e xe xax pepeeng me betiy ay, eno tyek se bong ambei a xe betiyeing.
LUK 14:28 “Wangwei xel wei xam on ti embei dev xomek vaxading ti. On tyek se na mendei tax me gyei e xe malew wei embei dev xomek o teyei, bei malew teyeimbei tyek dev xomek ema?
LUK 14:29 Ek wangwei se bong ambei nyon nei, qe balax mundeeng bandaing, de se teyeimbei dev epyap, on tyek xel sapa wei yei eno bo vyend wou e,
LUK 14:30 me na neimbei, ‘Tambiy tine ev xomek atax ekom se teyeimbei dev epyap.’
LUK 14:31 “O wangwei king ti embei na bong vevek wou king nge, on tyek se mendei tax me bounalei bo nimza, beip emaxow xe xel vevek on 10,000, de king nge yon lam is 20,000, om embei gyei bei e teyei?
LUK 14:32 Ek wangwei bounalei bei se teyei, on tyek beyal xel valu na baluk is king nge yon nanghei ingwei di lam dingta yo me teling wou e en xel gyeiwou qayeeng wei embei bo lalei vevopeing o.
LUK 14:33 Nambei nyon is, wangwei xel wei xam on ti embei se toung demi wou e xe lulul dalus, on tyek se mendei nambei a xe betiyeing.
LUK 14:34 “Mileeng on nimza, ekom wangwei nenyeing na veil, on tyek wang bong enox bo nenyeing ambei nya no?
LUK 14:35 Mileeng ambei nyon eno se nimza bei xey a toung eivek tembuing wei xuk o is manghaxo xei qe wa banex ena. “Xomaxoneing ti nenya bale lek e, ond wong e ngo qayeeng tine.”
LUK 15:1 Xel wei mi qou takis o me xel wei sewokeing o xel xouing dalus la qekuma vivekwou Yesu me di ngo e xe qayeeng.
LUK 15:2 Ekom xel Parisi lis xel putoung wei petieing o neil e, “Tambiy tine mi qou xel wei sewokeing o is xeilala me mi ya is xel.”
LUK 15:3 Woyom Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tine wou xel:
LUK 15:4 “Wangwei xam on ti xe sipsip 100, ekom ti nati on tyek se bong 99 on na toumbale eivek beyeeng wei myasapa yo dom na gyimexe tiwei lati yo deka gyeiwou le?
LUK 15:5 Me gyeik ingwei yeiwou eno wo xeilala de qalei lek ghandiwek me la beyeeng.
LUK 15:6 Woyom taxe e xe xel gweleeng me nipapu wei toundei paviy e yo qekuma me neil wou xel, ‘Xam ghe bong xeimlala is ay, en a xeiwou axe sipsip wei lati yo.’
LUK 15:7 A neil wou xam eivek sakwaing ambei nyon eno xeilala ngandoung mi qandi eivek tyoung gheyapu nei en sewokeing ti embei pekwi xow o, ghanaw 99 xomaxoneing wei bombek me xuk ma en ingwei embei pekwi xow o.
LUK 15:8 “O wangwei vex ti xe malew selewa xoumeeng ekom ti nati. On tyek vexo se byex eivek lam, me pepa xomek me gyimexe embo nimza deka gyeiwou le?
LUK 15:9 Me gyeik ingwei vexo yeiwou, eno taxe e xe gweleeng me nipapu qekuma me neil embei, ‘Xam ghe bong xeimlala is ay, en a xeiwou axe selewa wei lati yo.’
LUK 15:10 Eivek sakwaing ambei nyon, eno a neil wou xam, xeilala ngandoung mi qandi wou Anutu xe xel angela mendghalus en ingwei sewokeing ti pekwi xow o.”
LUK 15:11 Yesu neil no, “Inye tambiy ti neu moux yayuw.
LUK 15:12 Nge moun neil wou ma bei, ‘Mang, wa pum wa xe lulul na yuw me ghe bong veweeng wei wambei bong eno wou ay.’ Woyom moxo pum e xe lulul la yuw wou luw.
LUK 15:13 “Se denlek qe neu nge ghavis qou e xe lulul dalusateiv me la tembuing ba wei dingta yo. Nanghei inyon eno saing ning malew lek kwa nilul wei mi wong o.
LUK 15:14 Ka e saing ning lulul la ma, eno maxep ngandoung qandi wou tembuing sapa tiyon, om maxepya moxo.
LUK 15:15 Om moxo la wong xuk wou tambiy wei tembuing qes o ti, tambiy tiyon wong e la mi yeiteyei e xe xel bok me mi vet.
LUK 15:16 Moxo bambou ma om embei gya pil ninavi wei bok di ya yon, ekom xelti se wong lulul ti wou e.
LUK 15:17 “Gyeik ingwei moxo lu yeipyaing en xow om neil, ‘Mang xe xukxe dalus di qou lulul yaeing ngenong, de nanghei inye eno ambei mey en maxep.
LUK 15:18 Tyek a nox me na wou mang me na neil wou e bei: Mang, a wo sewokeing wou Anutu me wou wang is.
LUK 15:19 Me a se nimza bei wa taxe neum lek ay, qe wang gwei ay ambei wa xe xukxe ti.’
LUK 15:20 Om moxo qandi lek me la wou ma. “Ekom gyeik ingwei nanghei di la dingta eno ma yei e me lalei pyaxow en e. Om moxo veimya me la wou neu me sei mema eivek e de sesuvexe e.
LUK 15:21 “De neu neil wou e, ‘Mang, a wo sewokeing wou Anutu me wou wang is. A se nimza bei wa taxe neum lek ay.’
LUK 15:22 “Ekom ma neil wou e xe xel xukxe bei, ‘Xam la daing! Me qou teimb ding nimza me byex lek e. De byex ring lek e mema deyis me byex vaxalambes lek e vaxa.
LUK 15:23 De xam ghe na qou manghaxo wei ling tata nei me ghe nyeis e mey. En xey a bo mata me na gha me na bong xeindlala.
LUK 15:24 En a neung ne mey ekom loum wou xey mapieing no. Moxo lati ekom xey a xeiwou e.’ Om xel wo mata me di wo xeindlala.
LUK 15:25 “Dekalekom neu touk la toundei eivek xuk, gyeik ingwei lam paviy xomek, moxo ngo yengheeng me aweing.
LUK 15:26 Om moxo taxe xukxe ti lam me teling wou e, ‘Xel di wong vati?’
LUK 15:27 Xukxe neil wou bei, ‘Lim loumelam om mam leis manghaxo lingheing wei ling tata yo ti en nambei mam qou lim loum nimza.’
LUK 15:28 “Neu touk lalei wo vanei om pesek bei se na lalei. Om ma la myayaing me lam neil qayeeng xeiles wou e.
LUK 15:29 Ekom moxo neil elox wou ma bei, ‘Wei! Vakovek qes dalus eno a mi wong xuk bandaing wou wang me a se mi pyalek wa xe qayeeng. Ekom wa seng wong meme lingheing ti wou ay en a bong xeilala is axe xel gweleeng.
LUK 15:30 Ekom gyeik wa neum tiwei la saing wa xe lulul lek vex wei mi wong kwapesiv o loum beyeeng, wang leis manghaxo wei ling tata yo wou e!’
LUK 15:31 “Ma neil wou bei, ‘A neung, wang mindei is ay taxombouk, om lulul dalus wei a ne inye wa xe.
LUK 15:32 Ekom xey ambei bo xeindlala, me laleind bo nimza en nambei lim mey, ekom toundei mapieing no, moxo lati ekom xey a xeiwou.’”
LUK 16:1 Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei, “Tambiy wei lulul ana yo ti xe lei ngandoung wei mi yeiteyei xuk o ti mindei. Om xel valu lam me byex qayeeng lek e bei, ‘Wa xe lei ngandoung wo nol wou wa xe lulul.’
LUK 16:2 Om moxo taxe e la lalei me teling wou e, ‘Vati ingwei a ngo en wa xe kwa ne? Wang na menyex wou qayeeng wei xuk wei wang o me na neil wou ay, en tyek wa seng bo lei ngandoung no.’
LUK 16:3 “De lei ngandoung neil wou xow bei, ‘Tyek a bong vati gweimbeeng? Axe teiv zeim xuk veil ay. A ninkanzek ma en ingwei ambei bong xuk wou xel nge me qandax tembuing o, de a ning yaleeng en tayeing lulul.
LUK 16:4 A woulek vati wei ambei bong o, om gyeik ingwei a noum veil xuk eno tyek xomaxoneing na qou a me na eivek bend.’
LUK 16:5 “Om moxo taxe xel wei qou lul vateivek wou e xe teiv ekom se wong zeyi yo, xel titi mi la lalei, moxo teling tambiy tiwei tax o, ‘Wang qou a xe teiv xe lulul vamva?’
LUK 16:6 “Moxo neil embei, ‘800 deng oliv wel.’ “Lei ngandoung neil wou e, ‘Wa qou wa xe qapiya me mendei daing me na byex bei 400 deng.’
LUK 16:7 “Woyom moxo teling nge wei yuw o, ‘De wang qou vamva?’ “Tambiy on neil elox bei, ‘1,000 bek wit.’ “Lei ngandoung neil wou e, ‘Wa qou wa xe qapiya me na byex bei 800 bek.’
LUK 16:8 “De teiv woulek vati wei lei ngandoung nilul on wong o, om sanghoxe e lei en wong kwa yon nambei xel wei lupeyei nimza yo. En xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne eno kwa ghanaw veil, eno xel mi woulek sakwaing mema mema wei xel mi wong wou xel venaxow xe xel o, me xel ghanaw xel wei mi betiwou kwa wei xeiyaing o.
LUK 16:9 A neil wou xam, xam ghe bo xuk en malew wei tembuing ne en na puw xel nam me ghe bong gweleeng lek xel en kandek bouk wei qoueing malew ema, on xel a qou xam me na eivek xomek wei deing nimza luta luta yo.
LUK 16:10 “Wangwei xelti mi gyeiteyei lulul wei nayak o bo nimza on tyek gyeiteyei lulul wei ngandoung o bo nimza. Ek wangwei xelti se mi gyeiteyei lulul wei nayak eno bo bombek on tyek se gyeiteyei lulul wei ngandoung eno bo bombek is.
LUK 16:11 Om wangwei xam seng gweiteyei malew wei tembuing ne bo bombek, ond tyek eti bong lulul nimza wei tyoung gheyapu yo wou xam en xam ghe gweiteyei?
LUK 16:12 Me wangwei xam seng gweiteyei xel nge xe lulul bo nimza, on eti tyek bong wamaxow xe lulul wou wang?
LUK 16:13 “Xukxe ti se mi wong xuk wou teiv yayuw. En tyek lalei bo nol wou nge de lalei devind nge. O moxo tyek betiwou nge de na toung demi wou nge. Xam seng teyei bei bo xuk wou Anutu de malew is.”
LUK 16:14 Xel Parisi laleind mi vind malew, om xel ngo qayeeng tiyon dalus eno xel wo vyend wou Yesu.
LUK 16:15 Moxo neil wou xel bei, “Xam ghe mi wong xow wo nimza wou moux alis vex mend, ekom Anutu woulek xam laleimim. Lul vatiyeiw wei moux alis vex wou naleind bei inyon nimza maseim, eno inyon nilul ayang wou Anutu manghalus.
LUK 16:16 “Qayeeng petieing me qayeeng wei xel poropet o mi yeip me elam tyip wou bouk wei Yoan o. Eivek bouk kayon eno Xoulek Nimza wei Anutu xe tete lalei eno xel di neil e la teyei lek beyeeng sapa, me xel dalusateiv di wo ninkanzek me la eivek.
LUK 16:17 Inye se wo pok en ingwei tyoung aluw tembuing malang o. Ekom qayeeng wei xel byex eivek petieing eno ti tyek se nati.
LUK 16:18 “Xelti embei qateiv iingama wei luw venei de dii vex nge, on wo kwapesiv, de wangwei moux ti dii vex wei leya qateiv e veil iingama yo, on wo kwapesiv.”
LUK 16:19 Yesu neil no bei, “Inyei tambiy wei lulul ana yo ti mi vunek en teimb teleing me mateyek nimzamza de teyei lek bouk eno mi ya lulul nimza.
LUK 16:20 Nanghei lulul ana xe tete mya eno kanyo ti eno mindei inyon. E lei Laserus, qatyex sevunexe e ninavi.
LUK 16:21 Moxo mi wounalei bei gya lulul myapapu wei mi teila eivek lelek xeinghembi wei lulul ana xe yo, de woyom xel naw la mi myeil e xe qatyex.
LUK 16:22 “De bouk la wou eivek om kanyo tiwei mi tay eno mey me xel angela lam qou e me la toung wou Apraham byek. De tambiy wei lulul ana eno mey is me xel ev.
LUK 16:23 Eivek beyeeng wei meyeing xe yo eno moxo valwou myavanei ngandoung. Lulul ana moxo yeila Apraham toundei dingta me Laserus toundei wou e byek.
LUK 16:24 Om moxo taxe la wou e bei, ‘Mang Apraham, wa laleim e pyaxow en ay! Wang bong Laserus a toung mema deyis na eivek memiing me nam a toung lek a ghas en embo nityuweing nayaka, en a toundei eivek nenyex tine eno a axe myavanei ngandoung.’
LUK 16:25 “Ekom Apraham neil elox wou e, ‘Neung, wang bounaleim en ingwei wang mindei mapieing o, bei wang mi qou lul nimzamza de Laserus mi qou lulul wei nilul o, ekom gweimbeeng ne eno lalei wo nimza nanghei inye de wang valwou myavanei.
LUK 16:26 De lulti nge is, senghoing eivek xa de xam eno Anutu toung vul manghembi ti yeip zeyi woy. En kandek xel ne ti se teyeimbei qayil me nak wou xam de xam on ti se teyeimbei qayil me ghe nam inye wou xa.’
LUK 16:27 “Woyom moxo neil, ‘Nambei nyon a tay wou wang, mang, wang bong Laserus na mang beeng.
LUK 16:28 En a lingyeiw lim, om wong Laserus la peti xel en kandek xel se nam eivek beyeeng wei myavanei ngandoung ne is.’
LUK 16:29 “Ekom Apraham neil elox, ‘Mose xe petieing me xel poropet xe qayeeng eno di yeip wou xel om xel a mi ngo.’
LUK 16:30 “Lulul ana neil, ‘Ma, mang Apraham, ekom wangwei xel meyeing ti qandi lek me na wou xel on tyek xel bongis me pekwi xow.’
LUK 16:31 “Apraham neil wou embei, ‘Wangwei xel embei se ngo wou Mose me xel poropet, on tyek xel se teyei bei bongis tambiy wei qandi lek veil meyeing o.’”
LUK 17:1 Yesu neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei: “Lul leimalei wei embei bong xomaxoneing detei en sewokeing eno tyek qandi. Ekom tambiy tiwei wong etyip eno e gyaleeng.
LUK 17:2 Wangwei tambiy ti embei bong yakyak on ti detei en sewokeing, on inyon nimza bei xel banex e na eivek mamileeng is qakous ngandoung wei xel tup e vivekwou e kwa yo en e se bong kwa yon. Anutu tyek bong myaveweeng ngandoung ghanaw veil en ingwei xel wong o.
LUK 17:3 Om xam ghe gweiteyei xow. “Wangwei lim bong sewokeing ond wang na pepyawexe e, ek wangwei e pekwi xow ond wa semaleeng sewokeing wei e yo.
LUK 17:4 De wangwei e bong sewokeing lim yuw wou wang lek bouk tixemou, de lu lim yuw eno loumelam wou wang me neil embei, ‘A pekwi xow,’ ond wa semaleeng sewokeing wei e yo.”
LUK 17:5 Xel sinale neil wou Tambiy Ngandoung bei, “Wa tetulexe xa xe wongeingis ena bo ngandoung!”
LUK 17:6 Moxo neil elox bei, “Wangwei wongeingis wei xam eno nayaka nambei xax mastet vei on tyek wa neil wou xax ngandoung tine bei wa puw xow me ghe na dev xow eivek mamileeng on tyek betiwou wa xe qayeeng.”
LUK 17:7 “Wangwei xam on ti xe xukxe la qandax tembuing o la yeiteyei sipsip, gyeik ingwei xukxe loumelam, on tyek wa se teyei bei neil wou bei, ‘Lam dei me wa.’
LUK 17:8 Ekom tyek wa neil wou wa xe xukxe bei, ‘Wang gweiwou lul yaeing wou ay atax me ghe gweiwou xow me na duw lul yaeing en a gha me na num lek boy, dekakom wang gwa me na num lek.’
LUK 17:9 De tyek e neil dange wou xukxe en ingwei wo xuk ambei ingwei neil wou e yo? Ma.
LUK 17:10 Om xam is ambei nyon, gyeik ingwei xam ghe bong xuk dalus wei Anutu neil wou xam bei xam ghe bong o na ma, ond xam a neimbei, ‘Xa xukxe ne se nimza teyei lek. Xuk wei xa mi wong ne inye xuk wei xa mi yo.’”
LUK 17:11 Yesu betiwou sakwaing wei la Yerusalem o, om la wou sakwaing wei di yeip senghoing eivek distrik Samaria me Galili yo.
LUK 17:12 Ka moxo la eivek beyeeng ti eno moux xoumeeng wei vanei lepa wong xel eno la tyip wou e nanghei inyon, xel nale dingta,
LUK 17:13 me taxe xoulekeing bei, “Yesu! Teiv! Pyanaleim en xa!”
LUK 17:14 Gyeik ingwei Yesu yei xel, eno neil wou xel, “Xam la talex xow wou xel lumuki.” Ka xel di la eno xel ninavi wo nimzalek.
LUK 17:15 Gyeik xel on ti yei ingwei wo nimzalek, om loumelam wou Yesu, moxo di taxe me sanghoxe Anutu.
LUK 17:16 Moxo ev vaxakatu eivek me ma la eivek tembuing wou Yesu vaxa me wo dange wou e, inyon Samaria ti.
LUK 17:17 Yesu teling, “Inye xel xoumeeng dalus se wo nimzalek? Xel limvey la nya?
LUK 17:18 Xelti se pekwi ma me loumelam sanghoxe Anutu, qe tambiy ba tine venaxow.”
LUK 17:19 Woyom Yesu neil wou, “Qandi lek me la. Wa xe wongeingis wong wang wo nimzalek.”
LUK 17:20 Xel Parisi valu teling wou Yesu bei, “Gyeik inya Anutu xe tete lalei nam?” Yesu neil elox wou xel, “Anutu xe tete lalei embei nam, on tyek lulti se nam mendei nambei dee me xam ghe gwei lek mamim.
LUK 17:21 O tyek xomaxoneing se neimbei, ‘Toundei inye,’ o ‘Toundei inyei,’ en nambei Anutu xe tete lalei toundei eivek xam.”
LUK 17:22 Woyom moxo neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei, “Bouk di lam gyeik ingwei xam ghe wou naleimim being gwei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux xe bouk ti. Ekom tyek xam seng gwei.
LUK 17:23 Xomaxoneing tyek na neil wou xam bei, ‘Moxo toundei inyei’ o ‘Moxo toundei inye!’ On xam se daveimyamim me ghe na betiy xel.
LUK 17:24 En bouk wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei noum eno tyek nambei zivip mi nex mema nanghei tyoung myasepu valu me ela valu yo.
LUK 17:25 Ekom myaxeeng eno tyek na qou myavanei ngenong, me xomaxoneing wei bouk tine eno tyek pesek e.
LUK 17:26 “Kwa wei xel wong gyeik bouk wei Noaka yo, on nambei nyon tyek xel nox bong kwa kayon lek bouk wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei noum o.
LUK 17:27 Xomaxoneing di ya me num lek me di iima, me neuyeiw di iima lox me loum deka ela tyip wou bouk wei Noaka la eivek sip, woyom memiing butek me lam leis xel dalus.
LUK 17:28 “Xel wong kwa kayon nambei nyon eivek bouk wei Lot o, xomaxoneing di ya me num lek, me di xouv lulul, me di wong vateivek, xel di ev lulul vei eivek xuk, me xel di ev xomek.
LUK 17:29 Ekom ka bouk wei Lot la veil Sodom, nenyex is qakous wei wo gyand en nenyex tum lek o tei nambei luing nanghei tyoung nei me ya moux alis vex dalus.
LUK 17:30 “Tyek xel bong kwa nambei nyon lek bouk wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei noum yanyateiv o.
LUK 17:31 Lek bouk kayon, xelti embei toumendei lek xomek demi qetyei de e xe lulul nimza na toumendei eivek xomek lalei on tyek se douk me nox a qou lulul. De nambei nyon is, xelti embei toumendei eivek xuk on tyek se nox a qou e xe lulul ti.
LUK 17:32 Xam ghe bou naleimim en Lot venei!
LUK 17:33 Xelti embei zeimaxoun mapieing wei e yo, on tyek na saing e xe mapieing, ek xelti embei saing mapieing wei e yo, on tyek na zeimaxoun e xe mapieing.
LUK 17:34 A neil wou xam, lek boukeing tiyon eno tambiy yayuw di yeip lek zek tixemou, tyek Anutu na qou nge de nge na toumendei.
LUK 17:35 Vex yayuw di louk wit neing bei embo palawa wei belet o. Tyek Anutu na qou nge de nge na toumendei.”
LUK 17:37 Xel betiyeing teling, “Tambiy Ngandoung, lul on tyek qandi nanghei inya?” Moxo neil elox, “Lek beyeeng wei meyeing neing mi yeip lek o, inyon tyek xel menek tuw qeku nak inyon.”
LUK 18:1 Woyom Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tine wou e xe xel betiyeing, bei e talex wou xel en xel a mi zeimemend taxombouk, de xel se bo nimaing.
LUK 18:2 Moxo neil embei, “Eivek beyeeng ti eno tambiy wei mi zeim qayeeng o ti mindei, wei se mi yaleeng en Anutu, me se mi wounalei en moux alis vex.
LUK 18:3 De vexeiv ti mindei eivek beyeeng tiyon. Om mi qatoloum wou tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng o. Vexo neil, ‘Tambiy ti embei bo vevek wou ay. Om wa menyex wou qayeeng eivek uw senghoing.’
LUK 18:4 “Myaxeeng eno tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng eno se vind vexo. Dekakom moxo wounalei bei, ‘A se xaleeng en Anutu me a se wou kwang en xomaxoneing ti.
LUK 18:5 Ekom a xei vexeiv tiyon mi wo maying wou ay me qou e xe nimaying me lam wou ay, om a menyex wou qayeeng enok bo nimbayaing wou ay.’”
LUK 18:6 De Tambiy Ngandoung neil embei, “Xam ngo qayeeng wei tambiy nilul wei mi zeim qayeeng eno neil o.
LUK 18:7 De tyek Anutu menyex wou xomaxoneing wei e beyal o, me xel mi eng wou e bendiyeing aluw boukeing o, tyek na mi daxe de se devind xel daing?
LUK 18:8 A neil wou xam, tyek gyei me menyex wou xel daing. Ekom gyeik bouk wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei noum eno tyek gyei bei moux alis vex wei tembuing ne di wongis e?”
LUK 18:9 Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tine en xel valu wei mi wou naleind bei xel venaxow bombek de xel valu se nimza nambei xel.
LUK 18:10 “Tambiy yayuw lek me la eivek xomek vambuing en embei na zeimemend, nge Parisi ti de nge xel wei mi qou takis o.
LUK 18:11 Parisi tiyon nale me zeimema en xow: ‘O Anutu, a wong dange lak wou wang, en a se nambei moux amba, xel mi panax me mi wo nilul me mi wong kwapesiv, de a se nambei tambiy tiwei mi qou takis ne.
LUK 18:12 Bouk yayuw eivek sounda sapa eno a mi vambu yaeing, me na mi wong ti eivek xoumeeng en lul dalus wei a mi qou eno wou wang.’
LUK 18:13 “Ekom tambiy wei mi qou takis eno qandi lek me nale kwanding de se yeima la tyoung gheyapu nei, qe qatu bambou me neil embei, ‘Anutu, a mi wong sewokeing om wa laleim e pyaxow en ay.’
LUK 18:14 “A neil wou xam en tambiy tiwei mi qou takis on bei, gyeik lox beeng nei eno Anutu yei bei e bombek wou e manghalus. Dom Parisi eno ma. En xelti embei sanghoxe xow eno Anutu tyek beoux e, de xelti embei beoux xow eno Anutu tyek sanghoxe e.”
LUK 18:15 Xomaxoneing valu qou yakyak me la wou Yesu, xel embei e ni mema lek xel. Ekom gyeik ingwei xel betiyeing yei, eno xel neil xel.
LUK 18:16 Ekom Yesu taxe yakyak lam wou e de neil embei, “Xam ghe bong yakyak nam wou ay, xam se bale zeyi xel, en Anutu xe tete lalei nei eno xel wei xok ambei yakyak eno xel xe.
LUK 18:17 A neil wou xam zonghek, xelti embei se qou Anutu xe tete lalei nambei yakyak ne, eno tyek se na eivek.”
LUK 18:18 Gyovaxa ti teling wou Yesu bei, “Putoung nimza, tyek a bong vati de na qou deing mapieing luta luta?”
LUK 18:19 Yesu lewexe, “Nambei nya wang neimbei a nimza? Xelti se nimza qe Anutu venaxow.
LUK 18:20 Wang woulek qayeeng petieing: ‘Wa seng bo kwapesiv is xel nge, wa seng nyeis xel nge na mey, wa se panax, wa seng bong qayeeng tyonyeing en xel nge. Wa mi gwevek mam aluw tam xeinghembi.’”
LUK 18:21 Gyovaxa neil, “Gyeik a yak me elam tyip gweimbeeng ne, eno a mi betiwou petieing on dalus.”
LUK 18:22 Gyeik ingwei Yesu ngo inyon, eno neil wou e bei, “Wang ghei ma en lulti. Wang bo vateivek lek lulul dalus wei wang o, de ghe bong malew on wou xel kanyo, on tyek wa qou lulul nimzamza eivek tyoung gheyapu nei, woyom wang nam betiwou ay.”
LUK 18:23 Gyeik ingwei moxo ngo inyon eno lalei wo maying, en nambei tambiy yon xe lulul ngenong.
LUK 18:24 Yesu yei e me neil embei, “Inye wo pok en xel wei lulul ana embei na eivek Anutu xe tete lalei yo!
LUK 18:25 Wangwei kamel embei na eivek ying manghalus wei duweing lulul o ond tyek bo pok wou e? Ekom xel wei lulul ana embei na eivek Anutu xe tete lalei eno tyek bo pok ngandoung.”
LUK 18:26 Xel wei ngo inyon eno teling bei, “Wangwei nambei nyon nei ond tyek eti na mendei mapieing luta luta?”
LUK 18:27 Yesu neil elox bei, “Lulul wei xomaxoneing se teyeimbei bong eno Anutu teyeimbei tyek bong.”
LUK 18:28 Petele neil wou embei, “Wei, xa ghanaw xa xe lulul dalus de betiy wang.”
LUK 18:29 Yesu neil wou xel bei, “A neil wou xam zonghek, xelti embei saing beeng o venei o liyeiw o mamata o neuyeiw en Anutu xe tete lalei
LUK 18:30 on tyek xel a qou lul ngenong lumama lek bouk tine, me bouk wei embei nam eno tyek xel a qou deing mapieing luta luta.”
LUK 18:31 Yesu qou xel xoumeeng yuw me la nale beyaleing me neil wou xel. “Xey ambei zek me nana Yerusalem, me lulul dalus wei xel poropet byex lek Xomaxoneing Neu Moux eno tyek bo neing lek.
LUK 18:32 Tyek xel toung moxo na eivek xel amba memend. Tyek xel baluk seloukeing wou e, me bo nol wou e, me pesuv myenlouk lek e,
LUK 18:33 me sesa e, de nyeis e mey. Ekom lek bouk yal eno tyek qandi lek no.”
LUK 18:34 Xel betiyeing se woulek qayeeng tine qes en qes xupek en xel, me xel se woulek vati wei di neil o.
LUK 18:35 Ka Yesu la paviy beyeeng Jeriko, eno tambiy wei matekeing o ti mindei wou sakwaing nenyawes me mi tay lulul me malew wou xel.
LUK 18:36 Gyeik ingwei moxo ngo moux alis vex ngenongakes di lam, om teling wou xel bei, “Inyei xel di wo vati?”
LUK 18:37 Xel neil wou embei, “Yesu wei Nasaret eno di lamela.”
LUK 18:38 Matekeing moxo taxe bei, “Yesu, Dawit Neu Moux, wa laleim e pyaxow en ay.”
LUK 18:39 Xel wei di lam atax eno neil e me neil embei e mendei kanzek, ekom moxo taxe xoulekeing, “Dawit Neu moux, wa laleim e pyaxow en ay.”
LUK 18:40 Yesu nale me neil nikanzek bei xel a qou moux tiyon me na wou e. Gyeik ingwei moxo la paviy, Yesu teling e,
LUK 18:41 “Wambei am bong vati wou wang?” Moxo neil embei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, ambei gheina yo.”
LUK 18:42 Yesu neil wou moxo bei, “Wa mam e gyeina en wa xe wongeingis wong wang wo nimzalek.”
LUK 18:43 Lutika eno moxo ma yeila de betiwou Yesu, me di sanghoxe Anutu. Gyeik ingwei xomaxoneing dalus yei inyon eno xel sanghoxe Anutu.
LUK 19:1 Yesu la eivek Jeriko me di la.
LUK 19:2 Tambiy ti mindei inyon e lei Sakius. Moxo lei ngandoung wei xel wei mi qou takis o, me tambiy on lulul ana.
LUK 19:3 Moxo embei gyei bei Yesu yon nambei nya. Ekom moxo sepika om se teyeimbei gyei, en inye moux alis vex ngenongakes.
LUK 19:4 Om moxo veimya me la tax wou sakwaing wei Yesu embei na nox me lek xax basounghek ti en embei gyei e.
LUK 19:5 Ka Yesu la paviy xax qes eno veilma lek me neil embei, “Sakius, ouk me lam daing, en ambei na mendei eivek wa bam gweimbeeng.”
LUK 19:6 Om moxo ouk me lam daing me qou e is xeilala.
LUK 19:7 Xomaxoneing dalus wei yei inyon eno xel ngoung wouma me neil embei, “Moxo la dei is xel wei sewokeing o.”
LUK 19:8 Kalekom Sakius nale me neil wou Tambiy Ngandoung, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wei! Tyek a dembu lul wei ay eno na yuw de na bong veweeng wou xel kanyo. De wangwei a qou xelti xe lulti en tyonyeing on tyek a bong malew nox zeyi wou e lu vey.”
LUK 19:9 Yesu neil wou e bei, “Gweimbeeng Anutu vind xel wei xomek tine yo veil nilul, en nambei tambiy tine inye Apraham neu is.
LUK 19:10 En Xomaxoneing Neu Moux lam en embei gyimexe me devind moux alis vex wei lati yo noumenam.”
LUK 19:11 Ka xomaxoneing ngo tiyon, Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tine no is wou xel, en nambei la paviy Yerusalem, om xel wou naleind bei Anutu xe tete lalei tyek nam atyip daing.
LUK 19:12 Moxo neil embei, “Tambiy wei lei ngandoung eno neu ti la tembuing wei dingta yo, en embei xel balax embo king de woyom e noumenam beyeeng.
LUK 19:13 Om moxo taxe e xe xukxe xoumeeng me wong malew ghol titi wou xel, de neil embei, ‘Xam mendi bong vateivek lek malew on deka a noum le.’
LUK 19:14 “Ekom xel wei e beeng qes eno laleind wo nol wou e, me wong xel wei xel beyal o valu betiy e me la neil embei, ‘Xa bei tambiy tiyon e se bong xa xe king.’
LUK 19:15 “Ekom e wo king, me loumelam beyeeng. Woyom moxo wo qayeeng la wou xel xukxe wei wong malew wou xel o, en embei gyei bei xel titi wong xuk lek me qou malew vamva is lek mapu.
LUK 19:16 “Tambiy tiwei myaxeeng o lam me neil, ‘Teiv, a wong xuk lek wa xe malew ghol tiwei yo me na qou malew ghol xoumeeng is.’
LUK 19:17 “De moxo neil wou bei, ‘Wang on a xe xukxe nimza me wang wo xuk nimza. Wang weiteyei lul wei nayak o, om tyek wang gweiteyei beyeeng ngandoung xoumeeng.’
LUK 19:18 “Xukxe nge wei yayuw eno lam neil embei, ‘Teiv, a wong xuk lek wa xe malew ghol tiwei yo me na qou malew ghol lim is.’
LUK 19:19 “E xe teiv lewexe, ‘Nimza, wang gweiteyei beyeeng ngandoung lim.’
LUK 19:20 “Woyom xukxe nge lam, me neil embei, ‘Teiv, wa xe malew ghol tiyo inye, a toung eivek qaeing myasepu ti.
LUK 19:21 En a xaleeng en wang, en wa tambiy wei niseikeing o, wang mi qou vati wei wa seng toung o, me wang mi qou lul yaeing wei wa seng ev o.’
LUK 19:22 “Woyom king neil wou e xe xukxe, ‘Wa xukxe nilul. Tyek a bong qayeeng en wang en wamaxow xe qayeeng. Wang wei bei a tambiy wei niseikeing, a mi qou vati wei a se toung me na qou lulul yaeing wei a se ev o?
LUK 19:23 Nambei nya wa seng toung axe malew eivek xomek malew, en kandek gyeik ingwei a noum ond a qou is malew wei xel toung lek mapu yo?’
LUK 19:24 “Woyom king neil wou xel wei toukale paviy e yo, ‘Xam qou malew ghol tiyon veil e me wong wou tambiy wei e xe malew ghol xoumeeng o.’
LUK 19:25 “Xel neil wou e, ‘Teiv, xukxe yon qou malew ghol xoumeeng woy!’
LUK 19:26 “Moxo neil elox, ‘A neil wou xam, xel eti yeiw wei qou lulul, eno tyek am bong valu is wou xel, ekom wangwei xelti se qou lulul ti, on lul nayak kawei toundei wou e yon, tyek am bouveil e.
LUK 19:27 Ekom xel vevek amba wei ay yo embei a se bong king wei xel, eno xam a qou xel me ghe nam inye me ghe nyeis xel amey wou a mang.’”
LUK 19:28 Ka Yesu neil qayeeng on woy, om betiwou sakwaing me lek me la Yerusalem.
LUK 19:29 Ka Yesu la paviy Betpage me Betani lek qetyei wei xel mi neil embei lukendu Oliv, eno moxo wong e xe xel betiyeing yayuw la me neil wou luw,
LUK 19:30 “Muw ghe na eivek beyeeng tinei, wangwei muw ghe na, tyek muw ghe gwei dongi lingheing ti xel qoxoun nanghei inyon, xelti seng ghei dei lek. Muw a tul me na qou me ghe nam inye.
LUK 19:31 Wangwei xelti teling muw, ‘Muw ghe tul dongi yon enva?’ On muw a neil wou e bei, ‘Tambiy Ngandoung embei bong xuk en.’”
LUK 19:32 Betiyeing yuw wei wong luw la eno luw yei lul nambei ingwei e neil wou luw o.
LUK 19:33 Ka luw di tul yis veil dongi eno mayeiw teling wou luw bei, “Muw ghe tul dongi ne enva?”
LUK 19:34 Luw neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung embei bong xuk en.”
LUK 19:35 Om luw qou dongi me la wou Yesu. Xel toung xel xe teimb lek dongi demi de toung Yesu la dei lek.
LUK 19:36 Ka e di la, eno xomaxoneing liw xel xe teimb me teteyexe wou sakwaing.
LUK 19:37 Gyeik ingwei moxo la paviy beyeeng wei sakwaing lep me la lukendu Oliv nei, eno e xe xel betiyeing ngenongakes di wong xeindlala me sanghoxe Anutu me wo denduing en lulvako wei xel yei woy o. Xel neil,
LUK 19:38 “Mata ena wou king tiwei lam lek Tambiy Ngandoung lei yo!” “Lalei vevopeing e gyeip senghoing eivek Anutu wei tyoung gheyapu nei me xey de lei laeing ena wou Anutu.”
LUK 19:39 De xel Parisi valu toundei eivek xel ngenong on lalei, xel neil wou Yesu bei, “Putoung, wa neil wa xe xel betiyeing on, en xel se neil qayeeng on.”
LUK 19:40 Yesu neil wou xel, “A neil wou xam! Wangwei xel mendei kanzek, on tyek xel qakous ne taxe xoulekeing.”
LUK 19:41 Ka Yesu la paviy Yerusalem me yei beyeeng ngandoung on, eno moxo eng en.
LUK 19:42 Me neil embei, “Wangwei wamaxow ghe boulek bouk tine, en sakwaing wei lalei vevopeing lam wou wang ne, ekom gweimbeeng xupek en wa mam.
LUK 19:43 Bouk ti tyek nam, gyeik wa xe xel vevek nam a poux tembuing apup me bivekwou tete wei wang on. Me tyek xel bale ebivekwou danghei danghei nei zeyi wang.
LUK 19:44 Tyek xel lelolexe wang na lek tembuing, wang is neumyeiw wei toundei eivek wang on. Tyek xel se bong qakous nge na toumendei lek nge mapu, en nambei wa seng woulek bouk wei Anutu lam en embei devind wang o.”
LUK 19:45 Woyom Yesu la eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o me tiy xel wei di wong vateivek lek lulul o.
LUK 19:46 Moxo neil wou xel, “Xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, ‘Axe xomek ne, inye xomek wei zeimeing mema eivek o.’ Ekom xam ghe wong e wong ambei ‘beyeeng xupekeing wei xel panaxeing o.’”
LUK 19:47 Taxombouk eno Yesu mi teyoxe xel eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o. Ekom xel lumuki leitata yo, me putoung wei petieing o me gyovaxa wei xomaxoneing o, di wong me yei en xel embei nyeis e mey.
LUK 19:48 Ekom xel se yeiwou sakwaing ti, en nambei xomaxoneing wei toundei me ngo e xe qayeeng eno wo nikanzek.
LUK 20:1 Bouk ti eno Yesu di teyoxe xomaxoneing eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o me neil Xoulek Nimza wou xel, de xel lumuki leitata me putoung wei petieing o dalus is teivateiv lam tyip wou e.
LUK 20:2 Xel neil wou e bei, “Neil wou xa, wang qou lei ngandoung me nikanzek tiyon nanghei inya me ghe di wong lulul tiyon angya? Eti wong lei ngandoung on wou wang?”
LUK 20:3 Moxo neil elox wou xel, “Ay is ambei nyon ambei teling xam, xam neil wou ay,
LUK 20:4 gyeik ingwei Yoan lipek moux alis vex, inyon lul wei Anutu eivek tyoung gheyapu yo, o lul wei xomaxoneing o?”
LUK 20:5 Xel di luk wouma eivek xel venaxow senghoing me neil embei, “Wangwei xey a neimbei lul on Anutu yo, on tyek teling xey, ‘Nambei nya xam seng wongis e?’
LUK 20:6 Ekom wangwei xey a neimbei, ‘Lul on xomaxoneing o,’ on tyek moux dalus banex xey en qakous, en xel wongis bei Yoan on poropet.”
LUK 20:7 Om xel lewexe, “Xa se woulek bei inyon lam anghei inya.”
LUK 20:8 Yesu neil wou xel, “Ay is, tyek a se neil wou xam en lei ngandoung tiwei andi wong lulti beimambei nangya ne.”
LUK 20:9 Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tine wou xomaxoneing bei, “Tambiy ti wong e xe xuk wain ti, dom wou eivek xel xukana valu memend bei xel a mi bo xuk vateivek lek. De e venaxow la dei enden lek beyeeng nge.
LUK 20:10 Lek bouk wei uleing wain eno moxo wong xukxe ti la wou xel wei di yeiteyei wain o, en embei xel dul wain on neing valu wou e. Ekom xel wei di yeiteyei wain eno leis e me wong e lox mema bandaing.
LUK 20:11 Moxo wong xukxe nge lox me la no, ekom xel leis e is no me wo niyalenyeing wou e de wong e lox mema bandaing.
LUK 20:12 Moxo wong xukxe tiwei yal o lox me la no. Ekom xel leis e wo nol me nex e la myayaing.
LUK 20:13 “Woyom xuk wain ma neil, ‘Tyek am bong ambei nya? Tyek am bong a neung moux tiwei a laleing vind eno na, bei xel se gwevek e xe qayeeng xeinghembi.’
LUK 20:14 “Ekom gyeik xel xukana yei e neu di lam, eno xel neil wouma bei, ‘Neu moux tine tyek na qou xuk wain. Xey a leis e mey, de xe venaxow a qou xe xe xuk wain ne.’
LUK 20:15 Om xel nex moxo la myayaing veil xuk wain de leis e mey. “Om tyek xuk wain ma yon bong vati wou xel?
LUK 20:16 Moxo tyek nam nyeis xel wei di yeiteyei xuk wain on na mey, de bong xuk wain on wou xel amba.” Gyeik xomaxoneing ngo qayeeng tiyon eno xel neil embei, “Lul ambei nyon eno e se nox qandi no.”
LUK 20:17 Yesu yei xel kanzek, de teling bei, “Qayeeng tiwei xel byex ne qes ambei nya: “‘Qakous mundeeng ti myaxeeng wei xel kamunda pesek, eno wong ambei qakous tiwei nale me mi byexaxoun xomek o’?
LUK 20:18 Xel dalus wei oing me teila lek qakous on tyek bo tiptip. Ekom wangwei qakous tiyon detei lek xelti on tyek bo myapapu.”
LUK 20:19 Xel putoung wei petieing o me xel lumuki leitata yo di yimexe sakwaing en xel embei zeimaxoun e lutika, en xel woulek bei neil qayeeng pakeing tiyon lek xel. Ekom xel yaleeng en xomaxoneing.
LUK 20:20 Xel lumuki leitata me putoung wei petieing o mi yei Yesu teyei teyei, bei bong xel valu na xupekeing me gyei e teyei. Me tyoing lek bei xel bombek bei na ngo e xe qayeeng wei embei neil o, en kandek xel bong e na wou lei ngandoung wei seyap o.
LUK 20:21 Om xel teling wou embei, “Putoung, xa woulek qayeeng wei wang mi neil me ghe mi teyoxe eno mi la bombek, me wang mi neil qayeeng la teyeima wou moux alis vex wei lei laeing o me lei maeing o. Me qayeeng zonghek eno wang mi teyoxe xel en Anutu xe kwa.
LUK 20:22 Woyom wang wou naleim ambei nya, beip inye teyeimbei xey a toung takis wou Sisa o xe se toung?”
LUK 20:23 Ekom Yesu woulek bei xel tyoxe e, om neil embei,
LUK 20:24 “Talex selewa ti wou ay. Inye eti tenu me lei di yeip lek?” Xel neil elox bei, “Sisa.”
LUK 20:25 Me moxo neil wou xel, “Lul wei Sisa, eno xam ghe bong wou Sisa. De lul wei Anutu, eno xam ghe bong wou Anutu.”
LUK 20:26 Om xel se teyeimbei tyoxe e en qayeeng wei e neil o ti eivek moux alis vex mendghalus, om xel etek en qayeeng wei neil elox wou xel o, om xel dei kanzek.
LUK 20:27 Xel Sadyusi valu wei mi neil embei xel wei mey, eno tyek se qandi lek. Xel lam wou Yesu is telinyeing ti.
LUK 20:28 Xel neil embei, “Putoung, Mose byex qayeeng ti nambei nye wou xey, wangwei tambiy ti dii vex ti ekom mey veil venei de neu ma, ond li e dii vexeiv me bong li wei mey eno neu en mendi zeim li lei xoun.
LUK 20:29 Om xel wei lindama eno lim yuw. Tiwei myaxeeng eno ii vex ti ekom mey de neu ma.
LUK 20:30 Woyom li nge wei yuw eno ii vexeiv on.
LUK 20:31 De li tiwei yal eno ii vexeiv. Eivek sakwaing ambei nyon eno xel lim yuw wei lindama eno ii vex tiyon me neuyeiw ma, de xel mey.
LUK 20:32 Dekakom vex tiyon mey loxyus is.
LUK 20:33 Woyom gyeik bouk loxyus wei xel meyeing embei qandi lek, eno eti venei vex tiyon? En moux lim yuw eno ii vex tixemou yon.”
LUK 20:34 Yesu neil elox wou xel, “Xomaxoneing wei gweimbeeng ne mi iima me wong vex lox me loum wouma.
LUK 20:35 Ekom eivek bouk loxyus eno moux alis vex wei Anutu neil embei xel teyei lek en ingwei xel embei qandi lek veil meyeing me mendei mapieing, eno tyek se diima o bong xel nox me noum wouma.
LUK 20:36 Me tyek xel se nox me na mey no, en xel on teyei lek xel angela. Me xel on Anutu neuyeiw, en nambei xel qandi lek veil meyeing.
LUK 20:37 Ekom Mose talex wou xey bei xel wei mey eno tyek qandi lek veil meyeing, en pavulek wei byex en ingwei nenyex tum lek xax nayaka yo, en taxe Tambiy Ngandoung Anutu wei Apraham o me Anutu wei Isaka yo me Anutu wei Yakop o.
LUK 20:38 Moxo se Anutu wei xel meyeing, qe e Anutu wei xel wei mapieing. En eivek Anutu manghalus eno moux alis vex dalus toundei mapieing en e.”
LUK 20:39 Xel putoung wei petieing o valu ngo qayeeng wei Yesu neil o, om xel neil wou embei, “Putoung, wa xe qayeeng on nimza.”
LUK 20:40 De xelti se teyeimbei bong telinyeing wou Yesu en lulti no.
LUK 20:41 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel bei, “Nambei nya moux alis vex mi neil embei Kilisi yon Dawit Neu Moux?
LUK 20:42 Dawit venaxow neil eivek Qapiya Lalo bei, “ ‘Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou a xe Tambiy Ngandoung bei, “Wa mendei wou a memang payeiv
LUK 20:43 deka a toung wa xe xel vevek na kwanghembi eivek wang le.” ’
LUK 20:44 Dawit taxe e bei ‘Tambiy Ngandoung.’ Nambei nya Kilisi yon Dawit bu?”
LUK 20:45 Kale xomaxoneing dalus di ngo qayeeng wei Yesu di neil o, de neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei,
LUK 20:46 “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow en xel putoung wei petieing o, xel laleind mi vind en xel embei mi byex teimb ding me na ghavineeng. Xel laleind mi vind bei xel a mi neil bendiyeing teiv wou xel eivek beyeeng wei xel mi wong vateivek lek lulul o, me xel la mindei lek beyeeng nimza wei mya eivek xomek qekueing ama me xel la mindei lek leitata bend wei mya eivek mata wei ngandoung o.
LUK 20:47 Xel mi tyoxe xel vexeiv me panax xel xe xomek. De xel mi wou naleind bei xel nimza om xel mi zeimemend wo ding. Bouk loxyus eno tyek xel wei nambei nyon eno tyek na qou myaveweeng ngandoung.”
LUK 21:1 Ka Yesu veilma lek me yei xel wei malew ana yo la di toung xel xe da eivek qoupek malew wei xomek vambuing o.
LUK 21:2 De moxo yei vexeiv kanyo ti is eno toung selewa gyand nayak yayuw la eivek qoupek malew.
LUK 21:3 De Yesu neil embei, “A neil wou xam zonghek, vexeiv kanyo toung malew ngandoung ghanaw moux alis vex valu.
LUK 21:4 Xomaxoneing on dalus xe malew ngenong, om xel toung danghei ka la eivek deng xeikatu. De vexeiv on lulul maeing, ekom toung malew dalus wei embei devind e yo.”
LUK 21:5 Moxo xe xel betiyeing valu yei xomek vambuing me luk en bei, “Xel qou qakous nimzamza me da wei xel toung wou Anutu yo me vunekwou xomek tiyon en.” Ekom Yesu neil embei,
LUK 21:6 “Bouk ti tyek nam eno lulul tiwei xam ghe di wei yon, tyek xel lelolexe dalus me banex ena xonei lek tembuing de qakous ti tyek se gyeip lek nge mapu.”
LUK 21:7 Om xel teling Yesu bei, “Putoung, gyeik inya lulti yon tyek qandi? Me dee vati tyek talex lek bei lul dalus tine embim nam atyip?”
LUK 21:8 Yesu neil embei, “Xam ghe gweiteyei xow, enok xel a tyoxe xam. Xel ngenong tyek nam lek a leing, me nam a neimbei, ‘A Mesia yo,’ me tyek xel a neimbei, ‘Bouk moxo di lam paviy.’ Ekom xam se betiwou xel.
LUK 21:9 Gyeik ingwei xam a ngo vevek ngandoung me vevek wei seyap o ngenong qandi, yon xam seng detek. En lul beimambei yon tyek qandi tax, ekom bouk loxyus tyek sim nam daing.”
LUK 21:10 Woyom moxo neil wou xel: “Tembuing nge tyek qandi me bong vevek wou tembuing nge, de tete lalei nge tyek bong vevek wou tete lalei nge.
LUK 21:11 Gyeik inyon eno tyek tembuing api ngandoung, de eivek beyeeng valu eno maxep ngandoung tyek qandi me vanei ngandoung is. Me tyek xam ghe gwei dee ngandoung nelu nelu valu qandi eivek tyoung me bong yalenyeing ngandoung wou xam.
LUK 21:12 “Ekom gyeik ingwei lul dalus on seng ghei qandi, eno tyek xel a zeimaxoun xam me bo nol wou xam. Tyek xel a qou xam me na eivek xomek qekueing ama me bong qayeeng en xam, me na toung xam ghe na eivek xeitueing, me tyek xel a qou xam me na bale wou xel king me lei ngandoung wei seyap o mendghalus. En nambei xam ghe mi betiwou ay.
LUK 21:13 Lulti yon tyek bong ambei sakwaing wei xam ambei neil axe xoulek teyei wou xel o.
LUK 21:14 Ekom xam seng bou naleimim ngenong atax bei tyek xam bale zeyi xow ambei nya.
LUK 21:15 En tyek a bong qayeeng wou xam me na bong lupeyei nimza wou xam is, om xel wei embei bong qayeeng en xam eno tyek se pyalek o bakeilek qayeeng wei a wong wou xam o.
LUK 21:16 Xam mamatam, me limyeiw, me nimpapu, me gweleeng, eno tyek xel a neil xam teyei me na toung xam eivek xel ba memend me tyek xel nyeis xam valu na mey.
LUK 21:17 Xel xomaxoneing dalus tyek gyei xam ghe bo nol en xam ghe mi betiwou ay.
LUK 21:18 Ekom xam lumim velus ti tyek se teyeimbei puw veil.
LUK 21:19 Om wangwei xam bale nikanzek ond tyek xam mendei mapieing eivek bouk loxyus.
LUK 21:20 “Gyeik ingwei xam ghe gwei xel vevek bale ebivekwou Yerusalem, on xam ghe boulek bei bouk wei beyeeng embei lelolexe eno paviy.
LUK 21:21 Woyom moux alis vex wei toundei eivek Yudia eno xel a pek me na lukendu. De xel wei toundei eivek Yerusalem eno xel na myayaing veil. De xel wei toundei myayaing en Yerusalem eno se na eivek lalei.
LUK 21:22 En inye bouk wei Anutu embei bong myaveweeng o, nambei qayeeng wei xel byex eivek xoulek eno tyek bo neing lek.
LUK 21:23 Bouk tiyon tyek bo lalei pyaweingxow en vex wei neu pouyek o me vex wei di wong luul wou neu yo! En nimaying ngandoung tyek qandi wou tembuing de Anutu xe lalei vanei tyek detei lek xomaxoneing wei Yuda yo.
LUK 21:24 Tyek xel amey en ngeyeing vevek, me tyek xel a qou xel me na xeitueing nanghei tembuing bamba nei. De xel amba tyek bakei vaxend eivek Yerusalem me gyeiteyei deka bouk wei Anutu lax eno na boueivek le.”
LUK 21:25 Yesu neil no, “Dee nelu nelu tyek qandi eivek sayeiv, dentouk, me betum, de lek tembuing eno xel xomaxoneing wei tembuing tambak ne eno tyek bou naleind ngenong me gyaleeng ngandoung, en tyek xel a ngo mamileeng buklek me bong nindenduing ngandoung.
LUK 21:26 Me lulul wei tyoung gheyapu eno tyek bo pimapi me xomaxoneing tyek gyaleeng ngandoung me mend bivek en vati wei embei nam lek tembuing o.
LUK 21:27 Woyom lek bouk tiyon eno moux alis vex tyek gyei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux nam eivek laxap ti is nikanzek me e xe xeiyaing ngandoung.
LUK 21:28 Gyeik ingwei lulul beimambei yon di qandi, eno xam qandi lek me ghe beil lumim lek, en bouk wei Anutu embei tul xam veil nilul eno di lam paviy.”
LUK 21:29 Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing ti wou xel bei, “Xam ghe gwei xax basunghek me xax sapa yon is.
LUK 21:30 Gyeik ingwei xam venaxow ghe gwei xax a byex nelu duing lek eno xam ghe boulek bei sewis di lam paviy.
LUK 21:31 Om gyeik ingwei xam ghe gwei lulul on qandi, on xam ghe boulek bei Anutu xe tete lalei di lam paviy.
LUK 21:32 “A neil wou xam zonghek bei, neing ayang moux alis vex wei bouk tine eno tyek se mey qe ka lulul ti beimambei yon qandi bole.
LUK 21:33 Tyoung aluw tembuing tyek na tip, ekom axe xoulek tyek se nati.”
LUK 21:34 Yesu neil no, “Xam a mi gweiteyei xow, en xam se num me betiwou Kwa nol wei numeing o xam seng bou naleimim en lulul wei xe neing o, wangwei xam ghe bong ambei nyon, on tyek bouk wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe yo tyek qandi wou xam lutika nambei leliy mi eivek lepulek o.
LUK 21:35 En tyek lulti yon qandi wou moux alis vex dalus wei toundei lek tembuing sapa yo.
LUK 21:36 Xam a mi bale nikanzek me ghe gweiteyei xow taxombouk, me na mi zeimemamim wou Anutu, en kandek xam ghanaw lulul wei embei qandi yon. De tyek xam teyeimbei bale wou Xomaxoneing Neu Moux manghalus.”
LUK 21:37 Teyei lek bouk titi eno Yesu mi teyoxe xel eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o. De boukeing eno la mi yeip nanghei lukendu wei xel mi neil Oliv nei.
LUK 21:38 De satiboukeing lul eno xomaxoneing dalus mi qandi me lam xomek vambuing en embei na mi ngo e xe qayeeng.
LUK 22:1 Lek Bouk Wei Yaeing Belet Wei Yis Ma Veil, wei xel mi taxe bei Pasova eno lam paviy.
LUK 22:2 Xel lumuki leitata yo me xel putoung wei petieing o di yimexe sakwaing wei xel embei nyeis Yesu e mey yo. En xel yaleeng en xomaxoneing.
LUK 22:3 Woyom Sandang la eivek Yudas, xel mi neil embei Iskariot, xel wei xoumeeng yuw eno ti.
LUK 22:4 Me Yudas la luk is xel lumuki leitata yo me xel belimbo wei mi yeiteyei xomek vambuing me yimexe sakwaing wei embei neil Yesu teyei me na toung e na eivek xel memend.
LUK 22:5 Xel wo xeindlala en ingwei xel yei e yo me neil wou Yudas bei tyek xel bong malew wou e.
LUK 22:6 Om Yudas lewexe lek qayeeng wei xel neil on, de di yimexe sakwaing wei embei bou Yesu eivek xel memend gyeik ingwei moux alis vex ngenong se toundei is e yo.
LUK 22:7 Woyom Bouk Wei Yaeing Belet Wei Yis Ma Veil eno lam, wei xel mi leis sipsip lingheing en yaeing lek bouk wei xel mi wou naleind en Pasova yo.
LUK 22:8 Om Yesu wong Petele luw Yoan la me neil embei, “Muw ghe na gweiwou mata wei Pasova yo en xey a gha.”
LUK 22:9 Om luw teling wou e, “Wambei uw a na gheiwou nanghei inya?”
LUK 22:10 Moxo neil elox, “Ka muw ghe na eivek beyeeng ngandoung eno tambiy ti di qalei memiing eivek deng ti eno tyek nam a tyip wou muw. Eno muw betiy e me ghe na eivek xomek tiwei e la eivek o.
LUK 22:11 Me muw a neil wou tambiy wei e beeng o bei, ‘Putoung teling wang: Xomek lalei inya wei ambei gha mata wei Pasova is axe xel betiyeing o?’
LUK 22:12 Moxo tyek talex xomek lalei myasapa wei gheyapu nei wou muw, xel menyex wou dalus woy, om muw ghe gweiwou mata nanghei inyon.”
LUK 22:13 Luw la me yei lulul la teyei lek ingwei Yesu neil wou luw o. Om luw menyex wou mata wei Pasova yo.
LUK 22:14 Seivma la wou eivek ingwei yaeing o, om Yesu lis e xe sinaleyeiw la dei lek zek.
LUK 22:15 Me moxo neil wou xel bei, “A laleing vind bei ambei gha mata wei Pasova ne is xam natax dekakom qalei myavanei.
LUK 22:16 En a neil wou xam, tyek a se nox a gha no qe ka lul tine e bong neing lek eivek Anutu xe tete lalei le.”
LUK 22:17 Ka Yesu qou mayamya wei wain o ti me wong dange wou Anutu de neil embei, “Xam a qou tine me na num eivek ama senghoing.
LUK 22:18 En a neil wou xam tyek a se nox a num wain neing no qe ka Anutu xe tete lalei nam bole.”
LUK 22:19 De moxo qou belet ti, me wong dange wou Anutu me dembu, me wong wou xel betiyeing de neil embei, “Inye a neing wei a wong bei e devind xam. Xam a mi bong ambei nyon en na mi bou naleimim en ay.”
LUK 22:20 Gyeik xel ya woy eno qou mayamya wain me wong ambei nyon no me neil embei, “Mayamya tine inye qokatu vako, wei a gyand qapyex bei e devind xam o.
LUK 22:21 Ekom tambiy tiwei embei neil a teyei me na toung ay eivek xel vevek amba memend eno toundei me ya is ay lek zek.
LUK 22:22 Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek betiwou sakwaing wei Anutu wong wou e yo. Ekom nimaying tyek gyeip wou tambiy tiwei embei neil a teyei me na toung a na eivek xel amba memend o.”
LUK 22:23 Xel betiyeing ngo qayeeng tiyon eno xel di teling wouma eivek xel venaxow senghoing bei, “Eti tyek bong kwa tiyon?”
LUK 22:24 Dekakom xel betiyeing pyalek ama eivek xel venaxow senghoing me neil embei, eti wo lei ngandoung en xel.
LUK 22:25 Yesu neil wou xel bei, “Xel king wei xel amba eno xel mi wo lei ngandoung me yeiteyei moux alis vex, me xel qou leind ambei nye tambiy wei mi wo nimza wou xel o.
LUK 22:26 Ekom xam seng bong ambei nyon, qe xelti embei bo lei ngandoung eivek xam senghoing ond e nox yusayang, de xam xe gyovaxa e teyei lek xukxe wei xam o.
LUK 22:27 En inye eti lei ngandoung, beip inye tambiy wei toundei lek zek, o xukxe wei di duw lul yaeing o? Inyei tambiy tiwei toundei lek zek o. Ekom a toundei eivek xam senghoing nambei xukxe wei di duw o.
LUK 22:28 Ekom xam wei ghe nale is ay gyeik ingwei axeing lam wou ay yo.
LUK 22:29 Me a wong tete lalei wou xam, nambei ingwei mang wong wou ay yo.
LUK 22:30 En kandek xam a mi gwa me na num lek axe zek eivek axe tete lalei me mendei lek xel siaking me ghe pepyawexe xel veleivlei xoumeeng yuw wei Israel o.”
LUK 22:31 Yesu neil embei, “Simon, Simon, Sandang teling en embei daxe xam nambei xel mi seyex wit me wong ninavi veil o.
LUK 22:32 Ekom Simon, a zeimemang en wang, en wa xe wongeingis e se detei. Me gyeik ingwei wa pekwi me ghe noum eno wa mi byexaxoun limyeiw.”
LUK 22:33 Ekom Petele neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, a xeiwou xow bei tyek nana xeitueing is wang me na mey is wang.”
LUK 22:34 Yesu lewexe bei, “A neil wou wang, Petele, gyeik ingwei qouklex seng ghei sesa vya boukeing tine eno tyek wang dax a vun luyal me na neimbei wa seng woulek ay.”
LUK 22:35 Woyom Yesu teling xel, “Gyeik ingwei a wong xam ghe la bandaing veil vaxak malew o vaxak, o vaxalambes, eno xam seng wimexe xow en lulti?” Xel lewexe bei, “Ma.”
LUK 22:36 De moxo neil wou xel, “Ekom gweimbeeng ne wangwei wa xe vaxak malew, ond wa qou, me vaxak is ambei nyon, de wangwei wa se qou ngeyeing vevek ti, on wang bong vateivek lek teimb ding wei wang o de ghe bou ti.
LUK 22:37 Xel byex eivek xoulek eno nambei nye, ‘Moux alis vex yei e wo nol ambei tambiy wei nol o.’ A neil wou xam, qayeeng wei xel byex lek ay eivek qapiya eno tyek bo neing lek. Ee, en vati wei xel byex lek ay eno tyek qandi me bo neing lek.”
LUK 22:38 De xel betiyeing neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wei, ngeyeing vevek yayuw inye.” Moxo neil elox bei, “Inyon woy.”
LUK 22:39 Yesu la lukendu Oliv nambei ingwei mi wong lumama yo, me e xe xel betiyeing betiwou e.
LUK 22:40 Moxo la tyip wou beyeeng wei yo, eno neil wou xel, “Xam a mi zeimemamim, on tyek xam se detei en axeing.”
LUK 22:41 Moxo dula nayaka nambei ingwei xel mi nex qakous o veil xel, de ev vaxa qatu eivek me zeimema,
LUK 22:42 “Mang, wangwei wa laleim devind ond wa zeim mayamya tine veil ay. Ekom wa se betiwou a laleing, qe wa betiwou wamaxow laleim.”
LUK 22:43 Woyom angela wei tyoung gheyapu nei ti lam wou e me byexaxoun e.
