LUK 22:44 Yesu axe myavanei ngandoung, me zeimema nikanzek, me vanei tyip e nambei gyand me teila lek tembuing.
LUK 22:45 Gyeik ingwei moxo zeimema woy, eno qandi lek me lox me la wou e xe xel betiyeing. Loum yei ekom xel yeip, en xel wo nimaing en xel laleind wo maying.
LUK 22:46 Yesu teling xel, “Xam ghe weip en vati? Xam qandi lek me zeimemamim, on tyek xam se detei en axeing.”
LUK 22:47 Ka Yesu nanghei di luk eno xel ngenongakes lam tyip, tambiy tiwei xel neil embei Yudas, xel xoumeeng yuw eno ti qou xel me lam. Moxo la paviy Yesu en embei sesuvexe e,
LUK 22:48 ekom Yesu teling e, “Yudas, wambei neil Xomaxoneing Neu Moux teyei me na toung e na eivek xel amba memend en sesuvexeing?”
LUK 22:49 Gyeik ingwei Yesu xe xel betiyeing yei vati wei embei qandi, eno xel neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, tyek xa nyeis xel en xa xe ngeyeing vevek?”
LUK 22:50 De xel wei xel venaxow eno ti leis xukxe wei lumuki lukanzek o me qateiv e nenya nge payeiv tip me teila.
LUK 22:51 Ekom Yesu neil embei, “Woy! Xam seng bong kwa yon no!” De moxo zeim tambiy on nenya me wong e wo nimzalek.
LUK 22:52 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel lumuki leitata yo, de beyeiv wei xomek vambuing o me xel teivateiv wei lam en e yo bei, “Xam ghe qou ngeyeing vevek me pebumeeng me ghe lam en xam ambei zeim tambiy wei wo vevek, o panaxeing o?
LUK 22:53 A mindei is xam taxombouk eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o, ek xam seng zeimaxoun ay. Ekom inye xam xe seivma, wei mapetok yeiteyei yo.”
LUK 22:54 Woyom xel zeimaxoun Yesu me qou e me la eivek lumuki lukanzek o beeng. Petele di betiy xel me di la kwanding ka.
LUK 22:55 Ekom gyeik xel vev nenyex eivek tete lalei wei xomek tiyon masenghoing me xel xouing toundei wou, eno Petele la dei is xel.
LUK 22:56 Xukxe vex ti yei ingwei e toundei wou nenyex tumeing o. Vex on yei e kanzek me neil embei, “Tambiy tiyon mindei is e.”
LUK 22:57 Ekom Petele axvun me neil embei, “Vex, a se woulek e.”
LUK 22:58 Xel dei nayaka dekakom tambiy nge yei e me neil embei, “Wang on xel wei e yo ti.” Petele neil elox, “Ma, se ay ti!”
LUK 22:59 Nambei seivma ti la veil om moux nge luk nikanzek me neil embei, “Zonghek ayang tambiy tiyon mendei is e, en inyei e nanghei Galili.”
LUK 22:60 Petele neil elox bei, “Moux, a se woulek qayeeng tiwei wang di neil on!” Gyeik e ghei di luk eno qouklex wo vya lutika.
LUK 22:61 Woyom Tambiy Ngandoung pekwi ma me yei Petele bombek. Woyom Petele wounalei en qayeeng wei Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou e yo: “Gweimbeeng boukeing tine qouklex seng ghei sesa vya eno tyek wang dax a vun luyal.”
LUK 22:62 De Petele la myayaing me la eng ngenong.
LUK 22:63 Xel moux wei di yeiteyei Yesu eno xel di luk napeing lek e me petapexe e.
LUK 22:64 Xel tup e ma zeyi nangya qaeing de neil wou e bei, “Wa baluk poropet! Eti petapexe wang?”
LUK 22:65 Me xel lukyak ngenong lek e is.
LUK 22:66 De xeiyaing nexla eno teivateiv wei xel xomaxoneing o, is xel lumuki leitata yo, me xel putoung wei petieing wei kanzol o, xel dalus qekuma, me xel qou Yesu me lam eivek xel xe qekueing ama yon.
LUK 22:67 Me xel neil wou e, “Neil wou xa, wangwei bei inyon wa Kilisi?” Ekom neil elox bei, “Wangwei a neil wou xam, on tyek xam seng bongis ay,
LUK 22:68 me wangwei a teling wou xam en qayeeng valu, on tyek xam seng zewexe lek.
LUK 22:69 Ekom gweimbeeng me e mi na bouk loxyus eno Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek mendei wou Anutu nikanzek mema payeiv.”
LUK 22:70 Xel dalus teling wou e, “Inyon wa Anutu Neu Moux?” Moxo neil elox, “Xam venaxow ghe neil bombek. Inye ay.”
LUK 22:71 Woyom xel neil embei, “Xey a bei se qou pavulek valu en tambiy tine en emaxow mya neil qayeeng tine me xey a ngo woy.”
LUK 23:1 Woyom xel qendu dalus on qandi lek me qou Yesu me la wou Pailat.
LUK 23:2 Me xel wong qayeeng en e, me neil embei, “Xa xei tambiy tine wo nol wou kwa wei xa Yudayeiw o, me peti xa bei xa se toung takis wou Sisa. De mi neil embei e Kilisi, me e yon king ti.”
LUK 23:3 Om Pailat teling wou Yesu, “Inyon wa king wei Yudayeiw o?” Yesu neil elox wou, “Ee inyon nambei wang neil on.”
LUK 23:4 Woyom Pailat neil wou xel lumuki leitata is xel qendu ngandoung on bei, “A se xei sewokeing ti lek tambiy tine.”
LUK 23:5 Ekom xel luk nikanzek me neil embei, “Tambiy on mi ghavineeng me la danghei danghei nei eivek Yudia, myaxeeng anghei distrik Galili me mi lam a zenz inye is, me mi teyoxe xomaxoneing me zeim xel laleind lek.”
LUK 23:6 Pailat ngo tine om teling wou xel, “Moux tine inye Galili ti?”
LUK 23:7 Gyeik ingwei Pailat ngo bei Yesu yon nanghei Galili, woyom wong ela wou Herot en nambei Herot yeiteyei beyeeng danghei tiyon. De gyeik bouk kayon eno Herot toundei Yerusalem.
LUK 23:8 Gyeik ingwei Herot yei Yesu eno wo xeilala ngandoung, en nambei mi toung ma wou en embei gyei e, en vatiyeiw wei e ngo yo, moxo wounalei bei Yesu e bong lulvako valu me e gyei.
LUK 23:9 Herot wong telinyeing ngenong wou e. Ekom Yesu se neil qayeeng ti lox wou e.
LUK 23:10 Xel lumuki leitata yo me putoung wei petieing o toukale inyon, me wong qayeeng en e nikanzek.
LUK 23:11 Woyom Herot alis e xe xel vevek wong napeing wou Yesu me lukyak lek e woy, om xel qou teimb nimza maseim ti me byex lek e, dom wong e lox me la wou Pailat.
LUK 23:12 Lek bouk kayon eno Herot aluw Pailat wo gweleeng lek ama. Takwei eno luw mi wo vevek wouma.
LUK 23:13 Pailat taxe xel lumuki leitata yo me xel gyovaxa me xomaxoneing lam qekuma.
LUK 23:14 Me moxo neil wou xel bei, “Xam ghe qou tambiy tine me ghe lam wou ay me ghe neimbei mi zeim xel laleind lek bei xel bo vevek wou seyap. Om a wo telinyeing lumama wou e wou xam mamim, ekom a se xei sewokeing ti wou tambiy tine en vatiyeiw wei xam ghe wong qayeeng en e yo.
LUK 23:15 De Herot is ambei nyon, om wong e loum wou xey. Xam ghe wei, tambiy tine se wong sewokeing ti bei e mey.
LUK 23:16 Nambei nyon tyek a sesa moxo de woyom na bong e na.”
LUK 23:18 Ekom moux alis vex dalus poux avyend lekti me neil embei, “Leis tambiy on mey, de wong Barabas lam wou xa.”
LUK 23:19 Barabas on tambiy wei wong vevek eivek beyeeng ngandoung me leis xel valu mey o, om xel toung e la xeitueing.
LUK 23:20 Pailat embei bong Yesu na, om neil wou xel dalus no.
LUK 23:21 Ekom xel di tetulexe wou taxeing me neil embei, “Tuw e lek xax pepeeng! Tuw e lek xax pepeeng!”
LUK 23:22 Lu yayal eno moxo neil wou xel bei, “Enva? Tambiy tine wong sewokeing vati? A se xei sewokeing ti bei e mey, om tyek a sesa e de na bong e na.”
LUK 23:23 Ekom xel wo ninkanzek me taxe la xoulekeing bei, Pailat e tuw Yesu lek xax pepeeng. Me xel xe taxeing sevunexe Pailat ning qayeeng.
LUK 23:24 Om Pailat betiwou qayeeng wei xel o me neilteyei bei Yesu e mey.
LUK 23:25 Moxo wong tambiy tiwei toundei eivek xeitueing en ingwei wong vevek me leis xel valu mey, eno la myayaing, tambiy tiwei xel teling en o. De Pailat betiwou xel xe lalei vineing me wong Yesu wou xel vevek.
LUK 23:26 Ka xel vevek qou Yesu me la, eno xel yei tambiy ti lam anghei beyeeng myayaing nei en embei na eivek Yerusalem, moxo lei Simon wei beyeeng Sairini yo. Xel zeimaxoun e me liw xax pepeeng lek e ghandiwek de e qalei me betiwou Yesu.
LUK 23:27 De xomaxoneing ngenongakes di betiy e, is xel vex ngenong wei laleind pyaxow en e me di wong talot me eng o.
LUK 23:28 Yesu pekwi ma me neil wou xel bei, “Xam vex wei Yerusalem o, xam seng deeng en a ti, qe xam ghe deeng en xam venaxow de neumyeiw is.
LUK 23:29 En bouk ti tyek nam gyeik ingwei xam a neimbei, ‘Vex wei mi mouyeeng o, vex wei se wo neu yo me vex wei se di wong luul wou neu eno xel bo xeindlala.’
LUK 23:30 Woyom moux alis vex tyek “‘na neil wou xel lukendu bei, “Xam qepei lek xa!” me xel qetyei bei, “Xam sevun xa!” ’
LUK 23:31 Gweimbeeng xomaxoneing wong nimaying ne wou ay nambei xax wei nimwis o. Om xam ghe ghok xax wei mupek o om tyek bong ambei nya wou xam loxyus?”
LUK 23:32 Tambiy yayuw, luw xouing mi wong sewokeing, om xel qou luw me la is Yesu en xel embei na nyeis luw amey is e.
LUK 23:33 Gyeik xel la tyip nanghei tiyon, xel mi neil embei Lukanzek, nanghei tiyon eno xel tuw Yesu lek xax pepeeng, me tambiy nilul yayuw is, nge wou e mema payeiv de nge wou e mema qeinz.
LUK 23:34 De Yesu neil embei, “Mang, wa semaleeng sewokeing wei xel o, en xel se woulek vati wei xel di wong ne.” De xel vevek di nex qakous dee me pum e xe teimb wouma.
LUK 23:35 Xel xomaxoneing toukale me di yei e, de xel gyovaxa wo vyend wou Yesu bei, “Moxo mi vind xel ba, de wangwei e Kilisi wei Anutu beyal o, on wong e vind xow.”
LUK 23:36 Xel vevek wong vyend wou e is ambei nyon. Xel la paviy e me wong wain senyeing wou e.
LUK 23:37 De xel neil embei, “Wangwei wa king wei xel Yudayeiw o, ond vind xow.”
LUK 23:38 Lek xax pepeeng pundanghou eno xel byex qayeeng bei, “INYE KING WEI YUDAYEIW O.”
LUK 23:39 Tambiy nilul yuw wei xel teyu is Yesu, eno nge lukyak lek Yesu, “Wa Kilisi? Ond wa devind xow me uw is.”
LUK 23:40 Ekom nilul nge neil e, “Wa seng waleeng en Anutu? En wang qalei nimaying teyei lek ambei e?
LUK 23:41 Uw a qalei myavanei ne la teyei lek en nimaying vati wei uw a wong o. Ekom tambiy moxne se wong sewokeing ti.”
LUK 23:42 Woyom moxo neil embei, “Yesu, wang bounaleim en ay gyeik ingwei wang nam eivek wa xe tete lalei yo.”
LUK 23:43 Yesu lewexe wou e bei, “A neil wou wang zonghek, gweimbeeng eno tyek wang na mendei is ay eivek beyeeng nimza wei Anutu yo.”
LUK 23:44 Inye nambei seivma evlek eno mapetok ngandoung sevunexe tembuing sapa, me ela teyei lek seivma yal,
LUK 23:45 en nambei sayeiv siing eno tip, de qaeing wei xel teyu eivek xomek vambuing eno lex ela yuw.
LUK 23:46 Yesu taxe xoulekeing bei, “Mang, a wong axe laweeng lak eivek wa memam.” Gyeik moxo neil ambei nyon eno puw laweeng wei yus o de mey.
LUK 23:47 Beyeiv wei xel vevek o eno yei vati wei qandi yo, me sanghoxe Anutu. Me neil embei “Zonghek ayang, tambiy tine nye bombek.”
LUK 23:48 Gyeik xomaxoneing dalus wei qeku la toukale eno yeimend wou vatiyeiw wei qandi yo, xel laleind wo maying me qatu bambound de lox me la bend.
LUK 23:49 Ekom Yesu xe xel gweleeng dalus, is xel vex wei betiy e me lam anghei Galili eno xel toukale kwanding me yei vatiyeiw wei qandi yo.
LUK 23:50 Tambiy ti lei Yosep, inyon kanzol wei Yudayeiw eno ti, tambiy on nimza me bombek.
LUK 23:51 Moxo lalei se vind woueing nalei me kwa wei xel kanzol wong on. Moxo lam anghei Yudayeiw xe beyeeng nayak wei Arimatia, de moxo mindei me axe Anutu xe tete lalei.
LUK 23:52 Yosep la wou Pailat me teling wou e en embei qou Yesu neing.
LUK 23:53 Woyom moxo la zewax Yesu neing me qou me ouk me loum, de beliv eivek qaeing pus me qou me la liw eivek leiveeng meyeing wei xel kwelexe eivek qakous o. Xel seng ghei liw xelti eivek.
LUK 23:54 Inyon bouk wei menyexeing wou lulul en Sabat o, de Sabat lam paviy.
LUK 23:55 Xel vex wei lam anghei Galili is Yesu eno betiy Yosep me la yei leiveeng meyeing wei Yosep liw neing di yeip nambei nya yo.
LUK 23:56 Woyom xel lox benbend me yeiwou lulul is wel xeimangou yo. De inyon Sabat, om xel toundei lek nambei ingwei Mose xe petieing neil o.
LUK 24:1 Lek bouk ti myaxeeng wei sounda tiyon satiboukeing lul, eno xel vex qou lulul wei xeimangou wei xel menyex wou yo me la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei.
LUK 24:2 Xel yei qakous wei xel lax zeyi leiveeng meyeing eno xel tatekexe veil leiveeng meyeing mya.
LUK 24:3 Ekom gyeik ingwei xel la lalei eno xel se yei Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu neing.
LUK 24:4 Ka xel di wou naleind ngenong en inyon, lutika eno xel yei tambiy yayuw xe teimb on siing niseikeing nambei zivip me toukale wou xel wes.
LUK 24:5 Xel vex yaleeng me ev vaxendkatu eivek de mend la tembuing, ekom moux yuw on neil wou xel, “Xam ghe lam di wimexe tambiy wei mapieing o eivek beyeeng wei meyeing o en va?
LUK 24:6 Moxo se toundei inye, qe qandi lek! Xam ghe bou naleimim en qayeeng wei neil wou xam, gyeik nanghei toundei is xam eivek Galili yo.
LUK 24:7 Neil embei, ‘Tyek xel a toung Xomaxoneing Neu Moux na eivek xel wei sewokeing o memend, en xel atuw e lek xax pepeeng de bouk yal na veil, ond tyek qandi lek no.’”
LUK 24:8 Woyom xel wou naleind en Yesu xe qayeeng wei neil o.
LUK 24:9 Gyeik ingwei xel loum veil leiveeng meyeing eno xel neil lulti beimambei yon wou xel betiyeing xoumeeng ti me moux alis vex dalus.
LUK 24:10 Xel vex wei neil lulti beimambei yon wou sinaleyeiw eno inye, Maria wei Makdala yo, me Joana, me Maria wei Jems ta yo, me vex valu is xel.
LUK 24:11 Ekom xel se wongis xel vex on, en xel xe qayeeng on wong ambei lul bandaing.
LUK 24:12 Ekom Petele qandi lek me veimya me la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei. Dundek me yeila lalei, ekom qaeing toundei bandaing. Moxo lox me la beeng, de venaxow di wounalei bei inye vati wong ambei nye.
LUK 24:13 Lek bouk kayon eno Yesu xe xel betiyeing yayuw la beyeeng tiwei xel mi neil Emaus nei. Inyon nambei 11 kilomita nanghei Yerusalem.
LUK 24:14 Luw di la me luk wou ma en lul sapa wei qandi natax o.
LUK 24:15 Ka luw di luk wouma en lulul ti beimambei yon, eno Yesu venaxow la tyip me di tupwou sakwaing is luw.
LUK 24:16 Ekom lulti wong luw se yeimend wou bei inyon Yesu.
LUK 24:17 Moxo teling luw, “Muw ghe tupwou sakwaing eno muw ghe di luklek vati wouma me ghe lam?” Luw nale me mend talex lek bei luw laleind pyaxow.
LUK 24:18 Tambiy yuw on eno nge wei lei Kliopas, eno teling e, “Wa tambiy tixemou yon ghe la bei beyeeng amba eivek Yerusalem eno wa seng woulek vati wei qandi nanghei inyei lek bouk senghoing tine yo?”
LUK 24:19 Yesu teling luw, “Lul vatiyeiw?” Luw neil elox bei, “Uw andi luk en Yesu wei Nasaret o, moxo poropet ti, mi neil xoulek nikanzek me mi wong lulvako wou Anutu manghalus me xomaxoneing dalus mendghalus is.
LUK 24:20 Xel lumuki leitata yo me xe xe gyovaxa toung e la eivek seyap memend me xel wong qayeeng en me neil embei e mey, om xel tuw e lek xax pepeeng,
LUK 24:21 ekom xa di toung mami en moxo en inyon e tambiy tiwei Anutu wong e lam bei e nam a tul e xe xel Israel veil nilul o. Me lulti is no, inye bouk yal la veil en ingwei lulul tiyon dalus qandi yo.
LUK 24:22 De gweimbeeng xel vex wei xa eno valu wong xa etek. En xel la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei satiboukeing lul,
LUK 24:23 ekom xel se yei e neing. Xel loum neil wou xa bei, xel mend pekwi me xel yei angelayeiw wei neil embei moxo toundei mapieing.
LUK 24:24 Woyom xel wei xa eno valu la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei, me la yei lul toundei nambei ingwei vex vex neil o. Ekom xel se yei e.”
LUK 24:25 Yesu neil wou luw bei, “Muw ghe loung om muw naleimim se qandi lek daing me ghe wongis qayeeng dalus wei xel poropet neil o.
LUK 24:26 Beip Kilisi se teyei bei qou myavanei beimambei ne, dekakom na qou lei ngandoung is xeiyaing?”
LUK 24:27 Woyom neil myaxeeng wou luw en xoulek dalus wei Mose, me xel poropet o me veil luw lundlek en xoulek qes dalus wei xel neil lek e venaxow eivek xoulek o.
LUK 24:28 Ka lal la paviy beyeeng tiwei luw embei na yo, woyom Yesu wong ambei embeim di na.
LUK 24:29 Ekom luw neilaxoun e me neil embei, “Wa toumendei inye is uw en inye paviy soukeing, me inye embim a bouk.” Om moxo eivek la xomek lalei me la toundei is luw.
LUK 24:30 Gyeik ingwei Yesu la dei lek lelek is luw, moxo qou belet me wong dange wou Anutu, de dembu me embei mouk bong wou luw.
LUK 24:31 Woyom luw mend yeila me luw yeimend wou e, de moxo malang veil luw mend.
LUK 24:32 Luw neil wouma bei, “Qayeeng wei neil eno nyuw uw laleind gyeik ingwei e di luk is uw wou sakwaing me veil uw lundlek en Anutu xe xoulek qes o.”
LUK 24:33 De luti eno luw qandi lek me lox me la Yerusalem. Nanghei inyei eno luw yeiwou xel betiyeing xoumeeng ti is moux alis vex valu di qekuma me dei.
LUK 24:34 Xel neil wou luw bei, “Inye zonghek ayang Tambiy Ngandoung qandi lek! Moxo talex xow wou Simon.”
LUK 24:35 Woyom luw neil wou xel en vati wei qandi wou luw wou sakwaing o, me ingwei luw yeimend wou Yesu gyeik ingwei dembu belet o.
LUK 24:36 Ka xel betiyeing nanghei di luk wouma en tine, eno Yesu venaxow lam nale eivek xel senghoing me neil wou xel, “Lalei vevopeing e mi mendei is xam.”
LUK 24:37 Om xel etek me yaleeng en xel embeik nge xel yei meyeing ti nu.
LUK 24:38 Moxo neil wou xel bei, “Xam ghe etek en va? Me xam laleimim wo yuw en va?
LUK 24:39 Wei lam a memang luw xouing me a vaxang luw xouing. Inye a venaxow o! Xam axlek ay me wei. Meyeing nu eno leyeis me kanzek ma, se nambei ingwei xam ghe wei lek a ne.”
LUK 24:40 Gyeik ingwei moxo neil ambei nye, eno talex mema luw me vaxa luw wou xel.
LUK 24:41 Dekakom xel seng ghei wongis. En nambei xel wo xeindlala me di wou naleind ngenong, moxo teling wou xel, “Xam ghe di qou lul yaeing valu nanghei inye?”
LUK 24:42 Xel wong woing wei nekeing eno danghei ti wou e,
LUK 24:43 de moxo zeim me ya wou xel mendghalus.
LUK 24:44 Moxo neil wou xel, “Inye vati wei a neil wou xam gyeik ingwei anghei toundei is xam o, lul sapa wei xel byex lek ay eivek Mose xe petieing, me xel poropet xe qapiya, me qapiya lalo, eno embo neing lek.”
LUK 24:45 Woyom moxo veil xel lundlek bei xel boulek xoulek qes wei di yeip eivek qapiya vambuing o.
LUK 24:46 Moxo neil wou xel bei, “Inye vati wei xel byex eivek xoulek o, Kilisi tyek na qou myavanei me na mey de qandi lek veil meyeing lek bouk yal.
LUK 24:47 De eivek e lei eno xel a neil xoulek wou xomaxoneing wei tembuing tambak o en xel pekwi xow, me Anutu semaleeng sewokeing wei xel o. Xam ghe bong xuk tiyon nanghei Yerusalem a tax.
LUK 24:48 Xam on ingwei xam ghe wei mamim wou lulti beimambei ne dalus woy.
LUK 24:49 Tyek a na bong lul vati wei mang neil zonghek o wou xam, ekom xam a mi mendei eivek Yerusalem deka xam a qou nikanzek wei Anutu gheyapu yo bole.”
LUK 24:50 Gyeik Yesu qou xel betiyeing me la beyeeng Betani nei. Moxo zeim mema luw xouing lek la de wong mata wou xel.
LUK 24:51 Ka e di wong mata wou xel eno moxo la veil xel, de Anutu qou e me la eivek tyoung gheyapu nei.
LUK 24:52 Woyom xel wong lalo wou e, de lox me la Yerusalem is xeindlala ngandoung.
LUK 24:53 De taxombouk eno xel mindei eivek xomek vambuing me sanghoxe Anutu.
JOH 1:1 Eivek myaxeeng selis eno Qayeeng mindei, me Qayeeng mindei is Anutu, de Qayeeng on Anutu.
JOH 1:2 Inye mindei is Anutu eivek myaxeeng selis.
JOH 1:3 Eivek Qayeeng tine eno Anutu toung lulul sapa ne dalus, de embei ma veil eno lulti se woxow nambei e toung o.
JOH 1:4 Mapieing toundei eivek e, me mapieing tiyon eno inyon xeiyaing wei xel xomaxoneing o.
JOH 1:5 De xeiyaing tiyon mi siing eivek mapetok, ekom mapetok se teyei bei sevun xeiyaing.
JOH 1:6 Inyei tambiy ti Anutu wong e lam, moxo lei Yoan.
JOH 1:7 Moxo lam ambei tambiy wei neil Xeiyaing teyei, en kandek eivek moxo eno moux alis vex dalus a ngo e xe qayeeng me bongis.
JOH 1:8 Moxo venaxow se xeiyaing. Qe moxo lam bei na neil xeiyaing teyei.
JOH 1:9 Xeiyaing on zonghek wei mi wo xeiyaing wou xomaxoneing sapa, wei lam lek tembuing o.
JOH 1:10 Moxo mindei lek tembuing, me eivek e eno Anutu toung tembuing, ekom xomaxoneing wei tembuing eno se yeimend wou e.
JOH 1:11 Moxo la beeng qes, ekom xel wei e yo eno se qou e.
JOH 1:12 Qe moux alis vex dalus wei qou e eno xel wongis e lei, de moxo lewexe lek xel bei xel bong ambei Anutu neu.
JOH 1:13 Yakyak on se umbek en mamata gyand, o lalei vineing wei xomaxoneing neing o, o lalei vineing wei mayeiw o. Qe eivek Anutu eno wo xel umbek nambei e neuyeiw.
JOH 1:14 De Qayeeng wo xomaxoneing me lam dei eivek xa senghoing. Xa xei e xe xeiyaing ngandoung, inyei xeiyaing ngandoung wei Neu Moux tixemou tateis wei Ma wong e lam o, pup en lalei xeiles me zonghek.
JOH 1:15 Yoan neilteyei wou moux alis vex en e me taxe bei, “Inyei tambiy tiwei a neil wou xam bei, ‘Tambiy tiwei lam yus en ay eno ngandoung ghanaw ay, en nambei mindei takwei en ay.’”
JOH 1:16 De e xe lalei xeiles wei pup eivek e yo eno xey xouing a mi qou mata lumama titi teyeima.
JOH 1:17 En petieing eno wong wou xey eivek Mose mema, de lalei xeiles me zonghek eno lam wou xey eivek Yesu Kilisi.
JOH 1:18 Xelti se mi yei Anutu, qe Neu tixemou tateis, e maxow Anutu wei mindei wou Ma wes, eno talex Anutu wou xey.
JOH 1:19 De inye Yoan xe pavulek ne, gyeik xel Yudayeiw wei Yerusalem eno wong xel lumuki me Livaiyeiw la teling e bei, “Wang eti?”
JOH 1:20 Moxo neil teyei de se axvun qe neil teyei bei, “A se Kilisi.”
JOH 1:21 Xel teling e, “Woyom wang eti? Wa Eliya?” Moxo neil, “Se ay.” “Qe wa poropet tiwei xa di axe yo?” Moxo neil embei, “Ma.”
JOH 1:22 Woyom xel teling e no, “Wang eti? Wa neilteyei wou xa en xa nox a neil wou xel wei wong xa lam o. Wambei neimbei wamaxow eti?”
JOH 1:23 Yoan neil nambei poropet Yesaya neil o, “A tambiy tiwei vya taxeing ti lam eivek tembuing bandaing o, ‘Xam pepyawexe sakwaing embo bombek en Tambiy Ngandoung.’”
JOH 1:24 Xel Parisi valu wei xel wong xel lam
JOH 1:25 eno teling e, “Wangwei wa se Kilisi, o Eliya o poropet nei yond nambei nya wang lipek xel?”
JOH 1:26 Yoan neil elox bei, “A lipek xam en memiing, ekom tambiy ti toungale eivek xam senghoing eno xam seng woulek.
JOH 1:27 Inyon tambiy tiwei lam yus en ay yo, de a se nimza teyei bei a tul yis wei e xe vaxalambes o.”
JOH 1:28 Lulul tine dalus qandi lek nanghei Betani wei memiing Yorodan loxalu nei, wei Yoan mi lipek moux alis vex anghei yo.
JOH 1:29 Bouk nge eno Yoan yei Yesu di lam wou e, om neil embei, “Wei, Anutu xe Sipsip Lingheing, tambiy tiwei semaleeng sewokeing veil xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa yo!
JOH 1:30 Inye tambiy tiwei a neil gyeik ingwei a neimbei, ‘Tambiy tiwei lam yus en ay eno ngandoung ghanaw ay en nambei mindei takwei gyeik a se ghei umbek o.’
JOH 1:31 A maxow eno a se woulek e, ekom qes wei a lam lipek xel en memiing bei bong xel Israel gyeimend wou e.”
JOH 1:32 Woyom Yoan neil teyei bei, “A xei Laweeng Vambuing lep me lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei nambei beliy me la dei lek e.
JOH 1:33 A maxow se woulek e, qe tambiy tiwei wong a lam a lipek moux alis vex en memiing eno neil wou ay, ‘Tambiy tiwei wang wei Laweeng Vambuing lep me lam dei lek e eno tyek zipek xel en Laweeng Vambuing.’
JOH 1:34 A maxow a xei me na neil wou xam bei tambiy tiyon Anutu Neu Moux.”
JOH 1:35 Bouk nge eno Yoan toungale inyon no is e xe betiyeing yayuw.
JOH 1:36 De moxo yei Yesu di la eno neil embei, “Wei, Anutu xe sipsip lingheing!”
JOH 1:37 Ka betiyeing yuw on ngo ingwei e neil tiyon, eno luw la betiwou Yesu.
JOH 1:38 Yesu pekwi ma, me yei luw di betiy e om teling, “Muw ghe di wimexe vati?” Luw neil embei, “Labai” (qes ambei nye Putoung), “wang mindei inya?”
JOH 1:39 Moxo neil elox bei, “Muw lam wei.” Om luw la me yei ingwei mindei eivek o, me luw mindei bouk tiyon is e. Inyon nambei seivma qou vey soukeing.
JOH 1:40 Andrias wei Simon Petele li yo, inyon yuw wei ngo qayeeng wei Yoan neil me betiy Yesu eno nge.
JOH 1:41 Andrias la yimexe li Simon me neil wou e tax bei, “Xa xei Mesia” (qes ambei nye Kilisi).
JOH 1:42 De Andrias qou Simon me la wou Yesu. Yesu yei e de neil, “Wa Simon Yoan neu. Tyek xel taxe wa leim bei Sipas.” (Xey a pekwi bei Petele. Qes bei qakous.)
JOH 1:43 De bouk nge eno Yesu embei na Galili. Moxo yeiwou Pilip me neil wou e bei, “Wa betiy ay.”
JOH 1:44 Pilip on tambiy wei Betsaida yo, wei Andrias aluw Petele bend qes.
JOH 1:45 Pilip la yeiwou Natanael me neil wou e, “Xa xei tambiy tiwei Mose byex eivek petieing me xel poropet byex is ambei nyon o. Inyon Yosep neu Yesu wei Nasaret o.”
JOH 1:46 Natanael teling, “Nasaret ei! Inye lul nimza valu tyek nam anghei inyei?” Pilip neil embei, “Lam me wei.”
JOH 1:47 Ka Yesu yei Natanael di lam eno moxo luk en e bei, “Tambiy tine Israel zonghek. Eivek e eno tyonyeing ma.”
JOH 1:48 Natanael teling, “Wang woulek ay ambei nya?” Yesu lewexe bei, “Gyeik Pilip seng ghei taxe wang eno a xei wang toundei eivek xax basunghek xeinghembi.”
JOH 1:49 Woyom Natanael neilteyei bei, “Putoung, wang on Anutu Neu Moux, wa king wei Israel o.”
JOH 1:50 Yesu neil wou e, “Wang wongis en ingwei a neil wou wang bei a xei wang toundei eivek xax basunghek xeinghembi yo. Tyek wang gwei lul ngandoung valu ghanaw inyon.”
JOH 1:51 Woyom moxo tetulexe no, “A neil wou wang zonghek, tyek wang gwei tyoung gheyapu natax, me Anutu xe angelayeiw mendi zek me na gheyapu de mendi douk me noum lek Xomaxoneing Neu Moux.”
JOH 2:1 Lek bouk tiwei yal eno iingama ti qandi nanghei beyeeng Kana eivek Galili. Yesu ta la toundei inyon woy atax,
JOH 2:2 me Yesu is e xe xel betiyeing is ambei nyon, xel wo dik wou xel en iingama yon.
JOH 2:3 Gyeik ingwei wain ma, eno Yesu ta neil wou e, “Wain ma veil xel o.”
JOH 2:4 Yesu neil elox bei, “Tang, wang neil ambei nyon wou ay enva? Bouk wei ay eno se ghei lam.”
JOH 2:5 Moxo ta neil wou xel xukxe, “Xam ghe bong vati wei embei neil wou xam o.”
JOH 2:6 Deng qakous ngandoung limti mi nale paviy nanghei inyon, xel Yudayeiw mi lipek eivek nambei xel xe kwa. Memiing nimaying nambei 100 lita eno mi nale eivek titi.
JOH 2:7 Yesu neil wou xel xukxe bei, “Xam a taw memiing eivek deng qakous on xel xouing.” Om xel taw eivek me e pup.
JOH 2:8 Woyom moxo neil wou xel bei, “Xam zakouv valu gweimbeeng me na qou me na wou tambiy wei la tax en mata yo.” Om xel wong ambei nyon,
JOH 2:9 me teiv wei la tax en mata eno num me axe bei memiing pekwi wain. Moxo se woulek bei inyon lam anghei inya, qe xel xukxe wei di taw memiing eno woulek. Woyom moxo taxe moux wei embei dii vex o la beyaleing
JOH 2:10 me neil embei, “Xel dalus mi wong wain wei nenyeing o me xel mi num atax, deka xel num ngenong woy, xel wong ingwei lavus o me xel num yus. Ekom wang byexaxoun ingwei nimza yo de gweimbeeng kane eno wang qou me lam.”
JOH 2:11 Yesu wong e xe lulvako tiwei tax o nambei dee nanghei Kana, danghei wei Galili nei. Moxo talex e xe nikanzek ngandoung teyei me e xe xel betiyeing yei me wongis e.
JOH 2:12 Ka tine la veil eno moxo lep me la xo Kapenaom nei is ta me liyeiw me e xe xel betiyeing. Xel dei bouk valu nanghei inyei.
JOH 2:13 Ka bouk wo sepi lek en Yudayeiw xe Pasova, Yesu lek me la Yerusalem.
JOH 2:14 Eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing eno moxo yei xel moux di wong vateivek lek manghaxo, me sipsip me beliy, de xel valu toundei lek lelek me pakei malew wouma.
JOH 2:15 Om Yesu qou yis valu me viy me tiy xel vula veil xomek vambuing is sipsip me manghaxo. Moxo qapyex malew selewa wei xel di pakei eno veil de qapyex xel xe lelek is.
JOH 2:16 Woyom neil wou xel wei di wong vateivek lek beliy o bei, “Xam qou menek beimambei ne me la veil inye! Xam seng bong Mang xe xomek bong ambei xomek wei vateivek o!”
JOH 2:17 De e xe xel betiyeing wounaleind en qayeeng wei yeip eivek qapiya wei petieing o nambei nye, “A laleing vind wa xe xomek om a wong xuk nikanzek bei bong xomek ne na toumendei nimza.”
JOH 2:18 Woyom xel Yudayeiw neil wou Yesu bei, “Tyek wa talex dee wei lulvako en vati eno wou xa en xa boulek bei wang wo lei ngandoung en wambei mi bong lulti beimambei yon dalus?”
JOH 2:19 Yesu neil wou xel bei, “Xam lelolexe xomek vambuing tine, de tyek a dev epyap no eivek bouk yal.”
JOH 2:20 De Yudayeiw neil elox bei, “Xel wong xuk lek eveing xomek vambuing ne teyei lek vakovek qes mepyeiyuw me lak limti, de tyek wang dev e qandi lek eivek bouk yal?”
JOH 2:21 Ekom xomek vambuing wei moxo neil on inyon emaxow neing.
JOH 2:22 Ka Yesu qandi lek veil meyeing, e xe xel betiyeing wou naleind en vati wei e neil o. Woyom xel wongis xoulek wei di yeip eivek qapiya yo me qayeeng wei Yesu neil o.
JOH 2:23 Ka Yesu toundei Yerusalem eivek mata wei Pasova yo, eno xomaxoneing ngenongakes yei dee wei lulvako wei wong o me wongis e lei.
JOH 2:24 Ekom Yesu venaxow woulek xow om se wongis xel, en moxo woulek xomaxoneing dalus.
JOH 2:25 Moxo se wounalei en xelti bei na neil wou xomaxoneing, en moxo woulek vati wei toundei eivek xomaxoneing laleind o.
JOH 3:1 De tambiy wei Parisi yo ti lei Nikodimas, inyon gyovaxa wei kanzol wei xel Yudayeiw o ti.
JOH 3:2 Moxo lam wou Yesu eivek boukeing me neil wou, “Putoung, xa woulek bei wang on putoung tiwei Anutu wong e lam o. Wangwei Anutu se mendei is xelti on tyek se bong dee wei lulvako yo nambei ingwei wang mi wong on.”
JOH 3:3 Yesu neil elox wou e bei, “A neil wou wang zonghek, xelti embei se dumbek no on tyek se gyei Anutu xe tete lalei.”
JOH 3:4 Nikodimas teling, “Nambei nya tambiy dumbek no gyeik ingwei wo teiv takwei yo? Neing ayang moxo tyek se nox me na eivek ta veis luyuw me dumbek no!”
JOH 3:5 Yesu lewexe bei, “A neil wou wang zonghek, xelti embei se dumbek en memiing me Laweeng Vambuing on tyek se na eivek Anutu xe tete lalei.
JOH 3:6 Lul wei neing wong e umbek eno inyon neing, de lul wei Laweeng Vambuing wong e umbek eno inyon laweeng.
JOH 3:7 Wa seng detek en a xe qayeeng, ‘Qe wang dumbek no.’
JOH 3:8 De laweeng mi vei me la danghei danghei wei embei na yo. Eno wang mi ngo nindenduing, ekom wa seng woulek bei e lam anghei inya o embei na nya. Om inyon teyei lek xel dalus wei umbek vako en Laweeng Vambuing o.”
JOH 3:9 Nikodimas teling, “Lulti yon tyek bong ambei nya?”
JOH 3:10 Yesu neil wou, “Wa Israelyeiw xe putoung, ekom wa seng woulek lulti beimambei ne?
JOH 3:11 A neil wou wang zonghek, xa luk en vati wei xa woulek o, me xa neil qayeeng en vati wei xa xei woy yo, ekom xam xomaxoneing seng wongis xa xe qayeeng.
JOH 3:12 A neil wou xam en lul wei tembuing o ekom xam seng wongis, woyom wangwei a neil wou xam en lul wei tyoung gheyapu yo on tyek xam ghe bongis ambei nya?
JOH 3:13 Xelti se la eivek tyoung gheyapu ti qe tambiy tiwei lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei yo, inyon Xomaxoneing Neu Moux.
JOH 3:14 Inye nambei Mose zeim myeiy lek la eivek tembuing bandaing o, om Xomaxoneing Neu Moux eno tyek xel a zeim e zekna,
JOH 3:15 om xel dalus wei embei bongis e eno tyek na qou deing mapieing luta luta.
JOH 3:16 “En Anutu lalei vind xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa yo omek wong emaxow Neu Moux tixemou tateis on, en kandek eti yeiw wei wongis e eno se mey, qe xel a qou deing mapieing luta luta.
JOH 3:17 En Anutu se wong Neu Moux lam lek tembuing bei e nam bong qayeeng en xomaxoneing lek tembuing. Qe wong e lam bei e nam devind xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa veil meyeing.
JOH 3:18 Eti yeiw wei wongis moxo eno se nale lek qayeeng, qe eti yeiw wei se wongis e eno nale lek qayeeng woy. En nambei se wongis Anutu Neu Moux tixemou tateis on lei.
JOH 3:19 Xel xe qayeeng on qes ambei nye, xeiyaing lam eivek tembuing, ekom xomaxoneing laleind vind mapetok ghanaw xeiyaing en nambei xel xe kwa yon nilul.
JOH 3:20 Xomaxoneing sapa wei mi wo kwa nilul eno mi pesek xeiyaing, om xel embei se nam eivek xeiyaing, en tyek xel xe kwa nilul on nam yanyateiv.
JOH 3:21 Ekom eti yeiw wei mi betiwou kwa wei zonghek eno mi lam eivek xeiyaing en kandek xel gyei embo nimza bei lulul wei xel mi wong eno xel mi wong xuk en Anutu xe nikanzek.”
JOH 3:22 Ka tine la veil, eno Yesu lis e xe xel betiyeing la danghei wei Yudia nei. Moxo toundei is xel anghei inyon me lipek moux alis vex.
JOH 3:23 Yoan lipek xomaxoneing is ambei nyon nanghei Ainon paviy beyeeng Salim, en nambei memiing ngenong di yeip inyon, me xomaxoneing di lam bei e zipek xel.
JOH 3:24 Inyon atax gyeik xel se ghei toung Yoan eivek xeitueing o.
JOH 3:25 Xel betiyeing wei Yoan o valu is Yuda ti pyalek ama en kwa wei xel mi lipek me wo vako wou Anutu manghalus o.
JOH 3:26 Yoan xe xel betiyeing lam neil wou e bei, “Putoung, tambiy tiwei toundei is wang anghei memiing Yorodan loxalu nei me wang neil e xe qayeeng, eno di lipek moux alis vex, me xel dalus la wou e.”
JOH 3:27 Yoan neil elox wou xel bei, “Tambiy ti teyei bei qou vatiyeiw, wangwei Anutu wei tyoung gheyapu nei bong wou e yo.
JOH 3:28 Xam venaxow a neil teyei en qayeeng wei a neil o bei, ‘A se Kilisi, qe a tambiy tiwei Anutu wong a lam atax en e yo.’
JOH 3:29 Tambiy ti dii vex ti eno vex tiyon e venei. De e xe gweleeng mi nale me li nenya wou tambiy wei ii vex o xe lukeing me wo xeilala ngandoung. Om gweimbeeng xeilala tiyon eno pup eivek a laleing.
JOH 3:30 Moxo lei e zekna gheyapu, de a leing e deteiwou.
JOH 3:31 “Tambiy tiwei lam anghei gheyapu eno la ghey en lulul sapa, de tambiy wei lam anghei tembuing eno inyon tembuing, me mi luk en lul wei tembuing o. De tambiy tiwei lam anghei tyoung gheyapu eno la ghey en lulul sapa.
JOH 3:32 Moxo mi luk en vati wei yei me ngo yo, ekom xelti se zeimaxoun e xe qayeeng.
JOH 3:33 Tambiy tiwei zeimaxoun e xe qayeeng eno talex lek bei Anutu yon zonghek ayang.
JOH 3:34 En tambiy tiwei Anutu wong e lam eno mi neil Anutu xe qayeeng, en Anutu wong Laweeng Vambuing dalus wou e.
JOH 3:35 De Ma lalei vind Neu Moux me toung lulul dalus la eivek e mema.
JOH 3:36 Xelti bongis Neu Moux on qou mapieing luta luta, ekom xelti pesek Neu Moux on tyek se gyei mapieing, en tyek Anutu xe lalei vanei detei lek e.”
JOH 4:1 De Parisiyeiw ngo qayeeng bei Yesu lipek xomaxoneing me wong xel wo betiyeing ngenong ghanaw Yoan.
JOH 4:2 Ekom Yesu venaxow se lipek xel, qe inyon e xe xel betiyeing.
JOH 4:3 Yesu woulek bei xel Parisi ngo tine om la veil Yudia de lox me la Galili no.
JOH 4:4 Dom moxo tupwou sakwaing tiwei la senghoing eivek Samaria nei.
JOH 4:5 Om moxo la eivek beyeeng nayak ti lei Sikar eivek tembuing danghei wei Samaria yo. Beyeeng tiyon toundei paviy tembuing wei Yakop wong wou neu Yosep o.
JOH 4:6 Yakop xe leiveeng memiing ti toundei inyei, de Yesu nima en ingwei lam sakwaing anding o, om la dei paviy leiveeng memiing on. Inyon nambei seivma evlek o.
JOH 4:7 Gyeik Samaria vex ti lam en embei nam a puw memiing eno Yesu neil wou vexo, “Tyek wang bong memiing me a num?”
JOH 4:8 Moxo xe xel betiyeing la eivek beyeeng nayak en xel embei na bou lul yaeing.
JOH 4:9 Samaria vex neil wou e bei, “Wa Yuda ti de a Samaria vex ti. Nambei nya wang teling wou ay en numeing?” En Yudayeiw me Samariayeiw se mindei is ama.
JOH 4:10 Yesu lewexe wou vexo, “Wangwei wang boulek lul xeilala wei Anutu embei bong o me eti ingwei teling wang en numeing, on wa teling wou e me embong memiing wei mapieing o wou wang.”
JOH 4:11 Vex neil wou bei, “Teiv, deng me yis wei wambei puw memiing nangya eno ma de leiveeng memiing ne la ghembi. Tyek wa qou memiing mapieing tiyon nanghei inya?
JOH 4:12 Beip wang ghanaw xe bund Yakop, moxo wong leiveeng memiing tine wou xa de e venaxow is neuyeiw me manghaxo me sipsip is lul dalus mi num memiing tine?”
JOH 4:13 Yesu lewexe, “Xomaxoneing sapa wei mi num memiing tine eno tyek kwend a tip no,
JOH 4:14 ekom xelti embei num memiing wei ambei bong wou e ne tyek kwa se tip. De memiing wei ambei bong wou e eno tyek na mi puw lulaxeiv eivek e me bong mapieing luta luta wou e.”
JOH 4:15 De vex neil wou e bei, “Teiv, wang bong memiing tiyon wou ay en kandek a kwang se tip no de a se mi nox me noum inye en puweing memiing.”
JOH 4:16 Moxo neil wou vexo bei, “La, taxe leyam de muw xouing loum.”
JOH 4:17 Vexo neil elox bei, “A leyang ma yo.” Yesu neil wou e, “Wang neil neing, gyeik ingwei wang neimbei wa leyam ma yo.
JOH 4:18 En nambei wa leyam lim, de moux tiwei wang toundei is ne inye se wa leyam. Qayeeng vati wei wang neil on zonghek ayang.”
JOH 4:19 De vexo neil wou e bei, “Teiv, a xei bei inye wa poropet ti.
JOH 4:20 Xa bumiyeiw mi wong lalo lek lukendu tine, ekom xam Yudayeiw eno xam ghe mi neimbei beyeeng wei xomaxoneing a mi bong lalo eno eivek Yerusalem.”
JOH 4:21 Yesu neil teyei wou e bei, “Vex, wang bongis ay, bouk ti tyek nam eno tyek xam seng bong lalo wou Mang lek lukendu tine o eivek Yerusalem.
JOH 4:22 Xam Samariayeiw ghe mi wong lalo wou vati wei xam seng woulek o, de xa Yudayeiw a mi wong lalo wou vati wei xa woulek o, en vineing wei qou xa lam veil nilul eno lam wou xa Yuda.
JOH 4:23 Ekom bouk ti tyek nam, me gweimbeeng ne eno lam woy om gyeik xel embei bong lalo zonghek ond xel bong lalo wou Mang eivek Laweeng me zonghek, en Mang lalei vind xel ambei nyon bei xel a mi bong lalo wou e.
JOH 4:24 Anutu yon laweeng, om xel wei mi wong lalo wou e eno xel a mi bong lalo eivek Laweeng me eivek zonghek.”
JOH 4:25 De vexo neil embei, “A woulek bei Mesia tiwei xel mi taxe e bei Kilisi eno tyek nam. Om gyeik ingwei moxo embei nam, eno tyek na neil lul dalusateiv teyei wou xey.”
JOH 4:26 Woyom Yesu neilteyei wou e bei, “A tambiy tiyon, ingwei di luk is wang ne eno inye ay.”
JOH 4:27 Woyom ka e xe xel betiyeing loum eno xel etek en xel yei ingwei di luk is vex ti yo. Ekom xelti se teling, “Wa bei qou vati?” o “Nambei nya wang di luk is vex on?”
JOH 4:28 Woyom vexo ghanaw e xe memiing dengmuing toundei de lox me la beyeeng me neil wou xomaxoneing dalus nambei nye,
JOH 4:29 “Xam lam wei tambiy tiwei neil wou ay en lul dalus wei a mi wong takwei yo. Beip inyei Kilisi?”
JOH 4:30 Om xel lam veil beyeeng nayak on me la yei e.
JOH 4:31 Dekakom e xe xel betiyeing neil wou e bei, “Putoung, wa lulul ne.”
JOH 4:32 Ekom moxo neil wou xel, “A xe yaeing wei yaing eno xam seng woulek o.”
JOH 4:33 Woyom e xe xel betiyeing di neil wouma bei, “Beip xel valu qou lul yaeing me lam wou e?”
JOH 4:34 Yesu neil wou xel, “A xe lul yaeing eno nambei nye, a bei betiwou tambiy tiwei wong a lam eno lalei me na bong e xe xuk e na pyap lek.
JOH 4:35 Beip xam seng mi neimbei, ‘Dentouk qes vey di yeip zeyi bouk wei qekuwou lulul yaeing o?’ A neil wou xam, xam ghe gweina xuk danghei danghei nei! Lulul wo neing woy teyei lek qoueing.
JOH 4:36 Me gweimbeeng tambiy wei mi qekuwou lulul yaeing eno qou e xe xouveing me di qeku lul yaeing wei deing mapieing luta luta yo, om tambiy wei vuw lul o me tambiy wei wong xuk lek qoueing lulul neing o, eno luw xouing bo xeindlala.
JOH 4:37 Inye xel neil, ‘Tambiy nge vuw lulul eivek xuk de nge qekuwou lulul neing’ eno qayeeng ne zonghek.
JOH 4:38 A wong xam ghe la qekuwou lulul yaeing wei xam seng wo xuk lek o. Qe xel valu wong pok ngandoung lek, de xam ghe la qou vineing lek pok wei xel o.”
JOH 4:39 Xel Samaria ngenong wei beyeeng nayak tiyon eno wongis Yesu, en qayeeng wei vex on neil teyei yo, “Moxo neil wou ay en lulul dalus wei a wong takwei yo.”
JOH 4:40 Om gyeik ingwei Samariayeiw lam wou moxo eno xel neil wou bei e toumendei is xel, om moxo toundei bouk yayuw is xel.
JOH 4:41 En nambei Yesu xe qayeeng wei neil, eno moux alis vex ngenong wongis.
JOH 4:42 Xel neil wou vex on, “Xa se wongis en nambei vati wei wang neil o, qe gweimbeeng xa maxow a ngo me na woulek bei inye neing ayang, tambiy tine qou xey a loum veil nilul wei tembuing sapa yo.”
JOH 4:43 Ka bouk yuw on la veil eno Yesu la Galili.
JOH 4:44 Yesu venaxow neil qayeeng tine, xel se mi wevek poropet ti xeinghembi eivek emaxow beeng qes.
JOH 4:45 Om gyeik ingwei moxo la tyip Galili, eno Galiliyeiw wo xeindlala en e. En xel yei lul wei wong eivek Yerusalem gyeik mata wei Pasova yo, en xel la toundei inyei is.
JOH 4:46 Yesu lox me la beyeeng Kana eivek Galili no, wei nanghei inyon eno moxo pekwi memiing wo wain. De nanghei inyei eno king xe beyeiv ti neu moux vanei wong me e di yeip anghei Kapenaom.
JOH 4:47 Woyom tambiy tiyon ngo bei Yesu la veil Yudia me la toundei Galili, eno moxo la wou e me tay wou Yesu bei e nam bong e neu moux bo nimzalek, en neu e bim amey.
JOH 4:48 Yesu neil wou e, “Wangwei xam ne seng gwei dee wei lulvako yo ond xam seng mi wongis.”
JOH 4:49 King xe beyeiv neil wou e, “Teiv, wang nam axone daing enok a neung amey.”
JOH 4:50 Yesu neil elox wou e bei, “Wang nox en neum tyek na toumendei mapieing.” De moux tiyon wongis qayeeng wei Yesu neil o me la.
JOH 4:51 Ka moxo di la wou sakwaing, e xe xel xukxe lam pelong e me neil wou bei, neum toundei mapieing.
JOH 4:52 Woyom moxo teling xel en seivma wei neu wo nimzalek, eno xel neil wou e, “Gying ma veil e vezeiveeng soukeing wei seivma ti yo.”
JOH 4:53 Woyom ma woulek bei lek seivma kayon eno Yesu neil wou e, “Neum tyek na toumendei mapieing.” Om moxo is nipapu dalus wei e beeng eno wongis.
JOH 4:54 Inye dee wei lulvako luyuw wei Yesu wong gyeik e la veil Yudia me la toundei Galili yo.
JOH 5:1 Ka inyon la veil, eno Yesu lek me la Yerusalem en bouk ngandoung wei lalo wei Yudayeiw o.
JOH 5:2 Eivek Yerusalem paviy tete mya wei sipsip eno lounyeing ti mi yeip inyon, xel Hibru mi neil Betesda. Xomek nayak lim toukale wou lounyeing on nenyawes.
JOH 5:3 Xel ngenong wei vanei nelu nelu eno mi yeip eivek xomek nayak nanghei inyon, is xel wei matekeing o, me vaxa nol o me xel wei bezomb o. [
JOH 5:4 En Tambiy Ngandoung xe angela ti mi lam axone eivek bouk titi me la eivek lounyeing me wo pimapi wou, de tambiy ti embei na eivek lounyeing wei di wo pimapi yon atax eno wo nimzalek veil vanei wei wong e yo.]
JOH 5:5 Tambiy ti vanei me e mi yeip eivek xomek nayak wei xel byex wou yon teyei lek vakovek qes 38.
JOH 5:6 Yesu yei moxo di yeip inyon eno woulek bei vanei wong e me e mi yeip enden, Yesu teling wou e, “Wa being bo nimzalek?”
JOH 5:7 Tambiy wei vanei yon neil elox bei, “Teiv, xel wei embei devind a na eivek memiing gyeik ingwei embei bo pimapi eno ma. A venaxow a mi wong me na xei en ambei na eivek, ekom xel valu mi la eivek ghanaw ay.”
JOH 5:8 Woyom Yesu neil wou e, “Qandi lek! De qou wa xe ghus me la.”
JOH 5:9 Lutika eno moux on wo nimzalek, de moxo qou e xe ghus me la. Bouk tiyon eno inye Sabat,
JOH 5:10 om xel teivateiv wei Yudayeiw o neil wou moux tiwei wo nimzalek o, “Inye Sabat, petieing peti bei wa se qalei wa xe ghus lek.”
JOH 5:11 Ekom moxo neil elox bei, “Tambiy tiwei wong a wo nimzalek eno neil wou a bei, ‘Qou wa xe ghus me la vaxam.’”
JOH 5:12 Om xel teling e, “Tambiy eti ingwei neil embei wa qou ghus me ghe na vaxam on?”
JOH 5:13 Moux tiwei wo nimzalek eno loungen tambiy tiwei neil o, en Yesu la xupekeing eivek xel ngenong senghoing me la.
JOH 5:14 Kalekom Yesu yei e nanghei tete lalei wei xomek vambuing nei me neil wou e, “Wei, wang wo nimzalek woy. Om wa seng nox bong sewokeing no, enok nimaying ngandoung ti qandi wou wang.”
JOH 5:15 Woyom moux tiyon la neil wou teivateiv wei Yudayeiw o bei, “Tambiy tiwei wong a wo nimzalek eno inyon Yesu.”
JOH 5:16 Om nambei Yesu di wong lulti beimambei yon lek Sabat, om teivateiv wei Yudayeiw di wo nol wou e.
JOH 5:17 Yesu neil elox wou xel, “Mang mi wo xuk taxombouk me elam gweimbeeng, me ay is ambei nyon, a mi wo xuk.”
JOH 5:18 En qes tine Yudayeiw mi wo niqetyei qetyei en embei nyeis Yesu na mey, en se ingwei pyalek petieing wei Sabat o, qe mi neil embei e ma Anutu. Me wong emaxow teyei lek Anutu.
JOH 5:19 Yesu lewexe wou xel, “A neil wou xam zonghek, Neu Moux se mi wong lulti nangya emaxow xe kwa, qe moxo tyek bong lul kawei yei Ma wong o, en nambei vatiyeiw wei Ma wong eno Neu Moux tyek bong ambei nyon.
JOH 5:20 En Ma lalei vind Neu Moux me talex lulul dalus wei mi wong eno wou e. De ingwei embei bong etekeing wou xam eno Ma tyek talex lul ngandoung valu wou e ghanaw inyon veil.
JOH 5:21 En Ma mi piyexe xel wei mey o me wong mapieing wou xel, om Neu Moux is ambei nyon, moxo mi wong mapieing wou xomaxoneing teyei lek emaxow lalei.
JOH 5:22 Ma se mi wong qayeeng en xelti, qe wong xuk dalus wei wongeing qayeeng eno wou Neu Moux,
JOH 5:23 om xel dalus a mi sanghoxe Neu Moux nambei ingwei xel mi sanghoxe Ma yo. Xelti embei se sanghoxe Neu Moux on tyek se sanghoxe Ma tiwei wong e lam o.
JOH 5:24 “Neing ayang, a neil wou xam, xel tiwei ngo a xe qayeeng me wongis tambiy tiwei wong a lam eno qou mapieing luta luta woy de tyek se teyei bei bale lek qayeeng me na qou myaveweeng. Qe moxo sek me lam veil meyeing woy, de la dei mapieing.
JOH 5:25 Neing ayang, neing ayang, a neil wou xam, bouk di lam me gweimbeeng ne eno lam gyeik ingwei xel meyeing embei ngo Anutu Neu Moux vya yo me xelti embei ngowou eno dei mapieing.
JOH 5:26 En Ma xe mapieing toundei eivek emaxow, om moxo wong nikanzek wou Neu Moux bei e qou mapieing eivek venaxow.
JOH 5:27 Me Ma wong lei ngandoung wou e bei e mi bong qayeeng en moux alis vex, en nambei e Xomaxoneing Neu Moux.
JOH 5:28 “Xam seng bou naleimim ngenong en qayeeng tine, en bouk di lam, gyeik ingwei xel wei mey me di yeip eivek xel xe leiveeng meyeing eno tyek na ngo e vya
JOH 5:29 me lam myayaing. Xel wei mi wong kwa nimza eno tyek qandi lek me mendei mapieing, de xel wei mi wong kwa nilul eno tyek qandi lek me na qou myaveweeng.
JOH 5:30 A maxow se mi wong lulti, qe a mi wong qayeeng nambei ingwei a ngo yo, dom na mi zeim qayeeng en moux alis vex. Me qayeeng wei a mi zeim eno mi la bombek, en a se mi wong xeinglala en venaxow qe a mi wong e tiwei wong a lam o wo xeilala.
JOH 5:31 “Wangwei a neil qayeeng wei a maxow o teyei, ond qayeeng wei a neil on se zonghek.
JOH 5:32 Ekom inyei tambiy nge mi neil qayeeng wei ay yo teyei. Me a woulek bei e xe qayeeng on zonghek.
JOH 5:33 “Xam ghe wong xel la wou Yoan me e neil qayeeng wei zonghek o teyei.
JOH 5:34 A maxow se qou xomaxoneing xe qayeeng, qe a neil en ambei Anutu devind xam.
JOH 5:35 Yoan on nambei lam wei tum me wo xeiyaing om xam ghe beyal me ghe wo xeimimlala wou xeiyaing sepika.
JOH 5:36 “Ekom a xe qayeeng ne eno ghanaw ingwei Yoan o. En xuk dalus wei Mang wong wou ay bei a bong me e ma, eno neil a teyei wou moux alis vex bei Mang wong a lam.
JOH 5:37 De Mang wei wong a lam eno venaxow tul qayeeng en ay. Ekom xam seng mi ngo e vya o ghe mi wei e ma.
JOH 5:38 O moxo xe qayeeng wei mi neil eno se dei eivek xam laleimim, en xam seng wongis e tiwei moxo wong e lam o.
JOH 5:39 Xam ghe mi pyaw qayeeng qes wei yeip eivek xoulek me ghe wou naleimim bei tyek xam a qou mapieing luta luta. Qayeeng ti beimambei yon mi neil a teyei,
JOH 5:40 ekom xam ghe pesek, en xam ambei seng nam wou ay me na qou mapieing.
JOH 5:41 “Ambei se qou lei ngandoung wou xomaxoneing,
JOH 5:42 ekom a woulek xam. A woulek bei xam seng qou Anutu xe lalei vineing eivek laleimim.
JOH 5:43 A lam lek Mang lei, eno xam seng qou ay, qe wangwei xel nge nam lek e venaxow lei ond tyek xam a qou e.
JOH 5:44 Xam ghe mi pamilexe lei ngandoung wei xam ghe mi wong wouma yo de lei ngandoung wei lam wou Anutu venaxow eno xam a bei se qou. Om tyek xam ghe bongis ambei nya?
JOH 5:45 “Ekom xam seng bou naleimim bei tyek a byex qayeeng lek xam wou Mang manghalus, qe tambiy wei embei byex qayeeng lek xam eno inyon Mose, tambiy tiwei xam ghe toung mamim wou bei tyek devind xam o.
JOH 5:46 Wangwei xam ghe bongis Mose on tyek xam ghe bongis ay, en moxo byex qayeeng en ay.
JOH 5:47 Ekom xam seng wongis qayeeng wei byex o, om nambei nya tyek xam ghe bongis vati wei ambei neil o?”
JOH 6:1 Ka bouk valu lak veil en inyon, eno Yesu la lounyeing Galili loxalu nei, inyei lounyeing lei nge eno Taiberias.
JOH 6:2 De xomaxoneing ngenongakes betiy e me la, en nambei xel yei dee wei lulvako wei wong xel wei vanei eno wo nimzalek o.
JOH 6:3 Woyom Yesu lek lukendu me la toundei is e xe xel betiyeing.
JOH 6:4 De Yudayeiw xe bouk ngandoung wei Pasova eno lam paviy.
JOH 6:5 Gyeik ingwei Yesu veilma lek me yei xomaxoneing ngenong di lam wou e, eno neil wou Pilip bei, “Tyek xey a bou belet anghei inya me na bong wou xel beimambei ne en xel gya?”
JOH 6:6 Moxo teling tine en embei daxe Pilip, en moxo wounalei en vati wei embei bong o woy.
JOH 6:7 Pilip lewexe wou e bei, “Wangwei xey a bou belet lek malew vaxak yuw on tyek se teyei xel ne titi bei xel gya nayak kaka!”
JOH 6:8 Moxo xe betiyeing nge inyon Andrias wei Simon Petele li eno luk bei,
JOH 6:9 “Yak ti toundei inye eno di qou bali belet nayak lim de woing nayak yayuw, ekom tyek inye devind xomaxoneing ngenong ne nambei nya?”
JOH 6:10 Yesu neil embei, “Xam neil wou xomaxoneing on en xel mendei tembuing o.” Qeis ngenong toundei inyon, om xel dei lek. De moux wei dei yon teyei lek ambei 5,000.
JOH 6:11 Woyom Yesu qou belet me wong dange wou Anutu de wong wou xomaxoneing dalus wei toundei inyon eno xel ya me enden xel. Moxo wong ambei nyon wou woing is.
JOH 6:12 Ka xel dalusateiv ya woy, moxo neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei, “Xam qekuwou myapapu wei toundei yo en kandek ti se nati.”
JOH 6:13 Om xel qekuwou myapapu wei belet lim wei xel ya de toundei yo me sei eivek pasik xoumeeng yuw me epup.
JOH 6:14 Ka xomaxoneing yei dee wei lulvako wei Yesu wong o, eno xel neil embei, “Neing ayang inye Poropet tiwei Anutu neil embei bong e nam lek tembuing o.”
JOH 6:15 Yesu woulek bei xel embei nam tendu e me embo king wei xel o, om moxo venaxow la veil xel me lox me la lukendu no.
JOH 6:16 Sayeiv la eivek, eno e xe xel betiyeing lep me la xo wei lounyeing nei,
JOH 6:17 de xel la eivek bot ti me sepa lounyeing me la Kapenaom. Inye bouk, de Yesu se ghei la wou xel.
JOH 6:18 Laweeng nikanzek ti vei om lounyeing vuklek.
JOH 6:19 Xel di sepa me la teyei lek kilomita lim o limti, de xel yei Yesu di la lek lounyeing mapu me la paviy xel om xel yaleeng ngandoung.
JOH 6:20 Ekom moxo neil wou xel bei, “Inye ay yo, om xam seng gwaleeng.”
JOH 6:21 Woyom xel toung laleind lekti bei qou e me na eivek bot, de lutika eno bot la nenyawes lek beyeeng tiwei xel embei na yo.
JOH 6:22 Bouk nge eno moux alis vex nanghei toundei lounyeing nenyawes nge loxalu nei en xel yeimend wou bei bot tixemou di yeip inyei, de Yesu se la is e xe xel betiyeing, qe xel venaxow la.
JOH 6:23 Woyom xel Taiberias xe bot valu lam paviy beyeeng wei Tambiy Ngandoung wong dange en belet me xel ya yo.
JOH 6:24 De xel qendu yon yeimend wou bei Yesu lis e xe xel betiyeing se toundei. Om xel la eivek bot ti beimambei yon me la Kapenaom en xel embei na gyimexe Yesu.
JOH 6:25 Gyeik ingwei xel yeiwou e nanghei lounyeing loxalu nei, eno xel teling e, “Putoung, wang lam inye gyeik inya?”
JOH 6:26 Yesu lewexe, “A neil wou xam zonghek, xam seng wimexe ay en ingwei xam ghe wei dee wei lulvako yo, qe en ingwei xam ghe wa belet me e den xam o.
JOH 6:27 Xam seng bong xuk en lul yaeing wei mi wo nol o, qe en lul yaeing wei emi mendei mapieing luta luta yo, wei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek bong wou xam o. En moxo eno Ma Anutu beyal bei e bong lei ngandoung me bong ambei nyon.”
JOH 6:28 Woyom xel teling wou moxo, “Xa bong vati me na bong Anutu xe xuk?”
JOH 6:29 Yesu lewexe bei, “Anutu xe xuk eno nambei nye: Xam ghe bongis tambiy tiwei Anutu wong e lam o.”
JOH 6:30 Om xel teling wou e, “Tyek wang bong dee wei lulvako vati yo en xa ghei me na bongis wang? Tyek wang bo vati?
JOH 6:31 Xa bumiyeiw ya mana eivek tembuing bandaing, nambei xel byex eivek xoulek bei, ‘Moxo wong belet wei tyoung gheyapu yo me xel ya.’”
JOH 6:32 Yesu neil wou xel, “A neil wou xam zonghek, inye Mose se wong belet wei tyoung gheyapu eno wou xam, qe Mang wong belet zonghek wei tyoung gheyapu eno wou xam.
JOH 6:33 En belet wei Anutu xe eno inye e tiwei lam axone nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei me wong mapieing wou xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa yo.”
JOH 6:34 Xel neil embei, “Teiv, wa mi bong belet tiyon wou xa taxombouk.”
JOH 6:35 Woyom Yesu neilteyei bei, “A maxow belet wei mapieing o. Xelti embei nam wou ay eno tyek se na maxep, me xelti embei bongis ay eno tyek kwa se tip en memiing.
JOH 6:36 Ekom nambei a neil wou xam o, xam ghe wei ay ekom xam se ghei wongis.
JOH 6:37 Xel dalus wei Mang wong wou ay eno tyek nam wou ay, de xelti embei nam wou ay eno tyek a se saing xel.
JOH 6:38 En a lep me lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei en ambei se betiwou a maxow xe woueing nalei, qe woueing nalei wei tambiy tiwei wong a lam o.
JOH 6:39 De lalei vineing wei tambiy tiwei wong a lam eno nambei nye, tyek a se saing xel wei wong wou ay eno ti, qe tyek a piyexe xel lek bouk loxyus.
JOH 6:40 En Mang xe woueing nalei nambei nye xel eti yeiw wei yei Neu Moux me wongis e eno tyek na qou deing mapieing luta luta, de tyek a piyexe e lek bouk loxyus.”
JOH 6:41 Woyom Yudayeiw ngo inyon eno xel luk niseik seik en nambei moxo neil embei, “A belet wei lam axone nanghei tyoung gheyapu yo.”
JOH 6:42 Xel neil embei, “Beip inye se Yesu Yosep neu wei xey a woulek ma luw ta yo? Nambei nya gweimbeeng neil embei, ‘A lam axone nanghei tyoung gheyapu’?”
JOH 6:43 Ekom Yesu neil elox bei, “Xam tip lukeing ngenong on eivek xam venaxow senghoing.
JOH 6:44 Xelti tyek se nam wou ay qe ka Mang tiwei wong a lam eno na puw e nam le, de tyek a piyexe e qandi lek bouk loxyus.
JOH 6:45 Qayeeng yeip eivek xoulek wei xel poropet byex o bei, ‘Anutu tyek teyoxe xel.’ Xel eti yeiw wei mi ngo Mang me qou kwa wou e eno tyek nam wou ay.
JOH 6:46 Xelti se yei Mang. Qe e tiwei toundei is Anutu me lam eno emaxow yei Ma.
JOH 6:47 A neil wou xam zonghek, e tiwei mi wongis eno qou mapieing luta luta.
JOH 6:48 A maxow belet wei mapieing o.
JOH 6:49 Xam bumimyeiw ya mana eivek tembuing bandaing, ekom xel mey.
JOH 6:50 Ekom inye belet wei lam axone nanghei tyoung gheyapu, bei xomaxoneing gya dom xel se mey.
JOH 6:51 A maxow belet wei mapieing wei lam axone nanghei tyoung gheyapu yo. Wangwei xelti embei gya belet tine, on tyek mendei mapieing luta luta. Belet tine inye a leyeis, wei tyek a bong bei embong mapieing wou xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa yo.”
JOH 6:52 Woyom Yudayeiw di pyalek ama eivek xel venaxow senghoing me neil, “Nambei nya tambiy tine tyek bong emaxow leyeis me xey a gha?”
JOH 6:53 Yesu neil wou xel, “A neil wou xam zonghek, wangwei xam ambei seng gwa Xomaxoneing Neu Moux leyeis me na num e gyand ond xam seng qou mapieing eivek xow.
JOH 6:54 Xelti embei gya a leyeis me na num a gyand on tyek na qou mapieing luta luta, de tyek a piyexe e lek bouk loxyus.
JOH 6:55 En a leyeis on yaeing zonghek me a gyand on numeing zonghek.
JOH 6:56 Xelti embei gya a leyeis me na num a gyand yond mindei eivek ay de a mindei eivek e.
JOH 6:57 Nambei ingwei Mang wei mapieing eno wong a lam me a toundei mapieing en Mang, om xelti embei gya a leyeis on tyek mendei mapieing en ay.
JOH 6:58 Tine inye belet wei lam axone nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei yo. Xam bumimyeiw ya mana de mey, ekom xelti embei gya belet tine ond tyek mendei mapieing luta luta.”
JOH 6:59 Yesu neil lul tine gyeik ingwei di teyoxe xel eivek xomek qekueing ama nanghei Kapenaom o.
JOH 6:60 Xel ngo inyon de e xe xel betiyeing ngenong neil, “Teyoxeing on wo nimaying. Eti tyek na zeimaxoun inyon?”
JOH 6:61 Yesu woulek bei e xe xel betiyeing di luk ngenong en tine, om Yesu neil wou xel, “Qayeeng tine wo nol wou xam laleimim?
JOH 6:62 Wangwei xam ghe gwei ingwei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux nox me na tyoung gheyapu wei mindei takwei yo on tyek xam ghe bou naleimim ambei nya?
JOH 6:63 Laweeng mi wong mapieing wou moux alis vex. Xe neing se teyei bei devind xey. Qayeeng beimambei wei a neil wou xam eno inyon laweeng me xel on mapieing.
JOH 6:64 Ekom xam valu seng wongis.” En myaxeeng eno Yesu woulek e tiwei se wongis o me tyek na toung e na eivek xel ba memend o.
JOH 6:65 Moxo tetulexe me neil embei, “Inye vati wei a neil wou xam bei xelti se teyei bei nam wou ay, qe ka Mang bo nikanzek wou e le.”
JOH 6:66 Lek bouk tiyon eno e xe xel betiyeing ngenongakes pekwi me lox me la de xel se betiwou e no.
JOH 6:67 Yesu teling wou e xe xel betiyeing xoumeeng yuw on bei, “Xam is xam ambeing na veil ay?”
JOH 6:68 Simon Petele lewexe wou e, “Tambiy Ngandoung, tyek xa na wou eti? Wa xe qayeeng on mi wo mapieing luta luta.
JOH 6:69 Xa wongis me na woulek bei wang on Vambuing tiwei Anutu yo.”
JOH 6:70 Woyom Yesu neil elox bei, “A beyal xam xoumeeng yuw. Ekom xam on ti eno laweeng nol!”
JOH 6:71 Moxo neil inyon en Yudas wei Simon Iskariot neu moux o, inyon xel xoumeeng yuw eno ti, wei tyek na neil e teyei me na toung e na eivek xel ba memend o.
JOH 7:1 Ka tine la veil eno Yesu la di ghavineeng eivek Galili, en embei se nox Yudia en Yudayeiw embei nyeis e mey.
JOH 7:2 Ekom gyeik ingwei xel Yudayeiw xe Bouk ngandoung wei Xomek Laweeng eno paviy,
JOH 7:3 om Yesu liyeiw neil wou e, “Wang na veil Galili me ghe na Yudia, en kandek wa xe xel betiyeing gyei lulvako wei wa being bong o.
JOH 7:4 Wangwei xelti embei xomaxoneing boulek bei e lei ngandoung on se mi wong xuk eivek xupekeing. Wangwei wa being bong lulti beimambei yon, ond wa talex xow wou xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa nei.”
JOH 7:5 Embong emaxow liyeiw le, ekom xel se wongis e.
JOH 7:6 Nambei nyon Yesu neil wou xel, “A xe bouk se ghei lam, qe bouk dalus ne eno inye xam xe bouk nimza.
JOH 7:7 Xel xomaxoneing wei tembuing ne eno se teyei bei bo nol wou xam, qe xel mi wo nol wou ay en a mi neil kwa nilul wei xel mi wong o teyei.
JOH 7:8 Xam ghe na Bouk ngandoung on. Dom tyek a se zek me nana Bouk ngandoung tiyon, en nambei a xe bouk se ghei lam.”
JOH 7:9 Ka neil ambei nyon wou xel woy, dom toundei Galili.
JOH 7:10 Ka liyeiw la Bouk ngandoung veil, om moxo la is ambei nyon, se la yanyateiv, qe la xupekeing.
JOH 7:11 De eivek Bouk ngandoung eno teivateiv wei Yudayeiw toundei me di yei e teyei teyei me teling bei, “Tambiy tiwei yo inya?”
JOH 7:12 Eivek xel wei qekuma yon senghoing eno xel di ngoung lumama wouma me luk en moxo. Xel valu neil embei, “Moxo nimza.” De xel valu neil elox bei, “ Ma, tambiy on mi tyoxe xomaxoneing.”
JOH 7:13 Ekom xelti se neil lulti yeip yaing lek moxo en xel yaleeng en teivateiv wei Yudayeiw o.
JOH 7:14 Eivek bouk senghoing wei Bouk ngandoung eno Yesu lek me la eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o me di teyoxe moux alis vex.
JOH 7:15 De Yudayeiw etek me teling bei, “Tambiy nei qou lupeyei nei nambei nya moxo se wevek ti?”
JOH 7:16 Yesu lewexe, “A xe teyoxeing ne inye se a maxow xe. Qe inye lam wou tiwei wong a lam o.
JOH 7:17 Wangwei xelti beyal bei bong e teyei lek Anutu lalei ond tyek gyei bei teyoxeing wei a ne lam wou Anutu, o a di neil angya a maxow kwang.
JOH 7:18 Xelti embei neil qayeeng angya emaxow xe kwa ond inyon mi sanghoxe xow, ekom xelti embei bong xuk me sanghoxe tiwei wong e lam o lei, ond inyon tambiy wei zonghek o. De tyonyeing ma veil e.
JOH 7:19 Beip Mose se wong petieing wou xam? Ekom xam ti seng mi betiwou. Nambei nya xam a being nyeis a mey?”
JOH 7:20 Xel wei qekuma yon lewexe bei, Memo ti nale eivek wang. “Eti embei nyeis wang?”
JOH 7:21 Yesu neil wou xel, “A wong lulvako ti eno xam dalus ghe etek.
JOH 7:22 Mose wong kwa wei ghuweing ninavi yo, ekom inyon Mose venaxow se wong kwa yon qe inyon lam wou xe bundyeiw, om xam ghe mi ghuw yak ninavi lek bouk wei Sabat o.
JOH 7:23 Wangwei xam ambei mi ghuw yakyeis ninavi lek bouk wei Sabat o en kandek xam se pyalek Mose xe petieing, on nambei nya xam laleimim mi wo vanei wou ay en ingwei ambei bong tambiy ti bo nimzalek Sabat o?
JOH 7:24 Xam a tip pepyawexeing lul wei xam a being gwei nangya mamim o, de xam pepyawexe en sakwaing bombek.”
JOH 7:25 En qes tiyon xomaxoneing valu wei Yerusalem nei teling, “Beip inyei tambiy tiwei xel embei nyeis e mey o?
JOH 7:26 Inye moxo di luk wou xel yanyateiv me xel di yei me ngo e ekom xelti se nale zeyi e, en beip xel gyovaxa woulek neing bei e Kilisi?
JOH 7:27 Ekom xey a woulek ingwei tambiy tine lam anghei yo, de gyeik ingwei Kilisi embei nam eno tyek xelti se boulek ingwei lam anghei yo.”
JOH 7:28 Woyom Yesu nanghei di teyoxe xel eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o, me taxe bei, “Ee, xam ghe woulek ay, me xam ghe woulek ingwei a lam anghei yo? A se lam inye nangya a venaxow xe woueing nalei, qe tambiy tiwei wong a lam eno inye zonghek. De xam seng woulek e,
JOH 7:29 ekom a woulek e en nambei a lam anghei ingwei e toundei nei de moxo wong a lam.”
JOH 7:30 Gyeik ingwei Yesu neil tiyon eno xel di wong me yei en xel embei zeimaxoun moxo, ekom xelti se ax mema lek e en nambei moxo xe bouk se ghei lam.
JOH 7:31 Moux alis vex ngenong wei toundei eivek qekueing ama yon eno wongis Yesu. Xel neil embei, “Gyeik ingwei Kilisi embei nam eno tyek bong dee wei lulvako yo ngenong ghanaw tambiy tine?”
JOH 7:32 De xel Parisi ngo ingwei moux alis vex di ngoung wouma en lul wei e wong o. Woyom xel lumuki leitata yo me xel Parisi wong xel belimbo wei mi yeiteyei xomek vambuing eno la en xel embei na zeimaxoun e.
JOH 7:33 Yesu neil embei, “Tyek a toumendei bouk sepika is xam, dekakom nana wou tambiy tiwei wong a lam o.
JOH 7:34 Tyek xam ghe gwimexe ay, ekom tyek xam seng gweiwou ay, me ingwei a la toundei nei, eno xam seng teyei being nam.”
JOH 7:35 De Yudayeiw di neil wouma bei, “Tambiy tine tyek na inya me xe se ghei e? Tyek moxo na wou xel wei xey o, wei xel mindei lala eivek xel Grik senghoing o me teyoxe xel Grik?
JOH 7:36 Moxo neil tine en qes ambei nya gyeik ingwei e neil embei, ‘Tyek xam ghe gwimexe ay ekom tyek xam seng gweiwou ay,’ me ‘Ingwei a la toundei nei, eno tyek xam seng nam?’”
JOH 7:37 Lek bouk ngandoung tiwei yus o, eno Yesu nale me taxe bei, “Wangwei xelti kwa tip en memiing ond wong e lam wou ay me num.
JOH 7:38 Xelti embei bongis ay nambei Xoulek neil o, on tyek memiing veleivlei wei mapieing eno mendi na eivek e lalei me qapyex me na.”
JOH 7:39 Ekom neil en Laweeng wei xelti embei bongis e eno tyek na qou yo. De ela tyip bouk tine eno Laweeng seng ghei lam, en Yesu seng ghei wo lei ngandoung.
JOH 7:40 Xel ngo e xe qayeeng tiyon, eno xomaxoneing valu neil embei, “Neing ayang tambiy tiyon Poropet.”
JOH 7:41 De xel valu neil embei, “Moxo Kilisi.” De xel valu teling bei, “Nambei nya Kilisi tyek nam anghei Galili?
JOH 7:42 Beip xoulek se neil embei Kilisi tyek nam eivek Dawit neumambu me nam anghei Betelem, beyeeng wei Dawit mindei lek o?”
JOH 7:43 En nambei Yesu om xomaxoneing dembuma.
JOH 7:44 Xel valu embei zeimaxoun e, ekom xelti se ax mema lek moxo.
JOH 7:45 Se denlek en xel belimbo wei xomek vambuing o lox me la wou xel lumuki leitata yo me Parisiyeiw, xel teling wou xel, “Nambei nya xam seng qou e me ghe lam lalei?”
JOH 7:46 Xel belimbo neilteyei bei, “Xelti se mi neil qayeeng ambei tambiy tine.”
JOH 7:47 Xel Parisi neil wou xel bei, “Moxo tyoxe xam is ambei nyon?
JOH 7:48 Beip xam ghe wei bei xel gyovaxa me xel Parisi ti wongis e?
JOH 7:49 Ma! Ekom xel qendu tiyon se woulek lulti eivek petieing. Om tyek Anutu bong myaveweeng wou xel.”
JOH 7:50 Nikodimas, tambiy tiwei la wou Yesu takwei eno inyon ingwei xel o ti, om teling,
JOH 7:51 “Beip petieing wei xey o neil embei xey a bo qayeeng en xelti bandaing? Ma, myaxeeng eno xey a ngo e xe qayeeng me na ghei bei e wong vati?”
JOH 7:52 Xel neil elox bei, “Wang on Galili is? Wimexe e wo nimza eivek Anutu xe qapiya me wei, Poropet ti tyek se nam eivek Galili.”
JOH 7:53 Woyom xel titi lox me la bend bend.
JOH 8:1 Ekom Yesu la lukendu Oliv.
JOH 8:2 Ka satiboukeing lul eno moxo lox me la tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o no, me xomaxoneing qekuma vivekwou e, de moxo dei me di teyoxe xel.
JOH 8:3 De xel putoung wei petieing o me xel Parisi yei vex wei mi wong kwapesiv o ti me qou me lam. Xel wong vexo nale wou xomaxoneing wei toundei eivek qendu yon mend
JOH 8:4 me neil wou Yesu, “Putoung, xa xei vex tine wo kwapesiv.
JOH 8:5 Eivek petieing eno Mose neil embei xey a banex vex ambei nye en qakous me e mey. Wambei neil vati?”
JOH 8:6 Xel wong telinyeing tiyon wou e nambei lepulek, en xel di yimexe qes wei xel embei bong qayeeng en e yo. Ekom Yesu dundek me di byex lek tembuing en mema deyis.
JOH 8:7 Xel di embek teling e ngenong om moxo nale ghey me neil wou xel, “Wangwei xelti se mi bong sewokeing nei ond e banex vexo en qakous atax.”
JOH 8:8 Moxo lox me la dundek no me di byex lek tembuing.
JOH 8:9 Xel ngo qayeeng on eno xel titi la veil inyon xel wei vakovek qes ngenong eno la tax de xel valu la yus. Dom Yesu venaxow toundei de vex on toukale inyon.
JOH 8:10 Yesu nale ghey me teling wou vexo bei, “Vex, xel la inya? Beip xelti se toundei bei bo qayeeng en wang?”
JOH 8:11 Vexo neil embei, “Ma, teiv, xelti se toundei.” Woyom Yesu neilteyei bei, “Ay is ambei nyon a se wo qayeeng en wang. La de wa seng nox me na bong sewokeing no.”
JOH 8:12 Yesu lox me la luk wou xomaxoneing no, eno moxo neil embei, “A xeiyaing wei tembuing o. Xelti embei betiwou ay eno tyek se teyei bei na eivek mapetok, qe tyek na qou xeiyaing wei mapieing o.”
JOH 8:13 Xel Parisi neil wou moxo bei, “Wang mi neil xuk me kwa wei wamaxow o teyei, om qayeeng wei wang on se neing.”
JOH 8:14 Yesu lewexe bei, “Ee, a neil lulti beimambei ne lek venaxow, a xe qayeeng ne neing, en a woulek ingwei a lam anghei yo de ingwei ambei na yo. Ekom xam seng woulek ingwei a lam anghei yo me ingwei ambei na yo.
JOH 8:15 Xam ghe mi wo qayeeng en kwa wei xomaxoneing o, a se mi wo qayeeng en xelti.
JOH 8:16 Ekom wangwei ambei bo qayeeng en xelti, ond a xe qayeeng on zonghek, en nambei se a maxow, qe a mi nale is Mang, tiwei wong a lam o.
JOH 8:17 Eivek xam venaxow xe petieing eno xel byex ambei nye, wangwei tambiy yayuw embei neil qayeeng teyeima ond luw xe qayeeng on zonghek.
JOH 8:18 A maxow a mi neil qayeeng en venaxow, de tiwei mi yeimawou yo eno inye Mang tiwei wong a lam o.”
JOH 8:19 Woyom xel teling moxo, “Wa mam inya?” Yesu neil elox bei, “Xam seng woulek a Mang. Wangwei xam ghe boulek ay on tyek xam ghe boulek Mang is ambei nyon.”
JOH 8:20 Moxo neil qayeeng tine gyeik di teyoxe xel eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o paviy ingwei xel mi toung da eivek o. Ekom xelti se zeimaxoun e en nambei e xe bouk seng ghei lam.
JOH 8:21 Yesu neil no wou xel, “A la, dom tyek xam seng gwei ay, de tyek xam amey eivek sewokeing wei xam o. De ingwei ambei na nei eno tyek xam seng nam.”
JOH 8:22 Qayeeng tiyon wong Yudayeiw teling wouma bei, “Tyek moxo nyeis venaxow amey? Om neil embei, ‘Ingwei ambei na eno xam seng teyei bei nam’?”
JOH 8:23 Ekom Yesu tetulexe bei, “Xam on anghei nge xone de ay anghei nge gheyapu. Xam anghei tembuing de a se nanghei tembuing ne.
JOH 8:24 A neil wou xam woy bei tyek xam amey eivek xam xe sewokeing, wangwei xam seng bongis bei A Maxow Mindei Bei Nye, on tyek xam amey eivek sewokeing wei xam o.”
JOH 8:25 Xel teling, “Wang eti?” Yesu neil elox bei, “Kayon a neil wou xam myaxeeng eno.
JOH 8:26 A xe qayeeng ngenong di yeip en ingwei ambei neil me na bong qayeeng en xam o. Ekom tambiy tiwei wong a lam eno e xe kwa yon zonghek, yom vati wei a ngo wou e eno a neil wou xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa yo.”
JOH 8:27 Xel se woulek ingwei Yesu di neil wou xel en Ma yo.
JOH 8:28 Om Yesu neil embei, “Gyeik ingwei xam a zeim Xomaxoneing Neu Moux zekna, woyom tyek xam ghe boulek bei A maxow a mindei bei nye de a se mi wong lulti nangya kwang, qe a mi neil qayeeng nambei kawei Mang teyoxe wou ay yo.
JOH 8:29 Tambiy tiwei wong a lam eno mindei is ay, moxo se mi saing ay de a maxow a mindei, en a mi wong vatiyeiw wei e lalei vind o.”
JOH 8:30 Xomaxoneing ngo ingwei moxo neil ambei nyon, eno xel ngenong wongis e.
JOH 8:31 Yesu neil wou Yudayeiw wei wongis e yo bei, “Wangwei xam a zeimaxoun a xe qayeeng teyoxeing, ond neing ayang xam on a xe betiyeing.
JOH 8:32 Woyom tyek xam ghe boulek qayeeng zonghek, de qayeeng zonghek na tul xam ghe na nivax.”
JOH 8:33 Xel lewexe lek e bei, “Xa ne Apraham neumambu, xa se xukxe bandaing wei xelti yo. Nambei nya wang neimbei tyek xa na nivax?”
JOH 8:34 Yesu neil elox bei, “A neil zonghek wou xam, xel sapa wei mi wong sewokeing eno xel on xukxe bandaing wei sewokeing o.
JOH 8:35 Xukxe bandaing ti se mindei is mamata me neuyeiw takwei takwei qe neu mindei takwei takwei.
JOH 8:36 Om wangwei Neu Moux na tul xam ghe na nivax, ond xam ghe la nivax zonghek.
JOH 8:37 A woulek bei xam on velei wei Apraham o, ekom xam a being nyeis a mey, en nambei a xe qayeeng se yeip eivek xam laleimim.
JOH 8:38 A mi neil wou xam en vati wei a xei lam wou Mang o, de xam ghe mi wong vati wei xam ghe ngo wou xam mamim.”
JOH 8:39 Xel lewexe bei, “Apraham on xa mami.” Yesu neil embei, “Wangwei Apraham neuyeiw xam, woyom tyek xam ghe bong lul wei Apraham mi wong o.
JOH 8:40 A tambiy tiwei a mi neil qayeeng zonghek wei a ngo wou Anutu yo, ekom xam a being nyeis a mey. Apraham se mi wong kwa nambei nyon.
JOH 8:41 Xam ghe mi wong lulul wei xam venaxow mamim mi wong o.” Xel neil embei, “Xa tamiyeiw se wo kwapesiv me wou xa ti, qe Mang tixemou wei xa xe eno Anutu venaxow.”
JOH 8:42 Yesu neil wou xel, “Wangwei Anutu yon xam Mamim, on tyek xam laleimim devind ay, en a toundei is Anutu me na lam. A lam inye. A se lam angya a maxow kwang, qe moxo wong a lam.
JOH 8:43 Nambei nya a xe qayeeng se yeip yaing wou xam? En qes ambei nye xam seng teyei bei ngo vati wei a neil o.
JOH 8:44 Xam mamim on Sandang, me xam ambei mi bong kwa wei xam mamim mi wong o. Myaxeeng eno moxo mi leis xel mey, se mi zeim qayeeng zonghek, en inyei qayeeng zonghek se toundei eivek e. De mi neil qayeeng tyonyeing en inyon emaxow tyonyeing qes, en moxo tyonyeingana me wo ma en tyonyeing.
JOH 8:45 En nambei a mi neil qayeeng zonghek, ekom xam seng mi wongis ay!
JOH 8:46 Xel wei xam on valu yei bei a wong sewokeing? Wangwei a mi neil qayeeng zonghek, ond nambei nya xam seng wongis ay?
JOH 8:47 Tambiy tiwei Anutu xe eno mi ngo vati wei Anutu mi neil o. Xam on Anutu se xe en qes bei xam seng mi ngo vati wei e mi neil o.”
JOH 8:48 Yudayeiw lewexe wou moxo bei, “Xa neil neing en ingwei xa neimbei wa Samaria ti om memo ti nale eivek wang?”
JOH 8:49 Yesu neil embei, “Memo ti se toungale eivek ay ti, qe a mi sanghoxe mang lei de xam ghe mi beoux ay.
JOH 8:50 A se di ximexe lei ngandoung wei a maxow o. Qe inyei xelti di yimexe, de moxo inye tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng o.
JOH 8:51 Neing ayang a neil wou xam, wangwei xelti embei betiwou a xe qayeeng on tyek se teyei bei daxe meyeing.”
JOH 8:52 En tiyon eno xel Yudayeiw neil embei, “Gweimbeeng xa woulek bei memo dei eivek wang! Apraham mey me xel poropet is ambei nyon, de wang neimbei xelti embei betiwou wa xe qayeeng on tyek se teyei bei daxe meyeing.
JOH 8:53 Wang ghanaw xe mend Apraham? Moxo mey, me xel poropet is. Wang wou naleim bei wang eti?”
JOH 8:54 Yesu neil elox bei, “Wangwei a sanghoxe a maxow leing ond a leing on bandaing. Mang tiwei xam ghe neimbei xam xe Anutu eno mi sanghoxe a leing.
JOH 8:55 Xam seng woulek e, qe a woulek e. Wangwei a neimbei a se woulek e on a wo tyonyeing ambei xam, ekom a woulek e me na mi betiwou e xe qayeeng.
JOH 8:56 Xam bumim Apraham wo xeilala en embei gyei a xe bouk, moxo yei woy de wo xeilala.”
JOH 8:57 Yudayeiw neil wou moxo bei, “Wa xe vakovek qes se ghei la 50, de wang wei Apraham!”
JOH 8:58 Yesu lewexe bei, “A neil wou xam zonghek, takwei wei Apraham se ghei umbek eno A Maxow A Mindei.”
JOH 8:59 Woyom xel qou qakous en xel embei banex e, ekom Yesu xupek en xel me la myayaing veil tete wei xomek vambuing o.
JOH 9:1 Ka moxo di la, eno moxo yei moux ti matek gyeik umbek o.
JOH 9:2 Moxo xe xel betiyeing teling e, “Putoung, eti wong sewokeing, moux tine venaxow o ma luw ta, om ingwei matek gyeik umbek o?”
JOH 9:3 Yesu neil embei, “Moux tine se wong sewokeing o ma luw ta se wo sewokeing, qe lul tine qandi bei Anutu xe xuk e gyeip yaing eivek e xe mapieing.
JOH 9:4 Kawei bendiyeing ne eno xey a bong xuk wou tambiy tiwei wong a lam o. De boukeing nam eno xelti tyek se bong xuk.
JOH 9:5 Gyeik ingwei a toundei eivek tembuing sapa ne, eno a maxow xeiyaing wei tembuing sapa yo.”
JOH 9:6 Yesu neil ambei nyon, dom pesuv myalouk lek tembuing me wong e wo bandis de toung lek moux tiyon manghalus.
JOH 9:7 Moxo neil wou e, “La, wang na zipek eivek lounyeing wei Siloam nei” (qayeeng tiyon qes ambei inye wong e la). Om moux tiyon la lipek, de loum beeng eno manghalus yeila.
JOH 9:8 Moxo xe xel wei e beeng qes o me xel wei yei e takwei gyeik e mindei me tay lulul eno teling bei, “Beip inyei tambiy tiwei mindei me tay lulul o?”
JOH 9:9 Xel valu neil embei e inyon. De xel valu neil embei, “Ma, inye xel nge ekom ma nambei e.” Ekom moxo venaxow neil xow teyei bei, “Inye ay yo.”
JOH 9:10 Xel teling e, “Woyom nambei nya wa mamghalus yeila?”
JOH 9:11 Moxo neil elox bei, “Tambiy tiwei xel mi neil Yesu eno wong tembuing wo bandis me toung lek a mang. Moxo neil wou ay bei a na zipek anghei Siloam. Om a la lipek, de woyom a mang yeila.”
JOH 9:12 Xel teling e bei, “Moux tiyon inya?” Moxo neil embei, “A se woulek.”
JOH 9:13 Xel qou moux tiwei matekeing eno me la wou xel Parisi.
JOH 9:14 Bouk tiwei Yesu wong tembuing wo bandis me vindek moux tiyon malek eno inyon Sabat.
JOH 9:15 Om nambei nyon xel Parisi teling wou e no bei, “Nambei nya wa mam yeila?” Om moxo neil elox, “Moxo toung bandis lek a mang, me a lipek de gweimbeeng a mang yeila.”
JOH 9:16 Xel Parisi valu neil embei, “Tambiy tine se lam wou Anutu, en se betiwou petieing wei Sabat o.” Ekom xel valu teling, “Nambei nya xel wei sewokeing o tyek bong dee wei lulvako yo nambei nye?” Om xel dembuma.
JOH 9:17 Se denlek en xel pekwi mend wou moux matekeing on no, “Wambei neil ambei nya en e en ingwei wong wa mam yeila yo?” Moux tiyon neil elox bei, “Moxo poropet ti.”
JOH 9:18 Yudayeiw se ghei wongis bei moxo matek me mavindek lek, deka xel wo qayeeng la wou moux on ma luw ta wole.
JOH 9:19 Luw lam de xel teling wou luw, “Inye muw neumim? Inye tambiy tine muw ghe neimbei e matek gyeik umbek o? Nambei nya gweimbeeng e manghalus yeila?”
JOH 9:20 Ma luw ta lewexe bei, “Uw a woulek bei inye uw neumi, me uw a woulek bei umbek matekeing.
JOH 9:21 Ekom e yeila gweimbeeng ne nambei nya, o eti wong e ma yeila eno uw se woulek. Xam teling wou e. Moxo wo teiv om tyek na neil xow teyei.”
JOH 9:22 Moxo ma luw ta neil ambei nyon en luw yaleeng en Yudayeiw, en xel Yudayeiw tup qayeeng bei xelti embei neimbei Yesu e Kilisi, on tyek xel a tiy e veil xomek qekueing ama.
JOH 9:23 Inyon qes tiyon om ma luw ta neil embei, “Moxo wo teiv, om xam teling wou e.”
JOH 9:24 Om luyuw eno xel taxe moux tiwei matekeing o me neil wou, “Wa sanghoxe Anutu, en xa woulek bei tambiy tiyon mi wong sewokeing.”
JOH 9:25 Moxo neil elox bei, “Beip e mi wo sewokeing o ma, a se woulek. A woulek lulti bei a mang tek ekom gweimbeeng a mang yeila!”
JOH 9:26 Woyom xel teling wou e, “Moxo wong ambei nya wou wang? E wong wa mam yeila nambei nya?”
JOH 9:27 Moxo lewexe bei, “A neil wou xam woy ekom xam seng ngo. Nambei nya xam ambei ngo no? Xam a being bong ambei e xe betiyeing is?”
JOH 9:28 Woyom xel wo vyend wou e me neil embei, “Wang on tambiy tiyon xe betiyeing! De xa ne betiyeing wei Mose yo!
JOH 9:29 Xa woulek bei Anutu luk is Mose, ekom en tambiy tiyon, eno xa se woulek bei e lam anghei inya.”
JOH 9:30 De moux on lewexe bei, “Gweimbeeng xam ghe neil qayeeng on nelu ti! Xam seng woulek ingwei e lam anghei yo, qe moxo wong a mang yeila.
JOH 9:31 Xey a woulek bei Anutu se mi ngo xel wei sewokeing o. Qe moxo mi ngo xel wei mi wo lalo wou e me betiwou e yo.
JOH 9:32 Xelti se mi ngo ka bei, xelti wong tambiy wei umbek matekeing eno ma yeila.
JOH 9:33 Wangwei Anutu se bong tambiy tiyon nam, on tyek se bong lulti.”
JOH 9:34 Xel neil elox bei, “Sewokeing pup wang gyeik wang umbek o, wambei teyoxe xa!” De xel tiy moxo la.
JOH 9:35 Yesu ngo bei xel tiy e, de gyeik ingwei moxo yei e, eno neil wou bei, “Wang wongis Xomaxoneing Neu Moux?”
JOH 9:36 Moux on teling bei, “Teiv, tambiy tiyon eti? Wa neil wou ay en a bongis e yo.”
JOH 9:37 Yesu neil embei, “Gweimbeeng wang wei e, inye tambiy tiwei di luk is wang ne.”
JOH 9:38 Woyom moux on neil embei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, a wongis o,” de moxo wo lalo wou Yesu.
JOH 9:39 Yesu neil embei, “A lam eivek tembuing tine en qayeeng wongeing, en kandek xel wei mend tekeing eno gyeina de eti yeiw wei mend yeila eno tyek bo mend tekeing.”
JOH 9:40 Xel Parisi valu wei toundei is e eno ngo ingwei e neil ambei nyon om xel teling, “Vati? Wambei xa mami tek is?”
JOH 9:41 Yesu neil embei, “Wangwei xam mamim atek, on sewokeing ma veil xam, ekom xam ghe mi neimbei xam mamim yeila, om sewokeing nanghei di yeip wou xam.”
JOH 10:1 Yesu neil embei, “A neil wou xam zonghek, moux wei se la lox tete mya wei sipsip, qe lek wou tete nanghei ba nei me la lalei eno inyon panaxana me tambiy wei mi wo nol wou xel o.
JOH 10:2 De moux wei mi la lox tete mya eno inyon gyovaxa wei e xe sipsip o.
JOH 10:3 De tambiy tiwei mi yei tete mya teyei eno tax veil moxo, me sipsip mi ngo e vya. Moxo mi taxe e xe sipsip titi leind de mi dandiy xel me la myayaing.
JOH 10:4 Ka moxo qou e xe sipsip dalus me la myayaing, eno moxo mi la tax en xel, de e xe sipsip mi betiwou e en nambei xel woulek e vya.
JOH 10:5 Ekom xel se mi betiwou xel bange, xel mi pek en e en nambei xel se woulek xel bange vya.”
JOH 10:6 Yesu neil qayeeng pakeing tiyon wou xel, ekom xel se woulek vati wei moxo di neil wou xel o.
JOH 10:7 Dekalekom Yesu neil no, “A neil wou xam zonghek, a tete mya wei sipsip o.
JOH 10:8 Xel dalus wei lam a tax en ay eno panaxana me mi wo nol wou xel, ekom sipsip se mi ngo xel.
JOH 10:9 A tete mya, wangwei xelti embei nam wou ay me na eivek tete lalei on tyek Anutu devind e. Moxo tyek nam eivek lalei de doukna myayaing, me na qou lulul yaeing.
JOH 10:10 Panaxana mi lam en panaxeing tixemou me leiseing xel a mey me mi wo nol wou, ekom a lam bei xel a qou mapieing, me mapieing e pup xel.
JOH 10:11 “A maxow gyovaxa nimza wei sipsip o. Gyovaxa nimza wei sipsip eno mi saing e xe mapieing en sipsip.
JOH 10:12 De xukxe wei xel mi xouv e me e mi yeiteyei sipsip eno se gyovaxa wei wo ma en sipsip o, om gyeik ingwei yei naw bemeeng lam, eno saing sipsip de pek la. Woyom naw bemeeng nga sipsip de tiy xel vula.
JOH 10:13 De moux tiyon pek me la en nambei xel mi xouv en malew om se wounalei ngenong en sipsip.
JOH 10:14 “A maxow gyovaxa nimza wei sipsip o, a woulek a xe sipsip de a xe sipsip woulek ay,
JOH 10:15 nambei kawei Mang woulek ay de a woulek Mang. Me a saing a xe mapieing en sipsip.
JOH 10:16 A xe sipsip valu wei xel se mi nale eivek tete ne. Om a na qou xel me na nam is ambei nyon. De tyek xel a ngo a vyang is ambei nyon, me tyek xel bo sipsip qendu tixemou me gyovaxa wei sipsip o tixemou.
JOH 10:17 En qes tine om Mang lalei vind ay bei a saing a xe mapieing de na qou enoum no.
JOH 10:18 Xelti se zeim a xe mapieing veil ay, qe a maxow a zeim a xe mapieing veil. A ningkanzek teyei bei na zeim mapieing wei ay yo veil, de a ningkanzek teyei bei na qou enoum no. En Mang peti wou ay ambei nyon bei a bong.”
JOH 10:19 Lek qayeeng ti beimambei ne eno wong Yudayeiw dembuma no.
JOH 10:20 Xel ngenong neil embei, “Moxo memo nale eivek e me e wo bandol. Xam ambei ngo e enva?”
JOH 10:21 Ekom xel valu neil embei, “Inyei se qayeeng wei tambiy wei memo nale eivek o. Memo ti teyei lek bei bong xel wei matekeing o gyeina?”
JOH 10:22 Woyom bouk ngandoung wei lalo eno lam tyip en ingwei xel mi wou naleind en xomek vambuing wei xel wong wou Anutu nanghei Yerusalem o. Inyon bouk wei nityuweing o,
JOH 10:23 de Yesu toundei eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o me la di ghavineeng lek zek wei Salomo lei lek o.
JOH 10:24 De Yudayeiw lam nale vivekwou e, me neil embei, “Gyeik inya wa neil xow teyei? Wangwei bei inyon wa Kilisi, neilteyei wou xa.”
JOH 10:25 Yesu lewexe bei, “A neil wou xam woy, ekom xam seng wongis. De xuk wei a wong lek Mang lei eno neil a teyei,
JOH 10:26 ekom xam seng wongis en nambei xam on a se xe sipsip.
JOH 10:27 A xe sipsip mi ngo a vyang, me a woulek xel, de xel mi betiwou ay.
JOH 10:28 A wong deing mapieing luta luta wou xel, me tyek xel se teyei bei mey, de xelti tyek se tetei xel veil a memang.
JOH 10:29 Mang wei wong xel wou ay eno nikanzek ghanaw xel dalus, xelti tyek se tetei xel veil Mang mema.
JOH 10:30 Ay me Mang eno uw xouing tixemou.”
JOH 10:31 Xel Yudayeiw lox me la balu qakous no en xel embei banex e,
JOH 10:32 ekom Yesu neil wou xel, “A talex xuk nimza ngenong wei Mang o wou xam. En lul tina eno xam ambei banex ay en qakous?”
JOH 10:33 Xel Yudayeiw neil elox bei, “Xa bei se banex wang en qakous en xuk nimza wei wang wong on, qe en ingwei wang lukyak lek Anutu, en nambei wa xomaxoneing bandaing, ekom wang neimbei wa Anutu.”
JOH 10:34 Yesu lewexe wou xel, “Inye xel se byex eivek xam xe petieing, ‘A neimbei xam on anutuyeiw?’
JOH 10:35 Wangwei moxo na neimbei xel anutu yon inyon wou eti yeiw wei qou qayeeng wei Anutu yo om xoulek on tyek se pakei na ba nge.
JOH 10:36 Ekom nambei nya xam ghe neimbei a lukyak lek Anutu, en ingwei a neimbei ay Anutu Neu yo? Inye a tambiy tiwei Anutu beyal me wong e lam lek tembuing o.
JOH 10:37 Wangwei a se bong xuk wei Mang mi wong o ond xam seng bongis ay.
JOH 10:38 Ekom wangwei a bong e xe xuk, ek xam seng bongis ay, ond xam ghe bongis xuk wei ay yo me ghe boulek bei Mang toundei eivek a laleing, de a toundei eivek Mang lalei.”
JOH 10:39 Xel di wong me yei en xel embei zeimaxoun e no, ekom moxo ghanaw xel me la.
JOH 10:40 Woyom Yesu lox me la sek memiing Yorodan me la beyeeng wei Yoan lipek xel lek bouk myaxeeng o. Moxo toundei inyon
JOH 10:41 me xomaxoneing ngenong lam wou e. Xel neil embei, “Yoan se wong dee wei lulvako yo ti, qe lul dalus wei Yoan neil lek tambiy tine eno zonghek.”
JOH 10:42 De eivek beyeeng tiyon eno xel ngenongakes wongis Yesu.
JOH 11:1 Ekom inyei tambiy ti lei Laserus eno vanei wong. Moxo nanghei Betani, beyeeng wei Maria luw li vex Marata yo.
JOH 11:2 Maria tiyon, takwei eno taw wel xeimangou lek Tambiy Ngandoung me vu e vaxa en luvelus, eno li moux Laserus vanei wong me e di yeip.
JOH 11:3 Om li vex aluw wong qayeeng la wou Yesu bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, moux tiwei wa laleim vind eno vanei wong.”
JOH 11:4 Ka ingwei Yesu ngo inyon eno moxo neil embei, “Vanei yon se en ingwei xomaxoneing embei mey o. Ma, inyon embei talex Anutu xe nikanzek wou moux alis vex en xel bong e lei na, en kandek xel bong Anutu Neu Moux na qou lei ngandoung is.”
