JOH 11:5 Yesu lalei vind Marata me li vex me Laserus.
JOH 11:6 Ekom gyeik ingwei moxo ngo bei Laserus vanei wong, eno toundei inyon teyei lek bouk yuw is no.
JOH 11:7 Woyom moxo neil wou e xe xel betiyeing bei, “Xey ambei nox me na Yudia.”
JOH 11:8 Xel neil embei, “Putoung se ghei denlek ingwei Yudayeiw embei banex wang en qakous o ti, ekom wa being nox me na inyei no?”
JOH 11:9 Yesu lewexe, “Beip inye se seivma xoumeeng yuw lek bendiyeing ti? Tambiy tiwei mi velewexe bendiyeing eno se mi beng en mi yei tembuing xe xeiyaing.
JOH 11:10 Ekom gyeik ingwei e velewexe eivek boukeing eno tyek na beng en xeiyaing ma veil e.”
JOH 11:11 E neil tine dekakom moxo neil wou xel, “Xe xe gweleeng Laserus yeip, ekom ambei na inyei en nana piyexe e.”
JOH 11:12 E xe xel betiyeing neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wangwei emdi gyeip on tyek bo nimzalek.”
JOH 11:13 Yesu neil en ingwei e xe meyeing o, ekom e xe xel betiyeing embeik nge Laserus di yeip.
JOH 11:14 Om moxo neilteyei wou xel bei, “Laserus mey,
JOH 11:15 de en xam eno a wo xeinglala ngandoung en a se toundei inyei, om tyek xam ghe bongis. Ekom xey ambei na wou e.”
JOH 11:16 Woyom Tomas (wei xel mi neil Didimas) eno neil wou xel betiyeing valu bei, “Wong xey dalus a la, en nana mey is e yo.”
JOH 11:17 Gyeik Yesu la eivek Betani eno ngo bei Laserus mey woy me xel ev eivek leiveeng meyeing de bouk vey la veil.
JOH 11:18 Betani toundei paviy Yerusalem nambei kilomita yayal,
JOH 11:19 de xel Yudayeiw ngenong lam toundei is Marata luw Maria me byexaxoun luw en ingwei li moux mey o.
JOH 11:20 Marata ngo bei Yesu lam, eno la myayaing en embei na pelong e, dom Maria toundei eivek xomek.
JOH 11:21 Marata neil wou Yesu bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wangwei wa toumendei inye nei on tyek a ling se mey.
JOH 11:22 Ekom gweimbeeng a woulek bei Anutu tyek bong vati wei wambei teling wou e yo.”
JOH 11:23 Yesu neil wou vexo bei, “Wa lim moux tyek qandi lek no.”
JOH 11:24 Marata lewexe bei, “A woulek bei moxo tyek qandi lek no eivek bouk loxyus wei xel embei qandi lek o.”
JOH 11:25 Yesu neil wou vexo bei, “A maxow qandieing lek me mapieing qes. Xelti embei bongis ay eno tyek na toumendei mapieing gyeik e mey o,
JOH 11:26 de xel eti yeiw wei toundei mapieing me wongis ay eno tyek se teyei bei mey. Beip wang wongis tine?”
JOH 11:27 Marata neil wou Yesu bei, “Ee, Tambiy Ngandoung, a wongis bei wa Kilisi, Anutu Neu Moux, tambiy tiwei embei nam lek tembuing o.”
JOH 11:28 Deka Marata neil tine, eno lox me la taxe li Maria la nenyawes. De ngoung wou e, “Putoung lam toundei inye me di teling en wang.”
JOH 11:29 Maria ngo tine, eno vexo qandi lek daing me la wou Yesu.
JOH 11:30 Yesu seng ghei la eivek beyeeng, qe nanghei toundei beyeeng wei Marata la pelong e yo.
JOH 11:31 Xel Yudayeiw wei toundei is Maria eivek xomek me ghanduxoun e, eno yei ingwei vexo qandi lek daing me la myayaing om xel betiy e, xel embeik nge embei na bo talot anghei ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei.
JOH 11:32 Maria la tyip beyeeng wei Yesu toundei yo me yei e, eno vexo ev vaxakatu eivek wou moxo vaxa me neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wangwei wa toumendei inye nei on tyek a ling moux se mey.”
JOH 11:33 Yesu yei ingwei vexo eng, me Yudayeiw wei lam is e eno di eng is, om moxo lalei pyaxow me embei deeng.
JOH 11:34 Moxo teling bei, “Xam ghe liw e nanghei inya?” Xel neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, lam me wei.”
JOH 11:35 Yesu eng.
JOH 11:36 Woyom Yudayeiw neil embei, “Xam wei ingwei moxo lalei mi vind e mouyo!”
JOH 11:37 Ekom xel valu neil embei, “Tambiy tine mi wong xel wei mentekeing eno mi yeila, ekom nambei nya se teyei bei devind tambiy tine veil meyeing?”
JOH 11:38 Yesu lalei pyaxow no me la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei. Inyei eeng wei xel kwelexe eivek qakous me lax mya zeyi yo.
JOH 11:39 Moxo neil embei, “Xam wo qakous veil.” Marata wei li moux mey eno neil embei, “Ekom Tambiy Ngandoung, tyek bo niliy, en yeip inyon bouk vey la veil o.”
JOH 11:40 Woyom Yesu neil embei, “Beip a se neil wou wang bei wangwei wang bongis, on tyek wang gwei Anutu xe nikanzek ngandoung?”
JOH 11:41 Om xel qepei qakous veil. Woyom Yesu veilma lek me neil embei, “Mang, a wong dange wou wang en wang mi ngo ay.
JOH 11:42 A woulek bei taxombouk eno wang mi ngo ay, ekom a neil inye en nimza wei xomaxoneing wei toungale inye, bei xel bongis bei wang wong a lam.”
JOH 11:43 Ka Yesu neil tine woy, eno taxe xoulekeing bei, “Laserus, lam myayaing!”
JOH 11:44 Moux wei mey eno lam myayaing, xel beliv e mema luw me vaxa luw en qaeing de beliv qaeing vivekwou e ma. Yesu neil wou xel “Xam tul qaeing wei leiveeng meyeing eno veil de wong e la.”
JOH 11:45 Nambei nyon om Yudayeiw ngenong wei lam toundei is Maria, eno yei vati wei Yesu wong, om xel wongis e.
JOH 11:46 Ekom xel wei xel eno valu la neil wou xel Parisi en vati wei Yesu wong o.
JOH 11:47 Woyom xel lumuki leitata yo is Parisiyeiw taxe qekueing ama wei kanzol o. Xel teling bei, “Tyek xey a bong ambei nya? Tambiy tine wong dee wei lulvako yo ngenong.
JOH 11:48 Wangwei xey a bong emdi bong ambei nyon, on tyek xel dalus bongis e. De woyom tyek xel Rom nam lelolexe xe xe xomek vambuing de na qou xomaxoneing wei tembuing ne is.”
JOH 11:49 Woyom xel wei xel on ti, e lei Kaiapas, moxo wo lumuki lukanzek lek vakovek qes tiyon, eno luk wou xel bei, “Xam lumimpeyei se woulek lulti!
JOH 11:50 Xam seng woulek bei inye nimza wou xam en ingwei tambiy ti e mey en xomaxoneing dalus enok xel dalus wei tembuing tine eno na mey.”
JOH 11:51 Moxo se neil inyon nangya kwa, qe wo lumuki lukanzek lek vakovek qes tiyon om neil qayeeng poropet lek ingwei Yesu tyek na mey en xel wei Yudayeiw o,
JOH 11:52 De se en Yudayeiw venaxow qe en Anutu neuyeiw wei toundei lala yo en embei qeku xel dalus lekti me xel bo tixemou.
JOH 11:53 Om gyeik bouk kayon me e di la eno xel di luklek sakwaing wei xel embei nyeis Yesu e mey yo.
JOH 11:54 Nambei nyon om Yesu se lox me la ghavineeng yanyateiv eivek xel Yudayeiw senghoing. Moxo la veil inyon me la beyeeng wei di yeip paviy tembuing bandaing o, la beyeeng wei xel mi neil Epraim nei, me moxo is e xe xel betiyeing la mindei inyon.
JOH 11:55 Bouk la paviy Yudayeiw xe Pasova, om xel ngenong wei tembuing danghei danghei nei lek me la Yerusalem en embei na bo xow bo vako natax en Pasova.
JOH 11:56 Xel di yimexe Yesu, deka xel toukale eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing eno xel di teling wouma, “Xam ghe wou naleimim neing bei moxo tyek nam gyei bouk dalus wei Pasova ne?”
JOH 11:57 Ekom xel lumuki leitata me Parisiyeiw neil wou moux alis vex bei wangwei xelti boulek ingwei Yesu toundei yo, ond e neil wou xel en xel na zeimaxoun e.
JOH 12:1 Bouk limti nanghei di yeip zeyi Pasova, om Yesu la toundei Betani wei Laserus mindei lek o, inyon tambiy tiwei Yesu piyexe e qandi lek veil meyeing o.
JOH 12:2 Xel wo xeindlala en Yesu me wo mata ti wou e. Marata di duw yaeing, de Laserus toundei senghoing is xel wei di ya lek lelek is e yo.
JOH 12:3 Woyom Maria qou wel xeimangou wei malew ngandoung en o veweeng me taw lek Yesu vaxa de vu e vaxa nangya venaxow luvelus. Me xomek pup en wel on xeimangou.
JOH 12:4 Ekom e xe betiyeing ti, Yudas Iskariot, wei tyek na neil e teyei me na toung e na eivek xel ba memend loxyus o, eno neil embei,
JOH 12:5 “Nambei nya wel xeimangou ne xey se wo vateivek lek me na qou malew selewa vaxak yal lek en na bo wou xel kanyo?”
JOH 12:6 Tambiy on se neil inyon en embei devind xel kanyo, qe nambei moxon panaxana, moxo mi yeiteyei qoupek malew wei xel o, om mi panax malew wei xel mi toung eivek o.
JOH 12:7 Yesu neil elox bei, “Wong vex on venaxow toundei, inye wo bombek bei zeimaxoun wel xeimangou yon bei menyex wou a neing en bouk wei eveing o.
JOH 12:8 Xel kanyo tyek na mi mendei eivek xam senghoing taxombouk, ekom tyek a se mendei is xam taxombouk.”
JOH 12:9 Dekalekom xel qendu ngandoung wei Yudayeiw eno ngo bei Yesu toundei Betani om xel la, se en e maxow qe xel embei na gyei Laserus tambiy tiwei Yesu piyexe e veil meyeing o.
JOH 12:10 Om xel lumuki leitata di luklek inye en xel embei nyeis Laserus a mey is,
JOH 12:11 en nambei xel wounaleind en ingwei Yesu wong wou Laserus, om xel ngenong wei Yudayeiw eno di la wou Yesu me wongis e.
JOH 12:12 Bouk nge eno xel qendu ngandoung wei lam en Pasova eno ngo bei Yesu di lam Yerusalem.
JOH 12:13 Xel qou zangholeng mema me la myayaing en xel embei na pelong e, xel di taxe bei, “Hosana!” “Mata ena wou tambiy tiwei lam lek Tambiy Ngandoung lei yo!” “Mata ena wou king wei Israel xe yo!”
JOH 12:14 Yesu yei dongi lingheing ti me dei lek, nambei xel byex eivek xoulek o,
JOH 12:15 “Sayon neu vex wa seng gwaleeng, wei, wa xe king di lam, Moxo dei lek dongi lingheing ti.”
JOH 12:16 Myaxeeng eno e xe xel betiyeing se woulek lulti beimambei ne dalus qes. Qe ka Anutu wo lei ngandoung wou Yesu, om xel woulek xoulek wei yeip eivek qapiya yo, me xel wou naleind en lulti beimambei wei xel wong woy wou e yo.
JOH 12:17 Nanghei inyei eno xel qendu ngandoung wei toundei is e gyeik ingwei moxo taxe Laserus nanghei leiveeng meyeing me e qandi lek me lam veil meyeing eno xel di tetulexe qayeeng on lala.
JOH 12:18 En qes tine is ambei nyon xomaxoneing ngenong la pelong e en xel ngo ingwei e wong dee wei lulvako yo.
JOH 12:19 Om xel Parisiyeiw di neil wouma bei, “Wei, xey se teyei bei bo lulti. Xam ghe wei kwa yon, xel dalusateiv wei tembuing sapa eno la betiwou e.”
JOH 12:20 Xel Grik valu lam toundei senghoing eivek moux alis vex wei lam tyip en embei nam bo lalo lek bouk ngandoung tine yo.
JOH 12:21 Xel lam wou Pilip, tambiy wei nanghei Betsaida eivek Galili yo. Xel neil embei, “Teiv, xa bei ghei Yesu.”
JOH 12:22 Pilip la neil wou Andrias, de Andrias aluw Pilip la neil wou Yesu.
JOH 12:23 Yesu neil elox wou luw, “Bouk la wou eivek en ingwei Xomaxoneing Neu Moux embei bo lei ngandoung o.
JOH 12:24 A neil wou xam zonghek, Wangwei wit vei se detei lek tembuing me na mey, on tyek na toumendei nambei vei tixemou. Ekom wangwei e mey, on tyek bo vei ngenong.
JOH 12:25 Tambiy ti embei lalei devind mapieing wei e yo on tyek na saing e xe mapieing, ek wangwei tambiy ti embei toung demi wou e xe mapieing lek tembuing tine on tyek na zeimaxoun e xe mapieing luta luta.
JOH 12:26 Xelti embei bong a xe xuk ond e mi betiwou ay, me beyeeng wei ambei mendei eno a xe xukxe tyek mendei is ay. De Mang tyek bo lei ngandoung wou tambiy tiwei embei bong a xe xuk o.
JOH 12:27 “Gweimbeeng a laleing wo maying, me tyek a neil ambei nya? ‘Mang, wa devind a lek seivma tine’? Ma, a se neil ambei nye. En lek qes tiyon om a lam lek seivma tine.
JOH 12:28 Mang, wang bo leim bo ngandoung!” Woyom vya ti lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei bei, “A wong e wo ngandoung woy, me tyek a bong embo ngandoung no.”
JOH 12:29 Om xel qendu ngandoung wei toukale inyon ngo vya ti me neil embei dewek toung, de valu neil embei angela ti luk is e.
JOH 12:30 Yesu neil embei, “Vya tine embei devind xam, de se ay.
JOH 12:31 Gweimbeeng inye bouk wei Anutu embei bong qayeeng en tembuing tine, de tyek na tiy gyovaxa tiwei mi yeiteyei tembuing tine yo na.
JOH 12:32 Ekom Ay, eno wangwei xel a zeim a zekna veil tembuing, on tyek a puw moux alis vex dalus noum wou xow.”
JOH 12:33 Moxo neil tiyon en embei talex ingwei tyek na mey ambei nya yo.
JOH 12:34 Xel qendu ngandoung on neil embei, “Xa ngo eivek petieing bei Kilisi tyek na mi mendei luta luta, om nambei nya wang neimbei, ‘Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek xel a zeim e zekna’? Inyon ‘Xomaxoneing eti Neu Moux’?”
JOH 12:35 Woyom Yesu neil wou xel bei, “Tyek xeiyaing a toumendei is xam bouk sepika. Om xam a mi na eivek xeiyaing, enok mapetok nam sevun xam. Tambiy wei mi la eivek mapetok eno se mi woulek ingwei embei na yo.
JOH 12:36 Xam a mi bongis xeiyaing wei xam ghe qou yo. En kandek xam ghe bo xeiyaing neuyeiw.” Yesu luk woy, eno moxo la veil xel de la xupek en xel.
JOH 12:37 Yesu wong dee wei lulvako beimambei yon wou xel mend woy, ekom xel se wongis e.
JOH 12:38 Tiyon wo neing lek nambei qayeeng wei poropet Yesaya yo: “Tambiy ngandoung, eti wongis xa xe qayeeng me Tambiy Ngandoung mema talex lulul tine lam yanyateiv wou eti?”
JOH 12:39 En qes tiyon om moux alis vex se teyei bei bongis, en nambei Yesaya byex eivek qayeeng nge bei:
JOH 12:40 “Moxo wong xel mend tek Me wong xel laleind wo nikanzek, enok xel mend gyeina, o xel boulek eivek laleind, o xel pekwi me noum me a bong xel bo nimzalek.”
JOH 12:41 Yesaya neil tine en nambei moxo yei Yesu xe xeiyaing ngandoung om neil inyon en e.
JOH 12:42 Neing, xel gyovaxa ngenong wei Yudayeiw o wongis Yesu. Ekom nambei xel Parisi om xel se neil xel xe wongeingis teyei en xel yaleeng enok xel a tiy xel veil xomek qekueing ama.
JOH 12:43 En xel laleind mi vind ingwei moux alis vex mi sanghoxe xel ghanaw ingwei Anutu mi sanghoxe yo.
JOH 12:44 Woyom Yesu taxe bei, “Wangwei xelti embei bongis ay, ond moxo se wongis a maxow, qe wongis tambiy tiwei wong a lam o.
JOH 12:45 De moxo embei gyei ay, ond moxo yei tambiy tiwei wong a lam o.
JOH 12:46 A lam tembuing ne nambei xeiyaing, en kandek xel wei wongis ay eno tyek se mendei eivek mapetok.
JOH 12:47 “En nambei xelti embei ngo a xe qayeeng ekom se betiwou, ond tyek a se bong qayeeng en e. En a se lam en ambei bong qayeeng en moux alis vex wei tembuing o, qe ambei devind xel veil nilul.
JOH 12:48 Inyei tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng o ti toundei en embei bong qayeeng en tiwei se ngo ay me se qou a xe qayeeng o, qayeeng wei a mi neil eno tyek bo qayeeng en e lek bouk loxyus.
JOH 12:49 En a se mi neil inyon nangya kwang, qe Mang tiwei wong a lam eno peti wou ay en vati wei ambei neil me kwa wei ambei neil o.
JOH 12:50 A woulek bei e xe petieing on mapieing luta luta. Om vati wei a mi neil eno mi la nambei ingwei Mang neil wou ay bei a neil o.”
JOH 13:1 Inye bouk paviy mata wei Pasova yo. Yesu woulek bei bouk lam en ingwei embei na veil tembuing me na wou Ma yo. Moxo lalei vind emaxow xe xel wei toundei lek tembuing o, me e lam gweimbeeng ne eno moxo lalei vind xel ghanaw veil.
JOH 13:2 De soukeing wei xel di ya eno Sandang toung kwa eivek Yudas Iskariot, Simon neu woy, bei e toung Yesu na eivek xel ba memend.
JOH 13:3 Yesu woulek bei ma toung lulul dalus la eivek e xe nikanzek xeinghembi, me ingwei Anutu wong e lam me ingwei tyek nox me na wou Anutu yo,
JOH 13:4 om moxo qandi lek veil yaeing, me kwax e xe teimb ding veil, de vex vetivek ti vivekwou xeikatu.
JOH 13:5 Kalekom moxo taw memiing lek dipekta ti de mouk sekweyexe e xe xel betiyeing vaxend, me vu xel vaxend nangya vetivek wei vex evivekwou xeikatu yo.
JOH 13:6 Moxo lam wou Simon Petele, e tiwei neil wou bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, inye wa being zipek a vaxang?”
JOH 13:7 Yesu neil elox bei, “Wa seng woulek vati wei a wong gweimbeeng ne, qe kalekom tyek wang boulek loxyus.”
JOH 13:8 Petele neil embei, “Ma, wa seng teyei bei sekweyexe a vaxang se teyei.” Yesu lewexe bei, “Wangwei a se sekweyexe wang, on a se xe wang.”
JOH 13:9 Woyom Simon Petele neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wangwei nambei nyon nei on wa se sekweyexe a vaxang venaxow qe a memang me a lung is ambei nyon!”
JOH 13:10 Yesu neil embei, “Tambiy wei lipek woy eno tyek zipek vaxa venaxow dom neing dalus wo vako. De xam ghe wo vako, ekom se xam on dalus.”
JOH 13:11 En Yesu woulek tambiy tiwei embei toung e na eivek xel ba memend o, omek ingwei neil embei xam dalus seng wo vako.
JOH 13:12 Ka moxo lipek xel vaxend ma, eno moxo byex e xe teimb ding lek de lox me la dei lek nimbeeng. Moxo teling wou xel, “Xam ghe woulek vati wei a wong wou xam ne?
JOH 13:13 Xam ghe mi taxe a ‘Putoung’ me ‘Tambiy Ngandoung,’ om inyon nimza, en inyei ay ambei nyon.
JOH 13:14 A ne xam xe Tambiy Ngandoung me Putoung, de a lipek xam vaxamim, om xam is ambei nyon xam a mi zipek ama vaxamim.
JOH 13:15 A talex kwa ne wou xam bei xam a mi bong ambei ingwei a wong wou xam ne.
JOH 13:16 A neil wou xam zonghek, xukxe ti se ghanaw e xe teiv, o nenyalesana se ghanaw tambiy wei wong e la yo.
JOH 13:17 Gweimbeeng xam ghe woulek lulti beimambei ne, om wangwei xam ghe bong lulti yon dalus on tyek xam a qou mata.
JOH 13:18 “A se neil xam dalus. A woulek xam wei a beyal o. Ekom tine embo neing lek ambei ingwei di yeip eivek xoulek o. ‘Tambiy tiwei ya belet is ay eno tyek bo vaxaghelu zekna me bakei ay.’
JOH 13:19 “A neil inye natax wou xam gweimbeeng dom inye se ghei qandi, en kandek gyeik ingwei embei qandi on xam ghe bongis bei A maxow Tambiy Tiyon.
JOH 13:20 A neil wou xam zonghek, xelti embei qou eti yeiw wei a wong e lak on qou ay, me xelti embei qou ay on qou tambiy tiwei wong a lam o.”
JOH 13:21 Ka ingwei moxo neil tine, eno Yesu lalei wo maying, me neil embei, “A neil wou xam zonghek, xam venaxow ti tyek na neil a teyei me na toung a na eivek xel ba memend.”
JOH 13:22 Moxo xe xel betiyeing di yei ma kanzek en nambei xel se woulek bei neil eti.
JOH 13:23 De Yesu xe betiyeing tiwei lalei mi vind e eno di yeip pepeeng lek zek paviy e.
JOH 13:24 Simon Petele bimexe lu me neil wou betiyeing tiyon bei, “Teling wou e bei moxo neil eti.”
JOH 13:25 Om betiyeing tiyon li lu la paviy Yesu bambou de teling bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, inyon eti?”
JOH 13:26 Yesu lewexe bei, “Tambiy tiwei ambei toung belet danghei ti eivek louk me na bong wou eno tiyon inyon.” Woyom toung belet danghei ti eivek louk me wong wou Yudas Iskariot Simon neu.
JOH 13:27 Ka Yudas ya woy, Sandang la eivek e. De Yesu neil wou e, “Lul vati wei wa being bong, eno wang bong daing.”
JOH 13:28 Ekom xel wei toundei me ya eno ti se woulek bei nambei nya Yesu neil tiyon wou e.
JOH 13:29 En nambei Yudas mi yeiteyei qoupek wei malew o, om xel betiyeing valu embeik nge Yesu neil wou e bei e na bou lulul en mata wei bouk ngandoung, o bong lulul wou xel kanyo.
JOH 13:30 Lutika eno Yudas ya belet wei Yesu wong wou e yo, de moxo la myayaing. De inye bouk.
JOH 13:31 Yudas la veil woy, eno Yesu neil embei, “Gweimbeeng Xomaxoneing Neu Moux tyek bo lei ngandoung me Anutu tyek na qou lei ngandoung en Neu.
JOH 13:32 Wangwei Anutu na qou lei ngandoung en e, ond Anutu tyek bong lei ngandoung wou emaxow Neu Moux, me tyek bo lei ngandoung wou moxo lutika.
JOH 13:33 “A neungyeiw, tyek a toumendei is xam enden nayaka. De tyek xam ghe gwimexe ay, nambei ingwei a neil wou xel Yudayeiw o, om a neil wou xam gweimbeeng: Ingwei ambei na nei eno tyek xam seng nam.
JOH 13:34 “Ambei bong petieing vako wou xam: Xam laleimim e mi devind xel nge. Nambei ingwei a laleing vind xam o, om xam laleimim emi devind xel nge.
JOH 13:35 Nangya tine eno wangwei xam laleimim devind xel nge ond tyek xomaxoneing dalus boulek bei xam on a xe betiyeing.”
JOH 13:36 Simon Petele teling wou bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wa being na nya?” Yesu neil elox bei, “Ingwei ambei na nei eno tyek wa se betiwou gweimbeeng, qe tyek wa betiwou loxyus.”
JOH 13:37 Petele teling, “Tambiy Ngandoung, nambei nya tyek a se betiwou wang gweimbeeng? Tyek a saing a xe mapieing en wang.”
JOH 13:38 Woyom Yesu lewexe bei, “Neing, tyek wang teyei bei saing wa xe mapieing en ay? A neil wou wang zonghek, gyeik qouklex se ghei sesa vya, eno tyek wang dax a vun luyal!”
JOH 14:1 Yesu neil embei, “Xam laleimim se bo maying. Xam ghe bongis Anutu, me xam ghe bongis ay is ambei nyon.
JOH 14:2 Eivek Mang xe xomek nei eno lalei ngenong, wangwei se nambei nyon nei, on tyek a se neil wou xam. Om ambei na inyei me na menyex beyeeng wou xam.
JOH 14:3 Me wangwei a na menyex wou xam bamim nei, on tyek a noum a qou xam me nana is xow, me beyeeng wei ambei mendei eno tyek xam ghe na mendei is ay.
JOH 14:4 Xam ghe woulek sakwaing wei la beyeeng tiwei ambei na yo.”
JOH 14:5 Tomas neil wou e, “Tambiy Ngandoung, xa se woulek ingwei wa being na yo, om nambei nya tyek xa boulek sakwaing?”
JOH 14:6 Yesu neil embei, “A maxow sakwaing me zonghek me mapieing qes. Xelti tyek se nam wou Mang eivek sakwaing nge qe a maxow.
JOH 14:7 Wangwei xam ghe boulek a boy nei, on tyek xam ghe boulek Mang is. Gweimbeeng ne me e mi na eno xam ghe woulek moxo me ghe wei e.”
JOH 14:8 Pilip neil embei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, talex Mam wou xa, en e teyei lek xa laleimi yo.”
JOH 14:9 Yesu neil embei: “Pilip, inye wa seng ghei woulek ay? De a mindei eivek xam senghoing me enden eno? Xelti embei gyei ay eno yei Mang. Nambei nya wang neimbei, ‘Talex Mang wou xa’?
JOH 14:10 Beip wa seng wongis bei a toundei eivek Mang, de Mang toundei eivek ay? Qayeeng wei a neil wou xam eno inye se a maxow. Qe inye Mang toundei eivek Ay, me di wong e xe xuk.
JOH 14:11 Xam ghe bongis ay gyeik ingwei a neimbei a toundei eivek Mang de Mang toundei eivek ay, o xam ghe bongis xuk dalus wei a mi wong o.
JOH 14:12 A neil wou xam zonghek, xelti embei bongis ay on tyek bong vati wei a di wong ne, moxo tyek bong lul ngandoung beimambei ne ghanaw ingwei a wong ne, en nambei ambei na wou Mang.
JOH 14:13 De tyek a bong vatiyeiw wei xam ghe teling en eivek a leing o, en kandek Neu Moux bo lei ngandoung wou Ma.
JOH 14:14 Xam a mi teling wou ay en lul vatiyeiw eivek a leing, de tyek a bong.
JOH 14:15 “Wangwei xam laleimim devind ay, on tyek xam betiwou petieing wei a neil wou xam o.
JOH 14:16 De tyek a teling wou Mang, me e bong Vineing nge wou xam en e mi mendei is xam takwei takwei.
JOH 14:17 Vineing tiyon Laweeng wei zonghek o. Moux alis vex wei tembuing ne se qou e, en nambei xel se yei moxo, o xel se woulek e. Ekom xam ghe woulek e, en nambei moxo toundei is xam me tyek na toumendei eivek xam.
JOH 14:18 Tyek a se saing xam nambei yak pemboung. Tyek a mi nam wou xam.
JOH 14:19 Bouk sepika moux alis vex wei tembuing ne tyek se gyei a no, qe tyek xam ghe gwei ay. En nambei a toundei mapieing, de xam is ambei nyon tyek xam a toumendei mapieing.
JOH 14:20 Lek bouk tiyon eno tyek xam ghe boulek bei a toundei eivek Mang de xam ghe toundei eivek ay, de a toundei eivek xam.
JOH 14:21 Xelti embei qou a xe petieing me betiwou, ond tiyon lalei vind ay. Xelti embei lalei devind ay ond tyek Mang lalei devind e, me ay is ambei nyon tyek a laleing devind e me talex xow wou e.”
JOH 14:22 Woyom Yudas (se Yudas Iskariot) neil embei, “Ekom Tambiy Ngandoung, nambei nya wambei talex xow wou xa maxow de se wou moux alis vex wei tembuing sapa yo?”
JOH 14:23 Yesu neil elox bei, “Wangwei xelti lalei devind ay, ond tyek betiwou a xe teyoxeing. De Mang tyek lalei devind e, me tyek uw a nam wou moxo me na nam a mi mendei is e.
JOH 14:24 Tambiy ti lalei se mi vind ay eno tyek se betiwou a xe teyoxeing. Qayeeng beimambei wei xam ghe ngo ne eno inyon se a maxow xe, qe xel xouing on Mang tiwei wong a lam eno xe.
JOH 14:25 “A neil wou xam en lulul tine dalus gyeik a toundei is xam o.
JOH 14:26 Ekom Vineing, Laweeng Vambuing, wei Mang tyek bong e nam eivek a leing, eno tyek teyoxe xam en lul dalus me beil xam lumim lek en lulul sapa wei a neil wou xam woy yo.
JOH 14:27 Lalei vevopeing a wong e toundei is xam, a xe lalei vevopeing a wong wou xam. A se wong wou xam nambei xel wei tembuing sapa ne mi wong o. Om xam laleimim se bo maying me xam seng gwaleeng.
JOH 14:28 “Xam ghe ngo ingwei a neil o woy, ‘Ambei na de na noumenam wou xam.’ Wangwei xam laleimim devind ay, ond tyek xam ghe bo xeilala en ingwei ambei na wou Mang o, en Mang lei ngandoung eno ngandoung ghanaw ay.
JOH 14:29 A neil tiyon wou xam atax de se ghei qandi, en kandek gyeik ingwei embei qandi, on tyek xam ghe bongis.
JOH 14:30 Tyek a se puw qayeeng is xam, en gyovaxa wei mi yeiteyei tembuing ne eno lam. Moxo nikanzek se teyei bei bo lulti wou ay,
JOH 14:31 ekom ambei xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa eno boulek bei a laleing vind Mang me na mi wong nambei kawei Mang peti bei a bong o. “Xam qandi lek, en xey a na yo.”
JOH 15:1 Yesu neil embei, “A maxow yis wain zonghek de Mang on xuk wain ma.
JOH 15:2 Moxo pyaw mema dalus wei byexlek ay eno veil en xel se vuk neing lek, de mema mema wei mi vuk eno Mang qateiv veil en kandek embuk neing ngenong lek.
JOH 15:3 Xam ghe wo vako woy en qayeeng wei a mi neil wou xam o.
JOH 15:4 Xam a mi mendei eivek ay, de tyek a mi mendei eivek xam. Mema ti tyek se buk neing lek nangya emaxow, qe e mendei eivek wain bole. Xam is tyek xam seng buk neing lek qe ka xam mendei eivek a bole.
JOH 15:5 “A maxow wain qes, de xam mema mema. Wangwei tambiy ti embei mendei eivek ay me a mendei eivek e, ond tyek buk neing ngenong, ek wambei mendei beyaleing veil ay on tyek wa seng bo lulti.
JOH 15:6 Xelti embei se mendei eivek ay, ond inyon nambei mema wei xel nex ela me e mupek o, om mema nambei nyon tyek xel qekuwou me banex ena me besei lek nenyex.
JOH 15:7 Wangwei xam mendei eivek ay me a xe qayeeng mendei eivek xam, ond xam teling vatiyeiw en woueing nalei wei xam o, on tyek bong wou xam.
JOH 15:8 Xam ghe buk neing ngenong lek en e talex bei xam on a xe betiyeing, de inyon embong lei ngandoung wou Mang.
JOH 15:9 “Nambei ingwei Mang lalei vind ay, om a laleing vind xam. Gweimbeeng xam a mi mendei eivek a xe lalei vineing.
JOH 15:10 Wangwei xam betiwou a xe petieing ond tyek xam mendei eivek a xe lalei vineing, nambei ingwei a betiwou Mang xe petieing me na toundei eivek e xe lalei vineing o.
JOH 15:11 A neil wou xam en tine en kandek a xe xeilala e mi mendei eivek xam de xeilala tiyon e pup xam laleimim lek.
JOH 15:12 A xe petieing eno nambei nye: Xam titi laleimim e mi devind xel nge nambei ingwei a laleing vind xam o.
JOH 15:13 Lalei vineing ngandoung wei xelti eno nambei nye, tambiy ti e saing e xe mapieing en e xe gweleeng.
JOH 15:14 Xam on a xe gweleeng wangwei xam betiwou petieing wei a neil wou xam o.
JOH 15:15 Tyek a se nox me na taxe xukxe lek xam no, en nambei xukxe se woulek vati wei e xe teiv mi wong o, qe a taxe gweleeng lek xam, en lulul dalus wei a ngo wou Mang eno a neilteyei wou xam.
JOH 15:16 Xam seng beyal ay, qe a beyal xam bei xam ghe na me ghe buk neing lek, neing on tyek na mi mendei enden. Woyom Mang tyek bong vati wei xam ambei teling en eivek a leing eno wou xam.
JOH 15:17 Inye a xe petieing: Xam titi laleimim e mi devind ama.
JOH 15:18 “Wangwei moux alis vex wei tembuing ne bo lalei vanei wou xam ond xam ghe bou naleimim bei xel wong lalei vanei wou ay a tax.
JOH 15:19 Wangwei xam on ingwei tembuing ne yo, on tyek xel laleind devind xam nambei xel venaxow. Ekom xam se ingwei tembuing ne, en a beyal xam veil tembuing. En qes tiyon om moux alis vex wei tembuing ne di wo lalei vanei wou xam.
JOH 15:20 Xam ghe bou naleimim en qayeeng wei a neil wou xam o: ‘Xukxe ti se ghanaw e xe teiv.’ Wangwei xel bo nol wou ay, ond tyek xel bo nol wou xam is. Wangwei xel betiwou a xe teyoxeing ond tyek xel betiwou xam xe is.
JOH 15:21 Xel tyek bo nol wou xam en sakwaing ambei nyon en nambei a leing, en xel se woulek tambiy tiwei wong a lam o.
JOH 15:22 Wangwei a se nam me baluk wou xel nei ond sewokeing ma veil xel. Ekom gweimbeeng ne xel se teyei bei dax sewokeing wei xel eno vun.
JOH 15:23 Xelti embei bo lalei vanei wou ay ond wo lalei vanei wou Mang is.
JOH 15:24 Wangwei a se nam mendei eivek xel senghoing me na bong pok ngandoung wei xel nge se mi wong o ond tyek sewokeing ama veil xel. De xel yei lulvako beimambei ne woy, ekom xel laleind se vind ay me Mang is.
JOH 15:25 Ekom inye embei na teyei lek vati wei xel byex eivek petieing o: ‘Xel wo lalei vanei wou ay eno qes maeing.’
JOH 15:26 “Gyeik tiwei embei devind en ghanduxoun xam eno nam ond tyek ambong e nak wou xam, inyei lam wou Mang, inyon Laweeng wei zonghek o wei mindei is Mang me lam eno tyek moxo na neil qayeeng en ay.
JOH 15:27 Me xam a neil qayeeng en ay is ambei nyon, en nambei xam ghe mindei is ay eivek myaxeeng selis.
JOH 16:1 “A neil inye wou xam woy en ambei xam se toung demimim wou ay.
JOH 16:2 Tyek xel a tiy xam veil xomek qekueing ama, deka bouk wei yo nam on tyek xel nyeis xam amey, de tyek xel bounaleind bei xel sei xound nimza wou Anutu.
JOH 16:3 Tyek xel bong kwa ti beimambei yon en xel se woulek Mang o ay.
JOH 16:4 A neil wou xam woy en tine, en kandek gyeik ingwei bouk on embei nam on tyek xam ghe bou naleimim bei a peti xam woy. A se neil ti beimambei ne wou xam myaxeeng en nambei a toundei is xam.
JOH 16:5 “Ekom gweimbeeng ambei na wou tambiy tiwei wong a lam o, ekom xam ti seng teling ay bei, ‘Wa being na nya?’
JOH 16:6 Qe xam laleimim wo nimaying en nambei a neil ti beimambei ne woy wou xam.
JOH 16:7 Ekom a neil wou xam zonghek: Inye nimza wou xam en ingwei ambei na yo. Wangwei a se na, ond tyek Laweeng Vineing wei embei devind xam eno tyek se nam. Ekom wangwei a na, ond tyek a bong e nak wou xam.
JOH 16:8 Ka moxo embei nam, ond tyek bong moux alis vex wei tembuing o boulek sewokeing qes me kwa wei bombek eno qes me Anutu embei bong qayeeng eno qes:
JOH 16:9 Om sewokeing qes eno nambei nye, xomaxoneing se wongis ay.
JOH 16:10 Eivek kwa wei bombek eno nambei nye, ambei na wou Mang, de tyek xam seng nox mena gwei a no.
JOH 16:11 Me Anutu embei bong qayeeng eno qes ambei nye, gyovaxa tiwei mi yeiteyei tembuing eno nale lek qayeeng woy.
JOH 16:12 “A xe qayeeng ngenong wei ambei neil wou xam, ekom gweimbeeng xam seng teyei bei zeimaxoun.
JOH 16:13 Ekom gyeik e, Laweeng Zonghek nam, ond tyek beil xam lumim lek en qayeeng zonghek dalus. Moxo tyek se neil qayeeng nangya e maxow xe kwa, qe tyek na neil vati wei ngo yo teyei, me moxo tyek na neil lul wei mendi nam yus o wou xam.
JOH 16:14 Moxo tyek bong lei ngandoung wou ay, en nambei moxo tyek na qou lul wei a xe yo me na neilteyei wou xam.
JOH 16:15 Lulul dalus wei Mang xe eno inye a xe. En qes tiyon om ingwei a neimbei Laweeng tyek na qou lul wei a xe yo me na neilteyei wou xam.”
JOH 16:16 Yesu neil no bei, “Eivek bouk sepika eno tyek xam seng gwei a no, dekakom eivek bouk sepika eno tyek xam ghe gwei ay.”
JOH 16:17 Moxo xe xel betiyeing valu di neil wouma bei, “Inye neil qayeeng tine qes nambei nya, wei neil embei, ‘Eivek bouk sepika eno tyek xam seng gwei a no, dekakom eivek bouk sepika eno tyek xam ghe gwei ay.’ De moxo neil is ambei nye, ‘Qes bei ambei na wou Mang’?”
JOH 16:18 Xel di embek teling wouma bei, “Moxo neil ‘bouk sepika’ inye qes ambei nya? Xe se woulek vati wei e neil o.”
JOH 16:19 Yesu yei bei xel embei teling e en inyon, om moxo neil wou xel bei, “Xam ghe di teling ama en vati wei a neil o qes gyeik ingwei a neimbei, ‘Eivek bouk sepika eno tyek xam seng gwei a no, de woyom ka eivek bouk sepika eno tyek xam ghe gwei ay.’
JOH 16:20 A neil wou xam zonghek, tyek xam ghe deeng me ghe bo talot, de xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa eno tyek bo xeindlala, de xam laleimim tyek bo maying, ekom lalei maying wei xam eno tyek pekwi me bo xeilala.
JOH 16:21 Vex ti embei bou neu eno axe vanei en e ning bouk lam, ekom gyeik ingwei vexo neu umbek eno wo xeilala de nalei ma vanei yon en nambei neu umbek woy lek tembuing.
JOH 16:22 Om xam is: Gweimbeeng xam laleimim tyek bo maying, ekom tyek anghei xam no de tyek xam ghe bo xeimimlala, de xelti tyek se zeim xam xe xeilala veil.
JOH 16:23 De eivek bouk tiyon eno tyek xam se teling ay en lulti. A neil wou xam zonghek, Mang tyek bong vatiyeiw wei xam ghe teling en a leing eno wou xam.
JOH 16:24 Takwei eno xam seng teling lulul ti en a leing. Xam teling ond tyek xam a qou, de tyek xam xe xeilala na pup xam lek.
JOH 16:25 “A mi neil qayeeng wou xam eivek pakeing, de gyeik ingwei bouk ti tyek nam eno tyek a se nox a neil vya nambei nyon no qe tyek a neil e gyeip yaing wou xam en Mang.
JOH 16:26 Eivek bouk tiyon eno tyek xam teling en a leing. A se neimbei tyek a teling wou Mang en xam.
JOH 16:27 Ma. Mang venaxow lalei vind xam en nambei xam laleimim vind a woy me ghe wongis bei a lam anghei ingwei Anutu toundei nei.
JOH 16:28 A lam anghei ingwei Mang toundei nei me na lam tembuing, de gweimbeeng tyek a na veil tembuing me na nox me na wou Mang.”
JOH 16:29 Woyom Yesu xe xel betiyeing neil embei, “Gweimbeeng wang neil e yeip yaing dom wa seng neil qayeeng pakeing.
JOH 16:30 Xa xei bei wang woulek lulul dalusateiv me wa seng wou naleim bei xelti teling wou wang. Tine wong xa wongis bei wang lam anghei ingwei Anutu mindei nei.”
JOH 16:31 Yesu neil embei, “Gweimbeeng xam ghe wongis?”
JOH 16:32 Ekom bouk di lam paviy, me lam tyip paviy, gyeik ingwei xel embei tiy xam davuna bamim titi yo. Tyek xam ghe na veil ay me a toumendei venaxow, ekom a maxow se toundei, en Mang toundei is ay.
JOH 16:33 “A neil wou xam woy en lulul ti beimambei ne, en kandek eivek ay eno tyek xam a qou lalei vevopeing. De eivek tembuing ne eno tyek xam a qou nimaying. Ekom xam laleimim se bo maying! En a xoklek nikanzek wei tembuing ne yo.”
JOH 17:1 Ka Yesu neil tiyon woy, eno yeila tyoung gheyapu me zeimema: “Mang, seivma la wou eivek woy. Wang bong lei ngandoung wou Neum Moux, en kandek Neum Moux bo lei ngandoung wou wang.
JOH 17:2 En wang wong lei wei nikanzek eno wou moxo woy ghanaw xomaxoneing sapa wei e teyei bei bong mapieing luta luta wou xel wei wang wo wou e woy yo.
JOH 17:3 Inye deing mapieing wei luta luta yo: wei xel woulek wang o, wamaxow tixemou Anutu zonghek, me Yesu Kilisi wei wang wong e lam o.
JOH 17:4 A wong wa leim wo ngandoung lek tembuing, de na wong xuk wei wang wong wou ay bei a bong eno ma.
JOH 17:5 De gweimbeeng, Mang wang bong lei ngandoung wou ay eivek wa mamghalus, lei ngandoung tiwei a qou takwei gyeik a toundei is wang de tembuing se ghei qandi yo.
JOH 17:6 “A neil wa leim teyei wou xel wei wang wong wou ay veil tembuing ne yo. Xel ne wa xe, wang wong xel wou ay me xel mi betiwou wa xe qayeeng.
JOH 17:7 Gweimbeeng xel woulek bei lulul sapa wei wang wong wou a ne lam wou wang.
JOH 17:8 En a wong qayeeng dalus wei wang wong wou ay eno wou xel me xel qou dalus. De xel woulek neing ayang bei a lam anghei ingwei wang mindei yon, me xel wongis bei wang wong a lam.
JOH 17:9 A zeimemang en xel. A se zeimemang en xomaxoneing wei tembuing sapa yo, qe xel wei wang wong wou ay yo, en xel on wa xe.
JOH 17:10 Xel dalus wei a xe eno inyon wa xe, de xel dalus wei wa xe eno inyon a xe. Me lei wei ngandoung eno lam wou ay eivek xel.
JOH 17:11 Tyek a se toumendei enden lek tembuing, qe tyek xel a toumendei lek tembuing, de a di lam wou wang. Mang vambuing, wa mi bale zeyi xel nangya wa leim, lei tiyon wang wong wou ay, en kandek xel bo tixemou nambei uw a wo tixemou yo.
JOH 17:12 Bouk wei a mindei is xel, eno a mi nale zeyi xel en wa leim me na mi xeiteyei xel en lei tiwei wang wong wou ay yo. De xelti se lati qe tixemou wei tyek na qou nilul o, en kandek qayeeng wei di yeip eivek qapiya eno bo neing lek.
JOH 17:13 “A di lam wou wang gweimbeeng, ekom a neil ti beimambei ne gyeik a toundei lek tembuing ne, en kandek xel a qou a xe xeilala me e pup xel laleind lek.
JOH 17:14 A wong wa xe qayeeng wou xel de moux alis vex wei tembuing ne laleind wo nol wou xel, en xel ne eno se nanghei tembuing ne en nambei a se nanghei tembuing.
JOH 17:15 A xe zeimeing mema ne se en ingwei wambei zeim xel veil tembuing ne qe wa mi bale zeyi xel en tambiy tiwei nilul o.
JOH 17:16 Xel ne se nanghei tembuing, nambei a ne se nanghei tembuing.
JOH 17:17 Wang bong xel on bo vambuing beyaleing nangya wa xe qayeeng zonghek, en wa xe qayeeng on zonghek.
JOH 17:18 Nambei wang wong a lam lek tembuing, om a wong xel la eivek tembuing.
JOH 17:19 En a beyal venaxow wo vambuing en xel, en kandek xel bo vambuing zonghek.
JOH 17:20 “A xe zeimeing mema ne se en xel venaxow. Qe a zeimemang is ambei nyon en xel wei tyek na ngo xel xe qayeeng me bongis ay yo,
JOH 17:21 Mang, a bei xel bo tixemou, nambei wang mindei eivek ay de a mindei eivek wang o. Me xel mendei eivek uw en kandek moux alis vex wei tembuing ne bongis bei wang wong a lam.
JOH 17:22 A wong lei ngandoung tiwei wang wong wou ay eno wou xel en xel a mi mendei tixemou nambei uw a mindei tixemou yo.
JOH 17:23 A toundei eivek xel de wang toundei eivek ay. De ambei xel mendei tixemou en xel wei tembuing ne boulek bei wang wong a lam, de wa laleim devind xel nambei wa laleim vind ay yo.
JOH 17:24 “Mang, ambei moux alis vex wei wang wong wou a ne eno na mendei lek beyeeng wei ambei mendei yo, me gyei a xe xeiyaing ngandoung me lei ngandoung wei wang wong wou ay yo, en nambei wa laleim vind ay takwei wei tembuing anghei ma yo.
JOH 17:25 “Mang wei bombek o, xomaxoneing wei tembuing ne se woulek wang, qe a woulek wang, me xel woulek bei wang wong a lam.
JOH 17:26 A talex wang wou xel, en vati wei wa laleim vind o, me tyek a mi tetulexe wou xel. Woyom tyek xel a qou lalei vineing nambei ingwei wang wong wou ay yo, me tyek a maxow a mi mendei eivek xel.”
JOH 18:1 Ka Yesu zeimema woy, eno lis e xe xel betiyeing sek memiing Kidron me la. Nanghei loxalu eno xuk oliv ti toundei inyon, om Yesu lis e xe xel betiyeing la eivek.
JOH 18:2 Yudas tiwei embei neil Yesu teyei me na toung e na eivek xel ba memend eno woulek beyeeng tiyon, en nambei Yesu lis e xe xel betiyeing mi qekuma lumama nanghei inyon.
JOH 18:3 Om Yudas lam eivek xuk oliv on me qou xel vevek qendu ti me xel belimbo wei xel lumuki leitata me xel Parisi wong eno me lam, xel zeim lam me zounghexeing me lulul wei vevek o.
JOH 18:4 Yesu woulek lul dalus wei embei qandi wou e yo, om moxo la paviy me teling xel, “Xam ghe di wimexe eti?”
JOH 18:5 Xel neil elox bei, “Yesu wei Nasaret o.” Yesu neil, “Ay inye.” De Yudas tiwei embei toung e eivek xel memend eno toukale inyon is xel.
JOH 18:6 Xel ngo ingwei Yesu neil embei, “Ay inye,” eno xel duxeind me lox dom beng me yeip lek tembuing.
JOH 18:7 Moxo lox me la teling xel no, “Xam ghe di wimexe eti?” De xel neil, “Yesu wei Nasaret o.”
JOH 18:8 Yesu lewexe, “A neil wou xam woy bei ay inye. Wangwei xam mendi gwimexe ay, yond xam ghe bong xel moux beimambei ne na.”
JOH 18:9 Tine wong ambei nye en kandek qayeeng wei e neil eno embo neing lek: “Xel wei wang wong wou ay eno ti tyek se nati.”
JOH 18:10 Woyom Simon Petele puw e xe ngeyeing vevek me qateiv xukxe wei lumuki lukanzek xe yo nenya payeiv tip. Xukxe tiyon lei Malkus.
JOH 18:11 Yesu luk nikanzek wou Petele, “Toung wa xe ngeyeing vevek lox eivek myabelis! Wambei tyek a se num eivek mayamya wei Mang wong wou ay yo?”
JOH 18:12 Woyom xel vevek qendu ti me xel beyeiv is xel belimbo wei Yudayeiw o zeimaxoun Yesu. Xel qo moxo nangya yis
JOH 18:13 me qou e me la tax wou Anas, Anas on Kaiapas yeing wei wo lumuki lukanzek lek vakovek qes tiyon o.
JOH 18:14 Kaiapas tiwei wo xoulek wou xel lei ngandoung wei Yuda yo, inye nimza bei moux tixemou e mey en xomaxoneing.
JOH 18:15 Simon Petele me betiyeing nge di betiy Yesu. En nambei lumuki lukanzek woulek betiyeing tine, om moxo la is Yesu eivek tete lalei wei lumuki lukanzek xe yo,
JOH 18:16 ekom Petele toundei myayaing paviy qapomb me axe. De betiyeing nge wei lumuki lukanzek woulek, eno loumelam neil wou vexawo wei di yeiteyei qapomb o me qou Petele me la lalei.
JOH 18:17 Vexawo wei mi yeiteyei qapomb eno teling wou Petele, “Wang ond se e xe betiyeing ti?” Moxo neil elox bei, “Ma, se ay.”
JOH 18:18 Inye wo nityuweing, om xel xukxe me beyeiv toukale vivekwou nenyex wei xel vev me di pavang xow o. Petele is ambei nyon toukale is xel me pavang xow.
JOH 18:19 Dekalekom lumuki lukanzek teling wou Yesu en e xe xel betiyeing me e xe qayeeng wei mi teyoxe yo.
JOH 18:20 Yesu neil elox bei, “A mi neil qayeeng yanyateiv wou xomaxoneing sapa, taxombouk eno a mi teyoxe xel eivek xomek qekueing ama, o eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing wei xel Yudayeiw mi qekuma yo. A se neil qayeeng ti xupekeing.
JOH 18:21 Wang teling ay enva? Wa teling xel wei mi ngo a xe qayeeng o. En neing ayang xel woulek vati wei a mi neil o.”
JOH 18:22 Yesu neil qayeeng tine woy eno beyeiv wei toukale paviy eno ti petapexe moxo ling. De neil embei, “Inye kwa wei wa being zewexe lek lumuki lukanzek eno nambei nyon?”
JOH 18:23 Yesu neil elox bei, “Wangwei a neil lulti sewok, ond wa neil sewokeing tiyon teyei. Ekom wangwei a neil zonghek, ond nambei nya wang petapexe ay?”
JOH 18:24 Woyom Anas wong Yesu la is yis wei xel tup e xoun o wou lumuki lukanzek Kaiapas.
JOH 18:25 Ka Simon Petele toukale me pavang xow, eno xel teling e, “Wangwei bei wa se e xe betiyeing ti?” Moxo axvun me neil embei, “Ma, se ay ti.”
JOH 18:26 Ekom Lumuki lukanzek xe xukxe ti, inye nipapu wei tambiy tiwei Petele qateiv e nenya tip o neil embei, “Beip a xei wang eivek xuk oliv is e?”
JOH 18:27 Petele lox me la axvun no, de lutika eno qouklex sesa vya.
JOH 18:28 Woyom satiboukeing lul eno xel Yudayeiw qou Yesu me la veil xomek wei Kaiapas o me la xomek wei lei ngandoung wei seyap wei Rom o. Xel wou naleind bei tyek xel bo nilaxes wou Anutu ma, om tyek xel se gya mata wei Pasova yo. Om xel se la eivek xomek lalei wei lei ngandoung wei seyap o.
JOH 18:29 Om Pailat lam myayaing wou xel me teling, “Xam a being bong qayeeng lek tambiy tine en vati?”
JOH 18:30 Xel neil elox bei, “Wangwei e se bo kwa wei nilul o, ond tyek xa se qou e me na bong e nam wou wang.”
JOH 18:31 Pailat neil embei, “Xam venaxow a qou moxo me ghe na bong qayeeng en e nangya xam venaxow xe petieing.” Xel Yudayeiw neil elox, “Ekom xel peti xa bei xa se nyeis xelti mey.”
JOH 18:32 Tine wong ambei nyon en kandek qayeeng wei Yesu neil atax en e xe meyeing wei tyek na mey ambei nya eno bo neing lek.
JOH 18:33 Woyom Pailat lox me la eivek xomek lalei wei seyap o me taxe Yesu la wou e, de teling moxo bei, “Inye wa king wei Yudayeiw o?”
JOH 18:34 Yesu teling, “Inye wamaxow xe woueing nalei, o xel valu neil wou wang en ay?”
JOH 18:35 Pailat neil elox bei, “Inye a Yuda ti? Wa xe xel is xel lumuki leitata qou wang me lam wou ay. Wang wo vati?”
JOH 18:36 Yesu neil embei, “A xe tete lalei se nanghei tembuing ne. Wangwei nambei nyon on tyek a xe xel xukxe bo vevek zeyi ay, en kandek xel lei ngandoung wei Yuda eno se zeimaxoun ay. Ekom a xe tete lalei nanghei beyeeng bange.”
JOH 18:37 Pailat neil, “Inye wa king ti!” Yesu lewexe, “Inye wang neil bombek en ingwei wang neimbei a king ti yo. En qes tiyon om a umbek, me en tiyon eno a lam eivek tembuing en ambei nam a neil qayeeng zonghek teyei. Xel eti yeiw wei mi betiwou qayeeng zonghek eno mi ngo ay.”
JOH 18:38 Pailat teling, “Zonghek on vati?” De lox me la myayaing wou Yudayeiw no, wei di qekuma me neil embei, “A se xeiwou qayeeng qes ti eivek moxo bei xey a bo qayeeng en e.
JOH 18:39 Ekom inye xam venaxow xe kwa bei a mi bong xel wei toundei eivek xeitueing eno ti nak myayaing wou xam lek bouk wei Pasova yo. Xam ambei a bong king wei Yudayeiw o nak?”
JOH 18:40 Xel taxe elox bei, “Ma, se e! Qe wong Barabas lam wou xa!” Barabas on mi wo vevek me mi panax.
JOH 19:1 Woyom Pailat qou Yesu me la bei xel sesa e.
JOH 19:2 Xel vevek viy yis qapangek lekti me buwexe nambei qelumking me toung lek e lu. De xel byex teimb ding wei mateyek o ti lek e
JOH 19:3 de xel lam wou e lumama me neil embei, “Bendiyeing king wei Yudayeiw o!” Dom xel petapexe e ling.
JOH 19:4 Pailat loumelam myayaing no me neil wou xel Yudayeiw wei di qekuma yo bei, “Wei, a qou e me na loum myayaing bei xam ghe boulek bei a se xeiwou qayeeng qes ti lek e bei a bo qayeeng en e.”
JOH 19:5 Om Yesu lam myayaing is qelumking wei qapangek ying wei xel toung lek e lu me teimb ding wei mateyek o de Pailat neil wou xel bei, “Tambiy tiyo inye!”
JOH 19:6 Ka xel lumuki leitata me xel xe beyeiv yei moxo, eno xel taxe la bei, “Tuw e lek xax pepeeng! Tuw e lek xax pepeeng!” Ekom Pailat neil elox wou xel bei, “Xam venaxow qou e me tuw lek xax pepeeng, en ay eno a se xeiwou qayeeng qes ti bei a bo qayeeng en e.”
JOH 19:7 Lei ngandoung wei Yudayeiw neil elox bei, “Xe xe petieing ti, me petieing tiyon neil embei e mey, en emaxow neil embei e Anutu Neu Moux.”
JOH 19:8 Pailat ngo tine, eno moxo yaleeng ngandoung mouyo,
JOH 19:9 de moxo lox lalei eivek xomek seyap. Me teling wou Yesu, “Wang lam anghei inya?” Ekom Yesu se neil lulti wou e.
JOH 19:10 Pailat neil, “Wambei se baluk wou ay? Wa seng woulek bei a xe nikanzek teyei bei bo wang na myayaing o na tuw wang lek xax pepeeng?”
JOH 19:11 Yesu neil elox bei, “Wa se xe nikanzek ti ghanaw ay, wangwei Anutu se bong wou wang anghei gheyapu nei. Nambei nyon om tambiy tiwei qou a me lam wou wang ne eno wo sewokeing ghanaw wang veil.”
JOH 19:12 Woyom Pailat di wong me yei en embei bo Yesu na myayaing, ekom xel lei ngandoung wei Yudayeiw eno taxe la bei, “Wangwei wang bong tambiy tine na ond wa se gweleeng wei Sisa yo. Tambiy ti embei neimbei emaxow king ond wo vevek wou Sisa.”
JOH 19:13 Pailat ngo tine, eno moxo qou Yesu me la myayaing me deilek sia wei tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng o nanghei beyeeng wei xel mi neil qakous zek o. Eivek Hibru vyend eno xel mi neil Gabata.
JOH 19:14 Inye bouk wei Menyexeing lulul lek Sounda tiwei Pasova yo, inyon nambei seivma evlek. Pailat neil wou xel Yudayeiw, “Inye xam xe king.”
JOH 19:15 Ekom xel taxe la bei, “Qou e me la veil! Qou e me la veil! De tuw e lek xax pepeeng!” Pailat teling, “Teyei bei a tuw xam xe king lek xax pepeeng?” Xel lumuki leitata lewexe bei, “Xa se xe king ti qe Sisa venaxow.”
JOH 19:16 Om Pailat wong e la wou xel bei xel atuw e lek xax pepeeng. Om xel vevek qou Yesu me la.
JOH 19:17 De emaxow qalei e xe xax pepeeng me xel la beyeeng tiwei xel mi taxe lukanzek o. Eivek Hibru vyend eno xel mi taxe bei Golgata.
JOH 19:18 Nanghei inyon eno xel tuw e lek xax pepeeng is luw yayuw, nge wou valu de nge wou valu de Yesu eivek senghoing.
JOH 19:19 Pailat byex qayeeng ti me tuw lek xax pepeeng, qayeeng tine neil ambei nye: YESU WEI NASARET O, KING WEI YUDAYEIW O.
JOH 19:20 Yudayeiw ngenong pyaw dee tiyon, en beyeeng wei xel tuw Yesu lek xax pepeeng on toundei paviy beyeeng ngandoung, dee tiyon xel byex eivek Hibru vyend, me Rom me Grik.
JOH 19:21 De xel lumuki leitata wei Yudayeiw eno neil elox wou Pailat, “Wa se byex bei ‘King wei Yudayeiw o ti,’ qe tambiy tine neil embei, ‘A king wei Yudayeiw o.’”
JOH 19:22 Pailat lewexe bei, “Vati wei a byex, eno e toumendei nambei a byex woy.”
JOH 19:23 Xel vevek tuw Yesu lek xax pepeeng woy, eno xel qou e xe teimb dalus me dembu e la qendu vey, ti wou xel titi, is teimb ding wei xel duw en qaeing tixemou nanghei kwa me e la vaxa yo.
JOH 19:24 Xel neil wouma bei, “Xey ambei se zex teimb tine qe xey ambei banex qakous dee me na ghei bei eti tyek na qou.” Tiyon la teyei lek xoulek wei di yeip eivek qapiya wei neil embei, “Xel dembu a xe teimb wouma eivek xel venaxow senghoing de xel nex qakous dee en a xe teimb ding.” Om inye vati wei xel vevek wong o.
JOH 19:25 Paviy Yesu xe xax pepeeng eno ta me ta li vex toukale, me Maria wei Klopas venei me Maria wei Makdala yo.
JOH 19:26 Gyeik ingwei Yesu yei ta nanghei inyon me betiyeing tiwei e lalei vind o toukale paviyeing, eno Moxo neil wou ta, “Vex wei, wa neum moux inyon,”
JOH 19:27 woyom neil wou betiyeing tiyon bei, “Wei, vex tiyon wa tam.” Lek bouk kayon me e mi la, eno betiyeing tiyon qou vexo me la e maxow beeng.
JOH 19:28 Kalekom Yesu woulek bei lulul dalus la wou eivek en kandek xoulek wei di yeip eivek qapiya eno bo neing lek, de Yesu neil embei, “A kwang tip.”
JOH 19:29 Deng wain senyeing ti toundei inyei, om xel toung balam eivek wain me e pup, dom tup lek xax hisop mema de zeim e lek la wou Yesu mya.
JOH 19:30 Yesu num wain ma, eno neil embei, “Moxo ma yo.” De ivma eivek dom wong nulaweeng la.
JOH 19:31 Bouk tiyon inye bouk wei Menyexeing wou lulul o, de yanyeing eno inye bouk ngandoung wei Sabat o. Om xel lei ngandoung wei Yudayeiw embei xel neing se toungami lek xax pepeeng lek bouk wei Sabat o, om xel teling wou Pailat bei xel na pyaw xel vaxend apek de zewax xel neing veil.
JOH 19:32 Om xel vevek la pyaw tambiy nge myaxeeng wei tumilek xax pepeeng wou Yesu byek o vaxa pek. De woyom xel la pyaw nge wei tumi wou e byek valu yo.
JOH 19:33 Ekom gyeik ingwei xel lam wou Yesu eno xel yei bei mey woy, om xel se pyaw e vaxa luw xouing.
JOH 19:34 Ekom xel vevek ti beum Yesu byek en yiy, de lutika eno gyand aluw memiing lam.
JOH 19:35 De tambiy tiwei yeimalek eno neil qayeeng en, me e xe qayeeng on wo neing. Moxo woulek bei neil zonghek. Om neilteyei en kandek xam ghe bongis ambei nyon.
JOH 19:36 Lulul ti beimambei yon la teyei lek en kandek xoulek wei di yeip eivek qapiya yo bo neing lek: “Tyek xel se pyaw e kanzek ti pek.”
JOH 19:37 De qayeeng nge neil ambei nye, “Tyek xel mendi gyei tambiy tiwei xel beum o.”
JOH 19:38 Kalekom Yosep wei Arimatia yo la teling wou Pailat en Yesu neing. Yosep on Yesu xe betiyeing ti, ekom mindei xupekeing en nambei yaleeng en xel lei ngandoung wei Yudayeiw. Pailat lewexe lek e om la qou Yesu neing me la.
JOH 19:39 Nikodimas, tambiy tiwei takwei eno la wou Yesu eivek boukeing eno la is Yosep me qou wel xeimangou wei xel maleeng xax mer me aloes myalouk lekti yo me lam. Nimaying teyei lek xoumeeng yal (30) kilo.
JOH 19:40 Tambiy yuw on qou Yesu neing me pelei wel wei xeimangou yo lek de beliv eivek qaeing teleing teyei lek Yudayeiw xe kwa wei xel mi ev xel meyeing o.
JOH 19:41 Eivek beyeeng wei xel tuw Yesu lek xax pepeeng nanghei yon eno xuk ti toundei inyon, de eivek xuk tiyon eno leiveeng meyeing vako ti toundei, xel seng ghei liw xelti eivek.
JOH 19:42 En inyon nambei Yudayeiw xe bouk wei menyexeing lulul o de nambei leiveeng meyeing tiyon toundei paviy, om luw lak liw Yesu eivek nanghei inyon.
JOH 20:1 Satiboukeing lul wei di nexla lek bouk ti myaxeeng wei sounda tiyon, eno Maria wei Makdala la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei me yei bei qakous tatekexe veil leiveeng mya.
JOH 20:2 Om vexo veimya me loum neil wou Simon Petele luw betiyeing nge wei Yesu lalei mi vind o, me neil embei, “Xel qou Tambiy Ngandoung veil leiveeng meyeing, de xa se woulek ingwei xel liw anghei yo.”
JOH 20:3 Om Petele luw betiyeing nge yon qandi me la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei.
JOH 20:4 Luw xouing veimyend me la, ekom betiyeing nge yon veimya me ghanaw Petele me la ingwei leiveeng meyeing nei tax.
JOH 20:5 Moxo dundek me yeila qaeing di yeip inyon, ekom se la lalei.
JOH 20:6 Woyom Simon Petele betiy e me la inyon, me eivek la lalei me yei qaeing wei di yeip inyon o,
JOH 20:7 ka yei qaeing nge wei xel tup e vivekwou Yesu lu, eno xelti pyaw me toung beyaleing veil qaeing ba.
JOH 20:8 Woyom betiyeing nge wei la leiveeng meyeing nei tax, eno la lalei is ambei nyon. Moxo yei me wongis.
JOH 20:9 Neing, xoulek wei yeip eivek qapiya bei Yesu qandi lek veil meyeing eno xel seng ghei woulek.
JOH 20:10 Woyom betiyeing aluw lox me la bend.
JOH 20:11 Ekom Maria toukale myayaing paviy leiveeng meyeing me di eng. Ka vexo di eng, vexo dundek me yeila leiveeng meyeing lalei.
JOH 20:12 Me yei angela yayuw is teimb wei teltyip o. Luw toundei wou kawei xel liw Yesu neing lek o, nge toundei wou e lu de nge toundei wou e vaxa.
JOH 20:13 Luw teling wou vexo bei, “Vex, wang eng en vati?” Vexo neil embei, “Xel qou a xe Tambiy Ngandoung, de a se woulek bei xel liw e nanghei inya.”
JOH 20:14 Maria neil ambei nyon de pekwi ma me yei e vivekwou eno yei Yesu toukale inyon, ekom vexo se yeimawou bei inyon Yesu.
JOH 20:15 Yesu neil embei, “Vex, nambei nya wang di eng? Eti ingwei wang di wimexe yon?” Maria embeik nge inyon tambiy wei mi yeiteyei xuk o, om vexo neil wou bei, “Teiv wangwei wa qalei e me na nei, ond wa neil wou ay en ingwei wang liw e nanghei yo, en kandek a na qou moxo.”
JOH 20:16 Yesu neil wou vexo, “Maria.” De vexo pekwi ma me neil wou e eivek Hibru vyend, “Rabuni” qes ambei nye Putoung.
JOH 20:17 Yesu neil embei, “Wa seng daxlek ay, en a se ghei lox gheyapu wou Mang. Wang nox wou a lingyeiw me na neil wou xel, ambei nox me na wou Mang me xam Mamim, wou a xe Anutu me xam xe Anutu.”
JOH 20:18 Maria wei Makdala yo lox wou xel betiyeing me neil embei, “A xei Tambiy Ngandoung!” De vexo neil wou xel en qayeeng wei moxo neil wou e yo.
JOH 20:19 Lek soukeing wei bouk ti myaxeeng wei sounda tiyon, xel betiyeing qekuma, eno xel toung qapomb beimambei yond zeyi en xel yaleeng en lei ngandoung wei Yudayeiw, eno Yesu lam me nale eivek xel senghoing me neil, “Lalei vevopeing e mi mendei is xam.”
JOH 20:20 Ka moxo neil ambei nyon woy, moxo talex mema luw me byek wou xel. De xel betiyeing wo xeindlala ngandoung gyeik ingwei xel yei Tambiy Ngandoung o.
JOH 20:21 Yesu neil no bei, “Lalei vevopeing e mi mendei is xam! Nambei ingwei Mang wong a lam. De a wong xam ghe la.”
JOH 20:22 De is inyon eno moxo vei mya laweeng la lek xel de neil embei, “Xam ghe qou Laweeng Vambuing.
JOH 20:23 Wangwei xam semaleeng sewokeing wei xelti yo, on tyek Anutu semaleeng sewokeing veil. Ek wangwei xam se semaleeng sewokeing wei xelti yo, ond tyek Anutu se semaleeng sewokeing veil.”
JOH 20:24 Tomas wei xel mi taxe Didimas, xel xoumeeng yuw eno ti, se toundei is xel betiyeing gyeik ingwei Yesu lam o.
JOH 20:25 Om xel betiyeing ba neil wou e bei, “Xa xei Tambiy Ngandoung!” Ekom moxo neil wou xel bei, “Wangwei a se ghei beleim mya me na toung memang deyis eivek e mema luw, me na toung memang eivek yiy mya wei e byek o, ond tyek a se bongis.”
JOH 20:26 Ka sounda qes ti la veil eno e xe xel betiyeing lox me la dei eivek xomek no, me Tomas toundei is xel. De xel toung qapomb zeyi, Yesu lam nale eivek xel senghoing me neil embei, “Lalei vevopeing e mi mendei is xam.”
JOH 20:27 Woyom moxo neil wou Tomas bei, “Toung memam deyis lam inye me wei a memang aluw. De tatei memam lam me toung eivek a byek. Tip laleim yuw de wongis.”
JOH 20:28 Tomas neil wou e, “A xe Tambiy ngandoung me a xe Anutu.”
JOH 20:29 Woyom Yesu neil wou e bei, “En nambei wang wei ay om wang wongis, xeilala e mendei is eti yeiw wei se yei ay qe xel wongis o.”
JOH 20:30 Yesu wong dee wei lulvako eno ngenong eivek e xe xel betiyeing mendghalus, ekom xel se byex eivek qapiya tine.
JOH 20:31 Ekom qayeeng ti beimambei wei a byex ne eno xam a mi bongis bei Yesu e Kilisi, me Anutu Neu Moux, de nangya wongeingis tiyon eno tyek xam a qou mapieing eivek e lei.
JOH 21:1 Kalekom Yesu talex xow wou e xe xel betiyeing no, nanghei lounyeing wei Taiberias nei. Inyon qandi nambei nye:
JOH 21:2 Simon Petele, me Tomas wei xel mi taxe e lei nge Didimas, me Natanael wei Kana eivek Galili yo, de Sebedi neu luw, me betiyeing yayuw is eno xel xouing toundei lekti.
JOH 21:3 Simon Petele neil wou xel bei, “Ambei na qou woing.” De xel neil embei, “Xa bei na is wang.” Om xel la myayaing me la dei eivek bot, ekom boukeing tiyon eno xel se qou lulti.
JOH 21:4 Satiboukeing lul eno Yesu toukale wou mamileeng vi, ekom xel betiyeing se woulek bei inyei Yesu.
JOH 21:5 Woyom moxo taxe la wou xel bei, “Xam neungyeiw, xam ghe qou woing valu?” Xel neil elox bei, “Ma.”
JOH 21:6 Moxo neil embei, “Xam banex xam xe lewek na eivek bot nenya valu wei payeiv o on tyek xam a qou valu.” Om xel wong ambei nyon, eno xel se teyei bei puw lewek noum en nambei woing on ngenongakes.
JOH 21:7 Woyom betiyeing tiwei Yesu lalei mi vind eno neil wou Petele bei, “Inyei Tambiy Ngandoung!” Ka Simon Petele ngo moxo neil embei, “Inyei Tambiy Ngandoung,” om byex e xe teimb ding lek, en kwax veil de di wong xuk. De vyeip me la eivek memiing.
JOH 21:8 De xel betiyeing bamba di betiwou e eivek bot, de xel puw lewek wei pup en woing eno lam, en xel se toundei dingta veil nenyawes, inye nambei 100 mita.
JOH 21:9 Ka xel lam nenyawes eno xel yei nenyex bapax ti di tum de woing toundei lek, me belet valu is.
JOH 21:10 Yesu neil wou xel, “Xam a qou woing wei xam ghe qou yon valu me ghe nam.”
JOH 21:11 Simon Petele lek bot me la dandiy lewek la nenyawes. Inye pup en woing ngandoung teyei lek 153, xel woing ne ngenong ekom lewek se lex.
JOH 21:12 Yesu neil wou xel, “Xam lam wa.” Xel betiyeing yaleeng om ti se teling e bei, “Inyon wang eti?” En xel woulek bei inye Tambiy Ngandoung.
JOH 21:13 Yesu lam qou belet me wong wou xel de wong ambei nyon wou woing is.
JOH 21:14 Tine inye luyal en ingwei Yesu talex xow wou e xe xel betiyeing gyeik ingwei qandi veil meyeing o.
JOH 21:15 Ka xel ya woy, eno Yesu neil wou Simon Petele bei, “Simon Yoan neu, beip wa laleim vind ay zonghek ghanaw xel ne?” Moxo neil embei, “Ee, Tambiy Ngandoung, wang woulek bei a laleing vind wang.” Yesu neil embei, “Wa mi bet a xe sipsip lingheing ne.”
JOH 21:16 Yesu neil no, “Simon Yoan neu, wa laleim vind Ay zonghek?” Moxo lewexe bei, “Ee, Tambiy Ngandoung, wang woulek bei a laleing vind wang.” Yesu neil embei, “Wa mi gweiteyei a xe sipsip.”
JOH 21:17 Luyal eno moxo neil wou e, “Simon Yoan neu, wa laleim vind ay?” Petele lalei wo maying en nambei Yesu teling e luyal, “Wa laleim vind ay?” Moxo neil embei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wang woulek lulul dalus, om wang woulek bei a laleing vind wang.” Yesu neil embei, “Wa mi bet a xe sipsip.
JOH 21:18 A neil wou wang zonghek, gyeik ingwei wa ghavis eno wang vunekwou xow me ghe la teyei lek ingwei wang wou naleim en o, ekom gyeik ingwei wang wo teiv eno tyek wa tatei memam luw xouing na, de xel valu tyek bunekwou wang me na qou wang me na ingwei wa bei seng na yo.”
JOH 21:19 Yesu neil tine en sakwaing wei Petele tyek na mey de bo lei ngandoung wou Anutu yo. Woyom neil wou moxo bei, “Wang nam betiwou ay!”
JOH 21:20 Petele pekwi ma me yei betiyeing tiwei Yesu lalei vind eno di betiwou luw. Inyon tambiy tiwei liw lu la lek Yesu bambou me neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung, eti tyek na neil wang teyei me na toung wang na eivek xel ba memend?”
JOH 21:21 Ka Petele yei e, eno moxo teling bei, “Tambiy ngandoung nambei nya wou e?”
JOH 21:22 Yesu neil elox bei, “Wangwei a neimbei e toumendei mapieing deka a noum le, ond inye wo vati wou wang? Wa betiwou ay.”
JOH 21:23 Om pavulek la wo sapa eivek xel betiyeing, xel di neil embei betiyeing tine tyek se mey. Ekom Yesu se neil embei moxo tyek se mey, qe neil embei, “Wangwei a laleing devind bei e toumendei mapieing ond tyek na toumendei deka a noum le, ond inye wo vati wou wang?”
JOH 21:24 Tine inye betiyeing tiwei neil qayeeng neing en lulul ti beimambei ne de byex dalus eivek qapiya. Me xey a woulek bei e xe qayeeng ne zonghek.
JOH 21:25 Yesu wong lulul ngenong valu is ambei nyon. Om wangwei xel a byex dalus nei, ond tyek beyeeng wei tembuing ne na ma en ingwei xey ambei toung qapiya eivek o.
ACT 1:1 Tiopilas, Eivek a xe qapiya nge tax, a byex myaxeeng en lulul dalus wei Yesu wong a tax me teyoxe xel o
ACT 1:2 me elam tyip bouk wei Anutu qou e lek la tyoung gheyapu nei, me eivek Laweeng Vambuing eno neil wou sinaleyeiw wei e beyal en xuk leimalei wei xel a mi bong o.
ACT 1:3 Ka e qou nimaying woy eno moxo talex xow yeip yaing wou moux ti beimambei ne bei toundei mapieing. Moxo belup wou xel lumama teyei lek bouk mepyeiyuw (40) me luk wou xel en tete lalei wei Anutu xe yo.
ACT 1:4 Ka e nanghei toundei is xel, me ya is xel eno moxo peti xel, “Xam sim ghe na veil Yerusalem, qe xam a mi mendei inye me daxe lul xeilala wei Mang neil zonghek bei bong o. Wei xam ghe ngo ingwei a luk en o.
ACT 1:5 Yoan lipek moux alis vex en memiing, ekom bouk di lam paviy en ingwei tyek xam ghe zipek en Laweeng Vambuing o.”
ACT 1:6 Om gyeik xel sinale me Yesu qekuma, xel teling wou e, “Tambiy Ngandoung, gweimbeeng lek bouk tine eno tyek wang nox me na piyexe tete lalei wei Israel o no?”
ACT 1:7 Moxo neil wou xel: “Inye se yeip wou xam bei xam ghe boulek seivma o bouk wei Mang venaxow lax angya emaxow nikanzek o.
ACT 1:8 Ekom tyek xam a qou nimkanzek gyeik Laweeng Vambuing nam lek xam o, me vati wei xam ghe wei mamim wou woy eno tyek xam a neil a teyei eivek Yerusalem, me ena eivek Yudia dalus me distrik Samaria, me ena tyip wou tembuing myasepu nei.”
ACT 1:9 Ka Yesu neil qayeeng tine woy, Anutu qou e lek la gheyapu wou xel mendghalus de laxap sevun e om xel se yei e no.
ACT 1:10 Xel anghei di yei ingwei e la punei eivek tyoung gyeik e di la yo, lutika eno tambiy yuw byex teimb teleing me nale lip wou xel.
ACT 1:11 Luw neil wou xel, “Xam moux wei Galili yon, xam ghe toungale inye me ghe di domamim la wou tyoung en va? Yesu tiwei, Anutu qou veil xam me la eivek tyoung gheyapu nei, eno tyek noum me nam eivek sakwaing ambei kawei xam ghe wei e la eivek tyoung o.”
ACT 1:12 Woyom xel betiyeing la veil lukendu wei xel mi taxe bei Oliv, me lox me la Yerusalem wei toundei paviy lukendu Oliv o, teyei lek ambei kilomita ti.
ACT 1:13 Gyeik xel la tyip, xel la gheyapu eivek xomek lalei wei xel embei mi mendei eivek o. Eti yeiw wei lam eno leind ambei nye, Petele, Yoan, Jems, me Andrias, Pilip me Tomas, Batolomiu me Matai, Alpias neu moux Jems me Simon wei Selot me Yudas on Jems neu moux.
ACT 1:14 Xel xouing dalus mi qekuma me toung laleind lekti de mi zeimemend taxombouk, xel vex lam is me Maria wei Yesu ta, me liyeiw moux is.
ACT 1:15 Eivek bouk tiyon Petele nale eivek xel wongeingis on senghoing (xel on teyei lek 120)
ACT 1:16 me neil, “Xam lingyeiw, xoulek wei yeip eivek qapiya ne eno embei bong neing lek ambei ingwei Laweeng Vambuing luk takwei nei eivek Dawit mya en Yudas tiwei talex sakwaing wou xel wei embei zeimaxoun Yesu yo.
ACT 1:17 Yudas on tambiy wei xey yo ti, me mi wo xuk is xey.”
ACT 1:18 (Yudas qou malew en sewokeing wei talex Yesu teyei yo, me moxo la xouv tembuing ti en inyon woy. Woyom moxo teibouyek lek tembuing me leis bambou tek de xeixay qapyex lam myayaing.
ACT 1:19 Xel dalus eivek Yerusalem eno ngo tine, om xel taxe tembuing tiyon lei eivek vyend bei Akeldama qes ambei nye bei Tembuing wei Gyand o.)
ACT 1:20 Petele neil, “En inye xel byex eivek qapiya lalo bei, “‘Teyeimbei e beeng on mendei bandaing en xomaxoneing ti se mendei lek inyon,’ me, “‘teyeimbei tambiy nge e qou e nimbeeng en xuk wei la tax en xel o.’
ACT 1:21 Om inyon nimza bei xey a beyal moux wei mi la me loum is xey bouk sapa gyeik Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu mi dei is xey yo,
ACT 1:22 lek bouk sapa wei Yoan lipek xel me elam tyip gyeik Yesu lek la gheyapu veil xey o. Om xey a beyal tambiy wei yeimawou woy eno nge en e neil Yesu xe qandieing lek teyei.”
ACT 1:23 Om xel beyal moux yayuw: Yosep wei xel mi taxe bei Balsabas (lei nye bei Jastus) me Matias.
ACT 1:24 Woyom xel zeimemend, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wang woulek xomaxoneing titi laleind. Talex wou xa bei luyuw ne nge na wang beyal,
ACT 1:25 bei e gyeiteyei xuk sinale, wei Yudas ghanaw me la wou e maxow xe sakwaing o.”
ACT 1:26 Woyom xel nex qakous dee, om qakous teila wou Matias, om moxo la is sinaleyeiw xoumeeng ti yon.
ACT 2:1 Gyeik bouk wei Pentikos eno lam, om xel wongeingis dalus qekuma eivek xomek ti.
ACT 2:2 Se denlek en nindenduing nambei laweeng nikanzek ti lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei me pup eivek xomek lalei wei xel toundei eivek on.
ACT 2:3 Xel yei lulti nambei nenyex, xok ambei ghas eno dembuma me la dei lek xel on titi.
ACT 2:4 Laweeng Vambuing lam pupexe xomaxoneing on lek om xel luk vyend leimalei nambei ingwei Laweeng Vambuing wong wou xel o.
ACT 2:5 Gweimbeeng inyon xel wei toundei eivek Yerusalem on Anutu xe xel Yudayeiw wei mi yaleeng en Anutu xe petieing me betiwou e yo, eno lam anghei beyeeng tambak wei mindei xeinghembi en tyoung gheyapu.
ACT 2:6 Gyeik xel ngo nindenduing tine, moux alis vex ngenong on lam qekuma is etekeing, en nambei xel titi yon ngo xel di luk eivek xel venaxow titi vyend.
ACT 2:7 Xel etek niseikeing, om xel teling: “Beip xel moux alis vex dalus tine eno se Galiliyeiw?
ACT 2:8 Woyom nambei nya ekom xey titi ngo qayeeng eivek xe venaxow vyend?
ACT 2:9 Xey wei Patia me Midia me Elam me Mesopotamia me Yudia me Kapadosia me Pontus me Esia,
ACT 2:10 me Prigia me Pampilia me Izip me ela valu wei Libia paviy Sairini, me xe valu lam anghei Rom me na lam a toundei inye.
ACT 2:11 (Xel on valu Yudayeiw me xel ba wei mi betiwou petieing wei Mose yo). Me xel valu wei Krit me Arebia, eno xey a ngo xel di neil xuk nimza maseim wei Anutu xe yo teyei eivek xemaxow vyend.”
ACT 2:12 Xel etek me wou naleind ngenong, de teling wouma, “Tine qes nambei nya?”
ACT 2:13 Xel valu eno luk seloukeing en xel me neil, “Xel num wain ngenong o.”
ACT 2:14 Woyom Petele nale is sinaleyeiw xoumeeng ti yon, de luk me vya lekla dom neil qayeeng wou xel qendu ngandoung on bei, “Xam Yudayeiw me xam dalus wei ghe mindei eivek Yerusalem o, xam wong a neil qayeeng tine wou xam, xam a ngo embo nimza en vati wei ambei neil ne yo.
ACT 2:15 Moux ti beimambei ne eno se num me wo nol, nambei ingwei xam ghe di wou naleimim en o. Inye nanghei seivma limvey wei satiboukeing o!
ACT 2:16 Ma, inye vati wei poropet Yoel neil o:
ACT 2:17 “‘Anutu neil, “Eivek bouk loxyus, tyek a qapyex a xe Laweeng Vambuing lek xomaxoneing dalus. Xam neumim moux me xam neumim vex tyek baluk ambei poropet, de xam neumyeiw ghavis tyek mendghalus pekwi me gyei lul leimalei, de teivateiv wei xam o tyek gyei maviing.
ACT 2:18 Eivek bouk tiyon eno tyek a qapyex a xe Laweeng Vambuing lek a xe xukxe moux alis vex dalus, me tyek xel a neil qayeeng ambei poropet.
ACT 2:19 De tyek a talex lul nelu nelu eivek tyoung gheyapu nei, me dee wei lulvako eno lek tembuing axone, gyand me nenyex me nenyex lu ngandoung tyek na tyip.
ACT 2:20 Sayeiv tyek pekwi me bo mapetok de dentouk tyek bong ambei gyand natax en bouk ngandoung wei Tambiy Ngandoung nam is xeiyaing ngandoung me nikanzek wei e yo.
ACT 2:21 Me xel dalus tiwei tyek taxe Tambiy Ngandoung lei yo eno tyek Anutu devind xel noum veil meyeing.”’
ACT 2:22 “Xam xomaxoneing wei Israel o li nenyamim wou qayeeng tine, Yesu wei Nasaret on, Tambiy wei Anutu talex wou xam bei wong Yesu lak wou xam is lul nikanzek is dee wei lulvako yo wei xam ghe boulek bei Anutu wong e lam eivek xam senghoing eivek e maxow mema nambei ingwei xam ghe woulek o.
ACT 2:23 Yesu ne Anutu wou eivek xam memamim betiwou qes me ingwei wounalei en o pyap woy, eivek xel amba wei se mi betiwou qayeeng petieing o memend ekom xam ghe tuw e lek xax pepeeng me ghe leis e mey.
ACT 2:24 Ekom Anutu piyexe e qandi lek veil myavanei me tul e veil meyeing, en meyeing se teyeimbei zeimaxoun e.
ACT 2:25 De Dawit neil ambei nye lek e, “‘A xei Tambiy Ngandoung mindei paviy ay taxombouk, en moxo toundei wou a memang payeiv om tyek a se detek.
ACT 2:26 Nambei nyon a laleing mi wo nimza me a myang mi sanghoxe, me tyek a neing a mi mendei me na toung mang en inyon.
ACT 2:27 En tyek wa seng bong a nung na toumendei eivek beyeeng wei meyeing o, o tyek wa xe Tambiy Tiwei Vambuing eno se daxe pataleing.
ACT 2:28 Wang talex sakwaing wei a mi mendei mapieing eno wou ay me tyek wang bong xeilala e pup ay, wou wa mamghalus.’
ACT 2:29 “Xam lingyeiw, a neil neing wou xam en xe bund Dawit bei moxo mey me e xe eeng toundei inye is xey me elam tyip gweimbeeng ne.
ACT 2:30 Woyom tambiy on poropet ti om woulek ingwei Anutu neil neing is inya punei bei tyek bong e buyeiw ti mendei lek siaking wei e xe yo.
ACT 2:31 Dawit yei tax me neil en qandieing wei Kilisi yo, de Anutu nalei se ma e me wong e toundei eivek leiveeng wei meyeing o, me tyek xel se gyei e neing on patal.
ACT 2:32 Yesu tine Anutu piyexe e qandi lek me xa dalus a xei lek mami.
ACT 2:33 De woyom Yesu lek me la gheyapu woy me la dei wou Anutu mema payeiv me qou Laweeng Vambuing wou Ma, nambei ingwei neil zonghek o. Moxo qapyex tine lam me xam ghe di wei me ghe ngo yo.
ACT 2:34 En Dawit se lek me la eivek tyoung gheyapu, qe emaxow neil embei, “ ‘Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou a xe Tambiy Ngandoung, “Lam dei wou a memang payeiv.
ACT 2:35 Deka a toung xel wei mi wo vevek wou wang eno na kwanghembi eivek wa vaxam bole.” ’
ACT 2:36 “Nambei nyon xam xomexomek dalus wei Israel o ghe bongis bei Anutu wong Yesu tiwei xam ghe tuw lek xax pepeeng eno wo Tambiy Ngandoung me Kilisi.”
ACT 2:37 Gyeik xel xomaxoneing ngo tine, xel laleind wo nimaying me neil wou Petele me sinaleyeiw bei, “Xam lingyeiw, tyek xa bong vati?”
ACT 2:38 Petele neil elox bei, “Xam dalus on titi pekwi xow me xel zipek xam en Yesu Kilisi lei, en tyek semaleeng xam xe nilul sapa veil, dom tyek Anutu bong Laweeng Vambuing wou xam nambei byeind wei xam o.
ACT 2:39 Qayeeng wei neil zonghek ne eno inye wou xam me xam neumyeiw me inye wou xel dalus wei mindei dingta yo, me inye wou xel dalus wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe xe Anutu taxe yo.”
ACT 2:40 Petele peti xel en qayeeng ngenong. Me byexaxoun xel, “Xam a mi devind ama veil xel nilul wei bouk ti gweimbeeng ne.”
ACT 2:41 Om xel wei mi lewexe lek e xe qayeeng me lipek eno teyei lek 3,000 eno tendulek xel lek bouk tiyon.
ACT 2:42 Xel moux alis vex wo ninkanzek bei ngo sinaleyeiw xe teyoxeing me toung laleind lekti me wounaleind en Yesu eivek ingwei xel dembu belet o me zeimemend.
ACT 2:43 Me sinaleyeiw wong lul nelu nelu ngenong me dee wei lulvako yo ngenong om xel dalus on etek.
ACT 2:44 Xel dalus wei mi wongis Yesu eno mi dei is ama me wong lulul dalusateiv on is laleind tixemou.
ACT 2:45 Xel mi wo vateivek lek tembuing me lulul wei xel xe yo, de mi wong wou xel wei lulul maeing o.
ACT 2:46 Bouk tambak eno xel mi qekuma eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing wei qekueing ama yo. Xel mi dembu belet eivek xel xe xomek me ya lekti is laleind nimza me laleind vevopeing.
ACT 2:47 Xel mi sanghoxe Anutu me mi wo xeindlala en xomaxoneing sapa laleind mi wo nimza wou xel. Me bouk titi eno Tambiy Ngandoung qou xomaxoneing valu is no, me xel wongis e me tendulek xel bamba me xel wo ngenong.
ACT 3:1 Bouk ti Petele luw Yoan la xomek vambuing, lek seivma wei zeimeing mema yo, lek soukeing wei seivma yal o.
ACT 3:2 Nanghei nyon eno moux wei vaxa wo nol eivek ta veis eno xel qalei e me la toung paviy xomek vambuing on mya wei xel mi taxe bei Nimza yo, xel toung e nanghei inyon me e mi teling xomaxoneing wei mi eivek la tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o en malew.
ACT 3:3 Tambiy on yei Petele luw Yoan embim na eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing o, om moxo teling luw bei luw bo malew ti wou e.
ACT 3:4 Ekom Petele luw Yoan domend wou e me neil, “Wei uw!”
ACT 3:5 Om moxo yei luw, de e beiknge tyek na qou malew valu wou luw.
ACT 3:6 Woyom Petele neil wou e, “A selewa o ghol wei ambei bong wou wang eno ma, ekom vati wei a xe eno tyek a bong wou wang. Lek Yesu Kilisi wei Nasaret o lei, a neil wou wang, qandi lek me la.”
ACT 3:7 Om Petele zeim lek e mema payeiv me vind moxo nale gheyapu, lutika eno e vaxa qatu me vaxalambes wo nimzalek.
ACT 3:8 Moxo vyeip me nale me ghavineeng eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing is luw, la ghavineeng me wo vyeip vyeip me sanghoxe Anutu lei.
ACT 3:9 Xel xomaxoneing dalus yei ingwei moxo di ghavineeng me sanghoxe Anutu lei yo.
ACT 3:10 Xel woulek bei inyon tambiy kawei mindei wou xomek vambuing mya wei xel mi taxe bei Nimza yo, me mi teling lulul wou xel, om xomaxoneing dalus on etek niseikeing en ingwei moxo wo nimzalek o.
ACT 3:11 Moxo zeimaxoun Petele luw Yoan omva, xomaxoneing sapa nun la me etek dom tup me la wou lal lek xomek palanda wei xel mi taxe bei palanda wei Salomo yo.
ACT 3:12 Ekom Petele yei ingwei xel qeku lam o, om neil wou xel bei, “Xam lingyeiw Israel, xam ghe etek enva? Me xam ghe domamim wou uw enva? Beip uw a wong tambiy ne wo nimzalek angya nikanzek wei uw maxow o, o nangya ingwei uw a mindei nimza wou Anutu manghalus o?
ACT 3:13 Anutu wei Apraham me Isaka me Yakop o, inye Anutu wei xe mendyeiw me bundyeiw eno wong e xe xukxe Yesu lei wo ngandoung, inyon tambiy tiwei xam ghe pesek me ghe toung e eivek Pailat mema bei xel nyeis e mey, gyeik Pailat embei bong ena bandaing o.
ACT 3:14 Ekom xam ghe pesek xomaxoneing wei Vambuing me Bombek ayang o, dom ghe teling Pailat en tambiy wei mi leis xel mey o bei embong e noum wou xam.
ACT 3:15 Dom xam ghe leis tambiy wei mapieing lukes, ekom Anutu piyexe e qandi lek veil meyeing. De xa maxow a xei tine lek mami.
ACT 3:16 Moux tine tiwei xam ghe wei me ghe woulek eno wo nimzalek nangya e xe wongeingis lek Yesu lei. Om tambiy tiyon wongis Yesu lei me wong e wo nimzalek, nambei xam dalus ghe wei yon.
ACT 3:17 “Gweimbeeng, xam lingyeiw, a woulek inyon bei xam seng woulek om xam ghe wong tiyon, nambei kwa wei xam xe xel gyovaxa yo.
ACT 3:18 Ekom lulti beimambei yon, Anutu neil atax eivek xel poropet dalus myend, bei e xe Kilisi, tyek na qou myavanei, om wo neing lek eivek sakwaing wei xam ghe wong on.
ACT 3:19 Woyom xam pekwi xow, de pekwi me ghe nox wou Anutu, en kandek Anutu e semaleeng xam xe sewokeing veil, dom Tambiy Ngandoung tyek bong nikanzek vako wou xam,
ACT 3:20 me inyon tyek Anutu bong Kilisi, tiwei e beyal wou xam o nam, inyon Yesu.
ACT 3:21 Moxo mindei eivek tyoung gheyapu deka bouk wei Anutu embei bong lul dalus bo vako eno nam le, nambei e neil zonghek eivek mya; is e xe xel poropet vambuing atax o.
ACT 3:22 En Mose neil, ‘Xam xe Tambiy Ngandoung Anutu tyek beyal xam xe poropet ti nambei ay, eivek xam venaxow limyeiw senghoing, xam a ngo lul tambak wei embei neil wou xam o.
ACT 3:23 Xelti embei se ngo e, eno tyek semaleeng e veil e xe xel xomaxoneing.’
ACT 3:24 “Nambei nyon, xel poropet dalus eivek bouk wei Samuel me e lam eno xel ngenongakes luk, me eti yeiw wei lam yus eno luk me neil qayeeng en bouk wei di lam gweimbeeng ne yo.
ACT 3:25 Me xam on poropet neuyeiw, me xam on ingwei Anutu qokatu is xam bumimyeiw o. E neil wou Apraham, ‘Eivek wa neumambum xomaxoneing lek tembuing sapa tyek na qou mata.’
ACT 3:26 Woyom Anutu piyexe e xe xukxe qandi lek, de wong moxo lak atax wou xam, bei bong mata wou xam me pekwi xam titi veil xam xe sakwaing wei nilul o.”
ACT 4:1 Luw di neil xoulek wou xomaxoneing bembeeng on, de lumukiyeiw is beyeiv wei mi yeiteyei xomek vambuing o, me xel Sadyusi xel xouing lam wou Petele luw Yoan gyeik luw di neil qayeeng wou xel xomaxoneing on.
ACT 4:2 Xel laleind wo vanei ngandoung wou luw en xel woulek bei luw di teyoxe xomaxoneing sapa yon en ingwei Yesu qandi lek veil meyeing o.
ACT 4:3 Xel zeimaxoun Petele luw Yoan bei na toung luw na eivek xeitueing deka yanyeing le, en inye souk.
ACT 4:4 Ekom xel ngenong wei ngo xoulek eno wongis. Me xel moux nyouk teyei lek ambei 5,000.
ACT 4:5 De yanyeing eno xel leitata me teivateiv me xel putoung wei petieing o qekuma nanghei Yerusalem.
ACT 4:6 Anas lumuki lukanzek toundei inyon is Kaiapas, me Yoan, me Aleksanda me xel moux valu wei lumuki lukanzek nipapu eno is.
ACT 4:7 Om xel qou Petele luw Yoan me lam lax luw wou xel mendghalus dom teling wou luw bei, “Eivek nikanzek vati, me eivek eti lei eno muw ghe wong lulti beimambei yon nangya?”
ACT 4:8 Woyom Laweeng Vambuing pupexe Petele, om neil wou xel, “Xam leitata me teivateiv wei xel xomaxoneing o,
ACT 4:9 beip xam ambei teling uw en tambiy tiwei uw a wong e vaxa wo nimzalek o, me xam ambei teling bei, e vaxa wo nimza lek ambei nya.
ACT 4:10 Woyom xam ghe bouk lek qayeeng tine, xam me xomaxoneing sapa wei Israel o dalus ghe boulek bei, eivek Yesu Kilisi wei Nasaret o lei, tambiy tiwei vaxa wo nol ne eno wo nimza lek me nale wou xam mamim. Xam ghe tuw Yesu lek xax pepeeng. Ekom Anutu piyexe e qandi lek veil meyeing.
ACT 4:11 Yesu yon “‘qakous tiwei xam kamunda ghe pesek, eno wong ambei qakous lukanzek wei mi byexaxoun xomek o.’
ACT 4:12 Tambiy ti se teyeimbei devind xey veil meyeing qe Yesu venaxow, en, eivek tyoung gheyapu xeinghembi eno Anutu se neil lei bange wei xelti yo teyei bei devind xey a noum veil meyeing.”
ACT 4:13 Xel teivateiv on yei Petele luw Yoan luk is nikanzek de se yaleeng, om xel woulek inyon bei luw xouing se wevek xomek qapiya, luw on moux bandaing, xel etek me wou kwend bei yuw on mi la is Yesu.
ACT 4:14 De xel yei tambiy tiwei luw wong e wo nimzalek o toungale inyon is luw, om xel se teyeimbei neil qayeeng ti nox wou luw.
ACT 4:15 Om xel neil wou luw bei luw na veil xomek kanzol, luw la veil de woyom xel luk wouma.
ACT 4:16 Xel teling, “Tyek xey a bong vati wou moux yuw ne? En xel sapa wei toundei eivek Yerusalem ne eno woulek bei luw wong xuk dee ne inye nimza, om xe se teyeimbei daxvun.
ACT 4:17 Ekom tyek xey a peti luw en luw se neil qayeeng tine na bo sapa wou xomaxoneing en lei tine no.”
ACT 4:18 Woyom xel lox me la taxe luw me luk nikanzek wou luw bei luw se baluk o teyoxe xomaxoneing en Yesu lei no.
ACT 4:19 Ekom Petele luw Yoan neil elox bei, “Xam teling ama, beip inye nimza wou Anutu manghalus bei xa betiwou xam de se Anutu?
ACT 4:20 Ekom uw se teyeimbei tip lukeing en lul sapa wei uw a xei me na ngo woy yo.”
ACT 4:21 Xel kanzol on neil qayeeng nikanzek valu no wou luw dom wong luw la, de xel se wo nimaying ti wou luw, en nambei xomaxoneing sapa yon di sanghoxe Anutu lei en vati wei belup on.
ACT 4:22 En tambiy tiwei luw wong e wo nimzalek eno xe vakovek qes ghanaw xoumeeng vey (40).
ACT 4:23 Xel kanzol tul Petele luw Yoan woy, woyom luw lox wou luw maxow xe xomaxoneing, me neil qayeeng dalus wei xel lumuki leitata me teivateiv neil wou luw o.
ACT 4:24 Xel ngo qayeeng tine woy, xel xouing toung laleind lekti eivek zeimeing mema wou Anutu. Xel neil, “Tambiy Ngandoung nikanzekta, wang toung tyoung me tembuing me mamileeng, me lulul sapa wei toundei eivek o.
ACT 4:25 Myaxeeng eno wang luk eivek xa mami Dawit, wa xe xukxe mya nangya Laweeng Vambuing bei: “ ‘Nambei nya xomaxoneing sapa laleind wo myavanei, xomaxoneing beimambei ne tup qayeeng bandaing bei bong kwa nilul enva?
ACT 4:26 Xel king wei tembuing eno yeiwou xow en embei bo vevek. Me xel gyovaxa qekuma en xel embei bo vevek wou Tambiy Ngandoung me embei bo vevek wou Kilisi is.’
ACT 4:27 Xa woulek bei vati wei wang neil atax takwei eno wo neing lek zonghek. En Herot aluw Pontias Pailat qeku is xel ba me xel wei Israel, eivek beyeeng ngandoung bei bong nimaying wou Yesu, wa xe xukxe vambuing tiwei wang beyal o.
ACT 4:28 Gyeik xel wong lul tine, xel betiwou kwa me wamaxow laleim en nikanzek wei wang o. Takwei eno wang tup qayeeng atax bei lulti beimambei ne eno neing a tyip.
ACT 4:29 Gweimbeeng, Tambiy Ngandoung wa bounaleim en xel xe qayeeng wei xel neil me wo yalenyeing wou xa yo, de wa devind xa wei wa xe xukxe yo, bei xa neil wa xe xoulek is nikanzek dom xa se ghaleeng.
ACT 4:30 De wa ni memam na lek xel wei vanei yo en xel bo nimzalek me wang bong dee wei lulvako yo eivek wa xe xukxe vambuing Yesu lei.”
ACT 4:31 Ka xel zeimemend woy, beyeeng kawei xel di qekuma lek on wo pimapi. Me xel dalus pup en Laweeng Vambuing me neil Anutu xe xoulek nikanzek, dom xel se yaleeng.
ACT 4:32 Xel wongeingis laleind me lundpeyei eno la tixemou, xelti se neil embei lulti yon inyon emaxow xe, qe xel vind ama en lulul dalus wei xel xe yo.
ACT 4:33 Sinaleyeiw di tetulexe qayeeng neileing en ingwei Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu qandi lek o is nikanzek ngandoung me Anutu xe lalei xeiles wei ghanaw veil eno toundei is xel.
ACT 4:34 Inyon xel wei kanyo eno ti se toundei eivek xel senghoing, en eivek bouk titi xel eti yeiw wei xe tembuing, o xomek eno wo vateivek lek, me qou malew lek,
ACT 4:35 de toung ela wou sinaleyeiw vaxend, me xel pum malew on wou xel wei lulul maeing o.
ACT 4:36 Yosep, wei Livai nanghei Saiprus, xel sinale mi taxe e lei nge bei Banabas (qes ambei nye bei tambiy wei mi vind xomaxoneing en qayeeng nimza yo)
ACT 4:37 eno wong vateivek lek e xe tembuing de qou malew me toung ela wou sinaleyeiw.
ACT 5:1 Tambiy ti lei Ananias, de venei lei Sapira, luw wong vateivek lek tembuing wei luw eno danghei ti me tambiy nge xouv,
ACT 5:2 De venei woulek is ambei nyon om luw toung malew veweeng wou lumaxow, dom veweeng dalus eno luw qou me la toung wou xel sinale.
ACT 5:3 Woyom Petele neil, “Ananias, nambei nya ekom wang wong Sandang pup wa laleim lek, me wang tyoxe Laweeng Vambuing, de ghe toung malew valu wou xow wei wang qou lek tembuing o?
ACT 5:4 Myaxeeng wei wa seng ghei wo vateivek lek tembuing on, eno inyon wa xe zonghek. Deka wang wo vateivek lek, eno malew on inye wa xe. Om wang wou eivek naleim en kwa nilul on enva? Wa seng tyoxe xomaxoneing venaxow qe wang tyoxe Anutu is.”
ACT 5:5 Ananias ngo qayeeng tine eno moxo teibouyek lek tembuing de mey. Me xel dalus wei ngo qayeeng ne eno yaleeng ngandoung mouyo.
ACT 5:6 Woyom xel moux wei ghavis eno lam me beliv e neing eivek qaeing, de xel qalei e neing on me la ev.
ACT 5:7 Seivma yal lak veil, Ananias venei lam lalei, ekom vexo se woulek vati wei belup wou leya yo.
ACT 5:8 Om Petele teling wou e, “Neil wou ay bei malew wei muw ghe qou lek tembuing eno dalus inye?” Vexo neil, “Ee, malew dalus inyon.”
ACT 5:9 Petele neil wou vexo, “Nambei nya muw leyam ghe tyoxe Tambiy Ngandoung xe Laweeng? Wei! Xel moux wei qalei leyam me la ev eno vaxend toungale wou xomek mya yon, om tyek xel qalei wang me na myayaing is ambei nyon.”
ACT 5:10 Lutika eno vexo teibouyek lek tembuing wou Petele vaxa dom mey. Woyom xel ghavis lam lalei me yei bei vexo mey, om xel qalei e me la myayaing me la ev e paviy leya.
ACT 5:11 Om xel wongeingis dalus me xel amba dalus wei ngo qayeeng en vati wei belup on eno xel yaleeng ngandoung.
ACT 5:12 Sinaleyeiw wong lulvako me dee ngenong eivek xel xomaxoneing senghoing. Me xel wongeingis dalus mi toung laleind lekti me qekuma eivek xomek palanda wei xel mi taxe bei palanda wei Salomo mi dei lek o.
ACT 5:13 Xel bamba wei se ghei wongis Yesu eno yaleeng bei se na mindei is xel wei wongis o. Ekom xel ngenong mi sanghoxe xel wei wongis o nambei xel on nimza.
ACT 5:14 Dekalekom moux alis vex ngenong wongis Tambiy Ngandoung me lam tendulek xel wei wongis o me xel wo ngenong.
