ACT 5:15 Sinaleyeiw di wong lulvako nimza, om xomaxoneing mi qalei liyeiw wei wo vanei me la eivek sakwaing mema nayak o me liw xel lek lelek me ghus en kandek Petele nak ond e tenu liw la lek xel.
ACT 5:16 Xel qendu ngandoung wei mi qekuma eno lam anghei beyeeng wei vivekwou Yerusalem o, me mi qou xel xe xel wei vanei me eti yeiw wei laweeng nol wo nol wou xel, eno dalus wo nimzalek.
ACT 5:17 Woyom lumuki lukanzek me e xe xel dalus wei mi la lekti, xel on inyon Sadyusi, eno laleind mi wo nilul wou xel.
ACT 5:18 Xel zeimaxoun sinaleyeiw me toung xel eivek xeitueing wei beyeeng o.
ACT 5:19 Ekom eivek boukeing eno angela wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe yo tax xomek mya wei xeitueing o, dom qou xel me la myayaing.
ACT 5:20 Moxo neil, “Xam la, nale eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing wei qekueing ama yo me neil wou xomaxoneing en qayeeng dalus en mapieing vako tine.”
ACT 5:21 Xel ngo inye woy, de yanyeing eno xel eivek la tete lalei wei xomek vambuing wei qekueing ama yo, me teyoxe qayeeng wou xomaxoneing. De xel lumuki lukanzek me e xe xel lam tyip, xel taxe xel kanzol, me xel leitata wei Israel o lam qekuma, me wong xel la xomek xeitueing bei na qou sinaleyeiw me nam.
ACT 5:22 Xel belimbo la tyip xomek xeitueing ekom xel se yei xel sinale. Om xel lox me la neil wou teivateiv bei,
ACT 5:23 “Xa xei xomek xeitueing mya ekom xel toung zeyi, de xel belimbo toungale wou xomek mya. Ekom gyeik ingwei xa tax qapomb eno xa se xei xelti eivek xomek lalei.”
ACT 5:24 Woyom beyeiv wei mi yeiteyei xomek vambuing me xel lumuki leitata ngo qayeeng tine eno etek, me wounaleind ngenong bei lul tine nambei nya?
ACT 5:25 Woyom tambiy ti lam me neil, “Wei! Xel moux wei xam ghe toung eivek xomek xeitueing eno toungale eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing wei ngoeing qayeeng o me di teyoxe xomaxoneing.”
ACT 5:26 Om beyeiv tiyon la is xel belimbo me qou sinaleyeiw. Xel se wo lulti wou xel, en nambei xel yaleeng en xel xomaxoneing on tyek banex xel angya qakous.
ACT 5:27 Om xel la qou sinaleyeiw, me la lax xel wou xel kanzol mendghalus, bei lumuki lukanzek teling xel.
ACT 5:28 E neil, “Xa wong qayeeng petieing nikanzek wou xam bei, xam se teyoxe xel lek lei tine, ekom xam ghe wong beyeeng Yerusalem ne pup en xam xe teyoxeing me ghe di byex qayeeng lek xa bei xa leis e mey.”
ACT 5:29 Petele is sinale bamba neil elox wou xel bei, “Tyek xa betiwou Anutu de se xomaxoneing!
ACT 5:30 Xam ghe teyu Yesu lek xax pepeeng me ghe leis e mey. Ekom Anutu wei xe bundyeiw eno piyexe Yesu veil meyeing,
ACT 5:31 me toung e la dei wou emaxow mema payeiv, nambei gyovaxa me Tambiy wei vind xey veil nilul o. E wong ambei nye en kandek xel Israel pekwi xow veil nilul de e semaleeng xel xe sewokeing.
ACT 5:32 Xa xei mami wou lulti beimambei ne dalus woy, me Laweeng Vambuing byexaxoun qayeeng ne is ambei nyon bei lul beimambei ne neing ayang, wei Anutu wong wou xel wei mi betiwou e yo.”
ACT 5:33 Xel kanzol ngo qayeeng tine eno xel laleind wo vanei ngandoung om xel embei nyeis xel amey.
ACT 5:34 Ekom Parisi ti lei Gameliel, Putoung wei petieing o, wei xomaxoneing mi sanghoxe e lei yo, eno nale gheyapu wou xel kanzol dalus mendghalus me wong qayeeng nikanzek bei xel a qou sinaleyeiw me na myayaing nayaka le.
ACT 5:35 Woyom moxo neil qayeeng wou xel, “Xam moux wei Israel, xam ghe bounaleim bo nimza en vati wei xam ambeing bong wou xel moux ti beimambei ne yo.
ACT 5:36 Bouk valu la tax veil ekom Teudas lam tyip, me neil embei e lei ngandoung, me moux 400 eno mi betiwou e. Eno xel seyap leis e mey, de e xe xel betiyeing pek, om xuk dalus on wong ambei lul bandaing.
ACT 5:37 Ka bouk wei seyap qou xel xomaxoneing leind, Yudas wei Galili eno dandiy xomaxoneing ngenong la wou xow. E is ambei nyon xel leis e mey, de e xe xel dalus pek me vu ama lala.
ACT 5:38 Nambei nyon, gweimbeeng a neil wou xam, xam memamim tena xel moux beimambei ne na! En wangwei xel xe xuk wei xel di wong ne inye xomaxoneing xe, on tyek neing ama veil.
ACT 5:39 Ek wangwei inye lam wou Anutu, on xam seng teyeimbei bale zeyi xel moux beimambei ne, tyek xam venaxow gwei bei xam ghe di wo vevek is Anutu.”
ACT 5:40 Xel ngo Gameliel xe qayeeng me lewexe lek. Om xel kanzol taxe sinaleyeiw la lalei me wong beyeiv sesa xel. Woyom xel luk nikanzek wou xel bei, “xam seng nox a neil qayeeng lek Yesu lei no,” dom wong xel la.
ACT 5:41 Xel sinale ghanaw xel kanzol, me wong xeindlala en Anutu wounalei bei xel ne nimza teyei bei qou niyalenyeing en Yesu lei.
ACT 5:42 Teyei lek bouk sapa, xel mi la tete lalei wei xomek vambuing me xomek titi wei xomaxoneing o me teyoxe xel, de xel se tip neileing xoulek Nimza. Ma. Xel neil teyei bei Yesu yon Kilisi.
ACT 6:1 Eivek bouk ti beimambei yon eno xel betiyeing di nyouk, xel Yuda valu wei mi luk Grik vyend eno wo veweeng is xel Yuda wei mi luk Hibru yo. Me neil embei xel Yudayeiw mi pum yaeing wou kanyo yeiw de xel se mi vind xa xe vexeiv wei Grik o en yaeing teyei lek bouk.
ACT 6:2 Om xel sinale xoumeeng yuw qeku xel betiyeing dalus lekti me neil, “Inye se teyei lek bei xa saing Anutu xe xoulek neileing de na bo xuk lek pumeing lul yaeing.
ACT 6:3 Xam lingyeiw, xam beyal moux lim yuw eivek xam senghoing on wei xam ghe woulek bei Laweeng Vambuing pup xel me xel lundpeyei nimza yo. Tyek xa bong xuk tine e nox mena wou xel,
ACT 6:4 de tyek xa bale ding lek zeimeing mema me xuk wei neileing Anutu xe xoulek o.”
ACT 6:5 Qayeeng tine wong moux alis vex dalus laleind wo nimza, om xel beyal Setepan, moux wei pup en wongeingis me en Laweeng Vambuing, me Pilip, Plokolas, Nikanor, Timon, Palmenas, me Nikolas nanghei Antiok, wei mi betiwou qayeeng wei Yudayeiw o.
ACT 6:6 Xel qou xel moux ti beimambei ne me la wou xel sinale, me xel zeimemend wou xel de liw memend lek xel.
ACT 6:7 Om xoulek wei Anutu xe eno la wo sapa. Xomaxoneing ngenong wei Yerusalem eno wong ambei betiyeing me nyouk daing, me lumukiyeiw valu beti eno wongis ambei nyon.
ACT 6:8 Gweimbeeng Setepan on moux wei pup en Anutu xe lalei xeiles me nikanzek, me mi wong dee wei lulvako ngenong eno eivek xomaxoneing senghoing.
ACT 6:9 Ekom xomaxoneing valu qandi me wong veweeng is Setepan. Xel on anghei xomek qekueing ama wei xel taxe bei tul e la. Xel on nanghei Yuda eno lam anghei Sairini me Aleksandlia me lam anghei provins wei Silisia me Esia.
ACT 6:10 Ekom xel se teyeimbei bale zeyi e lupeyei me Laweeng Vambuing wei di luk angya yo.
ACT 6:11 Woyom xel xupek me zeim xel valu laleind lek me neil embei, “Xa ngo Setepan lukyak lek Mose me Anutu.”
ACT 6:12 Om xel zeim xomaxoneing laleind lek me teivateiv me putoung wei petieing o. Om xel zeimaxoun Setepan me qou e me la wou xel kanzol.
ACT 6:13 Xel beyal xel valu bei xel a byex qayeeng tyonyeing lek Setepan me neil ambei nye, “Taxombouk eno tambiy ne se mi tip lukeing nilul lek xomek vambuing tine me e xe qayeeng petieing.
ACT 6:14 En xa ngo e neil tiyon bei, ‘Yesu wei Nasaret o tyek lelolexe xomek vambuing tine me pelipek sakwaing wei Mose wong wou xey yo.’”
ACT 6:15 Xel dalus tiwei toundei eivek kanzol beeng eno domend wou Setepan, me xel yei e ma yon siing ambei angela ti manghalus.
ACT 7:1 Woyom lumuki lukanzek teling wou e, “Qayeeng tiwei xel neil lek wang ne inye zonghek?”
ACT 7:2 Om moxo neil elox, “Xam lingyeiw me xam mangyeiw, xam ngo wou a le! Xeiyaing wei Anutu xe eno lam tyip wou xe mend Apraham gyeik nanghei toundei eivek Mesopotamia, myaxeeng atax en ingwei mindei eivek Haran o.
ACT 7:3 Anutu neil wou e, ‘Wang na veil bam me nimpapu, dom ghe na tembuing tiwei tyek a talex wou wang o.’
ACT 7:4 “Om Apraham moxo ghanaw tembuing wei Kaldia me la dei eivek Haran. Ka bouk wei Apraham ma mey yo, Anutu wong e la tembuing tiwei xam ghe toundei lek gweimbeeng ne.
ACT 7:5 Anutu se wong tembuing ti wou Apraham nanghei inye, me se wong tembuing ti bombek wou e. Qe Anutu neil qayeeng atax wou moxo bei e me e neumambu wei loxyus en e yo tyek na qou nind tembuing kayon, gyeik Apraham neu nanghei ma yo.
ACT 7:6 Anutu luk wou Apraham eivek sakwaing tine: Wa neumambum tyek bong ambei xel ba eivek beyeeng wei se xel venaxow xe yo, me tyek xel bo pok ngandoung me xel on tyek bo nilul wou xel teyei lek vakovek qes 400.
ACT 7:7 Anutu neil, tyek a bong myaveweeng wou tembuing tiwei mi wo pok ngandoung wou xel o, dekalekom tyek xel nam myayaing veil beyeeng tiyon me bong lalo wou ay eivek beyeeng tine.
ACT 7:8 Woyom Anutu wong qokatu wei ghuweing ninavi yo. Me Apraham on Isaka ma gyeik xel ghuw e ninavi lek bouk lim yal o. Me Isaka yon Yakop ma, de Yakop on neuyeiw xoumeeng yuw mend wei xel wo lukanzek en velei xoumeeng yuw o.
ACT 7:9 “Yakop neuyeiw wei wo lukanzek en velei xoumeeng yuw on laleind wo vanei wou Yosep, om xel wo vateivek lek e wou xel amba, en xuk bandaing eivek Izip. Ekom Anutu vena mindei is e
ACT 7:10 me mi zeim e veil e xe nimaying dalus. De wong lupeyei nimza wou e om king Parao wei Izip o lalei vind Yosep. Om wong Yosep yeiteyei Izip me e xe lulul dalus wei e beeng o.
ACT 7:11 “Woyom maxep ngandoung ti yeip lek beyeeng Izip dalus me Kenan, om nimaying ngandoung lam wou xomaxoneing, me xe bundyeiw se teyeimbei gyeiwou yaeing ti.
ACT 7:12 Om gyeik Yakop ngo bei yaeing toundei eivek beyeeng Izip, moxo wong xe bundyeiw la Izip ti myaxeeng.
ACT 7:13 Xel lox me la luyuw, eno Yosep neil xow teyei wou liyeiw, me Parao woulek Yosep liyeiw is ambei nyon.
ACT 7:14 Om Yosep wong qayeeng la wou ma Yakop me e neumambu dalus bei xel nam wou e, xel xouing teyei lek 75.
ACT 7:15 Woyom Yakop la xo wei Izip nei, dekakom e me xe mend a bund eno xel xouing mey anghei nyon.
ACT 7:16 Xel qou neing wei xel xe meyeing me lox Sekem me toung xel eivek leiveeng meyeing wei Apraham xouv wou Hamor neuyeiw anghei Sekem en malew valu yo.
ACT 7:17 “Nambei bouk di lam paviy ingwei Anutu embei bong e xe qayeeng zonghek wei mi neil wou Apraham eno embo neing lek, de xel xomaxoneing Israel vamva wei mi dei eivek Izip eno di nyouk.
ACT 7:18 Woyom king nge, wei se woulek Yosep, eno yeiteyei Izip.
ACT 7:19 King tiyon mi yei xe xe xomaxoneing wo nilul me mi tyoxe xe bundyeiw me wong nilul wou xel, me mi tendu xel bei xel banex neuyeiw wei yakyeis eno na myayaing en kandek xel amey.
ACT 7:20 “Lek bouk kayon eno Mose umbek, me Mose yon yakyeis nimza ka wou Anutu manghalus. Moxo mindei eivek ma beeng teyei lek dentouk qes yal.
ACT 7:21 Om gyeik xel toung e la myayaing, Parao neu vex zeim e me qou me yeiteyei nambei emaxow neu moux.
ACT 7:22 Mose wevek xomek qapiya me qou kwa nimza dalus wei Izip o, me e tambiy wei mi luk nikanzek me mi wo xuk leimalei yon wo nikanzek.
ACT 7:23 “Gyeik Mose xe vakovek qes xoumeeng vey (40), moxo wou kwa bei embei na gyei liyeiw wei Israel o.
ACT 7:24 Moxo yei Izip ti di leis Israel ti, om Mose la vind li Israel on me qou e lu me leis Izip tiyon mey.
ACT 7:25 Mose wou kwa bei inyon emaxow xe xel Israel tyek boulek inyon bei Anutu wong e lam bei e devind xel, ekom xel se woulek.
ACT 7:26 De yanyeing eno Mose lam me yei Israel yayuw di leis ama. Moxo wong en embei bale zeyi luw me neil, ‘Inyon muw limim ama yo, nambei nya muw ghe leis ama?’
ACT 7:27 “Ekom xomaxoneing nge wei wo vevek atax eno tendu Mose la nenya de neil, ‘Eti beyal wang me wong wang wo gyovaxa me tambiy wei ngoeing qayeeng wei xa yo.
ACT 7:28 Wa being nyeis a mey nambei ingwei wang leis Izip ti mey vezeiveeng o?’
ACT 7:29 Gyeik Mose ngo qayeeng tine, moxo pek me la Midian, me la dei inyon ambei tambiy ba me wo neu moux yuw.
ACT 7:30 “Ka vakovek qes xoumeeng vey (40) la veil, woyom angela ti tyip wou Mose eivek nenyex magyand wei tum lek xax mema eivek tembuing bandaing paviy lukendu Sinai yo.
ACT 7:31 Gyeik Mose yei tine, moxo etek me dula paviy en embei gyei embo nimza, moxo ngo Tambiy Ngandoung vya neil ambei nye,
ACT 7:32 ‘A Anutu wei wa bumyeiw o, Anutu wei Apraham, Isaka me Yakop o.’ Mose etek is yalenyeing me embei se gyei.
ACT 7:33 “Woyom Tambiy Ngandoung neil wo e, kwax wa xe vaxalambes on veil, en beyeeng kawei wang toungale lek on inye tembuing vambuing.
ACT 7:34 A xei kwa nilul wei xel wong wou a xe xel xomaxoneing eivek Izip o woy. A ngo xel xe engeing, om a lam bei na qou xel noum veil nimaying. Om lam kane, en tyek a bong wang nox me na Izip.
ACT 7:35 “Mose tine kawei xel pesek e me neil, eti beyal wang en gyovaxa me tambiy wei ngoeing qayeeng wei xa yo? Mose moxo Anutu wong ela bei e gyeiteyei xel me na qou xel angya angela mema wei tyip wou e lek xax nayak o.
ACT 7:36 Mose tine qou xel me lam veil Izip me wong dee me lulvako eivek Izip, me nanghei Mamileeng Gyand me ela eivek tembuing bandaing on teyei lek vakovek qes xoumeeng vey (40).
ACT 7:37 “Mose kayon tiwei neil wou Israelyeiw bei, ‘Anutu tyek bong poropet ti nambei ay eivek xam venaxow xe xomaxoneing.’
ACT 7:38 Mose tine dei eivek qekueing ama yon eivek tembuing bandaing is xe bundyeiw, me is angela tiwei luk is Mose lek lukendu Sinai yo is xe bundyeiw, me moxo qou qayeeng mapieing me lam bei e nam bong wou xey.
ACT 7:39 “Ekom xe bundyeiw pyalek en xel embei se betiwou e. Qe xel pesek e me eivek xel xe woueing nalei bei xel embei nox me na Izip.
ACT 7:40 Om xel neil wou Aron, ‘Wa menyex anutuyeiw en xel natax en xa. En nambei Mose tine eno la tax en xa me lam myayaing veil Izip eno xa loungen bei vati wong e!’
ACT 7:41 Bouk tiyon eno xel betiy manghaxo neu ti tenu. De xel qou lul leimalei me wong ela wou nambei xound me wong xeindlala ngandoung me sanghoxe lul wei xel wong angya memend o.
ACT 7:42 Ekom Anutu toung demi wou xel me pelipek xel laleind eivek bei xel bong lalo wou sayeiv, dentouk me betum teyei lek qayeeng wei poropet byex eivek qapiya yo: “Xam xomek wei Israel o, beip xam ghe toung xound me da wou ay teyei lek vakovek qes xoumeeng vey (40) wei xam ghe mindei eivek tembuing bandaing o, ei?
ACT 7:43 Xam ghe qalei xomek wei Molek me betum wei xam xe anutu Lepan tenu bandaing wei xam ghe betiy bei na mi bo lalo wou yo. Nambei nyon tyek a bong xam ghe na eivek beyeeng tiwei yeip Babilon valu lox nei.
ACT 7:44 “Lek bouk wei xe bundyeiw dei eivek tembuing bandaing eno xel qalei xomek sel wei Anutu xe qoupek wei petieing mi yeip eivek eno is xel. Xomek tiwei xel lax ne eno Anutu neil wou Mose bei xel balax teyei lek tenu wei talex wou Mose yo.
ACT 7:45 Kalekom xe bundyeiw is Yosua qou xomek sel me qoupek wei petieing o me lam bei na qou tembuing wei xel amba xe yo. Anutu tiy xel la veil, dom lax xomek sel ne lek tembuing on me elam tyip wou bouk wei Dawit o.
ACT 7:46 Dawit tiwei Anutu lalei wo nimza wou e eno teling wou Anutu bei dev xomek nimza ti wou Anutu wei Yakop o.
ACT 7:47 Dekakom Salomo ev Anutu xe xomek tiyon.
ACT 7:48 “Ekom Anutu wei tyoung gheyapu nei se mindei eivek xomek wei xomaxoneing ev o. Nambei poropet neil,
ACT 7:49 “‘Tambiy Ngandoung neil, “Tyoung gheyapu yon a xe siaking, me tembuing on a xe zek wei a mi lax vaxang lek o. Om tyek xam ghe dev xomek vati wou ay? O beyeeng wei ambei qou laweeng eno yeip inya?
ACT 7:50 Beip a memang se toung lulul dalus ti beimambei ne?”’
ACT 7:51 “Xam xomaxoneing on lumimpeyei nikanzek me xam laleimim on wo mapetok me xam nenyamim on wo qatu. Me xam ghe teyei lek bumyeiw, me ghe mi pyalek Laweeng Vambuing.
ACT 7:52 Poropet eti eno xam bumyeiw se mi wo nilul wou e? Xel leis xel xomaxoneing wei mi neil Tambiy Ti Bombek o teyei, wei e bei nam o. Me gweimbeeng xam ghe neil e teyei de ghe leis e mey.
ACT 7:53 Xam on ghe qou petieing wou angela, ekom xam seng betiwou.”
ACT 7:54 Gyeik xel ngo qayeeng tine, xel laleind wo vanei ngandoung wou e, me nga vind wou e.
ACT 7:55 Ekom Laweeng Vambuing pup Setepan, om yeila tyoung gheyapu nei me yei xeiyaing wei Anutu yo, me yei Yesu toungale wou Anutu mema payeiv.
ACT 7:56 De moxo neil, “Wei, a xei tyoung gheyapu tax me Xomaxoneing Neu Moux toungale wou Anutu mema payeiv.”
ACT 7:57 Ka xel ngo tine xel sevun nenyend de ghak niseikeing, en xel embei se ngo e vya, xel xouing qapyex me la wou e,
ACT 7:58 de tetei e la myayaing veil beyeeng ngandoung on dom nex e gya qakous. De xel wei wong qayeeng en Setepan eno kwax xel xe teimb me toung wou moux ghavis ti lei Sol eno vaxa.
ACT 7:59 Ka xel nex Setepan nangya qakous, Setepan zeimema bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu, wa zeim a nung laweeng veil.”
ACT 7:60 Woyom moxo ev vaxa qatu eivek de eng niseikeing bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, wa seng bo myaveweeng wou xel en sewokeing wei xel o.” Ka neil tine woy, moxo yeip.
ACT 8:1 Sol toundei inyon me yei kwa wei xel wong wou Setepan me e mey yon, eno lalei wo nimza. Lek bouk kawei xel leis Setepan eno xel di wo nol wou xel wongeingis wei mindei eivek Yerusalem. Om xel dalus pek me vuwama lala eivek tembuing danghei wei Yudia me Samaria. Dom sinaleyeiw nanghei toundei eivek Yerusalem.
ACT 8:2 Anutu xe xel moux wei mi betiwou e xe qayeeng eno ev Setepan me mi wo talot en e xe meyeing.
ACT 8:3 Ekom Sol anghei di wo nol wou xel wongeingis. Me mi la eivek xomek tambak on titi me tetei moux alis vex, me toung xel eivek xeitueing.
ACT 8:4 Xel wei pek me vuwama lala, eno mi neil Xoulek Nimza la eivek beyeeng inyayeiw wei xel la dei yo.
ACT 8:5 Pilip la xo wei beyeeng ngandoung nei ti eivek Samaria me neil Kilisi teyei nanghei inyon.
ACT 8:6 Gyeik xel qendu ngandoung on ngo Pilip me yei dee leimalei wei e wong o, xel dalus liw nenyend me ngo vati wei e di neil o.
ACT 8:7 En xel laweeng nilaxes nyayek niseikeing de lam myayaing veil xel ngenong on, de xel ngenong wei bezomb o, me xel wei mema vaxa wo nilul eno wo nimzalek.
ACT 8:8 Om moux alis vex wo xeindlala ngandoung eivek beyeeng ngandoung tiyon.
ACT 8:9 Xomaxoneing ti mindei eivek beyeeng ngandoung tiyon, e lei Simon eno mi wong palak eivek beyeeng ngandoung ond, om xomaxoneing dalus wei Samaria eno etek, moxo mi byexvaxa bei e tambiy teiv ngandoung ti,
ACT 8:10 de xomaxoneing dalus, me xel wei leind ngandoung me leind nayak toung nenyend wou e me neil, “Moux tine qou nikanzek ngandoung nambei Anutu xe Nikanzek.”
ACT 8:11 De xel liw nenyend wou Simon en nambei e wong etekeing wou xel lumama en e xe palak.
ACT 8:12 Ekom gyeik Pilip di neil Xoulek Nimza wei Anutu xe tete lalei yo eivek Yesu Kilisi lei, omek xel wongis de xel lipek moux alis vex.
ACT 8:13 Simon venaxow wongis me lipek. Me moxo mi betiwou Pilip me la danghei danghei nei, me yei dee leimalei me lulvako ngandoung wei Pilip wong, om mi wounalei ngenong.
ACT 8:14 De woyom sinaleyeiw wei mindei eivek Yerusalem eno ngo bei Samariayeiw lewexe lek Anutu xe xoulek, om xel wong Petele luw Yoan la wou xel.
ACT 8:15 Gyeik luw la tyip, luw zeimemend wou xel bei xel a qou Laweeng Vambuing,
ACT 8:16 en nambei Laweeng Vambuing seng ghei lam lek xel valu qe xel qou lipekeing eivek Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu lei venaxow.
ACT 8:17 Woyom Petele luw Yoan li memend lek xel, me xel qou Laweeng Vambuing.
ACT 8:18 Simon yei inyon bei Laweeng Vambuing lam lek xel gyeik sinale luw xouing li memend lek xel on, om qou malew me la wou luw,
ACT 8:19 me neil, “Muw wong nikanzek tiyon wou ay, en kandek a ni memang lek xelti ond e qou Laweeng Vambuing o.”
ACT 8:20 Ekom Petele neil wou e, “Wa xe malew embo nol is wang, en wang wou kwam being bou lul wei Anutu wong bandaing o en malew!
ACT 8:21 Wa seng teyeimbei bong Anutu xe xuk tiwei uw andi wong ne, en nambei wa laleim on se wo bombek wou Anutu manghalus.
ACT 8:22 Wa pekwi xow veil kwa nilul tiwei wang wong o. Dom na zeimemam wou Tambiy Ngandoung bei e teyeimbei semaleeng wa xe kwa nilul wei di yeip eivek wa laleim on.
ACT 8:23 En a xei bei wa laleim on pup en lul nilul, me lul nilul on tup wang axound.”
ACT 8:24 Woyom Simon lewexe, “Muw zeimemamim wou Tambiy Ngandoung en ay, en kandek lulul wei muw ghe neil on ti se balwou ay.”
ACT 8:25 Om luw neil Tambiy Ngandoung xe xoulek teyei, de neil wou xel en lulul wei Tambiy Ngandoung wong wou luw o. De Petele me Yoan lox me la Yerusalem, luw di lox eno luw neil Xoulek Nimza eivek beyeeng ngenong wei Samaria yo.
ACT 8:26 Dekalekom angela wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe eno ti neil wou Pilip, “La xonei wou sakwaing tembuing bandaing, wei la xo Yerusalem nei me la Gasa yo.”
ACT 8:27 Om moxo qandi lek me la, me la tyip wou xomaxoneing wei Itiopia eno ti wou sakwaing, tambiy yon xel veil e nikanzek veil, tambiy yon lei ngandoung wei mi yeiteyei malew wei kwin Kandesi wei Itiopia yo. Xomaxoneing tine la Yerusalem bei na dundek wou Anutu,
ACT 8:28 om loum me lox me la beeng, de deilek e xe karis dom di pyaw qapiya wei poropet Yesaya byex o.
ACT 8:29 Laweeng Vambuing neil wou Pilip, “La paviy karis tiyon me la vaxam is e.”
ACT 8:30 Woyom Pilip veimya me la wou karis tiyon me ngo ingwei tambiy moxon di pyaw qayeeng wei poropet Yesaya byex o. Om Pilip teling wou e, “Beip wang woulek qayeeng wei wang di pyaw on?”
ACT 8:31 Moxo neil embei, “Wangwei xel ti se neil wou a nei, on tyek a boulek ambei nya?” Om moxo neil wou Pilip bei, e zekna mendei is e.
ACT 8:32 Tambiy tiwei xel veil e nikanzek veil eno di pyaw xoulek wei yeip eivek qapiya eno nambei nye: “Xel dandiy e nambei sipsip ti me la bei na nyeis e mey, ekom se neil qayeeng ti, me nambei sipsip lingheing wei xel qou me la bei na qateiv e nivlus veil o.
ACT 8:33 Xel wo niyalenyeing wou e om xel se zeim e xe qayeeng wo nimza. Om eti teyei bei tul pavulek en e neumambu? En xel zeim e xe mapieing veil anghei tembuing.”
ACT 8:34 Tambiy tiwei xel veil e nikanzek veil eno teling wou Pilip, “Wa neil neing wou ay, bei poropet di luk en eti, emaxow o xel nge?”
ACT 8:35 Woyom Pilip neil qayeeng wei di yeip eivek qapiya yo wou tambiy tiyon, me neil Xoulek Nimza wou e en Yesu.
ACT 8:36 Ka luw di la wou sakwaing me la tyip wou memiing valu om tambiy on neil, “Wei, memiing inye. Nambei nya ekom a se teyei bei zipek?”
ACT 8:37 [De Pilip neil, “Wangwei wang bongis laleim dalus nei, yond wang teyei being zipek.” De moxo lewexe me neil, “A wongis bei Yesu kilisi yon Anutu Neu Moux.”]
ACT 8:38 Om moxo neil me karis nale, de luw Pilip xouing teila eivek memiing me Pilip lipek e.
ACT 8:39 Ka luw lek loum veil memiing, Laweeng Vambuing wei Tambiy Ngandoung eno lam lutika me qou Pilip de malang, om tambiy on se lox yei e no, ekom moxo di la wou sakwaing is xeilala me la beeng.
ACT 8:40 De Pilip yei bei la toundei eivek beyeeng Asdot, om la beyeeng tiyon me neil Xoulek Nimza eivek beyeeng sapa yon dekalekom la tyip Sisalia.
ACT 9:1 Kalekom Sol di luk niseikeing en embei bo nol wou Tambiy Ngandoung xe xel betiyeing me nyeis xel a mey, om la wou lumuki lukanzek,
ACT 9:2 me teling wou moxo bei e byex qapiya ti ena wou xomek qekueing ama eivek Damaskus, en kandek wangwei e gyei eti yeiw mendi betiwou wou Sakwaing Tiyon, moux o vex, ond e zeim axound xel ambei xel wei xeitueing o de na qou me noum Yerusalem.
ACT 9:3 Ka moxo la wou sakwaing me la paviy Damaskus, eno xeiyaing ti lam lutika nanghei tyoung gheyapu nei me tel evivekwou e.
ACT 9:4 Moxo oing me teila lek tembuing de ngo vya ti neil wou e, “Sol, Sol, nambei nya wang di wo nimaying wou ay?”
ACT 9:5 Sol teling, “Tambiy Ngandoung wang eti?” Moxo neil, “A Yesu, tiwei wang di wo nimaying wou yo.
ACT 9:6 Gweimbeeng qandi lek me la eivek beyeeng wei Damaskus nei, en tyek tambiy ti na neil wou wang en vati wei wang bong o.”
ACT 9:7 Xel xomaxoneing wei di la is Sol eno nale inyon de se wo lukluk, xel ngo vya ti ekom xel se yei xelti.
ACT 9:8 Sol qandi lek veil tembuing, ekom gyeik ingwei vindek manghalus lek eno moxo se yei lulti. Om xel zeim e mema me la eivek Damaskus.
ACT 9:9 Teyei lek bouk yal eno moxo manghalus nanghei toundei matekeing, om se ya lulti, o se num.
ACT 9:10 Betiyeing ti toundei eivek Damaskus e lei Ananias. Tambiy Ngandoung taxe la wou e eivek ingwei manghalus pekwi yo me neil, “Ananias!” Moxo neil elox, “Tambiy Ngandoung a toundei yo.”
ACT 9:11 Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou e, “Qandi lek me la xomek wei Yudas o, wou sakwaing mema wei xel mi taxe bei Sakwaing Bombek nei, me teling en xomaxoneing wei lam anghei Tarsus, e lei Sol, wei!, moxo di zeimema.
ACT 9:12 Eivek ingwei manghalus pekwi eno yei moux ti lei Ananias lam me liw mema lek e bei bong e manghalus gyeina no.”
ACT 9:13 Ananias neil elox bei, “Tambiy Ngandoung, a ngo qayeeng ngenong en moux tine, me nimaying dalus wei mi wong wou wa xe xel wei mi wongis wang eivek Yerusalem o.
ACT 9:14 De e lam inye is nikanzek wei lumuki leitata wong wou bei e nam a zeimaxoun xel dalus wei mi taxe wa leim o.”
ACT 9:15 Ekom Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou Ananias, “La! tambiy tinei inye a xe xukxe wei a beyal bei e qalei a leing me na wou xel amba, me xel king me wou xomaxoneing wei Israel o.
ACT 9:16 Tyek a talex wou e en nimaying maying wei embei qalei en a leing o.”
ACT 9:17 Woyom Ananias la eivek xomek me la lalei. De li mema lek Sol, moxo neil, “Ling Sol, Ka wang di lam inye eno Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu tyip wou wang wou sakwaing, eno wong a lam bei wang gweina no me Laweeng Vambuing e pup wang lek.”
ACT 9:18 De lutika eno lulti nambei bis teila veil Sol manghalus, om moxo teyeimbei gyeina no. De moxo qandi lek dom lipek,
ACT 9:19 Ka e ya yaeing valu woy, eno moxo qou nikanzek no. Sol dei inyon bouk valu is xel betiyeing eivek Damaskus.
ACT 9:20 Lutika eno moxo neil xoulek eivek xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw bei Yesu yon Anutu Neu Moux.
ACT 9:21 Xel dalus tiwei ngo e eno etek me teling, “Beip inyon tambiy tiwei mi leis xel eivek Yerusalem wei mi taxe lei tiyon o? Beip se lam inye bei na qou xel nambei xel xeitueing me na wou xel lumuki leitata?”
ACT 9:22 Ekom Sol wo nikanzek kamouyo, me neil xoulek yeip yanyateiv wou Yudayeiw wei mindei eivek Damaskus bei “Yesu yon Kilisi.”
ACT 9:23 Ka bouk ngenong la veil, om Yudayeiw qekuma me tup qayeeng lekti bei, xel embei na zeimaxoun Sol dom nyeis e mey,
ACT 9:24 ekom Sol qou kwa woy wou xel xe woueing nalei. Bendiyeing aluw boukeing eno xel mi toung mend wou tete mya wei Damaskus o, en xel embei nyeis e mey.
ACT 9:25 Ekom e xe xel betiyeing qou e eivek boukeing me lek tete ngandoung wei vivekwou beyeeng on me wong e lep me la eivek pasik ngandoung me e la tete demi veil beyeeng on.
ACT 9:26 Ka e la tyip Yerusalem, me moxo embei na is xel betiyeing, ekom xel dalus yaleeng en e de xel se wongis bei e wo betiyeing ti neing.
ACT 9:27 Ekom Banabas qou e me la wou xel wei sinale yo. Moxo neil wou xel bei Sol di lam wou sakwaing eno yei Tambiy Ngandoung me Tambiy Ngandoung luk wou e, me eivek Damaskus e luk nikanzek wou xel on eivek Yesu lei.
ACT 9:28 Om Sol toundei is xel me ghavineeng eivek Yerusalem, moxo se yaleeng qe di luk nikanzek en Tambiy Ngandoung lei.
ACT 9:29 E luk me nganeng is Yudayeiw wei mi luk Grik o en Yesu, ekom xel di wong en embei nyeis e mey.
ACT 9:30 Gyeik liyeiw ngo qayeeng tine, xel qou e me la Sisalia me wong e la Tarsus.
ACT 9:31 Woyom xel wongeingis eivek Yudia, Galili me Samaria eno dei wo nimza is ama. Xel valu se wo nol wou xel, om Laweeng Vambuing byexaxoun xel, de xel dei xeinghembi eivek Tambiy Ngandoung. De xel wongeingis nyouk me wo ngenong.
ACT 9:32 Ka Petele ghavineeng me la eivek beyeeng valuvalu nei, moxo la en embei na gyei xel wongeingis wei toundei eivek beyeeng Lida nei.
ACT 9:33 Nanghei inyon eno moxo yei xomaxoneing ti lei Ainias, tambiy on bezomb, om moxo mi yeip lek zek teyei lek vakovek qes lim yal.
ACT 9:34 Petele neil wou e, “Ainias, Yesu Kilisi wong wang wo nimzalek. Qandi me vevilexe wa xe ghus.” Lutika eno Ainias qandi.
ACT 9:35 Xel dalus tiwei mindei eivek Lida me Saron eno yei moxo wo nimzalek, om xel pekwi me loum wou Tambiy Ngandoung.
ACT 9:36 Eivek Jopa inyon betiyeing ti lei Tabita (xel pekwi bei Dokas), taxombouk eno vexo mi wo nimza me vind xel wei kanyo yo.
ACT 9:37 Lek bouk kayon vexo qou myavanei ti me mey, om xel lipek vexo dom liw e la eivek xomek lalei wei yeip ghey yo.
ACT 9:38 Lida yon di yeip paviy Jopa, de xel betiyeing ngo bei Petele la toundei Lida, om xel wong tambiy yuw la wou e me neil wou e, “Wang nam daing wou xa!”
ACT 9:39 Petele la is luw, me gyeik e la tyip eno xel qou e me la xomek gheyapu wei Dokas di yeip eivek on, vexeiv dalus on toungale vivekwou e, xel di eng me talex teimb wei Dokas mi duw o gyeik e ghei toundei mapieing is xel o.
ACT 9:40 Petele wong xel dalus la myayaing veil xomek lalei, woyom moxo ev vaxakatu eivek dom zeim. De pekwi ma lox wou meyeing me neil, “Tabita, qandi.” Vexo vindek malek me yei Petele dom qandi me dei ghey.
ACT 9:41 Moxo zeim e lek me vind e nale lek vaxa, woyom taxe xel Wongeingis me xel vexeiv lam, dom talex Tabita wou xel bei toundei mapieing.
ACT 9:42 Xuk ti Petele wong ne eno qayeeng la teyei lek beyeeng sapa wei Jopa nei, me xomaxoneing ngenong wongis Tambiy Ngandoung.
ACT 9:43 Petele dei eivek Jopa teyei lek bouk valu is tambiy ti lei Simon, tambiy on mi wo xuk lek manghaxo ninavi.
ACT 10:1 Nanghei Sisalia eno tambiy ti mi dei inyon eno lei Konilias, inyon beyeiv wei xel 100 vevekyeiw o wei xel mi taxe bei vevekyeiw qendu ti wei beyeeng Itali yo.
ACT 10:2 Moxo lis nipapu mi yaleeng me betiwou Anutu teyei lek bouk tambak, me mi vind xel wei kanyo yo. De taxombouk eno mi zeimema wou Anutu.
ACT 10:3 Bouk ti lek seivma yal wei soukeing eno Konilias mapekwi me yei bei Anutu xe angela ti lam di neil qayeeng wou e me neil embei, “Konilias!”
ACT 10:4 Konilias yaleeng me doma wou e, Moxo teling, “Tambiy Ngandoung, inye va?” Angela lewexe, “Wa xe zeimeing me vineing wei wang mi wong wou xel kanyo eno la gheyapu wou Anutu manghalus nambei da wei woueing nalei en o.
ACT 10:5 Om wong moux valu la Jopa me qou tambiy tiwei lei Simon o me loum. Wei xel mi taxe e lei nge eno Petele.
ACT 10:6 Moxo mindei is Simon tambiy wei mi wo xuk lek manghaxo ninavi yo, wei e beeng di yeip wou mamileeng nenyawes o.”
ACT 10:7 Ka angela luk is e woy dom la, woyom Konilias taxe e xe xukxe yuw me xel vevekyeiw eno ti wei mi betiwou Anutu me mi yeiwou xow woy en xuk wei Konilias o.
ACT 10:8 Moxo neil wou lal en lulul sapa wei tyip on dom wong lal la Jopa.
ACT 10:9 Lek bouk nge yanyeing wei seivma evlek eno tambiy yal on la tyip paviy beyeeng ngandoung Jopa, de Petele lek la xomek demi qetyei bei na zeim mema.
ACT 10:10 Moxo maxepya om embei gya lul yaeing valu, ka xel di yeiwou lul yaeing, eno moxo manghalus pekwi me yei.
ACT 10:11 Moxo yei tyoung gheyapu tax me lulti nambei qaeing ngandoung ti, wei xel byex yis eivek nenyawes vey de wong e tei lam lek tembuing.
ACT 10:12 Eivek qaeing on eno pup en leliy leliy wei vaxa vey eno lam eivek tiyon me ingwei mi yelek tembuing me menek menek o.
ACT 10:13 Woyom vya ti neil wou e, “Petele, qandi, de leis me wa.”
ACT 10:14 Petele neil elox bei, “Se teyei, Tambiy Ngandoung! A se mi xa lul wei nilul o nilaxes o ti.”
ACT 10:15 Woyom vya tine neil wou e luyuw, “Wa se taxe lulti nilaxes wei Anutu wong e wo vako yo.”
ACT 10:16 Tine wo luyal, de lutika eno qaeing ngandoung tiyon leklox me la tyoung gheyapu.
ACT 10:17 Kalekom Petele di wounalei ngenong en ingwei manghalus pekwi me yei eno qes, de moux yal wei Konilias wong lal la eno la yeiwou Simon beeng om lal nale wou tete mya.
ACT 10:18 Xel taxe la me teling bei, “Simon tiwei lei nge bei Petele eno toundei inye?”
ACT 10:19 Ka Petele nanghei di wounalei en ingwei manghalus pekwi me yei vati yo, eno Laweeng Vambuing neil wou e bei, “Simon, moux yayal di yimexe wang o.
ACT 10:20 Om qandi me lep me la xonei, wa seng bounaleim ngenong en laeing is lal, en a wong lal lak.”
ACT 10:21 Petele la xonei me neil wou lal, “A tiwei mal ghe di wimexe eno inye. Mal ghe lam en va?”
ACT 10:22 Moux yal on neil elox, “Konilias beyeiv wei xel vevek o wong ghal a lam. E yon bombek me tambiy wei mi yaleeng en Anutu yo, e tiwei xel Yudayeiw dalus mi wevek e xeinghembi yo. Angela vambuing neil wou bei wang na e xe xomek en kandek e ngo vati wei wambei neil o.”
ACT 10:23 Woyom Petele neil wou moux yal on me qou lal me la eivek beeng me yeiteyei lal boukeing tiyon. Nge yanyeing eno Petele la is lal me xel wongeingis valu nanghei Jopa eno la is.
ACT 10:24 Yanyeing eno xel la tyip Sisalia. Konilias di wou kwa en xel, me taxe nipapu dalus me gweleeng yeiw wei mindei paviy e yo me xel qeku la toundei.
ACT 10:25 Ka Petele la eivek xomek, Konilias la pelong e me ev vaxa qatu eivek de wo lalo wou e.
ACT 10:26 Ekom Petele wong e nale ghey. De neil wou e, “Nale, a maxow ne moux bandaing.”
ACT 10:27 De Petele la lalei me luk is e, me yei xomaxoneing qendu ngandoung ti di qekuma.
ACT 10:28 Moxo neil wou xel, “Xam venaxow ghe woulek e wo nimza bei, Inyei se la teyei lek xa xe petieing bei Yudayeiw ti na mendei is xel amba o na paviy xel. Ekom Anutu talex wou ay bei a se taxe xelti bei e nilul o e nilaxes.
ACT 10:29 Om a se pyalek wa vyam wei wang taxe ay yo. Qe a lam teyei lek wa vyam, om ambei teling xam bei xam ghe taxe ay en va?”
ACT 10:30 Konilias lewexe, “Bouk vey lak veil eno a toundei eivek bang me na zeimemang lek seivma tine, lek seivma yal wei soukeing o. Lutika eno tambiy ti byex teimb wei teltyip eno nale wou a manghalus
ACT 10:31 me neil, ‘Konilias, Anutu ngo wa xe zeimeing mema me wounalei en wa xe wongeing wei wang mi wong wou xel kanyo yo.
ACT 10:32 Om wong xelti la Jopa en Simon wei xel mi taxe lei nge bei Petele yo. Moxo la toundei eivek xomek wei Simon wei mi wo xuk lek manghaxo ninavi yo, wei e xe xomek toundei wou mamileeng nenyawes o.’
ACT 10:33 Om a wong tambiy yal lak lutika, dom inye nimza bei wang lam. Gweimbeeng wei xe xouing dalus a toundei inye wou Anutu manghalus bei na ngo wou lul sapa wei Tambiy Ngandoung peti wou wang bei wa neil wou xa yo.”
ACT 10:34 Woyom Petele embei baluk: “Gweimbeeng a woulek zonghek bei inyon Anutu se mi talex lalei vineing wou xelti venaxow
ACT 10:35 qe mi lewexe lek xomaxoneing wei lam anghei tembuing tambak nei me mi yaleeng en e me mi wong vati wei bombek o.
ACT 10:36 Xam ghe woulek qayeeng wei Anutu wong ela wou xomaxoneing wei Israel o, me neil Xoulek Nimza wei lalei vevopeing wei lam eivek Yesu Kilisi yo, e tiwei wo Tambiy Ngandoung en lul dalusateiv o.
ACT 10:37 Xam ghe woulek lul tambak woy wei belup ela teyei lek tembuing sapa wei Yudia nei. Dekakom Yoan neil qayeeng wei lipekeing o. Lul ne qandi tax eivek Galili.
ACT 10:38 Xam ghe woulek bei Anutu beyal Yesu wei Nasaret o me wong Laweeng Vambuing me nikanzek wou e, me xam ghe woulek ingwei e la ghavinenyeing me vind xel me wong xel dalus wei mindei xeinghembi eivek nikanzek wei tambiy mapetok o wo nimzalek, en nambei Anutu toundei is e.
ACT 10:39 “Xa xei lek mami en lul dalus wei Yesu wong eivek tembuing tambak wei Yudayeiw me eivek Yerusalem o. Xel leis e mey nangya ingwei xel teyu e lek xax o,
ACT 10:40 ekom Anutu piyexe e veil meyeing lek bouk yal, de lenghek lek bei xomaxoneing gyei e.
ACT 10:41 Xomaxoneing dalus on se yei e, qe xel wei yei eno inyon Anutu beyal xel wongeingis wei xa mi xa me na num is e gyeik ingwei qandi lek veil meyeing o.
ACT 10:42 E wong qayeeng nikanzek wou xa bei xa neil qayeeng wou xomaxoneing me na neil teyeimbei, e tambiy tiwei Anutu beyal bei e zeim qayeeng wei mapieing me meyeing o.
ACT 10:43 Poropet dalus neil e teyei bei xel dalus wei wongis e eno mi semaleeng xel xe sewokeing veil eivek Yesu lei.”
ACT 10:44 Ka Petele nanghei di neil qayeeng tine, Laweeng Vambuing lam axone lek xomaxoneing dalus wei ngo qayeeng ne yo.
ACT 10:45 Xel wongeingis wei ghuw nindnavi me lam is Petele eno etek en vineing wei Laweeng Vambuing qapyex elam lek xel wei bamba yo is.
ACT 10:46 En xel ngo ingwei xel on di luk eivek vya vya me sanghoxe Anutu yo. Woyom Petele neil,
ACT 10:47 “Eti teyeimbei bale zeyi xomaxoneing ne en ingwei xel embei zipek eivek memiing o? En xel qou Laweeng Vambuing nambei ingwei xey a qou ne.”
ACT 10:48 Om moxo wong qayeeng nikanzek wou xel bei, “Xel a qou lipekeing eivek Yesu Kilisi lei.” Woyom xel teling wou Petele bei e toumendei is xel bouk valu.
ACT 11:1 Xel sinale me liyeiw wei mindei lala eivek distrik Yudia eno ngo qayeeng tiyon bei, xel amba eno qou xoulek wei Anutu yo is ambei nyon.
ACT 11:2 De gyeik Petele la pu wei Yerusalem nei, xel betiyeing wo ninkanzek en kwa wei ghuweing ninavi veil o, om xel neil qayeeng lox me loum lek e,
ACT 11:3 de xel neil, “Wang la eivek xel moux wei se ghuw ninavi yo bend me ghe wa is xel.”
ACT 11:4 Woyom Petele neilteyei wou xel bombek en lul sapa wei belup o:
ACT 11:5 Moxo neil, “A mindei eivek beyeeng ngandoung wei Jopa nei me na mi zeimemang eno a manghalus pekwi me na xei. A xei lulti nambei qaeing ngandoung wei xel byex yis lek nenyawes vey eno tei lam anghei tyoung gheyapu, me lam wou ingwei a toundei ghei yo.
ACT 11:6 A xei la eivek lalei me na xei leliy wei vaxa vey wei tembuing o, a xei leliy leliy bemeeng, me leliy leliy wei mi yelek bambound o, me menek menek wei gheyapu yo.
ACT 11:7 Woyom a ngo vya ti neil wou ay, ‘Petele, qandi lek, leis leliy on me wa.’
ACT 11:8 “A neil bei, ‘Ma, se teyei ti, Tambiy Ngandoung! Lul wei nilul o, me ingwei nilaxes o ti se mi lam eivek a myang ne.’
ACT 11:9 “Ekom vya tine luk e loum anghei tyoung gheyapu nei luyuw no, ‘Wa se taxe lul wei Anutu wong e wo vako yon nilaxes.’
ACT 11:10 Tine belup luyal, de woyom lul dalus tiyon leklox me la tyoung gheyapu no.
ACT 11:11 “Lek bouk kayon bombek, eno moux yal wei lam anghei Sisalia eno lam nale ghei ingwei a toundei ghei yo.
ACT 11:12 Laweeng Vambuing neil wou ay bei, ‘Wa seng bounaleim ngenong en ingwei wa being na is xel o.’ Moux limti beimambei ne lindama eno lam is ay, me xa la eivek moux moxon beeng.
ACT 11:13 Moxo neil wou xa en ingwei yei angela ti eno lam tyip wou e eivek e beeng on me neil, ‘Wong xel la Jopa wou Simon tiwei xel mi taxe e bei Petele yo.
ACT 11:14 Moxo tyek na qou qayeeng me nak wou wang, de eivek qayeeng on eno wang me wa xe xel dalus wei xomek on eno tyek Anutu devind xam veil meyeing.’
ACT 11:15 “Ka a di luk wou xel eno Laweeng Vambuing lam lek xel nambei ingwei lam lek xey myaxeeng o.
ACT 11:16 Woyom a wou naleind en vati wei Tambiy Ngandoung neil o: ‘Yoan lipek xomaxoneing en memiing, ekom tyek xam ghe zipek en Laweeng Vambuing.’
ACT 11:17 Om wangwei Anutu bong lul nimza ti wei teyeima nambei ingwei wong wou xe wei wongis Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu Kilisi, yond ay eti, a teyei bei paseisexe Anutu!”
ACT 11:18 Ka xel ngo qayeeng tine woy eno xel tip xel xe qayeeng lukeing lox me loum wouma dom sanghoxe Anutu me neil, “Woyom Anutu e zenghek lek xel amba bei xel pekwi xow me na qou mapieing.”
ACT 11:19 Gweimbeeng xel wongeingis ngenong pek me vuwama lala en ingwei xel leis Setepan mey o, eno valu pek me la Ponisia, Saiprus me Antiok, eno xel di neil qayeeng wou Yudayeiw venaxow.
ACT 11:20 Ekom moux valu nanghei Saiprus me Sairini eno la Antiok me luk wou xel Grik is ambei nyon, me neil wou xel en Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu xe Xoulek Nimza.
ACT 11:21 Tambiy Ngandoung nikanzek toundei is xel, om xomaxoneing ngenong wongis me pekwi xow me loum wou Tambiy Ngandoung.
ACT 11:22 Qayeeng tine eno la eivek xel wongeingis anghei Yerusalem o nenyend, om xel wong Banabas la Antiok.
ACT 11:23 Ka moxo la tyip me yei Anutu xe lalei xeiles wei wo neing lek eno toundei is xel, om moxo wo xeilala me byexaxoun xel dalus bei xel a mi mendei is laleind tixemou wou Tambiy Ngandoung is laleind dalus.
ACT 11:24 Moxo yon moux nimza, wei pup en Laweeng Vambuing me e xe wongeingis eno wo nikanzek. Me xomaxoneing ngenong eno xel lam is xel wei Tambiy Ngandoung o.
ACT 11:25 Woyom Banabas la Tarsus me la yimexe Sol,
ACT 11:26 ka moxo yeiwou e, qou e me la Antiok. Lek vakovek qes tiyon dalus, Banabas aluw Sol dei is xel wongeingis me mi teyoxe xomaxoneing ngenongakes. Nanghei Antiok eno xel betiyeing qou leind Klisten ti myaxeeng o.
ACT 11:27 Eivek bouk tine eno xel poropet valu lam anghei Yerusalem me lam axo wei Antiok ne.
ACT 11:28 Xel poropet on ti, lei Agabus, nale ghey me eivek Laweeng Vambuing eno moxo neilteyei bei tyek maxep ngandoung nam wou xel me na teyei lek tembuing sapa wei Rom o. (Tine lam eivek bouk wei Klodias toundei king o.)
ACT 11:29 Xel betiyeing titi wong malew e teyei lek xel xe nikanzek, xel embei devind liyeiw wei toundei eivek Yudia nei.
ACT 11:30 Xel wong tine, me wong xel xe vineing me Banabas aluw Sol qou me la wou teivateiv wei Yerusalem o.
ACT 12:1 Lek bouk ambei nye, king Herot zeimaxoun xel valu wei xel wongeingis o, en embei bo nol wou xel.
ACT 12:2 Moxo neil me xel wo nol wou Jems, inyon Yoan li moux, me leis e mey angya ngeyeing vevek.
ACT 12:3 Herot yei bei lul tiwei e wong ne wo nimza wou xel Yudayeiw mendghalus, om moxo di wong en embei zeimaxoun Petele is ambei nyon. Herot wong tine lek Bouk Wei Yaeing Belet Wei Yis Ma Veil o.
ACT 12:4 Ka xel zeimaxoun e, Herot toung moxo eivek xomek xeitueing, me wong e la eivek xel belimbo yon memend, xel belimbo yon qendu vey om xel embei qou e me na myayaing me bong qayeeng en e yanyateiv eivek xomaxoneing on mendghalus, loxyus en bouk wei Pasova yo.
ACT 12:5 Om xel di yei Petele teyei eivek xomek xeitueing, ekom xel wongeingis di zeimemend bei Anutu e devind Petele.
ACT 12:6 Boukeing nge wei la tax en ingwei Herot embei qou e me na eivek xomek wei zeimeing qayeeng o, eno Petele di yeip eivek xel vevek on yuw senghoing, xel tup en sen yuw, de vevekyeiw valu toungale zeyi xomek xeitueing on mya.
ACT 12:7 Se wo lululek en angela wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe eno lam tyip me xeiyaing tel la eivek xomek xeitueing on lalei. Angela byex mema lek e byek de piyexe e. Moxo neil, “Qandi lek Daing!” Dom sen kwax veil e mema.
ACT 12:8 Woyom angela neil wou e, “vex wa xe let vivekwou xow me byex vaxalambes lek.” Om Petele wong ambei e neil o. Angela neil wou e no, “Byex wa xe teimb ding de betiy ay.”
ACT 12:9 Petele betiwou e me la myayaing veil xeitueing, ekom moxo se woulek bei angela di wong tiyon neing ayang wou e, qe moxo embeik nge manghalus pekwi me yei.
ACT 12:10 Luw la ghanaw xomek mya tiwei tax o me la nge wei yuw o is xel belimbo yon dom lam wou tiwei mya aen wei la wou beyeeng ngandoung o. Xomek mya aen on venaxow tax en luw, dom luw la lox me la myayaing. Gyeik luw di tupwou sakwaing mema nayak on ti me la, se wou lululek en angela malang.
ACT 12:11 Woyom Petele mavindek lek de yeila me neil, “A se bou naleind ngenong en a woulek gweimbeeng bei Tambiy Ngandoung wong e xe angela lam zeim a veil Herot xe lalei vanei me veil lul dalus wei xomaxoneing wei Yudayeiw embei bong o.”
ACT 12:12 Ka e lu yeip yaing en tine, moxo la Maria beeng. Maria neu yon Yoan de e lei nge eno Malaka, nanghei inyon eno xomaxoneing ngenong qekuma me di zeimemend.
ACT 12:13 Petele leis mema lek qapomb tiwei myayaing o, me xukxe vex ti lei Roda lam en embei tax qapomb.
ACT 12:14 Ekom vexo woulek Petele vya, vexo wo xeilala mouyo, om veimya me lox dom se tax xomek mya qe lox me neil embei, “Petele toungale wou qapomb.”
ACT 12:15 Xel neil wou e, “Wang loung o.” Ekom vexo di wo lukendu lek me neil embei inye e yo, xel neil no, “Beind inyon e xe angela yo.”
ACT 12:16 Ekom Petele nanghei di leis mema lek qapomb, om xel tax qapomb me yei e, xel etek en e.
ACT 12:17 Om Petele pepeeng xel angya mema bei xel se baluk, qe e neilteyei wou xel en ingwei Tambiy Ngandoung qou e me lam myayaing veil xeitueing o woy, De moxo neil embei, “Xam aneil wou Jems me liyeiw en tine.” Woyom moxo la veil xel me la beyeeng nge.
ACT 12:18 De satiboukeing, eno xel vevekyeiw loung en Petele en mama, om xel etek me neil embei, “Petele la nya?”
ACT 12:19 Herot wo xuk lek Petele yimexeing ekom se yeiwou e, moxo lox me la wo telinyeing wou xel vevek me luk nikanzek bei xel a mey. Woyom Herot la nanghei Yudia me la Sisalia me la dei inyon nayaka.
ACT 12:20 Herot wo veweeng ngandoung is xomaxoneing wei Taia me Saidon o. Om xel xouing toung lekti me lam yei e bei embo lalei vevopeing is xel, en nambei xel xe beyeeng ngandoung on mi qou vineing en yaeing lam eivek king Herot xe tembuing. Om xel luk is Blastus wei king xe xukxe me e lalei la is xel.
ACT 12:21 Lek bouk wei Herot beyal, eno moxo vunek en e xe teimb ding wei king o, me dei lek e xe siaking de wong qayeeng wou xomaxoneing sapa yon.
ACT 12:22 De woyom xel wei ngo qayeeng on taxe bei, “Vya tine inye anutu ti vya, se xomaxoneing ti vya.”
ACT 12:23 Om lutika eno angela wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe eno ti leis e, me meii ya e lalei lalei ma de mey en Herot se sanghoxe Anutu.
ACT 12:24 Ekom xoulek wei Anutu yon la wo ngandoung me la beyeeng tambak.
ACT 12:25 De Banabas aluw Sol wong luw xe xuk sinale ma, om luw loum veil Yerusalem me lox me la Antiok, de luw qou Yoan wei lei nge Malaka eno is xow.
ACT 13:1 Eivek kongrikesin wei Antiok eno inye xel poropet me xel putoung mi dei inyon eno xel leind ambei nye: Banabas, me Simion wei xel mi taxe e lei nge bei Ningak me Lusias wei Sairini, me Manain (e nipapu wei Herot seyap ngandoung o) me Sol.
ACT 13:2 Ka xel di wo lalo wou Tambiy Ngandoung me di vambu yaeing, Laweeng Vambuing neil wou xel bei, “Xam beyal Banabas aluw Sol wou ay en xuk tiwei a taxe luw en o.”
ACT 13:3 Om ka xel vambu yaeing me zeimemend, xel liw memend lek luw dom wong luw la.
ACT 13:4 Laweeng Vambuing wong luw la xo wei beyeeng Selusia nei me qou sip nanghei inyon me la Saiprus, tembuing danghei tiwei di yeip eivek mamileeng o.
ACT 13:5 Luw la tyip Salamis, luw neil Anutu xe xoulek eivek xel Yudayeiw xe xomek qekueing ama. De Yoan mindei is luw nambei luw xe vineing.
ACT 13:6 Luw la tup eivek Saiprus tembuing nayak wei mi yeip eivek mamileeng on dalus dekakom luw la tyip beyeeng Papos. Nanghei inyon eno luw yei Yuda ti wei mi wo palak me e poropet wei tyonyeing o lei Ba-Yesu,
ACT 13:7 tambiy on mindei is lei ngandoung wei seyap o lei Segius Paulus, lei ngandoung wei seyap on lupeyei nimza om wong qayeeng la wou Banabas aluw Sol bei luw na neil Anutu xe xoulek en embei ngo.
ACT 13:8 Ekom Elimas on Ba-Yesu (en inye qes wei e lei eno nambei inye) tambiy wei wevek o eno mi pesek xuk wei luw o. En mi wong en embei pelipek seyap lei ngandoung lalei bei e se bongis Yesu.
ACT 13:9 Woyom Sol, e lei nge wei xel taxe eno Paulus, eno pup en Laweeng Vambuing, moxo yei Elimas kanzek dom neil,
ACT 13:10 “Wang on tambiy mapetok neu me wang mi wo vevek is lul dalus wei bombek o! Wang pup en lul nilul leimalei wei tyonyeing o. Gyeik inya ekom wa tip kwa wei wang mi pakei qayeeng neing wei Tambiy Ngandoung eno la wo qayeeng tyonyeing.
ACT 13:11 Ekom Tambiy Ngandoung mema wo vevek is wang. Wa mam on tyek na tuzeyi, me tyek wa seng gwei xeiyaing wei sayeiv o, qe tyek wa mendei nambei nyon enden ka.” Lutika eno laxap me mapetok lam beliv e manghalus, moxo la bandabanda, me di yimexe xel valu bei xel a zeim e mema me na.
ACT 13:12 Lei ngandoung wei seyap eno yei vati wei belup on, de moxo wongis, en nambei moxo etek en teyoxeing wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe yo.
ACT 13:13 Nanghei Papos, Paulus me e xe xel nipapu la lek sip me la beyeeng Pelga eivek tembuing danghei wei Pampilia yo, dekakom Yoan lox veil xel me la Yerusalem.
ACT 13:14 Nanghei Pelga eno xel la beyeeng nayak Antiok wei tembuing danghei wei Pisidia nei. Lek bouk Sabat eno xel la eivek xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o me la dei.
ACT 13:15 Ka gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama eno pyaw qayeeng Petieing, me qayeeng Poropet ma woy, tambiy wei mi yeiteyei xomek qekueing ama eno wong qayeeng la wou xel, me neil, “Xam lingyeiw, wangwei xam mendi qou qayeeng wei embei ghandu xound xel xomaxoneing nei, on xam a neil.”
ACT 13:16 Paulus nale ghey de pepeeng xel angya mema, dom neil: “Xam moux wei Israel me xam ba wei ghe mi waleeng en Anutu yo, xam ngo wou a le!
ACT 13:17 Anutu tiwei Israel xe eno beyal xa bumiyeiw. Moxo wong Israelyeiw wo ngenong gyeik xel mindei eivek Izip o, moxo qou xel lam myayaing veil beyeeng tiyon nangya nikanzek ngandoung wei e yo.
ACT 13:18 Moxo mi qalei nimaying wei xel xe deing o teyei lek vakovek qes xoumeeng vey (40) eivek beyeeng bandaing on.
ACT 13:19 Ka Anutu semaleeng xomaxoneing velei lim yuw eivek Kenan, wong xel xe tembuing wou e xe xomaxoneing nambei xel xe lulul nimza.
ACT 13:20 Lul tine dalus eno qandi teyei lek vakovek qes 450. “Ka tine la veil eno Anutu beyal xel gyovaxa wei xel gyeiteyei xel Israel me ena tyip wou bouk wei poropet Samuel o.
ACT 13:21 Woyom xel moux alis vex teling en king ti, om Anutu wong Sol wei Kis neu moux eno wou xel, inyon velei wei Benyamin o, wei yeiteyei xel teyei lek vakovek qes xoumeeng vey (40).
ACT 13:22 Ka Anutu laluwexe Sol, moxo beyal Dawit wo xel xe king. Moxo neil e teyei wou xel: ‘A xeiwou Dawit wei Jesi neu moux wei a maxow laleing vind o. Moxo tyek bong lul tambak wei ambei e bong o.’
ACT 13:23 “Om Anutu wong Yesu lam, inyon Dawit buyeiw ti, Tambiy wei vind xey veil nimaying eno wou xel Israel, nambei ingwei e neil zonghek o.
ACT 13:24 De gyeik Yesu se ghei lam, Yoan teyoxe xel en qayeeng wei pekwieing xow o me lipekeing eno wou xel Israel dalus.
ACT 13:25 Deka lam paviy ingwei Yoan wong e xe xuk ma, moxo neil, ‘Xam ghe wou naleimim bei ay eti? A se tambiy tiyon. Ma, ekom tyek moxo mendi nam yus en ay, e tiwei a se teyei bei tul yis veil e xe vaxalambes o.’
ACT 13:26 “Xam lingyeiw wei Apraham neuyeiw, me xam ba wei ghe mi waleeng en Anutu yo, eno xam ngo. Qayeeng tiwei Yesu embei devind e xe moux alis vex veil meyeing eno Anutu wong e lam wou xey.
ACT 13:27 Xel xomaxoneing wei mindei eivek Yerusalem me xel xe gyovaxa eno se yeimend wou qayeeng wei xel poropet o, wei xel mi pyaw eivek Sabat titi yo. Qe, xel byex qayeeng lek Yesu me qayeeng wei poropet neil eno wo neing lek.
ACT 13:28 De xel se yeiwou sewokeing ti eivek e bei bo qayeeng en e me nyeis e mey, om xel teling Pailat bei e nyeis e mey.
ACT 13:29 Xel wong lul dalus wei xel poropet byex eivek qapiya en e yo woy, eno xel zewax e tei lam veil xax me liw e eivek eeng ti.
ACT 13:30 Ekom Anutu piyexe e qandi lek veil meyeing,
ACT 13:31 de bouk ngenong eno Yesu talex xow wou xel wei mi la is e eno la veil Galili me la Yerusalem. Gweimbeeng xel wei yeimawou eno neil Yesu teyei wou xa xe xomaxoneing.
ACT 13:32 “Xa neil Xoulek Nimza wou xam: En vati wei Anutu neil zonghek is xe bundyeiw o
ACT 13:33 moxo wong qayeeng wo neing lek en xey wei xel neundyeiw o, en piyexe Yesu qandi lek veil meyeing. Nambei ingwei xel byex eivek qapiya lalo tiwei yuw o bei: “‘Wang on a neung, gweimbeeng a wong ambei wa mam.’
ACT 13:34 Om Anutu piyexe e veil meyeing, de se teyei bei patal, om neil eivek qayeeng ti beimambei ne: “‘Tyek am bong mata wei vambuing me zonghek wei a neil wou Dawit eno wou xam.’
ACT 13:35 Om moxo neil no eivek qapiya lalo nge nambei nye: “‘Tyek wa seng teyei bei bong wa xe tiwei vambuing eno daxe pataleing.’
ACT 13:36 “Eivek bouk wei Dawit mi dei eno mi betiwou Anutu lalei. Deka moxo mey, xel ev is mayeiw me e neing patal.
ACT 13:37 Ekom e tiwei Anutu piyexe e veil meyeing eno se axe pataleing.
ACT 13:38 “Nambei nyon, xam lingyeiw, xa neil wou xam bei. Xam ghe boulek bei Yesu wei xa neil wou xam eno teyeimbei semaleeng sewokeing wei xam o.
ACT 13:39 Petieing wei Mose yo se teyei bei semaleeng xam xe sewokeing veil. Ekom wangwei xelti bongis Yesu yond Anutu semaleeng e xe sewokeing dalus de wong e wo bombek.
ACT 13:40 Om xam ghe gweiteyei xow en kandek lul wei poropet neil ne eno se nam atyip wou xam:
ACT 13:41 “‘Wei, xam wei ghe mi wo vyamim wou Anutu xe qayeeng ne, eno tyek xam ghe detek me ghe bo nol, en tyek am bong lul tiwei tyek xam seng teyei bei bongis eno eivek xam senghoing de woyom wangwei xelti neil wou xam atax en inye nei, ond tyek xam seng bongis.’”
ACT 13:42 Ka Paulus aluw Banabas la veil xomek qekueing ama, xel xomaxoneing neil wou luw bei luw noum a neil qayeeng valu wou xel lek Sabat nge yus no.
ACT 13:43 Moux alis vex la myayaing veil xomek qekueing ama, eno xel Yudayeiw ngenong me xel amba wei mi betiwou kwa wei xel Yuda yo eno xel betiy Paulus aluw Banabas, de luw wo qayeeng wei e beil xel lundlek en xel ami mendei nikanzek eivek Anutu xe lalei xeiles.
ACT 13:44 Lek bouk Sabat nge yus eno xomaxoneing wei beyeeng ngandoung on valu beti qekuma me la ngo Tambiy Ngandoung xe qayeeng.
ACT 13:45 Gyeik xel Yudayeiw yei Xomaxoneing qendu ngandoung on, xel laleind wo nilul me lukyak lek Paulus en vati wei di neil o.
ACT 13:46 Woyom Paulus aluw Banabas luk nikanzek wou xel bei: “Xa bei neil Anutu xe qayeeng wou xam atax. Ekom xam ghe pesek me ghe toung demimim wou en xam ambei se qou mapieing luta luta, om xa pekwi me na la wou xel amba.
ACT 13:47 Inye vati wei Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou xa yo: “‘A wo wang wong ambei xeiyaing wei xel amba yo, en kandek wa devind xomaxoneing wei tembuing tambak veil meyeing.’”
ACT 13:48 Xel amba ngo tine, xel wo xeindlala me pamilexe Tambiy Ngandoung xe qayeeng. Me xel dalus wei Anutu beyal en mapieing luta luta eno wongis.
ACT 13:49 De Tambiy Ngandoung xe qayeeng on la wo tambak eivek tembuing danghei tiyon dalus.
ACT 13:50 Ekom Yudayeiw zeim xel vex wei leind tata wei mindei xeinghembi eivek Anutu me zeim xel gyovaxa wei beyeeng ngandoung on laleind lek. Om xel zeimaxoun Paulus aluw Banabas, me tiy luw la veil beyeeng ngandoung on.
ACT 13:51 Om luw pepa vegyuveeng veil vaxend bei xel on boulek bei xel wo sewokeing en kwa wei xel wong on, dom luw la veil Antiok me la beyeeng nayak Aikoniam.
ACT 13:52 De xel betiyeing eno pup en xeindlala me Laweeng Vambuing.
ACT 14:1 Eivek beyeeng nayak Aikoniam, Paulus me Banabas wong ambei ingwei luw mi wong o, me la eivek xomek qekueing ama wei xel Yudayeiw o. Nanghei inyon eno luw neil xoulek wo nimza om xel ngenong wei Yudayeiw me xel amba eno wongis.
ACT 14:2 Ekom xel Yudayeiw wei mi pesek en embei se bongis eno zeim xel amba laleind lek me xel laleind wo nilul wou xel wei wongis o.
ACT 14:3 Om Paulus aluw Banabas dei enden ka eivek inyon, de luw se yaleeng en neileing qayeeng wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe lalei xeiles o, om Anutu wong ninkanzek wou luw me luw wong dee wei lulvako leimalei yo.
ACT 14:4 Xel xomaxoneing wei beyeeng ngandoung on dembuma la yuw, om xel valu la is Yudayeiw, de valu la is sinaleyeiw.
ACT 14:5 Woyom xel amba me Yudayeiw is xel xe gyovaxa tup qayeeng wouma bei bo nol wou Paulus aluw Banabas me banex luw a mey angya qakous.
ACT 14:6 Ekom luw woulek inyon, om luw pek me la eivek tembuing danghei wei Likonia eivek beyeeng nayak yuw wei Listra me Debi, me beyeeng beyeeng wei toundei paviy yo,
ACT 14:7 nanghei inyon eno luw lox me la neil Xoulek Nimza no.
ACT 14:8 Eivek Listra inyon tambiy ti mindei, eno vaxa bezomb gyeik ingwei umbek o, om moxo se mi ghavineeng.
ACT 14:9 Moxo mi ngo ingwei Paulus mi luk on, Paulus doma wou e, me yeimbei moxo wongis me e teyeimbei bo nimza lek.
ACT 14:10 Om Paulus taxe la bei, “Nale lek vaxam!” Woyom moux moxo nale ghey de tetyeik me la.
ACT 14:11 Xomaxoneing qendu ngandoung on yei vati wei Paulus wong on, om xel taxe la eivek Likonia vyend bei, “Anutu lam axone wou xey nambei xomaxoneing!”
ACT 14:12 Banabas, xel taxe e lei bei anutu Sus, me Paulus xel taxe bei anutu Helmes, en nambei e mi la tax en lukeing.
ACT 14:13 Xomek lalo wei anutu Sus eno toundei paviy tete mya wei beyeeng ngandoung on, om lumuki wei xomek lalo yon me xel xomaxoneing on qou manghaxo moux me palawa me la tete mya wei beyeeng ngandoung on en xel embei besei xound wou luw.
ACT 14:14 Ekom sinale Banabas aluw Paulus ngo tine, luw lex luw xe teimb dom veimyend me la senghoing eivek xel qendu yon me taxe bei:
ACT 14:15 “Xam moux, xam ghe di wong tine en va? Uw ne xomaxoneing is me xomaxoneing nambei xam. Uw a di qou Xoulek Nimza me na lam wou xam, om uw a neil wou xam bei xam pekwi xow veil lul nilul tine de ghe na wou Anutu mapieing, e tiwei toung tyoung aluw tembuing me mamileeng me lulul sapa wei toundei eivek o.
ACT 14:16 Eivek bouk wei takwei yo eno moxo wong xel tembuing dalus on betiwou xel venaxow xe sakwaing.
ACT 14:17 Ekom e venaxow se xupek en xomaxoneing bei xel se boulek e. Ma. Taxombouk eno moxo mi talex e xe kwa nimza wou xam. Moxo mi wong luing lam anghei tyoung eivek xam xe lulul wei xam ghe ev eivek xuk o, me moxo wong yaeing ngenong wou xam is me wong xam laleimim wo xeilala.”
ACT 14:18 Luw neil qayeeng tine wou xel, ekom xel wo nikanzek bei besei xound wou luw. Om luw neil nikanzek bei xel se besei xound wou luw.
ACT 14:19 Woyom Yudayeiw valu lam anghei Antiok me Aikoniam me zeim xel qendu yon laleind lek. Om xel nex Paulus angya qakous me tetei ela myayaing veil beyeeng ngandoung on, de xel embeik nge moxo mey.
ACT 14:20 Ekom ka xel betiyeing qekuma vivekwou e, de moxo qandi lek me lox me la eivek beyeeng ngandoung on. De yanyeing eno Paulus aluw Banabas la Debi.
ACT 14:21 Luw neil Xoulek Nimza eivek beyeeng ngandoung tiyon me qou xel ngenong wo betiyeing. Woyom luw lox me la Listra, Aikoniam me Antiok,
ACT 14:22 me luw byexaxoun xel betiyeing laleind me neil qayeeng nikanzek wou xel bei, “Xam a mi mendei embo nikanzek eivek wongeingis me zonghek. Tyek xey a na eivek nimaying ngenong atax en kandek nana eivek tete lalei wei Anutu yo”.
ACT 14:23 Paulus aluw Banabas beyal xel gyovaxa eivek kongrikesin titi. De luw vambu yaeing me zeimemend, me toung xel la wou Tambiy Ngandoung, inyon eti yeiw wei wongis Tambiy Ngandoung o.
ACT 14:24 Ka luw la senghoing eivek tembuing danghei wei Pisidia, me la tyip eivek tembuing danghei wei Pampilia,
ACT 14:25 me luw la neil xoulek eivek beyeeng nayak Pelga, dekakom luw la xo wei beyeeng Atalia nei.
ACT 14:26 Nanghei Atalia luw la eivek sip me lox me la Antiok, inyon beyeeng wei xel wong luw la eivek lalei xeiles wei Anutu yo en xuk wei luw wong ema gweimbeeng ne yo.
ACT 14:27 Luw lam tyip inyon eno luw qeku xel kongrikesin lekti me wo qayeeng dalus wei Anutu wong wou luw me e tax xomek mya wei wongeingis eno wou xel amba yo.
ACT 14:28 De luw dei inyon enden ka is xel betiyeing.
ACT 15:1 Xel moux valu lam axone veil Yudia me la Antiok me di teyoxe xel amba wei wongis o bei: “Wangwei xam se ghuw nimim navi nambei Mose xe kwa nei, on tyek Anutu se devind xam veil meyeing.”
ACT 15:2 Paulus me Banabas ngo qayeeng wei xel moux on neil o om luw wo vevek wou qayeeng is xel me vuk lek qayeeng is xel lox me loum. Om xel beyal Paulus me Banabas bei luw na is xel wongeingis valu, bei xel na pu Yerusalem nei me na gyei xel sinale me teivateiv en telinyeing tine.
ACT 15:3 De kongrikesin wong xel la, om xel la lox Ponisia me Samaria senghoing, me di neil wou xel en ingwei xel amba pekwi xow o. Qayeeng nimza tine wong xel wongeingis wo xeindlala.
ACT 15:4 Ka xel la tyip Yerusalem eno xel wongeingis me xel sinale me gyovaxa qou xel. De Paulus aluw Banabas neil wou xel en lul dalus wei Anutu wong wou xel nangya luw memend o.
ACT 15:5 Woyom xel Parisi valu wei wongis eno nale me neil, “Xel amba na mi ghuw ninavi me betiwou petieing wei Mose yo.”
ACT 15:6 De xel sinale me teivateiv qekuma bei menyex wou telinyeing tine.
ACT 15:7 Ka xel neil qayeeng ngenong woy, Petele nale ghey me neil wou xel: “Xam lingyeiw, xam ghe woulek bei takwei eno Anutu beyal ay eivek xam senghoing bei a neil Xoulek Nimza wou xel amba en xel a ngo dom bongis.
ACT 15:8 Anutu, tiwei woulek xomaxoneing dalus laleind eno talex wou xey bei lewexe lek xel me wong Laweeng Vambuing wou xel, nambei ingwei wong wou xey o.
ACT 15:9 Moxo se wong kwa nge wou xel de nge wou xey, qe wong xel laleind wo vako en ingwei xel wongis o.
ACT 15:10 Woyom nambei nya xam ambeing bo axeing wou Anutu gweimbeeng? Xam se toung pelang nimaying lek xel betiyeing kwend, beip inyon xey o xe bundyeiw se teyei bei qalei?
ACT 15:11 Ma! Xey a wongis bei, eivek lalei xeiles wei xe xe Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu eno Anutu vind xey a lam veil meyeing nambei ingwei vind xel on.”
ACT 15:12 Xel dalus wei qekuma eno deduingma, en nambei xel di ngo Banabas me Paulus di neil qayeeng wei Anutu wong dee me lulvako eivek xel amba senghoing nangya luw memend o.
ACT 15:13 Luw tip qayeeng eno Jems luk elekla bei: “Xam lingyeiw, xam ngo a xe qayeeng.
ACT 15:14 Simon neil wou xam en vati wei Anutu talex myaxeeng en ingwei mi wou naleind en xel amba yo, bei na qou xel xomaxoneing me xel bong ambei emaxow xe.
ACT 15:15 Me qayeeng wei xel poropet eno la teyei lek is ambei nyon, xel byex eyeip eivek xoulek bei,
ACT 15:16 “ ‘Ka tine na veil eno tyek a noum me nam me na dev Dawit xe xomek sel no wei pek me teila veil o. Lulul wei xomek lelolexe eno tyek a menyex wou de na dev vako no,
ACT 15:17 en kandek moux alis vex wei xel amba wei se Yuda eno gyimexe Tambiy Ngandoung, me xel amba dalus wei mi wongis a leing o, Tambiy Ngandoung neil embei. E venaxow wong lul tine qandi.’
ACT 15:18 Xel woulek inyon takwei qenang nei.
ACT 15:19 “Nambei nyon a xe woueing nalei bei, xe se teyei bei bong lulti bo pok en xel amba wei pekwi xow me loum wou Anutu yo.
ACT 15:20 Embong ondek xey a byex qapiya wou xel, me na neil wou xel bei xel se qou yaeing wei xel toung ambei da wou tenu bandaing o, me kwa nilul wei kwapesiv o, me leliy leyeis wei xel bembinexe e kwa yo de xel se gya leliy wei gyand o.
ACT 15:21 En eivek beyeeng ngandoung titi eivek bouk wei myaxeeng o xomaxoneing valu mi neil petieing wei Mose yo teyei de xel mi pyaw eivek xomek qekueing ama lek bouk wei Sabat o.”
ACT 15:22 Woyom sinaleyeiw me teivateiv, is kongrikesin, xel embei beyal xel venaxow xe moux valu me bong xel na Antiok is Paulus me Banabas. Xel beyal Yudas (xel mi taxe lei nge bei Balsabas) me Silas, moux yuw on teiv eivek liyeiw senghoing.
ACT 15:23 Xel wong qapiya tine la is xel: Xa sinaleyeiw me teivateiv ne xam limimyeiw, xa byex qapiya ne lak wou xam wongeingis wei xel amba yo eivek Antiok, Siria me Silisia: Bendiyeing xam.
ACT 15:24 Xa ngo bei xomaxoneing valu qandi eivek xa senghoing me lak wo nol wou xam laleimim is xel xe qayeeng me wong nimaying wou xam. Ekom xa se lenghek lek xel me wong xel lak wou xam.
ACT 15:25 Om xa dalus a toung laleimi lekti me na beyal xel valu me na wong xel lak wou xam is xa xe gweleeng Banabas me Paulus wei xa laleimi vind o,
ACT 15:26 moux yuw on teyeimbei saing luw xe mapieing en xe xe Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu Kilisi lei.
ACT 15:27 Nambei nyon xa wong Yudas aluw Silas lak wou xam, bei luw nak a neil qayeeng wei xa byex eno wou xam eivek luw venaxow myend.
ACT 15:28 Inye wo nimza wou Laweeng Vambuing me xa bei xa se toung nimaying lek xam. Qe xa neimbei xam a mi betiwou kwa valu nambei nye.
ACT 15:29 Xam mendei dingta veil yaeing wei xel toung ambei da wou tenu bandaing o. Xam seng gwa leliy is gyand, me xam se gwa leliy leyeis wei xel qo e kwa yo me xam pesek kwa nilul wei kwapesiv o. Tyek xam ghe bo nimza wangwei xam pesek lulti beimambei ne. Xam a mi mendei embo nimza.
ACT 15:30 Woyom xel wong moux ti beimambei yon la xo wei Antiok nei, de xel qeku moux alis vex wei xel wongeingis eno lekti me wong qapiya wei xel byex o wou xel.
ACT 15:31 Xomaxoneing pyaw qayeeng tiyon me xel wo xeindlala en ingwei xel qou qayeeng nimza wei embei devind me bong nikanzek wou xel o.
ACT 15:32 Yudas me Silas, luw venaxow on poropet. Om luw neil qayeeng ngenong bei devind me bong nikanzek wou liyeiw.
ACT 15:33 Ka luw la dei inyon bouk valu is xel woy, woyom liyeiw wong luw lox is mata wei lalei vevopeing bei luw nox wou xel wei wong luw lam o.
ACT 15:35 Ekom Paulus aluw Banabas nanghei toundei eivek Antiok, nanghei inyon eno luw me xel ngenong di teyoxe me neil qayeeng wei Tambiy Ngandoung xe yo.
ACT 15:36 Bouk valu la veil woyom Paulus neil wou Banabas, “Uw ambei nox mena me na ghei lindyeiw eivek beyeeng on dalus wei xey a neil Tambiy Ngandoung xe qayeeng eivek o me nanghei bei xel toundei woy.”
ACT 15:37 Banabas embei Yoan wei xel mi taxe e lei nge bei Malaka, eno na is luw,
ACT 15:38 ekom Paulus wou kwa bei inye se nimza bei e qou Malaka, en nambei la veil luw anghei Pampilia me se lox me la wo xuk is luw no.
ACT 15:39 Luw pyalek ama niseikeing me dembuma om luw se wo xuk is ama no. Banabas qou Malaka de luw qou sip me la tembuing nayak Saiprus eivek mamileeng,
ACT 15:40 ekom Paulus beyal Silas me luw la, de liyeiw toung luw eivek lalei xeiles wei Tambiy Ngandoung o.
ACT 15:41 Moxo la eivek provins wei Siria me provins wei Silisia yo, me byexaxoun xel kongrikesin wei toundei inyon o.
ACT 16:1 Paulus la beyeeng nayak Debi me la beyeeng nayak Listra is ambei nyon, nanghei inyon eno betiyeing ti lei Timote mindei inyon. Moxo ta yon Yuda vexo wei mi wongis o eno ti, de ma yon nanghei Grik.
ACT 16:2 Xel wongeingis wei Listra me Aikoniam eno mi luk en Timote bei, e tambiy nimza.
ACT 16:3 Paulus embei qou Timote me na dingta ti is e, om moxo ghuw e ninavi nambei kwa wei Yudayeiw o. En wounalei en Yudayeiw wei mindei eivek beyeeng beimambei yon o, en xel dalus woulek bei e ma yon Grik.
ACT 16:4 Ka xel la eivek beyeeng nge me la nge, eno xel wong qayeeng wei sinaleyeiw me teivateiv luklek me tup woy eivek Yerusalem eno wou xel, bei xomaxoneing dalus betiwou.
ACT 16:5 Om xel kongrikesin on xe wongeingis wo nikanzek me xel di nyouk taxombouk.
ACT 16:6 Paulus me e xe xel wei mi wo xuk lekti eno la eivek tembuing danghei wei provins Esia nei, en nambei Laweeng Vambuing neil axound bei luw se neil qayeeng ti eivek Prigia me Galesia.
ACT 16:7 Ka xel la tyip wou tembuing danghei wei Misia, xel wong me yei en xel embei na eivek provins Bitinia, ekom Yesu xe Laweeng Vambuing peti xel bei xel se na inyon.
ACT 16:8 Om xel la senghoing eivek Misia de la xo beyeeng nayak Troas nei.
ACT 16:9 Eivek boukeing tiyon eno Paulus mapekwi me yei moux wei tembuing danghei wei Masedonia yo ti eno toukale me tay wou e, “Wang nam ingwei Masedonia ne me devind xa.”
ACT 16:10 Ka Paulus mapekwi me yei tine, xa xeiwou xow daing bei na Masedonia, xa woulek bei, Anutu taxe bei xa na neil e xe Xoulek Nimza wou xel nei.
ACT 16:11 Nambei nyon, xa qou sip nanghei beyeeng nayak Troas me na la bombek wou Samotres eivek mamileeng, de yanyeing eno xa la Neapolis.
ACT 16:12 Nanghei inyon eno xa la Pilipai, wei xel Rom yeiteyei me dei lek takwei yo. Inyon beyeeng ngandoung wei tembuing danghei tiwei myaxeeng wei provins Masedonia yo. Om xa dei inyon bouk valu.
ACT 16:13 Lek bouk Sabat eno xa la myayaing veil tete mya wei beyeeng ngandoung on me na la ingwei memiing vi nei, wei xa woulek bei inye beyeeng wei xomaxoneing mi zeim memend anghei yo. Woyom xa dei tembuing me na luk wou xel vex wei qekuma nanghei inyon o.
ACT 16:14 Vex wei mindei inyon eno ti lei Lidia, ngo qayeeng tine me mi wo lalo wou Anutu. Vex on beeng qes Taiataira, me vexo mi wo xuk malew en qaeing wei mateyek o. Tambiy Ngandoung pekwi vex on lalei, om li nenya wou qayeeng wei Paulus di neil on.
ACT 16:15 Ka vex on me e xe xel wei xel xouing mindei eivek xomek on lipek, vexo neil embei, “wangwei xam ghe gwei bei a wongis Tambiy Ngandoung nei, ond xam ghe nam mendei eivek a bang.” Om vexo wo nikanzek en xa, me xa betiwou e xe qayeeng.
ACT 16:16 Bouk ti xa la beyeeng wei zeimeing mema yo, de vexawo xukxe bandaing ti lam pelong xa, laweeng ti mindei eivek e me mi yei me neil vati wei tyek nam loxyus o teyei. Vex on mi qou malew ngenong wou mayeiw en xuk wei mi wong on.
ACT 16:17 Vexawo tine eno mi betiwou Paulus me xa dalus, me mi taxe bei, “Xel moux dalus tine inye xukxe wei Anutu Nikanzekta wei Gheyapu nei. Xel mi neil wou xam en sakwaing wei embei devind xam veil meyeing o.”
ACT 16:18 Vex tine mi wong ambei nye teyei lek bouk tambak. Dekakom Paulus lalei wo myavanei om pekwi ma wou me neil niseikeing wou laweeng on, “A neil wou wang eivek Yesu Kilisi lei bei, lam myayaing veil vex on!” De lutika eno laweeng la veil vexo.
ACT 16:19 Ekom vexawo yon mayeiw yei bei sakwaing wei qoueing malew eno lati, om xel zeimaxoun Paulus aluw Silas me tetei luw me qou luw me la nale wou xel gyovaxa mend eivek beyeeng wei xel mi wo vateivek o.
ACT 16:20 Xel qou luw me la wou xel wei mi ngo qayeeng o me neil, “Moux yuw ne inye Yuda, luw di wo nol wou xe laleind eivek xe bend ne.
ACT 16:21 Me luw embei puw xey a na betiwou kwa valu wei xey a lax petieing zeyi bei xey wei Rom eno se bong o.”
ACT 16:22 Xel moux alis vex tendulekti, me byex qayeeng lek Paulus aluw Silas. Me xel wei mi ngo qayeeng eno luk nikanzek wou luw de kwax luw xe teimb veil dom sesa luw en beyei.
ACT 16:23 Ka xel wo nol wou luw woy, woyom xel toung luw la eivek xomek xeitueing, de wong qayeeng nikanzek wou tambiy wei mi yei xomek xeitueing teyei yo bei, emdi gyeiteyei luw bo nimza.
ACT 16:24 Tambiy on ngo petieing wei nge wei mi ngo qayeeng o, om toung luw eivek xeitueing tiwei laleiyang me tup luw vaxend eivek pelang.
ACT 16:25 Lek boukeing masenghoing eno Paulus me Silas di zeimemend me wong lalo wou Anutu, me xel valu wei xeitueing eno di ngo luw.
ACT 16:26 De lutika eno tembuing pi me xomek xeitueing on wo pimapi me mundeeng wei xomek xeitueing eno pi. Lutika eno qapomb wei xomek xeitueing on tax, me xel dalus xe sen tax.
ACT 16:27 Tambiy wei mi yei xomek xeitueing teyei eno qandi, me yei bei xomek xeitueing xe qapomb tax, om moxo puw e xe ngeyeing vevek dom embei nyeis venaxow en embeik nge xel wei la xeitueing eno pek me la.
ACT 16:28 Ekom Paulus taxe la wou moxo bei, “Wa seng bo nol wou xow! En xa dalus a toundei inye.”
ACT 16:29 Tambiy wei mi yei xomek xeitueing teyei eno taxe bei xel a qou nenyex tumeing me nam, moxo veimya me la lalei is etekeing me yaleeng de teila paviy Paulus me Silas vaxend.
ACT 16:30 Woyom moxo qou luw me la myayaing me teling, “Teiv amuw, tyek am bong ambei nya en kandek Anutu e qou a noum?”
ACT 16:31 Luw neil elox bei, “Wang bongis Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu, on tyek Anutu devind wang nam veil meyeing me wa xe xel wei xomek o is.”
ACT 16:32 Woyom luw neil qayeeng wei Tambiy Ngandoung o wou e me xel dalus wei e beeng o is.
ACT 16:33 Eivek boukeing masenghoing eno tambiy wei xomek xeitueing on qou luw me sekweyexe luw xe qatyex, woyom lutika eno moxo lis nipapu dalus qou lipekeing.
ACT 16:34 Tambiy wei xomek xeitueing eno qou luw me la eivek beeng me toung lul yaeing eno lam wou luw en moxo pup en xeilala en nambei xel wongis Anutu, e me nipapu dalus.
ACT 16:35 Satiboukeing eno tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng eno wong e xe xel belimbo la wou tambiy wei xomek xeitueing is qayeeng tine bei: “Wong tambiy yuw on la.”
ACT 16:36 Tambiy wei mi yei xomek xeitueing teyei eno neil wou Paulus bei, “Tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng eno neil embei wang me Silas ghe na. Muw ghe na is laleim vevopeing.”
ACT 16:37 Ekom Paulus neil wou lei ngandoung wei xosepu yon: “Uw ne moux wei Rom o. Nambei nya xel wei mi ngo qayeeng eno se ngo qayeeng wei uw eno wo nimza, me yei bei uw a wong sewokeing ti o ma? Ekom xel leis uw bandaing me toung uw eivek xomek xeitueing. Om gweimbeeng xel embei qou uw xupekeing? Ma! Wong xel venaxow lam qou uw me la myayaing.”
ACT 16:38 Lei ngandoung wei xosepu eno wong qayeeng tine wou tambiy wei mi ngo qayeeng o, me xel ngo bei Paulus me Silas on Rom yuw, om xel yaleeng.
ACT 16:39 Woyom xel wei mi ngo qayeeng eno lam me beoux xow wou luw dom qou luw me la veil xomek xeitueing, de teling wou luw bei luw na veil beyeeng ngandoung on.
ACT 16:40 Ka Paulus aluw Silas lam myayaing veil xeitueing, luw la Lidia beeng, me la tyip wou liyeiw me byexaxoun xel en qayeeng valu, de woyom luw la.
ACT 17:1 Ka luw la eivek beeng nayak Ampipolis me beeng nayak Apolonia, luw la tyip beeng nayak Tesalonika, nanghei inyon eno xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o ti toukale.
ACT 17:2 Paulus la eivek xomek qekueing ama nambei e xe kwa wei mi wong o, me eivek Sabat yal eno mi luk is xel en qayeeng wei di yeip eivek Anutu xe qapiya yo.
ACT 17:3 Moxo mi neil Anutu xe qayeeng qes teyei me neil ambei nye, Kilisi tyek na qou myavanei ngandoung me na mey, dekakom tyek qandi lek veil meyeing. Moxo neil, “Yesu tiwei andi neilteyei wou xam ne, inye Kilisi.”
ACT 17:4 Xel valu wei Yuda eno wongis me betiwou Paulus aluw Silas, me Grik valu ngandoung wei mi wo lalo wou Anutu eno betiwou luw. Me vex ngenong wei leind tata eno betiwou luw is ambei nyon.
ACT 17:5 Ekom Yudayeiw qouwou luw, om xel qou xel wei nilul o valu nanghei ingwei beyeeng vateivek nei, me qeku xel ngenong is me xel wo nol wou beyeeng ngandoung tiyon. Xel veimyend me la wou Jeson xe xomek me la yimexe Paulus aluw Silas bei na qou luw me na myayaing wou xel qendu ngandoung on.
ACT 17:6 Ekom xel se yeiwou luw, om xel tetei Jeson is liyeiw valu me qou xel me la wou xel gyovaxa wei beyeeng on, dom taxe bei, “Moux tine mi wo kwa nol me ghavineeng e lala eivek tembuing sapa nei, om gweimbeeng ne xel lam inye,
ACT 17:7 me Jeson qou xel me la eivek beeng. Xel moux dalus tine mi pyalek Sisa xe qayeeng, me xel mi neil embei, king nge toundei, e lei Yesu”
ACT 17:8 Xel xomaxoneing is gyovaxa wei beyeeng nayak on ngo tine, eno xel tambak on etek ngandoung me di wo vyend lala.
ACT 17:9 Woyom xel wong Jeson me lei yeiw ba yon xouv xomek wei ngoeing qayeeng o dom wong xel la.
ACT 17:10 Ka di wo mangamong en embei bouk, Paulus aluw Silas lindyeiw wong luw la beyeeng nayak Belia. Luw la tyip inyon, me xel la eivek Yudayeiw xe xomek qekueing ama.
ACT 17:11 Xel Yuda wei mindei Belia eno xel xe kwa yon nimza ghanaw Yudayeiw wei Tesalonika yo, en xel ngo qayeeng wei Paulus neil on me xel laleind vind, teyei lek bouk eno xel mi pyaw qayeeng wei yeip eivek qapiya vambuing o me yeimbei xoulek wei Paulus neil on zonghek, o ma.
ACT 17:12 Xel wei Yuda yon eno ngenong wongis, me Grik vex ngenong wei leitata yo, me moux wei Grik eno xouing wongis ambei nyon.
ACT 17:13 Ekom xel Yudayeiw wei mindei eivek Tesalonika woulek bei Paulus di neil qayeeng wei Anutu xe yo eivek Belia, om xel la inyon is, me zeim moux alis vex on laleind lek me wong xel dalus etek mouyo.
ACT 17:14 Woyom xel lindyeiw wo daing me wong Paulus la xo mamileeng vi nei, ekom Silas aluw Timote nanghei toundei Belia.
ACT 17:15 Xel moux wei la is Paulus eno qou e me la beyeeng nayak Atens, de woyom Paulus wong qayeeng wou xel bei xel a neil wou Silas aluw Timote bei luw na wou e daing.
ACT 17:16 Ka Paulus di axe luw anghei Atens, moxo yei beyeeng ngandoung on pup en anutu tyonyeing ngenong. Om wong e lalei wo maying.
ACT 17:17 Om moxo la eivek xomek qekueing ama wei xel Yudayeiw o me luk is Yudayeiw me xel amba wei mi wo lalo wou Anutu yo. De lek bouk titi moxo mi la beyeeng vateivek me luk is moux alis vex wei lam mindei inyon o.
ACT 17:18 Xel moux wei lundpeyei nimza wei Epikurian me xel wei Stoik, eno wo veweeng is e en qayeeng. Xel valu teling, “Tambiy tiwei mi luk bandabanda nei embei neil va?” Om xel valu neil, “Beind moxo di neil qayeeng en anutuyeiw wei beyeeng bamba yo.” Xel neil tine en nambei Paulus di neil Xoulek Nimza en Yesu wei qandi lek veil meyeing o.
ACT 17:19 Woyom xel qou Paulus me la qekueing ama wei xel kanzol lek lukendu Areopagus, nanghei inyon eno xel neil wou e, “Teyei bei xa ngo qayeeng vako tiwei wang di teyoxe me ghe wong elam ne?
ACT 17:20 Wang wong qayeeng bange valu lam eivek xa nenyami, om xa bei ngo bei qayeeng tine qes ambei nya.”
ACT 17:21 (De xel Atensyeiw dalus me xel amba wei mindei inyon eno se mi wo lulti qe xel mindei bandaing me mi luk en lulvako wei xel ngo yo.)
ACT 17:22 Woyom Paulus nale ghey eivek qekueing ama wei xel kanzol lek lukendu Areopagus me neil: “Xam moux wei Atens! A xei xam ghe wo nimkanzek en wongeingis kwa leimalei wei lalo yo.
ACT 17:23 En nambei a la ghavinenyeing me na xei e wo nimza me na xei lul wei xam ghe mi wong lalo wou yo. Me a xei qeind ti xel byex qayeeng lek ambei nye: E NA WOU ANUTU TI WEI XA SE WOULEK O. Om Anutu tiwei xam seng woulek on xam ghe mi wo lalo bandaing wou e, om gweimbeeng ambei neil e xe qayeeng wou xam.
ACT 17:24 “Anutu tiwei toung tembuing me lulul dalus eivek o, inyon Tambiy Ngandoung wei tyoung aluw tembuing, me se mindei eivek xomek vambuing wei xel ev angya memend o.
ACT 17:25 Me se mi qou vineing en lul wei xomaxoneing wong angya memend o, me se teyei bei qou lulti, en nambei e maxow wong mapieing me laweeng wou xomaxoneing me lulul dalusateiv.
ACT 17:26 Eivek bu tixemou ne eno e toung xomaxoneing lam dei lek tembuing sapa, en kandek xel a mi gyeiteyei tembuing tambak, e maxow beyal bouk wei xel a mi mendei yo, me e maxow lax enghek wei xel xe tembuing o.
ACT 17:27 Anutu wong ambei nye en kandek xomaxoneing gyimexe e me nam wou me boulek e zonghek en nambei se dei dingta veil xey.
ACT 17:28 ‘En eivek Anutu eno xey a wo xomaxoneing me na toundei mapieing me na mi la me na loum me na dei lek tembuing.’ Nambei xam venaxow xe xel valu wei lupeyei eno neil embei, ‘Xe ne Anutu neuyeiw.’
ACT 17:29 “Nambei nyon xey a toundei nambei Anutu neuyeiw, om xey se bou naleind bei Anutu yon nambei ghol me silva me qakous, me xe se bou naleind bei e yon tenu bandaing wei xomaxoneing wong angya venaxow memend me lundpeyei wei xe venaxow o.
ACT 17:30 Takwei eno xomaxoneing lundpeyei ma, om Anutu se neil qayeeng ti en vati wei xel mi wong o. Ekom gweimbeeng ne neil qayeeng nikanzek wou xomaxoneing dalus lek tembuing sapa bei xel pekwi xow.
ACT 17:31 En e maxow lax bouk wei embei tyek bong qayeeng en xomaxoneing dalus wei tembuing o, om beyal tambiy ti woy. Tambiy tine eno mey ekom Anutu piyexe e qandi lek veil meyeing.”
ACT 17:32 Xel ngo Paulus neil qayeeng en xomaxoneing qandi lek veil meyeing, xel valu luk seloukeing lek e, ekom xel valu neil embei, “Xa bei ngo qayeeng valu en lul tine no.”
ACT 17:33 Dekalekom, Paulus la veil xel kanzol.
ACT 17:34 Xel moux valu betiwou Paulus me wongis. Ti lei Dionisius, e kanzol wei xel mi qekuma lek lukendu Areopagus, me vex nge is ambei nyon e lei Damaris, me xomaxoneing valu beti wongis.
ACT 18:1 Kalekom, Paulus la veil Atens me la beyeeng nayak Korin.
ACT 18:2 Nanghei inyon eno moxo la tyip wou Yuda ti, e lei Akwila. Tambiy on beeng qes anghei Pontus, e tiwei lam anghei Itali is venei Prisila yo, en nambei Klodias wo qayeeng wou Yudayeiw dalus bei xel na veil Rom. Om Paulus la en embei gyei xel,
ACT 18:3 Paulus mi dei me wo xuk is xel, en nambei Paulus, Akwila, Prisila, lal xouing mi wo xuk wei duweing sel o.
ACT 18:4 Lek bouk tambak wei Sabat eno Paulus mi la eivek xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o, me neil qayeeng lumama wou Yudayeiw me xel Grik bei em beil xel lundlek.
ACT 18:5 Woyom Silas aluw Timote lam anghei Masedonia, Paulus neil Anutu xe xoulek wou xel Yudayeiw teyei lek bouk tambak me neil wou xel bei Yesu yon Kilisi.
ACT 18:6 Ekom Yudayeiw se ngo e qe xel pesek e me lukyak lek moxo. Om Paulus pepa vegyuveeng veil e xe teimb me neil wou xel, “Wangwei xam a qou nilul, ond inyon di yeip wou xam venaxow, nimaying on se wou ay. Gweimbeeng ne tyek a na neil xoulek wou xel amba.”
ACT 18:7 Woyom Paulus la veil xomek qekueing ama me la eivek xomek wei Titius Jastus wei xel amba yo eno nale paviy xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o, tambiy yon mi wong lalo wou Anutu.
ACT 18:8 Klispas on gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o. E is venei neu dalus mi wongis Tambiy Ngandoung, me xel ngenong wei Korin eno ngo Paulus xe qayeeng me wongis de lipek.
ACT 18:9 Boukeing ti eno Tambiy Ngandoung luk wou Paulus eivek ingwei mapekwi yo me neil: “Wa seng gwaleeng qe wa toumbale ding lek lukeing, de wa se mendei kanzek.
ACT 18:10 En a toundei is wang, om xelti se teyei bei zeim wang me bo nol wou wang, en nambei a xe xel ngenong toundei eivek beyeeng ngandoung tine.”
ACT 18:11 Om Paulus toundei eivek Korin teyei lek vakovek qes ti me ela dentouk limti, me teyoxe Anutu xe xoulek wou xel.
ACT 18:12 Ka Galio wo lei ngandoung wei seyap en provins Akaya, xel Yudayeiw qeku lekti me wo vevek is Paulus me qou e me la wong qayeeng en e.
ACT 18:13 Xel wong qayeeng en e me neil, “Tambiy tine, mi teyoxe wou xomaxoneing bei xel se bongis petieing qe xel bong lalo wou Anutu en sakwaing ba.”
ACT 18:14 Ka Paulus embim a neil qayeeng nox wou xel, ekom Galio pekwi me neil wou xel Yudayeiw bei, “Wangwei tambiy tine qayil petieing o bo sewokeing ti wou xam, ond a teyeimbei ngo qayeeng wei xam o.
ACT 18:15 Ekom xam ghe di pyanaleimim en qayeeng me leimim me xam venaxow xe petieing, om xam ghe lam wou ay. A se teyei bei ngo qayeeng en lulul ambei nyon, om xam venaxow menyex wou qayeeng ne.”
ACT 18:16 Om moxo wong xel loum myayaing veil wongeing qayeeng.
ACT 18:17 De xel zeimaxoun Sostenes inyon gyovaxa wei xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o, me xel leis e paviy xomek wei ngoeing qayeeng o. Ekom Galio mou se di wounalei en lul ambei nyon.
ACT 18:18 Paulus toundei eivek Korin teyei lek bouk matika. Dekalekom moxo ghanaw liyeiw dom qou sip me la provins Siria, Akwila luw venei Prisila la is e. Ka xel embei na, moxo qateiv luvelus veil nanghei beyeeng nayak Senklia en nambei tup qayeeng ti is Anutu.
ACT 18:19 Xel la tyip beyeeng nayak Epeses, nanghei inyon eno Paulus ghanaw Prisila luw Akwila. De e maxow la eivek xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o me neil qayeeng wou xel.
ACT 18:20 Xel teling wou bei e toumendei bouk valu is xel, ekom moxo pesek.
ACT 18:21 Ekom ka e la, moxo neil wou xel, “Wangwei Anutu lalei devind nei ond tyek a noum wou xam.” Woyom moxo qou sip me la veil Epeses.
