ACT 18:22 Moxo la tyip Sisalia, dekakom moxo la pu wei Yerusalem nei me la neil bendiyeing wou xel kongrikesin on woy om la xo wei Antiok nei.
ACT 18:23 Paulus la dei Antiok bouk valu, dekalekom qandi nanghei inyon me la beyeeng nge me la nge teyei lek tembuing danghei wei Galesia yon me Prigia, me byexaxoun xel betiyeing en qayeeng.
ACT 18:24 Dekakom Yuda ti lei Apolos, tambiy wei beeng Aleksandlia, eno lam dei Epeses. Tambiy on mi luk qayeeng nimza, me moxo mi woulek e wo nimza en Anutu xe qayeeng wei di yeip eivek qapiya yo.
ACT 18:25 Xel teyoxe e woy en sakwaing wei Tambiy Ngandoung o, me e luk is nikanzek me mi neil wou moux alis vex en Yesu bombek, ekom moxo woulek lipekeing wei Yoan o.
ACT 18:26 Moxo neil qayeeng nikanzek eivek xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o. De Prisila me Akwila ngo e, luw qou e me la xomek wei luw o me neil sakwaing wei Anutu yo en Yesu wou e en kandek moxo boulek embo nimza.
ACT 18:27 Ka Apolos embei na Akaya, liyeiw wei mi dei Epeses eno byexaxoun e en qayeeng. Me byex qapiya wou xel betiyeing wei Akaya bei xel a qou e. Gyeik e la tyip inyon eno moxo wong vineing ngandoung wou eti yeiw wei Anutu wong lalei xeiles wou xel me xel wongis o.
ACT 18:28 Moxo wo nikanzek lek qayeeng neileing bei pelipek Yudayeiw nind qayeeng wou xomaxoneing mendghalus. Moxo neil xoulek eivek Anutu xe qapiya me talex e yeip yaing bei Yesu yon Kilisi.
ACT 19:1 Ka Apolos toundei eivek Korin, Paulus la ghavineng eivek beyeeng wei toundei lek lukendu nei dekakom la tyip Epeses. Nanghei inyon eno moxo la tyip wou xel betiyeing valu
ACT 19:2 me teling wou xel, “Beip xam ghe qou Laweeng Vambuing gyeik xam ghe wongis o?” Xel lenghek bei, “Ma yo, xa se ngo bei inyon Laweeng Vambuing ti toundei.”
ACT 19:3 Om Paulus teling, “Woyom xam ghe qou lipekeing vati?” Xel neil, “Yoan xe lipekeing.”
ACT 19:4 De Paulus neil embei, “Yoan xe lipekeing on lipekeing wei pekwieing xow o. Moxo neil wou xel xomaxoneing on bei xel bongis tambiy tiwei di lam yus en e yo, inyon Yesu.”
ACT 19:5 Ka xel ngo qayeeng tine, xel qou lipekeing eivek Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu lei.
ACT 19:6 Woyom Paulus li mema lek xel, me Laweeng Vambuing lam lek xel, de xel neil qayeeng eivek vya leimalei me neil qayeeng poropet.
ACT 19:7 Xel moux dalus tiyon teyei lek xoumeeng yuw.
ACT 19:8 Om Paulus la eivek xomek qekueing ama wei Yudayeiw o me neil qayeeng nikanzek nanghei inyon teyei lek dentouk qes yal, moxo luk is nikanzek wou xel me veil xel lundlek en lul dalus wei Anutu xe tete lalei yo.
ACT 19:9 Ekom xel valu laleind wo nikanzek, om xel se wongis, me eivek xomexomek mendghalus eno xel neil qayeeng nol lek Sakwaing Tiyon. Om Paulus qou xel betiyeing me la veil xomek qekueing ama, de taxombouk eno moxo mi luk wou xel eivek Tiranus xe xomek wei teyoxeing o.
ACT 19:10 Moxo mi wong ambei nye teyei lek vakovek qes yuw, en kandek Yudayeiw dalus me xel Grik dalus wei mindei eivek provins Esia eno na ngo Tambiy Ngandoung xe qayeeng.
ACT 19:11 Anutu wong lulvako leimalei wei nikanzek eno nangya Paulus mema,
ACT 19:12 om xel moux alis vex mi qou angesip me qaeing myasepu wei Paulus axlek o, dekakom xel mi qou me la toung lek xel wei vanei wong xel o, dom vanei wei xel eno ma, me laweeng nol eno la veil xel is ambei nyon.
ACT 19:13 Xel Yuda valu wei mi la ghavinenyeing me tiy laweeng nol. Xel valu wong en embei neil Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu lei, me na tiy laweeng nol veil xel moux alis vex. Xel mi neil ambei nye, “Eivek Yesu lei, e tiwei Paulus mi neil e xe qayeeng o, a neil nikanzek wou wang bei lam myayaing.”
ACT 19:14 Lumuki leitata wei Yudayeiw o ti lei Skeva eno neu moux lim yuw, eno xel mi wo kwa tine wou laweeng nilul.
ACT 19:15 Bouk ti, eno laweeng nol neil elox wou xel, “A woulek Yesu, me a woulek Paulus, ekom xam on eti yeiw?”
ACT 19:16 Woyom tambiy tiwei laweeng nol mindei eivek eno vyeip lek xel me leis xel dalus. Moxo leis xel on wo nol ayang, omva xel pek veil xomek on me la xeind touk is gyand.
ACT 19:17 Yudayeiw dalus me xel Grik wei mindei eivek Epeses eno ngo tine, om xel yaleeng ngandoung mouyo, om xel sanghoxe Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu lei.
ACT 19:18 Xel ngenongakes wei wongis woy, eno lam wou xel moux alis vex ba yon mendghalus, me neil xel xe sewokeing wei xel mi wong takwei eno teyei.
ACT 19:19 Moux alis vex ngenong wei mi wo wevek me palak, eno qekuwou qapiya yon me lam sei lek nenyex eivek xel moux alis vex on mendghalus. Xel pyaw memend wou qapiya wei xel xouv eno teyei lek 50,000 malew selewa.
ACT 19:20 Eivek sakwaing ambei nye eno Tambiy Ngandoung xe qayeeng wo ngandoung me vula wo tambak is nikanzek.
ACT 19:21 Ka lul dalus tine tyip woy, Laweeng Vambuing wo kwa wou Paulus bei e na Masedonia me Akaya dekakom na Yerusalem. Om moxo neil, “Kalekom a na Rom is ambei nyon.”
ACT 19:22 Woyom ka moxo wong e xe vineing aluw, Timote me Elastus la Masedonia, dom e maxow toundei eivek provins wei Esia nei me e den nayaka.
ACT 19:23 Lek bouk kayon eno xel valu wong vevek en qayeeng zeyi Sakwaing Tiyon.
ACT 19:24 Moux ti mindei, e lei Demitrius, tambiy on mi yeiwou lulul angya silva me yeiwou tenu nayak nayak teyei lek ambei xomek lalo wei anutu vex Atemis nangya silva, moxo se mi qou malew nayaka lek xuk wei mi wong on.
ACT 19:25 Moxo qeku xel xouing lekti, is xel wei mi wong xuk bange yo, me neil: “Xam moux, xam ghe boulek bei xey a mi qou malew wo nimza en xuk tiwei xey a di wong ne.
ACT 19:26 Me xam ghe wei me ghe ngo Paulus tiwei di wong me puw xomaxoneing ngenong eivek Epeses nei me pelipek xel laleind, de se eivek Epeses venaxow, qe paviy embim na eivek tembuing dalus wei provins Esia yo is. Me neil embei, ‘Anutu wei xey a wong angya memend ne se anutu zonghek.’
ACT 19:27 Qayeeng tiwei Paulus di neil ne teyei bei bo xe xe xuk vateivek ne lei bo nol. Me lul nge is ambei nyon, qayeeng wei e ne tyek teyeimbei bong xomek qekueing ama wei anutu vex Atemis o bong ambei lul bandaing eivek woueing nalei wei xomaxoneing o, me takwei eno xomaxoneing wei provins Esia me tembuing sapa wei xel mi wo lalo wou anutu vex tine yo. Ekom qayeeng wei Paulus eno embei semaleeng lei laeing wei e yo.”
ACT 19:28 Xel ngo qayeeng tine, eno xel laleind wo myavanei me taxe bei, “Atemis anutu wei Epeses, vex on lei laeing!”
ACT 19:29 Beyeeng ngandoung on dalus wo nindenduing ngenong, me xomaxoneing dalus on zeimaxoun Gaius me Alistakas me veimyend me la beyeeng wei qekueing ama yo. Tambiy yuw on nanghei Masedonia eno luw mi ghavineng is Paulus.
ACT 19:30 Paulus venaxow embei na senghoing is moux alis vex on, ekom xel betiyeing neil axound bei e se na.
ACT 19:31 Xel seyap valu nanghei Esia yon Paulus xe gweleeng, om xel wong qayeeng la wou Paulus bei, e se na eivek beyeeng wei qekueing ama yon.
ACT 19:32 Xel xomaxoneing dalus on lundpeyei yon la bandabanda. Xel valu di taxe lul nge de valu di taxe lul bange. Xel ngenong on se woulek bei xel di qekuma en vati.
ACT 19:33 Xel Yudayeiw tendu Aleksanda la mya nei wou xomaxoneing on mendghalus, xel valu wei toungale yon yei me neil embei, tambiy kawei sewokeing qes o inyon. Om Aleksanda embei neil qayeeng nox wou xel om pepeeng xel angya mema bei xel se baluk.
ACT 19:34 Ekom xel yei bei e yon tambiy wei Yuda yo ti, om moux alis vex on dalus ghak niseikeing teyei lek seivma yuw me neil embei, “Atemis wei Epeses ne lei yon ngandoung!”
ACT 19:35 Kuskus wei beyeeng ngandoung Epeses on pepeeng moux alis vex on bei xel denduing ama de neil: “Xam moux wei Epeses on ngo, xomaxoneing eti se woulek bei Epeses ne beyeeng wei yeingteyei xomek wei anutu vex Atemis o, me yeiteyei qakous vambueing tiwei tei lam anghei tyoung o?
ACT 19:36 Xomaxoneing ti se teyei bei pyalek qayeeng tine, nambei nyon xam deduingma, xam seng bo daing me ghe bong lulti.
ACT 19:37 Xam ghe qou tambiy yuw ne me ghe lam inye, ekom luw se panax lulti eivek xomek lalo, o lukyak lek xe xe anutu vex.
ACT 19:38 Woyom wangwei Demitrius me e xe xel xukxe eno xe qayeeng ti wou tambiy ti, ond bouk wei ngoeing qayeeng o di yeip. Me xel seyap toundei, bei xel menyex wou xel xe qayeeng.
ACT 19:39 Ek wangwei xam xe qayeeng valu nanghei, ond xam ghe nyeis inyon a mey eivek xel wei qekuma yon.
ACT 19:40 A neil ambei nyon en xey a toundei eivek nimaying ngandoung om seyap wei Rom eno teyei bei bo qayeeng en xey, en kwa wei xey a wong gweimbeeng ne eno qes ma. De wangwei xel teling xey bei xey a lam qekuma me na ghak enva, on tyek xey se teyei bei neil qayeeng ti nox.”
ACT 19:41 Ka kuskus neil qayeeng tine woy, moxo wong xel xomaxoneing on la.
ACT 20:1 Ka lukeing ngenong wei xomaxoneing on ma, Paulus taxe xel betiyeing qeku lam wou e me luk is xel. Woyom moxo neil qayeeng xeilala wou xel woy, me puw xel memend dom la Masedonia.
ACT 20:2 Moxo la ghavineeng eivek danghei tiyon, me wo qayeeng ngenong wou xomaxoneing bei na byexaxoun xel, de woyom la Grik wei xel mi taxe bei provins Akaya is ambei nyon,
ACT 20:3 moxo dei nanghei inyon teyei lek dentouk qes yal. Dekakom Yudayeiw tup qayeeng lekti, bei nyeis e gyeik ingwei embei na Siria yo, om moxo embei nox me na Masedonia.
ACT 20:4 Tambiy wei beyeeng Belia, inyon Sopata, Pilas neu moux, Alistakas me Sekandas on lam anghei Tesalonika, Gaius nanghei Debi, Timote is ambei nyon, me Tikikas me Tlopimas nanghei provins Esia nei.
ACT 20:5 Xel moux ti beimambei yon la tax en xa me di axe xa nanghei Troas.
ACT 20:6 Ka bouk wei Yaeing Belet Wei Yis Ma Veil o, eno xa qou sip me na la veil Pilipai, deka bouk lim la veil eno xa la wou xel wei la Troas atax o, me nanghei inyon eno xa dei teyei lek bouk lim yuw.
ACT 20:7 Lek bouk ti tax wei Sounda yo xa xouing a lam qekuma lekti bei dembu belet me na gha pasa. Paulus luk wou xel xomaxoneing on en nambei moxo tyek na veil xel lek bouk yanyeing, om moxo di puw qayeeng me ela boukeing masenghoing.
ACT 20:8 Inyon lam ngenong di tum eivek xomek lalei tiwei gheyapu yo, nanghei ingwei xa di qekuma yo.
ACT 20:9 De yak ghavis ti toundei paviy xomek mya nayak wei qoueing laweeng o e lei Yutikus, Paulus di puw qayeeng ngenong om moxo ma yeip me nalei maxow. Dekakom moxo oing me teila tembuing nanghei xomek lalei tiwei yal o, om xel la zeim e lek ekom moxo mey.
ACT 20:10 Paulus la xonei, me yeip lek ghavis on neing, de zeim e mema me neil, “Xam seng detek ti, moxo nanghei di pi yo!”
ACT 20:11 Woyom moxo lox me la gheyapu nei de dembu belet me ya is moux alis vex. Dekakom moxo mi luk me ela woyaing, om moxo la.
ACT 20:12 Yak ghavis on toundei mapieing, me xomaxoneing on qou me la beyeeng de xel laleind wo nimza.
ACT 20:13 Xa la eivek sip me na la beyeeng nayak Asos, me na di axe Paulus anghei Asos, e maxow neimbei xa na tax, en embei na vaxa.
ACT 20:14 De moxo la tyip wou xa ghei Asos, om xa qou e lam lek sip me xa xouing a la beyeeng Mitilini.
ACT 20:15 Yanyeing eno xa la eivek sip anghei inyon me na la tyip tembuing nayak Kios eivek mamileeng. De yanyeing nge eno xa la liveil me na teila tembuing nayak Samos eivek mamileeng, de yanyeing nge eno xa la tyip beyeeng nayak Miletus.
ACT 20:16 Paulus wou eivek nalei woy me qou sip me ghanaw Epeses en embei se mendei enden eivek provins Esia, qe embei na daing me na Yerusalem, wangwei e teyei nei, ond embei gyei bouk wei Pentikos o nanghei Yerusalem.
ACT 20:17 Nanghei Miletus, Paulus wong qayeeng la wou teivateiv wei kongrikesin wei Epeses bei xel nam wou e.
ACT 20:18 Xel la tyip woy, woyom moxo neil wou xel, “Xam ghe woulek kwa wei a mi wong gyeik a mindei is xam taxombouk o, myaxeeng wei a lam wou xam eivek provins Esia yo.
ACT 20:19 A mi wong Tambiy Ngandoung xe xuk me na mi beoux xow is mang louk, de na mi qalei nimaying wei Yudayeiw mi wong wou ay yo.
ACT 20:20 Xam ghe woulek bei a se xaleeng qe a mi neil qayeeng nimza wei embei devind xam o, me na mi teyoxe xam eivek beyeeng senghoing me na la xomek titi is me na teyoxe xam.
ACT 20:21 A mi neil e yeip yaing wou Yudayeiw me Grikyeiw bei xel pekwi xow me noum wou Anutu me bongis xe xe Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu.
ACT 20:22 “Me gweimbeeng, Laweeng Vambuing neil wou ay bei a na Yerusalem, de a se woulek vati wei embei balwou ay anghei inyei yo.
ACT 20:23 Ekom a woulek bei eivek beyeeng ngandoung sapa yon eno Laweeng Vambuing peti ay, bei tyek a balwou nimaying ngenong de xel a toung a na eivek xeitueing.
ACT 20:24 Ekom a se axe bei mapieing wei ay eno inyei lul nimza ti qe inye bandaing, en kandek a bong xuk pok me xuk wei Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu wong wou ay eno ema bole. Me na bong xuk tiwei neileing Anutu xe Xoulek Nimza wei lalei xeiles o.
ACT 20:25 “De gweimbeeng a woulek bei xam wei a neil qayeeng qes wei tete lalei wou xam o eno tyek xam seng nox me na gwei a manghalus no.
ACT 20:26 Nambei nyon, a neil e gyeip yaing wou xam gweimbeeng ne bei wangwei xel ti qou myaveweeng wei meyeing luta yo, on inye a se wong esewok.
ACT 20:27 En nambei Anutu xe qayeeng qes wei xam a being boulek, eno a se axvun.
ACT 20:28 Xam ghe gwei xow teyei, me moux alis vex dalus wei Laweeng Vambuing wong wou xam bei xam ghe gweiteyei yo, xam on Anutu xe gyovaxa wei kongrikesin o. Wei e xouv xam angya emaxow gyand o.
ACT 20:29 Ka a bei na ekom a woulek bei, naw bemeeng tyek nam eivek xam senghoing me bo nol wou sipsip yeiw ne.
ACT 20:30 De xam venaxow xe xel valu tyek qandi me bong qayeeng tyonyeing me na puw xel betiyeing valu betiwou xel.
ACT 20:31 Om xam ghe gweiteyei xow, xam ghe bounaleim bei teyei lek vakovek qes yal eno a se mi tip neileing wou xam titi boukeing aluw bendiyeing is mang louk.
ACT 20:32 “Gweimbeeng a toung xam eivek Anutu mema, en ambei xam ghe bou naleimim en e xe qayeeng wei lalei xeiles o. Lalei xeiles tine eno teyeimbei bo nikanzek wou xam, me tyek teyeimbei bong lulul nimza dalus wei Anutu mi wong wou xomaxoneing wei e wong xel wo vambuing o.
ACT 20:33 A se mi xei manglek silva me ghol me qaeing wei xelti xe yo.
ACT 20:34 Xam venaxow ghe woulek woy bei a maxow memang ne mi wong vineing wou xow me na mi vind xel wei mindei is ay yo.
ACT 20:35 Eivek lul tambak wei a mi wong o, a talex wou xam bei xey a betiwou kwa wei xey a bo xuk nikanzek. En kandek xey a devind xel wei nikanzek maeing o, xey a bou naleind en qayeeng wei Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu venaxow neil o: ‘Inye mata nimza ena wou xel wei mi tatei memend o ghanaw xel wei mi qou e lam wou xow o.’”
ACT 20:36 Paulus neil qayeeng tine woy, woyom moxo ev vaxa qatu eivek dom zeimema is xel gyovaxa yon dalus.
ACT 20:37 Moxoyeiw dalus eng me zeimaxoun Paulus dom ya e ling.
ACT 20:38 Xel xouing laleind pyaxow en qayeeng wei e neil o, en tyek xel se nox gyei e ma no. De woyom xel qou e me la eivek sip.
ACT 21:1 Ka xa la veil xel teivateiv on, xa la ingwei mamileeng nei me na qou sip de sepa me na la bombek wou ailan Kos. Deka woyaing xa la veil ailan Rodes me na la tyip beyeeng nayak Patara.
ACT 21:2 Nanghei inyon eno xa xei sip ti embei na distrik Ponisia, om xa la eivek sip tiyon me sepa me na la.
ACT 21:3 Ka xa ghei di xeip lek mamileeng eno xa xei la ailan Saiprus nanghei mema qeinz, ekom xa ghanaw tembuing nayak eivek mamileeng on me na la tyip Siria. Xa la liveil anghei beyeeng nayak Taia, nanghei inyon eno sip la toung qoupek teila.
ACT 21:4 Xa xei xel betiyeing nanghei inyon, om xa dei is xel teyei lek bouk lim yuw. Eivek Laweeng Vambuing eno xel neil wou Paulus bei e se na pu Yerusalem nei.
ACT 21:5 Ekom xa xe seivma la wou eivek, om xa ghanaw beyeeng on me na la. Xel betiyeing dalus lis venei neu xel xouing qou xa me la myayaing veil beyeeng on, de xa ev vaxami qatu eivek lek luzeeng wei mamileeng vi yon de na zeimemami.
ACT 21:6 Ka xa puw ama memami woy, woyom xa lek la sip, de moxoyeiw lox bend.
ACT 21:7 Xa la veil Taia, dom na la tei beyeeng Tolemes. Xa neil bendiyeing wou xel lingyeiw dom na toundei is xel bouk ti.
ACT 21:8 Lek bouk nge xa la tyip Sisalia me na toundei eivek Pilip xe xomek inyon sinale ti, e eivek xel lim yuw on eno ti wei mi vind xel sinaleyeiw o.
ACT 21:9 Moxo neuyeiw vexawo vey wei mi dei paleveeng, eno xel mi neil xoulek ambei poropet.
ACT 21:10 Ka xa dei teyei lek bouk valu eivek Sisalia, poropet ti lei Agabus eno lam veil Yudia me lam axo wei Sisalia ne.
ACT 21:11 Moxo lam wou xa, me qou Paulus xe let, de tup emaxow mema luw vaxa de neil, “Laweeng Vambuing neil ambei nye, ‘Eivek sakwaing tine Yudayeiw wei mindei eivek Yerusalem eno tyek bako tambiy tiwei e xe let ne yo me na toung e na eivek xel amba memend.’”
ACT 21:12 Xa ngo tine, eno xa me xel xomaxoneing on eno xa tay wou Paulus bei e se na pu wei Yerusalem nei.
ACT 21:13 Woyom Paulus neil embei, “Xam ghe di eng me ghe wong a laleing pyaw xow en va? A xeiwou xow woy bei xel a toung ay eivek xeitueing, me xel nyeis a mey nanghei Yerusalem en Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu lei.”
ACT 21:14 Paulus wo nikanzek bei embei na, om xa tip lukeing me na neil, “Lul wei Tambiy Ngandoung wounalei bei etyip, ond inyon etyip.”
ACT 21:15 Ka bouk valu la veil, xa xeiwou xow me na la pu wei Yerusalem nei.
ACT 21:16 Xel betiyeing valu wei mindei Sisalia eno lam is xa me qou xa me la Nason wei Saiprus eno beeng. Inyon betiyeing wei takwei yo ti wei tyek xa toumendei is e yo.
ACT 21:17 Ka xa la tyip Yerusalem, eno xel lingyeiw qou xa is xeilala.
ACT 21:18 Yanyeing eno Paulus me xa dalus a la xei Jems, me teivateiv dalus eno lam toundei inyon.
ACT 21:19 Paulus neil bendiyeing wou xel, de neil wou xel en vati wei Anutu wong eivek xel amba senghoing en e xe xuk wei wong o.
ACT 21:20 Ka xel teivateiv ngo Paulus xe qayeeng woy, xel sanghoxe Anutu. De xel neil wou Paulus: “Ling, wang wei, xel ngenongakes wei Yuda eno wongis, om xel dalus on di luk ngenong en qayeeng petieing wei Mose yo.
ACT 21:21 Ekom xel on valu neil wou xel en wang bei, wang di teyoxe Yudayeiw dalus wei mindei eivek xel amba senghoing bei xel a saing Mose xe petieing, de neil wou xel bei xel se ghuw neundyeiw ninavi, o xam se betiwou kwa wei takwei yo.
ACT 21:22 Tyek xey a bong vati? Gyeik xel a ngo inye neing bei wang lam,
ACT 21:23 om wong vati wei xa bei neil wou wang ne. Inyon moux vey toundei is xey, xel eti yeiw wei neil qayeeng zonghek ti is Anutu yo.
ACT 21:24 Qou xel moux beimambei ne, me xam xouing betiwou kwa wei deing vako yo me wa dexouv xel xe da en kandek xel a puw lund velus veil. Woyom tyek xel dalus boulek zonghek bei neing ma veil qayeeng tiwei xel byex lek wang ne, ekom wamaxow mendi betiwou petieing.
ACT 21:25 De xel amba wei wongeingis, eno xey a byex qapiya wou xel bei xel gyeiteyei xow en yaeing leliy wei xel sei da wou anutu tyonyeing o, me xel se gya leliy wei gyand toundei eivek o, me leliy leyeis wei xel tup xel kwend me xel se bong kwa nilul wei kwapesiv o.”
ACT 21:26 Paulus qou xel moux wei xel neil qayeeng zonghek is Anutu woy yo, de yanyeing eno emaxow betiwou kwa dalus wei e bei bo vako yo is xel. Woyom moxo la ingwei xomek vambuing nei me neil wou lumukiyeiw en bouk nge wei tyek xel bo vako yo de tyek xel titi nam a toung xel xe da.
ACT 21:27 Gyeik bouk lim yuw embim nama, xel Yudayeiw valu nanghei provins wei Esia eno yei Paulus eivek xomek vambuing. Om xel zeim moux dalus on laleind lek me zeimaxoun e,
ACT 21:28 de xel taxe niseikeing bei, “xam moux wei Israel o, vind xa! Moux tine inye tambiy wei mi teyoxe xomaxoneing dalus la danghei danghei nei me neil nilul lek xe xe xel xomaxoneing me Mose xe petieing me beyeeng tine. Me se tine venaxow, qe qou Grikyeiw me la eivek xomek vambuing lalei me wo nol wou xomek vambuing ne wo nilaxes.”
ACT 21:29 (En nambei takwei eno xel yei Tlopimas wei Epeses o toundei eivek Yerusalem is Paulus, me xel embeik nge Paulus qou tambiy on me la eivek xomek vambuing on lalei.)
ACT 21:30 Xel xomaxoneing dalus wei beyeeng ngandoung on etek mouyo, me xomaxoneing dalus veimyend me lam anghei danghei danghei nei. Me zeimaxoun Paulus, xel tetei e veil tete lalei wei xomek vambuing on, dom xel wo daing me toung tete mya dalus zeyi.
ACT 21:31 Kalekom xel di wong en embei nyeis e, om xel wong qayeeng la wou vevekyeiw xe lei ngandoung wei Rom o bei beyeeng ngandoung wei Yerusalem eno neilama me di leis ama bandabanda.
ACT 21:32 Moxo wo daing me qou beyeiv xel lei ngandoung me xel vevek valu dom xel veimyend me la wou xel qendu ngandoung on. Gyeik xel on yei lei ngandoung is e xe xel vevekyeiw, xel tip de se leis Paulus no.
ACT 21:33 Lei ngandoung on lam paviy me zeimaxoun Paulus me luk nikanzek wou xel vevek on bei xel atup e nangya sen yayuw. Woyom moxo teling Yudayeiw bei, tambiy yon eti me vati ingwei e di wong on.
ACT 21:34 Xel qendu ngandoung on valu taxe lul nge de xel valu taxe lul bange me neil qayeeng la bandabanda, om lei ngandoung wei xel vevek o se teyei bei ngo wou qayeeng qes, om luk nikanzek wou xel vevek bei xel a qou Paulus me na eivek bend.
ACT 21:35 Ekom gyeik Paulus la tyip wou lewing, xel vevekyeiw yei moux alis vex on ngenong embei nyeis e, om xel qalei moxo me la.
ACT 21:36 Xel moux alis vex wei di betiy xel on taxe niseikeing bei, “Leis e mey!”
ACT 21:37 Ka vevekyeiw qou Paulus me embei na eivek bend, moxo teling wou lei ngandoung bei, “Teyei bei a neil qayeeng ti wou wang?” Lei ngandoung neil embei, “Wang woulek Grik vyend?
ACT 21:38 Beip wang on Izip, tiwei wo vevek wou seyap de qou 4,000 moux wei mi wong vevek en ngeyeing me la eivek tembuing bandaing wei bouk valu la veil o?”
ACT 21:39 Paulus neimbei, “A ne Yuda ti, nanghei Tarsus eivek Silisia, a bang nei lei laeing. Teyeimbei a baluk wou xel xomaxoneing ne.”
ACT 21:40 Tambiy wei Lei ngandoung on lewexe lek telinyeing tiyon, Paulus nale lek lewing dom pepeeng xel qendu ngandoung on. Ka xel denduing ma, moxo luk wou xel eivek Yuda vyend.
ACT 22:1 “Xam lingyeiw me xam mangyeiw, xam ngo a xe qayeeng wei ambei neil gweimbeeng ne eno qes teyei.”
ACT 22:2 Xel ngo moxo di luk wou xel eivek xel venaxow vyend Hibru, om moxoyeiw denduing ma. De Paulus neil embei:
ACT 22:3 A ne Yuda ti, a umbek eivek Tarsus wei Silisia nei, ekom a ling eivek Yerusalem de Gameliel mi teyoxe ay en petieing wei Mose xe yo, me a mi byexaxoun Anutu xe kwa wei lalei vind xey nambei xam valu ghe di wong gweimbeeng ne.
ACT 22:4 An di wo nol wou xel wei wongis bei na nyeis xel amey, xel wei mi betiwou sakwaing tine, a zeimaxoun xel moux alis vex me na toung xel la eivek xomek xeitueing.
ACT 22:5 Lumuki lukanzek me xel kanzol dalus tyek na neil a teyei. A qou qapiya wou xel me na la wou lingyeiw eivek Damaskus, me na la inyei bei na bako xel xomaxoneing nanghei inyon me na qou xel me na nam Yerusalem en xel teivateiv bo myaveweeng wou xel.
ACT 22:6 “Bendiyeing wei seivma evlek a lam paviy Damaskus, de lutika eno xeiyaing teleing ti lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei me tel evivekwou ay.
ACT 22:7 A teila lek tembuing me na ngo vya ti neil wou ay, ‘Sol! Sol! Nambei nya wang di wo nol wou ay?’
ACT 22:8 “A teling bei, Tambiy Ngandoung, ‘Wang eti?’ “Moxo neil eloum bei, ‘A Yesu wei Nasaret, tiwei wang di wo nimaying wou yo.’
ACT 22:9 A xe xel wei mi la is ay yo eno yei xeiyaing, ekom xel se woulek tambiy tiwei di luk is ay eno vya.
ACT 22:10 “De a teling, Tambiy Ngandoung, ‘Tyek a bong vati?’ Tambiy Ngandoung neil, ‘Qandi lek me la eivek Damaskus. Nanghei inyon tyek xel a neil wou wang en vati wei wambei bong o.’
ACT 22:11 A xe xel wei la is ay eno zeim a memang me xa la eivek Damaskus, en nambei xeiyaing on byex a mang tekzeyi.
ACT 22:12 “Tambiy ti lei Ananias lam me yei ay. Moxo mi wevek Anutu xeinghembi me mi betiwou qayeeng petieing wo nimza. Me Yudayeiw wei mindei inyon eno mi neil embei e moux nimza.
ACT 22:13 Moxo nale paviy ay me neil, ‘Ling Sol, wa mamghalus e gyeina!’ De lutika eno a manghalus yeila me a xei e.
ACT 22:14 “Woyom moxo neil: ‘Anutu wei xe mendyeiw eno beyal wang bei wang boulek e xe lalei vineing me ghe gwei Tambiy Tiwei Bombek ayang o me na ngo e xe qayeeng eivek e mya.
ACT 22:15 Wang teyei lek e xe tambiy wei yeimawou woy o, om tyek wa qou vati wei wang wei lek mamghalus me ghe ngo yo me na neil teyei ena wou xomaxoneing sapa.
ACT 22:16 Om gweimbeeng ne wang di axe vati? Qandi lek me qou lipekeing. De taxe e lei en e sekweyexe wa xe sewokeing veil o.’
ACT 22:17 “Ka a loum Yerusalem me na di zeimemang eivek xomek vambuing, a xeip naleing ma,
ACT 22:18 me na xei Tambiy Ngandoung luk wou ay nambei inye. ‘La daing, me la veil Yerusalem lutika, en tyek xel se ngo wa xe qayeeng wei wambei neil a teyei yo.’
ACT 22:19 “A lewexe bei, ‘Tambiy Ngandoung, xel moux tine woulek bei a la Yudayeiw xe xomek qekueing ama, me na la nge me na toung moux alis vex wei wongis wang eno eivek xeitueing de na leis xel.
ACT 22:20 De gyeik xel leis Setepan mey, wa xe tambiy wei mi neil wa xe xoulek eno a toukale paviy me na xei e gyand qapyex o, me na xeiteyei eti yeiw wei leis e yo xe teimb.’
ACT 22:21 “Woyom Tambiy Ngandoung neil wou ay, ‘La. Tyek a bong wang na dingta lul nei wou xel amba.’ ”
ACT 22:22 Xel qendu tiyon ngo Paulus deka moxo neil tine. Woyom xel taxe niseikeing bei, “Leis e mey! Tambiy ambei nyon se toumendei mapieing lek tembuing!”
ACT 22:23 Ka xel wo vyend me kwax xel xe teimb ding me nex ela me nex vegyuveeng la gheyapu,
ACT 22:24 om lei ngandoung wei xel vevek o wo qayeeng nikanzek bei xel a qou Paulus me na bend. Moxo neil wou xel bei xel sesa e me bo telinyeing me gyimexe nimaying tiyon qes, embei boulek bei xel xomaxoneing on di wo vyendlek e en va.
ACT 22:25 Ka xel tup Paulus mema vaxa bei na sesa e, Paulus neil wou beyeiv wei xel xe yo, wei toukale paviy on me neimbei, “Inye se la teyei lek petieing bei wa sesa tambiy wei Rom wei xam seng ghei wo qayeeng en e yo?”
ACT 22:26 Beyeiv ngo qayeeng tine, om moxo la neil wou lei ngandoung wei vevekyeiw o. Moxo teling, “Tyek wang bong ambei nya? Moux tine inye tambiy wei Rom o.”
ACT 22:27 Lei ngandoung wei xel vevek o la wou Paulus me teling, “Neil wou ay, inyon wa Rom ti ei?” Moxo lewexe, “Ee inye ay yo.”
ACT 22:28 Woyom lei ngandoung neil wou e, “A wong malew ngandoung bei na bong ambei tambiy wei Rom o.” Paulus neil elox bei, “Ekom a umbek eivek beyeeng ne nambei tambiy wei Rom o ti.”
ACT 22:29 Eti yeiw wei di wong en embei sesa e eno duxeind lutika. Deka lei ngandoung woulek bei Paulus on tambiy wei Rom, om moxo yaleeng en venaxow neil wou xel vevek bei xel a tup Paulus en sen.
ACT 22:30 Yanyeing eno lei ngandoung wei xel vevek o embei boulek qes bei nambei nya ekom Yudayeiw byex qayeeng lek Paulus, om moxo kwax sen veil Paulus. De wong qayeeng la wou xel kanzol me lumuki leitata bei xel nam qekuma. De qou Paulus me lam wong e nale wou xel mendghalus.
ACT 23:1 Paulus doma wou xel kanzol me neil, “Xam lingyeiw eivek a laleing, a mi la bombek me sewokeing ma veil ay wou Anutu manghalus me e lam tyip gweimbeeng.”
ACT 23:2 Moxo neil ambei nyon, eno lumuki lukanzek Ananias neil nikanzek wou xel moux wei toukale paviy Paulus on bei xel petapexe e mya.
ACT 23:3 Woyom Paulus neil wou e, “Anutu tyek sesa wang, wang on nambei tete nol wei xel pelei teleing lek o! Wang wou kwam en wa bei betiwou petieing me ghe bo qayeeng en ay, om wang lam toundei inyon, ekom wamaxow ghe pyalek petieing me ghe neil nikanzek bei xel sesa ay.”
ACT 23:4 Xel wei toukale paviy Paulus eno neil, “Nambei nya wambei neil qayeeng nol lek Anutu xe lumuki lukanzek on?”
ACT 23:5 Paulus neil elox bei, “Xam lingyeiw, a se woulek bei inyon moxo lumuki lukanzek. En nambei xel byex eivek xoulek bei: ‘Xam se baluk nilul lek tambiy wei mi yeiteyei wa xe xel xomaxoneing o.’ ”
ACT 23:6 Woyom Paulus woulek woy bei, xel on valu yon Sadyusi me xel valu yon Parisi, om taxe la wou xel kanzol, “Xam lingyeiw, a ne Parisi, me Parisi neu moux ay. A nale lek qayeeng wongeing en nambei a mi toung manghalus bei xel meyeing tyek qandi lek.”
ACT 23:7 Paulus neil qayeeng tine, eno qayeeng vevek qandi eivek xel Sadyusi me xel Parisi, me xel wei di qekuma eno dembuma is ambei nyon.
ACT 23:8 (Xel Sadyusi neil embei xel meyeing tyek se qandi lek, me inyon angela ma me laweeng ma, ekom xel Parisi wongis lul tine dalus.)
ACT 23:9 Om bembeeng on wong nindenduing ngandoung kamouyo, me xel putoung wei petieing o valu eno Parisi wei toungale inyon eno luk nikanzek bei, “Xa se xei lulti sewok eivek tambiy ne. Beind laweeng o angela luk wou e.”
ACT 23:10 Qayeeng vevek wo ngandoung om lei ngandoung wei xel vevek o yaleeng enok moux alis vex tetei Paulus me e neing a tip. Om moxo wo qayeeng nikanzek wou xel vevekyeiw bei xel na tetei e veil xel me na qou e me na eivek bend.
ACT 23:11 Yanyeing boukeing eno Tambiy Ngandoung toungale paviy Paulus me neil, “Wa bale bo nikanzek! Nambei ingwei wang mi neil a xe xoulek eivek Yerusalem o, om wa mi neil a xe qayeeng ambei nyon eivek Rom is.”
ACT 23:12 Yanyeing satiboukeing eno Yudayeiw qekuma me tup qayeeng lekti, me xel neil neing is inya punei bei, tyek xel se gya o na num, qe ka xel nyeis Paulus amey bole.
ACT 23:13 Xel moux wei neil qayeeng tine eno teyei lek xoumeeng vey (40).
ACT 23:14 Xel la wou xel lumuki leitata yo me teivateiv me neil, “Xa neil neing is inya punei bei, xa se teyei bei gha lulti qe ka xa nyeis Paulus amey le.
ACT 23:15 Woyom gweimbeeng, xam me xel kanzol ghe bong qayeeng na wou lei ngandoung, en e qou Paulus me nam axone wou xam. Me na tyoxe e bei xam ambei ngo qayeeng neing valu en tine. Dom xa menyex wou xow en kandek na nyeis e gyeik moxo nam a tyip inye yo.”
ACT 23:16 Ekom Paulus li vex neu moux ngo qayeeng tine, om moxo la eivek xel vevekyeiw bend me neil wou Paulus.
ACT 23:17 Woyom Paulus taxe beyeiv ti me neil wou e, “Qou moux ghavis tine me la wou lei ngandoung wei vevek o. Moxo embei neil qayeeng ngandoung ti wou e.”
ACT 23:18 Om moxo qou e me la wou lei ngandoung wei xel vevek o. Beyeiv neil, “Paulus, tambiy wei la xeitueing, taxe a la me teling wou ay bei a qou moux ghavis tine me na nam wou wang en e bei neil lul valu wou wang.”
ACT 23:19 Lei ngandoung wei vevek o zeim moux ghavis on mema, de qou e me la nenyawes me teling e, “Inye wambei neil vati wou ay?”
ACT 23:20 Moxo neil, “Xel Yuda toung qayeeng lekti bei tyek teling wou wang bei wa qou Paulus me ghe na wou xel kanzol yanyeing. Xel embei tyoxe wang bei na ngo wou qayeeng on qes bo nimza en tambiy yon.
ACT 23:21 Wang seng bong e wou xel, en xel on teyei lek xoumeeng vey (40) eno di xupek me axe me neil neing is inya punei bei tyek xel se gya lulti o na num qe ka xel nyeis Paulus amey bole. Xel yeiwou xow gweimbeeng, xel di axe wang bei wang zenghek lek xel xe qayeeng.”
ACT 23:22 Lei ngandoung wei xel vevekyeiw o wong ghavis on la de luk nikanzek wou e, “Wa se neil wou xelti bei wang neil qayeeng tine wou ay.”
ACT 23:23 Woyom moxo taxe e xe beyeiv yuw me wo qayeeng nikanzek wou luw bei, “Muw ghe gweiwou me na qou 200 vevekyeiw is 70 vevekyeiw wei mi dei lek vuteiv o me na qou 200 moux wei mi wo vevek angya yiy o is. Me xam ghe na Sisalia boukeing lek seivma limvey.
ACT 23:24 Xam ghe gweiwou vuteiv wou Paulus is ambei nyon me na qou e me ghe na nimza wou Peliks lei ngandoung wei seyap o.”
ACT 23:25 Moxo byex qapiya nambei nye:
ACT 23:26 A Klodias Lisias, a byex qapiya ne lak wou wa Peliks lei ngandoung wei seyap o. Bendiyeing wang.
ACT 23:27 Tambiy tine eno Yudayeiw zeimaxoun me xel embim nyeis e, ekom a la is a xe xel vevekyeiw me na la qou e veil xel memend, en a woulek bei inyon e wei nanghei Rom o.
ACT 23:28 Ambei ngo wou bei nambei nya ekom xel byex qayeeng lek e, om a qou e me na la wou xel xe kanzol.
ACT 23:29 A xei bei xel byex qayeeng lek e me teling wou e en xel venaxow xe petieing, ekom xel se wong qayeeng ti teyei bei e mey o e na xeitueing.
ACT 23:30 De a ngo bei xel tup qayeeng lekti xupekeing en xel embei nyeis tambiy tine na mey, om a wong e lak wou wang lutika. Me a wong qayeeng nikanzek wou xel wei byex qayeeng lek e yo bei xel nak a neil qes tiwei xel zeim e eno wou wang teyei.
ACT 23:31 Om xel vevekyeiw, eno betiwou qayeeng nikanzek wei xel e lei ngandoung wei xel vevek o me qou Paulus me lak eivek boukeing me la beyeeng Antipatris.
ACT 23:32 Yanyeing eno xel wei mindei lek vuteiv eno la is e, de xel vevekyeiw valu loum bend nanghei Yerusalem.
ACT 23:33 Xel vevekyeiw wei mindei lek vuteiv o la tyip Sisalia, xel qou qapiya me la wong wou lei ngandoung wei seyap o de wong Paulus la wou e.
ACT 23:34 Lei ngandoung wei seyap o pyaw qapiya, woyom teling Paulus bei, “wang lam anghei provins tina.” Moxo woulek bei Paulus lam anghei Silisia,
ACT 23:35 Lei ngandoung wei seyap o neil, “Tyek a ngo wa xe qayeeng gyeik xel wei wong qayeeng en wang o nam a tyip inye.” Woyom e wo qayeeng nikanzek wou belimbo yeiw bei xel gyei Paulus teyei eivek Herot beeng.
ACT 24:1 Ka bouk lim la veil, woyom Ananias lumuki lukanzek la xo wei Sisalia nei is xel teivateiv valu me tambiy wei lupeyei yeip yaing en petieing wei xel Rom o lei Tetalas, me qou xel xe qayeeng wei xel embei bo qayeeng en Paulus eno wou lei ngandoung wei seyap o manghalus.
ACT 24:2 Woyom lei ngandoung Peliks taxe Paulus la lalei, de Tetalas wong qayeeng en e me neil ambei nye: “Lei ngandoung Peliks, xa dei ewo nimza eivek wa xe lalei vevopeing me wang vind xa xe xel me ghe menyex wou lulul ngenong wei takwei wei xel se dei ewo nimza yo.
ACT 24:3 Xa xei lulti beimambei ne, om xa laleimi wo nimza mouyo, me na neil dange ngandoung wou wang.
ACT 24:4 Ekom xa se teyei bei zeimaxoun wang enden. Ambei tay wou wang en wa laleim vevop wou xa me na ngo xa xe qayeeng sepi kane.
ACT 24:5 “Xa xei tambiy tine eno mi wo nilul ngenong, moxo mi zeim xel laleind lek en vevek eivek Yudayeiw senghoing me la teyei lek tembuing sapa. Tambiy on gyovaxa wei xel qendu tiwei la veil xa dom xel mi taxe bei Nasaret o.
ACT 24:6 Me moxo wong me yei en embei bong xomek vambuing on bo nilaxes wou Anutu manghalus, ekom xa zeimaxoun e, me xa bei bo qayeeng en e nangya xa maxow xe petieing.
ACT 24:7 Ekom Lisias lei ngandoung lam is e xe vevekyeiw me wo vevek is xa me tetei Paulus veil xa memami.
ACT 24:8 Dekalekom neil qayeeng nikanzek wou eti yeiw wei embei zeim qayeeng en e eno e nam wou wang. Om wa venaxow ghe gwei embo nimza. Me teling e en tine, me na qou kwa wou emaxow vya en lul beimambei ne bei xa wo qayeeng en e.”
ACT 24:9 Xel Yuda vind Tetalas is ambei nyon, me byex qayeeng lek Paulus bei inye zonghek.
ACT 24:10 Woyom lei ngandoung wei seyap o tetax kwa bei e baluk om Paulus neil elox: “A woulek bei lek vakovek qes valu eno wang mi zeim qayeeng wei xa xomaxoneing dalus ne. Om a laleind wo nimza me na lewexe lek wa xe qayeeng.
ACT 24:11 Wangwei wa teling enana nei, yon wang boulek bei bouk xoumeeng yuw la veil eno a la pu Yerusalem bei na bong lalo.
ACT 24:12 A xei bei xel wei Yuda eno se yei bei a wo veweeng is xelti eivek xomek vambuing, o xel se yei bei a zeim xel qekueing ama yon laleind lek eivek Yudayeiw xe xomek qekueing ama me eivek beyeeng ngandoung on ti. Ma.
ACT 24:13 Me xel se teyei bei talex bei qayeeng wei xel byex lek a ne eno inye zonghek.
ACT 24:14 Ekom ambei neilteyei bei, a mi wong lalo wou Anutu wei xa bumiyeiw o me na mi betiwou Sakwaing Tiyon, wei xel mi taxe bei bange. A wongis lul dalus wei Mose byex eivek petieing o me xel poropet byex eyeip eivek qapiya yo,
ACT 24:15 me a wongis me na di toung mang en Anutu nambei xel moux beimambei ne bei tyek na piyexe xel wei bombek o me xel wei nilul o eno xel xouing qandi lek veil meyeing.
ACT 24:16 Om nambei nyon a mi wo nikanzek me na mi xeiteyei laleing wo nimza bei emi mendei embo bombek wou Anutu manghalus me xel xomaxoneing mendghalus is ambei nyon.
ACT 24:17 “Ka a la dei vakovek qes valu eivek beyeeng ba, a loum Yerusalem me na qou lul wei xeilala yo valu wou a xe xel xomaxoneing bei na bong wou xel wei kanyo yo de na toung da.
ACT 24:18 De gyeik xel yei ay eivek xomek vambuing eno a wo vako woy wou Anutu manghalus. Me xel ngenong ti se toundei is ay, me wo nindenduing bandabanda.
ACT 24:19 Ekom Yudayeiw valu lam anghei provins wei Esia nei me zeimaxoun ay. Wangwei xel xe qayeeng ti mendei gyeip wou ay ond inye nimza bei xel venaxow nam inye wou wa manghalus me bong qayeeng en ay.
ACT 24:20 O xel beimambei wei toundei inye eno teyeimbei neil sewokeing vati wei xel yei eivek ay eno teyei gyeik ingwei a nale wou xel kanzol mendghalus o.
ACT 24:21 Om qayeeng tixemou wei a taxe eno nambei nye: ‘Qayeeng wei xel meyeing tyek qandi lek veil meyeing, om qes tine gweimbeeng xel wong qayeeng en ay.’ ”
ACT 24:22 Woyom Peliks woulek kwa wei xel xomaxoneing ne mi betiwou Sakwaing Tiyon wo nimza yo, om tetulexe bouk dom wong xel lox de neil, “Gyeik Lisias lei ngandoung wei xel vevek o nam, tyek a menyex wou wa xe qayeeng.”
ACT 24:23 Moxo wo qayeeng nikanzek wou beyeiv bei e toung Paulus eivek xel belimbo memend, me neil wou xel bei xel se bale zeyi e qe e mi ghavineeng me nox me num eivek xomek lalei me xel se bale zeyi e xe gweleeng qe xel a mi gyei e teyei en lulul vatiyeiw.
ACT 24:24 Bouk valu la veil, Peliks lam is venei Drusila, inye Yuda vex ti. Moxo wong qayeeng la wou Paulus me e lam de li nenya wou qayeeng wei e di neil o, Paulus neil wou e en kwa wei wongeingis Yesu Kilisi yo.
ACT 24:25 Ka Paulus luk is xel en sakwaing bombek, me ingwei xomaxoneing na mi gyeiteyei xow me ingwei Anutu tyek na zeim qayeeng en xey loxyus o. Omva Peliks moxo yaleeng me neil, “Gweimbeeng inye woy! Wang na. Deka anghei sakwaing ti gyeip yaing, on tyek a bong qayeeng nak wou wang.”
ACT 24:26 Lek bouk kayon bombek eno moxo embeik nge tyek Paulus bong malew valu wou e, en na zeimaxoun Peliks lalei de na tul e na nivax. Om lumama eno moxo mi wong qayeeng la wou e bei baluk is e.
ACT 24:27 Ka vakovek qes yuw la veil, Posias Festus qou Peliks nimbeeng. De Peliks embei bong Yudayeiw bo xeindlala en e, om wong Paulus toundei eivek xeitueing.
ACT 25:1 Festus wo seyap wei provins Yudia yo. Ka bouk yal la veil eno Festus la veil Sisalia me la tyip Yerusalem nei.
ACT 25:2 Om xel lumuki leitata me Yuda xe gyovaxa lam wou e me byex qayeeng lek Paulus. Xel luk nikanzek wou Festus bei,
ACT 25:3 e devind xel me bong Paulus na Yerusalem, en nambei xel di yeiwou xow bei nyeis Paulus amey wou sakwaing.
ACT 25:4 Festus lewexe bei, “Paulus toundei eivek xeitueing anghei Sisalia, me a maxow a bim ana inyei paviyeing ka.”
ACT 25:5 Om moxo neil, “Xam xe gyovaxa valu nam is ay me bong qayeeng en tambiy yon, wangwei moxo bong sewokeing ti nei.”
ACT 25:6 Ka Festus dei bouk lim yal o xoumeeng is xel, de moxo la xo wei Sisalia nei, de yanyeing eno moxo la dei eivek xomek wei ngoeing qayeeng me wong qayeeng nikanzek bei xel a qou Paulus me nam wou e.
ACT 25:7 Ka Paulus lam woy, xel Yudayeiw wei lam axone nanghei Yerusalem eno nale vivekwou e, xel byex qayeeng nilul leimalei lek e bei bong qayeeng en e, ekom xel se teyei bei talex wou Festus bei qayeeng ne neing.
ACT 25:8 Woyom Paulus neil e xe qayeeng lox wou xel: “A se wong sewokeing ti lek petieing wei xel Yudayeiw, o lek xomek vambuing, o wou Sisa, king wei Rom o.”
ACT 25:9 Ekom Festus e bei bong xel Yudayeiw laleind bo nimza wou e, om teling wou Paulus, “Beip wa being na pu wei Yerusalem nei me bale lek qayeeng wou ay anghei inyei en qayeeng ti beimambei ne?”
ACT 25:10 Paulus lewexe, “Gweimbeeng a nale lek Sisa xe xomek wei ngoeing qayeeng eivek o. Wei tyek a bo qayeeng o. En a se wo sewokeing ti wou xel Yudayeiw, nambei ingwei wamaxow ghe woulek e wo nimza yo.
ACT 25:11 Nambei nyon wangwei a bong sewokeing ti teyei bei a mey lek nei, Ond tyek a se pesek en meyeing. Ekom wangwei qayeeng wei xel byex lek a ne se neing, ond xel ti se teyei bei toung ay eivek xel on memend. Tyek a maxow a bong qayeeng wou Sisa me e ngo!”
ACT 25:12 Ka Festus luk is e xe xel kanzol, moxo neil: “Wang neimbei Sisa e ngo wa xe qayeeng. Om tyek wang na wou Sisa!”
ACT 25:13 Bouk valu lak veil, King Agripa me Benaisi la tei Sisalia bei na bong luw xe qayeeng nimza wou Festus.
ACT 25:14 Ka xel dei luk ngenong nanghei inyon, Festus neilteyei wou king en Paulus xe qayeeng. Moxo neil: “Inyon tambiy ti toundei inye eno Peliks wong e ghei toundei eivek xomek xeitueing.
ACT 25:15 Gyeik a la Yerusalem, xel lumuki leitata me teivateiv wei Yudayeiw eno byex qayeeng lek e me teling bei xel bo myaveweeng wou moxo.
ACT 25:16 “A neil wou xel bei inye se kwa wei xa wei Rom o bei xa toung nimaying lek tambiy ti bandaing, qe ka e bale wou xel wei wo qayeeng en e yo mendghalus bole me na neil qayeeng valu me bale zeyi xow en xel xe qayeeng.
ACT 25:17 Om ka xel lam inye is ay, a se wong xel mi axe ay. Qe a dei eivek xomek wei ngoeing qayeeng eno lek nge yanyeing me na wong qayeeng la bei xel a qou tambiy on me nam.
ACT 25:18 Gyeik xel wei wo qayeeng en e yo nale me luk, ekom xel se neil qayeeng nilul ti lek e nambei a wou eivek naleing o.
ACT 25:19 Qe xel wei pyalek ama is e en xel xe lalo me tambiy wei mey eno lei Yesu, ekom Paulus neil embei moxo toundei mapieing.
ACT 25:20 A se teyei bei gheiwou qayeeng tine qes, om a teling moxo bei e teyei bei na Yerusalem me na bale lek wongeing qayeeng tine.
ACT 25:21 Ekom Paulus neil, embei toumendei eivek xeitueing teyei lek ingwei king Sisa wei Rom eno na ngo qayeeng wei e yo. Om a wong qayeeng nikanzek la bei xel gyei e teyei eivek xeitueing dekakom am bong e na wou Sisa.”
ACT 25:22 Woyom Agripa neil wou Festus, “A venaxow ambei ngo tambiy tine xe qayeeng.” Festus neil elox bei, “Yanyeing tyek wa ngo e xe qayeeng.”
ACT 25:23 Om yanyeing eno Agripa me Benaisi lam is vunekeing nimza me la eivek xomek lalei wei qekueing ama yo is xel wei wo lukanzek en vevekyeiw o me tambiy wei mi la tax en xel moux wei beyeeng ngandoung on o. De Festus neil om xel qou Paulus me lam.
ACT 25:24 Woyom Festus neil, “King Agripa, me eti yeiw dalus wei toundei is xey ne, xam ghe wei tambiy tine! Xel xomaxoneing sapa wei Yuda eno xel taxe la nikanzek wou ay eivek Yerusalem me eivek Sisalia, xel taxe bei a nyeis e mey enok moxo mendei mapieing enden.
ACT 25:25 Ekom a xei bei moxo se wo sewokeing ti teyei bei e mey, om e maxow wong e xe qayeeng bei king Sisa e ngo e xe qayeeng, Om a wou naleing bei a bong e na Rom.
ACT 25:26 Ekom a se woulek e xe sewokeing ti bei a byex qayeeng vati na wou e xe teiv. Nambei nyon a qou e me na lam wou xam dalus, me na lam wou wang, king Agripa, en kandek xey a ngo e xe qayeeng me a byex lul valu eivek qapiya.
ACT 25:27 En a wou naleind bei inye se nimza bei a bong xel xeitueing ti na Rom wangwei a se byex sewokeing wei e wong eno eivek qapiya enak is.”
ACT 26:1 Woyom Agripa neil wou Paulus, “a lenghek lek wang bei wa baluk me na neil wamaxow xe qayeeng.” Om Paulus pepeeng angya mema de neil e xe qayeeng:
ACT 26:2 “King Agripa, a wou naleing ambei nye, inye nimza bei a bale wou wa mamghalus gweimbeeng me baluk dom wa ni nenyam wou qayeeng beimambei wei xel Yudayeiw byex lek a ne.”
ACT 26:3 Wang woulek kwa dalus wei Yudayeiw eno woy me vati wei xel mi vuklek ama yo. Nambei nyon ambei wa mendei kanzek dom na ni nenyam wou a xe qayeeng dalus.
ACT 26:4 “Xel Yudayeiw dalus on woulek a woy gyeik a yakayang, nanghei myaxeeng wei a mindei eivek a maxow xe tembuing ne, me na mindei eivek Yerusalem is.
ACT 26:5 Xel woulek a woy en xel yeimend wou ay takwei qenang nei, om wangwei xel laleind devind nei, ond xel venaxow teyei bei neil a xe kwa wou wang. Inyon betiwou petieing nikanzek wei xa xe lalo yo, a mindei nambei xel Parisi.
ACT 26:6 En nambei a mi axe me na toung mang wou vati wei Anutu neil qayeeng zonghek is xa mamiyeiw om a nale lek qayeeng gweimbeeng ne.
ACT 26:7 Tine inye qayeeng zonghek wei xa xe xel veleivlei xoumeeng yuw wei mi toung mend wou bei gyei neing en vati wei xel mi wong lalo wou Anutu bendiyeing aluw boukeing o. Woyom King, en qes tine Yudayeiw byex qayeeng lek ay.
ACT 26:8 Nambei nya xam valu ghe wou kwamim bei Anutu tyek se piyexe xel meyeing qandi lek?
ACT 26:9 “Ay is ambei nyon a wou naleing bei bong lul ngenong en na bo nol wou Yesu wei Nasaret o lei.
ACT 26:10 De inyon vati wei a mi wong anghei Yerusalem o. A qou leing ngandoung wou xel lumuki leitata bei na toung xel vambuing ngenong eivek xeitueing, ay is ambei nyon a neimbei xel amey.
ACT 26:11 Teyei lek bouk ngenong a mi la eivek xomek qekueing ama wei xel Yudayeiw o me na la nge bei bo myaveweeng wou xel me na tendu xel bei xel baluk yak lek Yesu. A mi wong me na xei en ambei xel a neil qayeeng nilul lek Tambiy Ngandoung. A laleing mi wo myavanei wou xel, om a mi la dingta me na ximexe xel bei bo myaveweeng wou xel.
ACT 26:12 “Bouk ti a qou qayeeng me lei wei ngandoung o wou xel lumuki leitata bei nana Damaskus om xel wong a la.
ACT 26:13 Woyom king, lek ambei bendiyeing wei seivma evlek eno a di tupwou sakwaing, a xei xeiyaing ti lam anghei tyoung gheyapu nei, xeiyaing ngandoung ghanaw sayeiv, eno siing vivekwou ay me a xe xel wei lam is ay yo.
ACT 26:14 Xa dalus a teila lek tembuing, de a ngo vya ti neil wou ay eivek Yuda vyend, ‘Sol, Sol, wang di wo nimaying wou ay en va? Wang byex vaxam lek lul wei manewou yo, me ghe wong vanei wou xow.’
ACT 26:15 “Woyom a teling, ‘Wang eti, Tambiy Ngandoung?’ “Tambiy Ngandoung neil eloum bei, ‘A Yesu, wei wang di wo nimaying wou yo.
ACT 26:16 Gweimbeeng qandi lek me nale ghey. A talex xow wou wang me na beyal wang ambei a xe xukxe me tyek wa neil lulul vati wei wang wei woy en ay yo teyei, me vati wei tyek a talex wou wang yus o.
ACT 26:17 Tyek a zeim wang veil wamaxow xe xomaxoneing me xel amba memend en xel se bo nol wou wang. Dom na bong wang na wou xel
ACT 26:18 en wa tax xel mend gyeina me pekwi xel veil mapetok de noum wou xeiyaing, me xel noum veil Sandang nikanzek de noum wou Anutu, om Anutu teyeimbei semaleeng xel xe sewokeing veil de xel teyeimbei mendei is xel wei wo vambuing nangya xel xe wongeingis o.’
ACT 26:19 “Woyom, king Agripa, a se pyalek lul tiwei a mang pekwi me na xei nanghei tyoung gheyapu yo.
ACT 26:20 Ti myaxeeng eno a neil xoulek wou xel wei toundei eivek Damaskus o, woyom a la wou xel wei Yerusalem me eivek Yuda dalus, me na la wou xel amba is, a neil qayeeng wei xel pekwi me noum wou Anutu me xam xe kwa yon e talex bei xam ghe pekwi xow woy.
ACT 26:21 Qes tiyon om Yudayeiw zeimaxoun ay eivek tete lalei wei xomek vambuing me xel embei nyeis a mey.
ACT 26:22 Ekom Anutu mi vind ay taxombouk me elam tyip gweimbeeng ne, om a nale inye wou wa mamghalus de na neil qayeeng wou xel wei leind maeing me xel wei leind tata yo is. A se neil qayeeng nge qe vati wei poropetyeiw me Mose neil eno tyek na tyip.
ACT 26:23 Inyon Kilisi tyek na qou myavanei me tyek qandi natax veil meyeing, de tyek na neil qayeeng wei xeiyaing eno teyei wou e maxow xe xomaxoneing me na neil wou xel amba is.”
ACT 26:24 Lek qes tine Festus taxe niseikeing me wo nol wou Paulus xe qayeeng. Moxo taxe bei, “Paulus wa lum on wo bandol o. Wang qou lupeyei ngenong me wa lumpeyei yon wong wang wo bandol.”
ACT 26:25 Ekom Paulus neil elox, “Lei ngandoung Festus, a se wo bandol. Vati wei a neil on zonghek me qes nimza.
ACT 26:26 King woulek lul dalus tine, om a teyei bei baluk wou e de a se xaleeng en e. En a woulek bombek bei lulul beimambei ne lam yeip yaingateiv.
ACT 26:27 King Agripa, wang wongis qayeeng wei xel poropetyeiw o? A woulek woy, bei wang wongis.”
ACT 26:28 Woyom Agripa neil wou Paulus, “Wang wou naleim bei inyon eivek seivma sepi kane eno tyek wang bong a bo tambiy wei na mi betiwou Kilisi yo?”
ACT 26:29 Paulus neil elox bei, “Seivma sepika o dingta, a mi zeimemang wou Anutu bei se wamaxow qe eti yeiw dalus wei di ngo ay gweimbeeng ne tyek xam xouing ghe ghok ay. Ekom ambei xel se tup xam angya sen me xam a toumendei eivek xeitueing.”
ACT 26:30 Woyom king qandi lek, is e xe lei ngandoung wei seyap o me Benaisi me eti yeiw wei toundei is xel o.
ACT 26:31 Xel la veil xomek lalei tiyon, me luk wouma, xel neil, “Tambiy tine se wong lulti wo nilul bei e mey o mendei eivek xeitueing.”
ACT 26:32 Agripa neil wou Festus, “Moux tine teyei bei na nivax, wangwei e maxow se neil wou Sisa bei e ngo e xe qayeeng nei.”
ACT 27:1 Nambei nyon xel tup qayeeng lekti bei xa na eivek sip me nana Itali. De xel toung Paulus me xel wei xeitueing eno valu eivek tambiy ti e lei Julias eno mema wei toundei nambei beyeiv eivek vevekyeiw qendu ti wei king lei ngandoung wei Rom o.
ACT 27:2 Xa la eivek sip wei beyeeng nayak Adlamitium. Sip tine tyek na tupwou mamileeng wei beyeeng nayak nayak wei provins Esia yo, om xa la eivek mamileeng me na la. Alistakas wei beyeeng Tesalonika nanghei tembuing danghei wei Masedonia eno la is xa.
ACT 27:3 De yanyeing eno xa la tei Saidon, me Julias lalei wo nimza wou Paulus, om wong Paulus la wou e xe xel gweleeng yeiw bei kandek xel bo vineing valu wou e.
ACT 27:4 Nanghei inyon eno xa la eivek sip no me na ghanaw tembuing nayak Saiprus eivek mamileeng, en laweeng ngandoung vei sip is xa.
ACT 27:5 Ka xa la eivek sip me na sek mamileeng me na la paviy Silisia me Pampilia eno xa teila nanghei beyeeng Maila eivek Lisia.
ACT 27:6 Nanghei inyon eno beyeiv wei xel vevek eno yei sip ti lam anghei Aleksandlia en embei na Itali om toung xa lek sip tiyon.
ACT 27:7 Xa mi la kaka teyei lek bouk valu en laweeng nikanzek vei sip is xa om wong pok wou xa en ingwei xa bei na Nidus o. Laweeng se wong xa la lox xa xe sakwaing, om xa se teyei bei na no, qe xa pekwi me na la tembuing nayak Krit eivek mamileeng paviy Salmone.
ACT 27:8 Xa wo pok me betiwou mamileeng vi me na la tyip wou beyeeng ti lei Beyeeng Nenyawes Nimza wei toundei paviy beyeeng nayak Lasea.
ACT 27:9 Xa la lek mamileeng bouk valu betiy lak veil, me gweimbeeng eno se bouk nimza wei laeing o, en bouk ngandoung wei Yudayeiw o, bouk wei xel mi vambu xow en yaing o, bouk tine la veil. Om Paulus peti xel bei,
ACT 27:10 “Xa me, a xei bei xe xe laeing eno tyek xey a qou nilul ayang eivek sip me xe xe qoupek valu tyek nati, me xemaxow is ambei nyon.”
ACT 27:11 Ekom beyeiv wei xel vevek o se ngo vati wei Paulus neil o, qe betiwou tambiy wei mi qou sip o me tambiy wei e xe sip on vyend.
ACT 27:12 Beyeeng tine se nimza bei sip na bale me ghupek eivek en laweeng ngandoung on, om xel moux ngenong on neil embei xel me di na eivek sip me na, xel embei betiwou mamileeng vi wei tembuing nayak Krit eivek mamileeng me na beyeeng nayak Piniks. Myakenu wei toundei nanghei nyon eno wo mya tambak la veweeng axo, me veweeng aning is. Xel embei mendei nanghei nyon en laweeng ngandoung tine tyip.
ACT 27:13 Gyeik laweeng axonei tyip kaka, xel wou kwend en vati wei xel laleind vind o. Om xel puw anka dom xel la paviy mamileeng vi wei Krit o.
ACT 27:14 Ekom se wo lululek en laweeng ti xel mi taxe bei valeivek eno lam anghei tembuing nayak Krit.
ACT 27:15 Laweeng ngandoung on vei sip nikanzek om sip se teyei bei na, om xel wong laweeng valeivek on vei sip di la.
ACT 27:16 Ka xa la daing me na la tembuing nayak on valu pu wei paseisexe laweeng, wei xel taxe bei Kauda. Xa wo pok ngandoung lek puweing bot nayak lam paviy sip.
ACT 27:17 Woyom xel moux on puw bot leklam lek sip. Dekakom xel tup sel angya yis eivek xeinghembi bei e zeimaxoun e bo nikanzek. Xel yaleeng bei tyek xel na bale lek qakous wei mamileeng masenghoing o paviy Afrika, om xel tup sel angya yis dom wong e teila lek mamileeng dom laweeng di vei sip di la kaka.
ACT 27:18 Valeivek tyip me mamileeng di nex xa lox me loum, omva yanyeing eno xel wei mi wo xuk eivek sip on qou qoupek on me nex ela eivek mamileeng.
ACT 27:19 Lek bouk yal, eno xel nex sel me yis me qasok la veil sip angya memend.
ACT 27:20 Bouk ngenong la veil eno xa se xei seiv o betum ti lam nale en valeivek tine di wo nol wo xa, om xa wou kwami bei tyek xa dalus amey.
ACT 27:21 Bouk tambak eno moux beimambei ne se ya bambound ti, om Paulus nale wou xel mend me neil: “Xam moux, wangwei xam a ngo a xe qayeeng ne me xe se na veil Krit, yon tyek xey se teyei bei balwou nimaying tine me lul sapa ne tyek se nati.
ACT 27:22 Ekom gweimbeeng ne a neil wou xam bei, xam laleimim se bo nimaying en tyek xam ti seng teyei bei mey, qe sip venaxow tyek lelolexe.
ACT 27:23 En vezeiveeng boukeing eno a tiwei Anutu xe, me a mi wong lalo wou eno wong e xe angela ti lam nale paviy a byek
ACT 27:24 de neil, ‘Paulus, wa seng gwaleeng. Tyek wang mi bale zam wou Sisa manghalus. En, Anutu ngo wa xe zeimeing mema is me wong mapieing wou xel wei la is wang lek sip o.’
ACT 27:25 Angela neil wou ay, om xam moux on xam seng gwaleeng qe xam bale nikanzek, en a wongis Anutu bei tyek bong neing a tyip nambei kawei neil wou ay yo.
ACT 27:26 Nambei nyon mamileeng emdi qalei sip me na deka xey a na pop lek tembuing nayak on ti eivek mamileeng.”
ACT 27:27 Lek boukeing xoumeeng vey eno laweeng vei xa la lek mamileeng ngandoung wei Mediterenian on me na dula mamileeng wei Adriatik o, de boukeing masenghoing eno xel wei mi yeiteyei sip on axe bei sip embim na paviy mamileeng vi ti.
ACT 27:28 Xel qou mita me yei mamileeng on teyei lek 120 manghembi. Se denlek en xel lox me la qou mita no me yei bei inyon 90 manghembi.
ACT 27:29 Xa xaleeng bei tyek sip na tu xow lek qakous, om xel qou anka vey nanghei ingwei sip nelu nei me wong e lepla dom mi zeimemend bei e boyaing daing.
ACT 27:30 Xel wei mi yeiteyei sip on yimexe sakwaing wei xel embei na veil sip o, om xel tul yis veil bot on teila dom tyoing lek bei xel embei toung anka valu lek sip nelu.
ACT 27:31 Woyom Paulus neil wou beyeiv me xel vevekyeiw on, “Wangwei xel moux tine se toumendei lek sip, on tyek xam xouing a mey ama.”
ACT 27:32 Om xel vevekyeiw on qateiv yis wei mi zeimaxoun bot on veil dom e teila me mamileeng qalei me la.
ACT 27:33 Paviy e bim boyaing om Paulus wong qayeeng wou xel dalus bei xel gya yaeing. Paulus neil, “Xam laleimim on se dei wo nimza, me xam seng wa lulti wou baboumim. En xam ghe mindei bandaing teyei lek bouk xoumeeng vey ne, dom xam seng wa lulti.
ACT 27:34 Gweimbeeng a luk nikanzek wou xam bei xam a qou yaeing valu me ghe gwa. En e devind xam ghe bo nimkanzek. Xam lumim velus ti lek xam ti lumim eno se teyei bei puw me nati veil.”
ACT 27:35 Ka moxo neil tine, moxo qou belet valu me wong dange la wou Anutu eivek xel dalus mendghalus. Woyom moxo dembu dom ya.
ACT 27:36 Xel dalus on laleind wo nimza no me xel venaxow ya xend yaeing valu.
ACT 27:37 Xa dalus tiwei xa toundei lek sip ne eno teyei lek 276.
ACT 27:38 Ka xel ya enden xel, woyom xel nex qoupek wit on la eivek mamileeng bei sip se bo nimaying.
ACT 27:39 De woyaing, xel se woulek tembuing, qe xel yei luzeeng wei mamileeng vi yo ti, inyon xel embei bong sip na bale ghei tiyon wangwei xel teyei nei.
ACT 27:40 Xel qateiv yis wei anka dalus on teila eivek mamileeng. Me xel tul yis wei xel tup lek qasok wei xel mi ngangi sip angya yo. Woyom xel puw sel lek la bei laweeng e davei dom sip ena lek luzeeng.
ACT 27:41 Ekom sip la pop lek luzeeng wei mamileeng on ti. Sip nelu yon viing lek inyon om se la, me mamileeng la di leislek sip on demi me wo dembu dembu.
ACT 27:42 Xel vevekyeiw tup qayeeng lekti bei nyeis xel xeitueing on dalus amey, enok xel deivek mamileeng me na yasewis dom na pek me na.
ACT 27:43 Ekom beyeiv wei 100 vevekyeiw embei devind Paulus en e toumendei mapieing, om nale zeyi xel xe woueing nalei yon. Moxo neil wou eti yeiw wei mi yeiplek mamileeng bei xel deivek mamileeng me na yasewis.
ACT 27:44 De xel valu na zeim lek pelang wei sip myasepu sepu wei dembu yon me gyeip lek me na. Eivek sakwaing wei xa xeip lek pelang eno xa dalus a la nimza lek tembuing. De xa ti se mey.
ACT 28:1 Xa lam ewo nimza lek mamileeng nenyawes, de xa woulek bei tembuing nayak ne xel mi taxe bei Malta.
ACT 28:2 Xel wei tembuing nayak on talex xel xe laleind vineing wou xa. Om xel vev nenyex wou xa de qou xa dalus me na la bei xa na mendei wou nenyex en nambei inye luing om wo nityuweing.
ACT 28:3 Paulus qeku nenyex qendu ti, me li lek nenyex on mapu, nenyex laxwou myeiy nilul ti om lam qateiv newou lek e mema me milek.
ACT 28:4 Xel xomaxoneing wei beyeeng on yei myeiy milek Paulus mema, om xel neil wouma bei, “Tambiy tine beind inye moux wei mi leis xel o ti, om moxo pek me lam veil mamileeng, om anutu wei mi wong myaveweeng lox eno embei e se mendei mapieing.”
ACT 28:5 Ekom Paulus bimexe mema is myeiy teila eivek nenyex, de moxo se axe myavanei ti.
ACT 28:6 Xel xomaxoneing on di axe bei tyek e mema buklek o detei lutika me na mey, ekom xel axe enden de xel se yei lulti wo nol wou e, om xel pelipek laleind dom neil embei moxo yon anutu ti.
ACT 28:7 Inyon tembuing ti dei yeip paviy beyeeng tiyon, tambiy ti lei Publias xe tembuing on me e yon gyovaxa wei tembuing nayak on. Moxo qou xa me la eivek beeng me mi yeiteyei xa wo nimzayang teyei lek bouk yal.
ACT 28:8 Moxo ma vanei ti wong om di yeip lek zek, en gying wong me e di beipek gyand. Paulus la lalei en embei na gyei e, loxyus en ingwei e zeimema, moxo li mema lek e me wong e wo nimza.
ACT 28:9 Ka lul tine belup, xel dalus wei tembuing nayak on, wei vanei wong xel eno lam wou e me moxo wong xel dalus wo nimzalek.
ACT 28:10 Xel wo xeindlala en xa me wo nimza wou xa is ambei nyon, de gyeik ingwei xa bei na veil xel me nana, eno xel wong lulul wei ma veil xa eno wou xa.
ACT 28:11 Xa mindei eivek tembuing nayak on teyei lek dentouk qes yal, woyom xa la lek sip wei toungale eivek tembuing nayak on gyeik bouk wei laweeng ngandoung on. Inyon Aleksandlia xe sip. Lek sip nelu xel toung tenu wei anutu Sus neu papyeng o, anutu Kasto me Poluks.
ACT 28:12 Xa la tyip beyeeng Silakyus, me na dei inyon teyei lek bouk yal.
ACT 28:13 Me nanghei inyon eno xa qou sip me na la tyip Regiam. De yanyeing eno laweeng wei xonei yo lam tyip, de lek bouk yal eno xa la tyip Puteoli.
ACT 28:14 Nanghei inyon xa xei limiyeiw valu de xel qou xa me xa la dei sounda qes ti is xel. Dekakom xa la Rom.
ACT 28:15 Xa limiyeiw nanghei inyon eno ngo bei xa di lam, om xel lam anghei inyon me la Beyeeng Vateivek wei Apias, me Xomek Yal wei Vateivek eno is. Paulus yei xel moux tine, om wong dange wou Anutu, me lalei qou nikanzek.
ACT 28:16 Ka xa la tyip Rom, seyap lenghek lek Paulus bei e venaxow na mendei eivek xomek ti, me xel vevekyeiw mi yei e teyei.
ACT 28:17 Ka bouk yal la veil moxo taxe xel gyovaxa dalus wei Yudayeiw wei toundei nanghei Rom. Gyeik xel la qekuma eno Paulus neil wou xel: “Xam lingyeiw, a se wong lulti lek xe xe xel xomaxoneing ne o lek xe bundyeiw xe kwa, qe xel zeimaxoun ay eivek Yerusalem me toung a la eivek Rom memend.
ACT 28:18 Xel Rom ngo a xe qayeeng ekom xel se yei sewokeing ti eivek ay bei xel nyeis a mey. Om xel embei tul a na bandaing.
ACT 28:19 Ekom Yudayeiw pesek, Om a ning sakwaing nge ma dom tyek Sisa na ngo a xe qayeeng, inye se nambei ambei bo qayeeng en a maxow xe xel xomaxoneing ne.
ACT 28:20 En qes tine a teling bei ghei wang me baluk is wang. En nambei a wongis me na mi axe lul tiwei xey Israel dalus na mi toung mendghalus wou yo. Qes tine om xel tup ay angya sen.”
ACT 28:21 Xel neil eloum, “Xa se qou qapiya ti wou Yudayeiw en wang, me limyeiw ti se lam anghei inyon me neil qayeeng ti wou xa en wang.
ACT 28:22 Ekom xa bei ngo qayeeng wou wa venaxow en wa xe woueing nalei, en xa woulek bei xomaxoneing lek tembuing sapa di byex qayeeng lek qendu tine.”
ACT 28:23 Xel beyal bouk ti dekalekom xel la dei is Paulus, de xel ngenong lam wou Paulus nanghei beyeeng wei toundei lek o. Satiboukeing me ela soukeing eno moxo neil qayeeng qes me neilteyei wou xel en tete lalei wei Anutu yo me neil nikanzek wou xel en Yesu eivek Petieing wei Mose me xel poropetyeiw o.
ACT 28:24 Xel valu qou qayeeng wei e neil o, ekom xel valu eno se wongis.
ACT 28:25 Xel pyalek ama me xel embei na veil Paulus gyeik e neil e xe qayeeng tiwei yus o: “Laweeng Vambuing luk zonghek wou xam bumimyeiw gyeik e neil eivek poropet Yesaya mya yo:
ACT 28:26 “‘Wang na wou xel xomaxoneing tine me na neil wou xel, “Tyek xam a mi ngo qayeeng lumama ekom tyek xam se ngowou qes, tyek xam a mi gwei lumama ekom tyek xam seng gweiwou lulti.”
ACT 28:27 En xel xomaxoneing tine laleind wo nikanzek me xel nenyend wo qatu om xel se ngo wou qayeeng, me xel mend tuzeyi. Enok xel gyei nangya mendghalus, me na ngo eivek nenyend, me boulek eivek laleind de pekwi xow, me a bong xel bo nimzalek.’
ACT 28:28 “Nambei nyon ambei xam ghe boulek bei Anutu vind xe veil meyeing eno la wou xel amba is, me tyek xel a ngo!”
ACT 28:30 Lek vakovek qes yuw dalus eno Paulus mi dei eivek xomek wei e maxow mi xouv wou xomek ma yo. Me mi wo xeilala bei na qou eti yeiw wei lam en embei nam gyei e yo.
ACT 28:31 Moxo se mi yaleeng en neileing Anutu xe tete lalei teyei me xelti se mi nale zeyi e, qe mi teyoxe xel en Tambiy Ngandoung Yesu Kilisi.
REV 1:1 Qayeeng xupekeing wei Yesu Kilisi wong e yeip yaing. Wei Anutu wong wou e bei e talex wou e xe xel xukxe en vati wei embim nam mendei yanyateiv o. E wong e xe angela ti lam wong qayeeng ne wou a Yoan, e xe xukxe,
REV 1:2 wei neil lulul sapa wei Yoan yei yo teyei, inye xoulek wei Anutu yo me pavulek en Yesu Kilisi yo.
REV 1:3 Anutu e bong mata wou tiwei mi pyaw qayeeng poropet ne yo, me e bong mata wou xel wei mi ngo qayeeng ne me betiwou vatiyeiw wei yeip eivek qayeeng ne yo, en bouk lam paviy.
REV 1:4 A Yoan, A byex qayeeng ne wou kongrikesin lim yuw wei provins Esia yo: Anutu xe lalei xeiles is lalei vevopeing e nak wou xam, inye lam wou e wei mindei gweimbeeng ne me e wei mindei takwei me e wei tyek mendi nam o, me lalei xeiles is lalei vevopeing lam wou laweeng lim yuw wei mi nale wou e xe siaking o,
REV 1:5 Yesu Kilisi tiwei mi neil Anutu xe qayeeng dalus la wo bombek. E tambiy tiwei qandi lek veil meyeing myaxeeng o, me wo gyovaxa en kingyeiyeiw wei tembuing o. Tiwei lalei vind xey me wong xey a lam myayaing veil sewokeing nangya e gyand o,
REV 1:6 me wong xey a teyei lek tete lalei me lumukiyeiw bei na bong xuk wei e xe Anutu me Ma yo, xeiyaing ngandoung me nikanzek wei yeingteyei lulul o ena wou e me na mi mendei luta luta! Zonghek.
REV 1:7 Wei, e di lam is laxap, me xomaxoneing sapa tyek gyei e lek mendghalus, me xel wei beum e en yiy eno tyek gyei is, me xel veleivlei dalus wei tembuing eno tyek bong talot en e! Om lul tine tyek bo neing lek! Zonghek.
REV 1:8 Tambiy Ngandoung Anutu neil, “A ne Tax me a Loxyus, wei a toundei ne, me a mindei takwei, me a wei tyek mendi nam o, Anutu Nikanzekta.”
REV 1:9 Ay, Yoan, xam limim me xe xouing a toundei is ama eivek myavanei me tete lalei me xe xouing a mi axe me nale nikanzek eivek myavanei wei xe xe yo eivek Yesu, me a deilek tembuing danghei tiwei di yeip eivek mamileeng wei Patmos o en xoulek wei Anutu yo me pavulek en Yesu yo.
REV 1:10 Lek Tambiy Ngandoung xe bouk eno a toundei eivek Laweeng Vambuing, me na ngo loum deming eno vya ngandoung ti nambei vukxax ti,
REV 1:11 wei neil embei: “Byex lek qapiya ti en vati wei wang wei yo me wong ela wou kongrikesin lim yuw. Ena wou Epeses, Smena, Pegamum, me Taiataira, Sadis, Piladelpia me Laodisia.”
REV 1:12 A pekwi mang bei na ghe vya wei di luk wou ay yo. Deka a pekwi mang eno a xei lam ghol vaxa lim yuw,
REV 1:13 me eivek xel lam vaxa yon senghoing eno tambiy ti nambei xomaxoneing neu moux ti, vunek en teimb ding wei la tei wou e vaxa me vex let ghol wei vivekwou e bambou kanzek.
REV 1:14 E lu me luvelus eno wo pus nambei sipsip nivlus, me wo teleing nambei laxap, me e ma nei xok nenyex wei tum magyand o.
REV 1:15 E vaxa nei nambei bras tumeing eivek nenyex ngandoung o me e vya ne nambei memiing nindenduing wei mi la nikanzek o.
REV 1:16 Eivek e mema payeiv e zeim betum lim yuw, me ngeyeing vevek wei manewou yuw valuvalu eno lam myayaing veil e mya. E ma ne nambei sayeiv wei mi siing ngandoung me la danghei danghei nei.
REV 1:17 Ka a xei e, a teila lek e vaxa de wambeik nge a mey. Woyom e liw mema payeiv lek a me neil, “Wa se gwaleeng. A ne Tax me a Loxyus.
REV 1:18 A ne a mindei mapieing o, a mey takwei nei. Ekom ngo, a toundei mapieing luta luta ne! Me a zeim xel ki wei meyeing me beyeeng wei meyeing o.
REV 1:19 “Byex qayeeng en vati wei wang wei ne, vati wei toundei gweimbeeng ne, me vati wei tyek nam yus o.
REV 1:20 Lul xupekeing wei betum lim yuw wei wang wei eivek a memang payeiv o me lam vaxa ghol lim yuw eno qes ambei nye: Betum lim yuw eno inye angelayeiw wei kongrikesin lim yuw o, me lam vaxa lim yuw eno inye kongrikesin lim yuw.”
REV 2:1 Woyom tambiy tiyon neil no, “Wa byex qayeeng ne na wou angela wei kongrikesin wei toundei eivek Epeses o. Inye qayeeng beimambei ne eno lam wou e wei mi zeim betum lim yuw eivek mema payeiv o me mi la senghoing eivek lam ghol vaxa lim yuw on.
REV 2:2 A woulek kwa dalus wei wang on woy, me wa xe pok de kwa wei wang mi nale nikanzek eivek nimaying o. Me a xei bei wa laleim se vind xel moux wei nilul on, de wang axe xel wei neil embei xel sinale ekom ma mouyo, wang wei bei xel on tyonyeingana.
REV 2:3 Wang mi nale nikanzek eivek nimaying me ghe qalei maying ngandoung on en a leing, de wa seng mi wo nimbayaing en pok ne.
REV 2:4 Ekom a qayeeng ti wou wang. Wang saing wa xe kwa wei lalei vineing wei myaxeeng eno veil.
REV 2:5 Inyei nambei wang tei gheyapu me ghe lam axone, wang bounaleim en kwa nimza wei wang mi wong myaxeeng o ekom ghe saing veil o! Wa pekwi xow me ghe bong xuk wei wang mi wong atax o. Wangwei wa se pekwi xow nei ond tyek a nak wou wang me na zeim wa nim lam vaxa veil e nimbeeng.
REV 2:6 Ekom wa xe kwa nimza eno di yeip is wang. Wa laleim wo nol en xuk nilul wei Nikolasyeiw o, ay is ambei nyon a laleing se vind kwa wei xel on.
REV 2:7 Woyom e ti nenyalis toundei lek e, yond e ngo embo nimza en vati wei Laweeng Vambuing di neil wou xel kongrikesin o. E ti bo vevek ghanaw nei on tyek a zewexe lek e bei ena gya xaxaneing wei mapieing o, wei toundei eivek beyeeng nimza wei Anutu yo.”
REV 2:8 Woyom tambiy tiyon neil no, “Wa byex qayeeng tine na wou angela wei kongrikesin wei toundei eivek Smena yo. Inye qayeeng beimambei wei tambiy wei Myaxeeng me Yusayang o, wei mey de qandi lek mapieing no yo.
REV 2:9 A xei wa xe myavanei wei wang qou yo me wa xe deing wei lulul ma veil wang o, ekom wang wo lulul ana! A xei xel wei mi lukyak me neil embei nyei xel Yudayeiw ekom xel on se Yuda qe xel on xomek qekueing ama wei Sandang o.
REV 2:10 Wa seng gwaleeng en myavanei vati wei wa bim a qou yon. A neil wou wang bei, tambiy mapetok tyek na toung xam on valu eivek xeitueing bei daxe xam, me tyek xam qalei myavanei me nimaying teyei lek bouk xoumeeng. Ekom wa mi zeimaxoun wa xe wongeingis me ena tip lek ingwei wa mey yo, en tyek a bong qelumking wei mapieing nambei xouveing eno wou wang.
REV 2:11 Woyom tambiy tiwei nenyalis toundei lek e yo, wong e ngo vati wei Laweeng Vambuing di neil wou xel kongrikesin o. Tambiy tiwei xoklek nimaying eno tyek meyeing nge wei yuw eno se semaleeng e, ma mouyo.”
REV 2:12 Woyom tambiy tiyon neil no, “Wa byex qayeeng tine na wou angela wei kongrikesin wei toundei eivek beyeeng Pegamum o. Inye qayeeng beimambei ne lam wou tambiy wei mi zeim ngeyeing vevek wei manewou yuw valuvalu xouing o.
REV 2:13 A xei mang wou ingwei wang mindei, nanghei ingwei Sandang xe sia nei. Ekom neing bei wang ghei toundei me ghe di zeimaxoun a leing wo nikanzek. Wa seng saing wongeingis wei wang mi wongis ay yo veil me ela tip lek bouk wei Antipas o, inyei tambiy wei mi neil a xe qayeeng la teyei lek o, eno xel leis e mey eivek xam senghoing nanghei ingwei Sandang mindei nei.
REV 2:14 Ekom a qayeeng valu wou wang, wa xe xomaxoneing valu nanghei di zeimaxoun qayeeng teyoxeing wei Balam o, wei teyoxe wou Balak bei e zeim Israelyeiw laleind lek en xel bo sewokeing nangya ingwei xel ya yaeing wei xel wong ambei da wou anutu tyonyeing o, me ingwei xel la eivek kwa nilul wei kwapesiv o.
REV 2:15 Woyom nambei inyon eno wa xe xel valu eno di zeimaxoun teyoxeing wei Nikolasyeiw o.
REV 2:16 Nambei inyon xam pekwi xow! Enok, a nak daing wou xam me na bo vevek is xel angya ngeyeing vevek wei toundei eivek a myang o.
REV 2:17 Woyom e tiwei nenyalis toundei lek e yo, wong e ngo vati wei Laweeng Vambuing di neil wou xel kongrikesin o. Tambiy tiwei xoklek nimaying o, tyek a bong mana valu wei mindei xupekeing eno wou e. Me tyek a bong qakous teleing ti is lei vako tiwei xel byex lek eno wou e, wei xelti se woulek inyon qe e wei qou yo venaxow.”
REV 2:18 Woyom tambiy tiyon neil no, “Wa byex qayeeng tine na wou angela wei kongrikesin wei toundei eivek Taiataira yo. Inyei qayeeng beimambei wei Anutu Neu moux o, tambiy wei ma xok ambei nenyex tumeing magyand me tambiy wei vaxa xok ambei bras wei xel lii e wo belin o.
REV 2:19 A woulek wa xe xuk woy, me wa xe lalei vineing me wa xe wongeingis, me wa xe xuk vineing me ingwei wang mi nale nikanzek eivek nimaying o, me ingwei gweimbeeng ne wang di wong e ghanaw ingwei wang wong atax o.
REV 2:20 Ekom a qayeeng valu wou wang. Wang mi lewexe lek vex tiwei Jesebel on, wei mi taxe xow bei e poropet vex ti. Me mi pakei a xe xukxeyeiw la eivek kwa nilul wei xel mi wong kwapesiv o nangya e xe teyoxeing, me ingwei xel mi ya yaeing wei xel wong ambei da wou tenu bandaing eno nangya e xe teyoxeing.
REV 2:21 A wong bouk wou e bei e pekwi xow, ekom embei se pekwi xow me na toung demi wou e xe kwapesiv on.
REV 2:22 Om tyek a bo vanei ngandoung wou vex on me na ni e lek zek wei myavanei yo, me xel wei mi wo kwapesiv is vex on, ek wangwei xel se pekwi xow veil e xe sakwaing nilul nei yon tyek a bong xel a qou myavanei ngandoung is ambei nyon.
REV 2:23 Tyek a nyeis vex on neuyeiw na mey. Woyom kongrikesin dalus tyek boulek bei a ne moux wei a mi xeila xel laleind me xel lundpeyei, me tyek am bo xouveing wou xam titi teyei lek xam xe kwa wei xam ghe mi wong on.
REV 2:24 Ekom gweimbeeng a neil wou xam valu wei nanghei toundei eivek Taiataira yon, me ena wou xam wei seng mi zeimaxoun vex on xe teyoxeing me xam seng qou lupeyei wou kwa wei xel taxe bei lul xupekeing wei manghembi wei Sandang o. (Me tyek a se toung nimaying nge nak lek xam).
REV 2:25 Qe xam mendi zeimaxoun kwa nimza vati wei xam xe yon bo nikanzek deka a nak le.
REV 2:26 Eti yeiw wei mi xoklek nimaying o me betiwou a laleing me e na tyip wou bouk wei lulul la tip lek o, tyek a bong nikanzek wei lei ngandoung wei e bo lukanzek en xomaxoneing tembuing tambak eno wou e.
REV 2:27 ‘Moxo tyek gyei xel teyei is patongeeng wei aen o, de tyek dembu xel na bo myapapu nambei dengmuing.’ Nambei kawei a qou nikanzek wei lei ngandoung wou mang o.
REV 2:28 Me tyek am bong betum wei satiboukeing eno wou e is ambei inyon.
REV 2:29 Om tambiy wei nenyalis toundei lek e yo, wong e ngo ewo nimza en vati wei Laweeng Vambuing di neil wou xel kongrikesin o.”
REV 3:1 Woyom tambiy tiyon neil no, “Wa byex qayeeng tine na wou angela wei kongrikesin wei toundei eivek beyeeng Sadis o. Inye qayeeng beimambei wei moux wei di zeim laweeng lim yuw wei Anutu yo me betum lim yuw. A woulek wa xe xuk neing. Wang wo leim en ingwei wang toundei mapieing o, ek ma, wang mey o.
REV 3:2 Wa qandi lek veil yeipeing! Me na byexaxoun lulul vati wei nanghei toundei yon wei embim a mey yo, en a se xei wa xe xuk neing ti la vup wou a xe Anutu manghalus.
REV 3:3 Wang bounaleim en vati wei wang ngo me ghe qou myaxeeng, wa zeimaxoun e bo nikanzek. Wa betiwou me pekwi xow. Ek wangwei wa se qandi lek veil yeipeing, on tyek a nak wou wang nambei panaxana ti, me tyek wa seng boulek bouk vati wei tyek a nak wou wang o.
REV 3:4 Ekom wa xe xel nuyuw ka eno toundei eivek Sadis wei xel se wo xel xe teimb wo nilaxes. Xel xe kwa yon nimza teyei lek ingwei xel vunek en teimb teleing me na vaxend is ay.
REV 3:5 Wangwei tambiy ti ghoklek nimaying, tyek bunek en teimb teleing nambei xel. On tyek a se teyeimbei davu e lei veil qapiya wei mapieing o, qe tyek a neil e lei teyei wou mang manghalus me e xe xel angela.
REV 3:6 Woyom tambiy tiwei nenyalis toundei lek e yo, wong e ngo vati wei Laweeng Vambuing di neil wou xel kongrikesin o.”
REV 3:7 Woyom tambiy tiyon neil no, “Wa byex qayeeng tine na wou angela wei toundei eivek kongrikesin wei Piladelpia yo. Inye qayeeng beimambei wei e wei vambuing o me zonghek o, wei mi zeim ki wei Dawit o. Vati wei e tax o, xelti se teyeimbei qepei qapomb noum zeyi. De vati wei e qepei qapomb zeyi eno xelti se teyeimbei tax.
REV 3:8 A woulek wa xe xuk woy. Wei, a tax qapomb ti wou wa mamghalus wei xelti se teyeimbei qepei qapomb zeyi. A woulek bei wa nimkanzek on nayaka, ekom wang mi zeimaxoun a xe qayeeng dom seng mi ax a leing vun.
REV 3:9 Tyek am bong xel wei xomek qekueing ama wei Sandang, wei xel mi neil embei xel Yudayeiw ekom xel ne se Yudayeiw, qe xel ne tyonyeingana. Tyek am bong xel nam me dev vaxend qatu wou wa vaxam me gyei lek mend bei a laleing vind wang.
REV 3:10 Nambei wang mi zeimaxoun a xe petieing de ghe mi axe myavanei enden, tyek a gheiteyei wang veil bouk wei axeing wei embei nam lek tembuing sapa nei bei daxe xel wei mindei lek tembuing o.
REV 3:11 Tyek a nak wou wang daing. Om wa Zeimaxoun vati wei wa xe yo, en kandek xelti se qou wa xe xouveing.
REV 3:12 E wei xoklek nimaying eno tyek a balax e nambei mundeeng wei xomek vambuing wei a xe Anutu yo. Tyek se teyeimbei e nox me na veil no. Tyek a byex a xe Anutu lei lek e me beyeeng ngandoung wei a xe Anutu yo lei lek e is Yerusalem vako, wei lam xone veil tyoung gheyapu wei a xe Anutu yo, me tyek a byex leing vako lek e is ambei inyon.
REV 3:13 E tiwei nenyalis toundei lek e yo, wong e ngo vati wei Laweeng Vambuing di neil wou xel kongrikesin o.”
REV 3:14 Woyom tambiy tiyon neil no, “Wa byex qayeeng tine na wou angela wei toundei eivek kongrikesin wei Laodisia yo. Qayeeng beimambei ne eno inyei lam wou tiwei Zonghek o, de mi wo Anutu xe xuk la wou eivek de mi tul xoulek taxombouk, de e qes wei Anutu mema xuk sapa yo.
REV 3:15 A woulek wa xe xuk woy, bei wa seng wo nityuweing o wa seng wo nivanei. A wou naleing bei wang bong ambei yuw on nge nityuweing o nivanei.
REV 3:16 Ekom ma a bim a pesuv wang nam veil myang, en wang noux nayaka, wa se nivanei me wa se nityuweing,
REV 3:17 wang neimbei, ‘A ne lulul ana, a mi qekuwou lulul ngenongakes om tyek a qou vati no me a se ma en lulul ti.’ Ekom wa seng woulek bei wang dei nilul ayang, teyeimbei xel a pyaw naleind en wang, me wang wo kanyo, me wa matekeing me wang toundei xeim dengeing.
REV 3:18 Om am bo kwa tine wou wang bei wang bou ghol wei a ne wei xel sei eivek nenyex me e wo belin ne yo, en kandek wang bo lulul ana. De wang bou Teimb teleing me na byex, en kandek wa sevun xeim dengeing, me wou denzi wei wa toung lek mamghalus o, en kandek wa mam e gyeina yo.
REV 3:19 Xel wei a laleing vind eno a luk nikanzek wou xel me na pepyawexe xel. Om wa laleim e mi qandi lek de wa pekwi xow.
REV 3:20 Ay inye! A toungale wou qapomb mya me na leis memang lek. Wangwei xelti e ngo a vyang me natax qapomb, tyek a nak lalei me na gha is e, de e gya is ay.
REV 3:21 Ena wou e wei mi xoklek nimaying o, tyek a zewexe lek e bei e mendei is ay lek a xe siaking, nambei kawei a xoklek nimaying me na dei is mang lek e xe siaking o.
REV 3:22 E tiwei nenyalis toundei lek e yo, wong e ngo vati wei Laweeng Vambuing di neil wou xel kongrikesin o.”
REV 4:1 Ka tine la veil, a xei qapomb ti tax me toungale eivek tyoung gheyapu wou a mang. Me vya wei a ngo natax o luk wou ay nambei vukxax eno neil, “Lam gheyapu ne, tyek a talex wou wang en vati wei embei nam yus en tine yo.”
REV 4:2 Lutika eno Laweeng Vambuing lam nale eivek ay, me a xei siaking ti toundei eivek tyoung gheyapu is xelti eno toundei lek.
REV 4:3 Me tiwei toundei lek nanghei inyon xok ambei qakous lei jaspa is qakous gyand lei kanilian. Myeiy liw on ti teyei lek qakous neluy nambei emeral, di vivekwou siaking.
REV 4:4 24 siaking bamba dei vivekwou siaking, me 24 teivateiv toundei lek siaking. Xel vunek en teimb teleing me toung qelumking wei ghol eno lek lund.
REV 4:5 Zivip nex mema lam eivek siaking, me wong nindenduing ngandoung de dewek toung ngandoung. Lam nenyex lim yuw wei di tum magyand eno toungale wou siaking. Xel tine inye laweeng lim yuw wei Anutu yo.
REV 4:6 Me toungale wou siaking nanghei inyon is eno xok ambei mamileeng wei dewek o, me inyei wo mabelin. Eivek masenghoing e vivekwou siaking eno lul mapieing vey, me xel mend ngenong eno sevunexe xel, wou manghalus me wou demi.
REV 4:7 Lul mapieing tiwei tax o nambei layon, de nge wei yuw eno nambei manghaxo, me nge wei yal eno ma ne nambei xomaxoneing ti, de tiwei vey eno nambei tuw wei mi zeivek o.
REV 4:8 Lul mapieing vey on titi eno banis teyei lek limti me manghalus ngenong sevunexe e vivekwou dalus, me eivek e banis xeinghembi. Me bendiyeing aluw boukeing eno xel se mi tip neileing.
REV 4:9 De lek bouk kawei lul mapieing bong xeiyaing ngandoung me bong e lei zekna me bo dange na wou e wei mindei lek siaking me mindei luta luta yo,
REV 4:10 24 teivateiv ev vaxend qatu eivek wou e wei mindei lek siaking o manghalus, me wo lalo wou e wei mindei mapieing luta luta yo. Xel liw xel xe qelumking ghol wou siaking me neil.
REV 4:11 “Wang on teyei lek, xa xe Tambiy Ngandoung me Anutu, bei na qou xeiyaing ngandoung me bong e lei zekna me nikanzek ngandoung, en wang toung lulul sapa yon, me nangya wa xe woueing nalei eno wang toung lulul on tyip me toundei.”
REV 5:1 Woyom a xei qapiya tiwei xel vevilexe is qayeeng wei xel byex lek yuw valuvalu xouing me xel betiy angya newiy lim yuw zeyi eno toundei eivek e wei toundei lek siaking eno mema payeiv.
REV 5:2 De a xei angela nikanzekta ti di taxe xoulekeing me neilteyei bei, “Eti teyeimbei zex xel newiy yon me bindek qapiya vevilexeing?”
REV 5:3 Ekom xel ma eivek tyoung gheyapu o lek tembuing o eivek tembuing xeinghembi wei teyeimbei bindek qapiya vevilexeing on me gyeina eivek lalei.
REV 5:4 A eng me na eng lumama en nambei eti se yeiwou xelti wei e teyeimbei bindek qapiya vevilexeing o e teyeimbei gyeina lalei.
REV 5:5 Woyom teivateiv on ti neil wou ay, “Wa seng deeng! Wei, layon wei velei wei Yuda yo, me Luselis wei Dawit buyeiw wei byex mangheeng lek eno wo vevek ma woy. E teyeimbei bindek qapiya vevilexeing me zex newiy lim yuw on.”
REV 5:6 Woyom a xei Sipsip Lingheing ti, di yeima nambei ingwei xel leis e mey o, toungale eivek siaking masenghoing, is xel lul mapieing vey on me teivateiv nale vivekwou e. E xe lu qepeind on lim yuw me manghalus on lim yuw wei inyei laweeng lim yuw wei Anutu yo wei Anutu wong ela eivek tembuing tambak on dalus.
REV 5:7 Moxo lam me qou qapiya vevilexeing veil e wei toundei lek siaking eno mema payeiv.
REV 5:8 Me ka e qou, eno lul mapieing vey on me 24 teivateiv on ev vaxend qatu eivek wou Sipsip Lingheing manghalus. Xel titi xe lul wei nambei gita me xel di zeim dipek ghol wei pup en nenyex lu xeiliy o, inye zeimeing mema wei xel vambuing.
REV 5:9 Me xel wong lalo vako ti: “Wang teyei lek bei qou qapiya vevilexeing me ghe zex e xe newiy de ghe bindek en inyei xel leis wang mey, me wang bey xomaxoneing en wa gyand me ghe wong xel la wou Anutu eivek veleivlei titi me vya titi me xomaxoneing ninavi titi me tembuing tambak titi.
REV 5:10 Wang wong xel on nambei tete lalei ti me lumukiyeiw wei embei bo xuk wou xe xe Anutu yo, me tyek xel bo king en xomaxoneing lek tembuing.”
REV 5:11 Woyom a xeila me na ngo angela ngenongakes vyend, teyei lek ngenong me ngenongakes kamouyo me tausen tausen. Xel vivekwou siaking me lul mapieing me xel teivateiv.
REV 5:12 Xel wong lalo niseikeing bei: “Sipsip Lingheing wei xel leis e mey, eno teyei lek bei na qou nikanzek ngandoung me lulul nimza me lupeyei nimza me nikanzek me bong e lei zekna me xeiyaing ngandoung me bo xeilala wou e.”
REV 5:13 Woyom a ngo lul mapieing sapa sapa eivek tyoung gheyapu me lek tembuing me eivek tembuing xeinghembi me lek mamileeng me lulul dalusateiv wei toundei eivek xel on, wo lalo nambei nye: “Xeilala me bong e lei zekna me xeiyaing ngandoung me nikanzek ngandoung wei luta luta yo eno ena wou tambiy wei toundei lek siaking o me ena wou Sipsip Lingheing!”
REV 5:14 Lul mapieing vey on neil, “Zonghek.” De xel teivateiv on ev vaxend qatu eivek dom wo lalo wou luw.
REV 6:1 Andi xei de Sipsip Lingheing lex newiy lim yuw eno tiwei tax wei wo zeyi qapiya vevilexeing o. Woyom a ngo xel lul mapieing vey on ti neil eivek vya nambei dewek toungheing me neil, “Lam!”
REV 6:2 A xei la, eno inyon vuteiv teleing ti toungale wou a mang. Tambiy wei dei lek vuteiv eno zeim vanzay ti me xel wong qelumking ti wou e, me e dei lek vuteiv me la nambei tambiy wei wo vevek ghanaw me di wo vevek ngenong o.
REV 6:3 Woyom Sipsip Lingheing lex newiy nge, yuw wei wo zeyi qapiya vevilexeing o, a ngo lul mapieing nge wei yuw o neil, “Lam!”
REV 6:4 Woyom vuteiv nge lam myayaing inyei gyand nambei nenyex magyand ti. Xel wo nikanzek wou tambiy wei toundei lek vuteiv on bei e zeim lalei vevopeing veil tembuing bei bong xomaxoneing nyeis ama me na mey. Xel wong ngeyeing vevek wei manewou yuw valuvalu yo ti wou e.
